viśvaprasiddham। tarkasaṃgrahasya dīpikāvyatiriktāni padakṛtyam, ityādīni bahūni vyākhyānāni mudritānyamudritāni ca upalabhyante। ityādayaḥ anekā vyākhyāḥ mudritā amudritāśca vartante। nīlakaṇṭhīyaprakāśikāyāśca paṭhanapāṭhanapracāro asti। saṃkṣiptaśailyā
paṭhanapāṭhanagocaratāyāṃ mukhyo hetuḥ। tatrāpi nīlakaṇṭhaprakāśikā cittarañjakatamā cakāsti। yeṣāṃ gādādharyādiṣu grantheṣu gāḍhaḥ jñātumanubhavituṃ ca śaknuvanti। vyākhyā cirāt nāvatīrṇā। yadyapi nīlakaṇṭhaputreṇa kṛtā
bālatārkikāṇāṃ nopakāriṇī sā। pratyuta bahuṣu sthaleṣu vyāmohameva janayati। iyaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaputreṇa na kṛtā syādityapi tādṛśasthalānāṃ darśanena matiḥ samupajāyate। ata eva mādṛśānāṃ en es rāmānujatātācāryān prārthayam। teṣāṃ savidhe
nyāyaśāstraṃ mayādhītamitīmaṃ sambandhaṃ puraskṛtya prārthanāmakaravam। prakāśikāyāḥ vyākhyāṃ nirmāya aduḥ। tasyāḥ prakāśanasamayo adhunā samupanata iti nitarāṃ momudyate cetaḥ। anayā vyākhyayā bālatārkikāḥ sarve api mahāntamupakāraṃ prāpyasyantīti niścapracam।
paṅktiḥ dṛśyate। asyāḥ paṅktervāstavārthaḥ ayam - ayadyatra sādhakaviparyayapratiyogyāpādyakatvaṃ tarkasyeti। bhāskarodayākārastu imamāśayamagṛhītvā kimapi likhati। darśayatīti samuditārthaḥ" iti।
pratiyogino ghaṭādeḥ sattvasya sattvaprasakteḥ' itiprakāśikā । atra tarkitā āpādanaviṣayabhūtetyarthaḥ। āpādanāśrayabhūteti bhāskarodayā । iti paṅktirdṛśyate । tasyā ayamarthaḥ- yatsaṃbandhītyasya yaddhetusaṃbandhītyarthaḥ। tathā ca yaddhetusaṃbandhi yat sādhyaṃ
tadabhāvavyāpyahetvantarasya jñānaṃ tatpakṣe asti sa satpratipakṣaḥ। sa yatsaṃbandhītyatra yatpadena gṛhīto heturgrāhya iti। bhāskārodayāyāṃ tu - ayatpadena prakṛtābhipretapakṣaparigrahaḥ। pakṣetyatra tadityādiḥ। tathā ca yatpakṣakaṃ yatsādhyaṃ
vyākhyānaṃ dṛśyate । atrānanvayādikaṃ viduṣāṃ spaṣṭam। gṛhyate' iti paṅktirdṛśyate । atra jñānasya grahaḥ jñānagrahaḥ prāthamikaścāsau jñānagrahaśceti karmadhārayaḥ। tena prāthamikatvaṃ jñānagrahaviśeṣaṇam। jñānagrahe prāthamikatvaviśeṣaṇāt
jñānagrahaḥ vyavacchidyata iti prakāśikāśayaḥ। vyākhyātam । visaṃvādipravṛttijanakatvāt yannaivaṃ tannaivam' iti dṛśyate । atra visaṃvādipravṛttītyatra visaṃvādinī yā pravṛttiḥ tajjanakatvādityarthaḥ। visaṃvādinītyasya viphaletyarthaḥ।bhāskārodayāyāṃ tu aviparītajñāna
vatpravṛttijanakatvādityarthaḥ' ityuktam। anena visaṃvādinaḥ pravṛttiriti vigraho abhipretaḥ। atrānaucityaṃ spaṣṭameva। kānicit sthalāni pradarśitāni। etādṛśasthaleṣubālapriyāyāṃ prāmāṇikarītyā vyākhyānaṃ kṛtam। villiyaṃpākkaṃ śrīsampatkumāratātācāryāṇāṃ sakāśāt labdhā।
tālapatrāgranthapuṣpikātaḥ avagamyate। api cātratyapramā tvānugamaḥ ratnapeṭikāyāṃdṛśyata। kiṃ ca tadīyagranthāntaraśailīmanukarotīyaṃ prasāraṇā। ato vyākhyeyaṃ śrīkṛṣṇatātācāryaiḥ kṛtetyatra na ko api saṃdehaḥ। asyāṃ prasāraṇāyāṃ
prāyaḥ sarveṣāṃ lakṣaṇānāmanugamāḥ vartante। tasmādiyaṃ vyākhyā mudrāpitā। yadi pūrvameveyaṃ samupalabdhā abhaviṣyat tadā iyamapi tattatsthalasyādhasyāt bālapriyayā sākaṃ mudrāpitā abhaviṣyat। athāpi saṃtuṣyatyantaraṅgam।
tamīśvaraṇām।' karuṇāvilāsavijṛmbhitam। prārthayamānaḥ sabhaktiśraddhaṃ samarpayāmi। bālatārkikāṇāṃ grantho ayaṃ mahāntamupakāramādhāsyati। satsvapi
rāmānujatātācāryebhyaḥ parāṃ kṛtajñatāṃ prakaṭayāmi। kārtajñyamāviṣkaromi। aḍayārkośālayādhikāribhyaśca hārdikīṃ kṛtajñatāṃ prakāśayāmi। mahāśayebhyaḥ kṛtajñatāṃ nivedayāmi।
nivedyate। akaravam। anusandhānamārgānusāreṇa likhito ayamupoddhātaḥ anusandhānakutūhalināmupakārāya kalpate। anavadhānataḥ mudraṇādau jātāḥ aśuddhayaḥ vidvadbhiḥ kṣantavyāḥ śodhanīyāśceti prārthaye।
।। । sarvasaṃpratipannam। tatra maṅgalācaraṇe kiṃ pramāṇam? kiṃ vā prayojanamiti maṅgalavāde nirūpyate। nyāyabhāṣyakāraḥ
maṅgalācaraṇamadhikṛtya na kimapyavādīt। nyāyavārtikakāro api maṅgalācaraṇaṃ vinaiva prabandhamārebhe। ṭīkākārastu vācaspatimiśraḥ maṅgalācaraṇapūrvakameva ṭīkāmārabhata। tatra paramaśiṣṭo api iṣṭadevatānamaskārarūpaṃ maṅgalaṃ kṛtavāneva। athāpi granthe tanna
nyaveśayat। na hi maṅgalakaraṃ yadyatkriyate tatsarvaṃ granthe niveśanīyamiti nirbandho astīti samādhānaṃ provāca ṭīkākāraḥ। maṅgalācaraṇe śiṣṭācāraḥ pramāṇamiti sūcayati। abhīṣṭadevatānamaskārapūrvakaṃ prekṣāvantaḥ pravartante। paraṃ tu dṛśyate
akṛtanamaskārasyāpi samīhitasiddheśca। na cātra avṛṣṭikāmaḥ kārīrīṃ karmakartṛsādhanavaiguṇyaṃ kalpayāmaḥ। tasmāt aarthakāma iha vaṭe śiṣṭācārasyāsaṃbhavāt। tathā ca kvacinmaṅgale samāptyabhāvaḥ karmakartṛsādhanavaiguṇyaprayuktaḥ। iha janmani asatyapi maṅgale
samāptistu janmāntarīyamaṅgalādhīneti samavarṇayan। etena ca। vighnavināyakāḥ protsāryante। tataḥ śāstraparisamāptirityarthavān praṇāmaḥ। yatra tu na samāptistatra praṇāmasyāsamyakatvamanumeyaṃ
karturadharmabāhulyaṃ vā। yatrāpyantareṇa praṇāmaṃ praṇāmo anumeyaḥ, sādhanāntarasādhyo vā dharmaḥ। vācikapraṇāme tvanyeṣāmapyupadeśasiddhiriti viśeṣaḥ। yasya tu vighnaheturadharma eva nāsti, tenāpi tadāśaṅkyā kartavya eva praṇāmaḥ। śatrvādyāśaṅkyā
bodhayanti। maṅgalakartavyatāyāṃ pramāṇaṃ tu te na pratyapādayan। maṅgalasya samāptiphalakatvameva bhāsarvañjñābhimatam। prayuñjānaḥ kaṇādo maṅgalamācarati smeti upaskārakāro vyācaṣṭe। maṅgalamanvatiṣṭhat। tatra kiraṇāvalyām - kṛtamaṅgalena cārabdhaṃ
karma parisamāpyate pracīyate ca। (pracayo nāma prāripsitasya granthasya gurūṇā śiṣyāya dānasyāvicchedaḥ।) na cānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vācyam। āgamamūlakasya kāryakāraṇabhāvasyābādhyatvāt। satyapi maṅgale samāptyabhāvastu karmakartṛsādhanavaiguṇyāditi pratyapādi।
devatā guruśca namaskriyate iti śiṣṭācāro ayam। phalaṃ ca namaskārasya vighnadhvaṃsaḥ। nanu kiṃ namaskārādeva vighnopaśamaḥ utānyasmādapi। na tāvannamaskārādevetyasti niyamaḥ। asatyapi namaskāre nyāyamīmāṃsābhāṣyayoḥ parisamāptatvāt। yadā
cānyasmādapi tadā niyamena maṅgalācaraṇam vyartham। tadanuṣṭhānāt। na ca nyāyamīmāṃsābhāṣyakārābhyāṃ na kṛto namaskāraḥ। kiṃ tu kṛto api granthe na nyabandhi। kathamidaṃ jñāyata iti cet - kartuḥ śiṣṭatayaiva। mleccho api tāvat gurvārambhe karmaṇi na
pravartate yāvadiṣṭān na namasyati। tathā ca paramāstikau smṛtirapi pramāṇam। tathā hi manuḥ jitendriya। nityamagnimatandritaḥ।।
nityaṃ ca prayatātmanām। vinipāto na vidyate ।।" iti। vinipāta ityasya vighna ityarthaḥ। atra dvitīyaślokaḥ maṇikāraiḥ
maṅgalavādānte pramāṇatayā udāhṛtaḥ। "ādyaṃ puruṣamīśānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam। vyaktāvyaktaṃ sanātanam।। yadviśvaṃ sadasatparam।
purāṇaṃ paramavyayam।। viṣṇuṃ vareṇyamanaghaṃ śucim। carācaraguruṃ harim।। sarvalokairmahātmanaḥ।
vyāsasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ।।" maṅgalācaraṇasyāvaśyakartavyatāṃ nivedayati। evaṃ viṣṇupurāṇe api prabhum। jagatāmīśamajamakṣayamavyayam।।
viṣṇunamaskārapūrvakaṃ granthamārabhate sma। sādhayāmāsuḥ। śiṣṭācārānumitaśrutireva maṅgalakartavyatāyāṃ pramāṇamityapi nyarūpayan। tato maṅgalasya vighnadhvaṃsaḥ phalamiti svasiddhāntaṃ vistareṇa samavarṇayan।
iti śrutiḥ granthārambhe maṅgalakartavyatāyāṃ pramāṇam। maṅgalasya samāptiḥ phalam। vighnadhvaṃso dvāram। vighnasamasaṃkhyākasya maṅgalasya kāraṇatvāt nānvayavyabhicāraḥ। janmāntarīyamaṅgalamādāya na vyatirekavyabhicāra iti nirūpayanti। prakāśikāyām maṅgalasya
vighnadhvaṃsaḥ phalamiti maṇikṛnmatamapi saṃgṛhītam। na kevalaṃ śrutiḥ pratipādayāmbabhūvuḥ prakāśikākṛtaḥ। dravyavibhajanamasaṃgatam। pṛthivyādinavadravyavyatiriktasya dīpikāyāṃ nyarūpyata। tatra mīmāṃsakānāmayamāśayaḥ- tamaso dravyatvaṃ
tāvadavaśyamaṅgīkaraṇīyam। anīlaṃ tamaḥ' iti pratītyā rūpavattvasya rūpavattvakriyāvattvābhyāṃ dravyatvavyāpyābhyāṃ dravyatvasiddheḥ। tathā ca ityanumānaṃ tamaso dravyatve pramāṇam। na ca yatra yatrālokābhāvaḥ uktahetuḥ svarūpāsiddha iti vācyam। ālokādyātmake tejasi
cākṣaṣupramāviṣayatvasyaiva sattvena vyabhicārāt uktavyāpterasaṃbhavāt। na ca tejobhinnatvaṃ niveśya vyāptirvaktavyā। tathā ca yatra yatra iti vyāpterna vyabhicāra iti vācyam। tathāpi tamastvena cākṣuṣapramāviṣayatvasyaiva sattvena vyabhicārasya durvāratvāt। evaṃ
pārthivaparamāṇugatanailyameva tama iti pakṣāḥ na saṃgacchante। abhāvarūpatvāsaṃbhavāt। nailyāśrayatayā pratīyamānasya tamasaḥ nailyarūpatvāsaṃbhavācca। na ca vidhirūpeṇa pratīyamānatvasya pradhvaṃsasyābhāvatvānupapattiriti vācyam।
bhāvarūpavastvantarānupalambhāt pralayasyābhāvarūpatvāt। api ca ghaṭasya pralayasyābhāvarūpatvam। tamasastu niṣpratiyogikatayā upalambhāt nābhāvarūpatvam। na pārthivatve tatra sparśopalambhaprasaṅgaṃ iti vācyam।
tatra vyabhicāreṇa uktaniyamāsaṃbhavāt। ityanumānena tamaso dravyatvābhāvasiddheḥ kathaṃ tasya dravyatvam। āhosvit rūpamātraṃ tama iti vādibhiḥ। nādyaḥ, tanmate tadghaṭitahetoścāsiddheḥ। na dvitīyaḥ, naiyāyikamate
ālokābhāvasyaiva tamastvāt pakṣadṛṣṭāntabhedābhāvāt। tathā ca doṣaḥ iti। divābhītādidṛśyamānairdravyairvyabhicārāt। yogidṛśyamānairdravyairvyabhicārāt।
jalāditvābhāve ca siddhe atiriktadravyatvaṃ sidhyatīti। atiriktadravyatvakalpane pramāṇābhāvaḥ। tamo na dravyaṃ tamaso dravyatvābhāve pramāṇam। tejassāmānyābhāvarūpaṃ tamaḥ pakṣa, dūṣaṇasya nāvakāśaḥ। atha vā tamaśśabdavācyaṃ pakṣaḥ ālokābhāvo
dṛṣṭānta iti na doṣaḥ। anīlaṃ tamaḥ' acalati tamaḥ' iti sidhyatīti naiyāyikamatam। rūpādimattāpratīterbhramatvaṃ na vaktuṃ śakyam। anīlaṃ tamaḥ' acalati iti bādhakapratītyanudayena tasyāḥ bhramatvāyogāt। kiṃ ca
pratītirūpapādanīyā। tathā sati kiñcinniṣṭhapītarūpāropeṇa kadācit pītaṃ tama iti pratītirapi syāt। ityādipratītivat। tasmādanyadīyanīlarūpādarāropāsambhavena siddhameva।
kasahakṛtacakṣurgrāhyatvaṃ syāt। dravyavṛttilaukikaviṣayatāsaṃbandhena tamaso atiriktadravyatvasiddhiḥ। na ca tamobhinnadravyacākṣuṣatvāvacchinnaṃ pratyevālokasya kāraṇatvāṅgīkārāt nānupapattiriti vācyam। kāryatāvacchedake tamobhinnatvaniveśena gauravāpatteriti cet - na।
ālokasahakṛtacakṣuṣaḥ kāraṇatvaṃ vācyam। tathā ca kāryatāvacchedakagauravasya duṣpariharatvāt। ataḥ tamobhinnaṃ tamaso atiriktadravyatvasiddhirniṣpratyūhaiveti। taijasatvaprastāvo na dṛśyate। paraṃ tu
bodhayati। tatra sūtre ataijasānām' iti padamadhikamāsīditi jñāyate। yato vedāntadeśikaiḥ sarvārthaṃsiddhau vaiśeṣikasūtramuddhṛtamasti। tena ca suvarṇasya taijasatvaṃ kaṇādasyāpi saṃmatamiti jñāyate। praśastapādabhāṣye
aākarajaṃ suvarṇādi' ityetāvanmātramuktam। tatra kandalīkāraḥ aākaraḥ sthānaviśeṣaḥ। tasmin suvarṇarajatādi taijasaṃ dravyaṃ jāyate। suvarṇādīnāṃ taijasatve tāvadāgamaḥ pramāṇam। anudbhūtarūpasparśaṃ piṇḍībhāvayogyaṃ suvarṇādikamārabhyate। tatra
pārthivadravyasamavetā rasādaya upalabhyante' ityāha। atra āgamapadena aagnerapatyaṃ prathamaṃ hiraṇyam' iti śrutivākyaṃ vivakṣitam। nyāyo abhihitaḥ। sa ca - sūvarṇe dravatvaṃ nāsti। gurutvamiva saṃyuktasamavāyāt pratīyata iti cet - na।
na pārthivam iti। prasādhitam। taijasatvaṃ sādhitavantaḥ। tatrānuktāni anyānyapi kānicidanumānāni maṇau pradarśitānīti viśeṣaḥ।
tāvatparyantamagnisaṃyuktajalamadhyasthapītaṭavat। vahnivat। kvathyamānajalamadhyasthitaghṛtavat। tannaivaṃ yathā jalaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā।
pṛthivītvavat। rūpavadvṛttidravyatvasākṣādvyāpyajātitvāt jalatvavat। jalaparamāṇuvat। taijasā vā tata eva, yannaivaṃ tannaivaṃ yathā ghṛtaparamāṇuḥ।
iti vā। taijasatvaṃ sādhayati। matāntaramupanyastam। teṣāmāśayastu apītaṃ suvarṇaṃ drutam' iti pratītyā pītarūpavati suvarṇe ata eva pārthive dravatvavattvamavagamyate।
vyabhicāro durvāraḥ। na ca tādṛśapratītirbhramarūpeti vācyam। bādhakābhāvāt। na ca tasya pārthivatve agnisaṃyogāttadīyarūpanāśaḥ kuto na bhavatīti vācyam। anubhavabalena rūpanāśaṃ prati tādātmyena suvarṇasya pratibandhakatvāṅgīkārāditi।
āvaśyakaḥ। tatra suvarṇasthapārthivabhāgamatadravatvanāśarūpakāryasya abhāvaḥ iti nirvivādam। tatra tādṛśaviśiṣṭābhāvarūpaḥ kāraṇābhāvaḥ na viśeṣyābhāvāt, atyantāgnisaṃyogarūpasya viśeṣyasya yatra sattvāt। pratibandhaka kiñcit dravadravyāntaraṃ tatrāstīti vaktavyam। tasyāpi
tathetyanavasthā syāt। ataḥ pratibandhakāntaraṃ vinā avinaśyaddravatvādeva tanna pṛthivī iti। pārthivabhāgasyāpi dravatvaṃ tejobhāgasyāpi dravatvamaṅgīkurvanti। apītadravyadravatvanāśa' adravadravyāntara' iti padayoḥ svārasyāt।
pārthivabhāgasya dravatvābhāva eva pratipāditaḥ। ata eva tadanusāreṇa vistareṇa nirūpayanti। prasādhya rūparahitatvāt vāyuḥ na pratyakṣavedya iti nyarūpayan। etattattvamadhunā parīkṣyate।
kāraṇam। tathā ca vāyorudbhūtarūpavirahāt na pratyakṣagocaratvam, kiṃ tvanumānaikavedyatā। tathā ca vaiśeṣikaṃ sūtram asparśaśca vāyoḥ' [vai sū ] iti। caśabdena śabdadhṛtikampā gṛhyanta। ataḥ sparśādibhirvāyuranumeyaḥ, na tu pratyakṣa iti sūtrārthaḥ।
iti। tatra sparśādanyasya tvacā agrahaṇāt। na ca vāyurvātīti jñānāt vāyuḥ pratyakṣa iti vācyam। tasya jñānasya sparśaliṅgakānumitirūpatvāt। spārśanatvamapi nivartate। ato vāyurna pratyakṣaviṣayaḥ, api tvanumeya
iti nyarūpayat। dravyaviṣayakaspārśanaṃ prati nodbhūtasparśamātraṃ prayojakam। tadvṛttisaṃkhyāderapi pratyakṣatā syāt। yogyavyaktivṛtteḥ saṃkhyāyāḥ yogyatvamiti niyamāt। na khalūṣmaṇi kareṇa parāmṛṣṭe api
tadgatāṃ saṃkhyāṃ ko apyadhyakṣayati। nāpi dravyapratyakṣaṃ prati prasajyeta। na hi nipuṇamavalokayannapi candraprabhādigataṃ saṃkhyādikaṃ kaścit paśyati। ataḥ pratyekaṃ vyabhicārāt udbhūtasparśaḥ udbhūtarūpaṃ cetyubhayamapi dravyapratyakṣatve prayojakamiti vaktavyam।
candrādyālokaḥ udbhūtarūpavānapi udbhūtasparśavānna bhavati। nidāghoṣmā udbhūtasparśavānapi nodbhūtarūpavān। śakyate। tathā ca vāyurudbhūtasparśavānapi nodbhūtarūpavāniti na pratyakṣaḥ।
prati nodbhūtasparśaḥ kāraṇam। tathā sati pakṣikāṇḍe calati pūrvadeśavibhāgottaradeśasaṃyogayoḥ pratyakṣatā na syāt। prabhāmaṇḍalātmakayoḥ pūrvottaradeśayoḥ udbhūtasparśaśūnyatvāt। ata udbhūtarūpameva dravyapratyakṣatāyāṃ tantramiti saṃpradāyavidaḥ।
pratyapīpadan। pakṣadharmadravyatvāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakamudabhūtarūpavattvamupādhiḥ। tathā ca maṇikāranirūpaṇasya sārāṃśaḥ। dīpikākāro apyamumeva panthānamavalalambe।
pratyakṣatvopapādanam। vyavāsthāpi। tathā hi - bahirindriyajanyadravyapratyakṣatvāvacchinnaṃ prati na rūpaṃ kāraṇaṃ, pramāṇābhāvāt। api tu cākṣuṣapratyakṣe rūpaṃ, kāraṇam। tathā ca sparśāśrayasya vāyoḥ tvācapratyakṣaviṣayatve na
kimapi bādhakam। yathā hi udbhūtasparśaśūnyāyā api prabhāyāḥ aprabhāṃ saṃkhyāpi gṛhyeteti maṇyuktadoṣasya kaḥ parihāra iti cet - ayam। sajātīyasaṃvalanarūpāddoṣāt kvacit vāyoḥ saṃkhyā na gṛhyate। doṣābhāve tu saṃkhyāgrahaṇamiṣṭameveti।
gacchati pūrvottarasaṃyogavibhāgau pratyakṣau। tatrāśrayasya śakyate। vāyau tu naitādṛśī yuktirasti। ato vāyurapratyakṣa eveti dinakaryādau spaṣṭam। rucidattamiśraḥ vāyoḥ pratyakṣatvameva samarthaṃyate। udbhūtarūpasparśavati
sauratejasi pratyakṣe api saṃkhyādikaṃ na pratyakṣam। svīkriyatām। yadvā udbhūtarūpavattvameva prayojakam। gṛhyate। tathāpi vāyoḥ spārśanatve udbhūtasparśamātraṃ prayojakamiti
vāyoḥ spārśaṃnatvaṃ nirābādhamiti tena nyarūpi। panthānamavalambya pramāyāḥ apramāyāśca lakṣaṇe abhihite। atra viṣaye prāktanānāmāśayaṃ nūtanalakṣaṇābhidhāne kāraṇaṃ ca vimṛśāmaḥ। ityādidvitīyasūtre tattvajñānaṃ mithyājñānasya nivartakamityavadat।
tena tattvajñānaṃ prameti sūtrakāro manyate। pramāyā eva bhramarūpamithyājñānanivartakatvāt। tasya bhāvaḥ tattvaṃ - viśeṣyavṛttidharmaḥ tasya jñānaṃ tattvajñānam। viśeṣyavṛttidharmaprakārakaṃ jñānaṃ tattvajñānamiti yāvat। anena viśeṣyavṛttidharmaprakārakajñānatvaṃ
pramāyāḥ lakṣaṇamiti paryavasyati। atra pakṣe yathārthasmṛtāvativyāptiḥ prasajati, tasyā api viśeṣyavṛttidharmaprakārakajñānatvāt। boddhavyamiti vadan bhāṣyakāraḥ aupalabdhi pramā' iti sūcayati। sūtrānusāreṇa upalabdhipadasya jñānam ityathaḥ।
nirviṣayakajñānasyāsaṃbhavāt arthaṃviṣayakajñānatvaṃ pramātvamiti labhyate। ata eva ayattat arthavijñānaṃ sā pramitiḥ' iti prathamasūtre bhāṣyam। arthaviṣayakatvāt jñānatvācca। hi śabdārthasaṃbandhaḥ। lokaśca
ityāhuḥ। arthāvyabhicāri smṛtibhinnaṃ jñānaṃ prameti tadarthaḥ। jñānasyārthāvyabhicaritatvaṃ yathāvasthitārthaviṣayakatvam। atra pakṣe api yathārthasmṛtāvativyāptidoṣo vartate।
pramāyāḥ lakṣaṇamuktam। anubhave samyaktvaṃ ca tathābhūtārthaniścayasvabhāvatvamiti nyāyabhūṣaṇe। śivādityamiśraiścābhyadhāyi। idaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bahudhā vikalpya khaṇḍana adūṣyata।
yathārthānubhavatvaṃ pramāyāḥ lakṣaṇamiti avadan। anubhavapadasaṃyojanena smṛtāvativyāptirnirākṛtā bhavati। anubhave yathārthatvaṃ yatra yadasti tatra tadviṣayakatvameva। tathā hi bhrāntinirvacanāvasare kusumāñjalau tasyāvagatiriti bhrāntyarthatvāt' ityabhāṇi।
ityavādi। evaṃ ca pramālakṣaṇam। maṇikārairapyetallakṣaṇaṃ siddhāntatvena svīkṛtamiti dīpikākāro api tadeva lakṣaṇaṃ provāca। yajjñānaṃ tadviśeṣyakam। tatpramā'
iti। tatra prathamaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bhramabhinnatve sati jñānatvamiti। atra lakṣaṇe śuktirajatayoḥ ahame rajate' iti jñānaṃ rajate rajataviṣayakatvāṃśe pramā itīṣyate। lakṣaṇamanusṛtam। tacca tadvadviśeṣyakatve sati tatprakārakaṃ jñānaṃ
prameti। smṛteḥ pramātvamiṣyata eva। atastasyā api pramālakṣaṇalakṣyatvānnātivyāptiḥ। yadi smṛteḥ pramātvamabhyupagamyate tarhitatkāraṇasya pañcamapramāṇatvamāpadyata iti cet - maivam।
pramāṇalakṣaṇasyānubhavaghaṭitatvāt। yathārthānubhavakaraṇaṃ pramāṇamiti pramāṇalakṣaṇam। smṛtikaraṇasyānubhavakaraṇatve nāsti, smṛteranubhavatvābhāvāt iti na pramāṇatvaprasaktiḥ iti। viśvanāthasyedamupapādanaṃ yuktarūpaṃ pratibhāti।
tadabhimatam। tenaiva apratyakṣānumānopamānaśabdāḥ pramāṇāni' (nyā anubhavaghaṭitameva pramāṇalakṣaṇaṃ kartavyamiti sūcitamiti। rajataraṅge' iti bhrame ativyāptiḥ। tasyāpi raṅgatvavadraṅgaviśeṣyakatve sati raṅgatvaprakārakatvācca। ato
pramālakṣaṇaṃ vācyamiti prakāśikāyāṃ niṣkarṣaḥ kṛtaḥ। prakāratāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyatānirūpakānubhavaḥ pramā। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāvacchedakasambandhena svāśrayavanniṣṭhatvasavanirūpitatvobhayasambandhena। yadvā prakāritāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyitāvadanubhavaḥ pramā। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svāvacchinnatvasvanirūpitaprakāratāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyatānirūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svāśrayavanniṣṭhatvasambandheneti। adhikaṃ prasāraṇākhyavyākhyāyāṃ draṣṭavyam। niṣkṛṣṭalakṣaṇasyāpi nirvikalpakāvyāptiḥ। niṣprakārake
nirvikalpakapadābhidheyajñāne tatprakārakatvaghaṭitapramālakṣaṇavirahāt। iti lakṣaṇaṃ vācyam। muktāvalīkṛtastu nirvikalpakaṃ bhramapramābahirbhūntamiti manyante। pratyekaṃ lakṣaṇamapi niṣkṛṣya pratipāditamasti। paraṃ
pratipādita iti manyante। etattattvamadhunā paryālocyate। sūtrākārasaṃmatamiti jñāyate। praśastapādabhāṣye api kāraṇatrayaṃ svīkṛtam। ayugapat trayāṇāṃ samavāyyasamavāyinimittakāraṇānāṃ vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ' ityādayo bhāṣyagranthāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ।
vartate। tathā hi nyāyadarśaṃne caturthādhyāne prathamāhnike aṣṭādaśaṃ sūtram akramanirdeśādapratiṣedhaḥ' iti। sūtramidaṃ śūnyameva jagadupādānakāraṇamiti matanirākaraṇasaṃdarbhe। tatra ca vyūhāntaraṃ cāpadyante।
utpadyate। dṛśyante iti। atra sūcitam। aavayavāstatsaṃyogāścāṅkurotpattihetavaḥ' ityanena sūcitam। nyāyavārtikakāro api trīṇi kāraṇāni tatra tatra kaṇṭharaveṇa
nirdiśati। atatkāritatvādahetuḥ' iti sūtrasthaṃ bhavati। yacca nimittaṃ tat itarayoḥ iti sūtrasthaṃ ana kiñcidapyekakāraṇakaṃ kāryaṃ dṛṣṭam। sarvaṃ hi kāryaṃ vārtikaṃ cātrānusandhānamarhataḥ। tathā
trividhamiti vibhāgaḥ prācīnagranthārūḍha iti siddham। navyagrantheṣu teṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ lakṣaṇānyeva pariṣkṛtya pratipāditāni। nāṅgīkurvantīti। naiyāyikā avayavātiriktamavayavinaṃ svīkurvanti। vedāntinastu tantūnāṃ saṃyogaviśeṣa eva paṭo na
tadatirikta iti prāhuḥ। vedāntināṃ mate tantuseyāṅgaḥ niviśate। naiyāyikānāṃ mate tu paṭanāmako avayavī kāryabhūtaḥ। sa ca tantusaṃyogaviśeṣādutpadyate। atastantusaṃyogo api kāraṇamiti svīkartavyam। tasya samavāyikāraṇatvāsaṃbhavena asamavāyikāraṇatvaṃ
pratipāditamiti। nimittakāraṇatvamevāstu iti cet atrocyate। nimittakāraṇabhūtatantuvāyanāśe api paṭarūpaṃ kāryaṃ tiṣṭhati। tantusaṃyoganāśe tu na paṭastiṣṭhati, api tu naśyati। ato
asamavāyikāraṇatvena svīkṛta iti। vaktavyam। na tāvannimittakāraṇanāśaḥ, kulālādisadbhāve api ghaṭanāśadarśanāt kulālādināśe api ghaṭasadbhāvadarśanācca। nāpi samavāyikāraṇanāśaḥ kāraṇam। dvyaṇukanāśānupapatteḥ। dvyaṇukasya
hi paramāṇuḥ samavāyikāraṇam। na hi tasya nāśaḥ saṃbhavati, nityatvāt। ato dvyaṇukasya samavāyikāraṇanāśānnāśo na nāśo vaktavyaḥ। tathā ca dvyaṇukanāśasya asamavāyikāraṇanāśo asamavāyikāraṇasvīkāra āvaśyakaḥ।
iti ceta - na। yadi samavāyikāraṇabhinnaṃ sarvaṃ kulālādināśe api ghaṭanāśāpattiḥ syāt। ato nimittakāraṇamatiriktatayā svīkaraṇīyamiti। tathā ca yuktiyuktatvāt prācīnagranthārūḍhaśceti siddham।
nirvikalpakaṃ savikalpakam ca। uktam। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasaṃbandhānavagāhi jñānaṃ nirvikalpakam, iti dīpikāyām। viśeṣyatāśūnyatvaṃ prakāratāśūnyatvaṃ prakāśikāyām। etattattvamidārnīṃ prāktanagranthāloḍanapūrvakaṃ
vicāryate। nirvikalpakasavikalpakaśabdābhyāṃ pratyakṣavibhāgaḥ kṛtaḥ। iti tātparyaṭīkākārāḥ nirūpayanti। paraṃ tu bhāṣye vārtike vā naivaṃvidhaṃ nirūpaṇamupalabhāmahe।
lābhaprakārastatra na pradarśitaḥ। nyāyabhūṣaṇe tu avyapadeśyapadena sayuktikaṃ pratyapādi। nirvikalpakapratyakṣaṃ pradarśitam। svarūpālocanamātramityasya svarūpamātrasya grahaṇamityarthaḥ। mātrapadena
jātyādisaṃbandhaviṣayakatvavyavacchedaḥ। tataḥ savikalpakapratyakṣaṃ sodāharaṇamupadarśitam। paraṃ tu nirvikalpakasavikalpakaśabdau na prayuktau। kumārilabhaṭṭa api prathamaṃ nirvikalpakam।
bālamūkādivijñānasadṛśaṃ śuddhavastujam।।' dharmairjātyādibhiryathā। sāpi pratyakṣatvena saṃmatā।।' savikalpakaṃ ca lakṣayāṃbabhūvuḥ। prakaraṇapañcikāyāṃ ca
dvividhā buddhiriṣyate। svarūpaviṣayetarā।।' nirvikalpakasavikalpakabhedena dvaividhyaṃ prādarśayan। nirvikalpakam' iti nirvikalpakalakṣaṇaṃ prādarśi।
vaiśiṣṭyānavagāhītyasyaiva vivaraṇaṃ niṣprakārakamiti। nirvikalpake vartate। tathā ca nirviśeṣyakaṃ jñānaṃ nirvikalpakamityapi śakyate vaktum। tathā anuktvā niṣprakārakamiti vadatāṃ nāpekṣitamiti।
anumitivat ityanumānam। yathā aparvato vahnimān' vaktavyam। tadeva vaiśiṣṭyāviṣayakaṃ nirvikalpakam। tathā ca na nirvikalpakapratyakṣaṃ sidhyatīti vācyam। etajjanmani pūrvaṃ gotvasyānanubhavena tatsmaraṇāsaṃbhavāt।
viśiṣṭapratyakṣaṃ janayatu। tathā ca gataṃ nirvikalpakeneti vācyam। tathetyanavasthāprasaṅgāt। tathā ca gotvaviṣayakaṃ nirvikalpakamarthātsidhyati। yaduktaṃ viśiṣṭabuddherviśeṣaṇajñānapūrvakatvānnirvikalpakaṃ sidhyatīti।
tanna। gauriti viśiṣṭajñānaṃ viśeṣaṇajñānajanyaṃ viśiṣṭajñānatvāt ityanumāne bhinnasāmagrīvedyaviṣayakatvasyopādhitvāt। yatra viśiṣṭapratyakṣam। tatra hi viśeṣaṇaṃ saurabhaṃ ghrāṇendriyavedyaṃ viśeṣyaṃ viśiṣṭapratyakṣaṃ bhavati। ekendriyavedyayorgotvayorekakāla
kalpanaṃ na yujyate। saṃbandho na bhāsate। tadeva nirvikalpakam। cet-na। saṃbandhapadena kiṃ svarūpaṃ vivakṣitam? ata samavāyaḥ? ādye nirvikalpakam। dvitīye cakṣuṣā saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇatākhyasaṃnikarṣeṇa
grahaṇaṃ bhaviturmahati। anyathā yogyasyāpi samavāyasya prathamamagrahaṇe paścādapi grahaṇaṃ na syāt। tathā ca saṃsargānavagāhi nirvikalpakajñānaṃ na yuktisahamiti। bhāsate। saṃbandhastu na bhāsate। saṃbandhajñānaṃ prati saṃbandhijñānasya
kāraṇatayā pūrvaṃ tadabhāvāt। tathā ca pūrvaṃ tatastayoḥ saṃbandhāvagāhi savikalpakaṃ jñānaṃ jāyate। samavāyāgrahaṇam' iti। sahakārivaikalyādityasya saṃbandhijñānavirahādityarthaḥ। tathā ca saṃbandho api kuto nirvikalpake
na bhāsata iti codyasya nāvasaraḥ। bhinnasāmagrīvedyaviṣayakatvamupādhiriti - tatradaṃ vaktavyam। viśeṣaṇajñānakalpanena tajjanyaiva viśiṣṭabuddhiḥ। tathā ca saṃbhavatīti।
pramāṇamiti cet-na। gauḥ iti ityanumānasya pramāṇatvāt। viśeṣaṇajñānasyāpi iti। iti sodāharaṇaṃ pradarśitam। prakāśikāyāṃ pratyakṣaṃ dvividhaṃ
laukikam alaukikaṃ ceti। laukikapratyakṣahetuḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ saṃyogādibhedena ṣaṅvidhaḥ। alaukikapratyakṣahetuḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ pratyapādi। nyāyavārtike prastutaḥ, sūtre bhāṣye vā na dṛśyate kvāpi। etaṃ
saṃnikarṣaśabdenocyate। saṃbhavī ca saṃbandhaḥ ṣaḍvidha eveti pratyapādayat। tathā sati ani' ityupasargasya vyarthatvāt। śabdamahimnā ṣaḍvidhatvalābhe niśabdo vyartha iti। karṣaśabdasya saṃbandhavācakatvena kutra prasiddhiriti bhavatā vaktavyam।
sambandhavācakatayā। tasmāt asam' ani' ityupasargadvayayukta eva iṇdhātuḥ samavāyam। tasmāt kṛṣadhātoḥ sambandhārthakatvadyotakatayā śabdamahimnā ṣaḍvidhatvalābha iti vyākhyānaṃ na samīcīnam। pratyakṣaṃ pratyanvayavyatirekabalāddhetutvaṃ sidhyati। nyāyasiddho ayamartho
ityunnīyate। aparamatamapratiṣiddhamanumatamiti hi tantrayuktiḥ' iti nyāyāt iti। sūcanamasti। tathā hi ātmaviṣayakapratyakṣaṃ prati manassaṃyogaḥ kāraṇamityuktam। tena
dravyaviṣayakapratyakṣaṃ prati indriyasaṃyogaḥ kāraṇamiti sūcitam। kāraṇamiti spaṣṭīkṛtam। tathā cakṣussaṃyuktasamavāyaḥ kāraṇamiti spaṣṭamuktam। saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyo heturiti vyañjitam। tathā-
śabdapratyakṣe heturiti dhvanitam। śabdatvapratyakṣe samavetasamavāyākhyaḥ saṃnikarṣo api sūcita eva। tathā iti sūtraṃ dṛśyate। virodhipratyakṣavat pratiyogighaṭapratyakṣatulyam। pratiyogino
abhāvapratyakṣamapi nāpalāpārhaṃ saṃnikarṣajanyaṃ cetyarthaḥ। abhāvapratyakṣe sahakārikāriṇadvayamapekṣitamiti vaśeṣaḥ। tadāha bhūtapratyakṣābhāvāt bhūtasmṛteriti। bhūtasya utpadya vinaṣṭasya ghaṭādeḥ pratiyoginaḥ upalabdhyabhāvāt smaraṇāccetyarthaḥ। evaṃ cābhāvapratyakṣasya
viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇabhāvātmakaṃ saṃnikarṣamapi samasūcayat। tathā ca vaiśeṣikatantrasūcita iti niścinumahe। praśastapādabhāṣye saṃnikarṣāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ। abhāvapadārthamadhikṛtya praśastapādabhāṣye yato vidyate। kandalīkārāstu ṣaḍvidhamapi saṃnikarṣaṃ sodāharaṇaṃ
pradarśayāmāsa। prādarśayan। sūtrādayaṃ vibhāgaḥ kathaṃ labhya iti śaṅkāyām saṃbhāvitāḥ saṃnikarṣā grahītavyā iti sūcitamiti samāhitam। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ proktaḥ। sa ca
prati ca heturiti prasādhitam। tatra ṭīkāyām dṛśyate। bhūtalādiviśeṣyakābhāvapratyakṣaṃ prati saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇatvaṃ saṃnikarṣaṃḥ। akāre anudāttasvaro saṃnikarṣa iti। nyāyasāre tu
ityabhihitam। samavetaviśeṣaṇatvam, samavetasamavetaviśeṣaṇatvam ceti tadāśayaḥ। sayuktikaṃ pratyapādi। tadvistaro bālapriyāyāṃ draṣṭavyaḥ। alaukikasaṃnikarṣastu prācīnagrantheṣu na dṛśyate। maṇikāraistatra tatra
vyavahṛtaḥ muktāvalīkārādibhiḥ prapañcitaḥ। anumānakhaṇḍe maṇau sāmānyalakṣaṇā pratyāsattiḥ paraṃ vistareṇa sthāpitetyāstāmiyatā। pramāṇāntaram। adhikaraṇajñānārthamapekṣitasyendriyasyaiva karaṇatvopapattau anupalabdheḥ karaṇatvāyogāditi dīpikākārāḥ।
etattattvamidānīṃ vicārya nirdhāryate। iti sūtreṇa catvāryeva pramāṇānītyetanna saṃgacchate। aitihyam trayāṇāmanumāne antarbhāvāt catvāryeva pramāṇānīti siddhāntitam। viṣaye nyāyasūtrataḥ kimapi nāvagamyate। nyāyabhāṣyakāraḥ
vāyvabhrasaṃyogasya pratipādakama। iti abhāṣata। toyapātarūpavṛṣṭyabhāvaḥ vāyumeghasaṃyogasya। ataḥ abhāvenāpyarthāntarapramityutpattyā abhāvo api pramāṇamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ।
siddhāntastu - satyamabhāvaḥ pramāṇam, na tvatiriktaṃ pramāṇam। abhāvasya liṅgavidhayā arthāntarapramitijanakatvenānumāne antarbhāvāt iti। vārtikatātparyaṭīkayorapyevamevopapāditam। paraṃ tveteṣu atupalabdhyākhyaṃ pramāṇaṃ tasya prastāva eva nāsti।
bhāṣyavārtikādito asyāśayasya sūcakaṃ kimapi nopalabhyate। abhāvapramāṇamadhikṛtya viśiṣya na kiñcidabhyadhāt। tathāpi aasaditi sūcitavāt। kandalīkāraḥ aghaṭaṃ bhūtalamiti ।
pramāṇāntaramanveṣṭavyamiti pratyapādayat। ityabhāṣanta। abhūtale indriyāsaṃnikṛṣṭaḥ tasya bodhakaṃ pramāṇam abhāva ityucyate। abhāvo nāma pramāṇābhāvaḥ, pratyakṣādipramāṇapañcakābhāva ityarthaḥ।
ayamevānupalabdhipadena paścātkālikairvyavahriyate। anupalabdheḥ pratyakṣānumānayorantarbhāvaṃ sādhayanti sma। tathā hi - kadāciccājñāyamānā। tatra jñātānupalabdheḥ anumāne, ajñātānupalabdheḥ pratyakṣe antarbhāvaḥ। jñātakāraṇasya parokṣajñānajanakatāyāḥ ajñātakāraṇasya
pratyakṣajñānajanakatāyāśca liṅgendriyādau darśanāt। nopalabdhaḥ' iti। asmācca mandire caitrasya yogyānupalabdhiṃ jñātvā nāsīt' iti। atra janayatīti। evameva prātaḥkālikābhāvapratītirapi vyākhyātavyā। tathā
nāsīditi। atra svayameva svakīyānupalabdhiṃ kālāntare jñātvā abhāvamanuminoti। tasmātprātaḥkālikasyābhāvasya pratītirmadhyāhne jñāyamānā jñātānupalabdhijanyatvādanumitirūpeti। tu jñānaṃ pratyakṣam। tatra catvāro hetava upanyastāḥ
apratipatterapārokṣyādindriyasyānupakṣayāt। bhāvāveśācca cetasaḥ।।' iti। manassahakāribhāvabhūtakaraṇasāpekṣatvācceti uktaślokasyārthaḥ। ete ca draṣṭavyāḥ।
yogyānupalabdhiriti vyavahriyate sma। pratyakṣatā। yogyādhikaraṇaviśeṣyakatvaniveśāt jalaparamāṇau pṛthivītvābhāvasya na pratyakṣatā। maṇikārāstu yogyā pariṣkāraṃ cakruḥ। dīpikādau
maṇikṛnmatānusāreṇaiva nirvacanaṃ kṛtam। prācīnamate api na kācidastyanupapattiriti dinakarīvyākhyāyāṃ rāmarudryāṃ spaṣṭam। pradarśayāmāsuḥ। tatra siddhāntavyāptiḥ। iyameva dīpikāyāṃ prakāśikāyāṃ ca anūditā।
taddhaṭakadalānāṃ prayojanāni ca vivecitāni। vyāpteriṣṭatvāt tatra kathaṃ samanvayaḥ। tathāhi - adhodeśe sūryasyodayo anumīyate, samudrasya vṛddhyā candrasyodayanumīyate। ūrdhvabhāgasthadhūmenādhobhāgasthavahniścānumīyate। etādṛśasthaleṣu
lakṣaṇāvyāptiḥ iti। sāmānādhikaraṇyasyopapattiḥ। deśataḥ vyadhikaraṇeṃṣūktasthaleṣu kālataḥ sādhyahetutāvacchedakatvaṃ svīkṛtya vyāptiḥ saṃpādanīyeti। jātiviśiṣṭavyaktāveva śaktiriti sthāpitam। etattattvaṃ
prācyanavyagranthavivecanapūrvakaṃ spaṣṭīkriyate। nyāyasūtrakārādyāśayaḥ cintyate। gavādiprātipadikasyārthaḥ kaḥ? kiṃ sandehaḥ। saṃdehasya kāraṇaṃ tu avinābhāvena vartamānāsu vyaktyākṛtijātiṣu gauriti śabdaḥ prayujyate। tatra na jñāyate kiṃ
tāsāmanyatamaḥ śabdārthaḥ? atha vā tāḥ tisro apīti। tatra vyaktivādī āhaśabdaprayogasāmarthyāddhi padārtho niścetavyaḥ। śabdaprayogaśyaśca vyaktimuddiśyaiva bhavati। tathā hi ayā gaustiṣṭhati' ayā gaurniṣṇā' iti gośabdārthasya sthityādīni viśeṣaṇāni dīyante। jāteḥ
vyāvartanīyāntarābhāvāt। vyakteḥ padārthatve tu yā govyaktirna tiṣṭhati tadvyāvartanārthaṃ tiṣṭhatīti viśeṣaṇaṃ saṃgacchate। evaṃ gauḥ vṛddhidānādikriyāsaṃbandhaḥ vyaktereva bhavati na jāteḥ। gauḥ śuklā kapiletyādau śuklādiguṇasaṃbandhaḥ vyakterevopapadyate। evaṃ
jāteḥ padārthatve viṃśatirgāva ityādivākyārthabodho anupapannaḥ। evaṃ gosukhamityādisamāse sukhādyanvayo govyaktereva śliṣyate। gairṅgāṃ janayatītyādau janmānvayaḥ govyakterna gotvajāteḥ। tasmāt vyaktireva padārtha iti।
na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ। ayaṃ gauḥ ayamaśva iti prāṇināṃ yā vyavasthā sā avayavasaṃyogarūpākṛtimapekṣya hi bhavati। tasmāt ākṛtiḥ padārtha iti। vyaktiḥ nāpyākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ। tāsāmānantyena tatra śaktigrahāsaṃbhavāt।
agāmānaya' ityādivākyoktaprokṣaṇānayanādikaṃ na kriyate। vyaktivāde ākṛtivāde ca tatrāpi tatprasaṅgaḥ। jāteḥ padārthatve tu mṛdgavake gotvajātyabhāvāt na prokṣaṇādikamiti। bhavitumarhantītyākṣepo vartate। ataḥ kaḥ padārtha iti
padārthaḥ' iti। asyaivaṃ vyākhyānam triṣvekā śaktiriti sūcanāyapadārtha ityekavacanam। kadācit vyakteḥ padārthatvamiti viśeṣasūcanāya tuśabdaḥ। yadā bhedavivakṣā padārthaḥ aṅge jātyākṛtī। yadā tu bhedo avivakṣitaḥ
spraṣṭavyetyādau। piṣṭakamayyo gāvaḥ kriyantāmityādau ākṛtiḥ padārtha iti। śaṅkā jāyate। atroktaṃ tātparyaṭīkāyām - gośabdaśravaṇānantaraṃ tīraṃ vāhīko vāvagamyate tathehāvagatiḥ। api tu
yugapadevāvagatiḥ। ato avagatirūpeṇa kāryeṇa kalpanīyā trayāṇāmekakāle avagatyāviśeṣāditi।iyaṃ prācīnanyāyagrantharītiḥ। jātyākṛtiviśiṣṭavyaktau ghaṭādipadānāṃ śaktiḥ। ātmādāvākṛtyabhāvāt jātiviśiṣṭavyaktau śaktiḥ।
ākāśādipadānāmupādhiviśiṣṭe śaktiḥ, ākāśajātyabhāvāt। tatrāpi ghaṭatvādeḥ śakyatve sati śakyatāvacchedakatvamapyaṅgīkriyate। vācyamiti gauravāt ityāhuḥ। jātiviśiṣṭavyaktāveva gavādipadānāṃ śaktiḥ। saṃsthāne ca pṛthageva
śaktirityāhuḥ। paraṃ tvasmin pakṣe sūtrasthamekavacanamasvarasaṃ bhavati। prathamopasthitatvājjātāveva śaktirityuktam, tadviparītam। āśrayapratītimantarā jātiguṇayorevāpratīteḥ। vyaktirhi prathamato jñāyate। tato vyaktigatavyañjakākṛtiviśeṣadarśanānantaraṃ
pratītirityanubhavasiddham। kiṃ ca saṃyuktasamavetaviṣayakacākṣuṣaṃ prati cakṣussaṃyuktasamavāyaḥ kāraṇam। śakyam। viśeṣaṇajñānapūrvakamāstheyam। viśeṣaṇajñānaṃ ca na
viśiṣṭārthaviṣayakam, anavasthāprasaṅgāt। ato jātimātraviṣayakaṃ vaktavyamiti cet satyaṃ viśiṣṭajñānaṃ viśeṣaṇajñānajanyamiti। tadeva ca viśeṣaṇajñānaṃ na jātimātraviṣayakam। jātiviṣayakatvavat tadāśrayavyaktiviṣayakatvasyāpi durvāratvāt। na
viśeṣaṇajñānāntarasyānapekṣaṇāt। ato viśeṣaṇajñānakāraṇatvabalāt jāteḥ prathamopasthitatvaṃ bhavediti pratyāśā na kāryā। śaktirityanupapannam। vyaktiparaprayogasyaiva bāhulyena bahutra vyaklikṣaṇāyāḥ kalpanīyatayā gauravāt। tadapekṣayā viśiṣṭavyaktau
yuktatvāt। avrīhibhiryajeta' ityādividhivākyeṣu sarvatra iti nyāyavirodhaśca syāt। paśyāmaḥ। vyaktivācakatvamupajīvya pravṛtteṣu sarūpādisūtreṣu gamyate। acādayo asattve' ityādiparyudāsācca
dravyavācitvaṃ gamyate। sādṛśyapratītimupajīvya pravartamānamupamānaṃ ca na vyaktivācakatāmantareṇa ghaṭate। agosadṛśo gavayaḥ' gavayapadavācya iti śaktigrahaḥ। liṅgaviśeṣanirṇayapuraskāreṇa pravṛttaḥ kośo api tadyogyavyaktivācakatvameva kalpayati। āptavākyaṃ ca
pravṛttinivṛttyanvayipadārthagocaraṃ vyaktiśaktiṃ vyanakti। vyavahāro api gavānayanapravṛttyādirvyaktivācakatva evopapadyate। vākyaśeṣāṃ'pi modamānatvādiviśeṣaṇārhavyaktivācakatāmeva draḍhayati। vivaraṇamapi pākaṃ karotītyādi kriyādivyaktivācakatāpakṣasvarasam।
ityādikaṃ dravyavācakatva eva saṃgatam। ato gavādiśabdānāṃ jātiśaktatve na kimapi pramāṇaṃ svārasikam। bādhakāni ca bhūyāṃsi liṅgasaṃṅkhyānanvayādīni pūrvamevāpapāditāni। gauvaryaktiniṣṭhetyapi prayogaḥ prasajyate। gavādipadānāṃ
jātimātravivakṣayā prayoge tvatalādyapekṣā ca na syāt। kiṃ ca khaṇḍo gauḥ śuklo gauḥ ityādisāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ na ghaṭate। khaṇḍatvāderjātāvananvayāt। yattvatrocyate mīmāṃsakaiḥ lakṣyārthavyaktau tadanvaya iti। kutrāpi vākye
lakṣyārthānvayiviśeṣaṇāprayogāt। na hi gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityādau prayujyate। pratyuta gabhīrāyāṃ nadyāṃ ghoṣa ityādau śakyārthanvayyeva viśeṣaṇaṃ prayujyate। tasmā jjātiviśiṣṭavyaktau padānāṃ śaktirityeva yuktam iti naiyāyikāḥ।
prāmāṇyavādaprakaraṇe। etattattvaṃ prācyanavyagranthavimarśapūrvakamadhunā vivriyate। jñānagataprāmāṇyajñānamapi pravṛttiheturiti vaktavyam। na cedaṃ jñānaṃ prāmāṇyajñānasya pravṛttihetutvaṃ nāstīti vācyam।
asaṃbhavāt। na ca tatrāpyāvaśyakārthaniśyādeva pravṛttiriti vācyam। tanniścayastaddheturityavaśyaṃ svīkaraṇīyam। yathā vyāptisaṃśaye vā jāyata iti pravṛttiṃ prati prāmāṇyaniścayaḥ kāraṇamiti sidhyati। tathā ca jñānapramātyaniścayaṃ vinā pravṛttyasaṃbhava iti। na ca jñāne
prāmāṇyasvatastvaparatastvavicāro anavasara iti vācyam। yatra idamitthamevetyavadhāraṇādeva saṃpādanīyā। taccāvadhāraṇaṃ jñānasya prayojakatvāt prāmāṇyaniścayo api saṃpādanīyaḥ। sa ca svataḥ parato veti vicāro yukta eva।
svatastvaṃ paratastvaṃ ca maṇau pañcadhā niruktam। tatra prathamaniruktimātraṃ dīpikāyāmanūditam। jñānaṃ yayā sāmagyā jñāyate tayaiva jñānagataṃ svatastvam। tatraprābhākarāḥ - ghaṭamahaṃ jānāmītyeva jñānākāraḥ। tasya prāmāṇyasyeti vadanti।
jñānagrāhakasāmagrījanyagrahaḥ tadviṣayatvaṃ prāmāṇyasyetyācakṣate।murārimiśrāḥ aayaṃ ghaṭaḥ' iti jñānānantaraṃ aghaṭamahaṃ jñānāmi' ityanuvyavasāyo jāyate। tena jñāne viṣayīkriyamāṇe tadgataṃ pramātvamapi viṣayīkriyate। tathā ca svatastvamityupavarṇayanti। matatraye api
sādhāraṇam। atra sāmagrīviśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। evamapi idaṃ jñānamaprameti jñānaniṣṭhasya tadvāraṇāya tadaprāmāṇyāgrāhaketi vaktavyam। tasmin aprāmāṇgrāhaketi tadarthaṃḥ। yādṛśaprāmāṇye svatastvamiṣyate
tādṛśaprāmāṇyāśrayaviśeṣyakāprāmāṇyaprakārakajñānajanaketi yāvat। idaṃ jñānamapremetyākārakajñānaniṣṭhaprāmāṇyagrāhakasāmagryāḥ। tadviśeṣyakāprāmāṇyajñānājanakatvānna doṣaḥ। naiyāyikairapi deyam। tacca sāmāgryāṃ na viśeṣaṇam। sarvābhirjñānasāmagrībhirekasya
jñānasyājananena yāvatsāmagrījanyagrahāprasiddhaṃḥ। api tu jñānaviśeṣaṇam। tathā ca jñānagrāhakasāmagrījanyayāvadgrahaviṣayatvamiti phalitam। naiyāyikairanaṅgīkārānna doṣaḥ। yāvattvasya ca vyāpakatvarūpatvāt
svatastvamiti dīdhitikārairniṣkarṣaḥ kṛtaḥ। sa niṣkarṣaḥ prakāśikāyāmanūditaḥ। tīrthakarā vipratipadyante। tatra prāmāṇyamaprāmāṇyaṃ cetyubhayaṃ svata iti sāṃkhyāḥ। ubhayaṃ parata iti vaiśeṣikādayaḥ। aprāmāṇyaṃ parata
iti bauddhāḥ। prāmāṇyaṃ svataḥ aprāmāṇyaṃ parata iti mīmāṃsakāḥ vedāntinaśceti catvāraḥ pakṣāḥ। prāmāṇyamaprāmāṇyaṃ cetyubhayamapi svābhāvikamiti। asvārasyamasmin mate asti।
prāmāṇyaṃ parata iti manyante bauddhāḥ। tathā hi yadi prāmāṇyaṃ jñānaṃ pramā apramā veti saṃśayo na syāt। ataḥ kāraṇabhūtasya guṇasaya jñānāt pravṛttisaṃvādācca prāmāṇyaṃ niścīyate। mānatvaṃ viniścetuṃ na śakyate।
kevalaṃ tat pratīyate।।' iti। aprāmāṇyaṃ tu svata evāvasīyate। ata eva vedādutpannaṃ jñānaṃ viparyayarūpam। ataḥ svato apramāṇaṃ vedāḥ iti bauddhānāmākūtam।
idamatra dūṣaṇam। prāmāṇyasya svābhāvikatvaṃ vaktavyam। anyathā niradhiṣṭhānabhramaprasaṅgāt। kiṃ ca apramāṇāt prameyasiddhiḥ' svataḥ pramāṇamiti vaktavyam। tathā nirvikalpakasya
vāsanopaplavaśūnyasya svata eva prāmāṇyamupagacchanti। savikalpakasyāpi svāṃśe prāmāṇyaṃ viṣayāṃśe aprāmāṇyaṃ ca vadanti। tathā ca kutracit prāmāṇyasvatastvaṃ teṣāmapyavarjanīyam। api ca sarveṣvapi jñāneṣu vyavasthāpanāt iti mīmāṃsakāḥ। naiyāyikāstu doṣataḥ aprāmāṇyaṃ
guṇataḥ prāmāṇyamityāhuḥ। sarvathā aprāmāṇyasvatastvaṃ na ghaṭate। mīmāṃsakamatam। evotpadyate jñāyate ca। aprāmāṇyaṃ tu parata utpadyate jñāyate ceti mīmāṃsakāḥ। prāmāṇyaṃ svata utpadyata ityasya prāmāṇyāśrayajñānasya yā
guṇādityarthaḥ। tena ca vedādutpannasya jñānasya yat prāmāṇyaṃ tatra bhavatīti teṣāmāśayaḥ। prāmāṇyaṃ svato jñāyata ityasya tadgataprāmāṇyasyāpi jñānaṃ bhavati। paścāttu bādhakajñānakāraṇadoṣajñānābhyāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ bādhyate। evaṃ ca apauruṣeye
jñātaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ tathaivāvatiṣṭhate। tathā ca vedaprāmāṇyasthirīkaraṇameva jñaptau svatastvasādhanasya prayojanamiti। ) iti sūtreṇa parataḥ prāmāṇyaṃ sūcitameva। nyāyabhāṣyakāraḥ apramāṇator'thapratipattau pravṛttisāmarthyādarthavatpramāṇam' iti।
jvaraharatakṣakacūḍāratnāharaṇopadeśakaṃ śāstram। idaṃ nyāyaśāstramapi tādṛśameva। tathā hi, ṣoḍaśapadārthatvajñānāddhi niḥśreyasayupadiśyate asmin śāstre। prameyādīnāṃ padārthānāṃ tattvajñānaṃ pramāṇatattvajñānāndhīnam। na hi pramāṇaṃ
tattvenānirṇītaṃ san svaviṣayaṃ avadhārayitumalam। pramāṇatattvāvadhāraṇaṃ ca pramātattvāvadhāraṇādhīnam। na hi pramāṃ tattvenānavadhārayan pramājanakasya tattvamavadhārayituṃ śaknoti। niścetumaśakyam। ghaṭādiviṣayagocaraṃ jñānamātmānamapi
svataḥ pakṣaḥ tāvanna yuktaḥ। jñānaṃ svayaṃprakāśam iti pakṣe api svagatāvyabhicāritvarūpapramātvaviṣayakatvaṃ durūpapādam। parataḥ śakyeta। atasteṣāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ jñānāntarebhyaścet teṣāmapi tathetyanavasthā। teṣāṃ pramātvaṃ svata iti tu
pūrvoktarītyānupapannam। tathā ca svataḥ parato vā pramātattvānavadhāraṇāt pramāṇatattvāvadhāraṇaṃ na sambhavati। tadasaṃbhavācca prameyāditattvajñānamapi na saṃbhavati। tasmāt ityādibhāṣyaṃ pravṛttamiti।
prāmāṇamarthavaditi pratijñā। pravṛttisāmarthyāditi hetuḥ। pramāṇamiti karaṇārthakalyuḍantaḥ śabdaḥ। arthavaditi nityayoge matup। nityatā cārthāvyabhicāritā। arthāvyabhicāritvaṃ ca tadvati tatprakārakatvam। tacca pramāṇasya jñānadvārakam। tathā ca pramāṇaṃ tadvati
tatprakārakajñānajanakamiti pratijñārthaḥ। samapravṛttijanakatvamiti tadarthaḥ। yadi pramāṇamarthāvyabhicāri nābhaviṣyat samarthāṃ pravṛttiṃ vivakṣitam। pramāṇasya arthapratipattijananadvāreṇetyāśayena pramāṇator'thapratipattāvityuktam।
saphalapravṛttijanakatvādityanumāna eva paryaṃvasānam। itthaṃ ca bhāṣyakārāśayaḥ। anumityantareṇeti yadi, tadānavastheti cetna। svatogrāhyatvāṅgīkārāt। tarhi aghaṭamahaṃ jānāmi'
tātparyaṭīkākārāḥ nirūpayanti। upapādayanti। āptaprāmāṇyakṛtam। kiṃ punarāptānāṃ guṇajanyatvākhyaṃ paratastvaṃ sūcitameva। kusumāñjalau jñaptau utpattau
vistareṇopapāditam। tadapekṣayāpi vistareṇa maṇau dodhitau gādādharīye ca vivecitam। dīpikāyāṃ prakāśikāyāṃ ca tatratyamevopapādanaṃ punaḥ saṃgṛhītamiti। khyātiriti vyapadeśaḥ śāstragrantheṣu vartate। tatra viṣaye vādino
bahudhā vadanti। loke yasya yasya yadyat jñānaṃ bhavati tatsarvaṃ prameti vaktuṃ na śakyate। tathā sati prativādino jñānamapi pramā syāt। tathā ca prativādyapi vijayeta। tathāsarvaṃ jñānamaprametyapi vaktuṃ na pāryate। tathā sati vādino yat jñānaṃ tadapyapramā syāt।
parājito bhavet। tasmāt kiñcit jñānaṃ pramā kiñcit jñānamapramā iti vibhāgaḥ sarvairabhyupagantavyaḥ। tatra apramātmake jñāne anyasya urarīkurvanti। anyathākhyāteḥ yā sāmagrī bhedājñānarūpa akhyātiḥ tathaiva vyavahāropapatteḥ akhyātipakṣa eva yukta iti prābhākarāḥ।
ityātmakhyātivādinaḥ। bhramasthale asadeva pratīyata iti asatkhyātivādinaḥ mādhyamikāḥ। bhrame sadasadanirvañcanīyaṃ vastūtpadyate pratīyate cetyadvaitinaḥ। etanmate anirvacanīyakhyātiḥ। anyathākhyātivādina iti prasiddhiḥ। nyāyadarśane prathamasūtreṇa
mithyājñānaṃ paramparayā saṃsāraheturiti pratipāditam। tatra atasmiṃstaditi jñānaṃ mithyājñānamiti manyate। vārttikakāro api akaḥ punarayaṃ viparyayaḥ। atasmiṃstaditi pratyayaḥ' iti kathayati। asya viparyasya anyathākhyātiriti saṃjñā tu paścātkālikīṃ।
iti। parīkṣakāṇāṃ vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ। kecit ityācakṣate। anye asadviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ vṛddhāḥ।'
anyathākhyātipakṣaḥ naiyāyikānāmiti jñāyate। samānam। tataḥ aidaṃ madhye viśiṣṭajñānamanāvaśyakamiti prābhākarāḥ iti। pravartakaṃ vācyam। tathā ca
ityanumānamanyathākhyātau pramāṇam। tathā anyathākhyātisādhakatayā maṇāvupanyastāni। evamanuvyavasāyātmakapratyakṣamapyanyathākhyātau mānam। tathā hi - śuktau ityanuvyavasāyo jāyate।
idaṃviśeṣyakarajatatvaprakārakajñānavāhanam iti hi tadarthaḥ। tatra iti। ākāreṇa purovartino viśiṣṭatājñānamanyathākhyātiḥ। anyatraiva sattvaṃ tu pravṛttivādhasahakṛtāt nāstīti bādhakapratyayānniścīyate। ato
praṃvṛttibādhavirahāt। na vā mantrādipratibaddhasyāgneḥ sphoṭajananādipravattibādhāt mithyātvaniścayaprasaṅgaḥ। tatra nāstīti bādhakapratyayasyābhāvāt। anyathākhyātiravaśyāśrayaṇīyā। tathā hiasatkhyātimate kimasat
asaditi pratīyate saditi vā? asaditi cet bhramatvāsaṃbhavaḥ। asataḥ asattvena bhānasya pramātvāt bādhapravṛttī ca na ghaṭetām। saditi pratīyate cet, asataḥ sattvena bhānāt anyathākhyātireva syāt। iti? ādyena bhramatvabādhapravṛttīnāmasaṃbhavaḥ। dvitīye jñānasyārthātmanā
bhānādanyathākhyātireva svīkṛtā syāt। jñānadvayamiti pratīyate kiṃ vā ekatvena? ādye bādhapravṛttyorasaṃbhavaḥ। dvitīye dvayasyaikatvena bhānāt anyathākhyātiḥ। ādye pravṛttyādyasaṃbhavaḥ। na jātu kaścit avidyamānatvena pratīte vastuni
pravartate। dvitīye avidyamānasya vidyamānatvena bhānādanyathākhyātiḥ iti। prādarśiṣātām। idaṃ kiñcidvicāryate। iti।
vārtikepyevameva pratipādyate। tena prāgabhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsaśceti dvividha evābhāvo bhāṣyavārttikakārayoḥ saṃmata iti pratīyate। tatraiva prakṛtāpekṣam। prakṛtaṃ pradhvaṃsamātra- prāgabhāvapratipādanam। paramārthatastu
bhāvaśceti। ityabhāvacatuṣṭayamapi nyāyadarśanasaṃmatamiti pratyapādayat। bhāvavadabhāvo api pramāṇavedyaḥ। yat pramāṇaṃ bhāvaṃ jñāpayati tadeva pramāṇenopalabdhiḥ।
tadvadanupalabdheḥ pradīpavat। pramāṇamasadapi prakāśayati।' prathamasūtre abhāṣi। tatrābhāvasyāpi pramāṇasiddhatve tasya bhāvavat pramāṇasyālambanaṃ svatantraṃ bhavati।
pratiṣedhamukhena pratipadyate।' iti tadāśayaḥ। abhāvacatuṣṭayābhyupagamaḥ sūcito vartate। prāgabhāvamanumanyate। utpatteḥ prāgavidyamānatā hi prāgabhāvo nāma।
mudgarapātādyanantaramabhāvaṃ pratipādayat dhvaṃsākhyamabhāvaṃ sūcayati। tādātmyābhāvarūpamanyonyābhāvaṃ vyañjayati। tataḥ ayaccānyadasadatastadasat' iti sūtram। tatra asacchabdadvayaṃ bhāvavapradhāno nirdeṃśaḥ। yat ataḥ asataḥ anyat asat
tat asat ityanvayaḥ। pūrvoktābhāvatrayāt anyo yo abhāvaḥ so atyantābhāve iti। evaṃ sthite abhāvasya pṛthaganupadeśaḥ bhāvapāratantryāt na tvabhāvāditi sidhyati। bhidyante paramārthataḥ।
vastvantaropādhiranyonyābhāva ucyate।। evāvadhiśūnyatvādatyantābhāvatāṃ gataḥ। tadanutpāda eva vā। bhedāstvaupādhikā matāḥ।।'
prāgabhāvapradhvaṃsabhedenābhāvo dvividhaḥ। anyonyātyantābhāvau prāgabhāva evāntarbhavataḥ। prāgabhāva eva vastvantarapratiyogikaścet anyonyābhāva ityucyate। sa evāvadhiśūnyaścet atyantābhāva iti kathyate iti nyarūpayan।
atiriktamabhāvaṃ nāṅgīkurvanti। abhāvaḥ buddhiviśeṣasvarūpaḥ, adhikaraṇasvarūpaḥ kālaviśeṣasvarūpaḥ iti pakṣatrayaṃ pradarśayanti। ca। dīpikāyāṃ tvadhikaraṇātmakatvapakṣaḥ anūdya dūṣita iti viśeṣaḥ। atra vicāryate।
api svīkurvanti। tatra ityādhārādheyabhāvaḥ pratīyate। sa cādhārādheyayorabhede api ādhāratāvacchedakayorghaṭābhāvatvapaṭābhāvatvayorbhedānniruhyate। tathā nirūḍhā bhaviṣyati। ataḥ adhikaraṇātmakatvamevābhāvasyāstu।
bhaviṣyati। yathā rasābhāvatvenetyaṅgīkriyate, tadvat। tathā ca śabdādyabhāvānāṃ pratyakṣatvānupapattirapi nāsti। jñānaviśeṣakālaviśeṣayoḥ pratyakṣatā saṃbhavatyeva।
ato abhāvasyānatiriktatve api na ko api doṣa iti। atra samādhīyate। prāyaśo loke bhinnayorevādhārādheyabhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ। sa cābhāvātiriktatvavādinaiyāyikamate sūpapādaḥ।
gatyantarasattve tathā nirvāhasyānucitatvāt। ato adhikaraṇātmakatvapakṣo na yuktaḥ। duruddharaḥ। tatra yaduktaṃ jñānatvena kālatvena ca rūpeṇa tatrocyate। rūpāntareṇāpi tayoḥ tādṛśapratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ na saṃbhavati।
kāraṇatvāsaṃbhavāt। na dvitīyaḥ, ekasmin abhāvajñāne bhūyasīnāṃ puruṣāntarīyajñānavyaktīnāṃ viṣayatvakalpane gauravāt। evaṃ tādṛśajñānotpattikṣaṇātmakakālasya pūrvapṛttitvābhāvāt। pūrvakṣaṇātmakakālasya ca tatkāle abhāvāt। na ca
vācyam। tathāpi tādṛśakṣaṇadvayāvasthāyinānāpadārtharūpasthūlakālasya muktāvalīmañjūṣākārāḥ। nirūpitam। etattatvaṃ kiñcidvicāryate। śabdajanyaṃ jñānam। śabdo nāma
parasparānvitārthaṃpratipādakapadasamūhātmakaṃ vākyam। padasamūho ananvitārthakapadasamūhasyāpi vākyatvaṃ syāt। ataḥ parasparānvitārthaketyuktam। gaurgacchati, aśvodhāvati ityanayoḥ dvayorvākyārthayoḥ parasparamananvayāt। tasmāt sākṣādvā paraṃparayā
viśeṣyabhūtārthapratipādakaṃ padamekavākyamiti paryaṃvasyati। idameva pūrvamīmāṃsāsūtre [] uktam। ekasminnarthe anyeṣāṃ ityuktam। kimavāntaraviśeṣyam? kiṃ mukhyaviśeṣyamiti vicāraṇīyaṃ bhavati।
panthānamāśrayante। ityanubhavāt kriyāpade prāyaḥ subantānāmanvaya iti pratīyate। nīlatvaviśiṣṭotpalakarmakamānayanamiti bodho bhavati। nīlatvaviśiṣṭotpalakarmakamānayanamityeva bodhaḥ। evaṃ ca
prathamāntārthasya kartṛkārakasyāpi tathaivānvaya ucitaḥ, samānanyāyāt। prakṛtyarthasya nīlatvaviśiṣṭotpalasyābhedasaṃbandhenānvayaḥ। karmaṃṇaḥ dhātvarthe anvayaḥ। tatrābhedasaṃbandhena prathamāntapadārthasya devadattasyānvayaḥ। kartuṃrapi dhātvarthe
ānayana'nvayaḥ। tathā ca cānayanamiti dhātvarthamukhyaviśeṣyako bodhaḥ। atra pramāṇaṃ tu iti mahābhāṣyavacanaṃ cetyāhuḥ। tiṅarthabhāvanāmukhyaviśeṣyakaṃ bodhaṃ varṇayanti। tathā hi
nirākāṅkṣaṃ bodhaṃ na janayantītyanubhavasiddham। tena tiṅantapadaṃ viśeṣyasamarpakamiti labhyate। tatrāpi aprakṛtipratyayau pratyayārthaṃ saha kṛtireva śābdabodhe mukhyaviśeṣyabhūtā। aevaṃ ca caitrastaṇḍulaṃ karmatvamarthaḥ। tatra taṇḍulasya ādheyatāsambandhenānvayaḥ। karmatvasya
tiṅarthakakṛtāvanvayaḥ। dhātvarthasya pākasya svakaraṇakaudanoddeśyakatvasambandhena kṛtāvanvayaḥ। caitrapadottaraprathamāyāḥ prātipadikārthaḥ caitro athaḥ। caitrapadaṃ tātparyagrāhakam। prathamārthasya caitrasya ādheyatāsaṃbandhena
bhāvanāyāmanvayaḥ। ākhyātārthakālasaṃkhyayo api bhāvanāyāmevānvayaḥ। ādheyatāsaṃbandhenānvaya iti viśeṣa। evaṃ ca caitraniṣṭhā bodhaḥ। abhāvapradhānamākhyātam' iti nirukte ākhyātaśabdaḥ tiṅparaḥ। bhāvaśabdaḥ bhāvanāvācī। tiṅśca saṃkhyā kālaḥ bhāvanā iti
trayor'thāḥ। teṣu bhāvanā pradhānabhūtā iti nirūpayanti। iti vākyam paṇḍitābhinnaścaitra iti bodho anubhūyate। tatra mukhyaviśeṣyatayā bhānaṃ na saṃbhavati। tathā ca kvacit
niṅntasamabhivyāhārasthalepi tathaiva bodhavarṇanaṃ yuktam। na ca tatrāpi yogyakriyādhyāhāreṇaiva śābdabodha iti vācyam। anadhyāhāreṇaiva nirvāhe adhyāhārasyāyuktatvāt। api ca iti vadantaḥ kauṇḍabhaṭṭāḥ tiṅantaśūnyamapi vākyamabhyupagacchanti।
bhūṣaṇasāre api tiṅantarahitavākyaprāmāṇyāṅgīkāraḥ pratīyate। evaṃ svīkāryatvāt caitraḥ pacatītyādāvapi tathaiva bodhavarṇanaṃ yuktam। taṇḍulapadottaradvitīyāyāḥ karmatvamarthaḥ। karmatve prakṛtyarthasya taṇḍulasyādheyatāsaṃbandhenānvayaḥ। karmatvasya nirūpakatāsambandhena
dhātvarthe pāke anvayaḥ। tatrānukūlatāsaṃbandhena dhātvarthapākasyānvayaḥ। kṛteśca āśrayatāsaṃbandhena prathamāntārthecaitre anvayaḥ। ākhyātārthasya vartamānakālasya kṛtāvevānvayaḥ। ākhyātaikavacanasya tu naikatvasaṃkhyā arthaḥ।
subekavacanenaiva ekatvalābhāt। tathā ca ekatvāśrayaścaitra ityanvayabodhaḥ। pūrvavākyārthe yaḥ pradhānaḥ tasyaiva tacchabdena parāmarśo vaktavyaḥ। ityatrānupapattiḥ। puruṣaḥ prayāti iti vākye pradhānasya gamanasya
pādayorabhivādayetyanenānvayasyāsaṃgateḥ। naiyāyikamate tu pādayorabhivādayetyanenānvayaḥ sādhuḥ saṃgataḥ। prayujyate। pratyakṣeṇa ca kārakāṇāṃ kriyānvaya evāvagamyate, na tu kṛtyaparaparyāyabhāvanānvayaḥ। ato mīmāṃsakamataṃ nocitam। nāpi
vaiyākaraṇamatam। pratyakṣe dharmasya prakāratāyāḥ dharmiṇo prathamāntārthaṃsyaiva viśeṣyatvaucityāt। tatrāpi devadattāderviśeṣyatvamucitam। sakalakarmādikārakaprerakasya hi ānubhavikam।
nānumanyate। tena ca prathamāntārthasya kriyāyāmanvayaḥ tasyā nānumata iti spaṣṭam। kriyāpradhānakatvanirbandhaḥ। tasmāt prathamāntārthaviśeṣyakabodha evāsati bādhake ucitaḥ। sati tu bādhake bhāvākhyātasthale caitreṇa
naiyāyikasiddhāntasāraḥ। AnTsb nidhāya hṛdi viśveśaṃ vidhāya guruvandanam । AnTsd bālānāṃ sukhabodhāya kriyate tarkasaṃgrahaḥ ।। sāmbamūrtiṃ praṇipatya girāṃ gurum।
ṭīkāṃ śiśuhitāṃ kurve tarkasaṅgrahadīpikām।। nibadhnan cikīrṣitaṃ pratijānīte -nidhāyeti। nanu maṅgalasya samāptisādhanatvaṃ nāsti। anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vyabhicārāt iti cet - na।
samāptyabhāvaḥ। kādambaryādau granthādbahireva maṅgalaṃ kṛtam, ato na vyabhicāraḥ। kartavyatve kiṃ pramāṇamiti cet - na। śiṣṭācārānumitaśrutereva pramāṇatvāt। tathā hi - maṅgalaṃ vedabodhitakartavyatākam,
alaukikāvigītaśiṣṭācāraviṣayatvāt, darśādivat। bhojanādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya alaukiketi। rātriśrāddhādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya avigīteti। śiṣṭapadaṃ spaṣṭārtham।"na kuryāt niṣphalaṃ karma"iti jalatāḍavanāderapi niṣiddhatvāt। tarkyante - pratipādyante iti
kriyate ityarthaḥ। kasmai prayojanāya iti, ata āha sukhabodhāyeti। sukhena - anāyāsena yo bodhaḥ padārthatattvajñānaṃ tasmā ityarthaḥ। nanu bahuṣu tarkagrantheṣu satsu kimarthamapūrvo ayaṃ granthaḥ kriyata iti, ata āhabālānāmiti। teṣāmativistṛtatvāt bālānāṃ bodho na jāyata ityarthaḥ। grahaṇadhāraṇapaṭurbālaḥ na tu stanandhayaḥ। kiṃ kṛtvā kriyata
iti, ata āha nidhāyeti।veśveśam - jaganniyantāram।hṛdi nidhāya - nitarāṃ sthāpayitvā। sadā taddhyānaparo bhūtvā ityarthaḥ। gurūṇām - vidyā - gūrūṇām,
- kṛtvā ityarthaḥ।। dakṣiṇāmūrtimavyayam। vindedgurusamānatām।। śiṣyaśikṣāyai nibadhnan cikīrṣitaṃ pratijānīte viśveśvaramiti।girāṃ gurum -
nikhilavidyānāmupadeṣṭāram। idamapi viśveśvare viśeṣaṇam। ityartho bodhyaḥ। svagranthasya itaragranathairagatārthatāṃ darśayati - śiśuhitāmiti।tarkasaṅgrahadīpikām - tarkasaṅgrahārthaprakāśikām।
tannibandhanasya ca phalaṃ darśayati cikīrṣitasya ityādinā। maṅgalasya kāraṇatā syāt cet tadā tadācāraṇaṃ yujyate। saiva na sambhavatītyaśaṅkatenanviti। kāraṇatvaniścaya ityabhisandhiḥ।
ato na vyabhicāra ityanenānvayaḥ। vighnānyūnasaṅkhyākasya tādṛśamaṅgalābhāvāt nānvayavyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ। janmāntara evetyarthaḥ। ataḥ kutracit granthakarturnāstikatve api na kṣatiḥ। ityarthaḥ। evaṃ ca kāraṇatvaṃ siddhyatīti bhāvaḥ। pare tu'ataḥ- uktahetudvayātna
aiti vyācakhyuḥ।maṇikṛtastu amaṅgalasya vighnadhvaṃsa eva phalam। samāptistu svasāmagrīvaśādeva' ityāhuḥ। etattattvamasmadīyacintāmaṇivyākhyāyāmanusandheyam। vyavasthāpayituṃ śaṅkate nanvitati। tadantarbhāveṇa vidheyatvamabhyupagamyate। tacchruteḥ anumiteḥ
śrutāvanumitatvavyavahāraḥ kathamiti śaṅkā nirastā। śrutau vidheyatvābhyupagamena tādṛśavyavahāre bādhakābhāvāt। evakāro apyarthakaḥ। tena amaṅgalaṃ kartavyam samāptiphalakatvāt' ityanumānarūpapramāṇāntarasattve api na kṣatiḥ। anye tu
'svabodhitakartavyatākatvasambandhena śrutereva sādhyatā। agrimagranthasyātraiva tātparyam। evaṃ ca śruteranumitatvopapattiḥ' ityāhuḥ। alaukikevidhimantarā rāgādiprāptabhinnetyarthaḥ।
avigīteti dharmaśāstāviruddhetyarthaḥ।śiṣṭeti vedoktatattvajñānena vedavihitakarmakārītyarthaḥ। vedoktāhiṃsādikartari bauddhe ativyāptivāraṇāya tṛtīyāntam।ācāraḥ- kṛtiḥ। tasyāḥ tadviṣayatvasya hetutvānudhāvanam। yathākramaṃhetuviśeṣaṇaprayojanamāha bhojanādauityādinā।
alaukikāvigītācāraviṣayatvasyaiva hetutāstu। aśiṣṭācāraviṣaye pariharati śiṣṭapadamiti। jalatāḍanādau aśiṣṭācāraviṣaye kuryāditi। svargādiphale vyabhicāravāraṇāyaācāraviṣayatveti।
vidheyatayā ācāraviṣayatvārthakamiti saṅkṣepaḥ। nirvaktitarkyantaiti। saṅkṣepeṇeti।svarūpakathanamsvarūpajñānānukūlaśabdaḥ। etāvatā prekṣāvatpravṛttyaṅgaṃ sūcitam। ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣabhramavāraṇāyāhasukheneti। sukhabodharūpaprayojanasyānyataḥ siddhatvena etadgranthakaraṇe
prayojanākāṅkṣā na śāmyatītyāśayenāvatārayatinanviti।teṣāmbhāṣyādigranthānam।। nissamābhyadhikasadguṇākaraṃ bhaktarakṣaṇarataṃ dayānidhim। stutaṃ vandiṣīya vṛṣaśailanāyakam ।। vedāntalakṣmaṇamunīndrapadābjabhṛṅgam।
śrīmannṛsiṃhaguruvaryamahaṃ namāmi ।। bahuśiṣyayuktam। śrīdevanāthagurumanvahamānato asmi ।। sambhāvanādiparipanthinamātmavantam।
śrīkṛṣṇatātaguruvaryamahaṃ prapadye ।। prauḍhagambhīrasaṃkṣiptavacovinyāsabhāsurā। dīpikāyāḥ prakāśikā ।। paricayo dṛḍhaḥ।
taṃ samyagjñātumīśate ।। yathāmati। bālapriyāṃ vyākhyāṃ karomyaham ।। mamoddeśyaṃ matastataḥ।
anapekṣitavistāravicārāvatra nādṛtau ।। gurumiti। nanu padārthaviṣayakajñānajanakasaṅkṣiptaśabdātmakagranthaprakāśikāmityarthaḥ। yathāśrutalabhyaḥ। tatra śabdātmakadīpikāgranthasya
tarkasaṅgrahagranthārthasyaiva prakāśanāt ityato vyācaṣṭetarkasaṃṅgrahāthaprakāśikāmiti। yathā apavarake āropito dīpaḥ grantho api tarkasaṅgrahāntarnigūḍhānarthān prakāśayatīti bhāvaḥ। tathā tarkasaṃṅgrahagranthapratipādyārthapara iti tātparyam। prayojanamiti labhyate। tatra maṅgala-granthasamāptyoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvo
"nanu maṅgalasya"ityādinā dīpikāyām। tatra prakāśikāyāmanvayavyatireketyādinām। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ- kāraṇatāniścayaṃ prati kāraṇam। niyatānvayasahacāro nāma āraṇavyāpakakāryakatvam। niyatavyatirekasahacāro nāma āraṇābhāvavyāpakakāryābhāvakatvam।
kāraṇāvyāpakakāryakatvamiti yāvat। vyatirekavyabhicāro nāma yāvat। tatra niyatānvayasahacārajñānaṃ prati anvayavyabhicārajñānaṃ pratibandhakam। niyatavyatirekasahacārajñānaṃ prati vyatirekavyabhicārajñānaṃ pratibandhakam। prakṛte maṅgalarūpakāraṇe
।। dakṣiṇāmrtivyāsaśaṅkararūpiṇam। candraśekharendrasarasvatom।। kāraṇavyāpakakāryakatvamiti। yatra yatra cakrādisahakṛtadaṇḍarūpaṃ kāraṇaṃ
niyatānvayasahacāravāniti bhāvaḥ। kāraṇābhāvavyāpakakāryābhāvakatvamiti। yatra yatra ghaṭābhāvaḥ। tathā ca svābhāvavyāpakakāryābhāvakatvāt daṇḍaḥ niyatavyatirekasahacāravāniti bhāvaḥ।
svavyāpakasamāptikamityākārakaniyatānvayasahacāraniścayo na bhavati। nāsti, maṅgalābhāvavati amāpteḥ sattvāt। tathā ca maṅgalaṃ na bhavati। tathā ca niyatānvayavyatirekasahacāraniścayarūpasya samāptinirūpitakāraṇatvāvagāhī niścayo na bhavatīti।
iti granthaḥ prāvartata। tena tu granthenānvayavyabhicāra eva dṛḍhīkṛtaḥ, vighnānyūnasaṅkhyākasyeti। maṅgalaṃ hi na sākṣāt samāptikāraṇam, kiṃ tu vighnadhvaṃsadvārā। bhavati। tathā ca vighnānyūnasaṅkhyākaṃ balavattaraṃ vā maṅgalaṃ
samāptikāraṇam। kiraṇāvalyādau ca vighnānāṃ bahutvāt tādṛśaṃ maṅlaṃ nāstīti samāptirūpaṃ kāryaṃ nābhūt। ataḥ kāraṇe sati kāryābhāvātmakaḥ anvayavyabhicāro nāstīti bhāvaḥ। vighnānyunasaṅkhyākasyeti।
satvāditi। tathā ca maṅgalābhāvavati samāptyabhāvābhāvarūpasamāpteḥ maṅgalābhāvavyāpakatvaṃ samāptyabhāvasya nāstīti bhāvaḥ। vighnanāśakatvamiṣyate। -balavattarasya veti। nanu kādambaryādau nāstikakṛte
kṛtamato na vyabhicāraḥ' iti dīpikāgranthaḥ pravṛttaḥ। tena cabahireva granthārambhe maṅgalanibandhanamakṛtvā, maṅgalaṃ kṛtam, labhyate। sa tu na yuktaḥ; nāstikena kādambaryādigranthapraṇetrā vyācaṣṭe-bahireveti।janmāntaraṃ evetyarthaiti। tathā ca tādṛśagranthakartuḥ etajjnamani nāstikatve api samāptiḥ। ataḥ kāraṇābhāve api kāryarūpaḥ vyatirekavyabhicāro
durvaca ityāśayaḥ। nanu janmāntarīyamaṅgalasya tadānīmeva vighnadhvaṃsadvāreti।evaṃ ca kāraṇatvaṃ sidhyatīti। pūrvoktarītyā samāptikāraṇatvaniścayo bhavatītyarthaḥ। athavā evaṃ ca - amāptayavyavahitapūrvavūttitvarūpaṃ kāraṇatvaṃ sidhyatīti bhāvaḥ।
kathaṃ kāraṇatvamiti। kāryāvyavahitaprākkṣaṇavṛttitvasyaiva kāraṇatvapadārthatvāditi bhāvaḥ। samāptyavyavahitetyādi। tathā ca sākṣātsambandhena samavāyena samāpteḥ samāptyavyavahitapūrvakṣaṇavṛttitvamastīti bhāvaḥ।
maṅgalaṃ kṛtam' iti pūrvagranthoktahetudvayādityarthaḥ। svasyāḥ- samāpteḥ sāmagrī - buddhipratibhādikāraṇakalāpāḥ tadvaśāt-tadadhīnatayetyarthaḥ। satyapi buddhipratibhādikameva samāptiṃ prati kāraṇam। maṅgalaṃ tu samāptipratibandhakavighnotsāraṇe kāraṇam iti maṇikārāśayaḥ।
jñānamantarā maṅgalaṃ na ko api kuryāt। adviṣayakakṛtiṃ prati tadviśeṣyakakṛtisādhyatājñānasya kāraṇatvāt। kartavyatvaṃ ca kṛtisādhyatvam। maṅgalaṃ kartavyamiti jñānaṃ ca śiṣṭānāṃ granthārambhe maṅgalam' itidīpikāyāmuktam। tena
maṅgalasya kartavyatve śiṣṭācārānumitā śrutiḥ pramāṇamiti labhyate। dīpikāgranthena। tadetadāha vyavasthāpayitumiti। pramāṇam। tādṛśaśruteḥ paṭhyamānavede kutrāpyadarśanāt
ityāśaṅkāyāṃ śiṣṭācārānumiteti śruterviśeṣaṇamupāttaṃdīpikāyām। yadyapi śrutiḥ na pratyakṣā tathāpi ācāreṇa liṅgena tādṛśī śrutiranumīyate। tathā ca ācārānumitā śrutiḥ pratīti। yathā yāgaviṣayakaprayatnaṃ prati ayāgaḥ matkṛtisādhyaḥ' kāraṇamiti bhāvaḥ।
tadāśayaḥ। ityādigranthena pradarśitaḥ। tasmin anumāne vedabodhitakartavyatākatvaṃ hi sādhyam, na tu vedaḥ। yat anumānasādhyaṃ - anumitividheyaṃ tadevānumintamityucyate। tathā
atrāyamāśayaiti। vedavodhitetyādi। vedabodhitakartavyatākatvarūpaṃ tadavacchedakatve apītyarthaḥ।apinā vidheyatvāsambhavarūpo virodho dyotyate।tadantarbhāveṇavidheyatāvacchedakāntarbhāveṇa।tacchruteḥ
asāmāptikāmo maṅgalamācareta' iti śruteḥ।anumiteḥpūrvamasiddhatvāditi। pūrvamasiddhatvameva anumitividheyatāyāṃ prayojakam। maṅgalasya vidheyatākhyaviṣayatā aṅgīkriyate। tataśca bhāvaḥ।
vahnitvasyāpi tādṛśānumitividheyatvaṃ syāt। tathā ca samādhatte-eteneti। anuminteḥ pūrvamasiddhasyaiva vidheyatāvacchedakasya anumitividheyatvāṅgīkāreṇetyarthaḥ। tathā ca iti bhāvaḥ।
vidheyatāvacchedakatārūpāṃ viṣayatāmityarthaḥ। viśeṣyatayā prayojakamiti svīkāreṇetyarthaḥ। śrutauvidheyatvābhyupagameneti। anumiteḥ pūrvamasiddhatvāditi śeṣaḥ।tādṛśavyavahāra iti। śrutiḥ anumitā iti vyavahāra ityarthaḥ।
vyavahāre anumiteḥ pūrvaṃ siddhatvaṃ bādhakam, tadabhāvāt ityarthaḥ। iti pratīyate। tanna saṅgacchate, maṅgalakartavyatāyāṃ amaṅgalaṃ evakāro apyarthakaiti। aperartho yasya saḥ apyarthakaḥ, apyarthasuccayārthaka ityarthaḥ। tathā ca
śruterevetyasya śruterapītyarthaḥ। apinā anumānasya pramāṇatvaṃ samuccīyate। ato nāsaṅgatiriti bhāvaḥ। upapāditaṃ prakāśikākāraiḥ। etaṃ kleśaṃ śruteranumitatvam ti। amaṅgalaṃ
svabodhitakartavyatākatvasambandhena vedaviśiṣṭam ityarthaḥ। tathā ca vedasyānumitatvamanāyāsenopapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। yathāśrutamūlārthatyāgaścāsvarasaḥāhurityanena sūcitaḥ। dīpikāyāmalaukikāvigītaśiṣṭācāraviṣayatvāditi। śiṣṭānāmācāraḥ śiṣṭācāraḥ
bhāvastattvam। alaukikatve sati avigītatve sati śiṣṭācāraviṣayatvaṃ heturiti phalitam। laukikatvaṃ vidhyatiriktapramāṇagamyatvam, tadbhinnatvamalaiṅkikatvam। hetau avigītaśiṣṭācāraviṣayatvarūpahetusattvāt vyabhicāraḥ syāt।
tadvāraṇāya alaiṅkikatvamupāttam। avigītatvaṃ dharmaśāstrāniṣiddhatvam। vyabhicāraḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya avigītatvamupāttam। rātriśrāddhādeḥ vyabhicāraḥ। prakāśikāyāṃvidhimantareti। liṅloṭtavyapratyayaghaṭitaṃ
vedavākyaṃ vidhiḥ।vedoktatattvajñāneneti। tṛtīyāyāḥ janyatvamarthaḥ karmakārītyatra kṛdhātvarthakṛtyanvayi। vedavihitakarmaviṣayakakṛtiḥ tadāśrayaḥ śiṣṭa ityarthaḥ।vedotthatattvajñāneneti kvacitpāṭhaḥ। vedajanyaṃ yattattvajñānaṃ tenetyarthaḥ। vedavihitakarmakartā śiṣṭaḥ
śiṣṭatvāpattiḥ। tadvāraṇāyavedotthatattvajñāneneti। bauddhasya yat ahiṃsāditattvajñānaṃ na tat vedajanyamiti nātivyāptiḥ। yadvāvedoktattvajñāneneti pāṭhaḥ ādhīyān। idaṃ vedoktamiti jñānapūrvakaṃ yaḥ vedavihitaṃ karma karoti sa śiṣṭaḥ। bauddhastu vedavihitamahiṃsādikaṃ karma
vedaprāmāṇyānabhyupagamāditi na tasya śiṣṭatvāpattiḥ। hetutvamastu, kimācāraviṣayatvaparyantasya hetutvānudhāvanena। na ca alaukiketi। vidhyatiriktapramāṇānavagamyatvarūpamalaukikatvamastīti bhāvaḥ।
sādhīyāniti। tathā śiṣṭatvamiti labhyate। maṅgalarūpa pakṣaniṣṭhatvābhāvāt kathaṃ hetutvamiti vācyam। kṛtirityādinā। vṛttiḥ ādheyatā tanniyāmakaḥ
sambandhaḥ vṛttiniyāmakaḥ sambandhaḥ saṃyogasamavāyādiḥ। viṣayatā tu na vṛttiniyāmakasambandhaḥ। viṣayatāsambandhena kṛtiḥ maṅgalavṛttiriti pratītyabhāvāt। vṛttiniyāmakasambandha eva ca hetutāvacdedakasambandhaḥ na tu vṛttyaniyāmako viṣayatādiḥ। tathā ca kṛteḥ
hetutvānudhāvanam। viṣayatvaṃ tu svarūpasambandhena hetuḥ, ācāraviṣayatvasya hetutvaṃ sambhavatītyāśayaḥ। prayojanaṃ mūle anuktamiti svayaṃ tatprayojanaṃ kathayatisvargādiphalaiti। tathā ca hetau syāt। svargādirūpe phale api tatsattvāt
ityupāttam। svargādestu kṛtiviṣayatvaṃ nāstīti na vyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ। nanu kṛteḥ uddeśyaṃ vidheyam upādānamiti viṣayatrayamasti। yāgaḥ vidheyaḥ svarga uddeśyaḥ prayājādyaṅgajātamupādānam। svarge
ti। tṛtīyāyā abhedor'thaḥ। ācāranirūpitavidheyatvābhinnaviṣayatvaṃ hetuḥ। svargādaiṃ bhāvaḥ। vyāpakāropastarkaḥ। tathā ca tarkasaṅgraha ityasya
bhavati। sa na yujyate, tarkasaṅgrahagranthena pratipādanādityāśaṅkya tarkaśabdena yathā granthapratipādyasakalapadārthaḥ। pratipādyeta tathā tarkaśabdo vyutpādyate dīpikāyāmityāhatarkapadasyetyādinā।āropārthakatvabhramamiṃti। vyāpyāropeṇa vyāpakāropārthakatvabhramamityarthaḥ। saṅgrahaśabdasyopādānamityapyartho asti। so atra na sambhavati;
uṇādipadārthānāṃ, dravyeṣvapi ākāśādināmupādānasyāsambhavāt। upādānaṃ hi hastakaraṇakavyāpāraviśeṣaḥ। tasmāt ityāhaupādānarūpeti। nanu svarūpakathanamityatra kathanaśabdasyoccāraṇamarthaḥ। uccāraṇaṃ nāma
tālvoṣṭhapuṭasaṃyogānukūlavyāpāraḥ। tasya śabdamātraviṣayakasya svarūpajñajñanānukūlaḥśabda iti। tathā ca prakṛte kathanaśabdasya noccāraṇamarthaḥ, kintu jñānānukūlaḥ śabdor'thaḥ। jñāne svarūpaviṣayakatvānvayāt nānupapattiriti bhāvaḥ।
anubandhacatuṣṭayamaṅgam। viṣayaprayojanasambandhādhikāriṇaḥ catvāro anubandhāḥ। anubadhnanti puruṣaṃ granthādhyayane ityeteṣāṃ caturṇāṃ jñānaṃ vinā na ko api granthādhyayane pravarteta। ti। tarkasaṃṅgrahapadasya
vyākhyānenetyarthaḥ। sukhabodhāya ityatra sukhasya bodha iti prayojanamiti labhyeta। tathā sati nikhilapadārthabodhakatvaṃ tarkasaṃṅgrahapadavyākhyānena sūcitaṃ virudhyeta। ataḥ sukhena guṇādipadārthānāmityasya upādānasyāsambhavādityanenānvayaḥ।
tṛtīyātatpuruṣatayā vyākhyātamityāha - ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣeti। anyataḥ siddhatveneti। bhāṣyādigranthāntarapaṭhanādapi siddhatvenetyarthaḥ।। AnTs dravyaguṇakarmasāmānyaviśeṣasamavāyābhāvāḥ sapta padārthāḥ ।। vibhajate -dravyeti। padasyārthaḥ padārtha iti vyutpattyā
abhidheyatvaṃ padārthasāmānyalakṣaṇam। nanu vibhāgādeva saptatve siddhe saptapadagrahaṇaṃ vyarthamiti cet - na। adhikasaṅkhyāvyavacchedārthakatvāt। nanu atiriktaḥ padārthaḥ pramito vā na vā। nādyaḥ; pramitasya niṣedhāyogāt। na dvitīyaḥ;
pratiyogipramitiṃ vinā niṣedhānupapatteriti cet - na। padārthatvaṃ dravyādisaptānyatamatvavyāpyamiti। vyavacchedārthakatvāt। nanu saptānyatamatvaṃ saptabhinnabhinnatvam। saptabhinnasyāprasiddhyā kathaṃ saptānyatamatvavyāptiniścaya iti cet - na। dravyādisaptānyatamatvaṃ
nāma dravyādibhedasaptakābhāvavattvam। evamagre api draṣṭavyam।। mūlai saptapadārthāiti। dravyatvādirūpāye padārthavibhājakāḥ saptopādhayaḥ tadanyatamavantaḥ padārthā ityarthaḥ।
tatra saptatvamapekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatvam। evamagrimagranthasyāpi atraiva paryavasānamavadheyam। sāmānyalakṣaṇakathanānantarameva vibhāgo yuktaḥ। tathā ca mūle kathamādau vibhāga iti nyūnatāṃ pariharatipadasyeti। padasyārthaḥ abhidheyaḥ iti vyutpattyā
padasambandhitvāṃśasyāvyāvartakatvādāhaabhidheyatvamiti। lakṣaṇaṃ labhyata iti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca na nyūnateti bhāvaḥ।vibhāgādeveti। padārthatvāvāntaradharmapuraskāreṇa dharmipratipādanādevetyarthaḥ।adhikasaṅkhyāvyavacchedārthakatvāditi। tādṛśasaṅkhyāniṣedhasiddhiphalakatvādityarthaḥ। uddeśyavidheyabhāvasthale
vidheyavyāpyatvabhānamautsargikamityāśayenāhapadārthatvamiti।iti vyavacchedārthakatvāditi। iti etadrūpo yo vyavacchedonirṇayastadarthakatvādityarthaḥ।saptabhinnabhinnatvamiti। vaktavyamityarthaḥ।dravyādibhedasaptakābhāvavattvamiti। dravyādibhedānāṃ pratyekaṃ prasiddhānāṃ saptānāṃ doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। vastutastu"padārthatvaṃ
dravyatvādisaptopādhyanyatamavattvavyāpyamityarthaḥ। tena bahuṣu dhyeyam। evaṃ rītyā dravyāṇītyādāvapītyarthaḥ।। iti yathāśrutamūlāt padārthāḥ saptatvasaṅkhyāvanta iti labhyate। tanna yuktam। dravyaguṇādīnāṃ pratyekamanekatvāt āhatya
dravyatvādirūpāityādinā।tathā ca hāvapradhānanirdeśāt dravyādipadāni dravyatvādiparāṇi। antimasya abhāvapadasya bhāvapradhānanirdeśāditi। bhāvaḥ prakṛtyarthaprakārībhūto dharmaḥ pradhānaḥ tātparyaviṣayo yasya śabdasya saḥ bhāvapradhānanirdeśaḥ। tathā ca
bhāvapradhānanirdeśatvam। lakṣaṇā। dravyatvādiṣu saptatvānvayaḥ। dravyatvādirūpāḥ ye padārthā iti vākyāt bodhaḥ। dravyādipadārthānāṃ nekatve api bhāvaḥ।
apekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatvamiti vyācaṣṭe -atra saptatvamiti। tadviṣayatvamityarthaḥ।agrimagranthasyāpīti। ityādivakṣyamāṇagranathasyāpītyarthaḥ।atraiva paryavasānamavadheyamiti। caturviṃśatitvādeḥ apekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatva eva niśceyamityarthaḥ।
dravyaguṇakarmetyādivākyaṃ padārthavibhāgavākyam। vibhāgo śabdaḥ। viśeṣadharmaprakārakajijñāsāyāṃ satyāmeva kartuṃ śakyaḥ। anyathā ajijñāsitārthakathanarūpārthāntaradoṣāpatteḥ। viśaiśajijñāsāṃ prati
sāmānyadharmaprakārakajñānaṃ kāraṇam। vibhāgāt pūrvaṃ mūle sāmānyadharmajñānasyeti। āmānyajñānasya viśeṣajijñāsāyāṃ svātantryeṇa, anekatve apīti। saptādhikasaṃkhyākatve apītyarthaḥ।
dravyatvaguṇatvādimantaḥ' ityākārakaṃ tajjanakaśabda ityarthaḥ। viśeṣajijñāsāyāmviśeṣadharmaprakārakajñānecchāṃ prati। gadādharabhaṭṭācāryāḥprāhuḥ। svatantrānvayavyatirekaśālitayā hetutvaṃ sāmānyajñānasya। athavā
viśeṣadharmaviśiṣṭajñānadharmikeṣṭasādhanatāprakārakajñānaṃ kāraṇam। dharmitāvacchedakībhūtaviśeṣadharmaprakārakaṃ jñānaṃ kāraṇam। viśiṣṭe vyavasthāpitatvāt। sāmānyadharmajñānasya viśeṣadharmajijñāsāyāṃ hetutvamitigadādharāśayaḥ। tathā ca sāmānyadharmajñānaṃ vinā viśeṣajijñāsā
notpattumarhatīti bhāvaḥ।sāmānyalakṣaṇakathanānantaramiti। padārthānāṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇe kathite viśeṣadharmajijñāsā bhavitumarhatīti bhāvaḥ। avaśyavaktavyārthākathanaṃ labhyate। katham abhidheyatvaṃ labhyata iti mūloktaṃ saṅgacchata ityāśaṅkyāha -padasyārthe abhidheyaiti। yadyapi śabdataḥ padasambandhyabhidhāviṣayatvaṃ labhyate,
padārthasāmānyalakṣaṇatvasambhavena padasambandhitvāṃśsya vyarthatvāt। ityākāraka jñānaṃ kāraṇam। tādṛśajñānaṃ prati dharmitāvacchedakānāṃ dravyatvādīnāṃ jñānaṃ kāraṇam। dravyatvādijñāne padārthatvarūpasāmānyadharmajñānaṃ kāraṇamityarthaḥ।
kāraṇamiti nirūpitam। tadatra anusaṃhitam। vivakṣitamityāśayaḥ। avyāptyativyāptyādivāraṇarūpaprayojanaśūnyatvādityarthaḥ। na śobhate।
vibhāgavākyaprayojakaviśeṣajijñāsājanakasāmānyadharmajñānotpādane anyonyaśrayādidoṣeṇaucityavirahāt। sūcitam। tato viśaiṣajijñāsāyāṃ dravyaguṇetyādivibhāgavākyamavatīrṇamiti kathanameva yuktam। tathaiva iti।
dharmipratipādanādeveti। padārthatvavyāpyadravyatvādidharmaṃviśiṣṭadravyādidharmipratipādakadravyādiśabdādityarthaḥ। bodhe api teṣu saptatvasaṅkhyāyāḥ kathaṃ bodha iti cet - atrāhuḥ। dravyaguṇetyādidvandvasamabhivyāhṛtabahuvacanādevetyarthaḥ। tathā
avaśyamaṅgīkaraṇīyaḥ। anyathā rāmalakṣmaṇabharataśatrughnā ityatra bahuvacanena tritvādibodhāpattyā anubhavavirodhāpatteḥ। evaṃ ca tādṛśasaṅkhyā saptatvasaṅkhyaṃveti bahuvacanena tatsiddhiriti।nīlakaṇṭhaprakāśikāyāapi kathañcidatraiva tātparyaṃ bodhyam। adhikasaṅkhyāvyavacchedārthakatvāditi। adhikasaṅkhyāyāḥ saptatvādhikāṣṭatvasaṅkhyāyāḥ vyavacchedaḥ
niṣedhanirṇayaḥ arthaḥ prayojanaṃ yasya tattvādityarthaḥ। tadāha -tādṛśasaṅkhyeti। evaṃ ca saptapadena aṣṭamapadārthanāstitvaṃ bodhyata iti phalitam। aṣṭamapadārthasya ityāśayena jñāta ityanuktvā pramita iti mūle uktam। pramita ityasya pramāviṣaya ityarthaḥ। pramāviṣayasya sattāniyamena
niṣedhāyogāt iti vaktu śakyata iti bhāvaḥ।tatraiva pratiyogipramiti vineti। yadyapyabhāvabuddhau pratiyogijñānameva ityākārakapramāyāḥ asambhavāt। tathāpi prakṛte pratiyogitāvacchedakaprakārakapratiyogiviśeṣyakapramaiva ivakṣitā। gaganābhāvabuddhiḥ sambhavati। prakṛte saptapadārthātiriktapadārthaṃsya pramā
nāstīti tanniṣedho nopapadyata itidīpikāśayaḥ। dravyādisaptānyatamatvaṃ vidhīyate। uddeśyavidheyabhāvasthale ca uddeśyatāvacchedake vidheyavyāpyatvaṃ bhāsata iti sāmānyaniyamaḥ। dravyādisaptānyatamatvamiti। tathā ca siddhyasiddhibhyāṃ vyāghāto
netyarthaḥ। tadetadāha -uddeśyavidheyabhāvasthalaiti।autsargikami ti। sāmānyanyāyasiddhamityarthaḥ। vacchedakaprakārakapratiyogiviśeṣyakajñānaṃ kāraṇamityevārthaḥ। na tu pratiyogiprakārakajñānamiti bhāvaḥ।
bhramitavyamiti bodhayituṃ vyācaṣṭe -etadrūpaiti। saptagrahaṇasyeti śeṣaḥ। nāma saptabhinnabhinnatvam। saptapadārthabhinnasyāprasiddhyā ityāśaṅkitaṃ ananu saptānyatamatvam' ityādinādīpikāyām। tatrāprasiddhiśaṅkāna na yujyate, ye dravyādayaḥ saptapadārthāḥ pratyekaṃ tadbhinnabhinnatvasya pratyekaṃ sattvāt।
sattvādityāśaṅkya vyācaṣṭe -dravyādayo ye sapteti। tadbhedasaptakaviśiṣṭaṃ yat tadbhinnatvaṃ saptānyatamatvam।tatra bhedasaptakaviśiṣṭamaprasiddham, dravye tadghaṭitasaptabhedasamudāyasyāsambhavāt, evaṃ guṇādāvapi। tathā ca saptabhinnabhinnatvamaprasiddhamiti śaṅkiturāśaya iti bhāvaḥ। dravye
tatsamudāyatvāvacchinnābhāvo atra saptānyatamatvam। padārthatvaṃ yatra ityāśayamāha -dravyādibhedānāmiti। dṛśyate। ataḥ padārthatvaṃ dravyādisaptānyatamatvavyāpyamiti dīpikāyāḥ vastutastviti।
vyāptiḥ prakṛte vivakṣitā। padārthatvaṃ dravye asti, tatra dravyatvādisaptānyatamabhūtadravyatvavattvamastīti। dravyādau vyāptiḥ sugrahā। anyatamatvaṃ ca tadbhinnabhinnatvameva। dravyatvādayaḥ ye sapta nāprasiddhiśaṅkāvakāśa iti bhāvaḥ। dravyatvaṃ
rītyetyarthaḥ।। AnTs tatra dravyāṇi pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśakāladigātmamanāṃsi navaiva ।। tatreti।tatra- dravyādimadhye। dravyāṇi navaivetyanvayaḥ। kāni tāni ityata āha -pṛthivīti।।
dravyamiti। vibhajate tatreti' itidīpikāgrantho anupapannaḥ। tathā hi - dravyapadottaraikavacanasya ekatvamarthaḥ। tasya prakṛtyarthe dravye anvayaḥ। tasya dvitīyārthe viśeṣyatve ādheyatāsambandhenānvayaḥ। viśeṣyatāyāḥ nirūpakatāsambandhena
dhātvarthaikadeśajñāne anvayaḥ। vipūrvakabhajadhātoḥ dravyatvavyāpyaparasparaviruddhanānādharmaprakārakapramātmakajñānajanakaśabdor'thaḥ।, iti adravyaṃ vibhajata' iti vākyāt bodhaḥ। tatra ekadravyaviśeṣyakaṃ sambhavati। pṛthivyādi rūpaikadravyaviśe atiriktatve
āvaśyakatejo abhāvarūpatvaṃ sidhyatītyapi bodhyam।। tamasaḥ daśamadravyatvaṃ siṣādhayiṣitam। tatra hetau tamaso dravyatvaṃ sādhanīyam। tatrāpi hetvasiddhiśaṅkā na kāryā; pratītyā tamasaḥ rūpavattvasya kriyāvattvasya ca siddheḥ। tadāhadīpikāyāṃ'nīlaṃ tama'ityādinā।pratītibalāditi
añcamyantasya rūpādhāratve kriyādhāratve cānvayaḥ। bādhitapratīterviṣayāsādhakatvāt abādhitetyuktam। prathamopasthitaparityāge mānābhāvāt। pratyakṣāsambhavasthala prātyakṣikapratītibalāditi।
sattvādityāśaṅkyāha -samavāyenanīlarūpavatteyetyarthaiti। tathā ca vivakṣitam। janyaguṇādau kālikasambandhāvacchinna bhramavāraṇāya rūpādhāratve kriyādhāratve cānvaya ityuktam। siddhāntāt। tathā ca nityaguṇādeḥ kālikasambandhena rūpādhāratvaṃ na
sambhavatītyamipretya janyaguṇādāvityuktam। vyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ।kālikasambandhena tasyeti। kālikasambandhāvacchinnarūpakriyādhāratvasyetyarthaḥ।atiprasaktatve api - dravyātiriktavṛttitve api।na kṣatiḥ- navyabhicāraḥ।evamagre api bodhyamiti।'tamaso nākāśādipañcake antarbhāvaḥ rūpavattvādityartho bodhya iti bhāvaḥ। pariśeṣānumāne hetughaṭakaṃ dravyatvaṃ sādhitam। atha hetughaṭakaṃ
kḷptadravyānantarbhūtatvaṃ sādhyatedīpikāyām tatra tamasaityādinā। nanu rūpavattvahetunaiva tamasaḥ vāyāvanantarbhāve ityāśaṅkyāha -sambandhabhedābhiprāyeṇeti।rūpavattvaṃ samavāyasambandhena hetuḥ। sparśābhāvastu svarūpasambandhena hetuḥ। samavāyasambandhena hetumuktvā svarūpasambandhena hetumāhetyarthaḥ। yadi tamo vāyāvantarbhavet
rūpavat na syāt sparśaśūnyaṃ ca na syāt। yataḥ tamaḥ rūpavat sparśaśūnyaṃ ca ato vāyau nāntarbhavatīti bhāvaḥ। vāyubhinnam, sparśābhāvāt' ityanumānaṃ phalitam। tatra sparśābhāvasya sattvāt vyabhicāraḥ। na ca
vivakṣitaḥ। sa ca na vāyāvasti, tatra samavāyena sparśasya sattvāt tadabhāvāsambhavāditi vācyam। kālikasambandhena vāyau sattvāt vyabhicāratādavasthyāt। na ca vivakṣitatvāt na vyabhicāra iti vācyam। evamapi
kriyāniṣṭhā ca yā ādheyatā tannirūpitādhāratvamityarthaḥ। vyabhicārasya durvāratvādityāśaṅkyāhaidaṃ ca dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvādhikaraṇaiti। tathā ca sparśaprāgabhāvavati prācīnamate na vyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ। ityarthaḥ। navyamate api vyabhicāraṃ vārayitumāha -vastutastuiti। tathā ca vāyau sparśātyantābhāvaḥ
niravacchinnadaiśikaviśeṣaṇatāsambandheneti na vyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ। kālikasambandhaśca navyanyāyagrantheṣu vyavahriyate। viṣamavyāptahetumiti। sādhyamātranirūpitavyāptimān hetuḥ iti cocyate। atamaḥ vāyubhinnam, rūpavattvāt'
vāyubhedanirūpitā vyāptiḥ hetau rūpavattve asti। yatra yatra vāyubhedaḥ sambhavati, vāyubhedavatyākāśādau rūpavattvābhāvena vyabhicārāt। ato rūpavattvaṃ viṣamavyāpto hetuḥ। evaṃ sparśābhāvo api। yatra yatra ghaṭādau sparśasyaiva sattvāt। atamaḥ vāyubhinnam,
hetuḥ। yatra yatra vāyubhedaḥ tatra tatra sadāgatimattvābhāva iti vāyubhedanirūpitavyāpteḥ sadāgatimattvābhāve ca sattvāditi। vāyumātravṛttirvilakṣaṇakriyetyarthaḥ। dīpikāyāṃ nāpi tejasīti। atamaḥ tejasi nāntarbhavati ityanumānam। tatra bhāsvararūpābhāvaḥ viṣamavyāptaḥ, uṣṇasparśābhāvaḥ
samavyāptaḥ। evaṃ atamaḥ jalabhinnam śītasparśābhāvāt nīlarūpavattvācca' viṣamavyāptam। atamḥ pṛthivībhinnam, gandhābhāvāt viṣamavyāptamiti ūhyam। nāsti, kuto daśamadravyatvam। tamastvabhāvākhye
। tatra tejo abhāvapadena tejo antarapratiṃyogikābhāvasattvena tama iti pratītiprasaṅgaḥ। pratītyanupapattiḥ। prakāśakaṃ yattejaḥ prakāśakatejastryaṇukakhadyotādimati pradeśe tamaḥpratītyanupapattiḥ। ataḥ
vivakṣaṇīyaḥ। prauḍhatvaṃ ca prakṛṣṭamahatvavattvam। tamaḥpratīternānupapattiḥ। tadetatsarvaṃ manasikṛtyāha -prauḍhaprakāśaketi। prakāśakapadaprayojanamāha -ataiti। ityuktau prakāśakapadaṃ vayartham। tejaḥparamāṇūnāṃ prakṛṣṭamahattvarūpaprauḍhatvābhāvādeva vāraṇasambhavāt। ataḥ
hiraṇyāditejovāraṇāya prakāśakapadamiti vaktavyam। evamapi pradeśe tamaḥpratītyanupapattiḥ। tadvāraṇāya udbhūtarūpavattvamapi tejasi viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। tathā ca prakṛṣṭamahattvavatprakāśakodbhūtarūpavattejastvāvacchinnapratiyogi tākābhāvastamaḥ।
atha vā pauḍhatvaṃ mahāprabhāvattvam। tenaiva paramāṇūnāṃ hiraṇyādeśca vāraṇasambhavāt prakāśakapadamanupādeyam। mahāprabhāvattvāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvastama iti phalitam। ti।
rūpidravyam' ityādyuktam। atra tamaso rūpavattvābhāvaḥ dravyatvābhāvaśca siṣādhayiṣitaḥ। tamo yadi rūpavat dravyaṃ vā bhavet, tadā gṛhyate ataḥ tamo na rūpavat na vā dravyamiti। yatra yatra yathā ālokābhāve iti vyāptisadbhāvāt। hetau
tadupādānam। ghaṭādirālokasahakṛtacakṣurgrāhyaḥ na tadasahakṛtacakṣurgrāhya iti na vyabhicāraḥ। tadāha -ghaṭādāviti। cakṣurjanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvam। cakṣurjanyajñānīyalaukikaviṣayatvamiti। tamoviṣayake cakṣurjanyapratyakṣa
ityarthaḥ।upanayamaryādaye ti। jñānalakṣaṇapratyāsattyetyarthaḥ। pāṭho dṛśyate। tatra atamovān ghaṭa iti' iti bhāgaḥ aprāmāṇikaḥ, siddhāntavirodhāt। atastadbhāgarahitaḥ pāṭhaḥ eva kvacit dṛśyamānaḥ
sādhuḥ। atha vā aghaṭavattamaḥ iti' iti śodhayitvā paṭhanīyam। āha -viśeṣābhāvamiti। viśeṣadharmāvacchinnābhāvo dṛṣṭāntaḥ। ato nānupapattiriti bhāvaḥ। māstu ityaprayojakaśaṅkāyāmuktaṃdīpikāyām - rūpidravyacākṣuṣapramāyāmityādi। yadi rūpidravyabhedo na syāt tarhi
ālokāsahakṛtacakṣurgrāhyaṃ na syāt। arthāt yadi rūpidravyaṃ syāt aprayojakaśaṅkānivārakaḥ vaktavyaḥ। sa ca tarkaḥ pradarśitaḥ। tatra pramāpadasya prayojanamāha -ālokaṃ vineti। tathā vyatirekavyabhicāraḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya pramāpadamiti bhāvaḥ।anyatheti।rūpidravyacākṣuṣapramāyāmālokasya
kāraṇatvābhāve ityarthaḥ। vyatirekavyabhiñcārāt। na ca tejobhinnaṃ yat rūpidravyaṃ vyatirekavyabhicāra iti vācyam। tejobhinnatvavat vināpi tamasaścākṣuṣatvasambhavāt। tathā ca
niṣpratyūhamevetyata āha-digiti। sarvāṃnūbhūyamānoṣṇasparśāśrayatayā tamaso abhāvarūpatve api kṣatyabhāvāt tadbhinnatvaniveśo anucitaḥ। suṣṭhūktamiti bhāvaḥ।। dravyatvajātimattvaṃ guṇavattvaṃ vā dravyasāmānyalakṣaṇam।
ityata āha -dravyatveti। saṃyogajanakatāvacchedakatayā dravyatvajātisiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakayorabheda ityata āha -guṇavattvamiti।dravyasāmānyalakṣaṇami ti। evaṃ ca sāmānyadharmākathanena na
nyūnateti bhāvaḥ। dravyatvajātimattvaṃ dravyasya lakṣaṇamuktam। tatra dravyatvajātau kiṃ mānamityāśaṅkyāha -saṃyogajanakatāvacchedakatayeti। anena dravyatvajātau anumānaṃ pramāṇamuktaṃ bhavati। tathā hi - dravyayoreva saṃyoga iti saṃyogaṃ prati dravyaṃ samavāyikāraṇam।
samavāyasambandhena saṃyogaṃ prati tādātmyasambandhena dravyaṃ kāraṇam। dravye vartate। tāṃ kāraṇatāṃ pakṣīkṛtya tatra kiñciddharmāvacchinnatvaṃ kāraṇatātvena hetunā sādhanīyam। lāghavamiti lāghavajñānasahakāreṇa dravyatvākhyajātisiddhiriti bhāvaḥ।
lakṣaṇāntaramuktaṃ mūle। tatkathate bījamāha -lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakayorabheda iti। dravyasya dravyatvaṃ lakṣaṇamitmukte lakṣyaṃ dravyam lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakayorabhedaḥ syāt। nanvastu nāma tayorabhedaḥ, tāvatā ko doṣa iti cet - śrūyatām। lakṣaṇasya hi lakṣye itarabhedānumitiḥ prayojanam। lakṣaṇaṃ
lakṣyoddeśyaketarabhedavidheyakānumitijanakamiti yāvat। yathā goḥ ityanumānena goḥ itarabhinnatvaṃ sidhyati। tathā prakṛte api ityanumānaṃ prayoktavyam। tatra adravyam itarabhinnam' ityanumitiḥ।
tāṃ prati itarabhedavyāpyadravyatvavat dravyamiti parāmarśaṃḥ kāraṇam। vyāptiśca hetuvyāpakasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyarūpā। tathā ca parāmarśasya ākāraḥ sampannaḥ। tatra dravyatve itarabhede dravyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyamapi bhāsate। tulyavittivedyatā
nāma ekajñānaviṣayatvam। anumittau ca pakṣavṛttitvātmakaṃ pakṣatāvacchedakasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ sādhye bhāsate। evaṃ ca siddhasādhanākhyo doṣaḥ prasajati। anumiteḥ pūrvaṃ pakṣe sādhyaniścayasattve siddhasādhanadoṣaḥ bhavati। ato dravyasya yadi
paryālocya lakṣaṇāntarānudhāvanaṃ kṛtamiti bhāvaḥ। śaṅkāparihārāyā mūle dravyasāmānyalakṣaṇamuktamityāha -evañceti। lakṣaṇākathanarūpā nyūnatetyarthaḥ। avyāptyādilakṣaṇam। dūṣaṇāni। lakṣyaikadeśāvṛttitvamavyāptiḥ। yathā goḥ kapilatvam।
alakṣye lakṣaṇasya vartanamativyāptiḥ। yathā goḥ śṛṅgitvam। lakṣyamātrāvṛttitvamasambhavaḥ। yathā gorekaśaphavattvam। viśeṣaṇībhūtadūṣaṇatrayarahitatvajñānaṃ vinā na sambhavati। dūṣaṇatrayarahitatvajñānaṃ tu viśiṣya dūṣaṇatrayajñānādhīnam।
tantratvādityāśayena dūṣaṇatrayaṃ darśayati -lakṣyaikadeśāvṛttitvamiti। lakṣaṇatāvacchedakatvābhimatasambandhena kiñcillakṣyāvṛttitvamityarthaḥ। mātrapadaṃ sambandhaviśeṣāvacchinnalakṣyavṛttitvasāmānyābhāvasphorakam। na cātra alakṣyavṛttitvarūpātivyāpterapi sattvāt saṅkara iti vācyam।
duṣṭasaṅkare api doṣāsaṅkara iti nyāyāt। iti śiṣyasya jijñāsā jāyate। tacchāntaye lakṣaṇasya lakṣaṇaṃ vaktavyam। tataḥ prāk avyāptyādīnāṃ lakṣaṇakathanamasaṅgatamityata āha -dūṣaṇatrayetyādinā। dūṣaṇatrayarahitadharmatvaṃ lakṣaṇasya lakṣaṇam। dūṣaṇatrayarahitatvaṃ ca dūṣaṇatrayābhāvavattvam। tathā ca
dūṣaṇatrayābhāvaviśiṣṭadharmatvaṃ lakṣaṇalakṣaṇamiti paryavasitam। tatra dūṣaṇatrayābhāvarūpaviśeṣaṇajñānaṃ kāraṇam। tādṛśaviśeṣaṇajñānaṃ ca kāraṇatvāt। ataḥ dūṣaṇatrayaṃ dūṣaṇānīti nṛsiṃhaprakāśikānumataḥ pāṭhaḥ।
bhāvaḥ। viśiṣya dūṣaṇatrayajñānādhīnamiti। atrāyamāśayaḥ - dūṣaṇatrayarahitatvaṃ nāma na dūṣaṇatrayatvāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvaḥ। tathā sati lakṣaṇatvāpatteḥ। kiṃ tu avyāptyativyāptyasambhavarūpadūṣaṇāni
dūṣaṇatrayarahitatvamiti vaktavyam। tathā ca lakṣaṇamiti phalitam। tādṛśajñānotpādanāya ādau avyāptyādīnāṃ svarūpamāhadīpikāyāmiti। lakṣyaikadeśāvṛttitvamavyāptiriti। kiñcillakṣyanirūpitādheyatvābhāvaḥ
avyāptisvarūpamityarthaḥ। goḥ kapilatvaṃ lakṣaṇam ityukte lakṣyā kapilatve astīti avyāpte dharme lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। nanu gotvādhikaraṇe avyāptalakṣaṇāsambhava ityāśaṅkyāha -lakṣaṇatāvacchedakatvābhimatasambandheneti। vṛttitvānvayi avacchinnatvaṃ tṛtīyārthaḥ। tathā ca lakṣyatāvacchedakādhikaraṇanirūpita
avyāpteḥ svarūpam। kapilatvaṃ kapilagavi samavāyena astīti samavāyasambandhaḥ lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhaḥ। sambandhena lakṣye vartate sa sambandhaḥ lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhaḥ। kapilatve lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। lakṣyatāvacchedakādhikaraṇatvaṃ ca
akṣyatāvacchedakatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā avyāptalakṣaṇasyātivyāpteḥ। evaṃ lakṣyatāvacchedakasamānādhikaraṇatve satītyapi avyāptalakṣaṇe viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। anyathā asambhavagraste ekaśaphavattvādau avyāptalakṣaṇasyātivyāpteḥ।,
gotvādhikaraṇanirūpitavṛttitvābhāvasya tatrāpi sattvāt। tasmin gotvādhikaraṇavṛttitvābhāvāt। lakṣyatāvacchedakaniṣṭhādheyatānirūpitādhikaraṇatāvannirūpitavṛttitvam। lakṣyatāvacchedakatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā
ekaśaphavattvasya sattvena asambhavagrastadharme avyāptalakṣaṇasyātivyāpteḥ। tannirūpitavṛttitvaṃ ekaśaphavattve nāstīti nātivyāptiriti। evaṃ vṛttitve lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā ekaśaphavattvasya kālikasambandhena govṛttitayā pūrvoktadoṣāpatteḥ। evaṃ
avyāptasya lakṣaṇamiti phalitam। adhikaṃ paṭṭābhirāmaṭippaṇyādau draṣṭavyam। lakṣyatāvacchedakatāvacchedakasambandhaḥ। vartanamativyāptiriti।
alakṣyamityasya lakṣyaniṣṭhapratiyogitākabhedavadityarthaḥ। saptamyāḥ nirūpitatatvamarthaḥ। tasya vartanaśabdārthe ādheyatve anvayaḥ। bhavatiṃ। yathā goḥ śṛṅgitvaṃ lakṣaṇamuktaṃ cet idaṃ vartanāt। atra lakṣyaniṣṭhapratiyogitāyāṃ lakṣyatāvacchedakāvacchinnatvaṃ
niveśanīyam। anyathā goniṣṭhapratiyogitākabheda ityanena vartamānatayā avyāptadharme ativyāptalakṣaṇasyātivyāpteḥ। tanniveśe tu tadvṛttitvaṃ kapilatve nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ। lakṣṇatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā gobhinne
pūrvoktadoṣāpatteḥ। tanniveśe tu lakṣaṇaṃ yena sambandhena lakṣye kapilatve abhāvāt na tatrātivyāptiḥ। evamapi asambhavagraste lakṣyatāvacchedakasamānādhikaraṇatve satīti viśeṣaṇamatrāpi deyam। ekaśaphavattvasya lakṣyatāvacchedakagotvādhikaraṇavṛttitvābhāvānna doṣaḥ।
lakṣaṇamiti phalitam। lakṣyamātrāvṛttitvamasambhavaiti। sarvatra lakṣye avartanamasambhavaḥ। kvacillakṣye avartanamavyāptadharme apyastīti sarvatretyuktam। goḥ asambhavadoṣadūṣitaṃ bhavati।
tu lakṣyavṛttitvapratiyogiko abhāvaḥ। kapilatvādyavyāpyadharme api sattvenātivyāptyāpatteḥ। tadvivakṣaṇe tu govṛttitvaṃ nāstīti mātrapadam। evaṃ lakṣyanirūpitavṛttitve lakṣṇatāvacchedakasambanghāvacchinnatvamapi niveśanīyam। anyathā
