tadvṛttitvābhāvavirahāt asambhavalakṣaṇe asambhavadoṣaḥ syāditi। tathā asambhava iti phalitam। sarvamidamabhisandhāyāhaprakāśikāyām mātrapadaṃ kṛtsnārthakamiti। lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhetyarthaḥ।lakṣyavṛttitvasāmānyābhāveti। lakṣyavṛttitvatvāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvetyarthaḥ।
ekatra anekadoṣasāṅkaryaṃ prasajatīti śaṅkate -na cātretyādinā। śaṅkeyaṃ yathāśrutātivyāptilakṣaṇābhiprāyeṇa। pūrvoktapariṣkṛtātivyāptisvarūpasya ekaśaphavattve virahāt। doṣabhedāt। duṣṭasyāpi bhedena bhavitavyamiti śaṅkiturbhāvaḥ।
ti। duṣṭasyaikatve api doṣasya ekatvaṃ netyarthaḥ। ekasmin anekadoṣāṇāṃ samāveśasambhavena doṣabhedāt tadāśrayaduṣṭabhedāpattirneti samādhāturāśayaḥ। maṇikāravacanasyāpyayamevārthaḥ।
etaddūṣaṇatrayarahitadharmo lakṣaṇam। yathā goḥ sāsnādimattvam। sa evāsādhāraṇadharma ityucyate। lakṣyatāvacchedakasamaniyatatvamasādhāraṇatvam। vyāvartakasyaiva lakṣaṇatve dharmaviśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। vyavahārasyāpi lakṣaṇaprayojanatve tu tat na
deyam। vyāvṛtterapi vyavahārasādhanatvāt। etaddūṣaṇatrayarahitaiti। uktadūṣaṇābhāvatrayaviśiṣṭa ityarthaḥ। nanvasādhāraṇadharmo lakṣaṇamiti hi siddhāntaḥ। tasmāt kāraṇāt kathaṃ dūṣaṇatrayarahito dharmo lakṣaṇamityata āha -sa eveti। abhiyuktairiti śeṣaḥ। nanu
asādhāraṇatvamanyādṛśaṃ nirvakti -lakṣyatāvacchedakasamaniyatatvamiti। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatve sati lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpyatvamityarthaḥ। avyāptyasambhavagrastayorvāraṇāya satyantam। ativyāptasya vāraṇāya viśeṣyam। dharmapadaṃ lakṣaṇatāghaṭakasambandhena vyāpakatvāditātparyagrāhakamiti bhāvaḥ।
etaddoṣā asādhāraṇatvasya vighaṭakāḥ। ativyāptau vyāpyatvasyetarayośca vyāpakatvasya bhaṅgāt। eteṣāṃ dūṣakatābījaṃ itarayośca bhāgāsiddhisvarūpāsiddhī iti। nanu vyāvartakasyaiveti। itarabhedānumitijanakasyaivetyarthaṃḥ।
tāvacchedakaviṣayatāviśeṣāśrayasyaivetiyāvat। etena vyāvahārikavyavacchedaḥ।lakṣaṇatvegavādilakṣaṇatve uktalakṣaṇalakṣaṇalakṣyatva iti yāvat।lakṣyatvaiti pāṭhe apyayamevārtho bodhyaḥ। lakṣaṇalakṣaṇe niveśanīyamityarthaḥ। yadyapi vyāvṛtterapi prācīnamate itarabhedasya vyāvartakatvābhāvena tatrātivyāptiḥ।
pṛthakkathanamiti dhyeyam। lakṣaṇalakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakaṃ vyāvartakatvam। na tāvat sāmānyato bhedānumāpakatvam। vyāvṛttyabhidheyatvāderapi tatrātivyāptikathanāsaṅgateḥ। sarveṣāmapi vyatirekadharmāṇāṃ
asādhāraṇyādighaṭakavyāpakatvādivairthyāpātācca। nāpi viśiṣya tattaddharmāvacchinnetarabhedānumāpakatvam। tathā sati prakṛtasādhyasya tattulyasya vā sādhyasyāsattvena vyabhicāraḥ syāt। pūrvoktadoṣāvasaraḥ। adhikavicārastu anyatrānusandheyaḥ।
vyavahāro api prayojanam। tena rūpeṇa vyavahartavyajñānaṃ vinā tadrūpāvacchinnabodhakaśabdarūpavyavahārāsambhavāt। evaṃ ca deyamityāha - vyavahārasyāpīti। nanu vyāvṛttāvativyāptivāraṇāya tadbhinnatvamāvaśyakam। vyāvṛttervyāvahārikatvābhāvāditi bhramaṃ
vārayati - vyāvṛtterapīti। apinā abhidheyatvādiparigraho dṛṣṭāntalābhāya। lakṣaṇamityarthaḥ। tathā ca kadoṣavatyapi kapilatvādau doṣatrayaṃ uktadūṣaṇābhāvatrayaviśiṣṭa iti। pratiyogini tritvaṃ na vivakṣitam,
kiṃ tu abhāve iti bhāvaḥ। ekadoṣavati ūrvoktāpattiriti dhyeyam। ekadoṣavatyapīti। avyāptirūpakaidoṣaviśiṣṭe apītyarthaḥ।
lakṣaṇatvāpattiriti। golakṣaṇatvaprasaṅgaḥ ityarthaḥ। pūrvoktāpattiriti। kapiṃlatvādergolakṣaṇatvāpattirityarthaḥ।
sādhāraṇabhinna ityarthaḥ। sādhāraṇa ityasya ca lakṣyavṛttitve sati alakṣyavṛttirityarthaḥ। lakṣyavṛttitvaviśiṣṭālakṣyavṛttitvavāniti yāvat। asādhāraṇa ityasya ca lakṣyavṛttitvaviśiṣṭālakṣyavṛttitvābhāvavānityarthaḥ। avyāptigraste
kapilatvādau alakṣyavṛttitvarūpaviśeṣyābhāvāt viśiṣṭābhāvo asti। viśiṣṭābhāvavān। tatathā ca ubhayoḥ asādhāraṇatayā lakṣaṇatvāpattiḥ, prakārāntareṇocyate dīpikāyāmityāha - nanu sādhāraṇyasyeti। anyādṛśamiti। lakṣyavṛttitvaviśiṣṭālakṣyavṛttitvābhāvāt
anyavidhamityarthaḥ। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatve satīti। lakṣyatāvacchadakaṃ yatra yatra vartate tatra sarvatra vartamānatvaṃ lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatvam। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpyatvam। lakṣyā gauḥ, lakṣyatāvacchedakaṃ gotvam, bhavati, atastat goḥ lakṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca
lakṣaṇamityuktaṃ bhavati। satyantasya prayojanamāha - avyāptyasambhavagrastayorvāraṇāyeti। avyāptigraste kapilatve tadvāraṇāya lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatve satītyuktam। gotvavati nātivyāptiḥ। nanu uktarītyā
tadvāraṇarūpaṃ prayojanaṃ na sambhavati। asambhavagrastasya ekaśaphavattvādeḥ atrāhuḥ। atrāsambhavagrastapadaṃ gaganarūpasyāsambhavagrastasya tātparyeṇa bodhakam। goḥ gaganaṃ lakṣaṇamuktaṃ cet tadasambhavi। gaganasya avṛttipadārthatayā kutrāpi gavi asattvāt। tathā cāsambhavagraste gagane
tadvāraṇāya lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatve satītyuktamiti। ativyāptasya vāraṇāya viśeṣyamiti। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpyatvarūpaviśeṣyadalābhāve lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatvaṃ lakṣaṇalakṣaṇaṃ syāt। tathā sati śṛṅgitvasya gotvavyāpakatvamastīti tatrātivyāptiḥ syāt।
tadvāraṇāya lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpyatvopādānam। śṛṅgitvasya nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। lakṣyatāvacchedakaniṣṭhādheyatānirūpitādhikaraṇatāvanniṣṭhātyantābhāvāprat iyogitvam। niveśyam। anyathā gotvasya kālikasambandhena adhikaraṇe mahiṣādau
lakṣaṇe sāsnādimattvādau asambhavāpatteḥ। evaṃ pratiyogitāyāṃ lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā samavāyena tatpratiyogitvasyaiva sāsnādimattve sattvena asaṃbhavāpatteḥ। evaṃ lakṣaṇe avyāptyāpatteḥ। kiṃ tu svavyāpakatatkatvam। svaṃ - lakṣaṇam,
tat - lakṣyatāvacchedakam। lakṣyatāvacchedakasya padārthatvasya lakṣaṇībhūtābhidheyatvavyāpakatvamastīti na pūrvoktadoṣaḥ। pariṣkāro yuktaḥ। svavyāpakatvaṃ ca svaniṣṭhādheyatānirūpitādhikaraṇatāvanniṣṭhātyantābhāvāpratiyogitvam।
tatrādheyatāyāṃ lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। asambhavāpatteḥ। evaṃ pratiyogitāyāṃ lakṣyatāvacchedakatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā tatpratiyogitvasyaiva gotve sattvena pūrvoktadoṣāpatteḥ।
lakṣyatāvacchedakasamaniyatatvamiti phalati। evaṃ ca gaganarūpe asaṃbhavagraste api na bhavati gaganādhikaraṇasyaivāprasiddheḥ। tathā tacchūnyāvṛttitvarūpavyāpyatvaniveśamabhipretyetyavadheyam। tathā cetyādi।
tādṛśapratiyogitvābhāvaḥ sāsnādimatve astīti। adhikamanyato avaseyamiti। sarvamidaṃ manasikṛtyaiva vyāpakatvāditātparyagrāhakam' ityuktam। asādhāraṇo na bhavatīti labhyate। tena
ativyāptyādidoṣāṇāmasādhāraṇyābhāvaprayojakatvaṃ labhyate। tadevopapādayati-atredaṃ bodhyamityādinā। etaddoṣāḥ-avyāptyativyāptyasambhavāḥ। asādhāraṇatvasya vighaṭakāḥ-asādhāraṇatvābhāvaprayojakāḥ। ativyāptau satyāmiti śeṣaḥ।
itarayośca satyoriti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca ativyāptirūpadoṣe sati rītyādoṣāṇāmasādhāraṇyavighaṭakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। doṣāstāvat lakṣaṇaṃ dūṣayanti। kathamiti cet - āha - eteṣāṃ dūṣakatābījaṃ tviti। ayamatrāśayaḥ lakṣaṇaṃ tāvat liṅgavidhayā lakṣye
itarabhedavidheyakānumitiṃ janayati। yathā goḥ itarabhinnā sāsnādimattvāditi। liṅgasya vyāptiḥ pakṣadharmatā ceti rūpadvayamapekṣitam। kasmiṃścit lakṣaṇe ativyāptirūpo doṣo asti vyabhicāradoṣeṇa vyāpterbhaṅgāt। tathā hi - gauḥ itarabhinnaṃ
śṛṅgitvāt ityanumānaṃ prayoktavyam। śṛṅgitvamativyāptaṃ gavetaretyādi। gavetarabhedarūpaṃ yat sādhyaṃ tadabhāvavadvṛttītyarthaḥ। gavetarabhedābhāvaśca gavetaratvarūpaḥ। tathā ca
gobhinnavṛttītyevārthaḥ। tathā cātivyāptatvajñānaṃ bhāvaḥ। vyāptivirodhivyabhicāreti। vyāptijñānapratibandhakajñānaviṣayo yo dūṣayati।
vyabhicārākhyadoṣayuktaṃ karotīti yāvat। evaṃ lakṣaṇe sarvalakṣyāvṛttitvarūpāsaṃbhavasattvekṛtsnapakṣāvṛttitvarūpasvarūpās iddhirdeṣaḥ। tābhyāṃ ca hetoḥ pakṣadharmatā bhajyate। tathā ca avyāptyasambhavayorlakṣaṇūdaṣakatvamiti।
vyāvartakasyaiva lakṣaṇatve ityadi। yat lakṣye kecit। yat na vyāvartakam api tu śabdaprayogarūpavyavahārasya nimittaṃ tadapi lakṣaṇamityante। tatra vyāvartakameva lakṣaṇamiti mate vyāvartakaṃ lakṣyaṃ bhavati। vyāvartakabhinnā vyāvṛttiḥ abhidheyatvādikaṃ
cālakṣyaṃ bhavati। tatrāpi lakṣyatāvacchedakasamaniyatatvasattvāt lakṣaṇalakṣaṇasyātivyāptirdeṣaḥ। tadvāraṇāya lakṣaṇalakṣaṇe vyāvṛttibhinnatvaṃ abhidheyatvādibhinnatvaṃ ca viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। kathaṃ gavetarabhedaḥ। saḥ lakṣyatāvacchedakagotvavyāpakaḥ gotvavatīṣu
sarvāsu goṣu gavetarāpekṣayā bhedasya sattvāt। evaṃ gavetarabhedasyāvṛtteḥ। evaṃ abhidheyatvādikaṃ abhidheyatvādeḥ sattvāt। evaṃ padārthatvavyāpyaṃ ca। yadyapi padārthatvaśūnyasyāprasiddheḥ। tathāpi svavyāpakatatkatvarūpaṃ vyāpyatvaṃ
sambhavati। svam - abhidheyatvam, tadvyāpakaṃ - padārthatvaṃ tatkatvasyābhidheyatve sadbhāvāt। evaṃ ca yadi vyāvartakameva tattadbhinnatvaṃ lakṣaṇe niveśanīyamiti dīpikāgranthasya bhāvaḥ। itarabhedānamitijanakasyetyartha uktaḥ। siddhasādhanadoṣeṇa vyāvṛtteḥ
itarabhedānumitijanakatvaṃ nāstīti paścādupapādayiṣyati। lakṣaṇarūpasya hetoḥ anamitijanakatvābhāvāt। na ca vyāvartakasyetyasya noktadoṣa iti vācyam। anumitijanake amūhālambanaparāmarśe ghaṭādīnāmapi viṣayatayā teṣāmapi vyāvartaṅkatvāpatteḥ। na
anakatāvacchedakatvamiti vācyam। janakatāvacchedakatayā tadāśrayasyetarabhedasyāpi vyāvartakatvāpatteḥ। evaṃ pakṣādīnāmapi vyāvartakatvāpatteśca। ato niṣkṛṣya vyācaṣṭe - itarabhedavidheyaketi। viṣayatāviśeṣapadena hetuniṣṭhaviṣayataiva
vyāvartakatvāpattiriti hṛdayam। gavetarabhedavyāpyavān ghaṭaścetyākārakaparāmarśe ityarthaḥ। janakatāvacchedakatvamiti। gauritarabhinnetyākārakāranumiti prati kāraṇatāvacchedakatvamiti bhāvaḥ।
tattvam। vyāvartakasyaiva gavādilakṣaṇatve api prakṛtalakṣaṇalakṣaṇe nānupapattirityato vyācaṣṭe - uktalakṣaṇalakṣaṇalakṣyatva iti। uktaṃ yat ityarthaḥ। atiyāptimupapādayati - gavādītarabheda iti। vyāvartakam vyāvahārikam ceti dvividham। tatra vyāvartakalakṣaṇameva
vyāvahārikabhinnatvaṃ niveśyamityevocyatām। vyāvahārikapadenaiva abhidhānasya vyarthatvāt ityāśaṅkate - yadyapīti। avyāvṛtterapi vyavahārasādhanatayā' iti grantheneti śeṣaḥ। saṃgrahasaṃbhavāditi। ekaśabdabodhyatvasaṃbhavādityarthaḥ। pṛthagabhidhānam
- bhinnabhinnaśabdairnirdeśaḥ। samādhatte - tathāpīti। ayamatrāśayaḥ - iti prācīnamate na saṃbhavati। tathā hi - itarabhedaḥ itarabhinnā itarabhedāt' ityevānumānasya prayoktavyatvāt। itarabhedavyāpyetarabhedavatī' ityākārakaparāmarśaḥ kāraṇam। sa
pakṣaviśeṣyakasādhyaniścayarūpo bhavati। tatkāle ca gauḥ pratibandhakatvāt। pakṣatāyā abhāve cānumitirna bhavitumarhati। itthaṃ ca lakṣaṇalakṣaṇasya sattvādativyāptiḥ iti।
viśiṣṭābhāvarūpapakṣatāsattvāt anumitirbhavatyeva। itthaṃ ca agavi cātivyāptiḥ' ityuktaṃ dīpikāyāmiti। nanu kimidamityādi। vyāvartakatvaṃ lakṣaṇalakṣaṇasya lakṣyatāvacchedakamiti labhyate। tatra kiṃ
bhedavidheyakānumitijanakatvam। vyāvṛttyabhidheyatvāderapi tatrātivyāptikathanāsaṅgateḥ। gauḥ goghaṭobhayabhinnā vyāvṛttyabhidheyatvādāvapi sattvāt। kiṃ ca sarveṣāmapi yatirekiṇāṃ vyatirekiṇāmiti।
bhedānumāpakatvāt iti bhāvaḥ। kevalānvayināṃ dharmāṇāṃ tu nāstīti vaktuṃ śakyetāpītyāśayena vyatirekiṇāmityuktam। tathā ca bhavitumarhantīti bhāvaḥ। ativyāptyaprasaktyeti। alakṣye lakṣaṇasattvaṃ hyativyāptiḥ, na tu lakṣye
iti bhāvaḥ। tadvārakasya vyāpyatvaviśeṣaṇasya ca vyarthatvaprasaṅgāt। vivakṣitam। ubhayabhedasya gotvāvacchinnetarabhedatvābhāvena vyāvartakatvāpattiḥ। kapilatvādeśca
vyabhicārācceti vāvyam। tathā sati abhidheyatvādāvativyāpterasambhavāt। abhidheyatve abhāvāt। tathā cābhidheyatvādāvativyāptikathanamasaṅgatamiti pūrvapakṣaḥ।
vyāvartakatvāpattiriti। viśiṣya niveśe agauḥ gavetarabhinnā ityevānumānaprayogo vācyaḥ। tatrādye sādhyahetvoraikyāt tādṛśānumitirna bhavati। dvitīye padārthetarasyāprasiddhyā tādṛśānumitirna sambhavati। ato vyāvṛttyabhidheyatvāderna
vyāvartakatvāpattiṃḥ। tathā cālakṣyatayā tatrātivyāptikathanaṃ yujyata iti viśiṣya bhedānumāpakatvaṃ vyāvartakatvamiti vakturāśayaḥ। na bhavatīti। tathā samanaiyatyaghaṭakavyāpakatvādidalasārthakyamiti bhāvaḥ।
lakṣyatāvacchedakamapyanumīyate। yathā aghaṭaḥ pṛthivī gandhavattvāt' lakṣyatāvacchedakamanumīyata iti। prakṛte sāsnādimattvaṃ lakṣyam। lakṣaṇalakṣaṇalakṣyatvāt। evaṃ ca sāsnādimattvaṃ pakṣīkṛtya tatra daurbhikṣyāt। ataḥ yatra yaddharmasamaniyatatvaṃ yatra
vyāptirvaktavyā। pṛthivītvasamaniyataṃ pṛthivītvāvacchinnetarabhedānumāpakaṃ gandhavattvaṃ dṛṣṭāntaḥ। doṣaḥ। tathā ca gevatarabhedarūpavyāvṛttai pūrvoktarītyā siddhasādhanāt। tathā ca
gotvāvacchinnetarabhedānumāpakatvarūpaṃ sādhyaṃ tatra nāsti। gotvasamaniyatatvarūpaheturastīnti tatra vyabhicāraḥ syāt। lakṣyatāvacchedakamapyanumīyata iti। prakāśikāyāṃ sāsnādimattvaṃ ityāśaṅkāṃ manasi nidhāyaivamuktam। atha vā evaṃ tātparyaṃ
sādhanīyaḥ। prakṛte gotvasamaniyatatvarūpasya lakṣaṇalakṣaṇasya lakṣyatāvacchedakaṃ gotvāvacchinnaterabhedānumāpakatvam। sāsnādimatve sādhanīyaḥ। tadavacchinnetarabhedaśca gotvāvacchinnetarabhedānumāpakatve sādhye ityuktagiti।
padārthetarasyāprasiddheriti vyabhicāraḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya abhidheyatvādibhinnatve sati iti viśeṣaṇaṃ dātavyam। tena yatra dīpikāgranthasyeti। paṅktīnāmartha ucyate। sāmānyato bhedānumāpakatvamiti।
śakyata ityarthaḥ। vyāvṛttyabhidheyatvāderapīti। agauḥ abhidheyatvāt' ityanumāne atra vivakṣite। ativyāptikathanāsaṅgateriti। lakṣye lakṣaṇasattvasyeṣṭatvāditi bhāvaḥ। vyatirekidharmāṇāmiti। kevalānvayidharmāṇāmabhidheyatvādīnāṃ
prayoktuṃ na śakyate, padārthetarasyaivāprasiddheriti bhāvaḥ। asādhāraṇyaghaṭaketi। lakṣyatāvacchedakasamaniyatatvarūpāsādhāraṇyaghaṭakaṃ yat vyāpakatvaṃ vyāpyatvaṃ ca tayorvaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt ityarthaḥ। nāpi viśiṣyeti। viśiṣyetyasya bhede anvayaḥ। atra
vyākhyātavyam। anyathā akapilagauḥ gavetarabhinnā kapilatvāt' ityanumānasambhavena pūrvoktadoṣasattvenāsya pakṣāntaratvānupapatteḥ। tādṛśalakṣaṇe niveśanīyamiti। tādṛśalakṣaṇarūpe hetau niveśanīyamityarthaḥ।
vyavahāro apītyādi। yathā lakṣaṇasya itarabhedānumitiḥ prayojanaṃ tathā śabdaprayogarūpo vyavahāro api prayojanam। kathamiti cet- ittham। purovarti govyaktau aiyaṃ gauḥ' ityākārakaṃ gotvaprakārakaṃ goviśeṣyakaṃ jñānaṃ kāraṇam।
taddharmaprakārakavyavahartavyaviśeṣyakajñānasya kāraṇatvāt। aiyaṃ gauḥ' vyavahāraḥ prayojanam। tathā ca lakṣaṇaṃ vyāvahārikamapi bhavatīti deyamiti bhāvaḥ। tena rūpeṇa vyavahartavyajñānamiti। taddharmaprakārakavyavahartavyaviśeṣyakajñānamityarthaḥ।
yāvat। vyavahāraprayojanakavyāvṛttyabhidheyatvādirūpalakṣaṇasyāpi। lakṣyatvāt lakṣaṇalakṣaṇalakṣyatvāt। tadbhinnatvam vyāvṛttyabhidheyatvādibhinnatvam। yathā
iti jñāpanāya iti bhāvaḥ।। cet - na। guṇasamānādhikaraṇasattābhinnajātimattvasya vivakṣitatvāt। na। ekārthasamavāyādeva tādṛśavyavahāropapattau guṇe guṇānaṅgīkārāt।
tatsattvamakṣatam। evaṃ ca guṇāśrayatvalakṣaṇaṃ sādhvityata āha - utpannavinaṣṭeti। yādṛśadravyārambhakasaṃyogajanakakriyotpatteḥ ityarthaḥ। navīnāḥ punaḥ asamavāyikāraṇasya kāryasahabhāvena kāraṇatāmavalambyotpannavinaṣṭaṃ nāṅgīkurvanti।
guṇādāvativyāptivāraṇāya guṇasamānādhikaraṇeti jātiviśeṣaṇam। sattāmādāyātivyāptivāraṇāya sattābhinneti। dravyaguṇānyataratvamādāyātivyāpitavāraṇāya jātīti। samavāyena tādṛśadharmavattvatātparyagrāhakam। ataḥ kālikādisambandhena
tadvattvamādāya nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। evamapīti। uktavivakṣayā avyāptivāraṇe api ekārthasamavāyādeveti। ekasminnarthe samavāyena sattvādevetyarthaḥ। tathā ca kḷptena
tatrākḷptaguṇavattvakalpanaṃ na sambhavati gauravāditi bhāvaḥ। guṇavattvaṃ vā dravyalakṣaṇamiti pūrvamuktam। tatra guṇavattvaṃ lakṣaṇam na akriyaṃ ca tiṣṭhati' iti nyāyena guṇavattvābhāvena avyāptidoṣāt। guṇavattvaṃ na dravyalakṣaṇamityādinā। tatra dvitīyasthalānudhāvane
bījamāha - nanvādyakṣaṇāvacchinne dravya iti। kālāntarāvacchinna iti। dvitīyādikṣaṇavacchinna ityarthaḥ। tatra tatsattvam - dravyaguṇasattvam। guṇaśrayatvamiti। guṇādhāratvamityarthaḥ। samavāyena guṇaḥ nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। yādṛśadravyārambhaketyādi। kriyā, kriyāto
tataḥ dravyotpattiriti kramaḥ। atra vibhāgaḥ saṃyogaśca avayavānāṃ pūrvottaradeśānāṃ ca। ghaṭotpādakaḥ yaḥ caturthakṣaṇotpannaḥ jāyate cet utpattyanantarakṣaṇe dravyasya nāśo bhavati। tathā cāyaṃ kramaḥ bhāvaḥ।
navīnāḥ punariti। asamavāyikāraṇena saha utpadyate। ghaṭanāśaśca tattṛtīyakṣaṇa eveti iti bhāvaḥ। guṇasamānādhikaraṇeti। guṇasamānādhikaraṇā guṇādhikaraṇavṛttiḥ yā
sattānyā jātiḥ tadvattvaṃ dravyasya lakṣaṇam। bhavati hi dravyatvarūpā jātiḥ lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। tatsamānādhikaraṇadravyatvajātisattvāt nāvyāptiḥ। jātau sattābhinnaguṇatvajātimattvasya guṇe sattvāt tatrātivyāptiḥ।
guṇatvagrahaṇāsambhavāt nātivyāptiḥ। guṇādhikaraṇadravyavṛttiḥ yā sattājātiḥ tadvattvasya guṇe api sattvādativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya jātau sattābhinneti viśeṣaṇam। jātipadasthāne dharmapadaṃ sattābhinnaśceti tadvattvasya guṇe api sattvādativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya
jātītyuktam। anyataratvaṃ tu na jātiḥ। nanu jātipade upātte api sattvādativyāptiḥ। samavāyasambandhena tādṛśajātimattvavivakṣāyāṃ tu jātipadaṃ vyartham। samavāyasambandhena sāmañjasyāt। dravyaguṇānyataratvarūpadharmasya svarūpameva sambandha iti
samavāyena tadvattvasya guṇe virahāditi cet - na। samavāyasambandhena tādṛśadharmavattvamatravivakṣitamiti dyotanāyaiva jātipadopādānāditi। tadāha prakāśikāyām - guṇādāvativyāptivāraṇāyetyādinā। nanvevamapīti।"ekaṃ rūpam' iti vyavahārāt rūpe
iti vyavahārāt rūpe pṛthaktvaguṇo astītyavagamyate। tathā ca guṇe sattvāt tatra dravyalakṣaṇasyātivyāptiriti śaṅkiturāśayaḥ। samādhatte - ekārthasamavāyāditi। ekasminnarthe samavāyādityarthaḥ। rūpam', arūpaṃ rasāt pṛthak' iti vyavahāra upapadyate। aekaṃ rūpam'
samavāyasambandhena ekatvavat iti। evaṃ ca uktaparamparāsambandhena rūpe samavāyasambandhena guṇo nāṅgīkriyate। samavāyasambandhena vivakṣitam। ato rūpādaiṃ nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। samavāyaghaṭitasāmānādhikaraṇyeneti। svāśrayasamavāyeneti yāvat।
samavāyasambandhaghaṭitasāmānādhikaraṇyam। tasya śodhane svāśrayasamavāya ityeva paryavasyati। akḷptaguṇavattvakalpanamiti। akḷptasya samavāyasambandhena guṇavattvasya kalpanamityarthaḥ। AnTs rūparasagandhasparśasaṃkhyāparimāṇapṛthaktvasaṃyogavibhāgaparatvāparatvagurutvadravatvasnehaśabdabuddhisukhaduḥkhecchādveṣaprayatnadharmādharmasaṃskārāś caturviṃśati guṇāḥ ।।
caturviṃśatirguṇāḥ। rūpeti। dravyakarmabhinnatve sati sāmānyavān guṇaḥ। guṇatvajātimānvā। catuviṃśatirguṃṇāḥ iti cet - na। ladhutvasya gurutvābhāvarūpatvāt
mṛdutvakaṭhinatvayoḥ avayavasaṃyogaviśeṣarūpatvāt। sāmānyavāniti। samavāyena sāmānyavattvaṃ bodhyam। tena kālikādisambandhena tadvati dhvaṃse nātivyāptiḥ। guṇa iti lakṣyanirdeśaḥ। lāghavādāha -
guṇatvajātimānveti। yadyapi lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakayorabhedaḥ tathāpi lakṣaṇamiti saṅkṣepaḥ। ekamagre api bodhyam। guṇatvajātisiddhistu guṇapadaśakyatāvacchedakatayeti guṇadīdhitau bhaṭṭācāryāḥ। na caivaṃ sidhyediti vācyam।
jātitvābhimatasaṅkarasyaiva jātitvabādhakatvāt। tathā coktam saṅkāro athānavasthitiḥ। jātibādhakasaṅgrahaḥ।।" iti। vyakterabhedaḥ
svāśrayavyakteraikyaṃ ākāśatvāderjātitve bādhakam। vyaktestulyatvaṃ ghaṭatvakalaśatvādyorbhinnajātitve। saṅkaraḥ bhūtatvamūrtatvāderjātitve। anavasthitiḥ- anāvasthā jāteḥ jātimattve। rūpahāniḥ svatāvyāvartakatvātmakarūpahāni viśeṣasya
jātimattve। asambandha asamavetatvam abhāvāderjātimattve iti saṃkṣepaḥ। samādhattelaghutvasyeti। iti। sāmānyaviśeṣasamavāyānāṃ
vaktumityālocya dhvaṃse ativyāptiruktā। yadyapi lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakayorabheda iti। guṇasya guṇatvajātimattvaṃ yadi lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchadakayorabhadaḥ syāt। astu ko doṣa iti cet - ucyate। lakṣaṇaṃ hi vyāvartakam।
lakṣyaviśeṣyakalakṣyetarabhedavidheyakānumitijanakam। tathā ca ityanumānaprayogaḥ kartavyaḥ। tatra parāmarśo vācyaḥ। tatra guṇatve itarabhedasāmānādhikaraṇye guṇatvasāmānādhikaraṇyamati bhāsitumarhati। tathā ca
śaṅkiturāśayaḥ। samādhatte - tathāpīti। hetau hetusāmānādhikaraṇyabhānaṃ na sambhavati। ato na siddhasādhnaprasaktiriti guṇatvajātimattvaṃ guṇalakṣaṇaṃ bhavitumarhatīti bhāvaḥ। guṇapadaśakyatāvacchedakatayeti। aguṇaniṣṭhā guṇapadaśakyatā
ityanumānena guṇatvajātiḥ sidhyatīti bhāvaḥ। bhūtatvasaṅkarasyeti। bhūtatvena sākamekatra samāveśasyetyarthaḥ। nanu jātitvābhimatadharmasaṅkara eva tathā। bhūtatvasya jātitvābhāve api samādhatte - jātitvābhimatasaṅkarasyaiveti। vyakterabhedatulyatvaṃ
saṅkaraśca jātimattve bādhakāni। anavasthā rūpahāniḥ asambandhaśca jātitve bādhakāḥ। jātibādhakasaṅgraha ityasya ityarthaḥ। svāśrayaikavyaktikatvamityarthaḥ।
bhedaviśiṣṭānyatvamiti yāvat। yasyāśrayabhūtā vyaktayaḥ anekāḥ sa nīlaghaṭabhedaviśiṣṭam। svaṃ nīlaghaṭabhedaḥ, svapratiyogī nīlaghaṭaḥ, tulyavittivedyatayeti। ekajñānaviṣayatayetyarthaḥ। nīlaghaṭabhedaviśiṣṭam। ākāśatvaṃ tu na tathā। bhedapadena
yadyapyākāśe asti, tathāti ākāśabhedānuyogighaṭādivṛttitvaṃ nāsti। tathāpi spapratiyogighaṭavṛttitvaṃ nāstīti। tathā ca svāśrayaikavyaktikam, atastat na jātiḥ। jātitvaṃ hi nityatve satyanekasamavetatvam। anekasamavetatvaṃ ca uktobhayasambandhena
bhedaviśiṣṭatvam। atra ca ākāśatvaṃ jātiḥ (uktobhayasambandhena jātibādhakatvamityavadheyam। anyūnānatiriktavyaktikatvamiti। anyūnānatiriktāśrayakatvamityarthaḥ। ghaṭatvakalaśatvayorīdṛśatulyatvasattvāt tayorna bhinnajātitvam।
tulyatvamityarthaḥ। idaṃ kambugrīvādimattvasya jātitve bādhakam। kambugrīvādimattve asti। yatraitādṛśaṃ tulyatvamasti atra jātitvaṃ nāsti। evaṃ caitādṛśatulyatvajñānasya jātitvābhāvavyāpyavattājñānavidhayā jātitvajñānapratibandhakatvam।
nāstīti। yathā pṛthivyādimano antānyatamatve। svaṃ tatsamaniyatatvaṃ pṛthivyādimanontānyatamatve astīti tanna jātiḥ। tathā ca svabhinnajātisamaniyatatvaṃ tulyatvam। dhikaraṇānyonyābhāvapratiyogitānavacchedakatvamiti bhāvaḥ।
parasparaṃ vihāya vartamānayordharmayorekatra vṛttiḥ। jātitvam। vādhikaraṇavṛttitva-svābhāvavadvṛttitva - kiñciddharmaviśiṣṭatvaṃ saṅkara iti phalitam। etādṛśasāṅkaryasya kathaṃ jātitvabādhakatvamiti cet - ucyate। liṅgavidhayaiva tasya
jātitvabādhakatvam। tathā hi - bhūtatvaṃ na jātiḥ uktatritayasambandhena svādhikaraṇetyādi। mūrtatve asti। evaṃ svaṃ bhūtatvaṃ svābhāvaḥ bhūtatvābhāvaḥ tadvat manaḥ tadvṛttitvaṃ mūrtatve asti। evaṃ svaṃ bhūtatvaṃ tadadhikaraṇamākāśaṃ
tadvṛttiryo atyantābhāvaḥ mūrtatvābhāvaḥ tatpratiyogitvaṃ mūrtatve asti। saṃkara ityarthaḥ। iti। gaganamanassaṃyogasya mūrtatvādhikaraṇamanovṛttitvāt gaganamanassaṃyogasya dṛṣṭāntatvam।
asya sāṅkarye akṣatatvāt। atha vā sākṣājjātitvajñānapratibandhakajñānaviṣayatvamakṣatamityāhuḥ। aprāmāṇikāttarottarakalpanāyāḥ viśrāntyabhāvaḥ। iyaṃ jāteḥ jātimattve bādhikā। arkavidhayā bādhakatvamasyāḥ।
vatovyāvartakatvarūpalakṣaṇasya bhaṅgaḥ। iyaṃ viśeṣasya jātimattve bādhikā। viśeṣo hi svatovyāvartakatvena lakṣitaḥ। viśeṣo yadi lakṣaṇaṃ bhagnaṃ syāt। ato viśeṣo na jātimān। evaṃ ca jātimattvabādhikā।
pratiyogitvānuyogitvānyatarasambandhena samavāyaśūnyatvam। ayaṃ ca samavāyābhāvayorjātimattve bādhakaḥ। yatra yatra jātimattvaṃ vartate tatra pratiyogitvānuyogitvānyatarasambandhena amavāyo asti। samavāye tasyeti।
pratibandhakajñānajanakajñānaviṣayatvasyetyarthaḥ। jātitvābhāvānumitīti। bhūtatvaṃ na jātirityākārikā yā jātitvābhāvavyāpyamūrtatvavat ityākārakaḥ tasyetyarthaḥ। tathā bhāvaḥ।
tarkavidhayeti। yadi syāditi tarko atra vivakṣitaḥ। svabhinnaliṅgakasvaviśeṣyakasvasajātīyetarabhedānumityaviṣayatvam। samavāyo astīti।
ghaṭatvasamavāyaḥ tadanuyogitvāt ghaṭasyeti। jātimattvaṃ tayoḥ। uktānyatarasambandhena samavāyābhāvaḥ jātimattvābhāvavyāpyaḥ। ataḥ asambandhajñānaṃ AnTs utkṣepaṇāvakṣepaṇākuñcanaprasāraṇagamanāni pañca karmāṇi ।।
- ākuñcana - prasāraṇa - gamanāni pañcakarmāṇi। utkṣepaṇeti। saṃyogabhinnatve sati saṃyogasamavāyikāraṇaṃ karma karmatvajātimadvā। nanu bhramaṇāderapyatiriktasya karmaṇaḥ sattvāt pañcetyanupapannamiti cet - na। bhramaṇādīnāmapigamane antarbhāvāt na
pañcatvavirodhaḥ। saṃyogabhinnatve satīti। saṃyogasamavāyikāraṇa dravye ativyāptivāraṇāya asamavāyīti। ityādinā recanasyandanordhvajvalanatiryaggamanānāṃ saṃgrahaḥ।
gamane antarbhāvāditi। na cotkṣepaṇādīnāmapi gamane anatarbhāvo astviti śaṅkyam। svatantrecchasya niyogaparyanuyogānarhasya munesaṃmatatvāditi bhāvaḥ। tadabhāvāditi।
pratiyogitāsambandhena samavāyavattvaṃ samavāyābhāvayerna bhavati। evaṃ anuyogitāsambandhena samavāyavattvaṃ tayorna bhavatīti bhāvaḥ। sati saṃyogāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ karmeti karmaṇo lakṣaṇamuktam। saṃyoge ativyāptiḥ।
tadvāraṇāya saṃyogabhinnatve satītyuktam। dravye ativyāptiḥ, tadvāraṇāya kāraṇe asamavāyīti viśeṣaṇam। tadāhasaṃyogāsamavāyikāraṇa iti। svatantrecchasyeti।
ityarthaḥ। paryanuyogaḥ - praśnaḥ। AnTs param aparaṃ ceti dvividhaṃ sāmānyam ।। sāmānyaṃ dvividham - param aparam ceti। - paramiti। param - adhikadeśavṛtti। aparam - nyūnadeśavṛtti।
sāmānyādicatuṣṭaye jātirnāsti। paramityādi। sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ agre mūlakṛtaiva vakṣyata iti na nyūnateti dhyeyam। sattāyā dravyatvādyapekṣayā adhikadeśavṛttitvena paratvameva।
ghaṭatvādīnāṃ nyūnadeśavṛttitvena aparatvameva। dravyatvādīnāṃ sattāto aparatvam ghaṭatvāditaḥ paratvamiti vivekaḥ। AnTs nityadravyavṛttayo viśeṣās tv anantā eva ।। nityeti। pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayaparamāṇavaḥ ākāśādipañcakaṃ ca
nityadravyāṇi। AnTs samavāyas tv eka eva ।। samavāyastu iti। nāstīti। na ca samavāyasyābhede sparśasamavāyavati vāyau
rūpavattāpratītiḥ syāditi śaṅkyam। rūpasamavāyasattve api rūpābhāvena tathā pratīterabhāvāditi dik। rūpavattāpratītiḥ syāditi। rūpasamavāyasyaiva rūpavattāpratītiniyāmakatvāditi bhāvaḥ।
rūpam। rūpasamavāyasattve apīti। nanu vāyau rūpasamavāyasattve rūpaṃ nāstīti - digiti। ayamāśayaḥ - vāyvanuyogikatvaviśiṣṭaḥ rūpavattāpratītiniyāmakaḥ। vāyvanuyogikatvaviśiṣṭasamavāye
śakya iti। adhikaṃ muktāvalīmañjūṣādau draṣṭavyam। AnTs abhāvaś caturvidhaḥ । prāgabhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsābhāvo atyantābhāvo anyonyābhāvaś ceti ।। abhāvaḥ caturvidhaḥ - prāgabhāvaḥ, pradhvaṃsābhāvaḥ, atyantābhāvaḥ, anyonyābhāvaśceti। abhāva iti।
AnTs[] gandhavatī pṛthivī । sā dvividhā nityānityā ca । nityā paramāṇurūpā । punas trividhā śarīrendriyaviṣayabhedāt । śarīram asmadādīnām । indriyaṃ gandhagrāhakaṃ ghrāṇaṃ nāsāgravarti । viṣayo mṛtpāṣāṇādiḥ ।। tatra gandhavatī pṛthivī। tatroddeśakramānusārāt prathamaṃ pṛthivyāḥ lakṣaṇamāha - tatreti। nāmnā padārthasaṅkīrtanamuddeśaḥ। uddeśakrame ca sarvatra icchaiva
niyāmikā। gandhānutpādādavyāptiḥ। na ca tatra gandhapratītyanupapattiriti vācyam। avayavagandhasyaiva tatra pratītisambhavena citragandhānaṅgīkārāt। kiṃ cotpannavinaṣṭaghaṭādāvavyāptiriti cet - na।
gandhasamānādhikaraṇadravyatvāparajātimattvasya vivakṣitatvāt। gandhapratīterativyāptiriti cet - na। anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ pṛthivīgandhasyaiva tatra bhānāṅgīkārat। nanu tathāpi kālasya sarvādhāratayā sarveṣāṃ lakṣaṇānāṃ kāle ativyāptiriti cet - na।
sarvādhāratāprayojakasambandhabhinnasambandhena lakṣaṇasya vivakṣitatvāt। prāthamye bījamāha - tatreti। pṛthivyādiṣu madhya ityarthaḥ। bodhyam। tṛtīyārthaḥ abhedaḥ। saṅkīrtanapadārthe pratipādakaśabde anveti। tathā ca vastupratipādakanāmamātramuddeśa
iti lakṣaṇaṃ paryavasyati। atra ghaṭa iti pade ativyāptivāraṇāya vastupadaṃ lakṣaṇīyavastuparam। lakṣaṇīyasya pṛthivyādeḥ sāmānyataḥ lakṣyatāvacchedakāvacchinnaparam। lakṣaṇavākye nāmasattvāt ativyāptivāraṇāya mātrapadamiti dhyeyam।
ārabdhe - janye। parasparavirodheneti। surabhigandhaṃ prati asurabhigandhasya asurabhigandhaṃ prati surabhigandhasya pratibandhakatvenetyarthaḥ। pratītyanupapattiriti। ataścitragandha evāpratibadhyaḥ svīkārya iti
bhāvaḥ। avayavagandhasyaiveti। svāśrayasamavetatvasambandhenetyādiḥ। tuṣyatu durjana iti nyāyenāṅgīkṛtyāha - kiṃ ceti। jalatvādikamādāya ativyāptivāraṇāya gandhasamānādhikaraṇeti। sattāvāraṇāya dravyatvāpareti dravyatvanyūnavṛttītyarthakam। teda
dravyatvavyudāsaḥ। gandhapratīteriti। surabhi jalamityādipratīterityarthaḥ। pṛthivīgandhasyaiveti। svāśrayasaṃyuktatvasambandhenetyādiḥ।
tatra - jalādau। yathāśrutagrāhī śaṅkate - nanviti। anugatarūpeṇa sarvādhāreti। vassutastu samavāyādīnāṃ samavāyatvādinaiva bodhyam।
gandhasamavāyikāraṇatāvacchedakatayeti। ityanumānaprayogo atra vivakṣitaḥ। nāmnā padārthasaṅkīrtanamuddeśa iti mūlam। padārthasya saṅkīrtanaṃ padārthasaṅkīrtanam। saṅkīrtanaśabdasya pratipādakaśabda ityarthaḥ।
padārthaviṣayakajñānakaśabdaḥ padārthasaṅkīrtanamiti yāvat। padārthaśabdo vastuparaḥ। nāmneti tṛtīyārthasya abhedasya phalati। pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśakāladigātmamanāṃsītyatra uddeśalakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। ghaṭa iti padasyāpi vastupratipādakatvāt
nāmatvācca tatroddeśalakṣaṇasyātivyāptiḥ। lakṣaṇīyavastuparaṃ vaktavyam। ghaṭādipadaṃ ca na tādaśamiti nātivyāptiḥ। prameyamiti padasyāpi lakṣaṇīyapṛthivyādipratipādakatvāt tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya
vastupadaṃ lakṣyatāvacchedakāvacchinnavastuparaṃ vācyam। prameyapadasya lakṣyatāvacchedakapṛthivītvādyavacchinnapṛthivyādibodhakatvābhāvānnātivyāptiḥ। pṛthivītvāvacchinnabodhakatvāt nāmatvācca tasyoddeśatvāpattiḥ। tadvāraṇāya nāmamātramityapi vaktavyam। mātrapadena
lakṣaṇādivācakapadāsamabhivyāhṛtatvamucyate। tathā ca niṣkarṣaḥ। tadāha - tṛtīyārtho abheda ityādinā। saṅkīrtane ityasya vivaraṇaṃ pratipādakaśabde iti। prameyatvarūpasāmānyadharmeṇetyarthaḥ। tṛtīyāyāḥ pratipattyanvayi
rakāratvamarthaḥ। kasyāpi gandhasyānutpādādavyāptiḥ। na ca notpadyata iti śaṅkanīyam। surabhigandhasya asurabhigandhaṃ prati tatrotpattyasambhavāt। na ca yadi tatra gandho notpadyate, tarhi kathaṃ tatra
iti। tathā ca prameyapade ityarthaḥ। gandhapratītirupadyate, gandhavattāsattvādavyāptiśca neti vācyam। pratītisambhave citragandhasyānaṅgīkārāt। tathā ca
tatrāvyāptitādavasthyam। kiṃ ca yo ghaṭaḥ prathamakṣaṇe utpannaḥ atha kṣaṇamaguṇam' iti nyāyena gandhavirahāt। dvitīyakṣaṇe dharmiṇa eva surabhyasurabhīti। gandhasamānādhikaraṇeti। gandhādhikaraṇavṛttiḥ dravyatvavyāpyā ca
yā jātiḥ tadvattvaṃ pṛthivyāḥ lakṣaṇam। gandhādhikaraṇaṃ puṣpāditadvṛttiḥ nāvyāptiḥ। dravyatvavyāpyajātimattvamātroktau dravyatvavyāpyā yā jalatvajātiḥ tadvattvasya jale sattvāt tatrātivyāptiḥ। ato gandhasamānādhikaraṇeti। jalatvasya gandhādhikaraṇavṛttitvābhāvāt na
doṣaḥ। gandhasamānādhikaraṇajātimattvamātroktau ativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya dravyatvavyāpyeti jātiviśeṣaṇam। nanu dravyatvajātimādāyajalādiṣvativyāptiḥ durvārā। dravyatvasya na। prakṛte dravyatvavyāpyatvaṃ na dravyatvaśūnayāvṛttitvam kiṃ tu
dravyatvanyūnavṛttitvarūpam। dravyatvaṃ ca na dravyatvanyūnavṛtti ityāśayāt। dravyatvanyūnavṛttitvaṃ ca ravyatvasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvam। tadāha - prakāśikāyām jalatvādikamādāyetyādi।
dravyatvasamānādhikaraṇeti। dravyatvādhikaraṇaṃ jalaṃ tadvṛttiryo bheda dravyatvanyūnavṛttitvam। dravyatvaṃ tu na dravyatvādhikaraṇāvṛttitvāditi dravyatvaṃ na dravyatvanyūnavṛttīti bhāvaḥ। jalādāvapi gandhapratīteriti। tathā ca gandhavattvarūpasya pṛthivīlakṣaṇasya
jalādau ativyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। anvayavyatirekābhyāmiti। jalādau ityanvayavyatirekābhyāmityarthaḥ। svāśrayasaṃyuktatvasambandheneti। svaṃ pṛthivīgandhaḥ, svāśrayaḥ pṛthivī, tatsaṃyuktatvaṃ jalādau।
sambandhaviśeṣānavacchinnaṃ gandhavattvameva lakṣaṇamityabhimānavān। anugatarūpeṇasarvādhāratāprayojakasambandhabhinnasambanghatvenetyarthaḥ। samavāyādau। lakṣaṇatāghaṭakasambandhāt lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhān samavāyādīn। samavāyādīnāṃ samavāyatvādinaiva saṃsargatayeti।
spaṣṭaṃ cedam vyadhikaraṇagādādharyām। AnTs[] sā dvividhā nityānityā ca । nityā paramāṇurūpā । anityā kāryarūpā । punas trividhā śarīrendriyaviṣayabhedāt । śarīram asmadādīnām । indriyaṃ gandhagrāhakaṃ ghrāṇaṃ nāsāgravarti । viṣayo mṛtpāṣāṇādiḥ ।। nityā anityā ceti। anityā kāryarūpā। punastrividhā - śarīra-indriya-viṣayabhedāt। śarīraṃ
asmadādīnām। indriyaṃ gandhagrāhakaṃ ghrāṇam। tacca nāsāgravarti। viṣayo mṛtpāṣāṇādiḥ। sā dvividheti। nityatvaṃ dhvaṃsāpratiyogitvam। anityatvam dhvaṃsapratiyogitvam। prakārāntareṇa vibhajate - punariti। ātmano
bhogāyatanaṃ śarīram। yadavacchinnātmani bhogo jāyate tadbhogāyatanam। sukhaduḥkhānyatarasākṣātkāro bhogaḥ। jñānakāraṇamanassaṃyogāśrayatvaṃ indriyatvam। śarīrendriyabhinno viṣayaḥ। evaṃ ca gandhavaccharīraṃ pārthivaśarīram, gandhavadindriyaṃ
bodhyam। pārthivaśarīraṃ darśayati-śarīramiti। pārthivendriyaṃ darśayati - indriyamiti। gandhagrāhakamiti prayojanakathanam। ghrāṇamiti saṃjñā। nāsogretyāśrayoktiḥ। evamuttaratra jñeyam। pārthivaviṣayaṃ darśayati - mṛtpāṣāṇādi iti।
nityatvamiti। pṛthivīmityanuṣajyate। atra viṣayāntargatatvamiti pṛthivyāstrividhatvam। ata eva mūle punastrividhetyuktiḥ saṅgacchate iti dhyeyam। anityapṛthivyā eva traividhyaṃ varṇayanti। uddeśakramānusāreṇa prathamaṃ
śarīralakṣaṇamāha - ātmana iti। āyatanaṃ avacchedakam। tathā ca militaṃ yādṛśaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sampannaṃ tādṛśamāha - yadavacchinneti। sukhaduḥkhānyatarasākṣātkārāvacchedakam iti yāvat। atra antyāvayavitve satīti viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। tena pādādīnāṃ
avacchedakatve api tatra na ativyāptiḥ। yathā śarīratvaṃ na jātiḥ, jātirityāśayenāha - śabdetarodbhūteti। ātmādāvativyāptivāraṇāya satyantam। śrotre avyāptivāraṇāya śabdetareti। cakṣurādau viśeṣaguṇasyānudbhūtarūpādeḥ
sattvenāvyaptivāraṇāya udbhūteti। udbhūtatvaṃ na jātiḥ śuklatvādinā sāṃkaryāt। na ca śuklatvādivyāpyaṃ nānaivodbhūtatvamiti vācyam। cākṣuṣādau udbhūtarūpatvādinā kāraṇatvānupapatteḥ। kiṃ tu śuklatvādivyāpyaṃ anudbhūtatvaṃ nānā
tadabhāvakūṭavattvamudbhūtatvam। tacca saṃyogādāvapi। tathā ca śabdetarodbhūtaguṇaṃ saṃyogamādāya asambhavavāraṇāya viśeṣeti। ativyāptivāraṇāya jñānakāraṇeti। prācīnamate vāraṇāya manaḥ padam। na ca ātmānyatve sati ityanenaiva ātmani
gurutaraśabdetarodbhūtetyādiviśeṣaṇeneti vācyam। tathā sati tatrātivyāpterityalaṃ vistareṇa। tattadarthaṃsya śarīrādisāmānyalakṣaṇatve cetyarthaḥ। nanu gandhavattvapraveśenaiva tallakṣaṇasya sāmañjasye gandhagrāhakatvaniveśanamanucitam। evaṃ ca
vyācaṣṭe-gandhagrāhakamiti। uttaratra indriyaṃ rasagrāhakam ityādau। pṛthivīsāmānyasya tredhā vibhāga ucyate kiṃ vā anityapṛthivyāḥ। nādyaḥ, śarīrendriyaviṣayeṣu kvacidantarbhāvo vācyamaḥ। sa ca na sambabhavati। indriye।
tayorubhayorapyanityatvāt। nāpi viṣaye, mṛtpāṣāṇādirūpasya viṣayasya nityatvābhāvāt। na dvitīyaḥ, punastrividheti punaḥśabdena ityāśaṅkya āha-atra nityapṛthivyā ityādinā। evaṃ ca pṛthivīsāmānyasyaiva punastredhā vibhāgaḥ। nityapṛthivyāḥ
bhāvaḥ। nirvāhe api tejaḥ prakaraṇe punastrividhamiti na saṅgacchate। viṣayeṣvantarbhāvāsambhavāt। janyatvaghaṭitabhaumatvādeḥ nityayejasyasaṃbhavāt। ataḥ anityapṛthivyā evāyaṃ vibhāgaḥ।
matamāha - kecittu iti। kecidityasvarasodbhāvanam। tadbījaṃ tu punaḥśabdāsvārasyāt nānityapṛthivyā ayaṃ vibhāgaḥ। na ca sa vācyam। vākyādau prayuktasya punaḥśabdasya vākyālaṅkāratāyāḥ kutrāpyadṛṣṭacaratvāt।
vākyālaṅkāratāyāstatra tatra dṛṣṭatvāt। kiṃ ca punaśśabdasya prakārāntaraparatvameva annambhaṭṭasyāpi saṃmatam। aprakārāntareṇa vibhajate - punastrividheti' ityavataraṇikādānāt। na ca tejaḥprakaraṇe anupapattiriti vācyam। tatra bhaumādiśabdānāṃ
bhūmisambandhi ityādyevārthaḥ, na tu bhūmijanyamiti। tathā ca viṣayāntarbhāvo yujyata iti। śarīramiti śarīralakṣaṇam। ātmapadottaraṣaṣṭhyāḥ samavetatvamarthaḥ। tasya bhoge anvayaḥ। bhogo nāma sukhaduḥkhānyatarasākṣātkāraḥ।
āyatanamavacchedakam। tathā ca bhavati। idaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ hastapādādau śarīrāvayave ativyāptam। sukhaduḥkhānyatarasākṣātkārasyotpādāt। ataḥ antyāvayavitve satīti viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। antyāvayavitvaṃ nāma dravyānārambhakatve sati
avayavitvam। hastādeḥ śarīrārambhakatayā satyantābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। tadāha - sukhaduḥkhānyatarasākṣātkārāvacchedakamiti yāvadityādinā pṛthivītvādinā saṅkarāditi। śarīratvaṃ vihāya pṛthivītvaṃ ghaṭādau, pṛthivītvaṃ vihāya śarīratvaṃ jalīyādiśarīre।
ubhayoḥ pārthivaśarīre samāveśāt saṅkara iti bhāvaḥ। tathā indriyatvaṃ na jātiriti। pṛthivītvaṃ vihāya indriyatvaṃ rasanādau । indriyatvaṃ vihāya pṛthivītvaṃ ghaṭādau, ubhayoḥ indriyatvaṃ na jātiriti bhāvaḥ। ātmādāvativyāptivāraṇāya
satyantamiti। ātmanyapyastīti tatrātivyāptiḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya satyantam। tadāśrayatvasyaivātmani sattvāt nātivyāptiḥ ityarthaḥ। tadanāśrayatvamityavyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya śabdetareti
viśeṣaṇam। viśeṣaguṇe udbhūteti viśeṣaṇādāne cakṣurādau tadāśrayatvamevāstītyavyāptiḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya udbhūteti viśeṣaṇam। viśeṣapadamanupādāya cakṣurādīndriyeṣvasabhbhavaḥ syāt; tadvāraṇāya viśeṣapadam।
viśeṣapadānupādāne api saṃyogo nopādātu śakyate। ityāśaṅkyāha - udbhūtatvaṃ na jātirityādinā। udbhūtatvaṃ iti sāṃkaryāt udbhūtatvaṃ na jātiḥ। śuklatvādivyāpyaṃ udbhūtatvaṃ nānaiva। tathā ca śuklatvaṃ vihāya
udbhūtatvaṃ nāstīti na saṃkara iti vācyam। udbhūtatvasya kāraṇamityevamanugatakāryakāraṇabhāvasya bhaṅgaprasaṅgāt। ataḥ śuklādibhedena tadvṛtti anudbhūtatvaṃ nānā। anudbhūtatvābhāvakūṭavattvameva codbhūtatvam। tadeva ca lakṣaṇe
niveśitam। tacca sayoge apyasti। saṃyogo hi nānudbhūta iti anudbhūtatvābhāvakūṭavattvasya tatra sattvāt। tathā ca viśeṣapadamiti bhāvaḥ। kālādāvativyāptivāraṇāya viśeṣyadalamiti।
śabdetarodbhūtaviśeṣaguṇānāśrayatvamastīti ativyāptiḥ syāt। nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ iti bhāvaḥ। manassaṃyoge jñānakāraṇeti viśeṣaṇasya prayojanamaha - tatraiveti। kālasya vibhutayā vibhutvasya ativyāptivāraṇāya jñānakāraṇetyuktam। kālānuyogikasya
manassaṃyogasya jñānakāraṇatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। prayojanamāha - prācīnamata iti। manaḥpadamanupādāya tadāśrayatvasya indriyāvayave sattvāt tatra ativyāptiḥ। navīnamate indriyāvayave ativyāptiḥ na sambhavati। tathāpi kāle rūpaṃ nāstīti
cakṣussaṃyogaḥ tadāśrayatvaṃ kāle astītyativyāptiḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya manaḥpadam। tathā sati viṣayendriyāvayavasaṃyogasya vā pūrvoktātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। pūrvaṃ satyantānupādāne ātmani ativyāptirityuktam। sā ca
niruktodbhūtatveti। anudbhūtatvābhāvakūṭavattvarūpaṃ yat udbhūtatvaṃ tadāśrayetyarthaḥ। śabdetaretyādigurutaraviśeṣaṇamiti śaṅkate - na ceti। samādhatte - tathā satīti। ātmānyatve sati
carmaṇyativyāptiḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya śabdetaretyādigurutaraṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ deyamityarthaḥ। AnTs śitasparśavatya āpaḥ । tā dvividhāḥ nityā anityāś ca । ntyāḥ paramāṇurūpāḥ । anityāḥ kāryarūpāḥ । punas trividhāḥ śarīrendriyaviṣayabhedāt । śarīraṃ varuṇaloke । indriyaṃ rasagrāhakaṃ rasanaṃ jihvāgravarti । viṣayaḥ saritsamudrādiḥ ।। āpaḥ। nityā anityāśceti। nityāḥ paramāṇurūpāḥ।
anityāḥ kāryarūpāḥ। punastrividhāḥ - śarīraindriya - viṣayabhedāt। śarīraṃ varuṇaloke। indriyaṃ rasagrāhakaṃ rasanam। tacca jihvāgravarti। viṣayaḥ saritsamudrādiḥ। śīteti। utpannavinaṣṭajale avyāptivāraṇāya
śītasparśasamānādhikaraṇadravyatvāparajātimattvaṃ vivakṣitam। aśītaṃ nātivyāptiḥ। anyatsarvaṃ pūrvarītyā vyākhyeyam। śītasparśasamānādhikaraṇeti। tatra viśeṣaṇaprayojanaṃ pūrvoktarītyā ūhyam। jalatvajātisiddhistu
snehajanakatāvacchedakatayeti dhyeyam। anyatsarve pūrvarītyeti। niveśya pṛthivīnirūpaṇoktarītyerthaḥ। ūhyamiti। dravyatvavyāpyajātimattvamātroktau dravyatvavyāpyapṛthivītvajātimatyāṃ pṛthivyāmativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya
śītasparśasamānādhikaraṇeti jātiviśeṣaṇam। dravyatvavyāpyeti। dravyatvavyāpyatvaṃ ca dravyatvanyūnavṛttitvam na tu tacchūnyāvṛttitvam। ato dravyatvajātimādāya noktadoṣa iti bhāvaḥ। snehajanakatāvacchedakatayeti।
jalatvajātisiddhirityarthaḥ। AnTs uṣṇasparśavat tejaḥ । tad dvividhaṃ nityam anityaṃ ca । niyyaṃ paramāṇurūpam । anityaṃ kāryarūpam । punas trividhaṃ śarīrendriyaviṣayabhedāt । śarīram ādityaloke । indriyaṃ rūpagrāhakaṃ cakṣuḥ kṛṣṇatārāgravarti । viṣayaś caturvidhaḥ । bhaumadivyaudaryākarajabhedāt । bhaumaṃ vahnyādikam । abindhanaṃ divyaṃ vidyudādi । bhuktasya pariṇāmahetur audaryam ākarajaṃ suvarṇādi ।। tejaḥ। tat dvividham - nityam anityam ceti। nityaṃ paramāṇurūpam। punastrividham - śarīraindriya
- viṣayabhedāt। indriyaṃ rūpagrāhakaṃ cakṣuḥ। tacca kṛṣṇatārāgravarti। bhauma-divya-udarya-ākaraja-bhedāt। divyamabindhanaṃ vidyudādi। bhuktasya pariṇāmaheturudaryam। ākarajaṃ suvarṇādi।
tejaso lakṣaṇamāha - uṣṇasparśavaditi। nātivyāptiḥ। viṣayaṃ vibhajate - bhaumeti। pārthivaṃ pītatvāt gurutvāt haridrāvat iti cet - na। rūpavattayā vāyvādiṣu anantarbhāvāt taijasatvasiddhiḥ।
pratibandhādanupalabdhiḥ। tasmāt suvarṇaṃ taijasamiti siddham। abindhanamiti। adbhiḥ indhanaṃ dīpanaṃ yasya tadityarthaḥ। bhuktasyeti। bhuktasyaudanādeḥ pariṇāmaḥ paripākaḥ, tatra heturityarthaḥ। ākarajamiti। ākaraḥ khaniḥ tatra jātamityarthaḥ।
vyavasthāpayituṃ śaṅkate - dīpikāyām nanviti। pārthivatvasādhakaṃ pītatvahetumuktvā taijasatvābhāvasādhakaṃ hetumāha - gurutvāditi। etena suvarṇarūpatejasi vijātīyapītarūpaṃ svīkriyate। apītaṃ suvarṇaṃ' ityabādhitapratyakṣapratītibalāt। evaṃ ca taijasatvasya
nirbādhatayā pṛthivītvaṃ na sidhyatīti kasyacit bhrāntirnirastā। gurutvasyāpratyakṣatvena tathā vaktumaśakyatvāditi dik। suvarṇasya - atyantānaleti। anumānaprayogastu tannaivam। jalamadhyasthaghṛtādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya asati
pratibandhaka iti। agnisaṃyogāsamānādhikaraṇadravatvavatighṛtādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya atyantānalasaṃyoge sati iti। dravadravyāntarasiddhāviti। aatyantānalasaṃyogī pītimāśrayaḥ jalamadhyasthaghṛtādivat' ityanumānena tatsiddhirdraṣṭavyā।
jalādikamādāyānumānaparyavasānaṃ vārayati - naimittiketi। nanu anupapannaṃ ityata āha - tasyeti। doṣavidhayetyādiḥ। sādhitam। tatra pītatvarūpeṇa aikena hetunaiva
ityāśaṅkyāha - pārthivatvasādhakamiti। tathā ca pītatvaṃ pārthivatvasādhakam। gurutvaṃ tu tejobhinnatvasādhakam। na ca dvitīyānumānaṃ vyarthamiti vācyam। paramatanirākaraṇapūrvakaṃ dvitīyānumānasya āvaśyakatvāditi bhāvaḥ।
anumānāntarapraṇayanavaiyarthyam। ekenaiva pītatvahetunā pārthivatvataijasabhinnatvayoḥ sādhanasambhavāditi cet - atrāhuḥ। asuvarṇaṃ pārthivam' ityādyanumāne suvarṇatvaṃ na pakṣatāvacchedakam। pārthivatvāsiddhiprasaṅgāt। tadarthamanumānāntarapraṇayane gauravācca।
nāpi rajatasādhāraṇaṃ hiraṇyatvaṃ pakṣatāvacchedakam। tathā sati bhāgāsiddhiprasaṅgāt। tasmāt gurutvahetvanusaraṇam। gurutvaṃ tu rajate apyastīti na bhāgāsiddhiriti। pūrvapakṣiṇaḥ suvarṇasya pārthivatvasādhane na nirbharaḥ। suvarṇe
iti pūrvapakṣasyāprasarāt। aākarajaṃ suvarṇādi' iti granthakṛtā pūrvapakṣasyaiva yuktatvāt। ata eva atasmāt suvarṇaṃ taijasam' iti siddhānte upasaṃhāro api saṅgacchate। evaṃ ca suvarṇasya tejobhinnatvamapyatra pūrvapakṣiṇā siṣādhayiṣitam। suvarṇasya
tatra pītatvasyopapatteḥ। ato gurutvāditi dvitīyahetūpanyāsaḥ। gurutvamupapadyata iti vaktumaśakyam। ato gurutvaṃ tejobhinnatvasādhane samarthamiti bhāvo atra pratīyate। spaṣṭīkṛtaśca ayaṃ bhāvaḥ aetane' ityādigrantheneti।
atyantānalasaṃyoge satītyādi। ayamarthaḥ - ghṛtādipṛthivyāṃ yat dravatvaṃ tasyātyantāgnisaṃyoge sati nāśo bhavati। tena kāryakāraṇabhāvo labhyate। paraṃ tu tulamadhyasthaghṛtadravatvasya pratibandhake' iti viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। tena
hetuḥ iti kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ phalati। jalamadhyasthaghṛte tu jalasya pratibandhakatvāt na dravatvanāśaḥ। tathā ca dravatvanāśarūpakāryābhāva iti na pūrvoktānvayavyabhicāraḥ। suvarṇe dravatvaṃ tannāśo na bhavati। ataḥ taddravatvanāśapratibandhakaṃ kiñcit
dravyaṃ suvarṇe astīti vaktavyam। tathā ca suvarṇe bhāgadvayamaṅgīkāryam। tathā anaṅgīkāre suvarṇasya kṛtsnasyāpi pārthivatve tadgatadravatvaṃ naśyet। evaṃ ca atyantāgnisaṃyoge taijasatvaṃ sidhyatīti। na ca tādṛśadravyasya rūpavattvamasiddhamiti kathaṃ
tena hetunā vāyvādibhedaḥ sādhya iti vācyam। tasya rūpaśūnyatve āvaśyakatvāt ityāśayāt। vastuto naimittikadravatvavattvenaiva hetunā vāyvādibhedo api śakyaḥ sādhayitum। tathā ca tejastvena viśeṣaśabdaiḥ sāmānyaśabdaiśca vyavahriyata iti sidhyati।
āvaśyakaḥ। tatra suvarṇasthapārthivabhāgagatadravatvanāśarūpakāryābhāvaḥ nirvivādam। tatra tādṛśaviśiṣṭābhāvarūpaḥ kāraṇābhāvaḥ na viśeṣyābhāvāt, atyantāgnisaṃyogarūpasya viśeṣyasya tatra sattvāt। pratibandhakaṃ kiñcit dravadravyāntaraṃ tatrāstīti vaktavyam। tasyāpi
tathetyanavasthā syāt। ataḥ pratibandhakāntaraṃ vinā avinaśyaddravatvādeva tanna pṛthivī iti। ayaṃ dīpikāgranthaḥ padayoḥ svārasyāt। muktāvalyāṃ tu ajalamadhyasthamaṣīkṣodavat pratipāditaḥ। tanmate suvarṇasya taijasatvasādhakānumānamanyadeveti।
suvarṇasya pītimagurutvāśrayato atiriktatvamiti। suvarṇaśabdavācyasya bhāgaviśeṣasya pṛthivībhāgādatiriktatvamityarthaḥ। anumāne aprayojakaśaṅkāvāraṇāyeti। suvarṇaśabdavācyasya ityevaṃrūpamanukūlatarkamāhetyarthaḥ। asati pratibandhake ityasya
pratibandhakābhāvaviśiṣṭamityarthaḥ। tasya dravatve anvayaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca saṃyogasamavāyaghaṭita ekakālāvacchinnaikādhikaraṇavṛttitvarūpasāmānādhi karaṇyasambandhena। atyantāgnisaṃyogaviśiṣṭamityarthaḥ। anvayaśca tasya dravatve eva। jalamadhyasthaghṛtādau vyabhicāravāraṇāyeti।
anucchidyamānadravatvarūpahetusattvāditi bhāvaḥ। agnisaṃyogāsamānādhikaraṇadravatvavati ghṛtādāviti। śikyasthaghṛtādau ityarthaḥ। atyantānalasaṃyogītyādi। pītimāśrayatvamātrasya
tadvāraṇāya atyantānalasaṃyogīti pakṣaviśeṣaṇam। iti tadvāraṇāya pītimāśraya iti। dravadravyāntarasya apratibandhakatve dravatvanāśapratibandhaketi sādhyaviśeṣaṇam। jalamadhyasthaghṛtādau viśeṣaṇam। anumānaparyavasānamiti।
ajijñāsitārthaṃsiddhirūpamarthāntaraṃ vārayitumityarthaḥ। suvarṇe upalabdhiḥ syāt। yataḥ na tayoḥ suvarṇe upalabdhiḥ ataḥ suvarṇaṃ uṣṇasparśeti। vastutaḥ suvarṇe vidyamānayorapi uṣṇasparśaśuklarūpayoḥ dīpikāyāmuktam। tacca pratibandhakatvaṃ doṣavidhayā na tu tadvattābuddhiṃ
doṣavidhayetyādiriti। AnTs rūparahitasparśavān vāyuḥ । sa dvividho nityo anityaś ca । nityaḥ paramāṇurūpaḥ । anityaḥ kāryarūpaḥ । punas trividhaḥ śarīrendriyaviṣayabhedāt । indriyaṃ sparśagrāhakaṃ tvaksarvaśarīravarti । viṣayo vṛkṣādikampanahetuḥ ।। śarīrāntaḥsaṃcārī vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ । sa caiko apy upādhibhedāt prāṇāpānādisaṃjñā labhate ।। rūparahitasparśavān vāyuḥ। nityaḥ anityaśca iti। nityaḥ paramāṇurūpaḥ। anityaḥ kāryarūpaḥ। punastrividhaḥ
śarīra - indriya - viṣayabhedāt। indriyaṃ sparśagrāhakaṃ tvak। viṣayo vṛkṣādikampanahetuḥ vāyuḥ। śarīrāntassañcārī vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ। sa caiko api upādhibhedāt prāṇāpānādisaṃjñāṃ labhate।
rūparahiteti। ākāśādau ativyāptivāraṇāya sparśavāniti। pṛthivyādau ativyāptivāraṇāya rūparahiteti। prāṇasya kutrāntarbhāva ityata āha - śarīreti। eka eva prāṇaḥ sthānabhedāt prāṇāpānādiśabdaiḥ vyavahriyata ityarthaḥ।
sparśānumeyo vāyuḥ। kvacidāśritaḥ guṇatvāt rūpavat। na cāsya āśrayaḥ pṛthivī, udbhūtasparśaṃvatpārthivasya udbhūtarūpavattvaniyamāt। na jalatejasī, anuṣṇāśītasparśavattvāt। na vibhucatuṣṭayam,
sarvatropalabdhiprasaṅgāt। na manaḥ, paramāṇusparśasya atīndriyatvāt। tasmāt ya pratīyamānasparśāśrayaḥ sa vāyuḥ । pratyakṣasparśāśrayatvāt ghaṭavat iti cet - na। udbhūtarūpavattvasyopādhitvāt। ayatra dravyatve sati
sādhyavyāpakatvam। pakṣe sādhanāvyāpakatvam। na caivaṃ taptavāristhatejaso api apratyakṣatvāpattiḥ iṣṭatvāt। tasmāt rūparahitatvāt vāyuḥ apratyakṣaḥ। śarīreti iti।
tathā ca prāṇasya viṣaye antarbhāva iti bhāvaḥ। ahṛdi prāṇa' ityādikośoktasthānabhedādityarthaḥ। mukhanāsikābhyāṃ niṣkramaṇapraveśanāt prāṇaḥ। malādīnāmadhonayanāt apānaḥ। āhāreṣu pākārthaṃ vahneḥ samunnayanāt samānaḥ। ūrdhvanayanāt udānaḥ।
nāḍīmukheṣu vitananāt vyānaḥ। svamataṃ darśaṃyati - sparśānumeya iti। asya - upalabhyamānasparśasya āśrayaḥ pṛthivī na ca ityanvayaḥ। catuṣṭayamiti। idaṃ ākāśādipratyekabhedasādhanābhiprāyeṇa।
sarvatropalabdhiprasaṅgāditi। ākāśādīnāṃ vibhutvāditi bhāvaḥ। pratyakṣaḥ - bahirindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayaḥ। anudbhūtasparśāśraye tvagindriye vyabhicāravāraṇāya pratyakṣeti।
upādhitvāditi। tathā ca hetau upādhivyabhicāreṇa sādhyavyabhicāronnayanasambhavāt na pratyakṣatvasiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। nanu sādhyāvyāpakatvāt kathaṃ tasyopādhikatvamityata āha - yatreti। tathā ca pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpako ayaṃ upādhiriti bhāvaḥ।
apratyakṣatvāpattiriti। udbhūtarūpābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ। vibhāvapi pratyekaṃ taccatuṣṭayabhedasambhavenābhimatāsiddheḥ। api tu idamākāśādipratyekabhedasādhanābhiprāyeṇeti। tathā ca hetāviti। apratyakṣasparśāśrayatvaṃ
vivakṣitaḥ। nanu avāyuḥ bahirindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayaḥ sambhavati। upādheḥ udbhūtarūpasya sādhyavyāpakatvābhāvāt ityāśaṅkate - nanu tādṛśapratyakṣatvasyetyādinā। bahirindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvasyetyarthaḥ। pakṣaḥ vāyuḥ
ityarthaḥ। evaṃ ca dravyatvaviśiṣṭabahirindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ guṇādau nāsti tatra dravyatvarūpaviśeṣaṇābhāvāt। api tu dravye ghaṭādāvevāsti। tatra ca udbhūtarūpamastīti udbhūtarūpasya pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakatvādupādhitvamupapadyata iti। upādhirhi
sādhanāvacchinnasādhyavyāpaka iti trividhaḥ। tatra madhyamo ayamupādhiriti bhāvaḥ। evamiti vyākhyeyaṃ padam। tasya pratyakṣatvānaṅgīkāra iti। udbhūtarūpasya sādhyavyāpakasya pratyakṣatvābhāvasya siddheriti bhāvaḥ।
kāryarūpapṛthivyādicatuṣṭayasya utpattivināśakramaḥ kathyate। īśvarasya jāyate। tataḥ paramāṇudvayasaṃyoge sati dvyaṇukamutpadyate। tribhireva dvyaṇukaiḥ tryaṇukaṃ utpadyate। evaṃ caturaṇukādikrameṇa mahatī pṛthivī, mahatya
āpaḥ, mahattejaḥ, mahāvāyuḥ utpadyate। evamutpannasya kāryadravyasya ityevaṃ pṛthivyādināśaḥ। asamavāyikāraṇanāśāt dvyaṇukanāśaḥ। samavāyikāraṇanāśāt tryaṇukānāśa iti saṃpradāyaḥ। sarvatrāsamavāyikāraṇanāśāt dravyanāśa iti navīnāḥ।
ghaṭavat। tryaṇukāvayavo api sāvayavaḥ mahadārambhakatvāt kapālavat। yaḥ dvyaṇukāvayavaḥ sa eva paramāṇuḥ। sa ca nityaḥ, tasyāpi kāryatve anavasthāprasaṅgāt। sṛṣṭipralayasadbhāve adhātā yathāpūrvaṃ akalpayat' ityādi śrutireva pramāṇam।
mahāpralayaḥ' iti vivekaḥ। vārayati idānīmiti। pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayanirūpaṇānantaram ityarthaḥ। vdyaṇukanāśa ityasya paramāṇudvayasaṃyoganāśādityādiḥ। sarvatreti। janyadravyasāmānya ityarthaḥ। sarvatra ekarītirevocitā
iti bhāvaḥ। cākṣuṣadravyatvāditi। cākṣuṣatve sati dravyatvādityarthaḥ। rūpādau ātmani ca vyabhicāravāraṇāya viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe। na ca idaṃ aprayojakamiti
śaṅkyam। cākṣuṣaṃ prati kāraṇasya mahattvasya truṭāvapekṣitatayā saṅkṣepaḥ। yatkiciñjjanyadravyadhvaṃsasya idānīmapi sattvāt sarveti। nityadravyāṇāṃ dhvaṃsāsambhavāt kāryeti। paramāṇuniṣṭharūpādīnāṃ tadānīmapi sattvāt dravyeti। dhvaṃsānāṃ dhvaṃsāṃsaṃbhavena
mahāpralaye api sattvāt bhāvetīti dik। paramāṇupuñjasyaiveti। paramāṇusamūhasyaivetyarthaḥ। atiriktāvayavina iti। paramāṇubhinnasya avayavina ityarthaḥ। vibhāgakathanamanupapannamiti। anityasya pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayasyābhāvāt
iti bhāvaḥ। mūle cikīrṣāvaśāditi। sisṛkṣāvaśādityarthaḥ। tribhireva vdyaṇukairiti। dvābhyāṃ dvyaṇukābhyāṃ tryaṇukotpattiḥ na bhavati। tryaṇukamiti matvā evamuktam। kāryadravyasya saṃjihīrṣāvaśāditi।
kāryandravyaviṣayakeśvarakartṛkasaṃhārecchāvaśādityarthaḥ। asamavāyikāraṇanāśāditi। dvyaṇukasya asamavāyikāraṇaṃ yaḥ tasya nāśāt dvyaṇukasya nāśa ityarthaḥ। samavāyikāraṇanāśāt nāśāt tryaṇukanāśa ityarthaḥ। dvyaṇukasya tu
samavāyikāraṇanāśāt nāśo na vaktuṃ śakyate। samavāyikāraṇasya paramāṇoḥ nāśāsambhavāditi bhāvaḥ। prathamānumānaṃ dvyaṇukasādhakam, dvitīyānumānaṃ paramāṇusādhakamiti vivekaḥ। syāt। ataḥ cākṣuṣaṃ ca tat dravyaṃ ca cākṣuṣadravyaṃ tasya bhāvaḥ iti
tritvasaṃkhyāketi। trīṇi aṇūni yasya tat tryaṇukamiti vigrahaḥ। tathā ca tritvaṃsaṃkhyāviśiṣṭāṇvavayavakatvaṃ tryaṇukaśabdasya pravṛttinimittam। tatra tribhirdvyaṇukaiḥ tryaṇukotpattāveva saṃgacchata iti bhāvaḥ।
bhāvaḥ iti samāso atra vivakṣitaḥ। tena cākṣuṣatvaviśiṣṭadravyatvaṃ heturiti phalati। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyasambandhena। ātmani cākṣuṣatve sati dravyatvādityartha iti। cākṣuṣatvamātroktau iti tadvāraṇāya dravyatvopādānam। dravyatvamātroktau ātmani
vyabhicāra iti tadvāraṇāya dravyatvopādānam। dravyatvamātroktau cakṣurindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvarūpacākṣuṣatvopādānam। viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇe iti। viśeṣyaṃ dravyatvam। viśeṣaṇaṃ cākṣuṣatvam।
cedamaprayojakamiti। cākṣuṣadravyatvarūpaheturastu, tadvārakatarkābhāvādityarthaḥ। aprayojakam ityasya vyabhicāraśaṅkānivartakatarkaṃśūnyamityarthaḥ। tryaṇukarūpe pakṣe sāvayavatvaṃ nāsti cet cākṣuṣadravyatvarūpaheturapi na syāt।
tadaiva cākṣuṣatvaṃ tasya bhavet। tryaṇuke mahattvaṃ tu aṅgīkāryam। tathā ca sāvayavatvasya mahattvadvārā nedamanumānaṃ aprayojakam ityāśayaḥ। ityāśaṅkyāha - saṅkṣepa iti।
tadāśrayadvyaṇukākhyāṇuvastunaḥ avaśyāṅgīkaraṇīyatvāditi bhāvaḥ। mahāpralaya iti। mahāpralayānantaraṃ punaḥ sṛṣṭyanabhyupagamenedam। sarvaṃbhāvakāryadhvaṃsarūpo mahāpralaya eva na syāt ityavadheyam। avāntarapralayānantarasṛṣṭiviṣayeti teṣāmāśayaḥ। mahāpralaye api
sattvāditi। tathā ca sarvakāryāntargatadhvaṃsasya dhvaṃsābhāvāt bhāvapadamiti bhāvaḥ। AnTs śabdaguṇam ākāśam । tac caikaṃ vibhu nityaṃ ca ।। śabdaguṇakamākāśam। tacca ekam, vibhu, nityam ca।
śabdaguṇakamiti। nanu ākāśamapi pṛthivyādivannānā kiṃ? netyāha - taccaikamiti। bhede pramāṇābhāvāt ityarthaḥ। ekatvādeva sarvatra śabdopalabdheḥ vibhutvaṃ aṅgīkartavyamityāha- vibhviti। sarvamūrtadravyasaṃyogitvam vibhutvam। mūrtatvam
paricchinnaparimāṇavattvaṃ, kriyāvattvam vā। vibhutvādeva ātmavat nityaṃ ityāha - nityaṃ ceti। dyotanāya। ghaṭākāśo maṭhākāśa ityādivyavahārasyopādhikṛtatvena asādhakatvāt ākāśasya anekatve pramāṇaṃ netyāha - bheda iti।
ekatvāditi। ākāśasyetyādiḥ। nanvekatve api avibhutvaṃmastu ityata āha - sarvatreti। sarvadigavacchedenetyarthaḥ। paricchinnaparimāṇavattvamiti। yadi
paramāṇuṣu avyāptamidaṃ lakṣaṇamityucyate tadāpyāhakriyāvattvamiti। vastutastu lāghavamevottarakalpānusaraṇe bījam iti dhyeyam। maṭhākāśa ityādivyavahārāt ākāśe api bhedo astītyavagamyate। tathā ca bhede pramāṇābhāvāditi dīpikoktiḥ na saṅgacchate।
ākāśagataṃ bhedam। ataḥ sa na bhede pramāṇamiti samādhānaṃ abhiprayan āha - ghaṭākāśa iti। ghaṭamaṭhajñadirūpāvacchedakagatabhedānimittakatvenetyarthaḥ। asādhakatvāditi। ākāśabhedāsādhakatvādityarthaḥ।
aṇutaratveneti। utkarṣāśrayāṇuparimāṇavattvenetyarthaḥ। nāpakarṣāśrayatvam। api tu paramamahatparimāṇabhinnatvam, ākāśādicatuṣṭayānyatamāsamavetatvaṃ vā। tathā ca
paramāṇuṣvapi vartata iti na tatrāvyāptiḥ। ato iti। AnTs atītādivyavahārahetuḥ kālaḥ । sa caiko vibhur nityaś ca ।। atītādivyavahārahetuḥ kālaḥ। sa ca ekaḥ vibhuḥ nityaśca।
atīteti। sarvādhāraḥ kālaḥ sarvaṅkāryanimittakāraṇam। anāgatādiparigrahaḥ। atītatvaṃ ca vartamānadhvaṃsapratiyogitvam। śabdaprayogādhikaraṇakālavṛttivam। bhaviṣyatvaṃ ca vartamānaprāgabhāvapratiyogitvaṃ। atra sarvatra kālasya ghaṭakatayā
śabdaprayogarūpātītādivyavahāre hetutvaṃ tasya iti dhyeyam। na ca tādṛśavyavahāraḥ sūryaparispandopādhimādāya sambhavatīti vācyam। atiriktakālasvīkārāditi dik। kālikasambandhenetyādiḥ। atra vibhinnakālikayoḥ
nāvataratīti bhāvaḥ। avacchedakaḥ sūryaparispandaḥ taddhetukaḥ। tathā ca atīta ityasya śabdaprayogādhikaraṇasūryaparispandavṛttidhvaṃsapratiyogītyarthaḥ। vartamāna ityasya śabdaprayogādhikaraṇasūryaparispandavṛttirityarthaḥ।
śabdaprayogādhikaraṇasūryaparispandavṛttiprāgabhāvapratiyogītyarthaḥ। iti। samādhatte - anugatasyeti। ekarūpaḥ atītaḥ ityādiḥ vyavahāraḥ ekarūpaṃ viṣayaṃ vinā na sambhavati iti ekaḥ kālaḥ svīkaraṇīyaḥ। sūryaparispandastu anekaḥ। ataḥ kālaghaṭanayaiva atītatvādikaṃ
nirvācyaṃ iti bhāvaḥ। atītādiviṣayeṣu sākṣātsambandhena nāsti। ataḥ sūryaparispandavṛttitvaṃ ghaṭādervaktavyam। tadapekṣatā lāghavāt sākṣātsambandhaśālikālasvīkaraṇamevocitamityāśayenāha - digiti।
kālikasambandhenetyādiriti kathitam। sarvādhāratvamatra vivakṣitamiti bhāvaḥ। svāśrayeti। svaṃ ghaṭasya।
vibhinnakālikayoriti। kriyāyāḥ bhinnakālikayorādhārādheyabhāvavirahāt। sarvādhāratvamityatra kriyāyāmativyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। AnTs prācyādivyavahārahetur dik । sā caikā vibhvī nityā ca ।।
prācyādivyavahārahetuḥ dik। sā ca ekā vibhvī nityā ca। prācīti। digapi kāryamātranimittakāraṇam। pratīcyādiparigrahaḥ। udayācalasannihitamūrtāvacchinnā dik prācī। astācalasannihitamūrtāvacchinna dik pratīcī।
merusannihitamūrtāvacchinna dik udīcī। tadvyavahitamūrtāvacchinnā tu dakṣiṇā। AnTs[] jñānādhikaraṇam ātmā । sa dvividhaḥ paramātmā jīvātmā ca । tatreśvaraḥ sarvajñaḥ paramātmaika eva । jīvātmā pratiśarīraṃ bhinno vibhur nityaś ca ।। jñānādhikaraṇam ātmā। saḥ dvividhaḥ jīvātmā paramātmā ceti।
paramātmā eka eva। pratiśarīraṃ bhinnaḥ। - jñāneti। ātmānaṃ vibhajate - sa dvividha iti। - tatreti। nityajñānādhikaraṇatvam īśvaratvam। nanu
īśvarasadbhāve kiṃ pramāṇam? na tāvat pratyakṣam। taddhi bāhyaṃ āntaraṃ vā। nādyaḥ, arūpidravyatvāt। na dvitīyaḥ, ātmasukhaduḥkhādivyatiriktatvāt। nāpyanumānam, liṅgābhāvāt। nāpyāgamaḥ, tathāvidhāgamābhāvāt iti cet - na। aaṅkurādikaṃ
sakartṛkaṃ kāryatvāte ghaṭavat' ityanumānasyaiva pramāṇatvāt। upādānagocarāparokṣajñānacikīrṣākṛtimattvaṃ kartṛtvam। upādānaṃ samavāyikāraṇam। sakalaparamāṇvādisūkṣmadarśitvāt sarvajñatvam। ayaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvaṃvit' ityādyāgamo api tatra pramāṇam।
jīva iti। sukhādyāśrayatvaṃ jīvalakṣaṇam। nanu amanuṣyo aham', śarīrameva ātmā iti cet - na। śarīrasya ātmatve karapādādināśe śarīranāśāt ātmano api nāśaprasaṅgāt। nāpi spṛśāmi' ityanusandhānābhāvaprasaṅgāt। anyānubhūter'the
anyasyānusandhānāyogāt। tasmāt dehendriyavyatiriktaḥ jīvaḥ sukhaduḥkhādivaicitryāt pratiśarīraṃ bhinnaḥ। sarvaśarīravyāpisukhādyanupalabdhiprasaṅgāt। na madhyamaparimāṇavān। tathā sati anityatvaprasaṅgena kṛtahāna - akṛtābhyāgamaprasaṅgāt।
tasmāt nityaḥ vibhuḥ jīvaḥ। mūle jñānādhikaraṇamiti। samavāyena jñānavadityarthaḥ। tatra - tayormadhye। dīpikāyām nityajñānādhikaraṇatvamiti। na ca a vijñānaṃ ānandaṃ brahma' iti
śrutvā virodha iti vācyam। ānandapadasya ānandavadarthakatāyā vijñānavadarthakatāsvīkāreṇa avirodhāt। na ca ānandapadasyaiva tādṛśārthakatvamasiddhamiti vācyam। arśa ādyajantatvāṅgīkāreṇa tādṛśārthasiddheḥ। anyathā napuṃsakatvānupapatteḥ। atra ānandaḥ
abhārāpagame sukhī saṃvṛtto aham' itivat duḥkhābhāve upacaryate। navīnāstu nityasukhamīśvarasyāṅgīkurvanti ityalamadhikajalpanena। arūpidravyatvāditi। bāhyapratyakṣaṃ prati udbhūtarūpasya hetutvāditi bhāvaḥ। ātmasukhaduḥkhādīti। vijātīyātmamanassaṃyogasya
mānasapratyakṣahetoḥ īśvare abhāvāditi bhāvaḥ। na cedaṃ aprayojakamiti śaṅyam। aprayojakamiti śaṅkyam। aprayojakatvābhāvāditi dik। yadyapi kartṛtvaṃ kāraṇatvapradarśanāya tathoktiriti dhyeyam।
vidadhātvartho viśeṣarūpeṇa jñānam। lakṣaṇamāheti। svarūpamāhetyarthaḥ। mūle pratiśarīraṃ bhinna iti। na jīvabhedābhāvāt idamasaṅgatam। evaṃ kāyavyūhasthale apīti
vācyam। samānakālikāyogajadharmājanyaśarīrabhedena jīvabhedasyaiva vivakṣitatayā adoṣāt। evaṃ ca etaccharīrāvacchinnabhogavān rītyā pratiśarīraṃ jīvabhedaḥ sādhya ityalam। śarīrasyaiveti। anyathā
asaṅgatirityabhimānaḥ nāśaprasaṅgāditi। samavāyikāraṇanāśasya dravyanāśakatvāditi bhāvaḥ। bhūtakālikadarśanavati sambhavati cākṣuṣaspārśanavatorbhedāditi bhāvaḥ। anusandhānāyogāditi। anyathā caitreṇānubhūtasya vastunaḥ maitreṇa
smaraṇāpatteriti bhāvaḥ। sarvaśarīravyāpitvaṃ ātmano astu। tathāpi vibhutvāṅgīkāre prayojanābhāva ityata āha - na madhyameti। anityatvaprasaṅgeneti। yanmadhyamaparimāṇaṃ tadanityam iti vyāpteriti bhāvaḥ।
akṛtasyābhyāgamaḥ prāptiḥ tatprasaṅgādityarthaḥ। kartuḥ ātmana uttarajanmani asattvāt, akartuśca sattvāditi bhāvaḥ। aṇutvameva āstām, tāvatā noktadoṣaḥ। sūkṣmadīpasya iti cet - na। tathā sati kāyavyūhasthale
sukhādisākṣātkārānupapatteriti dik। jñānavaditi। kālikasambandhena jñānavati kāle ativyāptivāraṇāya samavāyeneti। sambandhaviśeṣāvacchinnādhāratāsūcanāyaiva adhikaraṇapadam। anyathā jñānavān ātmā ityeva vadet iti
bhāvaḥ। dīpikāyām - bāhmam - bahirindriyajanyam। āntaram - manojanyam। rūpavato dravyasyaiva bahirindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvāditi bhāvaḥ। ātmasukhaduḥkhādivyatiriktatvāditi। yasya jīvātmanaḥ svīyamanasā
mānasapratyakṣaṃ janayet। tajjīvātmatadīyasukhādivyatiriktaṃ tadīyamanassaṃyogajanyapratyakṣaviṣayo na bhavati। ataḥ īśvaraḥ liṅgābhāvāditi। īśvaravyāpyasya liṅgasyābhāvādīśvare nānumānaṃ pramāṇamiti bhāvaḥ।
jñānādhikaraṇatvaṃ na sambhavatīti śaṅkate - na ca nityamiti। samādhatte - ānandapadasyeti। ānandārthakasya ānandaśabdasya napuṃsaka ānandaśabdaḥ sampadyate। tathā ca ānandamityasya ānandavadityartha eva vaktavyaḥ। tatsamabhivyāhṛtaḥ vijñānaśabdaḥ vijñānavadarthaka eva yuktaḥ।
iti bhāvaḥ। upacaryate - lakṣaṇayā prayujyate। vijātīyātmamanassaṃyogasyeti। parātmavyāvṛttasya svātmamātravṛtteḥ manassaṃyogasyetyarthaḥ। na cedamaprayojakamiti।
nāstīti bhāvaḥ। na cedamaprayojakamiti। kāryatvarūpaheturastu tacchūnyamityarthaḥ। kāryatvāvacchinnaṃ pratīti। nanu sakartṛkatvaṃ hi kartṛjanyatvam। pakṣe tadabhāvo astu iti śaṅkāyāṃ yadi na। sādhyaṃ sakartṛkatvaṃ na kartṛjayatvarūpam। tathā sati kartṛtvasyaiva
janakatāvacchedakatvaṃ syāt। kartṛtvaṃ ca kṛtimattvarūpaṃ syāt। ataḥ kṛtijanyatvameva sakartṛkatvam। kṛtitvameva ityetādṛśakāryakāraṇabhāvāśyatarkābhidhānāt। ityatrāha - digiti।
ucitamiti bhāvaḥ। dīpikāyām upādānagocareti। upādānaṃ tadvattvaṃ kartṛtvamityarthaḥ। upādānagocaretyasya triṣvapyanvayāt। yadyapītyādi। ajānāti', aicchati', ayatate', akaroti' iti cikīrṣāṃ prati jñānaṃ kāraṇamiti jñāpanāya dīpikāyāṃ tritayamuktam।
sādhyaṃ tu kṛtijanyatvameveti bhāvaḥ। nanu ayaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvavit' punaruktirityāśaṅkyāha - vidadhātvartha iti। tathā ca sarvajñaśabdena sāmānyataḥ prameyatvādinā sarvaviṣayakajñānamucyate। sarvavitpadena ghaṭatvapaṭatvādinā viśeṣarūpeṇa sarvaviṣayakajñānamucyate। ato na
punaruktiriti bhāvaḥ। lakṣaṇam। tathā ca tasya mlasya ajīvasya lakṣaṇamāha' ityavataraṇaṃ na yuktam ityata āha - svarūpamāhetyartha iti। vaktavyaḥ। tathā ca bālayuvādiśarīrabhede satyapi tadavacchinna ātmā eka
eva। evaṃ saubhariprabhṛtīnāṃ ātmana ekatve api jīvo bhinna iti kathaṃ saṅgacchata iti śaṅkāgranthasyārthaḥ। kāyavyūhasthala iti। ekena jīvena anekaśarīrādhiṣṭhānasthala ityarthaḥ।
samānakāliketi। samānakālikānāṃ yogajadharmājanyānāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ bhedo yatra tatra jīvabheda ityeva mūle vivakṣitam। nātmabhedavyāpyatayā mūlābhipreta iti nānupapattiḥ। tathā ca iti ajīvastu pratiśarīraṃ bhinnaḥ' iti mūlārthaḥ। tādṛśaḥ
śarīrabhedaḥ caitramaitrādiśarīreṣu tatrātmabhedo astīti bhāvaḥ। evaṃ cetyādi। avacchedyatāsambandhena taccharīrabhinnaśarīravattvāditi hetuḥ pūraṇīyaḥ। anyathetyādi। aahaṃ manuṣya' ityādipratītyā ahamarthe ātmani
munaṣyatvādidharmāḥ prakāratayā bhāsante। śarīra eva manuṣyatvādayaḥ bhavanti। tasmāt śarīramevātmā ityavagamayati। yadi tu śarīrātiriktaḥ ātmā tarhi bhramarūpā syāt na pramātmiketi bhāvaḥ। anyathā -
śarīrātiriktasyātmanaḥ ahamarthatve। pratyayasyaivāsaṅgatiriti। tathā pratīteḥ pramātvānupapattirityarthaḥ। manuṣyaśabdasya ahamarthe manuṣyaśarīrāvacchinnatvamavagāhate। ataḥ śarīrātmatvasādhikā ityuktam।
bhūtakāliketi। bhūtakālikacākṣuṣapratyakṣāśrayavartamānakālikaspārśanapratyakṣāśrayayoraikyamavagamyate। iti bhāvaḥ। dīpikāyām anyānubhūta iti। nanu ityeva vaktavyam। na tvevamiti kathameṣa grantho yojanīya iti
cet - śrūyatām। uktapratyabhijñā yathā vā cākṣuṣapratyakṣaviṣayasyaiva spārśanapratyakṣaviṣayatvamapyavagāhate। tatra spārśanapratyakṣaviṣayatvāvagāhinītvakkartṛkapratyabhijñā na syāt। ata cākṣuṣaspārśanapratyakṣayorāśrayaḥ eko aṅgīkāryaḥ। sa ca svātmanaḥ
pravṛtteriti। prakāśikāyāṃ hānaṃ nāśa iti। kṛtsa karmaṇo nāśo nāma niṣphalatvam। karmakartuḥ phalānubhavaṃ vinaiva nāśāt। karmaṇyakṛta'pi abhyāgamaḥ - phalaprāptiḥ। phalānubhavitā karmakarturanya eveti tasya karmānuṣṭhānaṃ vinaiva tatphaprāptiriti bhāvaḥ। tadāha -
kartuḥā mana iti। prabhāprasaraṇāṅgīkārāditi। jñānarūpaprabhāyāḥ sarvaśarīravyāptyaṅgīkārāt ityarthaḥ। kāyavyūhasthale iti। na syāditi bhāvaḥ। tatprabhāprasaro aṅgīkriyate। ato nāktānupapatti
rityaśaṅkyāhadigiti। yathā ekagṛhāntarāropitadīpasya prabhā na prasarediti bhāvaḥ। AnTs sukhādyupalabdhisādhanam indriyaṃ manaḥ । tac ca pratyātmaniyatatvād anantaṃ paramāṇurūpaṃ nityaṃ ca ।। sukhādyupalabdhisādhanam indriyaṃ manaḥ। tacca
pratyātmaniyatatvāt anantaṃ paramāṇurūpaṃ nityaṃ ca। sukheti। sparśarahitatve sati kriyāyattvaṃ manaso lakṣaṇam। tadvibhajate - tacceti। ekaikasyātmana ekaikaṃ mana āvaśyakam ityātmanāṃ anekatvāt manaso apyanekatvamityarthaḥ।
madhyamaparimāṇavattve anityatvaprasaṅgādityarthaḥ। sparśarahitatve sati dravyatvāt, ākāśādivat' iti cet - na। jñānānutpattiprasaṅgaḥ। na ca vibhudvayasaṃyogaḥ asttviti vācyam। purītadvyatiriktasthale ātmamanassaṃyogasya sarvadā vidyamānatvāt।
nissarati tadā jñānotpattirityaṇutvasiddhiḥ। laghulakṣaṇamāha - sparśarahitatve satīti। bhāvaḥ। tathā ca tasya paramamahatparimāṇavattvena pūrvoktadoṣānavakāśa iti bhāvaḥ।
vibhudvayasaṃyogānabhyupagamāditi bhāvaḥ। tathā ca tasya paramamahatparimāṇavattvena pūrvoktadoṣānavakāśa iti bhāvaḥ। abhāvāditi। vibhudvayasaṃyogānabhyupagamāditi bhāvaḥ। jñānānutpattīti। bhāvakāryasyāsamavāyikāraṇajanyatvaniyamāditi
bhāvaḥ। vibhudvayasaṃyogo astviti। tasya nityatvena asamavāyikāraṇakriyādyasattve api na kṣatiriti bhāvaḥ। bījamāha - manassaṃyogādīti। asukhādisākṣātkārasādhanatvaṃ manaso tasyāpi sukhādisākṣātkārasādhanatvāt। tadvāraṇāya indriyatvaṃ
niveśitam। indriyatvaṃ va aśabdetare' tyādirūpamiti tadghaṭitaṃ uktamiti bhāvaḥ। "sādhanamityasya karaṇamityarthaḥ। gauravāt"iti tu nṛsiṃhaśāstriṇaḥ prāhuḥ। teṣāṃ
dīpikāyāṃ lakṣaṇāntarakaraṇam। uktaṃ ca taireva -"nyūnatāparihārāya svayaṃ manolakṣaṇamāha"iti। nanu vibhadvayasaṃyogaḥ katha bhavet? saṃyogaṃ prati kriyāyāḥ saṃyogasya ca hetutvāt। vibhunośca kriyāśūnyatvāt kriyājanyaḥ saṃyogo na sambhavati। avayavaśūnyatvāt saṃyogajasaṃyogo api na saṃbhavatītyatrāha - tasya nityatvenati।
kriyādītyatra ādiśabdena saṃyogo gṛhyate। tathā ca janyasaṃyogaṃ pratyeva kriyādeḥ hetutvaṃ na tvasaṃyoge ajatvavirodhāditi bhāvaḥ। AnTs cakṣurmātragrāhyo guṇo rūpam । tac ca śuklanīlapītaraktaharitakapiśacitrabhedāt saptavidhaṃ pṛthivījalatejovṛtti । tatra pṛthivyāṃ saptavidham । abhāsvaraśuklaṃ jale । bhāsvaraśuklaṃ tejasi ।। guṇo rūpam। tacca śukla - nīla-pīta - raktahirata - kapiśa -
citrabhedāt saptavidham। pṛthivījalatejāvṛtti। tatra pṛthivyāṃ saptavidham। abhāsvaraśuklaṃ jale। bhāsvaraśuklaṃ tejasi। cakṣuriti। saṅkhyādāvativyāptivāraṇāya mātrapadam। rūpatve ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇapadam। rūpaṃ vibhajate - tacceti।
avyāpyavṛttinīlādisamudāya eva citrarūpam iti cet - na। rūpasya vyāpyavṛttitvaniyamāt। nanu citrapaṭe avayavarūpasyaiva pratītirastviti cet - na। rūparahitatvena paṭasyāpratyakṣatvaprasaṅgāt। na ca rūpavatsamavetatvaṃ
pratyakṣatvaprayojakam, gauravāt। tasmāt paṭasya pratyakṣatvānupapattyā citrarūpasiddhiḥ। rūpasyāśrayamāha - pṛthivīti। āśrayaṃ vibhajya darśayati - tatreti। mātrapadamiti।
taditi dhyeyam। na caivamapi tvagagrāhyacakṣurgrāhyaguṇavibhājakadharmavattve paryavasānena adoṣāt। ata eva paramāṇurūpādau nāvayāptiriti bodhyam। evakāreṇātiriktacitrarūpavyavacchedaḥ।
daiśikavyāpyavṛttitvetyarthaḥ। ityākārakapratītiviṣayatvakalpanena ca gauravamiti। rūparahitatveneti। prasaṅgāditi। dravyacākṣuṣaṃ prati samavāyena rūpasya kāraṇatvāditi bhāvaḥ। rūpavatsamavetatvamiti।
spāśrayasamavetatvasambandhena rūpam। pratyakṣatvaprayojakamiti। pratyakṣaviṣayatvaprayojakamastu ityarthaḥ। sākṣātsambandhena kāraṇatvāpekṣayā gauravādityarthaḥ। tatprayojakatvamaṅgīkartavyam। evaṃ ca truṭeḥ cākṣuṣatvānupapattirapi
draṣṭavyā। pratyakṣatvānupapattyeti। etena citrarūpavat citraraso api sidhyediti śaṅkānirastār। davayalaukikarāsanasya aprasiddhyā tadanupapattyabhāvena na citrarasāṅgīkāra iti saṅkṣepaḥ। cakṣurmātragrāhyatvaṃ rūpe asambhavi। cakṣuritarāgrāhyatve sati cakṣurgrāhyatvaṃ
hi cakṣurmātragrāhyatvam। jñānasāmānye manasaḥ kāraṇatvāt cakṣuritarāgrāhyatvasya rūpe abhāvāditi śaṅkate - yadyapīti। cakṣuritarāgrāhyatvaṃ cakṣuritarajanyapratyakṣāviṣayatvam। cakṣurgrāhyatvaṃ cakṣurindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvam। samādhatte - tathāpīti।
cakṣuritarapadena tvagindriyaṃ vivakṣitam। tathā ca cakṣurmātragrāhyatvam। asti cedaṃ rūpe iti nāsambhava iti bhāvaḥ। cakṣurindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvāt। tadupādāne tu saṅkhyāyāḥ nātivyāptiḥ। atīndriye dharmādāvativyāptivāraṇāya viśeṣyam। na
caivamapīti। prabhābhittisaṃyogasya tvagindriyāgrāhyatvāt cakṣurgrāhyatvācceti bhāvaḥ। tvagindriyajanyapratyakṣāviṣayaḥ lakṣaṇam। guṇavibhājakadharmaḥ rūpatvajātiḥ। sā ca tvagagrāhyā cakṣurgrāhyā tadindriyagrāhyau iti nyāyāt। rūpatvavattvaṃ ca rūpe astīti
lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। prabhābhittisaṃyoge vighamānaḥ saṃyogatvam। sa ca na tvagagrāhyo bhavati ghaṭapaṭasaṃyogādau nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। etādṛśajātighaṭitalakṣaṇakaraṇe paramāṇurūpe avyāptivāraṇamiti prayojanamitsayāha - ata eveti।
paramāṇugatarūpasya atīndriyatayā tatra cakṣūrgrāhyatvābhāvāt। avyāptiḥ। yathoktajātighaṭitalakṣaṇe tu paramāṇurūpe vidyamānaḥ guṇavibhājakadharmaḥ rūpatvam। sa tu ghaṭarūpe cakṣurgrāhya eva। tathā ca bhāvaḥ। nanu utpattikṣaṇe ghaṭādau rūpābhāvena rūpasya
ityasaṅgatamityata āha - daiśikavyāpyavṛttitveti। rūparahitatvena ityasaṅgatam ityata āha - samavāyenetayāditi। bhāvaḥ। nanu pratyakṣatvaṃ pratyakṣajñānavṛtti। pratyakṣajñāne ca pratyakṣaviṣayatvaprayojakamiti। pratyakṣatvapadamatra
pratyakṣaviṣayatvārthakamiti bhāvaḥ। viṣayatāsambandhena dravyapratyakṣaṃ prati svāśrayasamavetatvasambandhena rūpaṃ kāraṇam। paṭe samavāyena rūpābhāve api vāśrayasamavetatvasambandhena tanturūpaṃ tatra vartate। ataḥ tasya pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ bhavati। tasmāt citrarūpaṃ māstu ityāśayaḥ।
svasamavāyisamavetasamevatasamavatatvasambandheneti। kapālāvayavāḥ, tatsamavetatvaṃ kapāle tatsamavetatvaṃ ghaṭe। truṭeḥ cākṣuṣatvānupapattiriti। paramāṇugatarūpasya tryaṇuke paramāṇoravayave satyeva tadrūpasya uktasambandhena tryaṇuke sambhavāt।
cākṣuṣapratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ na syāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu citro rasa iti pratītyā atiriktacitrarasiddhirityata āha - saṅkṣepa iti। atiriktacitrarasatatprāgabhāvadhvaṃsādikalpane gauravāditi bhāvaḥ। AnTs rasanagrāhyo guṇo rasaḥ । sa ca madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭukaṣāyatiktabhedāt ṣaḍvidhaḥ । pṛthivyāṃ ṣaḍvidhaḥ ।।
rasaḥ। sa ca madhura - amla - lavaṇa - kaṭu - kaṣāya - tiktabhedāt ṣaḍvidhaḥ। tatra pṛthivyāṃ ṣaḍvidhaḥ। jale madhura eva। svāśrayeti। svaṃ
tanturūpaṃ tasyāśrayaḥ tantuḥ tatsamavetatvaṃ paṭasya। rasaneti। rasatve ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇapadam। rasasyāśrayamāha pṛthivīti। āśrayaṃ vibhajya darśayati - tatreti। rasatva iti।
rasanagrāhyaguṇavibhājakopādhimattve tātparyam। evaṃ gandhalakṣaṇe api। rasanagrāhyeti। rasanendriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayo yaḥ guṇavibhājako dharmaḥ tadvattvaṃ rasalakṣaṇam। phalādirase rasatvajātiḥ ayo guṇaḥ' bhāvaḥ। evaṃ gandhalakṣaṇe apīti। ghrāṇagrāhyaguṇavibhājakopādhimattvaṃ
gandhalakṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। AnTs ghrāṇagrāhyo guṇo gandhaḥ । sa ca dvividhaḥ surabhirasurabhiś ca । pṛthivīmātravṛttiḥ । gandhaḥ। sa dvividhaḥ - surabhiḥ asurabhiśceti। pṛthivīmātravṛtti। ghrāṇeti। gandhatve ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇapadam।
AnTs tvagindriyamātragrāhyo guṇo saparśaḥ । sa ca trividhaḥ śitoṣṇānuṣṇāśītabhedāt । pṛthivyaptejovāyuvṛttiḥ । uṣṇas tejasi । anuṣṇāśītaḥ pṛthivīvāyvoḥ ।। tvagindriyamātragrāhyo guṇaḥ sparśaḥ। saḥ trividhaḥ - śīta-uṣṇa-anuṣṇāśītabhedāt। pṛthivyaptejovāyuvṛttiḥ। tatra śītalaṃ jale। anuṣṇāśītaḥ pṛthivīvāyyoḥ।
tvagiti। sparśatve ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇapadam। saṃyogādāvativyāptivāraṇāya mātrapadam। mātrapadamiti। cakṣuragrāhyatvagindriyagrāhyaguṇavibhājakopādhimattvamiti phalitor'thaḥ।
paramāṇugatasparśe avyāptiḥ। tasyātīndriyatayā tvagindriyagrāhyatvābhāvādityāśaṅkyāha - cakṣuragrāhyeti। guṇavibhājako dharmaḥ tadvattvaṃ sparśasya lakṣaṇam। ghaṭādisparśeṣu paramāṇugatasparśe apyastīti samanvayaḥ। tvagindriyagrāhyaṃ
saṅkhyātvamādāya saṅkhyāyāṃ ativyāptivāraṇāya cakṣuragrāhyetyuktam। dharmādharmādiṣvativyāptivāraṇāya tvagindriyagrāhyetyuktam। guṇavibhājaketyupādhiviśeṣaṇam। guṇatvaṃ tu na guṇavibhājakamiti bhāvaḥ।
AnTs rūpādicatuṣṭayaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pākajam anityaṃ ca । anyatrāpākajaṃ nityam antyaṃ ca । nityagataṃ nityam । anityagatam anityam ।। pṛthivyāṃ pākajaṃ anityam। anyatra apākajaṃ nityamanityaṃ ca। nityagataṃ nityam। pākajamiti। pākaḥ
tejassaṃyogaḥ। tena pūrvayapaṃ naśyati rūpāntaramutpadyata ityarthaḥ। tatra paramāṇuṣveva pākaḥ na dvyaṇukādau। āmanikṣipte dhaṭe raktaghaṭotpattiḥ। tatra paramāṇavaḥ samavāyikāraṇam। tejassaṃyogaḥ asamavāyikāraṇam। adṛṣṭādikaṃ nimittakāraṇam। dvyaṇukādirūpe
asamavāyikāraṇamiti pīlupākavādino vaiśeṣikāḥ। pūrvaghaṭasya rūpāntarotpattiḥ iti piṭharapākavādino naiyāyikāḥ। ata eva pārthivaparamāṇurūpādikaṃ anityamityarthaḥ। jalādāvityarthaḥ। nityagatamiti। paramāṇugatamityarthaḥ। anityagatamiti।
dvyaṇukādigatamityarthaḥ। rūpādicatuṣṭayaṃ udbhūtaṃ pratyakṣam। anudbhūtamapratyakṣam। udbhūtatvaṃ pratyakṣatvaprayojako dharmaḥ। tadabhāvaḥ anudbhūtatvam। iti। paramāṇuṣveva pūrvarūpaparāvṛttyādijanakatejassaṃyoga
ityarthaḥ। evakāravyavacchedyaṃ vdyaṇukādāviti। āmanikṣipte ghaṭa iti। ghaṭe āmanikṣipte sati śyāmaghaṭanāśe paramāṇuṣu rūpāntarotpattāvityanvayaḥ। tatra paramāṇurūpe। avayavinipākānaṅgīkārādāha - kāraṇarūpamiti।
teṣu kriyā jāyate। tatayo vibhāgaḥ, tata ārambhakasaṃyoganāśe sati kriyāvibhāgādikrameṇa yathāsthitaṃ aparāvayaviparyantamutpattiriti। avayavinyapi pākasvīkāra ucitaḥ। ata eva aso ayaṃ ghaṭaḥ' iti pratyābhijñāpi saṅgacchate। anantāvayavināśādyakalpanena lāghavaṃ ceti।
hetutāyāṃ vyabhicāra iti vācyam। kāryatāvacchedakakoṭau vaijātyaniveśanena vyabhicāravāraṇasambhavāt। anyatreti - jalādāvityartha iti। yadyapi rūpādicatuṣṭayaṃ jalādau bādhitam, tathāpi yathāyogyamanvaye tātparyam। udbhūtatvaṃ
jātiḥ। na ca śuklatvādinā sāṅkaryam। guṇasāṅkaryaṃ na doṣa iti navīnamatābhiprāyako ayaṃ grantha iti na doṣaḥ। śuklatvādivyāpyamanudbhūtatvaṃ nānā। tadabhāvakūṭavattvameva udbhūtatvamityāhuḥ।
pūrvarūpaparāvṛttyādīti। ādipadena rūpāntarotpattiḥ gṛhyate। tatreti vyākhyeyaṃ padam। tasya vyākhyānaṃ paramāṇurūpa iti। paramāṇugate rūpe ityarthaḥ। nanu pākānaṅgīkārāditi। pīlupākavādivaiśeṣikamate avayavini
tatra rūpāntaraṃ prati pākasyāsamavāyikāraṇatvaṃ na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। yāvadavayavināśa iti। antyāvayaviparyantaṃ nāśa ityarthaḥ। ārambhakasaṃyogetyādi। dvyaṇukādyārambhako yaḥ paramāṇusaṃyogaḥ kriyā tajjanakatva ityarthaḥ। vaijātyaniveśaneneti।
avayavarūpaṃ āśrayanāśaśca heturiti bhāvaḥ। nityamanityaṃ ca' iti paramamūlam। anyatra ityasya jalādāvityarthaḥ। pūrvavākyāt rūpādicatuṣṭayamityanuvartane। tathā ca jalādau vidyamānaṃ rūpādicatuṣṭayaṃ apākajamityartho labhyate।
tadetadasaṅgatam। jalādau rūpādicatuṣṭayābhāvāt। jale yadyapītyādinā। yathāyogyamanvaya iti। rūpādicatuṣṭayamityasya rūpādicatuṣṭayaghaṭakamityarthaḥ। tadghaṭakaṃ ca trikaṃ dvayaṃ ekaṃ ca bhavatīti nānupapattiriti bhāvaḥ।
AnTs ekatvādivyavahārahetuḥ saṃkhyā । navadravyavṛttir ekatvādiparārdhaparyantā । ekatvaṃ nityam anityaṃ ca । nityagataṃ nityam anityagatam anityam । dvitvādikaṃ tu sarvatrānityam eva ।। ekatvādivyavahārahetuḥ saṅkhyā। ekatvādiparārdhaparyantā। ekatvaṃ nityagataṃ nityam। anityagatamanityam। dvitvādikaṃ tu sarvatrānityameva।
eketi। tu sarvatrānityameveti। hetubhūtāpekṣābuddhināśena dvitvādināśāditi bhāvaḥ। AnTs mānavyavahārakāraṇaṃ parimāṇaṃ । tac caturvidham । aṇu mahad dīrghaṃ hrasvaṃ ceti ।।
mānavyavahārāsādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ parimāṇam। taccaturvidham - aṇu-mahat-dīrghaṃ-hrasvaṃ ceti। - māneti। parimāṇaṃ vibhajate - tacceti। bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ। aṇutvaṃ mahatvaṃ dīrghatvaṃ hrasvatvaṃ cetyarthaḥ।
vibhajanamasaṅgatam। ataḥ dīpikāyām bhāvapradhāna iti। bhāvapradhāno nirdeśa iti। aṇumahadādayaḥ śabdāḥ mūle dharmapradhānakāḥ। tathā ca teṣāṃ śabdānāṃ aṇutvaṃ mahattvamityādiparimāṇarūpaguṇā evārtha iti nānupapattiḥ। tadāha -
parimāṇasyeti। AnTs pṛthagvyavahārakāraṇaṃ pṛthagtvaṃ ।। pṛthagvyavahārāsādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ pṛthaktvam। pṛthagiti। aidaṃ asmāt pṛthak' iti vyavahārakāraṇaṃ
pṛthaktvamityarthaḥ। AnTs saṃyuktavyavahārahetuḥ saṃyogaḥ ।। saṃyuktavyavahārahetuḥ saṃyogaḥ। saṃyukteti। aimau saṃyuktau' iti vyavahāraheturityarthaḥ।
saṅkhyādilakṣaṇe sarvatra। dikkālādau ativyāptivāraṇāya asādhāraṇeti viśeṣaṇīyam। karmajaḥ saṃyogajaśceti। ādyo hastakriyayā hastapustakasaṃyogaḥ। dvitīyo hastapustaka saṃyogāt kāyapusatakasaṃyogaḥ। avyāpyavṛttiḥ
saṃyogaḥ। svātyantābhāvasamānādhikaraṇatvaṃ avyāpyavṛttitvam। asādhāraṇetīti। kālādeḥ sādhāraṇakāraṇatvena tatra nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। svātyantābhāveti। svapratiyogitva -
svasāmānādhikaraṇyobhayasambandhena abhāvavattvamiti niṣkarṣaḥ। svapratiyogitveti। svaṃ kapisaṃyogābhāvaḥ, tatpratiyogitvaṃ ca kapisaṃyoge। tathā ca tasyāvyāpyavṛttitvam। svapratiyogitvasambandhena ghaṭābhāvaviśiṣṭasya
ghaṭasyāvyāpyavṛttitvavāraṇāya svasāmānādhikaraṇyaniveśaḥ। ghaṭasya ghaṭātyantābhāva sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ nāstīti na doṣaḥ। paṭasyāvyāpyavṛttitvavāraṇāya svapratiyogitvaniveśaḥ। paṭasya ghaṭābhāvapratiyogitvāt na doṣaḥ।
AnTs saṃyoganāśako guṇo vibhāgaḥ ।। guṇaḥ vibhāgaḥ। saṃyogeti। kālādau ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇa iti। rūpādau ativyāptivāraṇāya saṃyoganāśaka iti।
karmajaḥ, vibhāgajaśceti। ādyaḥ hastakriyatā hastapustakāvibhāgaḥ। dvitīyaḥ hastapusatakavibhāgāt kāyapustakavibhagāḥ। itīti। na ca tathāpi saṃyoge ativyāptiḥ। tasya pratiyogividhayā nāśaṃ prati kāraṇatvāditi vācyam।
kecit। iti niṣkarṣaḥ। etattatparyagrāhakaṃ guṇapadamityāhuḥ। vibhāga iti। ayamapyavyāpyavṛttiriti bodhyam। ādyatvamiha
svasamānādhikaraṇapatanapratiyogikadhvaṃsāsamānakālikatvam। nirāsa iti bhāvaḥ। saṃyāga iti। saṃyoganāśakatvaṃ hi saṃyoganāśajanakatvam। dhvaṃsaṃ kāraṇam। tathā ca saṃyoganāśajanakatvaṃ saṃyoge astīti
ativyāptirityarthaḥ। pratiyogitvenetyarthaḥ। pratiyogitāsambandhānavacchinneti। pratiyogitāsambandhena nāśaṃ prati nāstīti na saṃyoge ativyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। pare tviti।
vivakṣitam। saṃyoge tu sattve api uktavidhakāraṇatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। etattātparyagrāhakamiti। samavāyasambandhāvacchinnakāraṇatātātparyadyotakamityarthaḥ।
ādyatvamiheti। tadbhinnatvaṃ ādyatvamityarthaḥ। dvitīyapatanādi tadbhinnatvaṃ cādyapatane astīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। AnTs parāparavyavahārāsādhāraṇakāraṇe paratvāparatve । pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayamanovṛttīti । te dvividhe dikkṛte kālakṛte ca । dūrasthe dikkṛtaṃ paratvam । samīpasthe dikkṛtam aparatvam । jyeṣṭhe kālakṛthaṃ paratvam । kaniṣṭhe kālakṛtam aparatvam ।।
parāparavyavahārāsādhāraṇakāraṇe paratvāparatve। te dvividhe - dikkṛte kālakṛte ceti। dūrasthe dikkṛtaṃ paratvam। samīpasthe dikkṛtaṃ aparatvam। jyeṣṭhe kālakṛtaṃ paratvam। kaniṣṭhe kālakṛtaṃ aparatvam।
lakṣaṇamāha - parāpareti। paravyavahārāsādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ paratvam। aparavyavahārāsādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ apanaratvam ityarthaḥ। te vibhajate - te dvividhe iti। dikkṛtayorudāharaṇamāha - dūrastha iti। kālakṛte udāharati - jyeṣṭha iti।
AnTs ādyapatanāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ gurutvaṃ ।। ādyapatanāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ gurutvam। AnTs ādyasyandanāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ dravatvaṃ pṛthivyaptejovṛtti । tad dvividhaṃ sāṃsiddhikaṃ naimittikaṃ ca । sāṃsiddhikaṃ jale naimittikaṃ pṛthivītejasoḥ । pṛthivyāṃ ghṛtādāvagnisaṃyogajanyaṃ daravatvam । tejasi suvarṇādau ।। ādyasyandanāsamavāyikāraṇaṃ dravatvam। pṛthivījalatejovṛtti।
tat dvividham - sāṃsiddhikaṃ naimittikaṃ ceti। naikittikaṃ pṛthivītejasoḥ। pṛthivyāṃ ghṛtādau agnisaṃyogajaṃ dravatvam। AnTs cūrṇādipiṇḍībhāvahetur guṇaḥ snehaḥ ।।
cūrṇādipiṇḍībhāvahetuḥ guṇaḥ snehaḥ। ādyeti। dvitīyādipatanasya vegāsamavāyikāraṇatvāt vege ativyāptivāraṇāya ādyeti। ādyeti। syandanam - prasravaṇam। tejaḥsaṃyogajaṃ naimittikam।
tadbhinnaṃ sāṃsiddhikam। pṛthivyāṃ naimittikamudāharati - ghṛtādāviti। tejasi tadāha - suvarṇādāviti। cūrṇeti। kālādau ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇapadam। rūpādāvativyāptivāraṇāya cūrṇādipiṇḍībhāveti।
naimittikamāha ityarthaḥ। piṇḍībhāvaḥ saṃyogaviśeṣaḥ। AnTs śrotragrāhyo guṇaḥ śabdaḥ । sa dvividho dvanyātmako varṇātmakaś ceti । dvanyātmako bheryādau । varṇātmakaḥ saṃskṛtabhāṣādirūpaḥ ।। śabdaḥ। saḥ dvividhaḥ dhvanyātmakaḥ varṇātmakaśceti।
dhvanyātmako bheryādau। varṇātmakaḥ saṃskṛtabhāṣādirūpaḥ। śrotreti। śabdatve ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇapadam। rūpādāvativyāptivāraṇāya śrotreti। śabdaḥ trividhaḥ - saṃyogajaḥ vibhāgajaḥ śabdajaśceti। tatra ādyaḥ bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogajanyaḥ। dvitīyo
vaṃśe pāṭyamāne daladvayavibhāgajanyaḥ caṭacaṭaśabdaḥ। bheryādideśamārabhya śrotradeśaparyantaṃ dvitīyādiśabdāḥ śabdajāḥ। bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogajanya iti। ādye asamavāyikāraṇaṃ bheryākāśasaṃyogaḥ, nimittakāraṇaṃ bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogaḥ। dvitīye
nimittakāraṇam। tṛtīye tu pūrvaparvṛśabdaḥ asamavāyikāraṇam। pavanādi nimittakāraṇamiti vivekaḥ। AnTs sarvavyavahārahetur buddhir jñānam । sā dvividhā smṛtiranubhavaś ca । saṃskāramātrajanyaṃ jñānaṃ smṛtiḥ । tadbhinnaṃ jñānam anubhavaḥ ।। guṇaḥ jñānaṃ buddhiḥ।
smṛtiḥ anubhavaśceti। saṃskāramātrajanyaṃ jñānaṃ smṛtiḥ। tadbhinnaṃ jñānaṃ anubhavaḥ। AnTs[] sa dvividho yathārtho ayathārthaś ca । sarvavyavahāreti। kālādau ativyāptivāraṇāya guṇa iti। rūpādau
ativyāptivāraṇāya sarvavyavahāra iti। ajānāmi' ityanuvyavasāyagamyaṃ jñānatvameva lakṣaṇaṃ iti bhāvaḥ। seti। smṛteḥ lakṣaṇamāha - saṃskāreti। bhāvanākhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ। saṃskāradhvaṃse ativyāptivāraṇāya jñānamiti। anubhave
ativyāptivāraṇāya saṃskārajanyamiti। pratyabhijñāyāṃ ativyāptivāraṇāya mātrapadam। anubhavaṃ lakṣayati। tadbhinnamiti। smṛtibhinnaṃ jñānaṃ anubhava ityarthaḥ। anubhavaṃ vibhajate - sa dvividha iti।
jānāmītīti। jñānatvamātraṃ lakṣaṇam। pramāṇasiddhatvasūcanāya। tathā hi - aghaṭaṃ jānāmi' svīkartavyatvena lāghavāt jātitvasiddhiḥ। itthaṃ ca mūle sarvavyavahārahetuḥ iti buddheḥ svarūpakathanamiti bhāvaḥ।
trividhatvādāha - bhāvanākhya iti। pratyabhijñāyāṃ ativyāptīti। tatrātivyaptiriti bhāvaḥ। yadyapi saṃskāramātrajanyatvaṃ saṃskāretarājanyatve sati saṃskārajanyatvam। tacca smṛtau asambhavi। tatra saṃskāretarātmādijanyatvasya sattvāt। tathāpi cakṣurādyajanyatve
sati saṃskārajanyatve tātparyamavaseyam। svarūpaparam। ato nānupapattirityāha - itthaṃ ceti। jñānatvasyaiva jñānalakṣaṇatva ityarthaḥ। taddeśakālavṛttitveti।
taddeśakālavṛttitvarūpā yā tattā tadviṣayakasaṃskārajanyatvasyetyarthaḥ। tathāpi cakṣurādyajanyatvaṃ iti। pratyabhijñā tu ativyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। AnTs[] tadvati tatprakārako anubhavo yathārthaḥ । yathā rajata idaṃ rajatam iti jñānam । sa eva pramety ucyate ।
tatprakārakānubhavo yathārthaḥ। saiva prametyucyate। lakṣaṇamāha - tadvatīti। nanu aghaṭe ghaṭatvam' iti pramāyāṃ avyāptiḥ। ghaṭatve ghaṭābhāvāditi cet - na। yatra yatsambandho asti tatra nāvyāptiḥ। yathārthānubhava eva śāstre pramā ityucyata
ityarthaḥ। tatprakārakānubhava iti। saptamyartho viśeṣyitvaṃ āśrayatāsambandhenānubhavānvayī। tathā ca tadvadviśeṣyaka - tatprakārakānubhavatvaṃ yathārthānubhavasya lakṣaṇam। tatpadārthaḥ prakāraḥ,
tadvattavaṃ prakāratāvacchedakasambandhena grāhyam। tena kālikasambandhena nātivyāptiḥ। na ca tathāpi raṅgatvena rajatāvagāhini, rajatatvena ityākārakasamūhālambanabhrame ativyāptiḥ। tatra rajataviśeṣyakatva-rajatatvaprakāranakatvayośca sattvāditi vācyam।
adoṣāt। tathā hi - yayoḥ viṣayatayoḥ nirūpyanirūpakabhāvaḥ tannirūpitaviṣayitayoḥ avacchedyāvacchedakabhāva iti siddhāntaḥ। nātivyāptiḥ। smṛtivyāvṛttaye anubhavatvaniveśaḥ। etatphalaṃ anupadameva sphaṭībhaviṣyati।
aadhikaraṇe' ityarthakatayā aghaṭe ghaṭatvam' iti pramāyāmavyāptiḥ। ghaṭatvāmiti iti। tatsambandhinītyarthaḥ। evaṃ ca ghaṭatvasyāpi ghaṭasambandhitayā nāvyāptiriti samādhatte-yatreti। yathārthānubhava eveti। evakāreṇa
yathārthasmṛtivyavacchedaḥ। yathārthajñānabhātrasya pramātve smṛtikaraṇasya pramāṇāntaratāpatteḥ iti bhāvaḥ। viśeṣyitvamiti। atadvati' ityatra tacchabdaḥ prakārībhūtadharmaparaḥ। saptamyartho viśeṣyitvam। tatra prakṛtyarthasya tadvatpadārthasya
