nirūpitatvasambandhena anvayaḥ। viśeṣyitvasya āśrayatāsambandhena anubhave anvayaḥ। tathā ca tadvannirūpitaviśeṣyitvāśrayaḥ tanniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpakaḥ anubhavaḥ yathārthaḥ। sati anubhavatvaṃ yathārthānubhavasya lakṣaṇam। aayaṃ ghaṭa' iti pramāyāṃ
lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। smṛtau ativyāptivāraṇāya anubhavatvaniveśaḥ। iti tadvāraṇāya tadvanniṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpakatvaniveśaḥ। śuktirajatabhrame tu rajatatvābhāvavacchuktiniṣṭhaviśeṣyatākatvaniveśaḥ। na tu rajatatvavadrajataviśeṣyakatvamiti nātivyāptiḥ।
ityayathārthānubhave ativyāptiḥ। tatprakārakatvadalābhāve tatpadena śuktitvavadviśeṣyakatvānubhavatvayoḥ tatra sattvāt। tadvāraṇāya tatprakārakatvapadam। tanniveśe ca ekatra uccaritayoḥ tacchabdayoḥ niruktānubhave abhāvāt na ativyāptiḥ iti kecit। vastutastu
tatprakārakatvaniveśaḥ spaṣṭaṃ cedaṃ dinakaryādau। prakāratāvacchedakasambandhena grāhyamiti। prakṛte samavāyasambandhaḥ prakāratāvacchedakasambandhaḥ। tena sambandhena rajatatvavat rajatameva, na tu śuktiḥ। rajataviśeṣyakatvaṃ ca rajatabhrame nāstīti
nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। ajatatvapramātvāpattiriti। rajatatvavadviśeṣyakatvāditi bhāvaḥ। na ca tathāpītyādi।
raṅgarajate' ityākārakaḥ yaḥ samūhālambanabhramaḥ tatrātivyāptiḥ। tasmin bhrame raṅgaṃ rajataṃ ca ubhayaṃ viśeṣyam। raṅgatvaṃ rajatatvaṃ ca ubhayaṃ prakāraḥ। tathā ca raṅgatvavadraṅgaviśeṣyakatvasya rajatatvaprakārakatvasya ca sattvāt iti śaṅkiturāśayaḥ।
nānāmukhyaviśeṣyakaṃ jñānaṃ samūhālambanamityucyate। tadvadviśeṣyakatvāvacchinnetyādinā। tadvadviśeṣyakatvāvacchinnaṃ yat tatprakārakatvaṃ tadāśrayānubhavatvaṃ yathārthānubhavatvam। viśeṣyitvaprakāritvayoḥ avacchedyāvacchedakabhāvo bhavati।
raṅgatvavadraṅganiṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpitā। evaṃ rajatatvaniṣṭhaprakāratā rajatatvavadrajataniṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpitā। tathā ca abhāvāt nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। anupadameva sphaṭībhaviṣyatīti। dīpikāgranthavyākhyānāvasara ityarthaḥ।
ityarthakatayeti। tathā ca prakāratāvacchedakasambandhena labhyate। aghaṭe ghaṭaḥ prakāraḥ। prakāratāvacchedakasambandhaḥ ādheyatā। ādheyatvaṃ vṛttyaniyāmakam । ataḥ ādheyatāsambandhena
tādṛśapramāyāmavyāptiriti śaṅkiturāśayaḥ। tatsambandhinītyartha iti। bhāvaḥ। tathā ca atadvati' ityasya yadi avyāptiḥ syāt। sor'thastu prakṛte na vivakṣitaḥ। ādheyatāsambandhena
ghaṭatvam' iti pramāyāṃ sattvāt nāvyāptiriti samādhāturāśayaḥ। pramātva iti। yadi anubhavatvamaniveśya yathārthajñānatvaṃ pramātvaṃ ityucyate tarhi smṛterapi yathārthajñānatvāt prakātvaṃ prasajyeta। na ceṣṭāpattiḥ। pratyakṣādipramitivilakṣaṇasmṛtirūpapramākaraṇasya
sūtrakāroktyasāṃgatyāpatteriti bhāvaḥ। AnTs[] tadabhāvavati tatprakārako anubhavo ayathārthaḥ । yathā śuktāv idaṃ rajatam iti jñānam ।। tadabhāvavati tatprakārakānubhavo ayathārthaḥ। saiva apramā ityucyate।
ayathārthānubhavaṃ lakṣayati - tadabhāvavatīti। nanu aidaṃ saṃyogī' ti pramāyāmativyāptiriti cet - na। vivakṣitatvāt। saṃyogābhāvāvacchedena saṃyogajñānasya ghaṭasambandhīti।
ghaṭaprattiyogikādheyatāsambandhānuyogītyarḥtha। ativyāptiriti। saṃyogābhāvavati saṃyogaprakārakatvasya sattvāditi bhāvaḥ। yadavacchedeneti। yadavacchedena
tatprakārakānubhavasya vivakṣitatvādityarthaḥ। saṃyogābhāvāvacchedeneti। saṃyogābhāvāvacchedakāvacchedenetyarthaḥ। saṃyogāvacchedeneti। saṃyogāvacchedakāvacchedenetyarthaḥ। saṃyogasambandhasyeti। samavāyasambandhena saṃyogasyetyarthaḥ।
idaṃ avyāpyavṛttisaṃyogādiprakārakabhramānurodhena। tatprakārakatvaviśiṣṭānubhavatvam। pratiyogitāyāṃ prakāratāvacchedaka nātivyāptiḥ। sattve api nātivyāptiḥ ityalaṃ ativistareṇa।।
saṃyogābhāvavatīti। saṃyogasyāvyāpyavṛttitvāt tatprakārakatvarūpabhramalakṣaṇātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। yadavacchedenetyādi। tajjñānaṃ bhramaḥ। agrāvacchedena kapisaṃyogajñānaṃ tu pramaiva, tadavacchedena kapisaṃyogābhāvavirahāt। agrāvacchedena
vṛkṣaḥ kapisaṃyogīti pramāyāḥ bhramatvāpattiḥ। tadvāraṇāya yatsambandhāvacchinneti। mūlāvacchedena ramavāyasambandhāvacchinna - saṃyogāvagāhitvābhāvāt। na hi saṃyogasya saṃyogābhāvāvacchedakāvacchedenetyartha iti।
saṃyogābhāvasyāvacchedako yaḥ mūlādiḥ tadavacchedenetyarthaḥ। saṃyogāvacchedakāvacchedeneti। saṃyogasya avacchedakaḥ yaḥ agrādiḥ tadavacchedenetyarthaḥ। āha - atredamavadheyamiti। tatsambandhāvacchinnetyādi। śuktau
kriyate। samavāyasambandhāvacchinna pratiyogitakarajatatvābhāvavān purovartiśuktirūpapadārthaḥ। tadviśeṣyakatve sati rajatatvaprakārakatvaṃ uktabhrame asti iti । syāt। tathā sati aparvato vahnimān' iti pramāyāmativyāptiḥ।
parvate sattve api samavāyena sattā nāsti। ataḥ tathā apratīteriti। saṃyogāvacchedakatayā saṃyogābhāvasyāpratīterityarthaḥ। sati vahniprakārakatvaṃ aparvato vahnimān' iti pramāyāmastīti।
bhāvaḥ। viśeṣyitvaprakāritvayoriti। tathā ca rajatatvaprakārakatvaṃ cāstītyativyāpti syāt। atastayoḥ avacchedyāvacchedakābhāvavivakṣā। tathā ca tadabhāva vadviśeṣyakatvāvacchinnaṃ
yat tatprakārakatvaṃ tadviśiṣṭānubhavaḥ bhrama iti lakṣaṇaṃ bhavati। raṅgatvasyāprakāratvāt। evaṃ ca avacchedyāvacchedakabhāvo nāsti। yayorviṣayatayoḥ nirūpyanirūpakabhāvaḥ tannirūpitaviṣayitayoreva avacchedyāvacchedakabhāva iti niyamāt।
coktasamūhālambanapramāyāṃ abhāvānnātivyāpitariti bhāvaḥ। prakāratāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyatānirūpakatve satyanubhavatvaṃ bhramasya lakṣaṇam। niṣkarṣaḥ। AnTs yathārthānubhavaś caturvidhaḥ pratyakṣānumityupamitiśabdabhedāt । tatkaraṇam api caturvidhaṃ pratyakṣānumānopamānaśabdabhedāt ।।
caturvidhaḥ - pratyakṣa - anumiti - upamiti - śabdabhedāt। tatkaraṇamapi caturvidham - pratyakṣa - anumāna - upamāna - śabdabhedāt। vibhajate। prasaṅgāt pramākaraṇaṃ vibhajate - tatkaraṇamapīti। prakākaraṇamityarthaḥ। pramāyāḥ karaṇaṃ pramāṇam iti
pramāṇasāmānyalakṣaṇam। prasaṅgāditi। smṛtasya upekṣānarhatvaṃ prasaṅgaḥ tasmādityarthaḥ। sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ sphuṭayati - pramāyāḥ karaṇaṃ pramāṇamiti।
smṛtasyeti। bhāvaḥ। svāvacchedaketi। śuktiniṣṭhaviśeṣyatāyām। tathā ca uktobhayasambandhena
tannirūpakatve sati anubhavatvaṃ idaṃ rajatamiti bhrame astīti। AnTs asādhāraṇam kāraṇaṃ karaṇam । asādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ karaṇam। asādhāraṇeti। sādhāraṇakāraṇe dikkālādau ativyāptivāraṇāya
asādhāraṇeti। asādhāraṇetīti। tatra asattvāt nātivyāptiḥ। avyāpāravattve sati' ityapi vaktavyam। ataḥ cakṣuḥ-saṃyogādau
nātivyāptiḥ। śrotramanassaṃyogaḥ śabdo vā vyāpāraḥ saṃbhavatyeveti na śrotrendriyo karaṇalakṣaṇāvyāptiḥ-iti vadanti। tādṛśakāraṇatvābhāvāt na ativyāptiḥ। vyāpāratvenābhimatendriyasaṃyogādikameva karaṇam। etacca
aliṅgaparāmarśa evānumānam' iti mūle eva sphuṭībhaviṣyati। ata tu navyāḥ। adhikam asmadīyacintāmaṇiprabhāyāṃ anusandheyam। dikkālādṛṣṭāderiti। pramānirūpitāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvaṃ pramāṇasyalakṣaṇam। pramāniṣṭhā yā anubhavatvavyāpyadharmāvacchinnā
kāryatā tannirūpitakāraṇatvamiti yāvat। anubhavatvavyāpyadharmaḥ pramāṇalakṣaṇasya dikkālādāvativyāptiḥ syāt। tanniveśe tu nātivyāptiḥ। cakṣurāderiva tatsannikarṣāderapi niveśanīyam। na ca
pramāṇalakṣaṇasya śrotrendriye abhāvāditi vācyam। sattvāt - iti prācīnamatam। yadvilambādityādinā। na vyāpāravatkāraṇatvamasādhāraṇakāraṇatvam। ati tu yadvilambāt prakṛtakāryānutpādaḥ tattvam। kālādiṣu
etādṛśāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। vyāpāratvena navīnamatam। AnTs kāryaniyatapūrvavṛtti kāraṇam । kāryaniyatapūrvavṛtti kāraṇam।
kāraṇalakṣaṇamāha - kāryeti। apūrvavṛtti kāraṇaṃ' ityukte rāsabhādau ativyāptiḥ syāt, ataḥ niyateti। tāvanmātre kṛte kārye ativyāptiḥ, ataḥ pūrvavṛtti iti। niyateti।
niyatatvaṃ hi vyāpakatvam। tacca rāsabhādeḥ na saṃbhavatīti tatra na ghaṭakāraṇatvātiprasaktiriti bhāvaḥ। svavyāpakatvasya bhāvaḥ। kāryatāvacchedakasambandhena kāryādhikaraṇe kāraṇatvamiti samuditār'tho bodhyaḥ।
sati kāryapūrvavṛttitvaṃ kāraṇasya lakṣaṇam। kāryaniyatatvaṃ ca kāryavyāpakatvam। kāryapūrvavṛttitvamātroktau rāsabhāderapikadācit ghaṭapūrvavartitvamastīti ghaṭakāraṇatvāpattiḥ। tadvāraṇāya kāryavyāpakatvaniveśaḥ। kāryasyāpi kāryavyāpakatvāt
tatrativyāptivāraṇāya kāryapūrvavartitatvaniveśaḥ। tadāha-niyatatvaṃ hītyādīnā। kāryavyāpakatvaśarīra eva kāryapūrvavartitvamapi niveśya pariṣkaroti - kāryatāvacchedakasambandhenetyādinā। taṇḍādiṣvastīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। kāryatāvacchedakasambandhenetyanuktau
tadanavacchekadharmavattvamityasambhavaḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya-kārya-tāvacchedakasambandheneti। syāt। tadvāraṇāya pratiyogitānavacchedakadharmavattvaniveśaḥ। pratiyogitānavacchedakatvaṃ vivakṣitam। daṇḍatvacakratvādinā
daṇḍacakrādīnāṃ kāraṇatvaṃ vivakṣitam। daṇḍatvādestu tādṛśapratiyogitānavacchedakatvamasttyeva iti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। nātaḥ prameyatvamādāya rāsabhādāvativyāptiḥ। iti viśeṣaṇāt। ananyathāsiddhatvam anyathāsiddhirahitatvam।
pūrvavṛttitvamavagamyate taṃ prati tena tadanyathāsiddham। yathā tantunā tanturūpaṃ tantutvaṃ ca paṭaṃ prati। anyaṃ prati pūrvavṛttitve jñāta eva yasya yaṃ prati pūrvavṛttitvamavagamyate taṃ prati tadanyathāsiddham। yathā śabdaṃ prati pūrvavṛttitve jñāta eva paṭaṃ prati ākāśasya।
kḷptaniyatapūrvavartina eva kāryasambhave tatsahabhūtaṃ anyathāsiddham। yathā pākajasthale gandhaṃ prati rūpaprāgabhāvasya। evaṃ ca ananyathāsiddhaniyatapūrvavṛttitvaṃ kāraṇatvam। kāraṇaṃ syāditi।
tasya niyatapūrvavṛttitvāditi bhāvaḥ। nibandhāntareṣu anyathāsiddheḥ pañcavidhatve api maṇikāramatābhiprāyeṇāha - trividheti। yena sahaivetyādi। yena tantunā sahaiva yasya tatturūpasya tantutvasya ca yaṃ tantutvaṃ ca tena tantunā anyathāsiddhamityarthaḥ। atra sahitatvam
ekajñānaviṣayatvaṃ bodhyam। tanturūpasya paṭapūrvavṛttitvajñāne anatiprasaktatanturūpatvenaiva viṣayatā vācyā। tathā ca tanturūpaṃ anyathāsiddhamiti। evaṃ entutvasya pūrvavṛttitvajñānamapi tantuviṣayakameveti tadapyanyathāsiddhamiti bhāvaḥ। atra ayena' ityasya
asvatantrānvayavyatirekaśūnyasya' iti viśeṣaṇaṃ bodhyam। tena na tantunā anyathāsiddhiriti saṅkṣepaḥ।"itarānvayavyatirekaprayuktānvayavyatirekaśāli yat yat anyathāsiddham"iti tu pare। ākāśatvaṃ hi śabdasamavāyikāraṇatvam। tathā ca śabdakāraṇatvamagṛhītvā
ityākāśo anyathāsiddha ityarthaḥ। pākajasthale api tatsambhave rūpaprāgabhāvo anyathāsiddha ityarthaḥ। atha evaṃ satyantenaiva vāraṇasambhavāt iti cet - na। ghaṭasāmānyaṃ prati tantvāditaḥ ghaṭotpattyasambhavāditi।
anyathāsiddhaṃ ityekavidhameva anyathāmiddhatvam। laghutvaṃ ca śarīrakṛtamupasthitikṛtaṃ saṃbandhakṛtam ca। tatra prathamam - anekadravyasamavetatvāpekṣayā mahattve। dvitīyam - gandhaṃ prati upasthitatvena śīghraṃ tadupasthiteḥ। tṛtīyam -
svāśrayadaṇḍasaṃyogādirūpaparamparayā gurutvāt। evaṃ caitāvataiva vyutpattivaicitryāya। tṛtīyānyathāsiddhatvenaiva vāraṇāt niyatapadaṃ vyarthamiti vācyam। anyathāsiddhatvavyavahāraḥ tattadbhedakūṭaṃ niveśanīyam।
laghuniyatetyādikaṃ tu bhedapratiyogitattadvyaktiparicāyakam। vāraṇāt tattadbhedakūṭaniveśe gauravam। niyatānāṃ niveśanīyamityabhisandhiḥ। muktavalpāṃ ca। maṇikāraistu śaktivāde trividhā evānyathāsiddhayaḥ
pradarśitāḥ। tadanusāreṇa dīpikāyāmapi। sahitatvamekajñānaviṣayatvamiti। tathā ca yasya tat anyathāsiddhamiti phalati। atanturūpaṃ paṭapūrvavṛtti' iti jñāne pratyanyathāsiddhamityarthaḥ।
prathamānyathāsiddhatvamiti yāvat। anyathāsiddhatvamityāśaṅkyāhatanturūpasyeti। rūpatvasya sambhavati, anyūnānatiprasaktadharmasyaivāvacchedakatvāt। api tu vaktavyam। tasmin jñāne tu tantūnāmapi
iśeṣyatāvacchedakatayā viṣayatvamāvaśyakamiti bhāvaḥ। tantutvasya pūrvavṛttitvajñānamapi tantuviṣayakameveti। atantutvaṃ tantutvatvena tantutvabhānaṃ vaktavyam। tantutvatvaṃ ca tatkāryanirūpitetyādi। tatkāryaṃ paṭaḥ tannirūpitaṃ yat
tantuḥ tatkatvaṃ tanturūpe tanatutve cāstīti samanvayaḥ। viśeṣyatāvacchedakatayeti। tanturūpamityasya samavāyasambandhena tantuviśaṣṭa rūpamityarthaḥ। tathā ca atanturūpaṃ paṭapūrvavṛtti' iti viśeṣyatāvacchedakatvamāvaśyakamiti bhāvaḥ।
tantūnāmarpiṃ bhānamavarjanīyam। evaṃ ca tantuviṣayakatvanaiyatyamityāśayaḥ। yadvā yadviṣayakatvavyāpyaṃ yāvat। tantorapyanyathāsiddhatvaṃ syāt। evaṃ atantusaṃyogaḥ paṭapūrvavartī'
anyathāsiddhatvaṃ syāt iti, ata āha - atra yenetyasyetyādinā। tathā tadanyathāsiddhamiti phalati। tantutvasya svātantryeṇa paṭaṃ prati anvayavyatirekau na staḥ। kiṃ tu tantoranvayavyatirekāvanusṛtyaiva। tantoranyathāsiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। tantutvasya grahaṇāsambhavāt na
tantutvena tantoranyathāsiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। tantuvat tantusaṃyogasya svatantrānvayavyatirekā staḥ, asamavayikāraṇatvāt। ataḥ prathamayatpadena dvitīyayatpadena tasya grahaṇaṃ śakyamiti na tasyānyathāsiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। prayojanamāha - tena na atathābhūteneti।
svatantrānvayavyatirekaśūnyenetyarthaḥ। dvitīyayatpadārthe svatantrānvayavyatirekaśūnyatvaniveśaphalamāha na veti। lāghavādāhaitaranvayavyatirekaprayukteti। anyathāsiddhatvāt। tasya tu anyaṃ pratītyādi dvitīyānyathāsiddhatvam।
ghaṭaṃ prati ākāśasya pūrvavṛttitvaṃ ākāśatvena grāhyam। ākāśatvaṃ ca śabdasamavāyikāraṇatvam। tathā ca śabdaṃ prati pūrvavṛttitvaṃ anyathāsiddhamiti bhāvaḥ। apākajasthala ityādi। yatra ghaṭādau rūpaprāgabhāvasyānyathāsiddhatvāt vāraṇīyā। tasya a anyatra kḷpte'
tyādinoktaṃ tṛtīyānyathāsiddhatvaṃ bhavati। anyatra - pākajādanyasmin bhāvaḥ। aanyatra kḷpte' tyādirūpeṇa tṛtīyānyathāsiddhavarṇana ityarthaḥ। niyatapadaṃ vyarthamiti। ghaṭakāraṇatvāpattiriti tadvāraṇāya niyatapadamupāttam। tadupādāne
nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ। paraṃ tu tadghaṭādanyasmin ghaṭāntare rāsabhavāvaṇasambhavāt niyatapadaṃ vyarthamiti śaṅkiturāśayaḥ। satyantenaiveti। ananyathāsiddhatve satītyanenaivetyarthaḥ। samādhatte - ghaṭasāmānyaṃ pratīti। tadghaṭatvāvacchinnaṃ prati rāsabhasya
pīlupākavādināṃ matamanusṛtya। tanmate paramāṇugandhasyaiva dvyaṇukādigandhasya grahītuṃ śakyatvāt। piṭharapākavādināṃ mate tu avayavigandhasyāpi pākajanyatvāt apākajaḥ pārthivagandhaḥ aprasiddhaḥ। jale jalīyagandhasyopādānāsaṃbhavāt। tanmatānusādeṇa pākajarūpaṃ prati
iti śaṅkā, anyathāsiddhatvena samādhānaṃ ca vaktavyam। pratyanyathāsiddhatvaṃ na sambhavati। tadā hi aanyatra' ityasya ghaṭatvāvacchinnāt anyasmin ityarthaḥ। tathā ca ghaṭasāmānyabhinne tatrātivyāptivāraṇāya niyatapadamāvaśyakamiti bhāvaḥ।
punariti। laghu yat kāryaniyatapūrvavṛtti tata eva kāryakambhave tadbhinnaṃ anyathāsiddham। laghutvaṃ śarīrataḥ upasthityā sambandheneti trividham। pratyakṣaṃ prati anekadravyasamavetatvaṃ kāraṇaṃ vā mahattvaṃ tadbhinnaṃ anekasamavetatvaṃ anyathāsiddham। ato na tatpratyakṣakāraṇam।
eva kāraṇaṃ rūpaprāgabhāvastu anyathāsiddhaḥ। evaṃ ghaṭaṃ prati daṇḍaḥ kāraṇaṃ ubhayorniyatapūrvavṛttitve api daṇḍasya saṃyogasaṃbandhena kāraṇatvam। tadbhinnaṃ daṇḍatvadaṇḍarūpādikaṃ anyathāsiddhamityarthaḥ। vyutpattivaicitryāyeti। buddhivaiśadyāyetyarthaḥ।
durvacatayeti। laghutvasya śarīrakṛtasambandhakṛtādibhedena nānārūpatayā anyathāsiddhatvaṃ ekamanugataṃ na śakyate vaktum। evaṃ gurubhūtamityarthakatayā gurutvameva anyathāsiddhatvamiti paryavasānāt। tāvatpratiyogikabhedakūṭakavattvaṃ kāraṇalakṣaṇe niveśanīyam। tatra
niveśaḥ anāvaśyakaḥ। kāryavyāpakānāṃ daṇḍatvādīnāṃ tu bhedaḥ kāraṇalakṣaṇe niveśitavato granthakārasyāśaya iti bhāvaḥ। AnTs kāryaṃ prāgabhāvapratiyogi । kāryaṃprāgabhāvapratiyogi।
kāryamiti। AnTs kāraṇaṃ trividhaṃ samavāyyasamavāyinimittabhedāt । yat samavetaṃ kāryam utpadyate tat samavāyikāraṇam । yathā tantavaḥ paṭasya paṭaś ca khagatarūpādeḥ । kāryeṇa kāraṇena vā sahaikasminn arthe samavetatve sati yat kāraṇaṃ tad asamavāyikāraṇam । yathā tantusaṃyogaḥ paṭasya tanturūpaṃ paṭarūpasya । tadubhayabhinnaṃ kāraṇaṃ nimittakāraṇam । yathā turīvemādikaṃ paṭasya । samavāyi-asamavāyi-nimittabhedāt। yatsamavetaṃ kāryamutpadyate tatsamavāyikāraṇam। yathā
svagatarūpādeḥ। kāryeṇa kāraṇena vā saha ekasmin arthe samavetaṃ satkāraṇaṃ asamavāyikāraṇam। yathā tantusaṃyogaḥ paṭasya, tanturūpaṃ paṭagatarūpasya ca। tadubhayabhinnaṃ kāraṇaṃ nimittakāraṇam। yathā turīvemādikaṃ paṭasya।
AnTs tad etattrividhakāraṇamadhye yad asādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ tad eva karaṇam ।। tadetattrividhakāraṇamadhye yadasādhāraṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ tadeva kāraṇam। kāraṇamiti। samavāyikāraṇasya lakṣaṇamāha - yatsamavetamiti। yasmin samavetamityarthaḥ। asamavāyikāraṇaṃ lakṣayatikāryeṇeti। akāryeṇa'
ityetadudāharati - tantusaṃyoga iti। kāryeṇa paṭena saha paṭasyāsamavāyikāraṇamityarthaḥ। akāraṇena' ityetat udāharati - tanturūpamiti। kāraṇena paṭena saha ekasmin tantau samavetatvāt tanturūpaṃ paṭarūpasyāsamavāyikāraṇamityarthaḥ। nimittakāraṇaṃ lakṣayati
- tadubhayeti। samavāyyasamavāyibhinnakāraṇaṃ nimittakāraṇamityarthaḥ। kāraṇalakṣaṇamupasaṃharati - tadetaditi। samavetamityartha iti। yaddharmāvacchinnaṃ yaddharmāvacchinne samavāyikāraṇamiti paramārthaḥ।
svakārya-samavāyikāraṇena paṭena ityarthaḥ। tattadasamavāyikāraṇalakṣaṇe tattadbhinnatvaṃ deyamiti dik। yaddharmāvacchinnamiti। samavāyasambandhāvacchinnaghaṭatvāvacchinna - ghaṭasamavāyikāraṇasya lakṣaṇam। samavāyena kāryasāmānyaṃ prati
ityabhipretyaivamuktam। tādṛśakāryaṅkāraṇabhāvasya prāmāṇikatve tu sāmānyalakṣaṇamapi bhavitumarhati। kāryatāyāṃ ghaṭe ativyāptiḥ ataḥ tanniveśaḥ। kāraṇatāyāṃ ghaṭāsamavāyikāraṇe kapāladvayasaṃyoge ativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya
tanniveśaḥ। evaṃ samavāyasambandhāvacchinna - asamavāyikāraṇatvam। tatra kāryatāyāṃ nimittakāraṇatāvati ghaṭarūpe ativyāptiḥ। kāraṇatāyāṃ tādātmyasambandhāvacchinnakāraṇatāvati samavāyikāraṇe ativyāptiḥ।
pratyasamavāyikāraṇe tanturūpe avyāptiḥ। samavāyena paṭarūpaṃ prati tanturūpasya samavāyena akāraṇatvāt। ataḥ svasamavāyisamavetatvasambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। tāvanmātraniveśe paṭaṃ prati asamavāyikāraṇe tantusaṃyoge avyāptiḥ। ataḥ
anyatarasambandhaniveśaḥ। AnTs tatra pratyakṣajñānakaraṇaṃ pratyakṣam । indriyārthasannikarṣajanyaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣam ।tad dvividhaṃ nirvikalpakaṃ savikalpakaṃ ceti । tatra nirvikalpakaṃ jñānaṃ nirvikalpakaṃ yathedaṃ kiṃcit । saparakārakaṃ jñānaṃ savikalpakaṃ yathā ḍittho'yam brahmaṇo'yaṃ śyāmo'yam iti ।। pratyakṣajñānakaraṇaṃ pratyakṣam। indriyārthasannikarṣajanyaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣam।
nirvakalpakaṃ savikalpakaṃ ceti। niṣprakārakaṃ jñānaṃ nirvikalpakam। saprakārakaṃ jñānaṃ savikalpakam। yathā aḍitthaḥ ayam', abrāhmaṇaḥ ayam', aśyāmaḥ ayam', apācakaḥ ayam' iti। pratyakṣapramāṇalakṣaṇamāha - tatreti। pramāṇacatuṣṭayamadhya
ityarthaḥḥ। pratyakṣajñānasya lakṣaṇamāha - indriyeti। indriyaṃ jñānamityarthaḥ। taddvividhamiti। nirvikalpakasya lakṣaṇamāha - niṣprakārakamiti। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasambandhānavagāhi jñānamityarthaḥ। nanu nirvikalpake kiṃ
pramāṇamiti cet - na। agauḥ' iti viśiṣṭajñānaṃ ityanumānasya pramāṇatvāt। viśeṣaṇajñānasyāpi savikalpakatve anavasthāprasaṅgāt nirvikalpakasiddhiḥ। savikalpakaṃ lakṣayati - saprakārakamiti। nāmajātyādiviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasambandhāvagāhi
jñānamityarthaḥ। savikalpakamudāharati - yatheti। -viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyeti। viśeṣyādividhyā viśeṣyādyanavagāhijñānamityarthaḥ। tathā ca jñānatvaghaṭitaṃ lakṣaṇatrayaṃ paryavasitamiti bhāvaḥ।
niṣprakārakatvaṃ prakāratāśūnyatvam। prakāratā ca bhāsamānavaiśiṣṭyapratiyogitvam। saṃsargāvacchinnaviṣayateti yāvat mūlārthamāha-viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyetīnti-ityāhuḥ। taccintyam - gauravānavakāśāditi dik।
gauriti। viśiṣṭajñānatvāditi। viśiṣṭabuddhiṃ prati viśeṣaṇajñānasya kāraṇatvāt nāprayojakatāśaṅketi bhāvaḥ। anavasthāprasaṅgāditi। bhāvaḥ। viśeṣaṇaviśeśyasambandhāvagāhīti। atrāpyuktarītyā lakṣaṇatrayaṃ bodhyam।
turīyaviṣayatānirūpakasyeti। prakāratā - viśeṣyatā saṃsargatātrayātiriktacaturthaviṣayatānirūpakasyetyarthaḥ। viśeṣyādividhayeti। viśeṣyatvādiprakāreṇetyarthaḥ। nirvikalpake ghaṭaḥ ghaṭatvaṃ sambandhaśca bhāsate। parantu viśeṣyatvaṃ -
viśeṣaṇatva-saṃsargatvaiḥ ghaṭādikaṃ na bhāsate। tathā ca mūle prakāraśabdaḥ viśeṣyatva-viśeṣaṇatva-saṃsargatvarūpaprakāraparaḥ। bhāvāḥ। atrāpyuktarītyā lakṣaṇatrayamiti। prakāratānirūpakatvaṃ viśeṣyatānirūpakatvaṃ saṃsargatānirūpakatvamiti lakṣaṇatrayamityarthaḥ।
AnTs pratyakṣajñānahetur indriyārthasannikarṣaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ । saṃyogaḥ saṃyuktasamavāyaḥ saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ samavetasamavāyo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaś ceti । cakṣuṣā ghaṭapratyakṣajanane saṃyogaḥ sannikarṣaḥ । ghaṭarūpapratyakṣajanane saṃyuktasamavāyaḥ sannikarṣaḥ cakṣuḥsaṃyukte ghaṭe rūpasya samavāyāt । rūpatvasāmānyapratyakṣe saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyaḥ sannikarṣaḥ cakṣuḥsaṃyukte ghaṭe rūpaṃ samavetaṃ tatra rūpatvasya samavāyāt । śrotreṇa śabdasyākāśaguṇatvāt guṇaguṇinoś ca samavāyāt । śabdatvasākṣātkāre samavetasamavāyaḥ sannikarṣaḥ śrotrasamavete śabde śabdatvasya samavāyāt । abhāvaparatyakṣe viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ sannikarṣo ghaṭābhāvavad bhṛtalam ity atra cakṣuḥsaṃyukte bhūtale ghaṭābhāvasya viśeṣaṇatvāt । evaṃ snnikarṣaṣaṭkajanyaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣam । tatkaraṇam indriyam । tasmād indriyaṃ pratyakṣapramāṇam iti siddham ।। indriyārthasannikarṣaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ। saṃyogaḥ, saṃyuktasamavāyaḥ, viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaśceti। cakṣuṣā ghaṭapratyakṣajanane saṃyogaḥ sannikarṣaḥ। ghaṭarūpapratyakṣe saṃyuktasamavāyaḥ। cakṣussaṃyukte ghaṭe rūpasya
samavāyāt। rūpatvasāmānyapratyakṣe saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyaḥ। cakṣussaṃyukte ghaṭe rūpaṃ samavetam। tatra rūpatvasrū samavāyāt। śrotreṇa śabdasākṣātkāre samavāyaḥ sannikarṣaḥ। karṇavivaravṛttyākāśasya kṣotratvāt। śabdasya ākāśaguṇatvāt। guṇaguṇinoḥ samavāyāt।
śabdatvasākṣātkāre samavetasamavāyaḥ sannikarṣaḥ। śrotrasamavete śabde śabdatvasya samavāyāt। abhāvapratyakṣe viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ sannikarṣaḥ। viśeṣaṇatvāt। pratyakṣeti। saṃyogasannikarṣamudāharati - cakṣuṣeti। dravyapratyakṣe
sarvatra saṃyogaḥ sannikarṣaḥ। ātmā manasā saṃyujyate, mana indriyeṇa, indriyamarthena tataḥ pratyakṣajñānamutpadyate ityarthaḥ। saṃyuktasamavāyamudāharati - ghaṭarūpeti। tatra yuktimāha - cakṣussaṃyukta iti। saṃyuktasamavetasamavāyamudāharati -
rūpatveti। samavāyamudāharati - śrotreṇeti। tadupapādayati - karṇeti। nana dūrasthaśabdasya kathaṃ śrotrasambandha iti cet - na। pratyakṣatvasambhavāt। samavetasamapāyamudāharati - śabdatveti।
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvamudāharati - abhāveti। tadupapādayati - ghaṭābhāvavaditi। bhūtalaṃ viśeṣyam, ghaṭābhāvo viśeṣaṇam। bhūtale ghaṭo nāstītyatra abhāvasya viśeṣyatvaṃ draṣṭavyam। indriyeṇeti। saṃyujyate ityanenānvayaḥ। evamagre api।
utpadyate iti yojanāntareṇa। kathaṃ śrotrasambandha iti। na ca śaṅkyam। atiprasaṅgabhaṅgāya bhāvaḥ। prathamataḥ bherīdaṇḍasaṃyogena nabhasi śabda utpadyate, tena śabdāḥ, kadamveti।
viśeṣaṇatātvenaiva parigaṇanāt ca ṣaḍvidhatvahāniḥ। na caivaṃ vācyam; svatantrecchasyetyādinyāyānusāreṇa adoṣāditi। evamagre apīti। bhāvaḥ। atiprasaṅgabhaṅgāteti। sarveṣāmapi śabdānāṃ
pratyakṣaprasaṅgavāraṇāyetyarthaḥ। tathā ādyavīcī samīpadeśe śabdotpattikramaḥ। yathā prathamataḥ utpannaṃ kadambamukulaṃ sarvadigavacchedena adhikaśabdān janayatīti। paraṃ tu yaddigabhimukho śabdotpattikrama iti nṛsiṃhaprakāśikākārāḥ prāhuḥ।
atredamavadheyamityādi। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo nāma naikaḥ sannikarṣaḥ। api tu viśeṣaṇatvaṃ viśeṣyatvaṃ ceti sambandhadvayam। tatrābhāvaviśeṣaṇakapratyakṣe viśeṣaṇatvaṃ saṃnikarṣaḥ। abhāvaviśeṣyakapratyakṣe viśeṣyatvaṃ
saṃnikarṣaḥ। viśeṣaṇatvaṃ pañcavidham saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇatvam, samavetaviśeṣaṇatvam, samavetasamavetaviśeṣaṇatvam ceti। evaṃ samavetasamavetaviśeṣyatvam ceti pañcavidham। āhatya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo daśavidha iti nyāyabhūṣaṇe pratyapādi।
tīvratvābhāvaḥ, śabdatve bhedābhāvaḥ iti। na caivaṃ vācyam। viśeṣaṇatātvena pañcavidhaviśeṣaṇatānāṃ viśeṣyatātvena ṣaḍvidhatvasyāhāneḥ। na ca samavāyarūpāṇāṃ saṃyuktasamavāya - vācyam। svatantrecchena muninā kṛte ṣoḍhā vibhāge
niyogaparyanuyogayoḥ kartumaśakyatvāt। niyogaḥ ājñā, paryanuyogaḥ praśnaḥ। bhūtalaṃ tadviśeṣaṇatvaṃ ghaṭābhāvasya। tatsamavetaḥ sparśaḥ tadviśeṣaṇatvam uṣṇatvābhāvasya।
śuklatvābhāvasya। vīṇāśabdaḥ tadviśeṣaṇatvaṃ tīvratvābhāvasya। tatsamavetaṃ śabdatvaṃ tadviśeṣaṇatvaṃ bhedābhāvasya। bhūtalaṃ tinnarūpitaviśeṣyatā ghaṭābhāvasya।
tatsamavetaḥ sparśaḥ tannirūpitaviśeṣyatā uṣṇatvābhāvasya। śuklatvābhāvasya। vīṇāśabdaḥ tannirūpitaviśeṣyatā tīvratvābhāvasya। śabdaḥ tatsamavetaṃ śabdatvaṃ tannirūpitaviśeṣyatā bhedābhāvasya।
dvividhā। indriyasambaddhaviśeṣaṇatā, pūrvoktarītyā pañcavidhā। śabdābhāvapratyakṣam - ityabhiprayanti। aviśeṣaṇatayā śabdābhāvasya, saṃnikarṣavāde taiḥ kathanāt।। ।।
sannikarṣajanyajñānam pratyakṣam। tatkaraṇaṃ indriyam। tasmādindriyaṃ pratyakṣapramāṇam iti siddham।। pratyakṣaparicchedaḥ। pramāṇāntaratvanirākaraṇam।
pramāṇāntaratvaṃ nirastam। yadi atra ghaṭaḥ abhaviṣyat tarhi bhūtalamiva abhāvajñānopapattau anupalabdhaiḥ pramāṇāntaratvāsambhavāt। karaṇatvāyogāt। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasvarūpameva, nātiriktaḥ sambandhaḥ।
pratyakṣajñānamupasaṃharan tasya karaṇamāha - evamiti। asādhāraṇakāraṇatvāt indriyaṃ pratyakṣajñānakaraṇamityarthaḥ। pratyakṣapramāṇamupasaṃharati - tasmāditi।। abhāvapramāyā viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvasaṃnikarṣajanyatvapradarśanena।
pramāṇāntaratvam - pratyakṣādyatiriktapramāṇatvam। nanu anupalabdheḥ saṃbhavatītyāha - yadyatretyādinā। atra - cakṣussaṃyogādimadbhūtale tatkoṭiparyavasāyitvaṃ darśayati - darśanābhāvāt nāstīti। taddarśanābhāvāt tannāstītyarthaḥ। tarkitā āpāditā
tatpratiyogikaḥ abhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ tatsahakṛtenetyarthaḥ। upalabdheḥ anāhāryatvasūcanāya। tu paramārthaḥ। ālokasaṃyogādyasattvadaśāyāṃ yadyatra ghaṭaḥ syāt tarhi ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣamiti saṃkṣepaḥ।
tarkitetyādi। tarkitaṃ āropitaṃ yat pratiyogisattvam, tatsahakṛtenetyarthaḥ। itarakāraṇavirahaprayojyopalabdhyabhāvaḥ iti sūcitam। ata evāndhakāre upalambhābhāvasattve api na ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣam - ityāhuḥ।
indriyasya karaṇatvaṃ anupalabdheḥ sahakāritvaṃ ca tvayā kalpanīyam। adhikaraṇeti। nanu viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvākhyaḥ atiriktasambandhaḥ kalpanīyaḥ tvayetyata āha - viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāva iti। pratyakṣaṃ dvividham laukikam alaukikaṃ ceti। laukikatvaṃ ca
viṣayitāviśeṣaḥ। laukike ṣoḍhā saṃnikarṣaḥ kāraṇam। alaukike tu sāmānyalakṣaṇā, jñānalakṣaṇā, yogajadharmaśceti trividhā pratyāsattiḥ। tatra sāmānyalakṣaṇā dhūmatvādirūpā tajjñānarūpā vā। sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ svarūpaṃ viṣayo vā yasyā iti vyutpatteḥ। sā cāśrayāṇāṃ
nikhiladhūmādīnāṃ alaukikapratyakṣe upayujyate। asannikṛṣṭānāṃ pratyakṣājanakatvāt। jñānalakṣaṇā tu surabhi candanamiti cākṣuṣopanītabhāne saurabheṇa cakṣuṣo yogyasannikarṣābhāvāt। evaṃ kāraṇam iti saṃkṣepaḥ।।
nanvanupalabdherityādi। anupalabdhirnāma pratiyogiviṣayakapratyakṣābhavaḥ। abhūtalaṃ ghaṭābhāvavat' ityākārakaghaṭādyabhāvaviṣayakapramāṃ prati ghaṭopalabdhyabhāvaḥ kāraṇam। abhūtalaṃ ghaṭavat' iti ghaṭopalambhakāle ghaṭābhāvapramityanudayāt।
abhāvapramāṃ prati kāraṇatayā pṛthakpramāṇamiti bhāṭṭāḥ। naiyāyikāstu anupalabdhiḥ sahakāri kāraṇamātramityāśerate। avyāptistarkāpratihatiravasānaṃ viparyaye। iti tarkāṅgapañcakam।।'
pañca aṅgāni apekṣitāni। vyāptiḥ āpādakasya agnyabhāvādeḥ āpādyasya dhūmābhāvādeśca vyāpyavyāpakabhāvaḥ। tarkāpratihatiḥ - pratikūlatarkābhāvaḥ। viparyaye paryavasānam - yadi vahnyabhāvaḥ syāt ityevarūpe tadviparyaye paryavasānaṃ bhavati। aniṣṭatvam - āpādyasya
dhūmābhāvādeḥ aniṣṭatvaṃ praṣṭuḥ। ananukūlatvaṃ prativādipakṣasādhakatvābhāvaḥ। tatra viparyaye paryavasānaṃ pariṣkṛtyāha - āpādakābhāveti। āpādakaḥ vahnyabhāvaḥ tasyābhāvaḥ vahnyabhāvābhāvaḥ viparyaye paryavasānamityarthaḥ। prakṛte ayadyatra ghaṭaḥ syāt tarhi
āpādakābhāvasādhakaviparyaṃyapratiyogyāpādyakatvaṃ tarkasya। tathā ca darśitam। darśanābhāvādityasya ghaṭadarśanābhāvādityarthaḥ, nāstītyasya ghaṭābhāva ityarthaḥ। kevalānupalabdheḥ abhāvapratyakṣakāraṇatve ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣāpattiḥ। ataḥ yogyatāviśiṣṭānupalabdheḥ kāraṇatvaṃ
vaktavyam। yogyatā ca tarkitapratiyogisattvavirodhyupalabdhipratiyogikatvarūpā। pradarśitamiti bhāvaḥ। tarkitetyādimulaṃ vyācaṣṭetarkitā āpāditā ityādinā। yathāśrute pratiyogisattvasya
virodhinīti pratīyate। tadasaṅgatam - ghaṭopalabdheḥ ghaṭasattvavirodhitvābhāvāt। ataḥ sattvasya sattvaprasakteriti vyākhyātam। ghaṭasattvāroparūpaprasakteḥ ghaṭopalabdhi virodhinī। na hi prasañjayediti bhāvaḥ। anāhāryatvasūcanāyeti। anāhāryajñānasyaiva
virodhitvāditi bhāvaḥ। sattvasya sattvaprasakteriti vyākhyāne api āpāditatvarūpaṃ tarkitatvaṃ pratiyogisattvasyaiva na tu tatprasakteḥ। kiṃ paryavasānaṃ dṛśyate। mūlāttu pratiyogisattvarūpāpādakasyaiva prasañjitatvaṃ labhyate, na tvāpādyāyā upalabdheḥ। ataḥ tātparyārthamāha -
pratiyogisattāpādaneti। pratiyoginaḥ ghaṭādeḥ sattvasya āpādanena anupalabdhirityarthaḥ। yogyatāviśeṣaṇaprayojanamāha - ālokasaṃyogeti। āpādanāsambhaveneti। tathā ca anupalabdheḥ yogyānupalabdhistatra nāsti। ato na ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣamiti
bhāvaḥ। nanu yatra pratiyogisattvasya upalabdheścāpādānaṃ vinaiva - saṃkṣepa iti। pratiyogisattāpādanāpāditatvaṃ ca pratiyogisattāpādakakāpattiyogyatvam। ato nānupapattiriti bhāvaḥ। ata evāndhakāra iti।
ālokasaṃyogarūpakāraṇāntarābhāvaprayojyaḥ। tathā ca tatrābhāvāt na ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣamiti bhāvaḥ। dhūmatvādirūpetyādi। ādau lakṣaṇaśabda svarūpabodhakaḥ। dvitīye tu viṣayabodhakaḥ। prathamapakṣe
yāvaddhūmapratyakṣāpattirityasvārasyāt dvitīyapakṣānudhāvanam। cākṣuṣopanītabhāve iti। cākṣuṣaṃ yat smṛtasaurabhaviṣayakaṃ jñānamityarthaḥ।। AnTs anumitikaraṇam anumānam । parāmarśajanyaṃ jñānam anumitiḥ । vyāptiviśiṣṭapakṣadharmatājñānaṃ parāmarśaḥ । yathā vahnivyāpyadhūmavān ayaṃ parvata iti jñānaṃ parāmarśaḥ । taj janyaṃ parvato vahnimān iti jñānam anumitiḥ । yatra yatra dhūmas tatrāgnir iti sāhacaryaniyamo vyāptiḥ । vyāpyasya parvatādivṛttitvaṃ pakṣadharmatā ।।
anumānam। anumitikaraṇamiti। lakṣayatīti। pratyakṣopajīvakasaṅgatyā anumānaṃ nirūpayatītyarthaḥ। pratyakṣopajīvakasaṅgatyeti। pratyakṣakāryatvarūpayā saṅgatyā
ityarthaḥ। indriyeṇa mahānasādau vyāptipratyakṣādeva anumānaṃ bhavati। vyāptismaraṇarūpānumānaṃ prati vyāptipratyakṣasya anubhavavidhayā kāraṇatvāt। tathā ca kāryakāraṇabhāvarūpasaṅgatyā pratyakṣānantaramanumānanirūpaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। anena pramāṇayo
kāryakāraṇabhāva uktaḥ। anumityātmakapramiteḥ। jñeyaḥ। ।। jñānaṃ anumitiḥ।
anumitiṃ lakṣayati - parāmerśeti। nanu iti pratyakṣajananāt। na ca tatrānumitireva iti vācyam। na-pakṣatāsahakṛtaparāmarśajanyatvasya vivakṣitatvāt। parāmarśetīti।
pramāṇāntaratvaṃ sidhyatīti bhāvaḥ। viparītajñānottarapratyakṣaṃ prati nanviti। sthāṇupuruṣasaṃśayeti। idaṃ viruddhabhāvadvayakoṭikasaṃśayāṅgīkāreṇa। pare tu - sthāṇupuruṣeti। sthāṇutvatadabhāvapuruṣatvatadabhāvakoṭiketyarthaḥ - ityāhuḥ। puruṣa
aivati nirṇayasūcanāya। tatra - saṃśayottarapratyakṣasthale। anuvyavasāyavirodhāditi। idamupalakṣaṇam - apuruṣaṃ anuminomi' ityanuvyavasāyābhāvena pramāṇābhāvādityapi draṣṭavyam। pakṣateti। aitena avahnivyāpyadhūmavatparvatavānayaṃ deśaḥ' iti
parvataḥ' iti parāmarśasya kāraṇatve api na tatrātivyāptiḥ। saṅkṣepaḥ। vilakṣaṇapramātvāditi। pratyakṣapramiteḥ yat karaṇaṃ indriyaṃ anumitervilakṣaṇapramātvamiti bhāvaḥ। pramāṇāntaratvamiti।
pratyakṣāpekṣayā atiriktapramāṇatvamityarthaḥ। dīpikāyām nanvityādinā āśaṅkitā। tadidaṃ na saṅgacchate। saṃśayarūpaviparītajñānānantaraṃ aayaṃ puruṣaḥ' iti pratyakṣasyaiva asaṃbhavāt। tadvattābuddhiṃ prati pratyakṣajanakatvaṃ bhavatīti iśeṣadarśanasyeti।
vyāpyadharmadarśanasyetyarthaḥ। prakṛte apuruṣatvavyāpyakarādimān ayam' iti parāmarśo vivakṣitaḥ। bhāvadvayakoṭiketi। tatprakārakasaṃśayetyarthaḥ। sthāṇutvatadabhāveti। sthāṇutvaṃ tadabhāvaḥ
puruṣatvaṃ tadabhāvaśceti catuṣprakārakasaṃśayetyarthaḥ। asthāṇurvā na vā, puruṣo vā na vā' iti saṃśayasyākāraḥ। vikoṭikasaṃśayadvayaṃ vātra vivakṣitam। tatrānumitireva jāyata ityatra pramāṇābhāvādityarthaḥ। tathā ca aayaṃ puruṣaḥ' iti
sākṣātkāratvāvagāhī anuvyavasāyo nopapadyate। anumititvāvagāhī apuruṣamanuminomi' iti anuvyavasāya eva syāt। ato lakṣaṇasattvāt anumitilakṣaṇasyātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। dīpikāyāṃ pakṣatāsahakṛteti। tathā ca parāmarśajanyatvamātraṃ nānumiterlakṣaṇam।
api tu pakṣatāsahakṛto yaḥ parāmarśaḥ tajjanyatvam। matāntaramapyastīti darśitam। tathā hi - saṃśayottarapratyakṣamātre viśeṣadarśanaṃ vināpi ālokasamavadhānamātreṇaivopapatteḥ। tathāpi hetutvam। uktasthale ca vyañjakābhāvādhīnaḥ saṃśaya iti। adhikaṃ
draṣṭavyam। dvikoṭiketi। aparaḥ saṃśaya iti saṃśayadvayamityarthaḥ। pratyakṣahetutvāsambhavācca। tathā ca
pakṣatāsahakṛtaparāmarśajanayatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। tadāha prakāśikāyām saṃśayottarapratyakṣe jananīya iti। prayojanābhāveneti। pakṣatāyāḥ sahakāritvānaṅgīkāre anupapattyabhāvenetyarthaḥ। vakṣyamāṇahetunā ityarthaḥ। yadi
anumitilakṣaṇasya sattvāt ativyāptiḥ prasaktā। sāpi śakyata iti bhāvaḥ। tādṛśapratyakṣasya akṣatājanyatvābhāvāt। siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭasiddhyabhāvaḥ pakṣatā। sādhyasiddhiḥ anumitipratibandhikā। siddhisattve api aanuminuyām'
itīcchāyāmanumitidarśanāt siṣādhayiṣā uttejikā। tataśca hetutvena uktaparāmarśatvena hetutvābhāvāt। tathāpi uktaparāmarśatvāvacchinnajanakatā na niveśyeti bhāvaḥ। siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭasiddhyabhāvasyāpyanumitikāraṇatvam।
ghanagarjitena meghānumitau vyabhicāraḥ। ataḥ anyādṛśīṃ pakṣatāmāha - siṣādhayiṣeti। rsiṣādhayiṣāyāḥ sādhyānumitīcchāyāḥ samavāyena yaḥ tadviśiṣṭāyāḥ siddheḥ samavāyena abhāva ityarthaḥ। sādhyasiddhiḥ - sādhyatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭasādhyavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhiniścayaḥ। siddhau
siddhisattve apīti। atra siddhiśca aparvato vahnimān vahnivyāpyadhūmavāṃśca' iti samūhālambanarūpā। ataḥ parāmarśasampattiriti dhyeyam। pakṣatā' iti prācīnoktyupekṣāyāḥ bījamāha - yadyapītyādinā।
anumitihetutvāṅgīkārasya uddeśyam। tattu sādhyasaṃśayasya pakṣatātve api nirvahati। sādhyaniścayakāle sādhyasaṃśayarūpapakṣatāyāḥ ca sādhyasaṃśaya eva pakṣatā astu iti śaṅkiturbhāvaḥ। sādhyasaṃśayarūpapakṣatāyāḥ nānumitihetutvam। vināpi sādhyasaṃśayaṃ
samādhāturāśayaḥ। kāraṇābhāve api kāryotpattirūpo vivakṣitaḥ। anyādṛśīmiti। sādhyasaṃśayādanyavidhāmityarthaḥ। meghavān dhanagarjajavattvādityanumānamatra vivakṣitam।
siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭetyādi। yatra sādhyaniścayarūpā siddhirasti asti tadānumitirbhavati। siddhyabhāvamātrasya pakṣatātve sā na syāt, tatra sattvāt। atastatra pakṣatāsampattaye siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭeti siddherviśeṣaṇaṃ dattam।
siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭasiddhyabhāvasyākṣatatayā pakṣatā nirvahati। evaṃ ca siṣādhayiṣā uttejiketi phalitam। uttejakatvaṃ ca pratibandhakasamavadhānakālīnakāryotpādakaprayojaktvam। mantrāderuttejakatvam। uttejakābhāvaviśiṣṭapratibandhakābhāvasya
kāryotpattiṃ prati hetutvāt। bhāvaḥ। siṣādhayiṣā nāma sādhyānumitiviṣayakecchā। siṣādhayiṣāniṣṭhapratiyogitānirūpako abhāvaḥ। tatra pratiyogitāyāṃ samavāyasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā yatra siddhiḥ
sattvena tadabhāvarūpapakṣatā na syāt। tanniveśe ca tatra viśiṣṭābhāvarūpā pakṣatā nirvahatīti। evaṃ siṣādhayiṣāvirahavaiśiṣṭyaṃ sasiddhau sāmānādhikaraṇyasambanadhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ niveśanīyam। sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca svādhikaraṇavṛttitvam।
samavāyasambandhena। tathā ca siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭā yā siddhiḥ tadabhāvaḥ pakṣatā। svaṃ - samavāyasambanadhena vṛttimatī ya siddhiḥ tadabhāva iti yāvat। tatra siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭasiddhereva sattvena pakṣatā nopapadyeta।
pakṣatānupapattiḥ। evaṃ vṛttitve samavāyasambanadhāvacchinnatvāniveśe pakṣatā prasajyeta। ataḥ samavāyasambandhāvacchinnatvasya sāmānādhikaraṇyaghaṭakavṛttitve niveśaḥ। evaṃ siddhyabhāvaḥ siddhiniṣṭhapratiyogitānirūpako abhāvaḥ। tatra
pratiyogitāyāṃ samavāyasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśyam। anyathā prasajyeta। tadetatsarvamabhisandhāyāha - prakāśikāyām - siṣādhayiṣāyāḥ sādadhyānumitīcchāyā ityādi। svarūpasamavāyayobhayaghaṭiteti। sāmānādhikaraṇyaghaṭakādhikaraṇatāyāṃ
niveśanīyamiti bhāvaḥ। siṃddheḥ samavāyenābhāva iti। siddhiniṣṭhasamavāyasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāva ityarthaḥ। pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭa ityādi। ityarthaḥ। dravyatvena parvatāvagāhi adravyaṃ vahnimat'
pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। evaṃ aparvato dravyavān' prakāratāyāṃ sādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। evaṃ prakāratāyāṃ sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvamapi niveśanīyam। anyathā aparvataḥ ityanumitipratibandhakatvāpatteḥ।
siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭeti viśeṣaṇaṃ dattam। tacca tadaiva samavadhānaṃ syāt। tacca durghaṭam। tathā hi- yatra prathamaṃ siddhiḥ anantaraṃ siṣādhayiṣā, siṣāṣayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭatvaviśeṣaṇam। yatra krameṇa
siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭatvaniveśe api pakṣatā na nirvahati। yatra tu parāmarśanāśāt parāmarśarūpakāraṇavaikalyāt nānumitiḥ। jñānayorvā jñānecchayorvā ekakṣaṇotpattikatvaṃ tu nāṅgīkriyate। sārthakatvamityāśaṅkyāha - atra siddhiścetyādinā। pakṣatāghaṭakībhūtā
vivakṣitā। ayameva sādhyaniścayarūpatvāt sādhyavyāpyaniścayarūpatvācca siddhyātmakaparāmarśa iti vyavahriyate। tathā ca yatra ādau uktākāraḥ nirvahati। ataḥ siṣādhayiṣāvirahaviśiṣṭatvaṃ siddheḥ viśeṣaṇam। tatra sārthakyamupapādanīyamiti bhāvaḥ। ataḥ parāmarśasampattiriti।
melanamityarthaḥ। ।। vyāptiviśiṣṭapakṣadharmatājñānaṃ parāmarśaḥ। yathā avahnivyāpyadhūmavān ayaṃ parvataḥ' iti jñānaṃ parāmarśaḥ। tajjanyaṃ
aparvato vahnimān' iti jñānamanumitiḥ। vyāptīti। vyāptiviṣayakaṃ yat pakṣadharmatājñānaṃ sa parāmarśa ityarthaḥ। parāmarśamabhinīya darśayati - yatheti। anumitimabhinīya darśayati - tajjanyamiti। parāmarśajanyamityarthaḥ।
karmadhārayamaṅgīkaroti - vyāptiviṣayakamiti। nirgalitārthaḥ। abhinīya - abhilāpakaśabdamuccārya। vyāptiviśiṣṭapakṣadharmatājñānamityatretyādi। yatra liṅgaṃ dhūmavān' ityanumitiḥ jāyate। yadi tu vastuto vyāptiviśiṣṭe
parāmarśatvābhāvāt tajjanyajñānasya anumititvaṃ na syāt। ataḥ vyāptiviṣayakaṃ yat pakṣadharmatvāvagāhi jñānaṃ tat parāmarśaḥ। iti bhāvaḥ। vyāptyavacchinneti। vyāptyavacchinna yā hetuniṣṭhā prakāratā
tannirūpako niścayaḥ parāmarśa ityarthaḥ। bhavati ca avahnivyāpyadhūmavān parvata' iti niścayaḥ tādṛśaḥ। vyāptyavacchinnatvāt। vyāptyavacchinnatvaṃ ca sādhyaniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpitavyāptiniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpitatvam। tena
avyāpyadhūmavān parvataḥ' iti jñāne nātivyāptiḥ। adhūmo prakāratayā abhānāt। ato na tatrātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca parāmarśa iti niṣkarṣaḥ। tena adravyavyāpyadhmavān parvataḥ', ityanumitihetubhūtaparāmarśatvaṃ na prasajyata ityavadheyam।
nirgalitārtha iti। niṣkṛṣṭārtha ityarthaḥ। abhilāpakaśabdamuccāryeti। ākārapradarśakaśabdamuccāryetyarthaḥ। kāyikaceṣṭārūpasyābhinayasyātrāsambhavāt। ।।
agniḥ iti sāhacaryaniyamaḥ vyāptiḥ। yatreti। yatra dhūmastatrāgniriti vyāpterabhinayaḥ। sāhacaryaniyamaḥ iti lakṣaṇam। sāhacaryaṃ sāmānādhiṅkaraṇyam, tasya niyamaḥ। vyāptirityarthaḥ।
sambhavati; aidaṃ vācyam jñeyatvāt' ityādau avyāpteḥ। sādhyābhāvāprasiddherityālocyāha - hetusamānādhikaraṇeti। astīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। adhūmavān vahneḥ' ityādau tu dhūma iti nātivyāptiḥ। na ca avahnimān dhūmāt' ityādau
pratiyogitānavacchedaka-sādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnetyarthatātparyaṅkatayādoṣāt। pratiyogitāyāṃ sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। kṣatiḥ। hetupadaṃ hetutāvacchedakāvacchinnaparam। ataḥ adravyam hetvadhikaraṇaguṇādiniṣṭhatve api dravyatvābhāvasya nāvyāptiḥ।
hetutāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnā grāhyā। tena avahnimān dhūmāt' nāvyāptiḥ। na caivamapi akapisaṃyogī evadvṛkṣatvāt' ityādau vācyam। hetusamānādhikaraṇātyantābhāve pratiyogivaiyadhikaraṇyasya niveśanīyatvāt। kevalānvayisādhyake tādṛśasya ghaṭābhāvādeḥ
prasiddhatvāt nāvyāptiriti। adhikaṃ asmadīya-maṇidīdhitivyākhyāyā buddhikuśalairanusandheyam। sādhyābhāvāprasiddheriti। sādhyasya vācyatvasya kevalānvayitvena kevalānvayisādhyakasaddhetāvavyāptirityarthaḥ।
ityarthatātparyakatayādoṣāditi। tathā ca vacchinnasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ vyāptiḥ। aparvato vahnimān ghaṭatva-mahānasīyavahnitvādikam। tatpratiyogitānavacchedakaṃ lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। parvato dhūmavān vahneḥ ityādau hetuḥ vahniḥ
vyāptasya lakṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। pratiyogitāyāṃ sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyamityādi। aparvanto samavāyasambandhāvacchinnavahnitvāvacchinnapratiyogitāko abhāvaḥ।
tatpratiyogitāyāṃ avacchedakameva vahnitvaṃ ityavyāptiḥ syāt। sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। niveśe ca saṃyogasambandhāvacchinnatvāsambhavāt। tathā ca ghaṭatvādi anavacchedakaṃ ca vahnitvaṃ bhavatīti nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। na
kṣatiriti। tathā ca vyāptirityetāvatā phalitam। hetupadaṃ hetutāvacchedakāvacchinnaparamityādi। aghaṭo dravyam viśiṣṭaśuddhayoranatirekāt। hetoradadhikaraṇaṃ guṇakarmaṇī api;
dravyatvatve pratiyogitānavacchedakatvābhāvāt avyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya hetutāvacchedakāvacchinnahetvadhikaraṇatvaṃ niveśanīyam। guṇe tadavacchinnādhikaraṇatvaṃ na sambabhavati। guṇaḥ karma ca guṇakarmānyatvaviśiṣṭasattāvaditi pratītyabhāvāt। ataḥ
nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca sādadhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ vyāptiḥ। hetutāvacchadedakasambandhāvacchinnā grāhyeti। avahnimān dhūmāt' tatpratiyogitāvacchedakameva sādhyatāvacchedakaṃ vahnitvamityavyāptiḥ।
niveśanīyam। prakṛte tatra sattvāt। api tu parvatādireva bhavatīti nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। vahnisāmānyābhāvasya - vahnitvāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvasya। dhūsamavāyiniṣṭhatve api -
samavāyasambandheya dhūtādhikaraṇadhūmāvayavavṛttitve api। tathā ca tāvacchedakāvacchinnasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ vyāptiḥ। hetutāvacchedakāvacchinnahetuniṣṭhādheyatānirūpitādhikaraṇatāvadityarthaḥ। dhyavacchidyate।
na caivamapīta। aayaṃ mūlabhāgāvacchedena kapisaṃyogasyābhāvāt। tathā ca kapisaṃyogatvarūpaṃ sādhyatāvacchedakamityavyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। pratiyogivaiyadhikaraṇyasya niveśanīyatvāditi। tathā ca vṛkṣavṛttiḥ
vartamānatayā pratiyogisamānādhikaraṇo na pratiyogivyadhikaraṇaḥ। bhavatīti nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। sādhyābhāvavadavṛttitvasya vyāptitve iti। tathā ca hetoḥ jñeyatvasyādhikaraṇaṃ bhūtalādiḥ nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ।
tādṛśa iti। pratiyogivyadhikaraṇa ityarthaḥ। ativyāptyāpatteriti। saṃyogābhāvavati guṇādau sattāyāḥ sattvāt ayaṃ heturvyabhicārī। atra hetvadhikaraṇaṃ sattādhikaraṇaṃ guṇādi
saṃyogatvarūpaṃ sādhyatāvacchedakamityativyāptirvāraṇīyā। di tu saṃyogatve aratītyativyāptiḥ prasajyate। pratiyogivyadhikaraṇatvaṃ bhāvaḥ। vivakṣitam। pratiyogyanadhikaraṇatvaṃ ca
pratiyogitāvacchedakāvacchinnānadhikaraṇatvam। yathāśrute aghaṭaḥ guṇakarmānyatvaviśiṣṭasattāvān jāteḥ' ityatrātivyāpteḥ। ayaṃ vyabhicārī hetuḥ। atra jāteradhikaraṇe guṇe vartamānasya sattvāt ativyāptiḥ prasajati। pratiyogitāvacchedakāvacchinneti
nātivyāptiḥ। evaṃ pratiyogitāvacchedakasambandhena pratiyogyanadhikaraṇamityapi vaktavyam। anyathā aātmā jñānavān dravyatvāt' ityatrātivyāpteḥ। jñānābhāvavati ghaṭādau vyabhicārī। atra hetoḥ dravyatvasyādhikaraṇaṃ ghaṭādi tanniṣṭhaḥ abhāvaḥ
ityādāvavyāptiḥ। kapisaṃyogatve astīti। ato niṣkṛṣṭārthamāha - pratiyogyanadhikaraṇī bhūteti। pratiyogivyadhikaraṇahetvadhikaraṇavṛttītyantasya pratiyogyanadhikaraṇībhūtahetvadhikaraṇavṛttītyarthaḥ। saṃyogī
tatpratiyogitāvacchedakameva saṃyogatvamiti nātivyāptiḥ। kapisaṃyogatve astīti nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। ghaṭādiriti। ataḥ jñānatve astītyativyāptiḥ prasajyate।
tatpratiyogitāvacchedakatvameva jñānatvasyeti nātivyāptiḥ। tathā ca vacchinnasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ vyāptiriti phalitam। tadidamabhisandhāyāha - adhikaṃ asmadīyamaṇidīdhitivyākhyāyāmiti। parvatādivṛttitvaṃ pakṣadharmatā।
AnTs anumānaṃ dvividhaṃ svārthaṃ parārthaṃ ca । tatra svārthaṃ svānumitihetuḥ । tathā hi svayam eva bhūyo darśanena yatra dhūmas tatra agnir iti mahānasādau vyāptiṃ gṛhītvā parvatasamīpaṃ gatas tadgate cāgnau sandihānaḥ parvate dhūmaṃ paśyan vyāptiṃ smarati yatra dhūmas tatrāgnir iti । tadantaraṃ vahnivyāpyadhūmavān ayaṃ parvata iti jñānam utpadyate । ayam eva liṅgaparāmarṣaṃ ity ucyate । tasmāt parvato vahnimān iti jñānam anumitir utpadyate । tad etat svārthānumānam । yat tu svayaṃ dhūmād agnim anumāya parapratipattyarthaṃ pañcāvayavavākyaṃ prayukte tat parārthānumānam । yathā parvato vahnimān dhūmavattvāt । yo yo dhūmavān sa vahnimān yathā mahānasaḥ । tathā cāyam । anena pratipāditāl lingāt paro'py agniṃ pratipadyate ।। dvividham-svārtham, parārtham ceti। sādhyaṃ tadadhikaraṇavṛttitvaṃ dhyāptirityarthaḥ। pakṣadharmatāsvarūpamāha - vyāpyasyeti।
anumānamiti। svārthaṃ svānumitihetuḥ। tathā hi - sandihānaḥ vyāptiṃ smarati ayatra dhūmastatrāgniḥ' iti। tadanantaraṃ avahnivyāpyadhūmavān ayaṃ parvataḥ' iti jñānamutpadyate। ayameva
liṅgaparāmarśa ityucyate। tasmāt aparvato ityanumitirutpadyate। tadetat svārthānumānam। darśayati - svameveti। vyabhicāropalabdheḥ bhūyodarśanena kathaṃ vyāptigraha iti cet-na।
vyabhicārajñānavirahasahakṛtasahacārajñānasya vyāptigrāhakatvāt। vyabhicārajñānaṃ niścayaḥ śaṅkā ca। tadvirahaḥ kvacit tarkāt, kvacit svatassiddha eva। dhūmāgnyorvyāptigrahe kāryakāraṇabhāvabhaṅgaprasaṅgalakṣaṇaḥ tarko vyabhicāraśaṅkānivartakaḥ।
sakalavahnidhūmayorasannikarṣāt kathaṃ vyāptigraha iti cet - na। vahnitvadhūmatvarūpasāmānyapratyāsattyā sakalavahnidhūmajñānasambhavāt। tasmāditi। liṅgaparāmarśādityarthaḥ। svārthānumānamiti। svasyārthaḥ prayojanaṃ
svīyasaṃśayanivṛttiprayojakānumānamityarthaḥ। smṛtihetutvādityarthaḥ। kathaṃ vyāptigraha itīti। bhūyodarśanasya vyāptiniścayahetutvaṃ na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। adhikaraṇeṣu darśanamiti vārthaṃḥ। nādyaḥ, ekatraiva sahacāradarśanadhārayā
vyāptiniścayaprasaṅgāt। na dvitīyatṛtīyau, aetadrūpavān vyāptyaniścayaprasaṅgādityapi bodhyam। maṇikārasiddhāntamavalambyāha - vyabhicārajñānaviraheti। vyāptigrāhakatvāditi। vyāptiśca tāvacchedakāvacchinnasādhyādhikaraṇavṛttitāviśiṣṭahetutāvacchedakarūpaiva।
sāmānādhikaraṇyāntasya rāsabhādisādhāraṇyāt। dhūmatvādeḥ svarūpato vyāptitvamityavacchedyāvacchedakayoraikye api na kṣatiḥ। itthaṃ ca viparītagrahābhāvavidhayā hetuḥ। dhyeyam।
hetuvyāpakasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyameva vyāptiḥ। na ca vyāpteḥ bhūyastvābhāveneti। bahutaratvarūpānekatvātmakabhūyastvābhāvenetyarthaḥ। iṣṭāpatterayogāditi vācyam। yaddharmāṃvacchinnavyāpakatvaṃ
anumitihetutvopagamenādoṣāt। ata eva vyāptiśarīre lāghavamiti dik। śaṅkāceti। vyābhicārasaṃśayasyāpi tatsādhāraṇavyabhicārajñānatvāvacchinnābhāvo heturiti hṛdayam।
tadvirahaḥ - vyabhicāraśaṅkāvirahaḥ। kvaciriti tarkābhāvetaranikhilakāraṇasamavadhānasthala ityarthaḥ। kvacit svatassiddha eveti। itarakāraṇavirahasthale tādṛśakāraṇavirahaprayukta evetyarthaḥ। tathā ca tatra tarkāpekṣā
neti bhāvaḥ। dhūmāgnyorvyāptigrahe utpatsyamāne ityanvayaḥ। sa ca tarkaḥ adhūmo yadi vahnivyabhicārī syāt tarhi vahnijanyo na syāt' ityākārako bodhyaḥ। sambhavati। tathā ca parvatīyadhūmadarśanena vyāptismaraṇāsambhavāt
parāmarśānupapattirityāśayena āśaṅkate - nanviti। sambhavati। evaṃ ca parvatīyadhūme api vyāptergṛhītatvena dhūmadarśanena vahnitvadhūmatveti। matvā vyācaṣṭesvasyārtha iti। ekasambandhijñānamiti।
vyāptyākhyasambandhasya sambandhinau dvau hetuḥ sādhyaśca। tayoḥ ekasya iti bhāvaḥ। vastutastu dhūmadarśanaṃ na tu ekasambandhijñānamiti vidhayeti dhyeyam। pariṣkarotivyāptiścetyādinā। yadyapi pūrvaṃ
tādṛśasāmānādhikaraṇyākrāntatvāt vahnivyāpyatvaṃ prasajyeta। ataḥ pariṣkāryam। rāsabhe vahnisāmānādadhikaraṇyasattve api hetutāvacchedakībhūtadhūmatvavattvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। na ca dhūmatvasyāvacchedakatvāsambhavāt। avacchedyāvacchedakabhāvasya
bhedaniyatatvāditi vācyam। dhūmatvatvena rūpeṇa dhūtvaṃ vyāptiḥ svarūpato dhūmatvaṃ vyāptyavacchedakamityadoṣāt। cet-śrūyatām। sāmānādhikaraṇyaviśiṣṭahetutāvacchedakamityasya samānādadhikaraṇavṛttihetutāvacchedakamityarthaḥ। tathā
adoṣāditi। yadyapi evetyarthaḥ। ākāraḥ। dhūma iti vyabhicārajñānasya ākāraḥ। vyāptijñāne sādhyatāvacchedake
sādhyatāvacchedake pratiyogitāvacchedakatvaṃ bhāsate। tatra pratibandhakābhāvavidhayā vyāptijñānaṃ prati hetuḥ। vyāptijñāne bhāsate। sādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyagraha eva ityucyate। tādṛśasahacāragrahaḥ sādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaviśiṣṭo
heturiti। dhikamasmadīyapañcalakṣaṇīvyākhyāyāṃ bālabodhinyāṃ draṣṭavyam। sādhyādhikaraṇavṛttitāviśiṣṭeti। hetutāvacchedake sādhyādhikaraṇavṛttitāvaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyasambandhena। vahnyadhikaraṇavṛttitvasya ca ekatra dhūme sattvāt।
phalitor'thaḥ। viparītagrahābhāvavidhayeti। tadabhāvavattājñānābhāvatvenetyarthaḥ। atra tadvattābuddhiḥ pratiyogitānavacchedakatvavat sādhyatāvacchedakamiti buddhiḥ। pratiyogitāvacchedakaṃ sādhyatāvacchedakamiti buddhiḥ।
ityata āha-adhikamiti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ hetuvaiśiṣṭyaṃ cādheyatāsambandhena। tādṛśavyāptijñānaṃ prati viśiṣṭa sāmānādadhikaraṇyarūpasahacāragraho heturiti। bhūdityāśayenāha - vastunastviti।
bhramātmakarāsabhaliṅgakavahnyanumityāpattiḥ ityarthaḥ। yadyapi na tvavyāpyaliṅgakānumiterityāśayenaivamuktamiti dhyeyam। samādhatteyaddharmāvacchinneti। dhūmatvāvacchinnavyāpakatvaṃ vyāptighaṭakam, tasyānumitihetutvamiti bhāvaḥ।
vāraṇena vyāpte rāsabhādisādhāraṇye api kṣativirahādevetyarthaḥ। sāmānyalakṣaṇetyādi। sannikarṣaḥ। vahnitvadhūmatvātmakasaṃnikarṣeṇa pratyakṣitam। ataḥ dhūmadarśanena
bhavitumarhatīti bhāvaḥ। etena vyāptijñānasya bhramatvāt bhavati। vyāpte rāsabhasādhāraṇye ca bhramatvamiti bhāvaḥ। tatsmṛtiritiśaṅkā parāstā।
grahasambhavāt। ।। tatparārthānumānam। parārthānumānamāha - yattviti। yacchabdasya
atatparārthānumānam' iti tacchabdenānvayaḥ। parasamavetānumitikaraṇaliṅgaparāmarśor'thaḥ। ata eva manasi kṛtvā mūlamavatārayati - parārthānumānamāheti। madhyasthasyeti। yadyapi paraśabdaḥ anyaparaḥ, tathā
cānyasamavetānumitikaraṇamityeva svarasataḥ parārthānumānaśabdārthaḥ। vyākhyānaṃ kṛtam। parārthānumānaprayojaka iti। parārthānumānasya kāraṇabhūte pañcāvayavakamahāvākyarūpe nyāye। aupacārikaḥ
lākṣaṇikaḥ। kāraṇe kāryopacāraḥ parārthānumānaśabda iti yāvat। - ittham। pratijñādibhiḥ pañcabhirvākyaiḥ prathamataḥ attadvākyārthabodhaḥ jāyate। tarta ekavākyatāmāpannaiḥ pañcabhirvākyairekamahāvākyārthabodho jāyate। tataḥ tatsahakṛtena
parārthānumānaprayojakatvaṃ pañcāvayavavākyātmakanyāyasyeti। iti। ।। liṅgaparāmarśaḥ। kāryabhūtaliṅgaparāmarśavācakasya
ityarthaḥ। pratijñādipratyekavākyārthaviṣayakāḥ pañca bodhāḥ jāyante। dhūmajñānajñāpyetyādi। upanayārthe labhyate। tathā hi - dhūmāditi pañcamyantārthaḥ
dhūmajñānanirūpitajñāpyatvam। tasyāśrayatāsambandhena pratijñāghaṭakavahnipadārthe vahnāvanvayaḥ। vahnimatpadārthasyābhedena parvatapadārthe tasyābhedasambandhena upanayaghaṭakedapadārthe parvate anvayaḥ। udāharaṇe vahnipadasya dhūmavyāpakavahnau lakṣaṇā।
yatpadatatpadayathāmahānasapadānāṃ tātparyagrāhakatā। dhūmavataḥ abhedena dhūmavyāpakavahnimatyanvayaḥ। tasyacābhedena upanayasthedampadārthe anvayaḥ। abādhitāsatpratipakṣitadhūmajñānajñāpya upanayasthedampadārthe anvayaḥ। upanayavākyarthastu vahnivyāpyadhūmavadabhinnaḥ
parvatārthakatvācceti bhāvaḥ। mahānasaḥ, tathā ca ayam, tasmāt tathā iti। anena vākyena pratipāditāt liṅgāt paro apyagniṃ pratipadyate। AnTs pratijñāhetūdāharaṇopanayanigamāni pañcāvayavaḥ । parvato vahnimān iti pratijñā । dhūmavattvād iti hetuḥ । yo yo dhūmavān sa so'gnimān yathā mahānasa ity udāharaṇam । tathā cāyam iti upanayaḥ । tasmāt tatheti nigamanam ।।
pratijñāhetūdāharaṇopanayanigamanāni pañcāvayavāḥ। parvato vahnimān iti pratijñā। dhūmavattvāt iti hetuḥ। yo yo dhūmavān so agnimān yathā mahānasa ityudāharaṇam। tathā cāyaṃ ityupanayaḥ। tasmāt tatheti nigamanam।
pañcāvayavavākyamudāharati - yatheti। avayavasvarūpamāha - pratijñeti। udāhṛtavākye pratijñādivibhāgamāha - parvato vahnimāniti। sādhyavattayā pakṣavacanam pratijñā। pañcamyantaṃ liṅgapratipādakaṃ hetuḥ। vyāptipratipādakam udāharaṇam।
vyāptiviśiṣṭaliṅgapratipādakaṃ vacanaṃ upanayaḥ। hetusādhyavattayā pakṣapratipādakaṃ vacanaṃ nigamanam। abādhitatvādikaṃ nigamanaprayojanam। pratijñādyavayavapañcakasamudāyatvaṃ nyāyalakṣaṇaṃ bodhyam। anena
pratijñādyavayavapañcakasamudāyaprayojyaliṅgaparāmarśādityarthaḥ। sādhyavattayā pakṣavacanamiti। sādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinna-sādhyaprakāraka-pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinna-pakṣaviśeṣyakabodhajanakavākyamityarthaḥ। sādhyatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhijñānamiti tayornirāsaḥ।
vākyapadasya nyāyāvayavavākyaparatvāt nyāyabahirbhūtavākyavyudāsaḥ। evamagre api। aayaṃ na daṇḍāt taddaṇḍasaṃyogājanyadravayatvāt' liṅgapratipādakamiti। hetupratipādakamityarthaḥ। vyāptipratipādakamiti। prakṛtahetumati
prakṛtahetuvyāpakasādhyabodhakavākyamityarthaḥ। kathamudāharaṇasya hetuvyāpakatvaviśiṣṭe sādhye nirūḍhalakṣaṇayā। na ca dviruktayatpadasya vaiyarthyamiti śaṅkyam, tādṛśatātparyagrāhakatayā sārthakyāt। atha vā vyāpakatābodho mānasaḥ। tathā ca
dik। vyāptiviśiṃṣṭaliṅgapratipādakamiti। pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭaviśeṣyakaprakṛtasādhyavyāpyahetuprakārakabodhajanakavākyamityarthaḥ। śeṣapūraṇena pradarśitārtha eva yathākathañcit saṅgamanīyaḥ। hetusādhyavattayāpakṣapratipādakaṃ vacanamiti।
hetujñānajñāpyatvaviśiṣṭasādhyavadviṣayakabodhajanakavākyamityarthaḥ। uttarakālamabādhitāsatpratipakṣitatvaviṣayakabodho mānaso draṣṭavyaḥ। pariṣkṛtamāha - sādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnetyādi। parvato vanhimān parvato vahnimāniti vākye lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ।
udāharaṇavākye ativyāptiḥ। parvatatvāvacchinnaviśeṣyakatvābhāvāt na doṣaḥ। atathā cāyam' ityupanayavākye ativyāptiḥ। tajjanyasya parvatatvāvacchinnaviśeṣyakatvāt।
doṣaḥ। evaṃ pakṣaviśeṣyakatvamātroktau adravyaṃ vahnimat' iti vākye ativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviśeṣyakatvaniveśaḥ। aparvato sādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviśeṣyaketyuktam। aparvato dravyavān,
vaktavyam। nyāyabahirbhūteti। pañcāvayavakanyāyānantargatasya udāsīnasya aparvato vahnimān' iti vākyasya nirāsaḥ। hetvādivākyasamānākāre vākye nātivyāptiriti jñeyamityarthaḥ।
pañcamyantaṃ liṅgapratipādakaṃ heturiti dīpikā। pañcamyantatve sati liṅgaviṣayakabodhajanakatve sati vākyatvamiti tadarthaḥ। asti ca dhūmāditi bhāgasya tathātvamiti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। pañcamyantatve satītyanupādāne udāharaṇāditriṣvativyāptiḥ। teṣāmapi
liṅgabodhakatvāt। ataḥ pañcamyantatve satītyuktam। aayaṃ na daṇḍāt liṅgabodhakatve satītyuktam। prakṛtasādhyānumitihetuliṅgabodhakatvaṃ tadartha iti na doṣaḥ। nātivyāptiḥ। tasya bhāgasya nyāyāvayavanigamanāvayavatve api
nyāyāvayavatvāsvīkārāt। na caivaṃ sati aayaṃ na daṇḍāt' iti viśeṣaṇaṃ vyarthamiti vācyam। tarhi nyāyāvayavapratijñāvayavasyāpi nyāyāvayavatvādativyāptiprasakteḥ। na ca tarhi nigamanāvayave tasmāditi bhāge ativyāptiriti vācyam। pañcamyantatvamityanena
vivakṣitatvenādoṣādityāśayāt। nanu vyāptiviṣayakabodhajanakavākyatvamudāharaṇasya lakṣaṇamityavagamyate। tacca upanayanigamanayorativyāptam। tayorapi vyāptipratipādakatvāt। upanayaghaṭakatathāpadasya
prakṛtahetumatīti। ayo yo dhūmavān sa so agnimān' tatpadaṃ ca lakṣaṇātātparyagrāhakam। tathā ca dhūmavān dhūmavyāpakavahnimānityarthaḥ। tena lakṣaṇamiti labhyate। upanayanigamanayoḥ īdṛśalakṣaṇābhāvāt
nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। nanvevamapi adhūmavān dhūmavyāpakavahnimān' ityādivākyānāṃmapyudāharaṇatvāpattiḥ। na ceṣṭāpattiḥ। kathakasampradāyavirodhāt ityata āha - digiti। udāharaṇatvaṃ vivakṣitam। ato na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। ādhikamanyatra।
pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭetyādi। vahnivyāpyadhūmavāniti vākye ativyāptivāraṇāya pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭaviśeṣyakatvaniveśaḥ। prakṛtasādhyavyāpyatvaniveśaḥ। prakṛtasādhyaniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpitavyāptiniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpitahetuniṣṭhaprakāratāśālibodhajanakavākyamityarthaḥ।
yo dhūmastatprakārakatvādativyāptiritiśaṅkāyāḥ nāvasaraḥ। sādhyavattayā ca pakṣapratipādakatvaṃ nigamanasya lakṣaṇamityavagamyate। tathā sati nigamane asambhavaḥ। atasmāt tathā' iti nigamanavākyasya sādhyavattayā pakṣabodhakatve api hetumattayā pakṣabodhakatvābhāvāt।
pañcamyarthasya sādhye anvayena pakṣe anvayābhāvāt। evaṃ adhūmavān vahnimāśca parvataḥ' iti vākye ativyāptiśca। ato vyācaṣṭe - hetujñāneti। pañcamyāḥ jñānajñāpyatvamarthaḥ। jñāne viṣayatāsambandhenānvayaḥ। tathāśabdasya sādhyavānityarthaḥ। sādhye
pañcamyarthasya jñānajñāpyatvasyāśrayatayānvayaḥ। tathā ca nigamanāt jāyata iti nigamanavākye lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। - uttarakālamiti। tathā ca pūrvoktarītyā śābdabodhānantaraṃ ayaṃ heturabādhitaḥ asatpratipakṣaśceti mānasaṃ jñānamutpadyata iti bhāvaḥ।
AnTs svārthānumitiparārthānumityor liṅgaparāmarśa eva karaṇam । tasmāl liṅgaparāmarśā'numānam ।। svārthānumitiparārthānumityoḥ liṅgaparāmarśa eva karaṇam। tasmāt liṅgaparāmarśo anumānam। - svārtheti।
viśiṣṭaparāmarśaḥ kimarthamaṅgīkartavya iti cet-na। parāmarśasyaiva kāraṇatvāt। liṅgaṃ na karaṇam, atītādau vyabhicārāt। avyāpāravat kāraṇaṃ karaṇam' iti mate parāmarśandvārā vyāptijñānaṃ karaṇam। tajjanyatve sati tajjanyajanako
vyāpāraḥ। anumānamupasaṃharati - tasmāditi। gauravam। avahnivyāpyo dhūmaḥ, dhūmavān parvataḥ' iti jñānadvayasya nanviti। vahnivyāpyavānayamiti। atra tvadabhimatakāraṇasya asattvena vyabhicārāt na jñānadvayasya kāraṇatvaṃ sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। kathañcidapi
śābdeti। kalpanālāghavenetyarthaḥ। tathā hi - jñānadvaye viśiṣṭaparāmarśe tatkalpanasyaiva laghīyastvamiti। jñānadvayasādhāraṇyenana tanmate mantavyam। naiyāyikamate tu - kāraṇatāvacchedakalāghavam avadheyam। vinigamanāviraheṇa
- liṅgaṃ na karaṇamiti। bhūtabhaviṣyaddhūmāderasattvāditi bhāvaḥ। karaṇamiti dhyeyam। karaṇe ativyāptivāraṇāya - tajjanyatve satīti। śaṅkitam। śaṅkeyaṃ nopapadyate। viśiṣṭaparāmarśādeva
naiyāyikena vaktuṃ śakyatvāt। ataḥ śaṅkiturāśayamabhivyanakti - nanu viśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyetyādinā। tathā ca viśiṣṭaparāmarśasya ananyathāsiddhatvaṃ niyatapūrvavṛttitvaṃ cetyubhayaṃ kalpanīyam। kalpanīyam। jñānadvayasya tu ananyathāsiddhatvamātraṃ kalpanīyam, na tu
niyatapūrvavṛttitvamapi, kḷptatvāt। ato lāghavāt bhāva ityāśayaḥ। yatra avahnivyāpyavānayam' iti śabdaśravaṇāt prābhākaramataṃ dīpikāyāṃ khaṇḍitam। nanu prābhākaramate kāraṇatvamiṣyate। avahnivyāpyavānayam' iti śabdaparāmarśasyāpi
kathañcidapīti। yaṃa bhāvaḥ - vyāptijñānapakṣadharmatājñānayoḥ vahnimān' ityunamityāpattiḥ। ato vyāpyatāvacchedakatayā gṛhītadharmāṃvacchinne pakṣadharmatāvagāhi jñānatvena kāraṇatvaṃ vaktavyam। kāryotpattyā vyatirekavyabhicāraḥ prābhākaramate durvāra iti।
sphoraṇāyeti। dhūmatvopasthāpakapadābhāvādityarthaḥ। tathā hātyādi। niyatapūrvavṛttitvaṃ cetyubhaya kalpanīyam। tatra viśiṣṭaparāmarśasya naiyāyikamate lāghavamiti bhāvaḥ। sāmyamityāśaṅkyāha - vastutastviti।
dhūmavān' ityākārakaḥ। tathā coktaniścayaviśiṣṭoktaniścayatvaṃ prābhākaramate anumitikāraṇatāvacchedakam। naiyāyikamate tu vyāptiviśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhitvam। tattu dhūmatvānavagāhini vahnivyāpyavānayamiti śābdaparāmarśeṃ'pyasti। ataḥ
kāraṇatāvacchedakalāghavāt naiyāyikamatameva yuktamiti bhāvaḥ। vinigamanāviraheṇeti। jñāyamānaṃ liṅgaṃ karaṇam atha vā sādhutvasādhakayuktyabhāvenetyarthaḥ। liṅgasya anumitikaraṇatve jñāyamānābhyāmatītānāgatābhyāṃ liṅgābhyāṃ anumitiḥ na syāt।
avyavahitapūrvavṛttitvaghaṭitakaraṇatvāsambhavāt। liṅgajñānasya tadviṣayakajñānasattvādanumitirupapadyate। tadāha - tatrāpyanumiteriti। phalāyogavyavacchinnamiti। kāryāvyavahitapūrvavṛttitvaviśiṣṭaṃ vyāptijñānasya tu parāmarśavyavahitatvāt na karaṇatvamiti bhāvaḥ।
AnTs liṅgaṃ trividham । anvayavyatireki kevalānvayi kevalavyatireki ceti । anvayena vyatirekeṇa ca vyāptimad anvayavyatireki । yathā vahnau sādhye dhūmavattvam । yatra dhūmas tatrāgnir yathā mahānasa ity anvayavyāptiḥ । yatra vahnir nāsti tatra dhūmo'pi nāsti yathā mahāhrada iti vyatirekavyāptiḥ । anvayamātravyāptikaṃ kevalānvayi yathā ghaṭo'bhidheyaḥ prameyatvāt paṭavat । atra prameyatvābhidhyatvayor vyatirekavyāptir nāsti sarvasyāpi prameyatvād abhidheyatvāc ca । vyatirekamātravyāptikaṃ kevalavyatireki yathā pṛthivī tarebhyo bhidyate gandhavattvāt । yad itarebhyo na bhidyate na tad gandhavat । yathā jalam । tasmān na tatheti atra yad gandhavat tad itarabhinnam ity anvayadṛṣṭanto nāsti pṛthivīmātrasya pakṣatvāt ।। - anvayavyatireki, kevalānvayi, kevalavyatireki ceti। vyatirekeṇa ca vyāptimat anvayavyatireki। yathā vahnau sādhye dhūmavattvam। yatra dhūmastatrāgniḥ yathā mahānasaḥ ityanvayavyāptiḥ।
vyatirekavyāptiḥ। liṅgamiti। lakṣaṇati - anvayeneti। hetusādhyayoḥ vyāptiḥ anvayavyāptiḥ, tadabhāvayorvyāptiḥ vyatirekavyāptiḥ।
manasi kṛtvāha - liṅgaṃ vibhajata iti। tādṛśavyāptidvayaṃ prakāśayati - hetusādhyayoriti। lakṣaṇamiti pratīyate। tathā sati kevalavyatirekiṇyativyāptiḥ, anvayasahacāragrahagrāhyeti। sādhyahetvoḥ sāmānādadhikaraṇyaṃ
hetuvyāpakasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyarūpā anvayavyāptiḥ। sādhyābhāvavyāpakībhūtābhāvapratiyogitvarūpā vyatirekavyāptiḥ। tenānvayasahacārajñānajñāpyā vyāptiriti mūlāllabhyate। evaṃ tena vyatirekasahacārajñānajñāpyāvyāptiriti labhyata iti bhāvaḥ।
।। anvayamātravyāptikam kevalānvayi। yathā ghaṭaḥ abhidheyaḥ prameyatvāt paṭavat iti। atra prameyatvābhidheyatvayoḥ vyatirekavyāptiḥ nāsti, sarvasyāpi prameyatvāt abhidheyatvācca।
lakṣaṇamāha - anvayeti। kevalānvayisādhyakaṃ liṅgaṃ kevalānvayi। kevalānvayitvam। īśvarapramāviṣayatvaṃ sarvapadābhidheyatvaṃ ca sarvatra astīti vyatirekābhāvaḥ। ityālocya prakārāntareṇa pariṣkaroti - kevalānvayisādhyakamiti।
lakṣaṇam। tatra satyantānupādāne kevalavyatirekiṇyativyāptiḥ। viśeśyānupādāne kevalānvayinyativyāptiḥ। anvayavyatirekiṇo lakṣaṇam। kevalānvayitvaṃ niveśitam। tadeva nirvakti - atyantābhāveti।
niravacchinnavṛttimadatyantābhāvetyarthaḥ। gaganābhāvasaṃyogābhāvādisādhyakahetoḥ saṅgrahaḥ। sarvapadābhidheyatvamiti। lakṣaṇamiti pratīyate। tathā sati kevalānvayini vyatirekavyāpteḥ
prasiddhatve tacchūnyatvaṃ na sambhavati। tasyāḥ aprasiddhatve sutarāṃ anvayamātreti। kevalānvayisādhyakaḥ kevalānvayī hetuḥ aidaṃ vācyaṃ kevalānvayyeva। tathā cobhayasaṅgrahāya hetau kevalānvayisādhyaketi। vyatirekihetuḥ atyantābhāvapratiyogī
hetuḥ। kevalānvayitvamevetyarthaḥ। nanu atyantābhāvāpratiyogitvābhāvāt। evaṃ āha - niravacchinnetyādi। ākāśābhāvātyantābhāvaḥ tatpratiyogitvenetyarthaḥ। abhāvābhāvasya
pratiyogisvarūpatvāditi bhāvaḥ। saṃyogābhāvātyantabhāvaḥ tatpratiyogitvādityarthaḥ। kevalānvayitvopapattiḥ। gaganarūpo abhāvastu na vṛttimān gaganābhāve astīti tasyāpi kevalānvayitvamupapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। evaṃ
ca yat sarvatrāsti, na kvāpi tadabhāvaḥ tat kevalānvayīti labhyate। nanvabhidheyatvasya kathaṃ kevalānvayitvam। abhidheyatvaṃ hi padaśaktimattvam। tacca ghaṭapaṭādipadabhedena bhinnamiti paṭādiniṣṭhātyantābhāvapratiyogitvādityāśaṅkate - ghaṭapadeti।
sarvapadābhidheyatvamiti। sarva iti yat padaṃ tadabhidheyatvaṃ sarvatrāstīti sarvapadābhidheyatvaṃ kevalānvayi। tathā ca kevalānvayitvamupapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। ।।
vyatirekamātravyāptikaṃ kevalavyatireki। yathā pṛthivī itarebhyo bhidyate gandhavattvāt। yat itarebhyo na bhidyate na tat gandhavat yathā jalam। tasmāt na tathā iti। atra yat pṛthivīmātrasya pakṣatvāt।
kavelavyatirekiṇo lakṣaṇamāha - vyatireketi। tadudāharati - yatheti। nanu itarabhedaḥ prasiddho vā na vā। ādye yatra prasiddhaḥ tatra hetusattve anvayitvam, asattve asādhāraṇyam। dvītīye sādhyajñānābhāvāt kathaṃ tadviśiṣṭānumitiḥ। viśeṣaṇajñānābhāve
vyatirekavyāptijñānamapi na syāditi cet - na। melanaṃ pṛthivyāṃ sādhyate। tatra nānvayitvāsādhāraṇye। pratyekādhikaraṇaprasiddhyā sādhyaviśiṣṭānumitiḥ vyatirekavyāptinirūpaṇaṃ ceti।
vyatirekamātravyāptikamiti। niścitavyatirekamātravyāptikamityarthaḥ। anvayavyāptessattve api na lakṣaṇāsaṅgatiḥ। itadabhedaḥ - pṛthivītaratvāvacchinnapratiyogitākabhedaḥ। anvayasahacāragrahagrāhyavyāptimattvaṃ syādityarthaḥ।
sapakṣavyāvṛttatvarūpāsādhāraṇalakṣaṇākrāntatvāditi bhāvaḥ। sādhyetyādi। sādhyābhāvavyāpakābhāvapratiyogitvarūpetyarthaḥ। sādhyate। tathā ca toktadoṣāvasara ityāhajalādīti। jalādīnāṃ ce
trayodaśānyonyābhāvāsteṣāṃ kūṭaṃ sādhyata ityarthaḥ। samudāyasya prasiddhyasambhavādāha - pratyekamini। trayodaśatvāvacchinneti। iti samuditārthaḥ। pratyekaṃ prasiddhau apekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatvarūpasamudāyatvaviśiṣṭajñānaṃ sambhavati।
ca sambhavatītyāha - pratyekādhikaraṇetyādinā। yadyapi jalādi jalāditrayodaśetyādikathanam। na ca tanmate caturdaśānyonyābhāvaḥ prasiddhāḥ। abhāvasyādhikaraṇātmakasya tenāṅgīkārāditi dhyeyam। caturdaśānāmityarthaḥ। jalādītyādiḥ। uktavigraheṇa
caturdaśasvityarthaḥ। agre apyevaṃ bodhyam ityāhuḥ। sati vyatirekavyāptimattvaṃ kevalavyatirekiṇo lakṣaṇamityarthaḥ। tathā ityato vyācaṣṭe - niścitavyatireketi। tathā coktasthale vastutaḥ sattvāt kevalavyatirekitvamupapadyata iti bhāvaḥ।
pṛthivītaratvāvacchinnapratiyogitākabheda iti। pṛthivītareṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ bheda ityarthaḥ। tathā ca yadi pṛthivītareṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhedaḥ anvayavyatirekyanumānameva bhavet na kevalavyatireke। yadi hetorasādhāraṇatvāpattiḥ। yadi
syāt viśiṣṭabuddhau viśeṣaṇajñānasya kāraṇatvāt। evaṃ sādhyasyājñātatve sādhyābhāvaghaṭitavyatirekavyāptijñānamapi na syāt। dīpikāsthaśaṅkāgranthārthaḥ। anumitirmā bhūt viśeṣaṇajñānarūpakāraṇavirahāt।
bhavitumarhatyevetyāśaṅkyāha - aprasiddhasādhyake apīti। sādhyaviśeṣaṇakānumitireveti। sādhyaviśeṣaṇakānumitireva jāyata dūṣaṇam। sādhyaviśeṣyakānumitirjāyata iti pakṣe sambhabatīti bhāvo varṇanīyaḥ। jalādibhedakūṭamiti। jalādīnāṃ
tatsamūha ityarthaḥ। jalādīnāṃ ye trayodaśānyonyābhāvā iti। sādhanīyaḥ। tathā ca jalādicaturdaśānyonyābhāveti vaktavye tanmatānusāreṇa kathitam। kevalavyatirekyanumānasya pradarśanīyatvāt ityāhuḥ - tanna।
gandhavattvaliṅgena tatsādhanāsambhavāt। pṛthivīniṣṭhasya tatsādhanāsambhavāt। ataḥ jalāditrayodaśānyonyābhāvānāmityasya teṣāmanyonyābhāvā iti vigrahaḥ। jalāditayatra bahuvrīhiḥ। ato
iti vyākhyātavyam। upari prakāśikāyāṃ sarvamidaṃ spaṣṭībhaviṣyati। caturdaśānāṃ ye bhedāḥ caturdaśa te sarveṃ jalādiṣu na prasiddhāḥ। tathā trayodaśasu prasiddhaḥ, na tejasi। evaṃrītyā trayodaśasu prasiddhaḥ yaḥ ekaikabhedaḥ teṣāṃ melanaṃ pṛthivyāṃ sādhyate। arthāt
caturdaṃśabhedasamudāyaḥ pṛthivyāṃ sādhyate। trayodaśatvāvacchedena sādhyata iti yāvat। evaṃ ca caturdaśatvaviśiṣṭabhedasya kutrāpyaprasiddhatvāt nānvayitvaṃ na vā asādhāraṇyam। sādhyarūpaviśeṣaṇajñānasattvena sādhyaviśiṣṭānumitirupapadyate। evaṃ
vyatirekavyāptijñānamapi sulabhamiti nṛsiṃhaśāstriṇaḥ prāhuḥ। niścitasādhyatāvacchedaketi। sādhyatāvacchedakaṃ trayodaśatvaṃ caturdaśatvaṃ vā tadavacchinnāḥ bhedāḥ tadvata ityarthaḥ। pratyekaṃ prasiddhāviti। jalabhedādīnāṃ prasiddhatvāt tatra
apekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatvātmakaṃ yat caturdaśatvaṃ tajjñānaṃ bhavati। nirṇayaḥ hame bhedāḥ caturdaśa ityākārakaḥ utpadyate। tataḥ viśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhinī anumitiḥ sulabhā। gandhavattvamiti vyatirekavyāptijñānaṃ ca sulabhamiti bhāvaḥ।
kevalavyatirekyanumānasthale sādhyaviśeṣyikaivānumitiḥ। ataḥ pūrvaṃ sādhyasyāprasiddhāvapi na kṣatiḥ। evaṃ pṛthivītarabhedābhāvatvena rūpeṇa daurlabhyaṃ bhavet। api tu pṛthivītaratvavyāpakībhūtābhāvapratiyogi gandhavatī pṛthivī ityeva parāmarśaḥ। ataḥ dīpikāyāmāśritaḥ
prayāso viphala iti prāhuḥ। akṣatādīdhityādau spaṣṭametat। AnTs saṃdigdhasādhyavān pakṣaḥ । yathā dhūmavattve hetau parvataḥ ।। sandigdhasādhyavān pakṣaḥ। yathā dhūmavattve hetau parvataḥ। sandigdheti। nanu śravaṇānantarabhāvimananasthale avyāptiḥ। tatra
vedavākyairātmano niścitatvena sandehābhāvāt। kiṃ ca pratyakṣe api vahnau yatra icchayā anumitiḥ tatra avyāptiriti cet-na। uktapakṣatāśrayatvasya pakṣalakṣaṇatvāt। sandigdhasādhyavāniti। viśeṣyatāsambandhena
sādhyaprakārakasaṃśayaviśiṣṭa ityarthaḥ। sapakṣalakṣaṇādikamapyevaṃ pariṣkartavyam। pakṣalakṣaṇasyāvyāptimāśaṅkte - dīpikāyāṃ nanviti। kiñcati। pakṣalakṣaṇatvādityarthaḥ।
viśeṣyatāsambandheneti। aparvato vahnimān na vā' pakṣatāyāṃ dīdhitigranthaḥ। atra prasiddhasādhyakasthale sādhyaviśeṣyakānumitiriti sūcyate। tatra gadādharīyavyākhyānaṃ akiṃ ityādyuktaṃ draṣṭavyam।
sattvāt parvatasya pakṣatā। prakāratāsambandhena tādṛśasaṃśayasya vahnau sattvāt vahneḥ pakṣatvavāraṇāya viśeṣyatāsambandhenetyuktam। sapakṣalakṣaṇādikamapyevaṃ pariṣkartavyamiti। viśeṣyatāsambandhena pariṣkartavyamityarthaḥ। ātmā
dehendriyādivilakṣaṇa ityākārakānumitirūpaṃ mananaṃ na syāt। sādadhyaprakārakasandehavattvarūpapakṣatvābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ। AnTs niścitasādhyavān sapakṣaḥ । yathā tatraiva mahānasaḥ ।। sapakṣaḥ। yathā tatraiva mahānasaḥ।
AnTs niścitasādhyābhāvavān vipakṣaḥ । yathā tatraiva mahāhradaḥ ।। niścitasādhyābhāvavāna vipakṣaḥ। yathā tatraiva mahāhradaḥ। AnTs savyabhicāraviruddhasatpakṣāsiddhabādhitāḥ pañca hetvābhāsāḥ ।। hetvābhāsāḥ।
niściteti। niściteti। asaddhetūnnirūpayituṃ vibhajate - savyabhicāreti। anumitipratibandhakayathārthajñānaviṣayatvaṃ hetvābhāsatvam।
vyāptyādiviśiṣṭahetūnnirūpyetyarthaḥ। saddhetunirūpaṇe asaddhetusmaraṇāta prasaṅgasaṅgatyā tannirūpaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। mūle hetvābhāsā iti। hetuvadābhāsanta iti hetvābhāsāḥ। duṣṭahetavo nirūpyanta ityarthaḥ। nanu
bhavatītyāśayena doṣasāmānyalakṣaṇamāha - anumitīti। hetvābhāsatvamiti। hetorābhāsāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ hetuniṣṭhāḥ doṣāḥ, teṣāṃ bhāvaḥ tattvamityarthaḥ। ahrado vahnimān' ityādyanumitiṃ prati avahnyabhāvavān hrada' ityādibādhaniścayaḥ pratibandhakaḥ।
lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। atrānumitipadaṃ ajahallakṣaṇayā anumititatkaraṇānyataraparam। tena vyabhicārādijñānasya vyabhicārādiṣu nāvyāptiḥ। aparvato nirvahniḥ' iti bādhabhramasya tadviṣayavahnyabhāvādau ativyāptiḥ ataḥ yathārtheti। bhramābhinnetyarthaḥ।
vahnyabhāvavaddhradātmakabādhaikadeśe vahnyabhāvādau ativyāptiḥ। sattvāditi cet-na। yadrūpāvacchinnaviṣayakajñānasāmānyaṃ doṣatvamityarthaparyavasānenādoṣāt। yadrūpapadenopādānāsambhavāt। na ca tarhi yathārthapadaṃ vyartham।
uktarītyaiva vāraṇāditi vācyam। jñānapadasya jñānaviśeṣatātparyagrāhakatayā yathārthapadasārthakyāt। evaṃ ca paryavasitaḥ। tena vahnyabhāvavaddhradaviṣayakasya āhāryasya nāsambhava ityalaṃ pallavitena।
duṣṭānāmeva lakṣaṇam। parantu jñāyamānavyabhicārādeḥ pratibandhakatvamabhyupetya। tadarthastu anumitipratibandhakā ye tatprakārakayathārthajñānaviśeṣyatvam। adhūmavān vahneḥ' ityādau vahniḥ' ityākārakayathārthañjñānaviśeṣyatvamastīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ।
anumitipratibandhakībhūtavyabhicārādīnāmaprasiddhatvāt nātivyāptiḥ। syāditi tanniveśa ityāhuḥ। vyāptyādiviśiṣṭahetūniti। ādipadena pakṣadharmatā gṛhyate। tathā ca vyāpti-pakṣadharmatāviśiṣṭahetutvaṃ saddhetorlakṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ।
hetuvadābhāsanta iti। hetutvaprakārakabhramaviṣayāḥ ityarthaḥ। hetutvaṃ ca vyāptipakṣadharmatāviśiṣṭatvam। tathā ca vyāptipakṣadharmatāviśiṣṭatvaprakārakabhramaviṣayatvaṃ hetvābhāsatvam। hetvābhāsaśabdaḥ duṣṭahetupara iti bhāvaḥ। lakṣaṇasamanvaya iti।
bādhaḥ doṣaḥ। tādṛśadoṣavattvaṃ ca hetoḥ dhūmasya ekajñānaviṣayaprakṛtahetutāvacchedakavattvasambandhenāstīti duṣṭatvam। viṣayatvādityādikamūhanīyam। tadā bādhasatpratipakṣayorevedaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ samanviyāt। bādhaniścayasya
pratibandhakatvāt, tadviṣayatvarūpalakṣaṇasattvāt। vyabhicāravirodhasvarūpāsiddhiprabhṛtiṣu lakṣaṇamidaṃ na samanveti। sattvādityata āha - atrānumitipadamiti। tathā ca hetvābhāsalakṣaṇam। parāmarśapratibandhakatayaiveti। vyabhicārajñānaṃ
parāmarśe vyāptibhānāṃśe pratibandhakam। virodhajñānaṃ sādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyāṃśabhāne pratibandhakam। svarūpāsiddhijñānaṃ anumitikaraṇaparāmarśapratibandhakasattvāt nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। nirvāhāditi। lakṣaṇopapatterityarthaḥ। yathārthapadaprayojanamāha -
parvato nirvahniriti। tathā ca yathārthapadānupādāne parvate doṣatvaṃ syāt। tadvāraṇāya yathārthapadam। uktabhramasya yathārthatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। nanu bhramavāraṇamaśakyam। tasyāpi parvatatvavati parvatatvaprakārakatvena
bhramabhinnetyartha iti। tathā caprakṛtalakṣaṇaghaṭakaṃ yathārthapadaṃ tadabhāvavati tatprakārakabhinnārthakam। aparvato vahnyabhāvavān' iti tadbhinnaṃ na bhavatīti na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। bhramabhinnatvameva sarvāṃśe pramātvamityucyate। tacca vavyadhikaraṇaprakārāvacchinna yā yā
viśeṣyatā tattadanirūpakatvam। svavyadhikaraṇeti। svavyadhikaraṇetyasya svādhikaraṇāvṛttītyarthaḥ। śuktau idaṃ rajatamiti tadanirūpakatvaṃ idaṃ rajatamiti pramāyāmiti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ।
prakāratāviśiṣṭā yā viśeṣyatā tadanirūpakatvamiti yāvat। adhikamudgrantheṣu। athaivamapīti। bhramabhinnārthakayathārthapadaniveśe apītyarthaḥ। ahrado pratibandhakatayā tadviṣayatvaṃ vahnyabhāvavaddhra iva vahnyabhāve apyasti।
hetvābhāsalakṣaṇasya bādhānātmake vahnyabhāve ativyāptirityarthaḥ। samādhatte yadrūpāvacchinneti। tathā ca yadrūpapadena ityākārakānumitipratibandhakatvaṃ nāsti। ataḥ vahnyabhāvavaddhradatvameva yadrūpapadena dhartavyam।
tadavacchinnaviṣayakajñānasāmānyasyānumitipratibandhakatvāt। nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। aparvato vanhyabhāvavān' iti bhramaviṣaye vanhyabhāve ativyāptivāraṇāya hi yathārthapadamupāttam। śakyate।
aparvato vanhimān' ityanumitipratibandhakatvābhāvāt। tathā ca vanhyabhāve ativyāptyaprasaktyā yathārthapadaṃ vyarthamiti bhāvaḥ। jñānaviśeṣatātparyagrāhakatayeti।dya jñānapadena svanirūpitatveti।
śuktiniṣṭhaviśeṣyatāyāmasti। viśeṣyatāyāmasti। tādṛśaviśeṣyatānirūpakatvaṃ bhrame anirūpakatvaṃ pramāyāmiti samanvayo bodhyaḥ। sūcanāya yathārthapadamiti bhāvaḥ। anāhāryatvaṃ
bādhakālīnecchājanyatvābhāvavattvam। tadanupādāne ahrado vanhimān' cānumitipratibandhakatvābhāvādavyāptisyāt bādhe। tadvāraṇāya pratibanadhakajñāne anāhāryatvaṃ niveśanīyam। evaṃ aprāmāṇyajñānābhāvaviśiṣṭatvam। tadaniveśe ayatra hrado vanhyabhāvavān'
bādhajñānasyānumityapratibandhakatayā bādhe avyāptiḥ। syāt। tathā ca paryavasannam। pare tvityādi।
karmadhārayaḥ। asmin kalpe anumitipratibandhakānāṃ yathārthajñānamiti ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣaḥ। ahrado vahnimān dhūmāt' ityatra ahrado vanhimān' dhūme astīti dhūmasya duṣṭatvam। aparvato dhūmavān vanheḥ' ityatra ityākārakaṃ, tadviśeṣyatvaṃ vanhāvastīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। nanu
aparvato vanhimān dhūmāt' ityatrātivyāptiḥ। anumitipadena prakṛtānumitiparatayeti। prakṛtapakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnoddeśyaka-prakṛtasādhyatāvacchedakāvacch innavidheyakānumitiparatayetyarthaḥ। tatpratibandhakadoṣāprasiddhyā nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ।
darśitasambandheneti। ekajñānaviṣayaprakṛtahetutāvacchedakavattvasambanadhenetyarthaḥ। AnTs savyabhicāro'naikāntikaḥ । sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇānupasaṃhāribhedāt । tatra sādhyābhāvavadvṛttiḥ sādhāraṇo anaikāntikaḥ । yathā parvato vahnimān prameyatvād iti prameyatvasya vahnyabhāvavati hrade vidyamānatvāt । sarvasapakṣavipakṣavyāvṛtto'sādhāraṇaḥ । yathā śabdo nityaḥ śabdatvād iti । śabdatvaṃ sarvebhyo nityebhyo'ntyebhyaś ca vyāvṛttaṃ śabdamātravṛtti । anvayavyatirekadṛṣṭāntarahito'nupasaṃhārī । yathā sarvam anityaṃ prameyatvād iti । atra sarvasyāpi pakṣatvād dṛṣṭānto nāsti ।। savyabhicāro anaikāntikaḥ। saḥ
trividhaḥ-sādhāraṇa-asādhāraṇa-anupasaṃhāribhedāt। sādhāraṇaḥ। yathā parvato vanhimān prameyatvāt। atra prameyatvasya vanhyabhāvavati hrade vidyamānatvāt। sarvasapakṣavipakṣavyāvṛtto asādhāraṇaḥ। yathā śabdo nityaḥ
śabdatvāt। atra śabdatvaṃ sarvebhyaḥ nityebhyaḥ anityebhyo vyāvṛttam śabdamātravṛtti। anvayavyatirekadṛṣṭāntarahito anupasaṃhārī। yathā sarvamanityaṃ prameyatvāt। atra sarvasyāpi pakṣatvāt dṛṣṭānto nāsti।
vibhajatesa trividha iti। lakṣayatitatreti। udāharati - yatheti। lakṣayatisarveti। lakṣaṇamāhaanvayeti।
itīti। sāmānyalakṣaṇantu sādhāraṇādyanyatamatvaṃ sphaṭam। mūle tatreti। sādhāraṇādimadhya ityarthaḥ। sādhyābhāvavadvṛttiriti। sādhyatāvacchedakadharmasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvavannirūpitahetutāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnādheyatāvānityarthaḥ।
dhūmādervṛttitve api ca nātivyāptiḥ। atra ca sādhyābhāvavattāyāṃ vanhyādyabhāvasya kālikasambandhena parvatādau vṛtterativyāptiḥ। viśeṣaṇatāviśeṣaṇādhikaraṇāprasiddhyāvyāptiḥ। ataḥ vivakṣaṇīyam। vanhyādau sādhye tādṛśasambandho daiśikāviśeṣaṇatā,
ghaṭatvābhāvādau ca sādhye samavāyastatheti na doṣaḥ। akapisaṃyogī niravacchinnadaiśikaviśeṣaṇateti dik। viruddhe ativyāptiriti bhramitavyam। viruddhasādhāraṇye api kṣativirahāt। mūle sarvasapakṣavyāvṛtta iti।
sapakṣavattitvasāmānyābhāvavānityarthaḥ। sarvapadaṃ sapakṣavṛttitvasāmānyābhāvaniveśasphorakam। sapakṣapadaṃ niścitasādhyavadarthavadarthakam। sādhyasandehadaśāyāmasādhāraṇyasyeṣṭatvāt iti saṃpradāyavidaḥ।
svīkāre bādhabhramadaśāyāṃ bādhasyāpyaṅgīkārāpatteḥ। na hi vaiṣamye yuktiṃ paśyāmaḥ। evaṃ cātra sapakṣapadaṃ kevalasādhyavatparam। aśabdo ko api doṣa iti prāhuḥ। anvayeti।
kiñcidviśeṣyakaniścāviṣayasādhyābhāvakatvam। navīnamate tu - atyantābhāvāpratiyogitvaviśiṣṭasādhyādikatvamevānupasaṃhāratvim। tajjñānasya vyatirekavyāptijñānapratibandhakatā। tviti। savyabhicārasāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tvityarthaḥ।
sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhetyādi। sādhyaniṣṭhapratiyogitāyāṃ dhūmāt' ityatra dhūmasyāpi sādhāraṇahetvābhāsatvāpattiḥ। tathā hi - sattvāditi। sādhyatāvacchedakadharmāvacchinnatvasya pratiyogitāyāṃ kevalavanhitvāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvābhāvāt। api tu
dhūme nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ। evaṃ sādhyaniṣṭhapratiyogitāyāṃ sattvādativyāptiḥ। sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśe tu tanniyapitādheyatvaṃ dhūme nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ। ādheyatāyāṃ tannirūpitādheyatvaṃ dhūme astītyativyāptiḥ syāt। tanniveśe tu
saṃyogasambandhāvacchinnādheyatvaṃ nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ। hetumati parvatādāviti। etacca hetoḥ sādhyābhāvavannirūpitādheyatvamevāstīti sūcanārthamuktam। tattatsādhyābhāvasyeti। mahānasīyavanhyādyabhāvasyetyarthaḥ।
sambandhāntarāvacchinnāsādhyasāmānyābhāvasyeti। sādhyatāvacchedakasaṃyogasambandhātiriktasamavāyasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākavanhitvāvacchinnābhāvasyetyarthaḥ। sādhyābhāvavattāyāmityādi। sādhyābhāvavattāyāṃ yadi dhūme sattvāt saddhetāvativyāptiḥ।
vyabhicāriṇyativyāptiḥ। tathā hi- sādhyābhāvavati sādhāraṇavyabhicārī hetuḥ। atra sādhyābhāvaḥ ghaṭatvābhāvābhāvaḥ ghaṭatvarūpaḥ tasya svarūpasambandhenādhikaraṇamaprasiddham। bhāvānāṃ svarūpasambandhena kvāpyavṛtterityavyāptiḥ। ataḥ
vivakṣaṇīyam। sambandhaḥ sādhyavattāgrahavirodhitāniyāmaka iti kathyate। aparvanto ayogolakaḥ tannirūpitādheyatvaṃ vanhāvastīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। aparvataḥ saṃyogena vahnimān' iti buddherutpatteḥ। tathā ca
nātivyāptiḥ। aghaṭatvābhāvavān dravyatvāt' nāvyāptiḥ। aayaṃ vṛkṣaḥ kapisaṃyogī etadvṛkṣatvāt' ityatra avṛkṣaḥ pratibandhakaḥ sa sādhyavattāgrahavirodhitāniyāmaka iti kathyate। tadeva pariṣkṛtyāha - sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnetyādinā।
satyapi vṛkṣaḥ agre kapisaṃyogavāniti buddhyutpatteḥ। tathā ca nātivyāptiḥ। tathā ca phalitam। sādhyābhāvavannirūpitādhayatāyāḥ sattvāt ityata āha - digiti।
sādhāraṇatvamitivivakṣitam। viśiṣṭasattāyāḥ sattātvenaiva rūpeṇa hetutāvacchedakamiti nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। sādhāraṇalakṣaṇasyātivyāptiriti śaṅkate - na ca viruddha iti। upadheyasaṅkare apīti। ekasmin aneke doṣāḥ saṃbhavantīti bhāvaḥ।
doṣasyabhinnatā। guṇādireveti। na kapisaṃyogābhāvasattvāditi bhāvaḥ। sapakṣaśabdasya niścitasādhyavānityarthaḥ। viśeṣyatāsambandhena
sādhyaprakārakaniścayavāniti yāvat। sapakṣavṛttitvasāmānyābhāvavān phalitam। te addhetorapi yatkiñcitsapakṣavṛttitvābhāvasattvāt asādhāraṇatvaṃ syādityākṣepasya nāvasaraḥ। śabdo anityaḥ śabdatvāt tadavṛttitvaṃ śabdatve astīti śabdatvasya asādhāraṇatvam। yadā tu
nāsādhāraṇyam। tathā cāsādhāraṇyamanityadoṣa iti prācīnāḥ। navīnāstu - saddhetoḥ kādācitkamasādhāraṇyaṃ necchanti। tanmate sapakṣapadaṃ sādhyavanmātraparam। sādhyavadvṛttitvasāmānyābhāvaḥ asādhāraṇyam। saddhetau pakṣe sādhyasandehadaśāyāmapi pakṣaḥ sādhyavān
hetau nāstīti nāsādhāraṇyam। kiñcidviśeṣyaketi। sādhyaṃ bhavet। sarvamabhidheyaṃ prameyatvādityatra tu sarvasya pakṣatvāt abhidheyatvaṃ na kvāpi niścitam। ataḥ
heturbhavati। paraṃ tu atra sādhyābhāvasyāpratiddhatayā kiñcidviśeṣyakaniścayāviṣayasādhyābhāvakatvamiti dalaṃ na samanveti। ityāhaḥ। nanu ghaṭo abhidheyaḥ prameyatvāt ityatra saddhetorapīti।
sattvādityarthaḥ। śabde anityatvaniścayadaśāyāmasya saddhetutvāt ativyāptiḥ prasaktā। sāmānyābhāvaniveśe ca nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। cet - na। tatra anupasaṃhāritvajñānena
vyatirekavyāptijñānahetukānumitirna jāyate। anvayavyāptijñānamūlā anumitistu nirābādhaiva। cet-ittham। sādhyam atyantābhāvāpratiyogi iti jñānakāle sādhyapratiyogikaḥ atyantābhāvaḥ iti jñānaṃ ca na bhavati। tathā ca
bhavatīti। AnTs sādhyābhāvavyāpto hetur viruddhaḥ । yatra śabdo nityaḥ kṛtakatvād iti । kṛtakatvaṃ hi nityatvābhāvenānityatvena vyāptam ।। heturviruddhaḥ। yathā śabdo nityaḥ kāryatvāt ghaṭavat। ।
AnTs yasya sādhyabhāvasādhakaṃ hetvantaraṃ vidyate sa satpratipakṣaḥ । yathā śabdo nityaḥ śrāvaṇatvāc chabdatvavad iti । śabdo'nityaḥ kāryatvād ghaṭavad iti ।। yasya sādhyābhāvasādhakaṃ hetvantaraṃ vidyate sa satpratipakṣaḥ। yathā śabdaḥ nityaḥ śrāvaṇatvāt, śabdaḥ anityaḥ kāryatvāt ghaṭavat। AnTs asiddhas trividhaḥ । āśrayāsiddhaḥ svarūpāsiddho vyāpyatvāsiddhaś ceti । āśrayāsiddho yathā gaganāravindaṃ surabhy aravindatvāt sarojāravindavat । atra gaganāravindam āśrayaḥ । sa ca nāsty eva । svarūpāsiddho yathā śabdo guṇaś cākṣuṣatvāt । atra cākṣuṣatvaṃ śabde nāsti śabdasya śrāvaṇatvāt । sopādhiko vyāpyatvāsiddhaḥ । sādhyavyāpakatve sati sādhanāvyāpaka upādhiḥ । sādhyasamānādhikaraṇātyantābhāvāpratiyogitvaṃ sādhyavyāpakatvam । sādhanavann iṣṭātyantābhāvapratiyogitvaṃ sādhāraṇāvyapakatvam । parvato dhūmavān vahnimattvād ity atrārdrendhasaṃyoga upādhiḥ । tathā hi । yatra dhūmas tatrārdrendhnasaṃyoga iti sādhyavyāpakatā । yatra vahnis tatrārdrendhanasaṃyogābhāvād iti sādhanāvyāpakatā । evaṃ sādhyavyāpakatve sati sādhanāvyāpakatvād ardrendhanasaṃyoga upādhiḥ । sopādhikatvād vahnimattvaṃ vyāpyatvāsiddham ।।
āśrayāsiddhaḥ svarūpāsiddhaḥ vyāpyatvāsiddhaśceti। gaganāravindaṃ surabhi aravindatvāt sarojāravindavat। atra gaganāravindamāśrayaḥ। śabdaḥ guṇaḥ cākṣuṣatvāt। atra cākṣaṣatvaṃ śabde nāsti, śabdasya
śrāvaṇatvāt। vyāpyatvāsiddhaḥ। sādhyeti। yasyeti।
asiddha iti। - gaganeti। - yatheti। lakṣaṇamāha - sopādhika iti।
iti। sādhyābhāvavyāptiḥ sādhyavadavṛttitvam। asādhāraṇyasya tu niścitasādhyavadavṛttitvarūpatayā nābhedaḥ। navīnamate tu - nāsādhāraṇyābhedaḥ। etādṛśavyāptiviśiṣṭahetumattājñānaṃ sākṣādanumitipratibandhakamiti dhyeyam।
sādhyābhāvetyādi। yatsambandhi yatsādhyaṃ tadabhāvavyāpyahetvantarasya jñānaṃ pakṣe asti sa satpratipakṣa ityarthaḥ। prakṛtasādhyavyāpyatvena hetvantaramiti iti prāñcaḥ। navīnāḥ punarevaṃ varṇayanti - ityartha iti।
āśrayāsiddho yatheti। pakṣo vā। sa ca nāstyeveti। gaganīyatvaṃ nāstīti paryavasitor'thaḥ।
hetvabhāvaḥ hetvabhāvavān pakṣo vā। sopādhika iti। vyāpyatvāsiddhiḥ vyāptyabhāvaḥ, tasyāḥ bhāvaḥ। upādherdeṣatvamasambhavīti dīpikāyāṃ vyaktībhaviṣyatyagre। sādhye sādhyatāvacchedakābhāvaḥ sādhyāprasiddhiḥ। hetau
hetutāvacchedakābhāvaḥ sādhanāprasiddhiḥ। yathā kāñcanamayavahrimān kāñcanamayadhūmāt ityādau। tadgrahadaśāyāṃ sādhyatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭavyāptigrahapratibandhaḥ phalam। tayorvyāpyatvāsiddhāvantarbhāvāt na hetvābhāsādhikyamiti।
sādhyavadavṛttitvamiti। sādhyābhāvavyāptiḥ, sādhyābhāvābhāvavadavṛttitvam। tacca sādhyavadavṛttitvameva, sādhyābhāvābhāvasya sādhyātmakatvāditi bhāvaḥ। asādhāraṇyaṃ tayorbheda iti bhāvaḥ। navīnamate sādhyavadavṛttitvameva
virodhapadārthamāha - navīnamate tviti। sādhyābhāvasya sādhyavyāpakībhūtābhāvapratiyogitvaparyavasitam। śabdaḥ nityaḥ kṛtakatvābhāvaḥ tatpratiyogitvaṃ kṛtakatve astīti lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। sākṣādanumitipratibandhakamiti। tadvattābuddhiṃ prati
bhāvaḥ। virodhiparāmarśadvayakāla eva satpratipakṣatvamiti prāñcaḥ। navīnāḥ। tadāha - yatsambandhi-yatsādhyamityādi। yatsambandhītyasya yaddhetusambanadhītyarthaḥ। tathā ca yaddhetusambandhi yatsādhyaṃ
tadabhāvavyāpyahetvantarasya jñānaṃ tatpakṣe asti sa satpratipakṣaḥ। yathā śabdarūpe pakṣe astīti saḥ kṛtakatvahetuḥ satpratipakṣaḥ। pakṣo bhavati tādṛśahetuḥ satpratipakṣa iti yāvat। hetuḥ satpratipakṣa iti phalitor'thaḥ। yatsambandhisādhyetyādi।
