tādṛśo hetuḥ satpratipakṣaḥ। kṛtakatvasambandhi anityatvaṃ tadabhāvaḥ śabde asatīti kṛtakatvaṃ satpratipakṣam। pakṣatāvacchedakaviraha iti। gaganāravindaṃ surabhītyatra gaganīyatvaviśiṣṭamaravindaṃ pakṣaḥ। tatra pakṣe aravinde gaganīyatvaṃ
gaganīyatvābhāvaviśiṣṭamaravindaṃ vā āśrayāsiddhirityarthaḥ। saviśeṣaṇe hīti nyāyeneti। asaviśeṣaṇe hi vidhiniṣedhau sati viśeṣye bādhe viśeṣaṇamupasaṃkrāmataḥ' iti nyāyaḥ। saṃkrāmatīti nyāyasyārthaḥ। yathā śikhī dhvasta ityatra
bhāvaḥ। doṣatvenetyatrāha - upādherdeṣatvamasambhavīti। grantheneti śeṣaḥ। damavadheyamiti। kāñcanamayatvābhāvavān vahniḥ
pratibandhakam। evaṃ sambhavati। dhūmaviśeṣyakakāñcanamayatvaprakārakajñānaṃ prati dhūmaviśeṣyakakāñcanamayatvābhāvaprakārakajñānasya pratibandhakatvāt। sādhyāprasiddhisādhanāprasiddhyorhetvābhāsatvam। kathaṃ
vyāpyatvāsiddhāvanayorantarbhāva iti cet-śrūyatām। hi vyāptiḥ। sādhanāprasiddhisthale tayorvyāpyatvāsiddhāvantarbhāva iti। ।।
paryavasyatīti। etena paramamūle agaganāravindamāśrayaḥ, sa ca nāsatyeva' iti vākyamasaṃgatam। gaganāravindamityasya hi gaganīyatvaviśiṣṭamaravindamityarthaḥ। tatrāravindasya sattvāt tatra paryavasitaḥ, tatra cānupapatyabhāvāditi।
sati sādhanāvyāpakatvaṃ upādhitvam। sādhyasamānādhikaraṇātyantābhāvāpratiyogitvaṃ sādhyavyāpakatvam। sādhanavanniṣṭhātyantābhāvapratiyogitvaṃ sādhanāvyāpakatvam। parvataḥ dhūmavān vahneḥ ityatra ārdrendhanasaṃyogaḥ upādhiḥ। yatra
dhūmaḥ tatra ārdrendhanasaṃyoga iti sādhyavyāpakatayā। yatra vahniḥ tatra ārdrendhanasaṃyoga iti nāsti। ayogolake ārdrenadhanasaṃyogābhāvāt। evaṃ sādhyavyāpakatve sati sādhanāvyāpakatvāt ārdrendhanasaṃyoga upādhiḥ। sopādhikatvāt
vahnimattvaṃ vyāpyatvāsiddham। sādhyeti। upādhiścaturvidhaḥ - kevala - sādhyavyāpakaḥ, udāsīnadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakaśceti। ādyaḥ ārdrendhanasaṃyogaḥ। bahirdravyatvāvacchinnapratyakṣatvavyāpakaṃ udbhūtarūpavattvam। tṛtīyo
janyatvāvacchinnānityatvavyāpakaṃ bhāvatvam। caturtho yathā - prāgabhāvo bhāvatvam। iti। sādhyavyāpakatvasādhanāvyāpakatve ekarūpeṇa ekasambandhena ca grāhye। tena avahnimān dhūmāt' ityādau tattadvahnau vahnitvena
sādhanāvyāpakatve api tatrātivyāptiḥ। mūloktopādhi lakṣaṇe avyāptiṃ iti। yaddharmaviśiṣṭasādhyavyāpakatvaṃ taddharmaviśiṣṭasādhanāvyāpakatvaṃ lakṣaṇe niveśanīyam। anyathā dhūmatvāvacchinnāvyāpakatvāt ativyāptiḥ syāditi dhyeyam।
udāsīneti। pakṣadharmasādhanadharmābhyāṃ bhinnetyarthaḥ। bahirdravyatvam - ātmānyadravyatvam। idaṃ kevalapratyakṣatvasyaiva sādhyatvānusāreṇa। prāgabhāvo vināśī janyatvāditi। atra janyatvaṃ pakṣadharmo na bhavatīti sādhanāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakatvaghaṭitalakṣaṇam। anityatvavyāpakatiti।
vināśitvavyāpakamityarthaḥ। janyatvasyodāsīnatvaṃ sampādayituṃ prameyatvāditi। ativyāptam। mahānasīyavahnerapi vahnitvena rūpeṇa sādhanāvyāpakatvācca। sādhanavati dhūmavati vartate
mahānasīyavahnitvena rūpeṇa mahānasīyavahnerabhāvāt। evaṃ tatraiva ālokasyopādhitvāpattiḥ। vahnimati sarvatra saṃyogasambandhena ālokasya vidyamānayatā saṃyogasambandhena sādhyavyāpakatvāt। evaṃ sādhyavyāpakatvasādhanāvyāpakatve iti। tathā ca ye sambandhena yena
ca tasya sādhanāvyāpakatvaṃ vivakṣitam। ato vahnitvena nātivyāptiḥ। evaṃ saṃyogena vahnivyāpakasya ālokasya samavāyena nāstīti nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। vahnitvena sādhyavyāpakatvasyeti। sādhyavanniṣṭhātyantābhāvapratiyogitānavacchedakavahnitvavattvasyetyarthaḥ।
tattadvahnitvena sādhanāvyāpakatvasyeti। sādhanavanniṣṭhātyantābhāvapratiyogitāvacchedakatattadvahnitvavattvasyetyarthaḥ। sādhyavanniṣṭhātyantābhāvanirūpitasaṃyogasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitānavacchedakadharmavattvam। bodhyam। avyāptiṃ vārayitumiti। avāyuḥ pratyakṣaḥ
pratyakṣasparśāśrayatvāt' ityatra udbhūtarūpavattvamupādhiḥ। tatra mūloktaṃ sādhyavyāpakatvaghaṭitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ nāsti। pratyakṣatvarūpasādhyavati ātmani udbhūtarūpābhāvādityavyāptiḥ prasajyate। tāṃ vārayituṃ ityādidīpikāyā āśaya iti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca
sādhanāvyāpakatvaṃ lakṣaṇam। pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakasyopādheḥ lakṣaṇam। sādhanāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakasyopādheḥ sādhanāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakatve sati sādhanāvyāpakatvaṃ lakṣaṇam। lakṣaṇamiti rītyā lakṣaṇabhedo vivakṣita iti bhāvaḥ।
tadāha-yaddharmaviśiṣṭasādhyetyādi। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyasambandhena। dharmaikyavivakṣāyāḥ prayojanamāha - anyatheti। aparvato vahnimān dhūmāt' ityatra parvatīyavahneḥ sādhanāvyāpakatvaṃ cāsti। dhūmavati mahānase parvatīyavahnerabhāvāt
iti parvatīyavahnirupādhiḥ syāt। dharmaikyavivakṣaṇe tu dhūmāvyāpakatvaṃ nāsti। parvatatvaviśiṣṭadhūmavati parvate parvatīyavahneḥ sattvāt। ato nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। ārdrendhanasaṃyoga iti। aparvato dhūmavān vahneḥ' ityatra
ādrendhanasaṃyoga upādhiḥ। sa ca dhūmarūpasādhyavyāpakaḥ vahnirūpasādhanāvyāpakaśceti kevalasādhyavyāpako ayamupādhirityarthaḥ। dvitīyo yatheti। pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpaka upādhirityarthaḥ। udbhūtarūpavattvamupādhiḥ। sa ca kevalasādhyavyāpako na bhavati
pratyakṣaviṣayatvarūpasādhyavatyātmani udbhūtarūpavattvābhāvāt। ataḥ pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpako ayamupādhiḥ। pakṣasya dharmaḥ pakṣadharmaḥ tadavacchinnaḥ tadviśiṣṭaḥ tatsamānādhikaraṇaḥ ya sādhyaḥ tadvyāpakaḥ। bahirdravyatvarūpaviśeṣaṇābhāvāt। ato
pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakam। tathā lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। sādhanāvacchinnasādhyavyāpaka upādhirityarthaḥ। sādhanāvacchinnatvaṃ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyasambandhena sādhanaviśiṣṭatvam। aprāgabhāvo
vināśī janyatvāt' ityatra bhāvatvamupādhiriṣyate। sa vināśitvarūpasādhyavati prāgabhāve bhāvatvābhāvāt। ataḥ sādhanāvacchinnasādhyavyāpako ayamupādhiḥ। janyatvarūpasādhanaviśiṣṭaṃ vināśitvaṃ yatra yatrāsti ghaṭādau tatra bhāvatvasadbhāvāditi bhāvaḥ।
caturtho yatheti। udāsīnadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpaka ityarthaḥ। aprāgabhāvo vināśī pramevayatvāt' ityatra bhāvatvamupādhiḥ। pakṣadharmāt sādhanāccānyo dharma udāsīnadharmaḥ। janyatvaṃ hi pakṣe pakṣadharmaḥ। evaṃ sādhanāt prameyatvāccānyat iti udāsīnadharmaḥ।
udāsīnadharmāvacchinnasādhanāvyāpakaścopādhiriti bhāvaḥ। prakāśikāyām pakṣadharmasādhanadharmābhyāmiti। pakṣavṛttirdharmaḥ pakṣadharmaḥ sādhanarūpo dharmaṃḥ sādhanadharmaḥ। bahirdravyatvam ityasya vivaraṇaṃ ātmānyadravyatvamiti। vāyuḥ pratyakṣa ityatra pratyakṣapadasya
evalasādhyavyāpaka evopādhiḥ। yadā tu pratyakṣaviṣayatvamātraṃ sādhyaṃ bahirindriyajanyatvāghaṭitapratyakṣaviṣayatvamātrasyetyarthaḥ। udāsīnatvaṃ sampādayitumiti। yadi janyatvameva hetuḥ syāt tadā nodāsīnadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakatvam।
sādhanādanyasyaivodāsīnaśabdārthatvāt। ataḥ prameyatvasya hetutvānusaraṇam। adhunā tu janyatvaṃ sādhanāt prameyatvādanyaditi janyatvaviśiṣṭavināśitvaṃ udāsīnadharmāvacchinnasādhyamiti bhāvaḥ। AnTs yasya sādhyābhāvaḥ pramāṇāntareṇa niścitaḥ sa bādhitaḥ । yathā vahnir anuṣṇo dravyatvād iti । atrānuṣṇatvaṃ sādhyaṃ tadabhāva uṣṇatvaṃ spārśanapratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti bādhitatvam ।।
pramāṇāntareṇa niścitaḥ saḥ bādhitaḥ। yathā vahniḥ anuṣṇaḥ padārthatvāt। atra anuṣṇatvaṃ sādhyam, tadabhāva uṣṇatvaṃ tvācapratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti bodhyam। iti। bahirindrayajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ yatra yatra ghaṭādau tatra
udbhūtarūpavattvasattvāditi bhāvaḥ। tadaiva pakṣadharmeti। udbhūtarūpasya kevalasādhyavyāpakatvaṃ na sambhavati। ataḥ udbhūtarūpasyopapādanīyamiti bhāvaḥ।
lakṣaṇamāha - yasyeti। sākṣādanumitipratibandhakatvam। itareṣāṃ tu parāmarśapratibandhakatvam। tatrāpi sādhāraṇasyāvyabhicārābhāvarūpatayā, vyāptisaṃśayādhāyakatvena vyāptijñānapratibandhakatvam।
āchayāsiddhisvarūpāsiddhyoḥ pakṣadharmatājñānapratibandhakatvam। upādhistu vyabhicārajñānadvārā vyāptijñānapratibandhakaḥ। siddhasādhanaṃ tu pakṣatāvighaṭakatayā āśrayāsiddhāvantarbhavatīti prāñcaḥ। nigrahasthānāntaramiti navīnāḥ।
-sādhyābhāvavattāniścayasya। grāhyābhāvaniścayatveneti। anumitipratibandhakatvamityanenānvayi। virodhijñānasāmagrītveneti। idaṃ prācīnamate। vastutastu virodhiparāmarśasya
dhyeyam। vyabhicārādigrahāṇām। tatrāpi - vyabhicārādigraheṣvapi। sādhāraṇasyeti। bhāvapradhānanirdeśatayā sādhāraṇyasyetyarthaḥ। avyabhicārābhāvarūpatayā। tadgrahasyeti śeṣaḥ।
vyāptijñānapratibandhakatvamityanenānvayaḥ। hetau yo avyabhicāraḥ tadgrahapratibandhakateti bhāvaḥ। hetau hetuvyāpakatāvacchedakasādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnasāmānādhikaraṇyābhāvarūpatayā। vyāptisaṃśayādhāyakatveneti।
prācīnamatamabhipretyedam। pakṣadharmatājñānapratibandhakatvamiti। pakṣe pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭapakṣavṛttitvagrahāsaṃbhavāditi bhāvaḥ। upādhistviti। vyabhicārajñānadvāreti। tathā ca hetvābhāsalakṣaṇe paramukhanirīkṣakasyopādherna hetvābhāsatvamiti bhāvaḥ। nanu tathāpi
matamavalambyeṣṭāpattyā pariharati - siddhasādhanaṃ tviti। pakṣatāvighaṭakatayeti। tanmate pakṣatāyāḥ sādhyasaṃśayarūpatayā tadvighaṭakatvaṃ sādhyaniścayasyākṣatamiti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca na vibhogavyāghāta iti bhāvaḥ। darśitamatamatiśithilamityālocyāha
- nigraheti। na ca siddhānte anumitiṃ prati siddheḥ pratibandhakatayā tadviṣayasya kathaṃ hetvābhāsatā neti vācyam। siṣādhayiṣāyāḥ uktahetvābhāsalakṣaṇāsaṃsparśāt। adhikaṃ tarkakarkaśavicāracāturīdhurīṇairanusandheyam।।
grāhyābhāvaniścayatveneti। anumityā grāhyaṃ yat sādhyaṃ tadabhāvaprakārakaniścayatvenetyarthaḥ। tadvattābuddhiṃ prati tadabhāvavattāniścayavidhayeti yāvat। satpratipakṣasya - sādhyābhāvavyāpyapratihetumān pakṣa iti jñānasya।
sādhyābhāvavattājñānaṃ tajjanakatvena। tathā ca satpratipakṣajñānaṃ satpratipakṣasyānumitipratibandhakatvamiti। navīnāstu pratibandhakatvasambhavena gauravādityāhuḥ। itareṣāmityādi।
pratibandhakatvam। ahetumān pakṣa' iti pakṣadharmatājñanāṃśe āśrayāsiddhisvarūpāsiddhijñānayoḥ pratibandhakatvam। tathā hi - sādhyābhāvavadvṛttitvaṃ vyabhicāraḥ। tathā ca aparvato dhūmavān vahneḥ' tadvattābuddhiṃ prati tadabhāvavattāniścayavidhayā pratibandhakam।
pratibandhakam। etādṛśasiddhāntavyāptiviṣayakaparāmarśaṃ prati grāhyābhāvānavagāhitayā nāsti pratibandhakatvam। maṇimantrādinyāyenaiva pratibandhakatā vaktavyā। aśabdo nityaḥ pratibandhakatvam। asādhyavyāpyatvābhāvavān hetuḥ'
iti parāmarśeṃ hetau sādhyavyāpyatvajñānāṃśe pratibandhakatvam। aayaṃ saṃbhavati। pakṣe ca vyāptiniścayapratibandhakatvamasādhāraṇyānupasaṃhāritvajñānayoḥ। pratibandhakatvam। evaṃ ahrado vahnimān dhūmāt' ityatra
pakṣadharmatābhānāṃśe pratibandhakatvamiti। tadetatsarvamabhisandhāyāha - prakāśikāyāṃ hetau sādhyābhāvavadvṛttitvasyetyādinā। hetvābhāsā iti kathanamayuktam। hetau upādhijñānadaśāyāṃ vaktavyatvādityāśaṅkate nanu pañcatvoktirayukteti। anumitau vā
hetvābhāsatvam। upādhijñānaṃ tu vyabhicārajñānotpādanadvāraiva parāmarśaṃ pratibadhnāti na sākṣāditi na tasya hetvābhāsatvam। ato na pañcatvoktivirodhaḥ। hetvābhāsalakṣaṇa iti। sākṣādityasya pratibandhakatve anvayaḥ।
paramukhanirīkṣakasyeti। parāmarśapratibandhakaṃ vyabhicārājñānaṃ nirīkṣamāṇasyetyarthaḥ। anena upādhijñānasya sākṣātpratibandhakatvābhāvaḥ sūcyate। nanu yathā ahrado vahnimāt dhūmāt' ityādau hetvābhāsalakṣaṇākrāntatvādityāśaṅkate - nanu tathāpīti।
tanmata ityāti। tathā hetvābhāsalakṣaṇākrāntatvena sādhyavatpakṣasya hetvābhāsatvamiṣṭameva। na ca pañcadhāvibhāgavyāghāta iti vācyam। āśrayāsiddhe antarbhāvāt। kathamantarbhāva iti cet ittham। āśrayāsiddhirdvividhā
dharmisvarūpāprasiddhiḥ pakṣatvāprasiddhiśceti। tatra pakṣatvāprasiddhau siddhasādhanasyāntarbhāva iti। taduktaṃ kusumāñjalau "madhyamāpi āśrayasvarūpāpratītyā tadviśeṣaṇapakṣatvāpratītyā ceti dvayī। tatra caramā siddhasādhanamiti vyapadiśyate। vyāptisthitau pakṣatvasyāhatya vighaṭanāt"iti। darśitamatamatiśithilamiti।
saddhisādhanasya hetvābhāsatvam। pakṣatārūpahetvabhāvādanumitiḥ paraṃ notpadyate। ataḥ siddhasādhanasthale na hetvābhāsodbhāvanam, api tu vādino nigrahamātramiti bhāvaḥ। siddheranumitipratibandhakatvaṃ vācyam। tathā
siddhānta iti। pratibandhakatvam। siddhisattve api sā siddhiryadi siṣādhayiṣāsahitā bhavati tadā anumityutpattyā siddhernānumitipratibandhakatvam। sādhyavatpakṣe nāstīti samādhatte-siṣādhayiṣāyā ityādinā।
durvāramityata āha - adhikamiti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - pratyakṣitaviṣaye api parāmarśasattve anumityutpattau na kiñcidbādhakam। ataḥ siddhernānumitiṃ prati pratibandhakatvam। evaṃ anumitihetuḥ। tathā ca siddheḥ anumitiṃ prati vā anumitikāraṇaṃ
hetvābhāsalakṣaṇākrāntateti। ।। AnTs upamitikaraṇam upamānam । saṃjñāsaṃjñisaṃbandhajñānam upamitiḥ । tatkaraṇaṃ sādṛśyajñānam । atideśavākyārthasmaraṇam avāntaravyāpāraḥ । tathā hi kaś cid gavayaśabdārtham ajānan kutaś cid āraṇyakapuruṣād gosadṛśo gavaya iti śrutvā vanaṃ gato vākyārthaṃ smaran gosadṛṣaṃ piṇḍaṃ paśyati । tadanantaram asau gavayaśabdavācya ity upamitir utpadyte ।। upamitikaraṇamupamānam। saṃjñāsaṃjñisambandhajñānamupamitiḥ।
tatkaraṇaṃ sādṛśyajñānam। tathā hi -kaścit gavayaśabdārthamajānan gataḥ vākyārthaṃ smaran gosadṛśaṃ piṇḍaṃ paśyati। tadanantaraṃ ayaṃ gavayapadavācyaḥ ityupamitirutpadyate। upamitikaraṇamiti।
lakṣayatīti। avasarasaṅgatyā upamānaṃ nirūpayatītyarthaḥ। upamitisvarūpaṃ vyutpādayati - mūle saṃjñeti। saṃjñā - gavayapadam। saṃjñī - gavayaḥ, tayoḥ sambandhaḥ śaktiḥ, tajjñānamityarthaḥ। lakṣaṇaṃ tu upaminomi ityanuvyavasāyagamyopamititvameva। vākyārthaṃ smaran
gosadṛśaṃ piṇḍaṃ paśyatīti। etane smaraṇaṃ sādṛśyadarśanajanyam udbodhakāntarajanyaṃ vā। ubhayamapi sādṛśyadarśanasahakāni, na tu sādṛśyadarśanajanyameva smaraṇaṃ sahakārīti sūcitam। smaran' ityatra vartamānasāmīpye pratyayaḥ। vākyārthaṃ
smariṣyannityarthaḥ। evaṃ ca vākyārthasmaraṇasya sādṛśyadarśanajanyatālābhena vyāpāratālābhaḥ ityāhuḥ। tadanantaramityādi। gavayatvarūpalaghudharmadharmitāvacchedakakopamitirutpadyata ityarthaḥ।
idamupalakṣaṇam - vaidharmyadarśanenāpyupamitiriti dhyeyam। ato nopamānaṃ pramāṇāntaram - ityāhuḥ। padavācyatvapramiteranubhavaddhitvāt। avasarasaṅgatyeti।
pratibandhakajijñāsānivṛttau avaśyavaktavyatvamavasaraḥ। anumānasya nirasanīyabahuvādivipratipattikatvāt। tathā cānumāne upamānanirūpaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। saṃjñā - vācakaḥ śabdaḥ, gavayādipadam। saṃjñī - vācyor'thaḥ gavayādiḥ। tayoḥ yaḥ sambandhaḥ śaktyākhyaḥ
tadviṣayakajñānamupamiti। agavayo gavayapadavācyaḥ' ityādyākārakaṃ śaktijñānamupamitiriti yāvat। sādṛśyajñānakaraṇakaṃ lakṣaṇamucitamityabhipretyāha - lakṣaṇaṃ tviti। pratibandhakībhūteti।
upamānanirūpaṇa iti śeṣaḥ। labhyate, tadayuktam। gosadṛśapiṇḍadarśanānantarameva atideśavākyārthasmaraṇāt ityāśaṅkyāha - eteneti। vartamānasāmīpya iti। avartamānasāmīpye vartamānavadvā'
ityanuśāsanena bhaviṣyati laṭi śatṛpratyayena smaranniti rūpam। smariṣyan ityarthaḥ। evaṃ cādau sādṛśyaviśiṣṭagavayapiṇḍadarśanaṃ yujyata iti bhāvaḥ। gavayapadavācyaḥ' ityākārikaivopamitirastu। na ceṣṭāpattiḥ,
gavayo gavayapadavācya ityākāriketi। upamiteḥ agosadṛśo vācyam। gosādṛśyaṃ gavayatvāpekṣayā guru iti jñānadaśāyāṃ agavayo gavayapadavācyaḥ' ityākārakataivopamiteryukteti bhāvaḥ। idamupalakṣaṇam। tatprakārakaśābdabodhe tadavacchedena śaktijñānasya
tu gavayatvaprakārakaḥ। anubhūyate ca gavayapadāt gavayatvaprakāraka eva śābdabodhaḥ। ataḥ gavayatvāvacchedena gavayapadavācyatvāvagāhī agavayo gavayapadavācya' iti jñānameva upamitirityapi bodhyam। vaidharmyadarśanenāpyupamitiriti। yatra kenacit govidharmā aśva
atideśavākyeti। tadvadidamiti vākyamatideśavākyam। prakṛte gosadṛśo gavaya iti vākyam atideśavākyam। gosadṛśapiṇḍeti।
piṇḍaśabdaḥ ākṛtiviśiṣṭavyaktiparaḥ। gosadṛśākāragavayavyaktidarśanamityarthaḥ। jñānamupamitiriti bhāvaḥ। vaiśeṣikāstvityādi।
ityunamānaprayogo atra vivakṣitaḥ। tathā ca gavayo gavayapadavācya iti pramā anumitireva na tadvilakṣaṇā। ato nopamānaṃ pramāṇāntaramiti vaiśeṣikāśayaḥ। tanmataṃ nirākaroti - vyāptijñānamantareṇāpīti।
kusumāñjalyādigrantheṣvityarthaḥ। ।। AnTs āptavākyaṃ śabdaḥ । āptas tu yathārthavaktā । vākyaṃ padasamūhaḥ । śaktaṃ padam । asmāt padād ayam artho boddhavya itīśvarasaṃketaḥ śaktiḥ ।। āptavākyaṃ śabdaḥ।
āptastu yathārthavaktā। āpteti। āptaṃ lakṣayati - āptastviti। śabdaṃ lakṣayatīti। upajīvyopajīvakatvasaṅgatyā śabdaṃ ni - payatītyarthaḥ। atra
upamitiśābdabodharūphalayoḥ saṅgatirbodhyā। tathā hi - śaktiparicchittirevopamitiḥ। tasyāśca śābdabodhopajīvyatvena phalayorupajīvyopajīvakatvasambhavaḥ। tādṛśasaṅgateśca karaṇaniṣṭhatvāt karaṇayoranantarābhidhānaprayojakatvam। śabdajñānasya
saṅgatiriti mantavyam। iti। śabda iti lakṣyanirdeśaḥ। pramāṇaśabda iti tadarthaḥ। āptavākyamiti lakṣaṇam। siñcatītyādiśabdaḥ āptoktavākyam। na tu vahninā
yathārthavaktṛtvarūpāptatvābhāvāt। niṣkarṣaḥ। vākyaprayoge vākyārthañjñānasya hetutvāt lakṣaṇasaṅgatiḥ। sphuṭametat śabdamaṇau। upajīvyopajīvakatvasaṅgatyeti। upamānam upajīvyaṃ
kāraṇam, śabdaḥ upajīvakaḥ kāryaḥ। tathā ca śabdopamānayoḥ upamānānantaraṃ śabdanirūpaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। upajīvyopajīvakabhāvamevopapādayati - atretyādinā। bhāvaḥ-pramāṇayorūpajīvyojīvakabhāvo atra durvacaḥ। śabdapramāṇaṃ hi
jñāyamānaḥ vākyātmakaḥ śabdaḥ। upamānapramāṇaṃ tu sādṛśyadarśanam। tatkāryatvaṃ tu śabde nāstīti। śabdopamānātmakapramāṇayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvo na sambhavati। śabdopamānajanyapramityorevātrakāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ। śabdajanyāpramitiḥ
śābdabodhaḥ। upamānajanyā pramitiḥ ayamasau gavayapadavācya ityādyākārakaḥ śaktigrāhaḥ। śaktigrahajanyatvaṃ ca śābdabodhe vartata iti। na ca kāryakāraṇabhāvātmakasaṅgateḥ pramitidvayaniṣṭhatve api śabdapramāṇanirūpaṇe tādṛśasaṅgaternopayoga iti vācyam।
svāśrayajanakatvasambandhena pramāṇaniṣṭhatvāt। svaṃ - kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ, svāśrayau upamitiśābdabodhau, tajjanakatvamupamānaśabdayoriti। tathā pramāṇaniṣṭhatvāt upamānānantaraṃ śabdanirūpaṇaṃ saṅgatamiti। idaṃ prācīnamatānusāreṇa।
śabdajñānameva śabdapramāṇam। upamitirapi gavayo gavayapadavācya pakṣaviṣayakatvāt śabdajñānarūpaiva। sā ca sādṛśyajñānarūpopamānapramāṇajanyā। evaṃ ca kāryakāraṇabhāvarūpā saṅgatirastīti।
upamānopajīvakatvābhāvāditi। upamānapramāṇajanyatvābhāvādityarthaḥ। śaktiparicchittiriti। śaktiviṣayakajñānamityarthaḥ। tasyāśca - śaktiparicchitteśca। śābdabodhopajīvyatvena - śābdabodhajanakatvena।
karaṇayoranantarābhidhānaprayojakatvamiti। karaṇayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ yat saṃgaterityarthaḥ। āptakartṛkoccāraṇaviṣayabhūtaṃ vākyamityarthaḥ। āptastu yathārthavakteti abādhitārthaviṣayakajñānajanakaśabdaprayogakartetyartho labhyate।
yathābhūto abādhitār'tho yathārthaḥ। tasya vaktā iti vigrahāt। vaktā tadviṣayakajñānajanakaśabdaprayogakartā। āptavākyaṃ śabda iti mūlācca śabdapramāṇasya lakṣaṇamiti pratīyate। tadapekṣayā bhavitumarhatītyāśayenāha - prakṛtavākyārtheti।
lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। tadāha - vākyaprayoga iti। sphuṭametat śabdamaṇāviti। tattvacintāmaṇau śabdakhaṇḍe - gaṅgeśavākyamatrābhisaṃhitam। ।।
padasamūhaḥ। asmāt padāt ayamartho boddhavya iti īśvarasaṅgetaḥ śaktiḥ। vākyamiti। padalakṣaṇamāha - śaktamiti। arthasmṛtyanukūlapadapadārthasambandhaḥ śaktiḥ। sā ca
padārthāntaramiti mīmāṃsakāḥ। tannirāsārthamāha - asmāditi। padārthāntaramityarthaḥ। arthasmṛtyanukūleti। śābdabodhajanaka-arthasmṛtyanukūlaḥ ghaṭādipadaghaṭādirūpārthayoḥ sambandhaḥ śaktirityarthaḥ।
iha prayojakatvam। tacca kāraṇatāvacchedakapadapadārthasambanadhe apyakṣatam। vivakṣitārthakam। anyasambandhajñānasyārthasmṛtijanakatve api śābdabodhajanakasmṛtijanakatvābhāvāt। arthasmṛtyanukūlatvasya
adṛṣṭādisādhāraṇyāt viśeṣyamiti dhyeyam। tattatpadārthatāvacchedakābhāvakūṭavadityarthaḥ। tenātiriktapadārthatvasya anyamatāprasiddhatve api na vyāghātaḥ। asmāt padāt ayamartho boddhavya ityākārakeśvarecchā śaktirityarthaḥ।
padārthāntaramiti। na ceśvarīyajñānasyecchāyāḥ kṛtervā śaktirūpatvamiti vinigamanāvirahāt atiriktaiva śaktiriti vācyam। vinigamakasaṃbhavena, icchāyā eva śaktitvasvīkārāt। ghaṭapadavācyatvasya atiprasaṅgaḥ। evaṃ
śaktyaiva tadbodhasambhave lakṣaṇocchedāpattiriti - vācyam। yataḥ tattatpadajanyabodhaviṣayatvaprakāratānirūpiteśvarecchīyaviśeṣyatāvattvam। tādṛśaprakāratānirūpitaviśeṣyatāsambandhena tadicchāvattvaṃ vā। tathā ca tādṛśasya ghaṭapadavācyatvasya paṭe asattvāt nātiprasaṅgaḥ।
svātantryeṇa bhānamīśvarecchāyāṃ upeyate। itthaṃ ca icchāvattvasya tīre asattvena na kṣatiriti saṅkṣepaḥ। śābdabodhajanaketi। anekapadārthasaṃsargāvagāhijñānaṃ śābdabodhaḥ। tasya janakaṃ padārthānāṃ smaraṇam, tadanukūlaḥ
padapadārthasambandhaḥ śaktiḥ। tadanukūlatvaṃ ca tajjanakajñānaviṣayatvam। vākyaghaṭakapadajñānāt tattatpadārthasmaraṇaṃ bhavati। padajñānaṃ hi janayati। yathā pūrvaṃ sambaddhatayā dṛṣṭayoḥ hastihastapakayordhadhye aparamartharūpaṃ sambandhinaṃ smartuṃ śaknoti। tathā ca
vivakṣitaḥ। padapadārthasambandhasyārthasmṛtijanakatvābhāvādasambhavaḥ। ata āha - kāraṇakāraṇatāvacchedakobhayasādhārāṇam। sambandhaviśiṣṭajñānaṃ ityarthaḥ। tathā ca arthasmṛtikāraṇam
sambandhaviśiṣṭajñānam। tatra viṣayitāsambandhena vidyamānatayā padapadārthasambandhasya kāraṇatāvacchedakatvamakṣatam। kāraṇe vidyamānasyaiva kāraṇatāvacchedakatvāt। tathā ca padapadārthasambandhasya arthasmṛtiprayojakatvāt tadanukūlatvaṃ sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca
śakterlakṣaṇamiti paryavasannam। tatra viśeṣyānupādāne adṛṣṭādiṣvativyāptiḥ। teṣāṃ kāryasāmānyaṃ prati kāraṇatayā arthasmṛtiṃ pratyapi kāraṇatvāt। tadvāraṇāya viśeṣyopādānam। adṛṣṭādeḥ padapadārthasambandhatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ।
kālikādisambandhaḥ tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya viśeṣaṇam। tasyāḥ smṛteḥ śābdabodhajanakatvaṃ nāsti। ataḥ nātivyāptiḥ। tadāha ghaṭādipadetyādinā। vivakṣitārthakamiti। śābdabodhajanakasmṛtyanukūlatvārthakamityarthaḥ।
labhyate। tathā sati naiyāyikamate aprasaddhiḥ। kḷptapadārthātiriktatvasya aprasiddhatvāt। tathā ca mīmāṃsakena naiyāyikaṃ prati tatsādhane vyācaṣṭe-tattatpadārthatāvacchedakābhāvakūṭavadityartha iti। pratyekaṃ śaktirityarthaḥ। anyamatāprasiddhatve apīti। naiyāyikamate aprasiddhatve api
ityarthaḥ। na vyāghātaḥ - nānupapattiḥ। asmāt padādityatra pañcamyāḥ janyatvamarthaḥ। tasya budhadhātvarthabodhe anvayaḥ। ṇyatpratyayasya vaṣiyatvamarthaḥ। tathā ca etatpadajanyabodhaviṣayo ayamartha iti labhyate। tadāha-iti mūlasyeti। ādhunikasaṅketasyetyādi।
vyaktiviśeṣabodho bhavatīti svīkāraṇīyam। aghaṭadipadāt ayamartho ghaṭādibodha iti vaktavyam। saṅketatvaṃ ca dharmaḥ। tathā ceśvarecchāyāḥ śaktitve ekavidhameva kāraṇatvam। tattatpadajanyabodhaviṣayatvaprakārakasya
gauravam। ataḥ īśvarecchaiva śaktirityarthaḥ। vinigamakaṃ vinigamanā iti padayoḥ anyatarapakṣasādhakayuktirityarthaḥ। ityādi। īśvarecchāyāḥ sarvaviṣayakatvamekatvaṃ cāṅgīkriyate। sā cet śaktiḥ tarhi paṭāderapi aghaṭādipadavācyatvaṃ prasajyeta। tathā
vaktavyam। aghaṭapadajanyabodhaviṣayo ghaṭo bhavatu' ityākārikāyāṃ bhagavadicchāyāṃ ghaṭo viśeṣyaḥ ghaṭapadajanyabodhaviṣayatvaṃ prakāraḥ। ghaṭapadaśakyatvam। īśvarecchāyāśca ekatvāt tasyāḥ kuḍyaṃ bhavatu' ityādyākārakatvamapyaṅgīkaraṇīyam। tathā
paṭādāvapi sattvāt paṭāderapi ghaṭapadavācyatvaprasaṅgaḥ। evaṃ lakṣaṇāyāḥ bhaṅgaśca prasajyeteti śaṅkāyāḥ āśayaḥ। ghaṭapadaboddhavyatvaprakārakatadicchāyā iti। ghaṭapadajanyabodhaviṣayatvaprakārakeśvarecchāyā ityarthaṃḥ।
yatastatpadavācyatvamityādi। viśeṣyatāsambandhena yena pūrvoktadoṣau syātām। api tu tatpadavācyatvam। īśvarecchāyā ekatvena tasyāṃ sarvasya viśeṣyatve prakārabhedena bhinnabhinnā bhavati। evaṃ ca aghaṭapadajanyabodhaviṣayo
anavagāhanāt। ataḥ paṭādeḥ। evaṃ lakṣaṇāsthale agaṅgāpadajanyo bodho bhavatu' īśvarecchāyāmaṅgīkriyate। īśvarecchāvattvameva gaṅgāpadavācyatvam।
tīrasya nāstīti tīre gaṅgāpadalakṣaṇāyāḥ svīkāryatayā। na lakṣaṇocchedāpattiśceti bhāvaḥ। tadṛśasya ghaṭapadavācyatvasyeti। ghaṭapadavācyatvasyetyarthaḥ। nātiprasaṅgaḥ - na paṭasya ghaṭapadavācyatvaprasaṅgaḥ।
padārthabodho bhavati tatraiveśvarecchāyāṃ āvaśyakatā। lakṣaṇatā yatra bodhaḥ, tatra neśvarecchāyā āvaśyakatvam। śakyasambandhamātrasyaivāpekṣitatvāt। tathā ca agaṅgāpadajanyo bodho bhavatu, bodhaviṣayastīraṃ bhavatu', ityadyākārakecchākalpanaṃ mudhā।
tīrasya gaṅgāpadavācyatvaṃ tu prāguktaprakāreṇaiva vāryate। āha - saṅkṣepa iti। kāryasāmānyaṃ prati īśvarecchāyāḥ kāraṇamiti vaktavyam। tatra kimākārā īśvarecchā kāraṇamiti iti bhāvaḥ।
prathamamupasthitatvāt। vyaktilābhastu ākṣepāditi kecit। tanna - sambhavena, jātiviśiṣṭavyaktāveva śaktikalpanāt। vyavasthāpayituṃ mīmāṃsakamataṃ upanyasya dūṣayatigavādīti। śaktikalpanaṃ na sambhavati। ataḥ jātigrahasya prathamamapekṣitatvena
jātāveva śaktikalpanaṃ ucitam lāghavāt ityāha - viśeṣaṇatayeti। prathamamupasthitatvāditi। viśiṣṭagrahāt pūrvamavagatatvādityarthaḥ। kathaṃ tarhi vyaktilābha ityata āha - vyaktīti। arthāpattipramāṇādityarthaḥ। vyaktāveva sambhaveneti।
anubhavasiddhatvena cetyapi bodhyam। viśiṣṭavyaktāveveti। evakāreṇa kevalajātikalpanavyavacchedaḥ। bodhyam-jāti-tadvaiśiṣṭya-tadāśrayeṣu triṣu śaktiḥ kalpanīyā। śābdabodhe bhānāsambhavāditi।
kalpanīyeti vadanti। vyavasthāpayitumiti। gavādipadānāṃ gotvādijātiviśiṣṭavyaktau śaktiṃ nirdhārayitumityarthaḥ। viśiṣṭagrahāsambhaveneti। gotvaviśiṣṭavyaktijñānāt pūrvaṃ gotvarūpaviśeṣaṇajñānaṃ āvaśyakam।
śaktikalpanamucitam, na tu tadviśiṣṭavyaktāviti bhāvaḥ। evakāreṇa vyaktiṣu śaktivyavacchedaḥ। vyaktīnāmānantyāt jāteścaikatvāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu jātau śaktisvīkāre gavādipadāt gotvādijātereva bodhaḥ syāt na tu vyakteḥ।
ghaṭāderapi bodhaḥ syādityaśayena śaṅkate - kathaṃ tarhīti। arthāpattipramāṇādityartha iti। jātiviṣayakajñānasya gopadajanyaśābdabodhe vyakterbhānamiti bhāvaḥ। gopadasya govyaktau śaktyabhāve api lakṣaṇā aṅgīkriyate। ato
lakṣaṇayā śābdabodhe vyaktibhānamityapi draṣṭavyam। etena bhānāpattirityapāstam। anupapattipratisandhāneti। vyaktibhānaṃ vinā vyaktibhānasyānubhavasiddhatayā nārthāpattipramāṇāt vyaktibhānam। na lakṣaṇayā vyaktibhānamityarthaḥ। kevalajātikalpanavyaccheda iti।
kevalajātau śaktikalpanasya vyavaccheda ityarthaḥ। gotvajāteḥ gotvasamavāyasya ca bhānopapattiḥ। śakyatāvacchedakatvāt samavāyasya kathaṃ bhānam। na cākāṅkṣayā bhānamiti vācyam। dvābhyāṃ bodhyamityādinā। tathā ca ghaṭatva-samavāya-ghaṭeṣu triṣu ghaṭapadasyaikā
sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। padārthadvayasambandhasyaiveti। ityanena vivakṣitaḥ। evakāreṇa śakya-śakyatāvacchedakayoḥ sambandho vyavacchidyate। padadvayasamabhivyāhāralabhyatveneti। āvakāṅkṣābhāsyatvenetyarthaḥ। akāṅkṣayā alabhyasya
ghaṭatvādijāteścetyarthaḥ। navyāstviti। yathā śaktiḥ na kalpanīyeti bhāvaḥ। ca śābdabodhāpattiḥ। pṛthivī pṛthivīpadaśakyā itivat
pṛthivīpadaśakyamityākārasya śaktigrahasya sambhavāt। tīratvāvacchinne tīrabodha itivat। tathā ca lakṣaṇayā śakyārthabodhe api niyamo na syāt। śakyatāvacchedake śaktisvīkāre tu pṛthivīpadāt pṛthivītvenaiva śābdabodha iti niyama upapadyate।
ataḥ śakyatāvacchedake api śaktiḥ svīkaraṇīyetyāhuḥ। taccintyam। tādṛśaśābdabodhahetuḥ। śakyatāvacchedakaśca sarvatra svarūpasambandharūpāvacchedakatvānaṅgīkārāt। tathā ca
śakyatāvacchedakatvam। atastatra śakyatāvacchedakatvajñānaṃ pramātmakaṃ na sambhavatīti na tasya pramātmakaśābdabodhahetutvam। lakṣaṇāsthale tu śābdabodhaheturupeyate। tathā ca śaktisthale pṛthivītvenaiva śaktyā tathā śakyatāvacchedake api na śaktiriti navīnānāmāśayaḥ। tadetatsarvaṃ
padābhyāṃ sūcitamiti dhyeyam। vṛddhavyavahāreṇa। vyutpitsurbālaḥ agāmānaya' iti aśvatvaviśiṣṭe śaktiriti vyutpadyate। vṛddhavyavahāreṇeti। śaktigrahastu vṛddhavyavahārādinā sambhavatītyarthaḥ।
ādinā vyākaraṇādiparigrahaḥ। ata eva vyākaraṇopamānakośāptavākyādvyavahārataśca। śeṣādvivṛtervadanti sānnidhyataḥ siddhapadasya vṛddhāḥ।। saṅgacchate। vyākaraṇāt prakṛtipratyayādīnāṃ śaktigrahaḥ। upamānāt
śaktigrahastu adhastāddarśitaḥ। gaṇeśatvaviśiṣṭe śaktigrahaḥ। tatraikadantādiśabdānāmeva padārthatayā teṣāṃ vibhinnatvena dvandvopapattiḥ। akokilaḥ pikaśabdavācyaḥ' ityāptavākyāt pikapadasya kokile śaktigrahaḥ।
upapādayati - vyutpitsuriti। śaktigrahecchāvānityarthaḥ। uttamavṛdveti। prayojakavṛddhetyarthaḥ। madhyamavṛddhasyeti। prayojyavṛddhasyetyarthaḥ। gavānayanaṃ dṛṣṭvā pravṛttimupalabhya cetyanvayaḥ। upalabhyetyasyānumāyetyarthaḥ। aiyaṃ kriyā prayatnapūrvikā
vilakṣaṇakriyātvāt svīyakriyāvat' ityanumānaprayogo bodhyaḥ। pravṛttijanakajñānasya - gavānayanagocaraprayatnajanakagavānayanajñānasya। samabhivyāhāralabhyatvāt। aananyalabhyo hi śabdārtha' iti nyāyādityabhisandhimāha - aśvamānayetyādi।
āvāpaḥ - saṅgrahaḥ। vyutpadyata iti। vyutpattyāśrayo bhavatītyarthaḥ। jāyate patraśātanam। yavāḥ kaṇiśaśālinaḥ।।'
dīrghaśūkaviśiṣṭe śaktinirṇayaḥ। priyaṅgau tu śaktibhramāt prayogaḥ। śaktigrahaḥ। prasiddhapadasānnidhyāt śaktigrahastu avikasitapadme madhukaraḥ' ityādyagrimagranthena sphuṭībhaviṣyati ityalaṃ pallavitena। vṛddhavyavahāreṇeti। vaddhayoḥ jñānavatoḥ vyavahāraḥ pravṛttiḥ
śabdaprayogaśca vṛddhavyavahāraḥ। prakṛtipratyapādīnāmiti। abhū sattādirūpārthe śaktigrahaḥ। alaḥ karmaṇi ca bhāve cākarmakebhyaḥ' ityādivyākaraṇāt pratyayasyārthaṃviśeṣe śaktigrahaḥ। adhastāddarśita iti। pūrvamupamānapariccheda darśitaḥ। nanu aapyekadantaheramba'
ekārthavācakatayā kathaṃ dvandvasamāsaḥ। padārthabheda eva dvandvasamāsāṅgīkārādityatrāha - tatraikadantādīti। ete śabdāḥ etādṛśārthabodhakā iti jñāpanārthaṃ hi kośaḥ। tatraikadantādayaḥ śabdāḥ tattadānupūrvīkaśabdarthakā eveti bhāvaḥ।
vyutpitsurbāla ityādi। kaścit bālakaḥ gavādipadānāṃ kasminnarthe śaktiriti jijñāsate। sa kadācit kenacit prerakeṇa ācāryādināṃ paśyati। tataḥ gavānayanarūpakriyāṃ prati kāraṇabhūtaṃ prayatnamanuminoti। tataḥ kiñcitkriyāviṣayakaprayatnaṃ prati
niścinoti। tataśca prayojyavṛddhasya gokarmakānayanaviṣayakaṃ jñānaṃ agāmānaya' iti vākyajanyamiti niścinoti। tatra vyavahārasya śaktigrāhakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। pravṛttiśabdaḥ prayatnaparaḥ। śaktiḥ kalpyatāmityatrāha - prakāśikāyām vākyasyeti। viśiṣṭer'the
iti। gokarmakatvaviśiṣṭānayanarūpe vākyārthe ityarthaḥ। tathā ca bhāvaḥ। api ca gopadasyānayanānvitagavi śaktisvīkāre agāṃ badhāna' ityatrāpi tādṛśagobodhopapattiḥ। evamānayapadasya gokarmakānayane śaktisvīkāre aaśvamānaya' ityatrāpi tadbodhāpattiḥ। ataḥ gopadasya
gotvaviśiṣṭe ānayapadasya ānayanatvaviśiṣṭe ca śaktirniścīyate। suniścayam। etadabhiprāyeṇaiva āvāpodvāpopanyāsa iti bhāvaḥ। vyutpatyāśrayo bhavatīti। śaktiniścayavān bhavatītyarthaḥ। vivaraṇādyatheti।
tatsamānārthakapadāntareṇa tadarthakathanaṃ vivaraṇam। aśaktigrahaṃ manasikṛtyoktam - alaṃ pallaviteneti। iti cet - na। akāśyāṃ tribhuvanatilako bhūpatirāste' ityādau ca।
vyavahārasya। kāryaparatvāditi yojanā। kāryaparatvaṃ ca kṛtisādhyānayanādirūpakriyātātparyakatvam। vyutpattiḥ - śaktigrahaḥ। vyavacchedyaṃ sphuṭayati - na siddheti। siddhe api vyavahārāditi। tathā ca
siddhe api śaktigrahastvāvaśyakaḥ। anyathā tatrānubhavasiddhasya śabdabodhasya apalāpāpatteriti bhāvaḥ। ityatra siddhaśabdaḥ kriyāvyatiriktaparaḥ। śabdavṛttiḥ। śakyasambandho lakṣaṇā। gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityatra
kalpyate। saindhavādau lavaṇāśvayoḥ parasparasambandhābhāvāt nānāśaktikalpanam। jahallakṣaṇā, ajahallakṣaṇā, jahadajahallakṣaṇā ceti। yatra vācyārthasyānvayābhāvaḥ tatra jahallakṣaṇā। yathā mañcāḥ krośantīti। yatra
vācyārthasyāpyanvayaḥ tatra ajahaditi। yathā chatriṇo gacchantīti। yatra ekadeśānvayaḥ tatra jahadajahaditi। kalpyata iti। gaṅgāpadasyeti śeṣaḥ। nanu evaṃ saindhavādipadānāṃ āha - saindhavādāviti। ādinā haryādiparigrahaḥ। sambandhābhāvāditi।
saṃyogādirūpasambandhābhāvādityarthaḥ। vinigamakābhāvena ubhayatra śaktikalpanasyāvaśyakateti। mañcā iti। mañcapadaṃ mañcasthapuruṣe lākṣaṇikam। vācyāryasya
krośanakartṛtvānvayābhāvādityarthaḥ। apinā lakṣyasamuccayaḥ। ekasārthavāhitvena chatryacchatriṣu gamanakartṛtvānvayaḥ। tātparyānupapattireva lakṣaṇābījam। na ca kathamidamudāharaṇamiti vācyam। apratipādyasambandha eva lakṣaṇā'
ityetadabhiprāyeṇa tadudāharaṇadānāt। anyathā akākebhyo dadhi rakṣyatām' ityādyudāhartavyam। tatra kākapadasya kākataditarasādhāraṇadadhyupavātakatvāvacchinnaparatvāt। ekasārthe lakṣaṇā। taddhitārthaḥ sambandhī। tathā caikasārthaṃsambandhino
gacchantītyanvayabodhaḥ ityāhuḥ। tattvamasīti। viśeṣaṇāṃśaparityāgaḥ। tathā ca tatpadalakṣyasya śuddhasya tvaṃpadalakṣyeṇa saha abhedānvayopapattirityabhiprāyaḥ। idamudāharaṇaṃ tu
jīvabrahmaṇoraikyaṃ bruvatāṃ brahmavādināṃ matābhiprāyeṇa। naiyāyikamate tasyāsaṃmatatvāt। naiyāyikamatarītyā tu asāyam devadatta' sambhavādahānamiti jahadajahallakṣaṇāmācakṣate। jahadajahallakṣaṇayeti vadanti।
saṃyogādirūpasambandhābhāvāditi। tathā ca saindhavapadasya śaktirityarthaḥ। mañcasthapuruṣa iti। svārasikatvādityāhuḥ। mañcapadaśakyārthasya mañcasya
lakṣaṇeti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca yādṛśapade jahallakṣaṇā, jahatī ca sā lakṣaṇā ceti karmadhārayāt। athavā śakyārthaṃ jahataḥ tyajataḥ padasya lakṣaṇā jahallakṣaṇeti ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣaḥ। yatra ajahallakṣaṇā। ayathā chatriṇo gacchanti' iti। atra chatripadasya
chatryacchatrighaṭitasamudāye lakṣaṇā। ekasārthavāhitveneti। ekasamudāyaghaṭakatvenetyarthaḥ। tṛtīyāyāḥ vaiśiṣṭyamarthaḥ। tasya chatryacchatriṣvanvayaḥ। chatripadalakṣyeṣu ekasamudāyaghaṭakatvaviśiṣṭeṣu chatryacchatriṣu gamanakartṛtvānvaya iti bhāvaḥ।
lakṣaṇāyā bījam। ayaṣṭīḥ praveśaya' ityādau yaṣṭipadavācyānāṃ tātparyānupapattireva lakṣaṇābījamiti। yaṣṭidharatātparyeṇaiva ayaṣṭīḥ nopapadyeteti lakṣaṇābījaṃ tatrāpyastīti bhāvaḥ। ekakāreṇānvayānupapattivyavacchedaḥ।
padamiti padalakṣaṇāt chatrin iti vākyameva। chatrapadasya chatre prakṛtipratyayarūpapadadvayasamūharūpatvāt chatripadasya। vākye ca sambhavati। tathā ca chatrinnityasya ajahallakṣaṇodāharaṇatvaṃ na sambhavatīti śaṅkate-na ca chatrītyasyeti। sambandhārthaketyarthaḥ।
pratipādyasambandha iti। bodhyārthasambandha ityarthaḥ। tathā ca lakṣaṇopapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। śakyasambandha eva lakṣaṇeti svīkāra ityarthaḥ। kākataditarabiḍālādisādhāraṇaṃ
yat dadhināśakatvaṃ tadavacchinne kākapadasya lakṣaṇetyarthaḥ। dadhināśakatvena rūpeṇa kākasyāpi bodhāt ajahallakṣaṇātvam। vadatāṃ matamāha - kecittviti। ekasamudāyatva ityarthaḥ। chatriṇo gacchantītyasya ekasamudāyatvavavanto
gacchantītyarthaḥ। samudāyatvaṃ cāpekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatvam। atha vā ghaṭakatvarūpasambandhaviśiṣṭor'thaḥ। āhuḥ ityasvarasodbhāvanam। bhānābhāvāt atratyalakṣaṇāyā ajahatsvārthatvānupapattiriti। ityādi। tattvamasītyatra tatpadasya sarvajñatvādiviśiṣṭacaitanyaṃ
vācyor'thaḥ। tvaṃpadasya antaḥkaraṇaviśiṣṭacaitanyaṃ vācyor'thaḥ। samānavibhakterabhedor'thaḥ। sa ca viśiṣṭayorbādhitaḥ। ataḥ caitanyamātraṃ dvābhyāṃ padābhyāṃ lakṣyate। so ayaṃ devadatta ityādāviti। tatpadasya taddeśatatkālavṛttitvaviśiṣṭor'thaḥ।
idaṃpadasya etaddeśaitatkālaviśiṣṭor'thaṃḥ। viśiṣṭayoraikyaṃ ca bādhitam। ataḥ tatpadaśakyārthaviśiṣṭaikadeśasya tatpadasya lakṣaṇā। evaṃ ca yatra viśeṣaṇasya śakyaikadeśasya tyāgena viśeṣyasya śakyaikadeśasya bodhastatra jahadajahallakṣaṇetyuktaṃ bhavati।
pare tviti। yathā jahadajahallakṣaṇā māstviti bhāvaḥ। lakṣyamāṇaguṇasambandhasvarūpā। yathā agnirmāṇavaka iti। vyañjanāpi anyathāsiddhā।
vṛttyantaratvaṃ nirācaṣṭe - gauṇyapīti। nanu agaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa' lakṣaṇayā nirvāha ityata āha - lakṣyamāṇeti। lakṣyamāṇo yo guṇaḥ śucitvādiḥ tatsambandharūpāṃ ityarthaḥ। ayamabhiprāyaḥ - śakyasambandho hi lakṣaṇā। sa ca kvacitsākṣātsambandhaḥ, kvacitparamparāsambandhaḥ। evaṃ ca
śakyasyāgneḥ svaniṣṭhaśucitvavattvasambandha eva lakṣaṇeti। śaityapāvanatvādipratītyartham। na ca sā pratītirlakṣaṇayā upapadyate śaityapāvanatvādiviśiṣṭalakṣaṇāyāṃ mānābhāvāt। tasmāt vyañjanāvṛttiraṅgīkartavyeti। tanmataṃ nirasyati -
vyañjanāpīti। śaktilakṣaṇāntarbhūteti। ayambhāvaḥ - nānārthakasthale adūrasthā bhūdharā pratītiḥ sambhavati। agaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa' ityādau tu śaityapāvanatvādiviśiṣṭatīrapratītirapi lakṣaṇāsāmrājyādeva। tatra
kiṃ vyañjanayeti। vyañjanāyā anyathāsiddhatve api arthaśaktimūlāyāstasyā nānyathāsiddhiḥ। śivāḥ। bhūyāt yatra gato bhavān।।"
tava gamanottaraṃ mama prāṇanāśo bhaviṣyati। ato na gantavyam' ityādyartho vyajyate। na hyatra śaktilakṣaṇābhyāṃ nirvāhaḥ। itthaṃ ca vyañjanāyā āvaśyakatetyata āha - arthaśaktimūlā ceti। anumānādineti। anumānaprayogastu - aiyaṃ
ityādirūpaḥ। ādinā saṃbhāvanādi parigrahaḥ। utkaṭaikatarakoṭikasaṃśayassambhāvanā। autkaṭyaṃ ca viṣayatāviśeṣaḥ। mantavyam। guṇa ityādi। lakṣyamāṇaḥ śakyārthavṛttiryo guṇaḥ
tatsajātīyaguṇavattvaṃ gauṇīvṛttirityarthaḥ। agnirmāṇavaka ityatra tatsajātīyaśucitvavān māṇavaka iti bodhaḥ। nanvetādṛśyāḥ ayamabhiprāya iti। śakyārthapratiyogikaḥ sambandho lakṣaṇā। sambandhaśca sākṣātparamparāsādhāraṇaḥ। gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityādau
gaṅgāpadaśakyārthasya saṃyogarūpaḥ sākṣātsambandhastīre asti। svavṛttiguṇasajātīyaguṇavattvarūpaḥ paramparāsambandhaḥ māṇavake asti। ubhayorapi sambandhayorlakṣaṇātvameveti bhāvaḥ। punariti। yadi agaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa' ityādau tīravṛttirghoṣa
tīre ghoṣa iti। ghoṣānanvitārthavācakaṃ gaṅgāpadaṃ ca prayuñjīta। ato atra śakyārthavṛttiśaityapāvanatvādirūpor'tho api ghoṣe vivakṣitaḥ। sa ca atīre ghoṣa' ityato na budhyeta। gaṅgāpadaprayoge tu śakyate। na ca gaṅgāpadasyaiva śaityapāvanatvādiviśiṣṭatīre
vyañjanayā na prayojanamiti vācyam। anvayānupapattirhi lakṣaṇābījam। pramāṇābhāvāt। tasmāt vyañjanākhyā atiriktā vṛttiḥ svīkaraṇīyā, bhāvaḥ। ayaṃ bhāva ityādi।
dūrasthitasya ramyatvaṃ prakṛtor'thaḥ। asthiracittatvāt rājāno api dūrasthā eva ramyā ityaprakṛtor'tho apyatra pratīyate। sā ca pratītiḥ bhūdharaśabdaśaktimūlā। tathā ca nānārthasthale arthaprakaraṇādinā śabdaśaktimūlāvyañjanā ityālaṅkārikāḥ। tatra bhūdharaśabdena
naiyāyikāḥ। evaṃ gaṅgāyāṃ ghoṣa ityādau gaṅgāpadasya śaityādipratītirupapadyate। yadyapyatrānvayānupapattirnāsti, tathāpi vinānupapatteḥ। tātparyānupapattireva lakṣaṇābījam nānvayānupapattiriti pūrvamevoktaṃ vakṣyati ca dīpikāyām। tathā ca
kṛtaṃ vyañjanayeti bhāvaḥ। śaṅkate - nanviti। anyathāsiddhatve api - śaktyā lakṣaṇayā vā gatārthatve api। arthasāmarthyāt yatrārthāntaraṃ pratīyate tatrārthaśaktimūlā vyañjanā। yathā agaccha gacchasi
pravāsottarakālikamaraṇarūpor'tho abhivyajyate। tena ca gamanābhāvo vyajyate। asyārthasya padavṛttyā śaktyā lakṣaṇayā vā pratītyasambhavāt vyañjanākhyā vṛttiḥ svīkāryetyāśayaḥ śaṅkituḥ। lakṣaṇābījam। tatpratītīcchayoccaritatvaṃ tātparyam। tātparyajñānaṃ ca
vākyārthajñāne hetuḥ nānārthānu rodhāt। prakaraṇādikaṃ tātparyagrāhakam। lakṣaṇābījatve yaṣṭīḥ praveśaya ityādau lakṣaṇānupapattiḥ। yaṣṭidhare lakṣaṇā sambhavatītyāśayenāha - tātparyānupapattiriti।
tatpratītīti। tīrādirūpārthapratītītyarthaḥ। nānārtheti। tatkāraṇatvasyāvaśyakatve tadanurodhena sarvatra tadāvaśyakateti bhāvaḥ। na caṃ mauniślokādau śābdabodhānupapattiḥ। tatra niruktatātparyasya tādṛśatātparyasya sattvenādoṣāt। na ca tathāpi
śaṅkyam। tatreśvarecchāmādāyaivānupapatteḥ parihārasambhavāt iti śaṅkyam। tatreśvarecchāmādāyaivānupapatteḥ parihārasambhavāt parihārasambhavāt ityalamadhikajalpanena। ādinā tātparyanirṇāyakasya asaśaṅkhacakra' iti viśeṣaṇādeḥ parigrahaḥ।
kathaṃ prakaraṇādeḥ tātparyagrāhakatvamiti cet - ittham। aidaṃ iti rītyā gṛhāṇa। niyatakāla iti। kālavyavasthetyarthaḥ। nānārthakasthale śābdabodhe
tātparyajñānasya kāraṇatvānusāreṇetyarthaḥ। tātparyajñānasyāvaśvakatetyarthaḥ। nanu tātparyajñānamasambhavīti śaṅkate - na ca mauniślokādāviti। maunikartṛkavākyabodhakalipyādāvityarthaḥ। nirūktatātparyasya -
tatpratītīcchayā uccaritatvarūpatātparyasya। tātparyaṃ tatpratītīcchāmātram। tattu maunināmapyasti। tajjñānācca lipyāditaḥ śābdabodha upapadyata ityāśayena samādhatte - tātparyasyeti। nanu tatpratītīcchāpi na tātparyam। śukādeḥ tādṛśecchāvirahe api
na ca tathāpīti। śukoccāritādasmādvākyāt etādṛśārthabodho bhavatu ityākārakeśvarecchaiva tatra tātparyam। tajjñānācca śābdabodha iti bhāvaḥ। alamadhikajalpaneneti। visaṃvādiśukavākye śikṣakasyecchaiva
tātparyam, ato na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। nirvāhāt tātparyajñānasya śābdabodhahetutvamāvaśyakam। uktam। tatrādipadagrāhyamāha - ādineti। prakaraṇaṃ nāma
bhojanagamanādiprastāvaḥ। viśeṣaṇādaiḥ ityādipadane ābhimukhyādiparigrahaḥ। bhojanaprakaraṇe uktatvāditi। yannaivaṃ tannaivaṃ yathā pramāṇaprakaraṇe prayuktaṃ saindhavapadamiti śeṣaḥ pūraṇīyaḥ। iti rītyeti। ityanumānavidhayetyarthaḥ।
ityādau apidhehi' iti śabdādhyāhāraḥ। nanu arthajñānārthatvāt śabdādhyāhārāsambhavāt arthādhyāhāra eva yukta iti cet-na। padaviśeṣajanyapadārthopasthiteḥ śābdajñāne hetutvāt। anyathā aghaṭaḥ karmatvamānayanaṃ kṛtiḥ' ityatrāpi śābdajñānaprasaṅgāt।
nirākariṣyamāṇaḥ svasiddhāntaṃ darśayati - dvāramiti। arthajñānārthatvācchabdasyeti। śabdajñānasya arthajñānaphalakatvādityarthaḥ। etāvatā prathamata evārthānusandhāne lāghavamiti sūcitam। kiṃ ca aarthaṃ arthāndhyāhārasyaivāvaśyakatetyāha-arthamavijñāyeti।
ityāha - padaviśeṣeti। viśeṣapadasyāpi prayojanaṃ darśayituṃ aghaṭaḥ karmatvam' ityādyanudhāvanam। tatra śābdabodhaprasaṅga iti bhāvaḥ। padaviśeṣajanyetyatra vṛttyā padaviśeṣajanyetyapi bodhyam। tena aghaṭamānaya' ityādau
ghaṭādipadādākāśāderupasthitāvapi na śābdabodha iti dik। arthajñānaphalakatvāditi। śābdabodhātmakārthajñānahetutvādityarthaḥ। yathā śabdānusandhānarūpaśabdādhyāhāraṃ pratyapi arthajñānaṃ kāraṇam। tataśca
śābdabodhanirvohe kiṃ śabdādhyāhāreṇeti bhāvaḥ। śābdabodhaṃ prati padārthasmaraṇaṃ kāraṇam। padārthasmaraṇe padajñānajanyatvaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। anyathā yatra padāt na tatrodbodhakādijanyapadārthasmaraṇasya śābdabodhahetutvāpatteḥ। evaṃ
padajñānarūpaśabdādhyāhāra evāvaśyaka iti bhāvaḥ। yathākathañcidityasya padajñānātiriktenodbodhakādirūpopāyenetyarthaḥ। tādṛśopasthitisampattaya iti। padajanyapadārthopasthitiniṣpattaya ityarthaḥ। ghaṭādipadāditi। ghaṭādipadasya
ghaṭādiśabdaḥ ākāśaśceti dvau sambandhinau। tatraikasya ghaṭādipadasya ekasambandhijñānamaparasambandhismārakamiti nyāyāt। tathā ca padajñānajanyapadārthasmaraṇaṃ śābdabodhaheturiti vācyam। vṛttiśca śaktilakṣaṇānyatararūpaḥ sambandhaḥ। ghaṭapadādākāśasmaraṇasya
bhāvaḥ। vṛttyā padajñānajanyatvaṃ ca vṛttijñānasahakṛtapadajñānajanyatvam। yogarūḍhiḥ। samudāyaśaktī rūḍhiḥ। niyatapadmatvādijñānārthaṃ samudāyaśaktiḥ। anyathā kukude api prayogaprasaṅgāt।
ceti। tanmātreṇārthapratipādakamādyam। yathā pācakādipadam। rūḍhiḥ samudāyaśaktiḥ। tanmātreṇārthapratipādakaṃ dvitīyam। yogarūḍhibhyāṃ parasparasahakāreṇārthapratipādakaṃ tṛtīyam। yathā paṅkajādipadam।
caturtham। yathā udbhitpadam yogena tarugulmādeḥ rūḍhyā tu yāgaviśeṣasya ca vācakam। tathāpi yogarūḍhaṃ paṅkajādīti। rūḍhirityarthaḥ। nanu paṅkajādiśabdeṣvapi yoga evāstu tāvataiva
rūḍhirāvaśyikītyāha - niyateti। niyatapadmatvāvacchinnabhānānubhave vipratipannaṃna pratyāha - anyatheti। ityarthaḥ। paṅkajapadaprayogetyarthaḥ। yogo avayavaśaktirityādi। avayavaśaktimātreṇārthabodhakaṃ padaṃ
yaugikam। pācakapade pac aka ityavayadvayamasti। tatra pacdhātoḥ pākor'thaḥ, akapratyayasya kartā arthaḥ। pācakapadena pākakartā budhyate। avayavārthamātrasyaiva bodhāt pācakapadaṃ yaugikam। mātrapadena yogarūḍhapadavyavacchedaḥ। samudāyaśaktimātreṇārthabodhakaṃ rūḍham,
mātrapadenāvayavaśaktivyavacchedadvārā yogarūḍhapadavyāvṛttiḥ। yathā gavādipade samudāyagatā śaktireva vartate। śaktapadaghaṭitatve sati samāsabhinnatve sati śaktinirūpakatvaṃ yaugikatvam। yathā pācakapade pākakartṛtvarūpaikadharmāvacchinnaśaktikatvamastīti samanvayaḥ।
rūḍhe ativyāptivāraṇāya śaktapadaghaṭitatve satīti। amāse ativyāptivāraṇāya samāsabhinnatve satīti। yadyapyevamapi samāse ativyāptivāraṇāyeti। na ca samāse śaktyanaṅgīkārāt śaktinirūpakatvābhāvāt kathamativyāptiprasaktiriti vācyam।
rājaviśiṣṭapuruṣatvarūpaikadharmāvacchinnaśaktikatvamastītyāśayāt। śaktinirūpakatvamityanena vivakṣitam। pākakartṛtvarūpatādṛśadharmāvacchinnaśaktikatvāt pācakapade samanvayaḥ। tatrātivyāptiḥ। rūḍhatvaṃ tu padāghaṭitatve sati śaktinirūpakatvam।
gotvāvacchinnaśaktatvācca śaktinirūpakatvamastīti samanvayaḥ। yaugike ativyāptivāraṇāya satyantam। apabhraṃśe ativyāptivāraṇāya viśeṣyam। śaktapadaghaṭitatve sati avayavārthāghaṭitadharmāvacchinnaśaktikatvra yogarūḍhatvam। paṅkajapade
avayavārthāghaṭitapadmatvāvacchinnaśaktikatvaṃ cāstīti samanvayaḥ। yaugikarūḍhatvam। udbhidādipade ud - bhid - samudāyatvaṃ tadvattvasattvāt samanvayaḥ। yaugike rūḍhinirūpakatācachedakatvaṃ viśeṣaṇam। rūḍhe
gavādipade ativyāptivāraṇāya śaktapadaghaṭitatvaniveśaḥ। yogarūḍhe padaviśeṣaṇamiti nṛsiṃhaśāstripradarśitaḥ panthāḥ। yogarūḍhibhyāṃ parasparasahakāreṇeti। yogaśaktyā paṅkajanikartṛ ucyate, rūḍhyā padmamucyate। tābhyāṃ parasparasahakāreṇa paṅkājjāyamānaṃ
padmamucyate। śaktiḥ' iti prābhākarāḥ। anvayasya vākyārthatayā bhānasambhavāt anvayāṃśe api śaktirna kalpanīyeti gautamīyāḥ। rūḍhinirūpakatāvacchedakaṃ iti samudāyatve anveti।
rūḍhyarthatāvacchedakāsamānādhikaraṇeti dharmaviśeṣaṇam। darśayati - itarānvita iti। anvite śaktiḥ iti tu niṣkarṣaḥ। anvayāṃśe api śaktirapekṣitā। anyathā tādṛśasāmānyakāryakāraṇabhāvabhaṅgaprasaṅgāt। na ca
śaktyanaṅgīkāre api na kṣatiriti vācyam। tathā sati kāryatāvacchedakagauravāpatteḥ। evaṃ ca aanvito ghaṭo ghaṭapadavācyaḥ' ityākārakaśaktijñānameva śābdabodhaprayojakamiti। kecittu-itarānvite śaktirityasya kāryānvite śaktirityarthaṃ āhuḥ।
naiyāyikamataṃ darśayati - anvayasyeti। padārthasaṃsargasya tādṛśasaṃsargāṃśe api śaktirna kalpanīyeti samuditārthaniṣkarṣaḥ। sambhavati, śaktilakṣaṇobhayasādhāraṇasya vṛttitvasya durvacatvāt। api tu tacchaktapadajñānajanyatadupasthititvenaikā kāraṇatā।
svīkartavyā। parasparatattadupasthitijanyaśābdabodhe vyabhicāravāraṇāya niveśanīyam। evaṃ ca vṛttyanupasthitasyāpi padārthadvayasaṃsargasya kimanvayāṃśe śaktikalpanena। aitarānvite śaktiḥ iti prābhākarāḥ' ityayuktam। akāryānvite
iti। akāśyāṃ tribhuvanatikalo bhūpatirāste' pariṣkṛtavanta iti tanmatamanūdyata iti bhāvaḥ। siddhaparavākye api sarvatropapattiriti। itaraḥ svasamabhivyāhṛtapadārthaḥ tadanvite śaktiḥ samabhivyāhṛtapadārthaśca kāryarūpo vā siddharūpo vā। itarāṃśasyāpi
- anvite śaktiriti। nanu anvayāṃśasya iti। kathañcidupasthitānāmiti। padavṛttijñānātiriktakāraṇajanyopasthitiviṣayāṇāmityarthaḥ। padārthānāmanvayaḥ śābdabodhe bhāṣate। anvayāṃśe śaktyasvīkāre
śābdabodhaḥ na syāditi bhāvaḥ। ghaṭamānaya ityatra kāraṇam। anvayaniṣṭhā yā saṃsargatā tacchāliśābdabodhaṃ prati tu śaktijñānajanyā anvayopasthitirnāpekṣitā। anvayaviṣayakaśābdabodhasya bhāvaḥ। kāryatāvacchedakagauravāpatteriti।
saṃsargatābhinnatadviṣayatāśāliśābdabodhatvasya gurutvāditi bhāvaḥ। etanmate śaktigrahasyākāramāha - evañceti। tathā ca ghaṭamānayetyatra śābdabodhe bhāsate। ghaṭaniṣṭhakarmatānirūpakamānayanaṃ kāryamiti śābdabodhāt। tatra ghaṭapadasya ghaṭarūpārthamātre śaktisvīkāre
śābdabodhe bhānaṃ na syāt। ataḥ ghaṭapadasya śaktiḥ। saṃsargaṃviśiṣṭatvaṃ ca ghaṭasya saṃsargapratiyogitvarūpam। tatra ca ghaṭapadasya śaktiḥ। evaṃ ampadasyāpi ghaṭapratiyogikatvopalakṣitānvayaviśiṣṭe karmatve śaktiḥ।
anvayāṃśaḥ padaśaktyaiva bhāsate। evaṃ ampadārthakarmatvadhātvarthānayanayoḥ saṃsargo api padadvayaśaktilabhya iti prābhākarāśayaḥ। naiyāyikāśayamāviṣkaroti - padārthasaṃsargasyetyādinā। vācyam। tathā ca tādṛśakāraṇabalādeva saṃsargāṃśasya śābdabādhe
bhānasambhave saṃsargeṃ śaktikalpanaṃ nocitam। ananyalabhyasyaiva śabdārthatvāditi bhāvaḥ। padasamabhivyāhāreti। padasamabhivyāhāro nāma avyavahitottaratvasambandhena padaviśiṣṭapada - tvam। nanu śābdabodhe kathaṃ bhānam। tathā sati uktakāryakāraṇabhāve
spaṣṭīkaroti - ayamāśaya ityādinā। tathā ca pūrvoktaḥ vṛttitvasya durvacatvāt। tadarthaviṣayakaśābdabodhe kāraṇam। kalpanīyam। evamapi yatra ghaṭaviṣayakaśaktijñānajanyaghaṭopasthityā
vaktavyaḥ। lakṣaṇājñānādhīnaśābdabodhasya tatra śaktijñānajanyopasthityabhāve api na vyatirekavyabhivāraḥ। vyatirekavyabhicāradoṣāt। tathā ca anvayaviṣayakaśābdabodhasya vyatirekavyabhicāraprasaṅgaḥ। ataḥ kāryakāraṇabhāve vyabhicārabhiyā
nānvayāṃśe śakti kalpanīyeti bhāvaḥ। duvacatvāditi। na ca śaktilakṣaṇānyataratvameva vṛttitvaṃ suvacamiti vācyam। tadbhinnabhinnatvaṃ hyanyataratvam। tathā ca bhedadvayāvacchinnabhedavatvaṃ tat। bhedadvayatvaṃ ca
ekabhedaviśiṣṭāparabhedatvam। tathā ca bhedayorviśeṣyaviśeṣaṇabhāve ityāśayāt। tathā ca anvayāṃśaḥ ākāṅkṣālabhya eveti sthitam। AnTs ākāṅkṣā yogyatā saṃnidhiś ca vākyārthajñānahetuḥ । padasya padāntaravyatirekaprayuktānvayānanubhāvakatvam ākāṅkṣā । arthābādho yogyatā । padānāmavilambenoccāraṇaṃ saṃnidhiḥ ।। AnTs ākāṅkṣādirahitaṃ vākyam apramāṇam । yathā gaur aśvaḥ puruṣo hastīti na pramāṇam ākāṅkṣāvirahāt । agninā siñced iti na pramāṇaṃ yogyatāvirahāt । prahare prehare'sahoccāritāni gām ānayetyādipadāni na pramāṇaṃ saṃnidhyabhāvāt ।।
sannidhiśca vākyārthajñānahetuḥ। padasya padāntaravyatirekaprayuktānvayānanubhāvakatvamākāṅkṣā। arthābādho yogyatā। padānāmavilambenocchāraṇaṃ sannidhiḥ। ākāṅkṣādirahitaṃ vākyaṃ na pramāṇam। yathā gauraśvaḥ puruṣo hastī iti vākyaṃ na
pramāṇam। agninā siñcatīti vākyaṃ na pramāṇam। yogyatāvirahāt। prahare prahare asahoccaritāni gāmānaya ityādipadāni na pramāṇaṃ sānnidhyābhāvāt। ākāṅkṣeti।
ākāṅkṣādijñānamityarthaṃḥ। anyathā ākāṅkṣādibhramāt śābdabhramo na syāt। ākāṅkṣāṃ lakṣayati - padasyeti। yogyatālakṣaṇamāha - artheti। sannidhilakṣaṇamāha - padānāmiti। avilambena padārthopasthitiḥ sannidhiḥ। uccāraṇaṃ tu tadupayogitayoktam। gauraśva iti। ghaṭaḥ
karmatvamityapi anākāṅkṣodāharaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam। ākāṅkṣādeḥ śābdabodhahetutvaṃ abhihitaṃ mūlakṛtā। tacca ākāṅkṣādijñānamiti। ādinā yogyatāparigrahaḥ। anyathā śābdabodhahetutve। yatpadasya
ākāṅkṣetyarthaḥ। prayuktatvaṃ ca akāraṇābhāvātkāryābhāvaḥ' iti pratītisākṣikaḥ svarūpasambandhaviśeṣaḥ। ajanakatvāntaṃ paricārakam। saṃśayaniścayasādhāraṇatattajñānatvāvacchinnaṃ śābdadhīhetuḥ। taddheturiti dik।
tacca navīnamate na sambhavatīti। ākāṅkṣā astīti bhramo asti tatra śābdabodha iṣyamāṇo na syāt। tadviṣayakabhramātmakajñānāt śābdabodha upapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। evaṃ yogyatābhramācchābdabodho na syāt। ato yaugayatājñānasya
śābdabodhahetutvu vaktavyamiti bhāvaḥ। yatpadasya ampadasamabhivyāhṛtatvaṃ ākāṅkṣā। kāraṇābhāvāt kāryābhāva iti। ampadarūpakāraṇābhāvāt śābdabodharūpakāryābhāva ityarthaḥ। ajanakatvānta paricāyakamiti। tathā ca
tatpadasamabhivyāhṛtatatpadatvamevākāṅkṣā। bhāvaḥ। paricāyakatvaṃ ca lakṣaṇāghaṭakatve sati lakṣaṇaghaṭakapadārthajñāpakatvam। svaghaṭakaikapadapratipādyarthaviśiṣṭāparapadārthapratipādakatvaṃ yogyatā।
yogyatā। etādṛśayogyatāviṣayakaṃ saṃśayātmakaṃ niścayātmakaṃ vā jñānaṃ śābdabodhahetuḥ। ekapadārthe svarūpataḥ satī hetuḥ na tu tādṛśayogyatājñānaṃ kāraṇamiti bhāvaḥ। vākyārtho apūrvaḥ tatra pūrvaṃ tādṛśayogyatājñānasyāsaṃbhavaḥ।
kāraṇatvakalpanamanāvaśyakam। tadvattabuddhiṃ prati tadabhāvavattāniścayaḥ ityata āha - digiti। tatadvākyaghaṭakatattatpadārthasmaraṇe sati kvacinniścayarūpaṃ kvacitsaṃśayarūpaṃ vā yogyatājñānaṃ sambhavati। tādṛśaprātyakṣikaniścayātmakaṃ yogyatājñānaṃ kāraṇam। yatra tu
saṃśayātmakaṃ yogyatājñānaṃ kāraṇam। ataḥprathamapakṣe na doṣaḥ। sambhavati। ghaṭābhāvavat bhūtalamiti niścayottaramapi vyabhicāraprasaṅgāt। api tu pratibadhyapratibandhakabhāvo vaktavyaḥ। āhāryānumiteranaṅgīkārāt
pratibandhakatā। evameva śābdabodhe api pṛthageva pratibandhakatvaṃ śābdabodhakāraṇatvamavaśyakalpanīyamiti। dvitīyapakṣe api na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। AnTs vākyaṃ dvividham । vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ ca । vaidikam īśvaroktatvāt sarvam eva pramāṇam । laukikaṃ tv āptoktaṃ pramāṇam । anyad apramāṇam ।।
AnTs vākyārthajñānaṃ śabdajñānam ।। vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ ceti। vaidikaṃ īśvaroktatvāt sarvamapi pramāṇam। laukikaṃ tu āptavākyaṃ pramāṇam। anyadapramāṇam। vākyārthajñānaṃ śābdajñānam। evaṃ yathārthānubhavo
nirūpitaḥ। vākyamiti। vaidikasya viśeṣamāha - vaidikamīśvaroktatvātaditi। anāditvāt kathamīśvaroktatvamiti cet - na। avedaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ vākyasamhatvāt bhāratādivat' ityanumānena pauruṣeyatvasiddheḥ।
vede api sakartṛkatvasmaraṇena sādhanavyāpakatvāt। atasmāttepānāttrayo vedā ajāyanta' iti śruteśca। evāyaṃ gakāra iti pratyabhijñābalāt। tathā ca katha vedasya anityatvam iti cet - na। autpanno gakāraḥ, vinaṣṭo gakāraḥ'
pratyabhijñāyāḥ aseyaṃ dīpajvālā' itivat sājātyāvalambanatvāt। varṇānāṃ nityatve apyānupūrvīviśiṣṭavākyasya atityatvācca। tasmāt īśvaroktāḥ vedāḥ। mīmāṃsakaḥ śaṅkate - nanviti। vedasya
īśvaroktatvaṃ anumānena vyavasthāpayati - veda iti। nanu bhāratādau kartā upalabhyate। tathā ca bhevadityāśaṅkate - na ceti। gautamādibhiḥśiṣyaparamparayā vede kartuṃrūpadeśe vivadantaṃ pratyāha - tasmāditi।
sa evāya gakāra iti। atra etatkālikagakāre pūrvakālikagakārābhedo bhāsate। sa ca varṇānāmanityatve na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। tarhi pratyabhijñāvirodha ityata āha - so ayamiti।
tathātvakalpane lāghavamiti hadayam। aagnimīle' ityādau ānupūrvīṃ - ākārottaragakārottaranatvādirūpā। tatrottaratvamavyavahitottarakṣaṇavṛttitvaṃ vācyam। itthaṃ ca varṇanāṃ sidhyatīti varṇānāmanityatvamevocitamityāha-varṇānāmiti।
mīmāṃsaka iti। vedāpauruṣeyatvavādīti śeṣaḥ। sādhayatītyarthaḥ। dīpikāyām pauruṣeyatvasiddheriti। tathā coktānumānena vedānāṃ puruṣanirmitatvasiddhyā anāditvamasiddham। ato anāditvāt
kathamīśvaroktatvamiti śaṅkāyā nāvasara iti bhāvaḥ। upādhitvāditi। yatrayatra pauruṣeyatvaṃ bhāratādau tatra sādhanāvyāpakatvam। ataḥ smaryabhāṇakartṛkatvamupādhiriti uktānumānaṃ sopādhikatvāt duṣṭamiti kathaṃ pauruṣeyatvasādhakamityarthaḥ।
gotamādibhiriti। gotamaḥ svaśiṣyāya vedāḥ sakartṛkā śiṣyaparamparayā gautamīyāḥ vedānāṃ sakartṛkatvaṃ smaranti। tathā ca nopādhitvamiti dīpikoktaṃ na saṅgacchate। gotamādayaḥ tathopadidiśurityatra pramāṇābhāvāt iti śaṅkāyā arthaḥ।
tasmāditīti। tepānāt tapaḥ kurvata īśvarāt trayo vedā ajāyanteti śrutyarthaḥ। tathā ca anayā śrutyaiva nāpekṣeti bhāvaḥ। sambhavatīti। yadi varṇāḥ utpattivināśavantaḥ tarhi
pratyabhijñā na saṅgaccheteti bhāvaḥ। nanu pratyabhijñā nābhedamavagāhate। api tu tajjātīyatvam। pratijñāyā arthaḥ iti dīpikoktaṃ na yujyate। aso ayaṃ gakāra' iti utpattervināśasya ca varṇe āropamātramityapi vaktuṃ śakyatvāt। atha vā
cārtha ityapi vaktuṃ śakyatvāt। tathā ca varṇanityatvaṃ nirbādhamityāśaṅkyāha - utpattivināśapratyayayoriti। utpanno gakāraḥ vinaṣṭo gakāraḥ iti pratītyorityarthaḥ। anyārthakatvakalpaneti। abhivyaktyādyarthakatvakalpanamapekṣyetyarthaḥ।
ācārāṇāṃ ca vedamūlakatayā prāmāṇyam। smṛtimūlavākyānāṃ idānīmanadhyayanāt tanmūlabhūtā kācit śākhā utsanneti kalpyate। na। tathā sati kadāpi varṇānupūrvījñānābhāvena bodhakatvāsambhavāt। tathāpi teṣāmāptatve vipratipannaṃ pratyāha - manvādīti।
ācārāṇāmiti। ācārapratipādakaśiṣṭavākyānāmityarthaḥ। etena pramāṇavibhāgavyāghātaśaṅkā nirastā। vedārthaṃ jñātvaiva manvādibhiḥ tadarthakasmṛtyādīni viracitāni। atasteṣāṃ prāmāṇyamiti mana si kṛtvāha - vedamūlakatayeti। nanu tarhi sa vedaḥ kuto nopalabhyata
ityata āha - smṛtimūleti। tanmūletyādi। ityarthaḥ। vākyotsādanasya - vākyocchedasya। nanu viprakīrṇeti। smṛtyādisamānārthakavākyānāṃ
paṭhyamānavede anupalambhāditi bhāvaḥ। nityo anumeyarūpa ityarthaḥ। varṇānupūrvījñānābhāveneti। tādṛśajñānasyāpiśābdabodhahetutvāt। anyathā nadīdīnādiśabdaiḥ arthaviśeṣabodhānāpattiriti bhāvaḥ।
ācārapratipādaketi। ācārasya anuṣṭhānasya bodhakāni yāni śiṣṭānāṃ vākyāni teṣāmityarthaḥ। ācārapadasyoktavākyaparatayāvyākhyānenetyarthaḥ। vedārthaṃ jñātvaiveti। vedamūlakatvamityuktaṃ bhavati।
śabdasyānumānāntarbhāvaravaṇḍanam। saṃsargajñānasambhavāt śabdo na pramāṇāntaramiti cet - na। ityanuvyavasāyasākṣikasya sarvasaṃmatatvāt। - nanvetānītyādinā। etāni padāni - ghaṭamānaya ityādipadāni।
smāritārthasaṃsargavantīti। smāritārthasaṃsargajñānapūrvakāṇītyarthaḥ। saṃsarge tātparyaviṣayatvaṃ niveśanīyam। tena saṃsargāntaramādāya nārthāntaratā। ākāṅkṣādītyādinā yogyatāsatyoḥ parigrahaḥ। ākāṅkṣādirahite padakadambake vyabhicāravāraṇāya ākāṅkṣādīti।
sarvasaṃmatatvāditi। tathā ca kāryavailakṣaṇyānurodhena śabdaḥ pramāṇāntaraṃ iti bhāvaḥ। smāritārthasaṃsargajñānapūrvakāṇītyartha iti। tadbiṣayakajñānapūrvakāṇītyarthaḥ। tathā ca smāritārthajñānapūrvakatvaṃ
sādhyam। sādhyaghaṭakaṃ yat jñānaṃ tat aarthaṃ buddhvā śabdaracanā' vartate। na caivamapi vākyārthajñānapūrvakatvasya vākyārthajñānasya vā pramāṇatvamiti vācyam। saṃsargaviṣayakatvaviśiṣṭajñānasya sādhyatvena vidheyakoṭipraviṣṭasya saṃsargasyāpi sādhyatvāt।
saṃsargāntaramādāyeti। ghaṭamānayetyādau ghaṭakarmatvayoḥ vāraṇāya saṃsarge tātparyaviṣayatvaṃ viśeṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। padārthe padārthāvagāhitātparyajñānameva kāraṇam। tathā tādṛśajñānapūrvakatvasiddhimādāyārthāntaram। karmantvam
ghaṭatvāvacchinnaghaṭīyatvenādheyatāsaṃsargakajñānasyaivābhimatatvāt। ityarthaḥ। evaṃ cāmpadārthaḥ ādheyatvānavagāhitvānnārthāntaraprasaktiḥ"iti। dinakaryāmapi -"tātparyajñāne itarapadārthasyetarapadārthatvena praveśāt saṅkṣipyoktamatrānusandheyam। ākāṅkṣādirahite padakadambaka
iti। ghaṭaḥ karmatvam ānayanaṃ kṛtirityādau। kāryavailakṣṇyānurodheneti। kāryamatrānuvyavasayaḥ anumitisthale pratyemītyekārakaḥ। atha vā kāryaṃ anumitiḥ śābdabodhaśca tayorviṃlakṣaṇatvānusāreṇetyarthaḥ।
iti cet - na। adevadatto rātrau bhuṅkte divābhuñjānatve sati pīnatvāt' ityanumānenaiva rātribhojanasya siddhatvāt। śatepañcāśaditi sambhavo apyanumānamave। aiha vaṭe yakṣastiṣṭhati' ityaitihyamapi ajñātamūlavaktṛkaśabda eva। ceṣṭāpi śabdānumānadvārā
vyavahāraheturiti na pramāṇāntaram। tasmāt pratyakṣānumānopamānaśabdāḥ catvāryeva pramāṇāni। śaṅkate - nanviti। adivā na bhuṅkte' ityarthe dṛṣṭe - pratyakṣato jñāte, śrute - śabdādavagate। etena dṛṣṭārthāpattiḥ
śrutārthāpattiścetyarthāpattidvaividhyaṃ sūcitam। pīnatvānyathānupapattyeti। pīnatvasyarātribhojanaṃ vinānupapattyetyarthaḥ। atredamavadheyam - yadvinā yadanupapannaṃ upapādakajñānaṃ phalam, upapādyajñānaṃ karaṇam।
phalakaraṇayorarthāpattiśabdo vartate। phale aarthasya āpattiḥ kalpanā' iti vyutpattyā। karaṇe tu aarthasya āpattiḥ kalpanā yasmāt' iti vyutpattyeti। vyatirekyanumānenaiva gatārthatvāt arthāpatteḥ pramāṇāntaratvaṃ anucitamiti samādhattedevadatta iti।
divāmātrabhojini pīṃne vyabhicāravāraṇāya satyantam। ahorātrābhojinyapīṃne vyabhicāravāraṇāya viśeṣyam। tacca yogādyajanyapīnatvaparam। tena bhojanaśūnye yogini pīne na vyabhicāraḥ।
dūṣayati - śate pañcāśadityādinā। anumānameva, na tu pramāṇāntaramityarthaḥ। śatavānityukte pañcāśadvāniti jñānaṃ sambhavati tasyānumānenaiva nirvāhāt। śatasya pañcāśadvyāpyatvāditi bhāvaḥ।
viśiṣyāniścitaprathamavaktṛkaḥ śabdaḥ na tu pramāṇāntaramityarthaḥ। tādṛśaśabdasya yathārthatve śabdapramāṇamadhye antarbhāvaḥ। anyathā tu apramāṇameveti hṛdayam। nanvanayā ceṣṭayā ayamartho boddhavya iti pramāṇāntaratvaṃ iti vadantaṃ nirasyati - ceṣṭāpīti।
śabdānumānadvāreti। śabdadvārā anumānadvārā vā, na tu svātantryeṇetyarthaḥ। ceṣṭayā kalpitasya śabdasya pramāpakatve gauravāt anumānānusaraṇam। pramātmakajñānetyarthaṃḥ। upasaṃharati - tasmāditi।
ityartha iti। divā bhojanābhāvarūper'the ityarthaḥ। pratyakṣato vinānupapattiḥ tasya rātribhojanākhyasyārthasya kalpanaṃ dṛṣṭārthāpattiḥ। rātribhojanasya kalpanaṃ śrutārthāpattiḥ। nanvarthāpattipramiteḥ
arthāpattipramāṇasya ca kiṃ lakṣaṇam। na hi tallakṣaṇamavijñāya atredamavadheyamityādi। yadvinā rātribhojanaṃ vinā yadanupapannaṃ pīnatvamanupapannam। tat rātribhojanaṃ tadupapādakaṃ pīnatvasyopapādakam। upapādyajñānena upapādakajñānamarthāpattirūpā
pramitiḥ। upapādyasya pīnatvasya jñānena upapādakasya rātribhojanasya samanvayaḥ। na ca vācyam। upapādyajñānatvenopapādyajñānajanyatvasya vivakṣitatvāt। upapādyajñānatvena tajjanyatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। tathā
lakṣaṇam ityuktaṃ bhavati। tādṛśajñānakaraṇatvamarthāpattipramāṇasya lakṣaṇam। pramitau pramāṇe cetyarthaḥ। vyatirekyanumānenaiveti।"devadatto rātrau bhuṅkte divā vivakṣitaḥ। kecitu - yo divā abhuñjānatve sati pīnaḥ saḥ rātrau
ityanvayyanumānenāpyarthāpattergantārthatāmāhuḥ। vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya divā abhuñjānatve satīti viśeṣaṇam। divā bhuñjānatvameva yajñadatte astīti na vyabhicāraḥ। divā abhuñjānatvādityeva hetuḥ syāt। tathā sati yastāpasaḥ
tatra vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya pīnatvāditi। tasmiṃstāpase ca pīnatvābhāvāt na vyabhicāraḥ। nanvevamapi yo yogī na bhuṅkte yogajanyamiti yogajanyapīnatvābhāvāt na vyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ। ityādi। śatasaṅkhyākabrāhyaṇādhikaraṇe adhiveśane
nirṇayātmakapramittyutpatyā sambhavo api pramāṇāntaramiti kecit। tanna pramitiḥ, ato na sambhavaḥ pramāṇāntaramiti bhāvaḥ। śatasya pañcāśavdyāpyatvāditi। yatra śatasaṅvyākapadārthāḥ tatra pañcāśatsaṅkhyākapadārthā iti vyāptiḥ।
śabdadvāreti। yathā na pramāṇamiti bhāvaḥ। ceṣṭamānasyābhiprāyaviśeṣānumānadvāretyarthaḥ। ayaṃ vivakṣitaḥ। nanu vyavahāraheturityatra vyavahārapadasya pravṛttiparatve
pramātmakajñānetyartha iti। vyavahriyate aneneti vyutpatyā vyavahārapadaṃ prakṛte pramātmakajñānārthakamityarthaḥ। ।। tatprakārakatvaṃ svatogrāhyaṃ parato veti vicāryate। tatra vipratipattiḥ
iti। atra vidhikoṭiḥ svatastvam niṣeghakoṭiḥ paratastvam। pramātvasya parato grāhyatvaṃ vyavasthāpayiṣyan āha - jñānānāmiti। ṣaṣṭyartha ādheyatvam। tasya cānvayaḥ tadvati tatprakārakatve। tacca tadvadviśeṣyakatvāvacchinnatatprakārakatvam। tacchabdārthoghaṭatvādirūpaḥ।
svatogrāhyamiti। jñānagrāhakasāmagrījanyagrahaviṣaya ityarthaḥ। parata iti। grāhyamityanuṣajyate। anumānādijanyagrahaviṣaya ityarthaḥ। tatra - vicāre। prayojakatvaṃ saptamyarthaḥ vipratipattāvanveti। kathaṃ tasyāḥ vicāraprayojakatvamiti cet - atra vadanti।
viruddhārthapratipādakavākyadvayaṃ hi vipratipattiḥ। tayā janyata ityekatarakoṭiniścayāya nyāyaprayogādirūpo vicāraḥ। vipratipattervicāropayogitvamakṣatamiti। jñānaprāmāṇyamiti pakṣanirdeśaḥ। atra tadvati tatprakārakajñānatvarūpameva prāmāṇyaṃ pakṣaḥ, na
jñānapadam। vastutastu tadvati tatprakārakatvasya taddharmaprakārakajñānagrāhakayāvadgrāhyatvameva sādhanīyam। na tu sāmānyato jñānagrāhakayāvadgrāhyatvamiti tātparyagrāhakaṃ jñānapadam। tadaprāmāṇyetyādi। tadaprāmāṇyāgrāhikā yāvatī jñānagrāhikā sāmagrī
tajjanyagrahaviṣayo na vetyarthaḥ। tādṛśagrahaḥ gurumate vyavasāyaḥ। murārimiśramate anuvyavasāyaḥ। bhāṭṭamate ca jñātatāliṅgakānumitiḥ। atra gurumate sarvasminneva jñāne mitimātṛ-meya-etattrayaṃ bhāsate। tanmate aghaṭatvena ghaṭaṃ ahaṃ
jānāmi' ityākārakasyaiva vyavasāyasya utpatteḥ। evaṃ ca vyavasāyasya prāmāṇyasya svatogrāhyatvam। viśiṣṭabuddhiṃ prati viśeṣaṇajñānasya bhānasambhavāt। miśramate aayaṃ ghaṭaḥ' ityākārakajñānānantaraṃ jñānaviṣayakalaukikamānasamutpadyate, tena prāmāṇyasya grahaṇam।
prāthamikajñānagraharūpatayā tayā prāmāṇyaṃ gṛhyate। anumānaprayogastu - ghaṭatvaprakārakajñātatāvattvāt yannaivaṃ tannaivam iti। jñātatā ca saviṣayako jñānajanyaḥ atirikta padārtha iti matavivekaḥ। catvāri pramāṇāni nirūpitāni। evaṃ ca pramāṇe jñāte adghaṭakasya
pravartayatītyāha pramāṇaprasaṅgāditi। pramāṇanirūpitaprasaṅgasaṅgatyetyarthaḥ। vyavasthāpayiṣyanniti। paramatanirākaraṇapūrvakaṃ sādhayiṣyan ityarthaḥ। ṣaṣṭyartha ādheyatvamityādi। tathā ca ayaṃ ghaṭa ityādijñānaniṣṭhaṃ
svatogrāhyaṃ parato veti vicāryata ityarthaḥ। jñānaniṣṭhamiti pramātve viśeṣaṇamupāttam। taddhaṭakasyeti। pramātvaviśiṣṭapramājanakasya pramāṇaśabdārthatvāditi bhāvaḥ।
jñānānāṃ iti bahuvacanam। jñānaviṣayakajñānajanikā yā sāmagrī tajjanyaṃ yat jñānaṃ tadviṣaya ityarthaḥ। asya samanvayaprakāraḥ paścādbhaviṣyati। anumānādi ityādipadena āptavākyarūpaḥ śabdo gṛhyate। pramātvaṃ svatogrāhyaṃ
ityekaṃ vākyam, pramātvaṃ parato grāhyam ityaparaṃ vākyam। tatra prathamaṃ mīmāṃsakasya, dvatīyaṃ naiyāyikasya। etat paratogrāhyaṃ veti saṃśayo jāyate। tataḥ madhyasthasya prathamaṃ veti saṃśayo jāyate।
vicāraḥ kriyate। tathā ca nyāyaprayogarūpavicāraṃ prati madhyasthasaṃśayaḥ kāraṇam। vicāraprayojakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। atra"vicāro jalpaḥ, viparītodbhāvakaparavijigīṣayā nyāyaprayogarūpaḥ।
jananīrvipratipattīrityartha"iti gadādharagrantho anusandheyaḥ। dīpikākārasyaivetyāhuḥ। saṃśayajanikāyā ityarthaḥ। pakṣanirdeśa ityuktam। tatra prāmāṇyamityeva pakṣanirdeśo astu,
jñānapadaṃ kimarthamityāśaṅkāyāmāha-atra tadvatīti। prāmāṇyaśabdasya pramākaraṇatvamarthaḥ। bhāvārthakalyuḍantāt pramāṇaśabdāt bhāveṣyañā niṣpannasya prāmāṇyaśabdasya pramātvamarthaḥ। iti sūcanāya jñānapadam। na ca pramākaraṇatvameva pakṣo astviti
vācyam। tatra svatogrāhyatvarūpasādhyābhāvena bādhāt। na ca jñānapadopādānena kathaṃ pramākaraṇatvavyāvṛttiḥ। pramākaraṇatvasya vyāptijñānasādṛśyajñānāditānaniṣṭhatvāt iti vācyam। jñānasyaiva jñānamātravṛttiprāmāṇyaṃ pakṣatayābhimatam। pramākaraṇatvarūpaṃ prāmāṇyaṃ
tu na jñānamātravṛtti, tasya anaḥ prabhṛtivṛttitvāt। pramātvarūpaṃ ityāśayāt। kathamiti cet - atrāhuḥ। viśeṣyatāvacchedakāvacchedena jñānamātravṛttitvānvayo vācyaḥ। pramākaraṇatvatvākrānte
pratyakṣapramākaraṇatve jñānamātravṛttitvabādhāt। ataḥ pramātvamevātra prāmāṇyapadārthaḥ। tadvati tatprakārakajñānatvatvarūpapramātvatvāvacchinne tu jñānamātravṛttitvānvayaḥ। sabhbhavatīti tadvalāt atra pramātvarūpaṃ prāmāṇyameva gṛhyata iti।
jñānapadasārthaṅkyam। viśiṣya tadvati tatprakārakajñānatvasya pakṣatve iti। kasyāpi prāmāṇyasyeti । ghaṭatvavati syāt। ato ghaṭatvaghaṭitaṃ pakṣaḥ tadā ghaṭatvaprakārakajñānagrāhakasāmagrīgāhyatvameva sādhyam। na tu
sūcanāya jñānapadamiti bhāvaḥ। na tu sāmānyata iti। sādhyamiti lābhāyetyapi bodhyam। manaḥ prabhṛtīti। manasaḥ mānasapratyakṣarūpapramākaraṇatvāditi bhāvaḥ।
tadaprāmāṇyetyādi। jñāyate। jñānaviṣayakajñāne eva jñānagataṃ pramātvamapi viṣaya ityarthaḥ। tatra prābhākaramate jñānaṃ tripuṭīrūpamaṅgīkriyate। tripuṭītyasya jñātṛ-jñeya-jñānaitattritayaviṣayakamityarthaḥ। tanmate ādau aayaṃ ghaṭa'
ityanuvyavasāyātmakaṃ jñānamiti nāṅgīkriyate। api tu prathamata eva vyavasāyātmakam। tasmin jñāne viṣayaḥ ghaṭaḥ, jñātā ahamarthaḥ, jñādhātvarthajñānaṃ ceti trayaṃ viṣayaḥ। ata eva jñānasya svaviṣayakatvarūpaṃ svayaṃprakāśatvam। tathā ca jñānaviṣayakaṃ svātmakaṃ jñānaṃ
viṣayīkaroti tadvat। jñānatvaviśiṣṭajñānaviṣayakatvavat pramātvaviśiṣṭajñānaviṣayakatvamapi vyavasāyasya svīkriyate। na ca pramātvasya kathaṃ bhānamiti vācyam। tādṛśakāraṇatāyā anaṅgīkārāt। tathā ca
svatastvopapattiḥ। jānāmītyakārakaḥ anuvyavasāyaḥ। tasya ghaṭatvaprakārakaghaṭaviśeṣyakajñānavānityarthaḥ। tathā ca tanmate jñānaviṣayakajñānamanuvyavasāyaḥ। tena jñāne viṣayīkriyamāṇe
pramātvamapi viṣayīkriyate। ataḥ jñānaviṣayakajñānaviṣayatvarūpasvatastvopapattiḥ। prathamataḥ ayaṃ ghaṭa ityeva jñānamudeti। tena jñānena ghaṭe jñātatāravyaḥ kaścit saviṣayako dharmo jāyate। tayā jñātatayā
jñānamanumīyate। tathā ca jñātatāliṅgakānumitireva tanmate jñānaviṣayakajñānam। tayā anumityā jñānagataṃ pramātvamapi viṣayīkriyata iti jñānaviṣayatvarūpasvatastvopapattiḥ। nirvācyam। jñānagrahe prāthamikatvaviśeṣaṇāt
vyavacchidyate। svaprakāśātmakatayeti। svaviṣayakatayetyarthaḥ। grahaṇāditi। viṣayīkaraṇādityarthaḥ। jñānaviṣayakalaukikamānasamiti। mānasapratyakṣamityarthaḥ। idameva mānasam anuvyavasāya ityucyate।
tena prāmāṇyasya grahaṇamiti। tena mānasapratyakṣeṇa pramātvasya viṣayīkaraṇamityarthaḥ। jñānaviṣayakamānasapratyakṣanirūpitā pramātvaniṣṭhaviṣayateti yāvat। tayā pramāṇyaṃ gṛhyate - anumityā prāmāṇyaṃ viṣayīkriyate। ghaṭatvavadviśeṣyaketi। tathā cāsyāmanumitau
ghaṭatvavadviśeṣyakaghaṭatvaprakārakatvarūpapramātvamapi viṣayaḥ। anumānādigrāhyatvena siddhasādhanavāraṇāya yāvaditi। aidaṃ aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketi। aidaṃ jñānaṃ apramā' aprāmāṇyāgrāhakatvābhāvāt svatastvaṃ na syāt ataḥ taditi। tasmin
grāhyaprāmāṇyāśraye aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketyarthaḥ। udāhṛtasthale svatastvasiddhiḥ। darśayati - anumāneti। siddhasādhaneti। prāthamiketi।
prāthamikaṃ yat jñānaviṣayakajñānaṃ tadviṣayatvamityarthaḥ। aidam jñānam pramā' ityāptavākyena ca grāhyatvāditi bhāvaḥ। naiyāyikamate api niṣedhe sādhye bādhavāraṇāyetyapi bodhyam। yāvaditīti। nanu sāmagryāṃ yāvattvaviśeṣaṇamayuktam,
yāvatsāmagrījanyagrahāprasiddheḥ। na hi sarvābhiḥ jñānasāmagrībhiḥ ekaṃ jñānaṃ janyate। na ca yāvatīḥ sāmagīḥ viśiṣyopādāya tattajjanyagrahaviṣayatvaṃ sādhyata iti vācyam। matatrayasādhāraṇyānirvāhāditi cet - na। yato yāvaditi phalato
grahaviśeṣaṇm। tathā ca jñānagrāhakasāmagrījanyayāvadgrahaviṣayatvamiti phalitam। niṣkarṣa iti saṅkṣepaḥ। vyavasāyaniṣṭhetyādiḥ। prāmāṇyāviṣayīkaraṇādityarthaḥ। aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketīti। tathā ca
prāmāṇyasyāgrahaṇe api na bādha iti bhāvaḥ। anuvyavasāyaniṣṭhetyādi। tadgrāhakasyetyarthaḥ। asāmānye napuṃsakam' iti napuṃsakanirdeśaḥ। svatastvaṃ na syāditi। yadā niruktaprāmāṇyasya sidhyedityarthaḥ। saptamītatpuruṣamabhipretyāha - tasminniti। etasyaiva
vivaraṇaṃ grāhyaprāmāṇyāśraya iti। yādṛśaprāmāṇyaṃ agrāhakāntārthaḥ। idaṃ jñānaṃ apramā - udāhṛtasthala iti। idaṃ jñānaṃ aprametyatretyarthaḥ। adhikaṃ asmadīyamaṇidīdhitivyākhyāyāmanusandheyam।
iti dīpikāyāmuktam। tasmin aprāmāṇyāgrāhikā yāvatī jñānagrāhikā sāmagrī tajjanyagrahaviṣayatvamiti tadarthaḥ। aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketyasya aprāmāṇyaprakārakajñānājanaketyarthaḥ। tadekadeśajñāne tasminniti saptamyantārthasya tadviśeṣyakatvasyānvayaḥ।
anumityā grāhyaṃ tādṛśaprāmāṇyāśraya ucyate। tathā ca svatastvamiti paryavasannam। ayaṃ ghaṭaḥ ityākārakajñāne idaṃ jñānaṃ ghaṭajñānaviśeṣyakāpramātvajñānaṃ jāyata iti। tādṛśasāmagrījanyaṃ pramātve astīti samanvayaḥ। atra dalaprayojanakathanāvasare prathamaṃ
prayojanamuktaṃ dīpikāyām। tatra prathamopasthitasya agrāhakāntasya prayojanakathanaṃ nyāyyam। tatparityajya kimarthaṃ viparyayeṇa prayojanamuktamityāśaṅkāyāmāha - yāvatvaviśeṣaṇe satyeveti। spaṣṭīkartuṃ śakyat iti ādau tayoḥ prayojanaṃ pratipādyate।
yāvajjñānagrāhakasāmagrīgrāhyatvaṃ svatastvamiti bhavet। tathā ca aidaṃ tadgrāhyatvabhapramātva evāsti, na tu pramātva iti bādhaḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya sāmāgryāṃ aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketi viśeṣaṇamupāttam। idaṃ tādṛśagrahajanakasāmagryāḥ aprāmāṇyagrāhakatvāvaśyambhāvāt। tathā ca
tajjanyānuvyavasāyādirūpajñānagrahaviṣayatvaṃ pramātve astīti na bādhaḥ। tadvāraṇāya yāvatpadam। tathā sati vyavasāyānuvyavasāyādīnāmapi siddhasādhanamiti dvayoḥ dalayoḥ prayojanasthitiḥ। tatra yāvattvadale satyeva aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketi sārthakam। anyathā
grahaṇena tadviṣayatvasya pramātve sambhavāt। tathā ca bādhāprasaktyā tadvāraṇaphalakamagrāhakāntaṃ vyarthaṃ syāt। yāvatpade sati tu aidaṃ agrāhakāntaṃ sārthakamityuktaṃ pramāśikayāmiti। bādhavāraṇāyeti।
sādhyaḥ। yāvatpadamiti bhāvaḥ। abhāvasādhyakasthalepakṣe pratiyogimattvameva bādha ityāśayenedam। yāvatpadasya tajjanyagrahaviṣayatvaṃ sādhyamiti phalati। tathā sati yāvatsāmagrījanyaḥ
ekaḥ jñānagrahaḥ aprasiddha iti sādhyāprasiddhiḥ prasajyate। yataḥ jñānagraho na bhavatīti। sāmagrīṇāṃ yāvatvena na niveśaḥ, api tu viśiṣyaiva। tathā ca śaṅkāgranthārthaḥ।
yāvaditi। nanu jñānagrāhakasāmagrījanya yāvadgrahaviṣayatvasya phalitārthamāha - tattaddharmeti। yaddharmaghaṭitaprāmāṇyaṃ pakṣaḥ taddharmaprakāretyarthaḥ। tathā ca pratijñāvākyam। ghaṭatvaprakārakajñānam ayaṃ ghaṭa ityākārakajñānaṃ
tādṛśaviṣayitānirūpakatvaṃ ca pramātve astīti samanvayaḥ। anuvyavasāyādisāmagrījanyagrahatvavyāpakatvāt siddhasādhanam। prāmāṇyaviṣayitāyāḥ vyāpakatvaṃ tu na vivakṣituṃ śakyam। naiyāyikamate sādhyāprasiddheḥ। aghaṭatvena imaṃ jānāmi'
saṅkṣepa iti। pratijñā na vivakṣitā, yenoktadoṣaḥ syāt। apitu iti pratijñā vivakṣitā। ato na sādhyāprasiddhyādikamiti bhāvaḥ। adhikaṃ prāmāṇyavādagādādharyāṃ draṣṭavyam।
jñānamaprameti jñāneneti। tathā ca aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketi jñānagrāhakasāmagrījanayayāvadgrahaviṣayatvaṃ svatastvamiti syāt। tathā evāsti na tu pramātvarūpapakṣa iti bādhaḥ syāt। tadvāraṇāya aprāmāṇyāgrāhaketiviśeṣaṇam। apramātvagrāhājanaketi tadarthaḥ।
bhāvaḥ। vyavasāyaniṣṭhetyādiriti। idaṃ rajatam ityākārakavyasāyaniṣṭhaṃ tadaviṣayakatvādityarthaṃḥ। tathā ca pramātve yāvadantargatatādṛśajñānāviṣayatvāt bādha iti bhāvaḥ।
tādṛśajñānasāmagryā iti। idaṃ jñānaṃ apramā ityākārakajñānajanakasāmagryā ityarthaḥ। sādhyakoṭyapraviṣṭatvāditi। apramātvagrāhakatvena aprāmāṇyāgrāhakatvarūpaviśeṣaṇānākrāntatvāditi bhāvaḥ।
syāditi tadvāraṇāya tadaprāmāṇyāgrāhaketi tatpadam। aprāmāṇyagrāhaketi tadarthaḥ। yādṛśapramātve svatastvamiṣyate tadaprāmāṇyāgrāhaketyasyārthaḥ। idaṃ jñānaṃ apramā noktadoṣa iti। idaṃ jñānaṃ aprametyanuvyavasāyaniṣṭheti।
jñānaviṣayakatvādasya jñānasyānuvyavasāyaśabdena vyapadeśaḥ। ataḥ nāśaṅkanīyam। sāmānye naṃpusakamiti। sāmānyadharmāśrayavivakṣayā napuṃsakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। niruktaprāmāṇyasyeti।
aprāmāṇyavadviśeṣyakatvaviśiṣṭāprāmāṇyaprakārakatvarūpaprāmāṇyasyetyarthaḥ। tasyeti। niruktaprāmāṇyasyetyarthaḥ। na sidhyediti। tathā ca bādha iti bhāvaḥ। svatogrāhyatvasiddhiriti। tādṛśaprāmāṇyāśrayabhūtaḥ yaḥ idaṃ satvāt na bādha iti bhāvaḥ।।
vyavasāyarūpapratyāsattestulyatvāt। purovartini prakārasambandhasyaiva vipratipattimupanyasya mīmāṃsakamatamupanyasyati - nanviti। svata evetyādi। ghaṭatvādighaṭitaprāmāṇyaṃ niruktasāmagrīta eva gṛhyata ityarthaḥ। apyarthakenaivakāreṇa anumānādiparigrahaḥ।
anuvyavasāyeneti। idaṃ ca miśramatābhiprāyeṇa। matatrayasādhāraṇyena tu prāthamikajñānagraheṇeti dhyeyam। tatsambandhasyāpīti। ghaṭaghaṭatvayoḥ yaḥ sambandhaḥ tasyāpītyarthaḥ। nanu anuvyavasāye kathaṃ vyavasāyarūpapratyāsatteraviśeṣādityāha - vyavasāyeti। tāvatā kathaṃ
prāmāṇyasya bhānamata āha - purovartini prakārasambandhasyaiveti। purovartini yaḥ prakārasambandhaḥ tadghaṭitasyaivetyarthaḥ। tairaṅgīkārāt। parantu purovartini ghaṭādau ghaṭatvādirūpaprakārasambandhabhānaṃnāṅgīkurvanti। atastatra
sarvasaṃmatatvāditi। ghaṭatvādighaṭitaprāmāṇyamiti। tadāśrayajñānagrāhakasāmagryaiva gṛhyata ityarthaḥ। ayaṃ ghaṭa manassaṃyuktasamavāyena ca bhāsete iti tadaṃśe laukikatvam।
ghaṭaghaṭatvayostu jñānalakṣaṇayā pratyāsattyā bhānam। sattvāt vyavasāyasya ghaṭaghaṭatvobhayaviṣayakatvāt। tathā ca yaḥ sambandhaḥ samavāyarūpaḥ tasyāpi bhānamāvaśyakam। vyavasāye tasyāpi bhānena vyavasāyātmakasannikarṣāt tatsambandhabhānasyāvaśyambhāvāt। na
jñānaviṣayakagrahaviṣayatvāravyaṃ svatastvaṃ kathaṃ sidhyediti vācyam। sambandhabhānasyaiva pramātvabhānarūpatvāt। etadeva kathamiti cet - tatparyavasyati। viṣayo yādṛśadharmavattayā vyavasāye bhāsate mīmāṃsakāśayaḥ। sa eva dīpikāyāṃ prakāśikāyāṃ cānūdita
iti। yadyapi svīkriyate। tatra viṃśeṣyatāprakāratayoranupasthitayo api bhānam। rajatatvavatvaṃ na bhāsate ityaṅgīkriyate। mīmāṃsakāstu viśeṣaḥ। purovartinaṃ ghaṭatvena jānāmītyākārakasyeti।
purovartiniṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpakaghaṭatvaniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpakajñānavānahamityarthaḥ। ajalajñānaṃ pramā na vā' ityanabhyāsadaśāyāṃ pramātvasaṃśayo na syāt। anuvyavasāyena prāmāṇyasya niścitatvāt। tasmāt svatogrāhyatvābhāvāt parato grāhyatvameva। tathāhi - prathamaṃ
vyatirekiṇā pramātvaṃ niścīyate। dvitīyādijñāneṣu gṛhyate।। jalajñānamityādi। jalajñānaṃ pramā na vā ityākārakaḥ। anabhyāsadaśāyām -
prāthamikajalajñānagrahottaradaśāyām। anubhavasiddhaḥ pramātvasaṃśayo na syādityarthaḥ। tadvattāniścayasya tadabhāvavattājñānaṃ prati pratibandhakatvāditi bhāvaḥ। atra ajñāto ghaṭa' iti pratīteḥ bodhyaḥ।
anabhyāsadaśāyāṃ saṃśayānubhavādityarthaḥ। etasya svatogrāhyatvābhāve anvayaḥ। paratīgrāhyatvamiti। prāmāṇyasyānumānāditi eva grāhyatvamityarthaḥ। pravṛttau satyāmiti। vyabhicāro darśitaḥ। na ca niṣkampapravṛttāveva prāmaṇyaniścasya
vyabhicārasya durvāratvāt। na caivaṃ jalādijñāne aprāmāṇyaniścakāle pravṛttiḥsyāditi śaṅkanīyam। agṛhītāprāmāṇyakajalādijñānatvena, taddhetutāsvīkāreṇa adoṣāditi saṅkṣepaḥ। nirākṛtā। idānīṃ pakṣasyāsattvādāha - pūrvotpannamiti। samartheti।
tadvadviśeṣyakatatprakāraketyarthaḥ। anvayyudāharaṇāsambhavāt vyatirekyudāharaṇaṃ sadṛṣṭāntamāha - yannaivaṃ tannaivamiti। yadapramā tatsamarthapravṛtyajanakamityarthaḥ। vyatirekiṇā - vyatirekavyāptimatā। niścīyate - anumīyate। dvitīyādijñāneṣu - dvitīyādijalajñāneṣu।
tatsajātīyatvaliṅgena - pūrvajñānasajātīyatvarūpaliṅgena। samarthapravṛttijanakatveneti yāvat। prāmāṇyamanumīyata ityarthaḥ। prāthamikajalajñānagrahottaradaśāyāmiti। prāthamikaṃ yat
taduttarakāle ityarthaḥ। tathā ca prāthamikajalajñānagrahe yadi jalajñānadharmikapramātvaniścayātmakapratibanadhakasatvāditi bhāvaḥ। jātu abhyāsadaśāpannamityucyate। tasya prāthamikajalajñānagrahottaramityuktam। tadabhāvavattājñānaṃ।
pramātvaniścayasya pratibandhakatvādityarthaḥ। tannirasanaprakāra iti। jñātatānirāsaprakāra ityarthaḥ। eteneti। prāthamikajalajñānānantarameva pravṛttiriti kathanenetyarthaḥ।
mīmāṃsakairabhyupagatāyāmiti। kasmiṃścit viṣaye jñāte sati jāte vadanti। jalajñānānantaraṃ idaṃ jñānaṃ pramā vyatirekavyabhicārāditi। na ca niṣkampeti। pravṛttirdvividhā - niṣkampā sakampā ceti। utkaṭā pravṛttiḥ niṣkampā, anutkaṭā pravṛttiḥ
sakampā। utkaṭatvānutkaṭatve pravṛttigatau viṣayitāviśeṣau। tatra kāraṇam, tadviṣayakānutkaṭapravṛttiṃ prati tu prāmāṇyasaṃśayaḥ kāraṇam। prāmāṇyasaṃśayasya sakampapravṛttitvaṃ kāryatāvacchedakam। yatra pravṛttiḥ sakampetyaṅgīkriyate। tasyāṃ ca
prāmāṇyaniścayasya pravṛttihetutvaṃ nirbādhamiti śaṅkiturāśayaḥ। tathāpīti। yatra prāmāṇyasya aprāmāṇyasya vā saṃśayo vā niścayo vā prāmāṇyasaṃśayasya pravṛttihetutā na bhavatīti samādhāturāśayaḥ। na caivamiti। prāmāṇyaniścayasya vā prāmāṇyasaṃśayasya vā pravṛttiṃ prati
hetutvānaṅgīkāre yatra jalajñāne aprāmāṇyaniścayaḥ tatkāle।pi pravṛttiḥ syāt, pravṛttihetoḥ jalajñānasya satvādityarthaḥ। agṛhīteti। aprāmāṇyajñānābhāvaviśiṣṭajalādijñānameva pravṛttihetorabhāvāditi bhāvaḥ।
prāmāṇyagrahaviśiṣṭārthaniścayasyaiva pravṛttihetutvam। yuktaṃ iti। prāmāṇyagrahasya kathañcit pravṛttyupayogitve api parataḥ nābhiniveṣṭavyamiti bhāvaḥ। etāvateti। jalalābhe
satīti kathanenetyarthaḥ। vakṣyamāṇasya prāmāṇyavyavasthāpakahetoriti। samarthapravṛttijanakatvarūpahetorityarthaḥ। svarūpāsiddhiśaṅkā - pakṣāvṛttitvaśaṅkā। pravṛtteḥ sāmarthyaṃ hi jalalābhenaiva। tathā ca sūcitamiti bhāvaḥ। prāmāṇyānumitisamaya ityarthaḥ।
pūrvajñānasajātīyatveti। gṛhītaprāmāṇyakapūrvajñānasajātīyatvaliṅgenetyarthaḥ। saphalapravṛttijanakatvarūpeṇa। tathā ca saphalapravṛttijanakatvameva hetuḥ, pūrvajñānamanvayadṛṣṭānta iti sūcanāya pūrvajñānasajātīyetyuktam।
prāthamikajalajñānamiti। ityanavyavasāyo bhavati, na tu ghaṭaṃ ghaṭatvena jānāmīti। pramātvaṃ pramābhramobhayaniṣṭhatvāt। kiṃ tu ghaṭatvavadviśeṣyakatvaviśiṣṭaghaṭatvaprakārakatvam। idaṃ ca
nānuvyavasāye bhāsate। tatra ghaṭatvaviśiṣṭaniṣṭhatayā viśeṣyatāyā agrahaṇāt। vyavasāye idantvenaiva ghaṭasya viśeṣyatvāt grahaṇāsaṃbhavāt। ataḥ prāmāṇyaṃ na svatogrāhyamiti naiyāyikānāmāśayaḥ iti kecit।"tathāpyanuvyavasāyānantaraṃ vyavasāyasya
tadbiṣayaḥ"iti maṇigranthaḥ teṣaramanukūlaḥ। tatprakārakatvasya grāhakatve anuvyavasāyasyāsāmatharyaṃ kalpyate। tena rajatatvaprakārakamiti na grahaḥ"iti prāhuḥ। arthatadvattvāviṣayakatve nirbharo nocita"ityāhuḥ।
guṇajanyatvamutpatau paratastvam। pramāsādhāraṇakāraṇa guṇaḥ, apramāsādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ doṣaḥ। tatra pratyakṣe viśeṣaṇavadviśeṣyasannikarṣo guṇaḥ। anumitau vyāpakavati vyāpyajñānam। upamitau yathārthasādṛśyajñānam। śābdajñāne yathārthayogyatājñānam
ityādyūhanīyam। ityāhuriti। prāmāṇyaghaṭakaḥ kaścidaṃśaḥ jñānajñāne na bhāsata iti vaktavyam। sa cāṃśaḥ purovartini ghaṭatvavattvarūpa iti dīdhitikārādayaḥ।
iti gadādharabhaṭṭācārtha iti vivekaḥ। paratastvaṃ vyavasthāpya utpattau paratastvaṃ nirūpayati pramāyā iti। pramāsādhāraṇakāraṇamiti। pramātvādhikadeśavṛttidharmānavacchinnapramāniṣṭhakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatāśālītyarthaḥ।
bhramajanakapittādidoṣāṇāṃ ca vyudāsaḥ। apramāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvamapyevaṃ pariṣkartavyam। caturvidhapramāyāṃ hetubhūtaṃ guṇaṃ krameṇopapādayati tatreti। caturvidhapramāmadhya ityarthaḥ। apītaḥ śaṅkhaḥ' ityādibhrame
ūhanīyamityarthaḥ। pramātvādhikadeśavṛttīti। pramātvavyāpakadharmānavacchinnā yā lakṣaṇamityarthaḥ। pramāniṣṭhakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatvamātroktau jñānasāmānyaṃ prati hetubhūte ātmamanassaṃyogādāvativyāptiḥ।
pramātvādhikadeśavṛttidharmānavacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। ātmamanassaṃyogādau tadanavacchinnakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatvamiti nātivyāptiḥ। tatrānivyāptivāraṇāya kāryatāyāṃ pramāniṣṭhatvaniveśaḥ। pittādeḥ pramāniṣṭhakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatāśālitvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ।
tadāha - teneti। evaṃ pariṣkartavyamiti। apramātvādhikadeśavṛttidharmānavacchinnāpramāniṣṭhakāryapariṣkartavyami ti। doṣasya lakṣaṇamityarthaḥ। gṛhyate।
pittādidoṣajanyatvamutpattau paratastvam। paratastvaṃ sayuktikaṃ darśayati - purovartinīti। aviṣayīkaraṇādityarthaḥ। tathā ca pratyāsatterabhāvāt apramātvasyānuvyavasāyena grahaṇaṃ na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। apramātvam -
tadabhāvavadviśeṣyakatvaviśiṣṭatatprakārakatvam। parata eva gṛhyata iti। anumānādita eva gṛhyata ityarthaḥ। anumānaprayogastu - idaṃ jñānaṃ apramā visaṃvādipravṛttijanakatvāt yannaivaṃ tannaivaṃ yathā pramā iti। pratyāsatterabhāvāditi। saṃnikarṣābhāvādityarthaḥ। viśeṣye
prakārasaṃbandhaghaṭitapramātvagrahaṇaṃ kathañcit prasaktaṃ pūrvaṃ nirākṛtam। sambhavatīti apramātvaṃ na prāthamikajñānagrahaviṣayatvarūpasvatastvavat। api tu anumānavedyatvākhyaparatastvavaditi bhāvaḥ। visaṃvādipravṛttīti।
viphalapravṛttītyarthaḥ। anyathākhyātisamarthanam। jñānānāṃ yathārthatvāt ayathārthajñānameva nāstīti। na ca aśuktau anyathākhyātisiddhiriti vācyam। rajatasmṛtipurovartijñānābhyāmeva
pravṛttisambhavāt। svatantropasthiteṣṭabhedāgrahasyaiva sarvatra cet - na। satyarajatasthale purovartiviśeṣyakarajatatvaprakārakajñānasya viśiṣṭajñānasyaiva kalpanāt। anyathākhyātiṃ vyavasthāpayati - nanvityādinā। yathārthatvāt -
pramātvāt। ayathārthajñānameva nāstīti। tadabhāvavadviśeṣyakatatprakārakatvarūpāyathārthatvaṃ jñānavṛtti netyarthaḥ। tena na siddhyasiddhibhyāṃ vyāghātaḥ। ayathārthatvasya tu prasiddhiricchādau bodhyā। tadanaṅgīkāre
syāditi bhāvaḥ। klptaniyatapūrvavartibhyāmityādiḥ। sambhavāditi। tathā ca pravṛttiṃ prati viśiṣṭajñānatvena kāraṇataiva nāstīti tadanurodhena anyathākhyātikalpanaṃ na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। syādityata āha - upasthiteti। etāvatā smṛtirūpakāraṇāpekṣā
sphuṭīkṛtā। iṣṭabhedāgrahasyaiva - rajatādirūpeṣṭabhedagrahābhāvasyaiva। evakāreṇa viśiṣṭajñānasya pravartakatvavyavacchedaḥ। rajate śuktau cetyarthaḥ। satyarajatasthale viśiṣṭajñānatvenaiva pravṛttiṃ prati kāraṇatvameṣṭavyam।
kāraṇatāpatteḥ। evaṃ ca tatra pravṛttiṃ pratyanvayavyatirekābhyāṃ - satyarajateti। rajatatvaprakārakajñānasyeti। tādṛśajñānatvāvacchinnasyetyarthaḥ। pravṛttijanakatayā - pravṛttitvāvacchinnajanakatayā। viśiṣṭajñānasyaiva -
purovartiviśeṣyakeṣṭatāvacchedakaprakārakajñānasyaiva। etena iṣṭabhedāgrahasya vyavacchedaḥ। kalpanāt - anumānāt। tatprayogastu pravṛttitvāt, rajatasthalīyapravṛttivat' iti। syādetat - pratyakṣe maivam।
jñānalakṣaṇapratyāsattereva prakṛte sambhavāt। gurumatamiti। sarvāṇi jñānāni tadvati tatprakārakatvarūpapramātvavanti। tadabhāvavati prābhākaramatamityarthaḥ। nanu dīpikāyām ayathārthajñānameva nāstīti
gurumatānuvādo na yuktaḥ। ayathārthajñānasya prasaddhitve taninaṣedho na yuktaḥ। ayathārthajñānasyāprasiddhatve ca pratiyogyaprasiddhyā tanniṣedho tadabhāvavaditi। ayathārthatvaṃ pakṣaḥ, jñānavṛttitvābhāvaḥ sādhyaḥ, jñānatvavyāpakapramātvaviruddhatvāt iti hetuḥ। tadanaṅgīkāra
iti। tadabhāvavadviśeṣyakatatprakārakajñānarūpānyathākhyātyanaṅgīkāra ityarthaḥ। purovartiviśeṣyaketi। purovartiviśeṣyakapravṛttiṃ prati purovartiviśeṣyakeṣṭatāvacchedakaprakārakajñānaṃ hetuḥ। rajatārthinaḥ iṣṭatāvacchedakarajatatvajñāne vinā pravṛtteranudayāt। tathā ca
pravṛttirna ghaṭate। ataḥ pravṛttyanusāreṇa taddhetubhūtā anyathākhyātiraṅgīkāryeti śaṅkiturāśayaḥ। saṃvādipravṛttiḥ saphalapravṛttiḥ। viphalapravṛttiḥ। ityuktamityatrāha - kḷptaniyatapūrvavartibhyāmityādiriti।
