rajatasmaraṇaṃ ceti jñānadvayaṃ bhavatītyaṅgīkriyate। viśiṣṭajñānamanāvaśyakamiti bhāvaḥ। viśiṣṭajñānatveneti। purovartiviśeṣyakarajatatvādiprakārakajñānatvenetyarthaḥ। nanvevamiti। rajatasmṛtipurovartijñāne eva pravṛttikāraṇe;
viśiṣṭajñānaṃ tu na pravṛttikāraṇamityaṅgīkāra ityarthaḥ। pravṛttiḥ syāditi। rajatasmṛtipurovartijñānayoḥ sattvāditi bhāvaḥ। rajatādirūpeti। rajatādirūpaṃ yat iṣṭaṃ tatpratiyogikabhedajñānābhāvasyetyarthaḥ। tathā ca
pravṛttyāpattiriti bhāvaḥ। idamiti viśiṣṭajñānasyaikasya kāraṇatve lāghavamiti mūle abhipretam। tadāha - satyarajatasthala ityādinā। yadyapi dharmadharmijñānayoḥ kāraṇatvaṃ naiyāyikena viśiṣṭajñānatvāvacchinnasya kāraṇatvamucyate। tatra
kāraṇatāvacchedakalāghavaṃ naiyāyikasyaiveti bhāvaḥ। sāmānyataḥ pravṛttitvāvacchinnaṃ pratīti। saṃvādivisaṃvādipravṛttisādhāraṇapravṛttitvāvacchinnaṃ pratītyarthaḥ। tatkāryatāvacchedakāvalīḍhatayeti। tasya viśiṣṭajñānasya yat
kāryatāvacchedakaṃ pravṛttitvaṃ tadāśrayatayetyarthaḥ। visaṃvādipravṛtteḥpūrvamityarthaḥ। rajatatvāṃśe tadabhāveneti। sannikarṣābhāvena cakṣussaṃyuktaśaktisamavāyābhāvenetyarthaḥ। jñānalakṣaṇeti। rajatasmaraṇātmakaṃ yat rajatatvaprakārakajñānaṃ sa eva
rajatatvabhānaprayojakaḥ saṃnikarṣa iti bhāvaḥ। AnTs ayathārthānubhavas trividhaḥ saṃśayaviparyayatarkabhedāt । ekasmin dharmini viruddhanānādharmavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhi jñānaṃ saṃśayaḥ । yathā sthāṇur vā purṣo veti । mithyājñānaṃ viparyayaḥ । yathā śuktāv idaṃ rajatam iti । vyāpyāropeṇa vyāpakāropas tarkaḥ yathā yadi vahnir na syāt tarhi dhūmo'pi na syād iti ।। ayathārthānubhavastrividhaḥ - saṃśaya-viparyaya-tarkaṃbhedāt। ekasmin dharmiṇi viruddhanānādharmavaiśiṣṭyajñānaṃ saṃśayaḥ। yathā
sthāṇurvā puruṣo veti। mithyājñānaṃ viparyayaḥ। yathā śuktau idaṃ rajatam iti। vyāpyāropeṇa vyāpakāropastarkaḥ। yathā yadi vahnirnasyāt tarhi dhūmo api na syāt iti। iti। svapnasya mānasaviparyayarūpatvāt na traividhyavirodhaḥ।
saṃśayalakṣaṇamāha - eketi। ghaṭapaṭāviti samūhālambane ativyāptivāraṇāya eketi। aghaṭaḥ dravyam' ityādāvativyāptivāraṇāya viruddheti। aghaṭatvaviruddhapaṭatvavān' ityatra ativyāpitavāraṇāya nāneti। viparyayalakṣaṇamāha - mithyeti।
tadabhāvavati tatprakārakanirṇaya ityarthaḥ। tarkaṃ lakṣayati - vyāpyeti। bhedena saṅkīrtanam। bādhitārthaviṣayakasya anubhavasiddhatvādata āha - svapnasyeti। yadyapi pradeśaviśeṣāvasthitamanassaṃyogaḥ svapnaḥ। tathāpi
tadasamavāyikāraṇakajñāne svapnaśabdo bhākta ityavadheyam। cākṣuṣādirūpatvāsambhavādāha - mānaseti। yattu smṛmirūpaṃ svapnajñānamiti tat bhāṣyādiviruddhamityupekṣitam। darśayitumāha - ghṭatvaviruddheti।
nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। na ca śaṅkyam। ekadharmāvacchinnaviśeṣyatāghaṭitapariṣkārakāraṇena adoṣāditi dik। tantrāntare brahmabhinne sarvasminnevamithyāśabdasya tadabhāvavatīti।
samūhālambane atiprasaṅgaḥ। saṃśayasya icchāyāśca vāraṇāya saṃśayānyajñānārthakaṃ niścayayadamiti saṅkṣepaḥ। vyāpyāropeṇeti। āhāryavyāpyavattābhramajanya - āhāryavyāpakavattābhramastarka ityarthaḥ।
āhāryajñānamātre atiprasaṅgavāraṇāya janyāntam। yatra nāyam puruṣa ityādyāhāryāropaḥ tatrātivyāptivāraṇāya prathamamāhāryapadam। ityanāhāryajñāne ativyāptivāraṇāya dvitīyamāharyapadam। tarke dhyeyam। tarkastu mānasaviparyayarūpa eveti kathamayathārthasya
traividhyakathanamityāha - yadyapīti। pramāṇānugrāhakatvam - pramāṇena pramāyāṃ jananīyāyāṃ pratibanadhakavighaṭanadvāropayogitvam। bhedeneti। tarkatvarūpavailakṣaṇyenetyarthaḥ। tarkasya prāmāṇānugrāhakatvajñāpanāya tathā kathanamiti bhāvaḥ।
bhākta iti। lākṣaṇikaḥ kārye kāraṇopacāra ityarthaḥ। tathā ca svāpnaṃ vijñānaṃ viparyaye antarbhūtamiti bhāvaḥ। bhāṣyādiviruddhamiti।"uparatendriyagrāmasya pralīnamanaskasya indriyadvāreṇaiva bhāvaḥ। ekadharmiviśeṣyakaviruddhanānādharmaprakārakajñānaṃ saṃśayaḥ।
tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya ekadharmiviśeṣyaketyuktam। nātivyāptiḥ। ghaṭo dravyamiti jñānasya ghaṭarūpaikadharmiviśeṣyakatvāt ghaṭatva-dravyatvarūpānekadharmaprakārakatvācca tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya viruddheti dharmaviśeṣaṇam। ghaṭatvadravyatvayoparekatra ghaṭe
vartamānayorekatrāvartamānatvarūpaviruddhatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya nānādharmaprakāraketyuktam। yadyapi ekasmin dharmiṇi tayoḥ prakārakatvaṃ nāstīti nātivyāptiḥ। jñānaparyantānudhāvanaṃ dīpikāyāmayuktamityatrāha - koṭyoriti।
niveśanīyam। koṭyoravyāpyavṛttitvajñānaśūnyakālīne samuccaye eva koṭyorviṃrodho viṣayaḥ। tayoravyāpyavṛttitvajñānakālīne samuccaye tu koṭyorvirodho na bhāsate। tathā coktasamuccayasya virodhaviṣayakatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। tathā cāyaṃ
jñānaparyantānudhāvanam। tasya jñānasya virodhaviṣayakatvāt prasaktāyā ativyāptervāraṇāya nāneti viśeṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ। ekadharminiṣṭhaviśeṣyatetyādi। ayaṃ ghaṭatvaviruddhapaṭatvavān iti jñāne ghaṭatvamapi prakāraḥ paṭatvamapi prakāraḥ।
paṭatvaniṣṭhaprakāratā paṭaniṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpitā। dvayoḥ nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। aparvato vahnimān dravyaṃ parvatarūpaikadharmiviśeṣyake ativyāptiḥ। bhāvaḥ। ekadharmāvacchinneti। tathā ca
saṃśayasya lakṣaṇam। aparvato vahnimān, dravyaṃ vahnyabhāvavat' iti nātivyāpitariti bhāvaḥ। ghaṭābhāvavacca' ityākārake samuccaye ativyāptiḥ। tasyāpi - niṣṭhaprakāratānirūpakatvādityata āha-digiti।
saṃśayatvam। tacca samuccayavyāvṛttam। samuccaye virodhābhānena koṭidvayaviṣayitayoḥ virodhaviṣayitvānirūpitatvāt। saṃśaye lakṣaṇasamanvaya iti bhāvaḥ। etena samuccaye ativyāptivāraṇāya jñāne
viruddhatvaviśeṣaṇaṃ ca vyartham। tayorjñānayoḥ virodhaviṣayakatvābhāvenaiva vāraṇāditi śaṅkāyāḥ nāvasaraḥ। uktapariṣkāra eva prakṛtagranthatātparyāditi। svaghaṭitetyādi।
saṃśaye astīti samanvayaḥ। advaitavedānte। tathā ca mithyāviṣayakaṃ jñānaṃ viparyaya ityuktau tadabhāvavati tatprakārakanirṇaya iti vyākhyānaṃ kṛtamiti bhāvaḥ। pramāvāraṇāyedamiti। tatprakārakanirṇayaḥ viparyayaḥ
api ghaṭatvādiprakārakatvāt। tadvāraṇāya tadabhāvavatīti viśeṣaṇam। ghaṭatvābhāvavadviṣyakatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। na samūhālambane atiprasaṅga iti। raṅgarajatayoḥ aime raṅgarajate' iti pramāyāṃ nātivyāpitarityarthaḥ। tasyāḥ pramāyāḥ
rajatatvasyāprakāratvāditi bhāvaḥ। avaśiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ pratyakṣapariccheda evoktamityāśayenoktam saṅkṣepa iti। vyāpakāropastarkaḥ। āropaśabdasya āhāryabhramaityarthaḥ। āhāryatvaṃ ca bādhakālīnecchājanyatvam। tṛtīyāyāḥ janyatvamarthaḥ। tasya
vyāpakārope anvayaḥ। vyāpyasyāropaḥ vyāpyāropaḥ। ṣaṣṭhyāḥ viṣayatvamarthaḥ। tathā ca bādhakālīnecchājanyavyāpyaviṣayakabhramajanyaḥ bādhakālīnecchājanyavyāpakaviṣayako bhramastarka iti phalati। yadi ityākārakastarkaḥ। tatra vyāpyaḥ vahnyabhāvaḥ tadviṣayakaḥ āropaḥ
dhūmābhāvasya āropaḥ tarhi dhūtābhāvavān syādityākārakaḥ। sa eva tarkaḥ। vyāpyaviṣayakabhrame āhāryatvaviśeṣaṇādāne śākhāyāṃ tatrātivyāptiḥ tadvāraṇāya āhāryatvaviśeṣaṇam। śākhāyāṃ karabhramaḥ na āhārya iti nātivyāptiḥ। vyāpakārope āhāryatvaviśeṣaṇādāne
rajataṃ ityākārake anāhāryabhrame ativyāptiḥ। tadāha - āhāryavyāpyavattetyādi। nāyaṃ puruṣa iti niścayasatva iti। aayaṃ puruṣa' iti bhramasya āhāryatvasampādanāyaitaduktm। rajatatvavyāpyābhāvavattāgrahakāle iti।
iti। āpādyaḥ prasañjanīyaḥ, dhūmābhāvaḥ tadvyatirekaḥ vahnyabhāvasya ca yā vyāptiḥ tanniścayaśca tarke kāraṇamityarthaḥ। kathamayathārthasya traividhyakathanamiti। saṃśayo viparyayaśceti dvaividhyakathanasyaiva yuktatvādityarthaḥ। pratibandhakavighaṭanadvāreti।
pratibandhakībhūtavyabhicāraśaṅkānivartanadvāretyarthaḥ। pṛthaṅnirdeśa ityarthaḥ। tathā ca viparyaye tarkatvākāraḥ viśeṣajñāpanāya viparyayatvatarkatvābhyāṃ vibhāga iti bhāvaḥ। AnTs smṛtir api dvividhā । yathārthāyathārthā ca pramājanyā yathārthā । apramājanyāyathārthā ।।
ceti। pramājanayā yathārthā। apramājanyā ayathārthā। AnTs sarveśām anukūlatayā vedanīyaṃ sukham ।। AnTs sarveśāṃ pratikūlatayā vedanīyaṃ duḥkham ।। AnTs icchā kāmaḥ ।।
AnTs krodho dveṣaḥ ।। AnTs kṛtiḥ prayatnaḥ ।। AnTs vihitakarmajanyo dharmaḥ ।। AnTs niṣiddhakarmajanyas tv adharmaḥ ।।
AnTs buddhyādayo'ṣṭāv ātmamātraviśeṣaguṇāḥ ।। AnTs buddhīcchāprayatnā dvividhāḥ । nityā īśvarasya ।। anukūlatayā vedanīyaṃ sukham। pratikūlatayā vedanīyaṃ duḥkham। icchā kāmaḥ। kṛtiḥ prayatnaḥ। vihitakarmajanyo dharmaḥ।
niṣiddhakarmajanyo adharmaḥ। buddhyādayaḥ aṣṭau ātmamātraviśeṣaguṇāḥ। nityā anityaśca। nityā īśvarasya। smṛtiriti। sukhaṃ lakṣayati - sarveṣāmiti। asukhī aham'
ityādyanuvyasāyagamyaṃ sukhatvādikameva lakṣaṇam। yathāśrutaṃ tu svarūpakathanamiti draṣṭavyam। sukhatvādikameva lakṣaṇamityāha - sukhī ahamityādyanuvyavasāyeti। sukhatvādītyādinā dukhatvaparigrahaḥ।
sarveṣāmanukūlatayā ityādikamityarthaḥ। anukūlatvaprakārakajñānaviṣayatvaṃ sukhasya lakṣaṇamiti pratīyate। tathā ityāha - nanu sarveṣāmityādinā। AnTs saṃskāras trividhaḥ । vego bhāvanā sthitisthāpakaś ceti । vegaḥ pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayamanovṛttiḥ । anubhavajanyā smṛtihetur bhāvanātmamātravṛttiḥ । anyathā kṛtasya punas tadavasthāpādakaḥ sthitisthāpakaḥ kaṭādipṛthivīvṛttiḥ ।।
vegaḥ bhāvanā sthitasthāpakaśceti। vegaḥ pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayamanovṛttiḥ। anubhavajanyā smṛtihetuḥ bhāvanā। ātmamātravṛttiḥ। anyathā kṛtasya punaḥ tādavasthyāpādakaḥ sthitasthāpakaḥ। kaṭādipṛthivīmātravṛttiḥ।
- saṃskāra iti। saṃskāratvajātimān saṃskāra। vegasyāśrayamāha - vega iti। vegatvajātimān vegaḥ। bhāvanāṃ lakṣayati - anubhaveti। anubhavadhvaṃse ativyāptivāraṇāya smṛtīti। ātmādāvativyāptivāraṇāya anubhaveti। smṛterapi saṃskārajanakatvaṃ
navīnairuktam। sthitasthāpakaṃ lakṣayati - anyatheti। saṅkhyādayaḥ aṣṭau naimittikadravatvavegasthitasthāpakāḥ sāmānyaguṇāḥ। anubhavetīti। anubhavatvasyāpi jātitvena jñānatvāpekṣayā gauravāsaṃbhavāt। na ca
kāraṇatvasambhave vyāpakadharmasyānyathāsiddhinirūpakatvāditi। sakṛtadanubhūtasya smaraṇottaraṃ asmaraṇaprasaṅgāt। na ca taduttaraṃ paṭādismaraṇānupapattiḥ, tattadviṣayakasaṃskārābhāvāt। paṭādismārakatvāyogāt। ataḥ svajanyacaramasmṛterevānāyatyā
janakatāyāmapi na doṣa iti vācyam।, anyūnaviṣayakasyaiva phalasya nāśakatvāṅgīkāreṇa adoṣāt। jāyate ca punaḥ punaḥ smaraṇāt dṛḍhataraḥ saṃskāraḥ। dārḍhyaṃ ca saṃskāragataḥ jātiviśeṣaḥ jhaṭiti smṛtyutpādaprayojakaḥ। na ca daivavaśasampannāt jhaṭiti
tatprayojakatayā saṃskāragataḥ jātiviśeṣaḥ siddhyatīti vācyam। saṃskārātiśayakhaṇḍane śāstrādāvabhyāsasyaivānāpatteḥ। kiṃ ca parityajya prāhuḥ। tanmataṃ darśayati - smṛterapīti। apinā anubhavaparigrahaḥ। niveśanīyam।
vyāpyadharmapuraskāreṇeti। vyāpyadharmaḥ anubhavatvam, vyāpakadharmaḥ jñānatvam। anyathāsiddhinirūpakatvāditi। na hi daṇḍasya dravyatvena rūpeṇa ghaṭakākaraṇatvamiti bhāvaḥ। saṃskārasya phalanāśyatayeti। smaraṇarūpeṇa phalena nāśyatayetyarthaḥ। tathā ca
naṣṭatvāt। na ca ghaṭasmaraṇāt punaḥ। saṃskāro jāyate tena punarghaṭasmaraṇamiti bhavatā vaktuṃ śakyate। anubhavatvena kāraṇatvapakṣe saṃskārotpādakatvāyogāt। jñānatvena kāraṇatve tu smaraṇe api bhāvaḥ।
na ca svajanyetyādi। naṣṭatvāt। na ca tatra ghaṭasmaraṇajanyasaṃskāraḥ paṭādismṛtiṃ janayatīti vācyam। ghaṭasmaraṇajanyasaṃskārasya ghaṭaviṣayakatayā tasya paṭādismṛtijanakatvāyogāt। tadviṣayakasmṛtiṃ prati
anyaviṣayakasaṃskāreṇānyāviṣayakasmaraṇāsambhavāt। tathā ca antimasmṛtireva saṃskāreṇānyaviṣayakasmaraṇāsambhavāt। tathā ca vācyam। itthaṃ ca anubhavatvāvacchinnaṃ saṃskārasmṛtyorheturiti smṛtihetutvamastu iti śaṅkāgranthābhiprāyaḥ।
anyūtaviṣayakasyaivetyādi। saṃskāre yāvantaḥ padārthāḥ viṣayāḥ tāvatpadārthaviṣayakasamaraṇameva saṃskāranāśakam। tathā-ca paṭādismaraṇamupapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। smaraṇe saṃskāranyūnaviṣayakatvaṃ ca saṃskāraviṣayatāvyāpakaviṣayatākatvam। saṃskāraṃ prati
jñānatvenaiva hetutve yuktyanataramāha - jāyate ceti। punaḥ punaḥ ityanubhavasiddham। tacca jñānatvena saṃskārahetutva eva saṅgacchate, smaraṇasyāpi jñānatvena tataḥ saṃskārotpattisambhavāt iti bhāvaḥ। udbodhakasamavadhānāditi। udbodhakaṃ sambandhidarśanādi।
saṃskārātiśayakhṇḍana iti। saṃskāragatadārḍhyākhyajātiviśeṣakhaṇḍana ityarthaḥ। abhyāsasyaivānāpatteriti। saṃskāragatadārḍhyākhyajātiviśeṣakhaṇḍana ityarthaḥ। abhyāsasyaivānāpatteriti। saṃskāradārḍhyārthameva abhyāsakaraṇāditi
bhāvaḥ। nanu jhaṭiti smṛtyarthaṃ jhaṭiti saṃskāradārḍhyārthaṃ ityataḥ doṣāntaramāha - kiṃ ceti। niścitāvyabhicārakaṃ rūpamiti। yaddharmāvacchinnai tādṛśaṃ dharmamityarthaḥ।
dharmamiti yāvat। gṛhyamāṇavyabhicārakeṇeti। yaddharmāvacchinne vyabhicāro gṛhyate tena dharmeṇetyarthaḥ। prakṛte dvitīyasmaraṇātpūrvamanubhavābhāvāt। tathā cānubhavatvāvacchinnaṃ gṛhyamāṇavyabhicārakam। dvitīyasmaraṇātpūrvamapi jñānatvāvacchinnasya
niścitāvyabhicārakam। ataḥ niścitāvyabhicāreṇa jñānatvenaiva smṛtihetutvam, na gṛhītavyabhicāroṇānubhavatveneti bhāvaḥ। nanu bhāvanā' iti lakṣaṇaṃ tatrāvyāptamityata āha - etanmata iti। tathā ca etanmate jñānajanyatve sati smṛtihetutvameva saṃskārasya lakṣaṇam।
bhāvaḥ। viśeṣaguṇāḥ। viśeṣaguṇatvam। dravyavibhājakopādhīti। pṛthivītvajalatvādirūpaṃ
dvitvapṛthaktvasaṃyogādayaḥ tadavṛttijātimadguṃṇatvamityarthaḥ। lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। nanu idaṃ lakṣaṇa ekatvādiṣvativyāptam ekatvatvādi jāterapi tādṛśatvāt। na ca tadarthaḥ। evaṃ caikatvādiṣu saṅkhyātvādeḥ sattvāt
tādṛśajātiśūnyatvasyāsattvena nātivyāptiriti vācyam। evamapi parimāṇādiṣvativyāpteḥ। parimāṇatvādeḥ tādṛśajātitvāsambhavāt guṇatvamiti tadarthaḥ। yadrūpāvacchinnasāmānādhikaraṇyasya ghaṭatvāderdhartumaśakyatvāt ghaṭādau ativyāptiḥ, ato viśeṣyam।
sthitasthāpake ativyāptivāraṇāya sthitasthāpakavṛttibhinneti। sthitasthāpakasya pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayavṛttitvamate tu na deyam। rūpādiṣu lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। pārthivānuṣṇāśītasparśasya vāyavīyāpekṣayā vijātīyasyaiva anubhavasiddhatvāt। saṅkhyādayastu sāmānyaguṇā
tatra nātivyāptiḥ। tādṛśajātimadbhinnaguṇatvameva sāmānyaguṇānāṃ lakṣaṇamavaseyam। viśeṣaguṇasya dīpikāyāṃ lakṣaṇamuktam। tatra dravyavibhājakopādhidvayaṃ vyācaṣṭe - pṛthivītvajalatvādirūpamiti। pṛthivītvajalatvayorubhayoḥ
prasiddham। tadvṛttayaḥ dvitvapṛthaktvasaṃyogādayaḥ tadavṛttirjātiḥ tādṛśajātimadguṇatvasya rūparasādau sattvāt lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। rūpasya rasādeḥ vā avṛtteḥ। ato dviniṣṭhaṃ dvitvādikameva tādṛśaṃ tadavṛttitvaṃ rūpatvādijātāvastīti bhāvaḥ। atra pratyekamityasya
tadadhikaraṇavṛttitve apītyavadheyam। ādipadena gṛhyate। na ca rūpatvarasatvādijātimādāyaiva samanvayasambhave vācyam।"atra pravadantī"tyādinā vakṣyamāṇapariṣkāra eva samanvayasya kartavyatvāt। dravatvāvāntarajātimiti। dravatvatvavyāpyāṃ
sāṃsiddhikadravatvatvarūpāṃ jātimityarthaḥ। snehādiṣu daśasviti। snehaśabdabuddhisukhaduḥkhecchādveṣaprayatnadharmādharmeṣvityarthaḥ। saṃskāratvāvāntarajātimiti। saṃskāratvavyāpyāṃ bhāvanātvajātimityarthaḥ।
śaṅkate - nanvidamiti। pratyekamadhikaraṇe pṛthivyāṃ jale ca ekatvaṃ nāsti। ubhayatrāvṛtteḥ। tathā ca tādṛśopādhidvayasamānādhikaraṇāḥ sāmānyaguṇe ekatve ativyāptiriti bhāvaḥ।
dravyavibhājakopādhidvayasamānādhikaraṇāvṛttitvādityarthaḥ। na ca tādṛśeti। tādṛśetyasya dravyavibhājaketyarthaḥ। tathā ca rūpādāvasti। ekatve tu nāsti, saṅkhyātvarūpatādṛśajātimattvasyaiva sattvāt। ato nātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। guṇatvanyūnavṛttīti।
guṇatvavyāpyetyarthaḥ। viśeṣaguṇalakṣaṇatve apītyarthaḥ। parimāṇādiṣvativyāpteriti। aṇutvamahattvādirūpaṃ parimāṇaṃ pratyekavṛtti na vyāsajyavṛtti। ataḥ bhāvaḥ। tādṛśajātitvāsambhavāditi।
dravyavibhājakopādhidvayasamānādhikaraṇavṛttiguṇatvavyāpyajātitvāsambhavādityarthaḥ। yadyadrūpeti। yadyadrūpaṃ guṇatvaṃ nīlādiṣvastīti samanvayaḥ। atra guṇatvarūpaviśeṣyadalasya prayojanamāha - yadrūpāvacchinneti। tathā ca yadrūpapadena ghaṭatvaṃ
nopādātuṃ śakyam। tadavacchinnasya ghaṭasyādhikaraṇe kapāle dravyavibhājakopādhidvayasya jalatvapṛthivītvadvayasyāsattvāt। ataḥ guṇapadam। na ca yadrūpapadena ghaṭatvamapyupādātuṃ śakyate tadbhinnatvaṃ ca ghaṭatve nāstīti kathaṃ ativyāptiprasaktiriti vācyam।
ghaṭatvajātiḥ tadvattvāt ghaṭe ativyāptiprasaktirityāśayāt। sthitasthāpaka iti। tadvadguṇatvasya sthitasthāpake sattvāt tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya jātau sthitasthāpakavṛttibhinneti viśeṣaṇam। sthitasthāpakatvaṃ tu
sthitasthāpakavṛtti, na tadṛbhinnamiti na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। na deyamiti। tanmate sthitasthāpakādhikaraṇaṃ jalaṃ pṛthivī ca tadvṛttitvaṃ sthitasthāpakavṛttibhinneti viśeṣaṇaṃ na deyamiti bhāvaḥ। bhavatīti kathaṃ rūpe lakṣaṇasamanvaya ityata āha - rūpatvāderiti। tathā
bhāvaḥ। nanu sparśe kathaṃ lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। na tāvat sparśatvamādāya। tasyāpi yadrūpapadenopādātuṃ śakyatvāt। tathā hi-yadrūpaṃ bhavati iti sparśatvamādāya samanvayaḥ kartumaśakyaḥ। nāpi pārthivānuṣṇāśītarspaśasyeti। tathā ca anuṣṇāśītatvavyāpyā
pārthivasparśe avidyamānā kācana jātirasti। tāṃ tāmādāya pāthivasparśe vācavīyasparśe ca samanvayaḥ। tathā hi - yadrūpapadena sā jātiḥ na pārthiṃvasparśeṃ samanvayaḥ। evaṃ vāyavīyasparśe api samanvayo bodhya iti bhāvaḥ।
iti। tathā caikatve vaijātyābhāvāt sakalaikatvasādhāraṇamekatvatvaṃ jalatvapṛthivītvarūpopādhidvayam। atastadbhinnā ekatvatvabhinnā ekatvatvajātiḥ na bhavatīti naikatve ativyāptirityāśayaḥ। tādṛśajātimadbhinnaguṇatvamiti।
dravyavibhājakopādhidvayasamānādhikaraṇāvṛttijātimadbhinnaguṇatvamityarthaḥ। AnTs calanātmakaṃ karma । ūrdhvadeśasaṃyogahetur utkṣepaṇam । adhodeśasaṃyogahetur apakṣepaṇam । śarīrasaṃnikṛṣṭasaṃyogahetur ākuñcanam । viprakṛṣṭasaṃyogahetuḥ prasāraṇam । anyat sarvaṃ gamanam । pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayamanomātravṛtti ।। calanātmakaṃ karma। ūrdhvadeśasaṃyogahetuḥ utkṣepaṇam। adhodeśasaṃyogahetuḥ
apakṣepaṇam। śarīrasannikṛṣṭasaṃyogahetuḥ ākuñcanam। śarīraviprakṛṣṭasaṃyogahetuḥ prasāraṇam। anyatsarvaṃ gamanam। AnTs nityam ekam anekānugataṃ sāmānyam । dravyaguṇakarmavṛtti । tad dvividhaṃ parāparabhedāt । aparaṃ dravyatvādiḥ ।। anekānugataṃ sāmānyam। dravyaguṇakarmavṛtti। paraṃ sattā। aparaṃ
dravyatvādi। AnTs nityadravyavṛttayo vyāvartakā viśeṣāḥ ।। vyāvartakā viśeṣāḥ। - calaneti। utkṣepaṇādīnāṃ kāryabhadamāha - ūrveti। śarīreti।
vakratāsaṃpādakaṃ ākuñcanam। ṛjutāsampādakaṃ prasāraṇamityarthaḥ। nityamiti। saṃyoge ativyāptivāraṇāya nityamiti। jalaparamāṇugatarūpe ativyāptivāraṇāya eketi। samavetatvam tena nābhāvādau ativyāptiḥ।
nityeti। sarvasaṅgrāhakaṃ na bhavatītyāha - vakrateti। nityamitīti। atra ekataraniveśenāpi saṃyogādervāraṇāt। ekapadaṃ
svarūpakīrtanamātraparamiti draṣṭavyam। iti। nityadravyāṇāṃ paraspara bhedasādhakā ityarthaḥ atha viśeṣapadārthe kiṃ pramāṇam। na ca atyantasaṅkīrṇānāṃ paramāṇūnāṃ vācyam, ekatvādivyaktereva bhedakatvasaṃmbhavāt iti cet - na।
etadekatvādereva hetutā vācyā। na ca tayoḥ paramāṇvoḥ bhedāsiddhau ekatvādau etatvaṃ sugraham। etatparamāṇusamavetatvaṃ hi tasyaitatvam। tasmāt pratinityadravyameṣṭavyo viśeṣapadārthaḥ। sa eva viśeṣāntarāpekṣā nāsti। ato nānavasthā iti sampradāyaḥ।
nityadravyavṛttitve sati bhedasādhakatvaṃ viśeṣasya lakṣaṇamiti labhyate। nityadravyāṇāṃ parasparabhedasādhakā ityartha iti। atyantasaṅkīrṇānāmiti। atyantaṃ miśritānāmityarthaḥ। ekatvādivyaktereveti। ayaṃ paramāṇuḥ tatparamāṇoḥ bhidyate ekatvāt
ityanumānamatra vivakṣitam। yata etatparamāṇāviti। etadekatvāditi hetuḥ prayoktavyaḥ। etadekatvaṃ nāma etatparamāṇumātrasamavetamekatvam। ekatve bhede ajñāte durgraham। tathā ca hetujñānābhāvāt nānumiti।
pūrvameva bhede jñāte cānumānavaiyarthyam। anumānasya bhedasiddhyarthatvāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu etatparamāṇuḥ tatparamāṇoḥ bhinnaḥ paramāṇubhedassādhanīyaḥ। tatra etatparamāṇugataviśeṣe paramāṇvantarabhedasādhakatvaṃ na bhavati। tadarthaṃ viśeṣe
viśeṣāntarasvīkāre anavasthetyata āha - sa eva svasajātīyānāmiti। svaparanirvāhakatvāṅgīkārāt, ato nānavastheti bhāvaḥ। AnTs nityasaṃbandhaḥ samavāyaḥ । yayor dvayor madhya ekam avinaśyadaparāśritam evāvatiṣṭate tāv ayutasiddau । yathāvayavāvayavinau guṇaguṇinau kriyākriyāvantau jātivyaktī viśeṣanityadravye ceti ।। samavāyaḥ। yayormadhye ekamamavinaśyadavasthaṃ
aparāśritamevāvatiṣṭhate tau ayutasiddhau। yathā avayavāvayavinau, guṇaguṇinau, kriyākriyāvantau, jātivyaktī, viśeṣanityadravye ceti। nityeti। saṃyoge ativyāptivāraṇāya nityeti। ākāśādāvativyāptivāraṇāya sambandheti। ayutasiddhalakṣaṇamāha -
yayoriti। nīlo ghaṭa iti daṇḍīti viśiṣṭabuddhivat iti samavāyasiddhiḥ। avayavāvayavināviti। dravyasamavāyikāraṇamavayavaḥ, tajjanyaṃ dravyaṃ avayavi।
iti। samavāyikāraṇatvasya antyāvayavini sattvāt dravyeti। paramāṇuvāraṇāya janyeti। avinaśyadavasthamaparāritamevāvatiṣṭhate paṭādiriti manasikṛtya mūle avinaśyadityuktam। dravyanirūpitasamavāyikāraṇatvaṃ avayavasya lakṣaṇamiti labhyate।
ghaṭarūpadravyasamavāyikāraṇatvasya kapāle sattvāt lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। tatra tatsamavetarūpādisamavāyikāraṇatvasattvāt tatrātivyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya samavāyikāraṇatve dravyanirūpiteti viśeṣaṇam। dravyanirūpitasamavāyikāraṇatvābhāvāt nātivyāptiḥ। tadāha -
samavāyikāraṇatvasyeti। kapālarūpe avayavini avayavatvasyeṣṭatayā tatrātivyāptirneti sūcanāya antyāvayavinītyuktam। janyaṃ lakṣaṇamuktam। tatra janyatvamātroktau janyaguṇadāvativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya dravyatvamupāttam। dravyatvamātroktau avayave
paramāṇāvativyāptiḥ। tadvāraṇāya janyatvamupāttm। tadāha - paramāṇuvāraṇāyeti। paramamūle ayayormadhye granthena ayutasiddhayorlakṣaṇamuktam। yayormadhye tantupaṭayormadhye ekaḥ paṭaḥ tantvāśrita evāvatiṣṭhate iti tau tantupaṭāvayutasiddhau।
tatra vinaśyadavastha ityasya nāśapūrvakṣaṇasya ityarthaḥ। avinaśyadavastha ityasya nāśāvyavahitapūrvakṣaṇāt pūrvakṣaṇeṣu vidyamāna ityarthaḥ। nāśaviśiṣṭatvaṃ vinaśyadavasthatvamiti yāvat। tatra avinaśyadavasthamityādinā। ayamatrāśayaḥ-yadi ekamityasya
syāt। tathā sati tantupaṭayoravyāptiḥ। tantupaṭayormadhye ekasya tantvanāśritasyaivāvasthānāt। ataḥ paṭasya avinaśyadavasthetiṃ viśeṣaṇam। tantunāśakṣaṇasthaḥ paṭaḥ vinaśyadavasthaḥ, uttarakṣaṇe paṭasya nāśāvyavahitapūrvakṣaṇasthatvarūpavinaśyadavasthalakṣaṇākrāntatvāt। ataḥ
tantvāśritatayaivāvasthānāt nāvyāptiriti। tantvādināśakṣaṇe ityarthaḥ। AnTs anādiḥ sāntaḥ prāgabhāvaḥ । utpatteḥ pūrvaṃ kāryasya । sādir anantaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ । utpattyanantaraṃ kāryasya । traikālikasaṃsargāvacchinnapratiyogitāko'tyantābhāvaḥ । yathā bhūtale ghaṭo nāstīti । tādātmyasaṃbandhāvacchinnapratiyogitāko'nyonyābhāvaḥ yathā ghaṭaḥ paṭo na bhavatīti ।। prāgabhāvaḥ। utpatteḥ pūrvaṃ kāryasya। sādiranantaḥ pradhvaṃsābhāvaḥ।
utpatteranantaraṃ kāryasya। traikālikaḥ saṃsargāvacchinnābhāvaḥ atyantābhāvaḥ। yathā bhūtale ghaṭo nāsti iti। tādātmyāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvo anyonyābhāvaḥ। yathā ghaṭaḥ paṭo na bhavatīti।
- anādiriti। ākāśādau ativyāpitavāraṇāya sānta iti। ghaṭādau ativyāpitavāraṇāya anādiriti। pratiyogisamavāyikāraṇavattiḥ pratiyogijanako bhaviṣyatīti vyavahārahetuḥ prāgabhāvaḥ। dhvaṃsaṃ lakṣayati-sādiriti। ghaṭādau ativyāpitavāraṇāṇa ananta iti।
ākāśādau ativyāptivāraṇāya sādiriti। pratiyogijanyaḥ pratiyogisamavāyikāraṇavṛttiḥ dhvasta iti vyavahārahetuḥ dhvaṃsaḥ। traikāliketi। anyonyābhāve ativyāptivāraṇāya saṃsargeti।
dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvayorativyāptivāraṇāya traikālika iti। anyonyābhāvaṃ lakṣayati - tādātmyeti। pratiyogitāvacchedakāropyasaṃsargabhedādekapratiyogikayoratyantānyonyābhāvayorbhinnatvam। ghaṭatvāvacchinnapratiyogitākasāmānyābhāvaśca atiriktaḥ।
evamanyonyābhāvo api। pramāṇamāha - bhaviṣyatīti। tādātmyātiriktasaṃsargetyarthaḥ। matābhiprāyeṇa traikāliketi viśeṣaṇam। anyathā anyonyābhāvavārakeṇaiva tayorvāraṇāt tadvyarthatāpatteḥ। yadi
traikāliketi siddhānte api sārthakaṃ traikālikatvamiha nityatvarūpam। nāstīti। atra ghaṭābhāvāṃśe bhūtalasya viśeṣyatvaṃ sambandhaḥ, svarūpasambandhaviśeṣau na jñānīyaviṣayatāviśeṣau। na ca vācyam। tādṛśapratītyoḥ vailakṣaṇyāya prathamāyāṃ
durlabhatvāt। na ca tādṛśapratītyoḥ saṃsargāṃśe avilakṣaṇatve api viśeṣaṇatāyā eva sambandhatāstviti vācyam। tāvatāpi abhūtale ghaṭo aghaṭābhāve bhūtalam' ityanayośca pratītyoḥ vailakṣaṇyānirvrāhāt। svarūpasambandhaviśeṣayoḥ saṃsargatā। tathā ca abhūtalavān ghaṭābhāvaḥ'
bhūtalam ityatra ca bhūtalāṃśe abhāvasya viśeṣyatāsaṃsargaḥ bhāsate। sa ca tatra abādhita iti abhramatvanirvāha iti saṅkṣepaḥ। netyāha - pratiyogiteti। prācīnamatābhiprāyeṇa। atra saṃsargabhedo apyatyantābhāvabahutvaprayojakaḥ।
draṣṭavyam। tadeva darśayati-kevaleti। kevaladevadattābhāvāt viśiṣṭābhāvo atirikta ityanvayaḥ। anyathā kevaladevadattavati adaṇḍī nāsti' iti pratyayānāpatteḥ। ubhayābhāvasyātiriktatve pratītiṃ pramāṇayati - ekasattve apīti। ghaṭapaṭau dvau na sva ityādau ghaṭatvaṃ
kevalapaṭavati yatkiñcidubhayavati ca tathā pratyayāt। sambandhabhedenābhāvasyātiriktatvaṃ darśayati - saṃyogeneti। sāmānyaviśeṣābhāvayoḥ bhedaṃ darśayati - tattaditi। anyathā yatkiñcit ghaṭavati ghaṭo nāstīti pratyayāpatteḥ।
evamanyonyābhāvo apīti। avacchedakabhedāt tattadghaṭabhedaḥ tataḥ ubhayabhedaḥ ghaṭabhedaśca atirikta ityarthaḥ। mūlam। saṃsarṅgābhāva ityasya saṃsargāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāva ityarthaḥ। tatra
nityatvāt। tadvāraṇāya saṃsargāvacchinnapratiyogitāka ityuktam। na ativyāptitādavasthyamiti vācyam। saṃsargābhāva ityanena vivakṣitatvāt। tadāha - tādātmyātiriktasaṃsargetyartha iti। traikālika iti। nanu samavāyena ghaṭādhikaraṇe saṃyogena
samavāyasambandhāvacchinnaghaṭābhāvayorbhedo vaktavyaḥ। tadarthaṃ cātyantābhāvīyapratiyogitāyāṃ sambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ aṅgīkriyate। saṃsargāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvaṃ aprāmāṇikam। tathā ca saṃsargābhāva viśeṣaṇaṃ vyarthaṃ ityata āha - dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvayorapīti।
bhāvaḥ। dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvayoḥ sambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvānaṅgīkāra ityarthaḥ। anyonyābhāvavārakeṇaiveti। anyonyābhāve ativyāpitavāraṇāya tādātmyātiriktasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvaviśeṣaṇenaivetyarthaḥ।
tayorvāraṇāt - dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvayorativyāptivāraṇasambhavāt। tadvyarthatāpatteḥ - traikāliketi viśeṣaṇavaiyarthyāpatteḥ। tathā ca saṃsargābhāva ityasya anyonyābhāvabhinnābhāva ityarthaḥ। tatrātivyāptivāraṇāya trekāliketi viśeṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ।
tadavasthetyata āha - traikālikatvamiha nityatvarūpamiti। nityatvaṃ ca dhvaṃsāpratiyogitve sati prāgabhāvāpratiyogitvam। dhvaṃsāpratiyogitvaniveśāt prāgabhāvanirāsaḥ। prāgabhāvāpratiyogitvaniveśāt dhvaṃsanirāsaḥ।
iti prācīnairuktaṃ na saṅgacchate। bhūtalaṃ ghaṭābhāvavat iti ityukterasaṅgatatvāt। tathā ityādinā। viśeṣyatvaviśeṣaṇatvesvarūpasambandhaviśeṣāviti। yathā
ghaṭābhāvasvarūpam। sambandhatayocyamānaṃ viśeṣyatvaṃ viśeṣaṇatvaṃ ca na svarūpasambandhātmakam। tathā ca abhūtale ghaṭo nāsti' ityatra bhūtalasya prakāratayā bhānāt pratīteḥ pramātvameveti। na ca viśeṣaṇatākhya iti। tathā ca bhūtalaghaṭābhāvayoḥ viśeṣaṇatvamiti
eka eva sambandhaḥ। na ca ekasyaiva sambandhasya dvayorapi pratītyorviṣayatve tayorvailakṣaṇyaṃ kathamiti vācyam। sambandhaikye api abhūtale ghaṭo pratītyoḥ vailakṣaṇyasya vaktuṃ śakyatvāditi śaṅkituḥ āśayaḥ। samādhatte - tādṛśapratītyoriti। abhūtale ghaṭo
nāsti' iti pratītāvityarthaḥ। abhūtalaṃ ghaṭābhāvavat' iti pratītāvityarthaḥ। tādṛśapratītyoriti। tathā cobhayatrāpi pratīntyoḥ viśeṣaṇatvanāmakaḥ eka eva sambandhaḥ viṣayaḥ। tathāpi abhūtale ghaṭo nāsti' iti pratītau
bhūtalaniṣṭhā। abhūtalaṃ ghaṭābhāvavat' iti pratītau tādṛpratītyorvailakṣaṇyaṃ na sambandhavailakṣaṇyāditi śaṅkiturabhiprāyaḥ। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvabhedāditi। viśeṣyatākhyaviṣayatāvailakṣaṇyādityarthaḥ।
tāvatāpīti। abhūtale ghaṭo nāsti' iti pratītau ghaṭābhāve vailakṣaṇyaṃ na syāt। evaṃ abhūtalaṃ ghaṭābhāvavat' iti pratītau durupapādamiti bhāvaḥ। evaṃ ca svarūpātmakaviśeṣaṇatākhyamekameva pratīterabhramatvamupasaṃharati - tasmāditi। tathā ca abhūtale ghaṭo
ityanayorvailakṣaṇyam। abhūtalaṃ ghaṭābhāvavat' ityatra bhūtalāṃśe ghaṭābhāvasya viśeṣaṇatvaṃ saṃsargaḥ। aghaṭābhāve bhūtalam' ityatra vailakṣaṇyamiti bhāvaḥ। viśeṣyatāviṣayakatvāt vailakṣaṇyaṃ na syāt। evaṃ abhūtalavān
iti। pratītīnāṃ vailakṣaṇyamupapādanīyam। yayoḥ pratītyoḥ viṣayatāvailakṣaṇyaṃ nāsti tayoḥ sambandhavailakṣaṇyamasti। yayoḥ pratītīnāṃ vailakṣaṇyam। tattassambandhasyābādhitatvāt pramātvaṃ
copapadyata iti bhāvaḥ। kṛte api tātparyājñānāt ācāryacaraṇān apṛccham। te api bahudhā ālocya prakāśikāyāmīṣat śodhanaṃ kṛtvā tātparyamavarṇayan। tathaivāhamatrālikham।
bhidyate। evaṃ pratiyogitāvacche dakadharmabhedāt dīpikāyāṃ nirūpyate। dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvayostu tathā bhedo na nirūpitaḥ, tatra kāraṇamāha - dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvayoriti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - kiñciddharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvaṃ vā nāṅgīkriyate। ataḥ
caikavidhatvameva। atyantānyonyābhāvayostu tadaṅgīkārāt pratiyogitāvacchedakasambandhabhedācca bhinnatvameva। ekapratiyogikānāṃ tādātmyasyaiva pratiyogitāvacchedakasambandhatvāt। tathāpi pratiyogitāvacchedakadharmabhedāt bhedo vaktuṃ śakyata iti bhāvaḥ।
prācīnamatābhiprāyeṇeti। saṃsargāropajanya pratītiviṣayo abhāvaḥ atyantābhāvaḥ। saṃsargāropo nāma tādātmyātiriktasambandhena pratiyogyāropa iti pracīnā āhuḥ। tathā iti bhāvaḥ।
tadevātyantābhāvatvamityāhuḥ। tanmatānusāreṇa tu pratiyogitāvacchedakasambandhabhedādatyantābhāvabheda ityūhmam। ukta ityavadheyam। kevaladevadattābhāvāditi। devadattābhāvasya pratiyogitāvacchedakadharmabhedāt devadattābhāva-daṇḍyabhāvayorbhedaḥ।
pratītirapi na bhavet। bhavati tu tādṛśī pratītiḥ। ataḥ bhāvaḥ। iti। kevalaghaṭavati vā kevalapaṭavati vā pradeśe aghaṭapaṭau dvau na
iti vā pratītiḥ na bhavati। ataḥ kevalaghaṭābhāvāt kevalapaṭābhāvācca atiriktatayā ghaṭapaṭobhayābhāvaḥ svīkartavyaḥ। na staḥ' ityākārakobhayābhāvāvagāhipratītyanupapatteḥ। tathākevalapaṭavati ghaṭapaṭātiriktayatkiñcidubhayavati ca pradeśe tādṛśapratītiḥ na syāt। ataḥ ghaṭatvaṃ paṭatvaṃ ubhayatvaṃ ceti tritayaṃ
pratiyogitāvacchedakam। bhavitumarhatīti bhāvaḥ। saṃyogenetīti। tathā ca samavāyasambandhāvacchinnaghaṭābhāvo anya iti svīkaraṇīyam। anyathā
na bhavati tathā samavāyena ghaṭo nāstī ti pratītirapi na syāt। evaṃ saṃyogena ghaṭo nāstīti pratītirapi syāditi bhāvaḥ। sāmānyaviśeṣābhāyoriti। sāmānyābhāvaviśeṣābhāvayorityarthaḥ।
sāmānyadharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvaḥ sāmānyābhāvaḥ। viśeṣadharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvaḥ viśeṣābhāvaḥ। aghaṭo nāsti' sāmānyābhāvaḥ। anīlaghaṭo nāsti', araktaghaṭo nāsti' viśeṣābhāvaḥ। yadi sāmānyābhāvo nātiriktaḥ tadā nīlaghaṭavati
ghaṭasāmānyābhāvāvagāhinī pratītiḥ syāt। śakyate। ataḥ viśeṣābhāvātiriktaḥ sāmānyābhāvo aṅgīkaraṇīya iti bhāvaḥ। avacchedakabhedāditi। nīlaghaṭabhedasya
nīlaghaṭabhedaghaṭapaṭobhayabheda-ghaṭabhedādīnāṃ bhinnatvaṃ vaktavyamityarthaḥ। nāsti' iti pratītyā vyadhikaraṇadharmāvacchinnābhāvo nāṅgīkriyate। paṭe ghaṭatvaṃ nāstīti tadarthaḥ। atiriktatve sa kevalānvayī। ghaṭatveneti। abhāvadhiyaḥ
vyadhikaraṇadharmāvacchinnābhāve mānābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu tarhi tādṛśapratyayasya kā gatiriti ata āhapaṭa iti। nanu aghaṭatvena paṭo sambhavati। asati bādhake tacchabdollekhipratīteḥ kathamapyapratīteḥ। kintu avacchinnapratiyogitākatvasambandhena abhāvāṃśe
svātantryeṇa ghaṭatvāvagāhitvameva। aabhāvabuddhiḥ viśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhimaryādāṃ nātiśete' iti niyamastu na। cet - astu tarhi atiriktatvaṃ tasyetyāha - atiriktatva iti। saḥ - vyadhikaraṇadharmavacchinnapratiyogitākaḥ।
bhāvaḥ। ayuktamityata āha - prasaṅgāditi। smṛtasya upekṣānarhatvarūpaprasaṅgasaṅgatyetyarthaḥ। nṛsiṃhaśāstricaraṇāḥ prāhuḥ।
dīpikāyām ghaṭatvena paṭo nāstītyādi। vyadhikaraṇadharmāvacchinnābhāvo nāsmābhiraṅgīkriyate। tādṛśapratīteḥ ghaṭatvāvacchinnapaṭaniṣṭhapratiyogitānirūpakābhāvaviṣayakatvādityarthaḥ। samānādhikaraṇadharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākaśceti।
pratiyogitāśrayāvṛttirdharmaḥ vyadhikaraṇadharmaḥ। pratiyogitāśrayavṛttirdharmaḥ samānādhikaraṇadharmaḥ। aghaṭatvena paṭo vyadhikaraṇadharmāvacchinnābhāvaḥ। aghaṭo nāsti' ityatra samānādhikaraṇardhmavacchinnābhāvaḥ ityāhuḥ।
abhāvadhiya iti। abhāvabuddhirviśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhimaryādāṃ iti vaktavyam। prakṛte ghaṭatvaviśiṣṭapaṭāprasiddhyā viṣayīkaroti। api tu śaśaśṛṅgaṃ nāstīti pratītiḥ yathā śṛṅge pratītirapi paṭe ghaṭatvābhāvamavagāhate। ataḥ uktapratītiḥ
vyadhikaraṇadharmasya pratiyogitāvacchedakatvasādhanāya nālamiti bhāvaḥ। nanu ghaṭatvenetyādi। tadullikhatapratītāvapi viṣaya iti vācyam। tatra tādṛśaśabdāt tādṛśaśabdollikhitapratīterapi tadviṣayakatvameva yuktamiti bhāvaḥ।
kintu iti। ghaṭatvenetyatra tṛtīyāyāḥ avacchinnapratiyogitākatvamarthaḥ, tasyābhāve anvaya ityabhiprāyaḥ। vibhaktyartharūpeṇa sambandhenānvaya iṣṭa eva। ata eva dinakaryām sākṣādityasyāpi vyutpattau niveśāt"ityuktam। tatra rāmarudrīye
padārthasya saṃsargavidhayā bhānānaṅgīkārāt। tathāpi abhūtale ghaṭa' bhānamādṛtamṛ"ityuktam। etena apastā। avacchinnapratiyogitākatvasambandhenābhāve anvayo vaktavyaḥ। tathā ca ghaṭe
niyamasya bhaṅga itya āha - abhāvabuddhiriti। aghaṭatvena ghaṭo tadviśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhitvamabhāvabuddheriti niyamāsambhavaḥ। tathā ca tādṛśaniyamabhaṅgaiṣṭa eva iti bhāvaḥ। astu tarhīti। tathā ca ghaṭatvena ghaṭo
vyadhikaraṇadharmāvacchinnāpratiyogitākābhāvo api sidhyatīti bhāvaḥ। virodhivirahāditi। virodhī। ghaṭatvaviśiṣṭasya ghaṭasya sattveghaṭatvāvacchinnaghaṭābhāvaḥ na sambhavati। ghaṭaśūnyasthala eva tādṛśābhāva iti sa na kevalānvayī।
kevalānvayīti bhāvaḥ। atyantābhāva eva samayaviśeṣe pratīyamānaḥ। ghaṭābhāvavati ghaṭānayane ghaṭatyantābhāvapratītiniyāmakatvaṃ kalpyate। ghaṭavati tatsaṃyogaprāgabhāvadhvaṃsayorasattvādeva atyantābhāvasyāpratītiḥ।
ghaṭāpasaraṇe tu saṃyogadhvaṃsasya sattvāt pratītiriti। ghaṭasattvadaśāyāṃ na tadabhāvabuddhiḥ anyadā tu jāyate। ataḥ nirākartumāha - sāmayiketi। pratiyogivirahasamaye pratīyamāno atyantābhāva eva sāmayikābhāvaḥ। na tu
utpādavināśaśālyatirikta iti samuditor'thaḥ। nanvevaṃ bhūtale āha - ghaṭābhāvavatīti। niyāmakatvameva samupapādayati - ghaṭavatīti। tadatyantābhāvabuddhirityapi draṣṭavyam। utpādavināśaśālyatirikta iti। pratiyogivirahakāle utpadyamānaḥ
pratiyogikāle vinaśyaṃścātyantābhāvaḥ sāmayiko atyantābhāvaḥ। tathā traikāliko atyantābhāva iti teṣāmāśayaḥ। dīpikākārāstu sāmayikābhāvastu traikālikātyantābhāvāt nātiricyate। sarvadā ityucyate, na tu samayaviśeṣe utpattimattvena। nanu
iti cet - na। yataḥ ghaṭānayanānantaraṃ vidyamāno api bhūtalaghaṭasaṃyogadhvaṃsaśca prayojaka iti kalpyate। ghaṭānayanānantaraṃ vā nāstīti kāraṇābhāvāt na ghaṭātyantābhāvapratyakṣam। ghaṭātyantābhāvapratyakṣaṃ bhavati। evaṃ ca nityasyaivātyantābhāvasya
praghaṭṭakārthaḥ। samādhānāntaramāha - tattatkālāvacchinneti। yasmin ghaṭaśūnyakāle na bhūtale ghaṭātyantābhāvapratītiriti bhāvaḥ। padārthāntaramiti guravaḥ। tanna-abhāvānaṅgīkāre kaivalyasya
nirvaktumaśakyatvāt। nirācaṣṭe - kevaleti। yadyapyananteṣu adhikaraṇeṣu atroktanyāyasyānavatāraḥ। kiṃ ca abhāvasyādhikaraṇasvarūpatve jalādau - abhāvāvaṅgīkāra iti। atiriktābhāvānaṅgīkāra ityarthaḥ। atha
tadabhāvasvarūpatāpattvāta tadānīmapi ghaṭābhāvavattābuddhiprasaṅgaḥ। kaivalyanirvacanamaśakyamityāha - kaivalyasyeti। yadyapyananteṣviti। ekasya ghaṭātyantābhāvarūpasya dharmiṇaḥ kalpanaṃ laghutaramiti bhāvaḥ। nanu
kalpanīyam। dharmakalpanāpakṣe tu abhāvatvarūpadharmamātraṃ kalpanīyam। dūṣaṇāntaramāha - kiṃ ceti। abhāvaḥ yadyadhikaraṇasvarūpaḥ tarhi jale ghrāṇendriyāgrāhyatvāpattirvā iti bhāvaḥ। itarendriyagrāhyatāpattiriti। ghrāṇetaracakṣurādigrāhyatāpattirityarthaḥ।
ityādidūṣaṇānīti। abhāvasyādhikaraṇātmakatve bhedavyāpyatvāditi dūṣaṇamādipadagrāhyam। eva। nātiriktaḥ, anavasthāprasaṅgāt। dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvaḥ prāgabhāvadhvaṃsaśca pratiyogyeveti prāñcaḥ। abhāvābhāvaḥ atirikta eva tṛtīyābhāvasya
prathamābhāvarūpatvāt na anavastheti navīnāḥ। syādata āha - abhāvābhāva iti। dhvaṃsaprāgabhāvaḥ pratiyogisvarūpaḥ, tatprāgabhāvarūpaśca। prāgabhāvadhvaṃsastu pratiyogisvarūpaḥ, taddhvaṃsarūpaśca ityasyārthaḥ avaseyaḥ। tena
copapattiḥ। nanu kāle dravyatvaṃ nāsti iti pratyayaḥ na jāyate, kalpanīyam। itthaṃ ca bhramatvameva syāt। bhāvasya viśeṣaṇatāviśeṣeṇa vṛttyanaṅgīkārāt। abhāveti। tarhi anavasthetyata āha - tṛtīyeti।
ghaṭadhvaṃsaprāgabhāvaḥ ghaṭaprāgabhāvadhvaṃsaśca ghaṭasvarūpa iti labhyate। ghaṭadhvaṃsaprāgabhāvaviṣayakapratītiḥ na syāt tadānīṃ ghaṭābhāvāt। evaṃ ghaṭasyābhāvādityataḥ tātparyamāha - dhvaṃsaprāgabhāva iti। ghaṭadhvaṃsaprāgabhāvaḥ ghaṭasvarūpaḥ ghaṭaprāgabhāvasvarūpaśca। tathā ca
pratītiḥ udayate। ghaṭotpatyanantaraṃ jāyamānā aghaṭadhvaṃso bhaviṣyati' iti pratītistu ghaṭātmakaṃ ghaṭadhvaṃsaprāgabhāvaṃ viṣayīkaroti। evaṃ ghaṭaprāgabhāvadhvaṃsaḥ ghaṭasvarūpaḥ, ghaṭadhvaṃsasvarūpaśca। ataḥ ghaṭakāle viṣayīkaroti। ghaṭadhvaṃsakāle aghaṭaprāgabhāvo naṣṭaḥ' iti pratītiḥ
ghaṭadhvaṃsarūpaṃ ghaṭaprāgabhāvadhvaṃsaṃ viṣayīkaroti। tathā ca na kāpyanupapattiriti bhāvaḥ। nāstītyādi। kāle dravyatvaṃ nāstīti pratītiḥ na jāyate, kāle dravyatvābhāva iti pratitistu jāyate। tadarthaṃ nañapadaṃ
vyutpattiḥ svīkaraṇīyā। ghaṭe paṭatvaṃ nāstītyasya paṭatvābhāva ityarthaḥ। kāle kālikasambandhena dravyatvābhāvasya bhavatīti vaktavyam। itthaṃ ca bhūtale ghaṭābhāvo nāstīnti iti vaktavyam। ghaṭābhāvābhāvo yadi ghaṭasvarūpaḥ syāt tadā
tādṛśapratīterbhramatvaṃ syāt। iṣyate tu pramātvam। ataḥ abhāvābhāvaḥ na bhāvarūpaḥ api tu atiriktaḥ। ghaṭābhāvābhāvasya iti navīnānāmāśayaḥ। navīnatarāstu bhāvānāmapi daiśikaviśeṣaṇatāsambandhena vṛttiṃ aṅgīkurvanti। tanmate
abhāvābhāvaḥ nātiriktaḥ। etattattvaṃ kūṭaghaṭitalakṣaṇagādādharyāṃ draṣṭavyam। AnTs sarveṣāṃ padārthānāṃ yathāyatham ukteṣv antarbhāvāt saptaiva padārthā iti siddham ।। sarveṣāmapi padārthānāṃ ukteṣveva antarbhāvāt saptaiva padārthā iti siddham।
sarveṣāmiti। sarveṣāṃ saptasvevāntarbhāva ityarthaḥ।"ātmaśarīrendriyārthabuddhimanaḥ dvādaśabidhaṃ prameyam। pravṛttiḥ-dharmādharmau। rāgadveṣamohāḥ doṣāḥ। rāgaḥ-icchā। mohaḥ-śarīrādau ātmabhramaḥ। pretyabhāvaḥ-maraṇam। apavargaḥ-mokṣaḥ। sa ca
svasamānādhikaraṇuduḥkhaprāgabhāvāsamānakālīnaduḥkhadhvaṃsaḥ। prayojanam-sukhaprātiptaḥ duḥkhahāniśca। dṛṣṭāntaḥ-mahānasādiḥ। prāmāṇikatvena abhyupagator'thaḥ siddhāntaḥ। sa ca pramāṇaphalam।
ākṣipati - nanviti। pratyakṣapramāṇasya dravye, anumānādīnāṃ ca ātmetyādinā। ātmaśarīrendriyāṇāṃ dravye, arthasya pṛthivyādirūpasya dravyādiṣu, buddheḥ guṇe, antarindriyasya manasaḥ dravye antarbhāvaḥ। evamagre api yathāyathamantarbhāvaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ।
tajjaniketyarthaḥ। etacca sphuṭamākare। rāgaḥ । maraṇamiti। maraṇānantarabhāvi jananamityarthaḥ। tathā ca padavyutpattiḥ pretya mṛtvā bhāvaḥ jananamitiḥ। caramaprāṇaśarīrasaṃyogadhvaṃsaḥ maraṇam। ādyaśarīraprāṇasaṃyogaḥ jananam। muktātmasaṃyogadhvaṃsavataḥ
ghaṭasya muktatvāpattivāraṇāya - duḥkhadhvaṃsa iti। duḥkhadhvaṃsavatāṃ asmadādīnāmapi muktatvāpattivāraṇāya kālīnāntam। duḥkhaprāgabhāvaviśeṣaṇam। na ca prāgabhāveti vyarthamiti vācyam। yathāsanniveśe vaiyarthyābhāvāditi
dik। saṃśayasya nirūpitatvāt prayojanasvarūpaṃ darśayati - prayojanamiti। dravya iti। indriyaṃ pratyakṣapramākaraṇam। tatra cakṣuṣaḥ tejasi, dravye antarbhāva ityarthaḥ। anumānādīnāṃ ca guṇa iti।
ityevamanumānādīnāṃ jñānarūpe guṇe antarbhāva ityarthaḥ। evamagre apīti। pravṛttidoṣādīnāmapi yathāyathaṃ sapatasvevāntarbhāva ityarthaḥ। nanu dīpikāgrantho asaṅgata ityata āha - tajjaniketyartha iti।
dharmādharmayorjanikā pravṛttirityarthaṃḥ। kārye kāraṇopacāra iti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca pravṛtteḥ guṇe antarbhāvaḥ। sphuṭamākara iti।"pravṛttisādhano dharmādharmau pravṛttiśabdenoktau yathā annasādhanāḥ āsmin sūtre pravṛttirityucyete। kasmāt, tatsādhanatvāt annaṃ vai pravṛtterdharmādharmajanakatvaṃ mūlagrantheṣu spaṣṭamiti bhāvaḥ।
icchāviśeṣa iti। tathā ca rāgasyecchātmake guṇe antarbhāvaḥ। mithyājñānaṃ nāma bhramātmakajñānam। maraṇānantareti। pretya-mṛtvā bhāvaḥ। jananamiti vyutpattyā maraṇānantarakālikajanya pretyabhāvaśabdārthaḥ। caramasya prāṇaśarīrasaṃyogasya dhvaṃsaḥ maraṇam।
ādyaḥ śarīraprāṇasaṃyogaḥ janmaḥ। tathā ca pretyabhāvasya saṃyogarūpe guṇe antarbhāvaḥ। prāṇaśarīrasaṃyoge caramatvaṃ ca svasajātīyaśarīravṛttiprāṇasaṃyogaprāgabhāvānadhikaraṇatvam। ādyatvaṃ ca svasajātīyaśarīravṛttiprāṇasaṃyogadhvaṃsānadhikaraṇatvam।
bhoga iti। bhogo nāma sukhaduḥkhānubhavaḥ। tathā ca phalasya anubhavarūpajñānātmake gaṇe antarbhāvaḥ। svasamānādhikaraṇeti। svasamānādhikaraṇaḥ yaḥ duḥkhaprāgabhāvaḥ। tadasamānakālīna duḥkhadhvaṃsaḥ mokṣa ityarthaḥ। idānīmasmākaṃ vidyamānaḥ yatkiñcidduḥkhadhvaṃsaḥ
bhaviṣyadduḥkhaprāgabhāvasamānakālikaḥ। muktau yaḥ duḥkhadhvaṃsaḥ saḥ dukhaprāgabhāvāsamānakālikaḥ punarduḥkhasyājaniṣyamāṇatvāditi bhāvaḥ। muktātmasaṃyogetyādinā। duḥkhadhvaṃsaḥ ityatra duḥkhapadānupādāne ghaṭasyāpi muktatvaṃ syāt। tadvāraṇāya duḥkhadhvaṃsa ityuktam।
saṃyogadhvaso na duḥkhadhvaṃsa iti tasya na muktitvamiti bhāvaḥ। taddhvaṃsavatvaṃ ghaṭasya kathaṃ bhavet। ghaṭe naṣṭe tu pradeśe asti, tadā tatpradeśāvacchedena muktātmaghaṭasaṃyogo asti। sa naśyati, pradeśāntarāvacchedena anyaḥ saṃyogo jāyate। tathā cānaṣṭe
muktatvaprasaṅga ityāśayāt। duḥkhadhvaṃsavatāmiti। tathā ca suṣuptikāle duḥkhadhvaṃsasattvāt muktatvāpattiḥ। tadvāraṇāya kālīnāntam। adya vidyamānasya asmadīya duḥkhadhvaṃsasya bhāvaḥ। tathā ca duḥkhaprāgabhāve svasamānādhikaraṇeti
tadasamānakālīnaduḥkhadhvaṃsavatvābhāvāt śukādīnāmamuktatvaṃ syāt। tadvāraṇāya svasamānādhikaraṇeti viśeṣaṇam। tadupādāne ca svaṃ pūrvoktadoṣa iti bhāvaḥ। tādṛśaduḥkhaprāgabhāvāsamānakālīneti viśeṣaṇena। na ca asmākaṃ
suṣuptau duḥkhābhāvāt। tathā ca duḥkhāsamānakālīnetyuktau। duḥkhaprāgabhāvāsamānakālīnetyuktau tu duḥkhaprāgabhāvasamānakālīnatvāt vāraṇamiti vācyam। dhvaṃsasya śaṅkate - na ca sbasamānādhikaraṇeti।
yathāsaṃniveśa iti। yadyapi duḥkhāsamānakālīnatvaviśeṣaṇena vāraṇaṃ tasya na vaiyarthyathmati bhāvaḥ। na ca laghunāduḥkhāsamānakālīnatvenaiva vaiyarthyameveti vācyam। yatra gurudharmaghaṭakena laghudharmeṇa nirvāhaḥ tatraiva gurudharmasya vaiyarthyam। prakṛte tu
duḥkhāsamānakālīnatvatvāvacchinnābhāvaḥ duḥkhāsamānakālīnatvam। duḥkhaprāgabhāvāsamānakālīnatvam। anayoścābhāvayoḥ ghaṭakatvābhāvāt na vaiyathyavikāśa ityāśayāt। nanu nānārthakatvāpattiḥ ityata āha - digiti। atrānuyogini svatvaṃ na
vivakṣitam, kiṃ tu pratiyogini। tathā ca tattadvyaktibhedaviśiṣṭaduḥkhadhvaṃso mokṣaḥ। evaṃ ca sakalamuktisādhāraṇatayā na muktipadasya nānārthakatāpattiriti bhāvaḥ। irttha cāpavargasya mokṣe antarbhāvaḥ। saṃśayasya
ityāśayena mūle saṃśayasyākathanam। tadāha - saṃśayasya nirūpitatvāditi। sukhaprāptirnāma sukhameva। duḥkhahāniśca duḥkhadhvaṃsaḥ। tathā ca prayojanasya guṇe abhāve cāntarbhāṃvaḥ। dṛṣṭāntasya yathāyathaṃ dravyaguṇādiṣvantarbhāvaḥ। siddhānto api dravyādirūpa eva।
prāmāṇikatvena svīkṛtārthasyaiva siddhāntatvāt। nirṇayasya jñānarūpe guṇe antarbhāvaḥ। avayavānāṃ śabdarūpatayā prāguktatvāt bhramātmakajñāne antarbhāvaḥ iti tayoḥ atrākathanam। vādajalpavitaṇḍānāṃ śabdarūpatayā guṇe antarbhāvaḥ।
kathā vādaḥ। ubhayasādhanavatī vijigīṣukathā jalpaḥ। svapakṣasthāpanāhīnā aparapakṣavidalanamātrāvasānā vitaṇḍā। kathā nāma nānāvaktṛkapūrvottarapakṣapratipādakavākyasandarbhaḥ। ubhayasādhanavatīti।
parapakṣanirākaraṇasvapakṣasādhanavatī। idaṃ ca vitaṇḍāyāṃ ativyāptivāraṇāyeti dhyeyam। atra vijigīṣu kathetyanuvartate। ekena pūrvapakṣaḥ kriyate, anyena ca vākyasamūhasyāvaseyam।
parapakṣetyādi। vijigīṣukathā jalpaḥ ityetāvanmātroktau vitaṇḍāyāmativyāptiḥ। ataḥ svapakṣasādhanavatītyuktam। parapakṣanirākaraṇasvapakṣasādhanavatītyatra nātivyāptyādivāraṇāya। vijigīṣupadenaiva vādasya vāraṇasambhavāta।
duṣṭaheturūpāṇāṃ hetvābhāsānāṃ yathāyathaṃ dravyādiṣvantarbhāvaḥ। pratyuktasyārthāntaraṃ parikalpya dūṣaṇaṃ chalam। chalamiti। yathā nava kambalāḥ santi ati daridratvāt' ityādi।
śabdarūpatvāt guṇe antarbhavati। asaduttaraṃ jātiḥ। asaduttaramiti। svavyāghātakatvam। tathā ca svavyāghātamuttaraṃ jātiriti lakṣaṇaṃ
paryavasyati। svāsādhakatāsādhāraṇyeneti। paramatāsādhakatvasādhanāya hi jātirūpamuttaramucyate। taccet svamatāsādhakatāmapi sādhayet tadā jātirityarthaḥ। parakīyahetoḥ parāsādhakatve sādhyamāne
jātyuttaramiti bhāvaḥ। tādṛguttaraviśeṣo jātiriti phalitor'thaḥ। anupalabdhi - nitya - anitya - kāryaṃ-akārya-samā jātayāḥ। darśayati - sādharmyetyādinā। dvandvānte śruyamāṇasya samāśabdasya
pratyekaṃ yogaḥ। sādharmyasamā vaidharmyasametyādayaḥ caturviśatiḥ jātayaḥ। sādharmyeṃṇa sthānāhetudūṣakamuttaram sādharmyasamā। yathā eva kiṃ na syāta। na ca atra kiṃñcit vinigamakamasti' iti। sodāharaṇaṃ lakṣaṇamāha - sādharmyeṇeti। vādinā svasādhyasādhanārthaṃ
svasādhyāsādhakatvasādhakamuttaraṃ sādharmyasametyathaiḥ। ākāśavadityapi vaktuṃ śakyatvāt' iti dūṣayati। etādṛśaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ sādharmyasametyarthaḥ। dūṣakamuttaram vaidharmyasamā। yathā tatraiva kriyāvato loṣṭasya
niṣkriya eva kiṃ na syāt। na hi tatsādharmyāt kriyāvatā bhavitavyam, niyāmakamasti iti। svasādhyāsādhakatvakathanaṃ vaidharmyaṃsamā। vibhutvaṃ paramamahatparimāṇavattvam। tathā ca vādinā ātmā kriyāvān
sakriyaloṣṭavidharmatvāt iti prativādī vadati। sakriye loṣṭe niṣkriya eva kuto na syāditi dūṣanaṃ vaidharmyasametyuktaṃ bhavati। tadavyāpakasya dharmasya pakṣe āpādanam utkarṣasamā। yathā śabdo anityaḥ ghaṭavadaśrāvaṇo api syāt' iti।
lakṣaṇamāha - paroktasādhanādeveti। pareṇa svasādhyasādhanāya yo prasañjanaṃ utkarṣasametyarthaḥ। yathā śabdo anityaḥ kṛtakatvādityatra tenaiva hetunā śabdaḥ ghaṭavad aśrāvaṇo api syāditi। atra hetoḥ kṛtakatvasya avyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ aśrāvaṇatvaṃ tasya pakṣe āpādanaṃ kriyate।
īdṛśamuttaraṃ utkarṣasamā।"vyāptimapuraskṛtya utkarṣasamaḥ। yathā śabdo anityaḥ kṛtakatvāt iti sthāpanāyām syāt। evaṃ śrāvaṇaśabdasādharmyāt kṛtakatvāt ghaṭo api śrāvaṇaḥ syādaviśeṣāt"iti viśvanāthaḥ।
abhāvasādhanam apakarṣasamā। yathā tasminneva anumāne ayadi ghaṭavadaśrāvaṇo api syāt' iti। avidyamānadharmaprasañjanaṃ utkarṣaṃsamā। vidyamānadharmābhāvaprasañjanaṃ apakarṣasamā। tadāha - paroktadṛṣṭāntasādharmyeṇeti। pareṇa vādinā
arthāntarasyābhāvasādhanam apakarṣasamā। yathā śabdo anityaḥ hetoḥ śabdaḥ ghaṭavat aśrāvaṇo api syāditi। atra pakṣe śabde kriyate iti samanvayaḥ।"sādhye dharmābhāvaṃ dṛṣṭāntāt prasajato apakarṣasamaḥ"iti bhāṣyam।
sthāpanīyasya dṛṣṭāntadharmasya pakṣe sādhanam varṇyasamā। yathā bhavatu kriyāvattvam। ātmanastu kriyāvattve tajjanakanodanākhyasaṃyogavattvamapi syāt' iti। - varṇyasyeti। dṛṣṭānte vidyamānasya pakṣe sthāpanīyasya sādhanaṃ
varṇyasamā। yathā ātmā kriyāvān kriyāhetuguṇavattvāt kriyājanakanodanākhyasaṃyogavattvāt kriyāvattvaṃ bhavatu। ātmanastu bhavediti। īdṛśamuttaraṃ varṇyasamā।"khyāpanīyo varṇyo viparyayādavarṇyaḥ"iti bhāṣyam।
sādhyahetvordharmayorapi pakṣe tulyatāsādhanam avarṇyasamā। ātmanyasiddham। tathā ca tulyatayā yathā asiddhena kriyāhetuguṇena tajjanakaguṇavattvamapi kimiti na sādhyate niyāmakābhāvāt iti। avarṇyasamāmāha - sādhyahetvoriti। pakṣe
tadavarṇyasamā। yathā ātmā sakriyaḥ kriyāhetuguṇavattvāt loṣṭavat kriyāhetunodanākhyasaṃyogavattvamapyasiddham। tatrāsiddhena sādhyate niyāmakābhāvāt ityevaṃ yaduttaraṃ tadavarṇyasametyarthaḥ। pradarśya dārṣṭāntikavikalpakathanaṃ vikalpasamā। yathā tatraiva anumāne
kiñcidakriyam yathā ātmā। pūrvavikalpo bhavati ayaṃ tu na bhavatītyatra kiṃ nayāmakaṃ syāt' iti। dṛṣṭāntāvikalpaṃ pradarśyeti। dṛṣṭānte vividhaṃ kalpaṃ pradarśya dārṣṭāntike api vividhakalpapradarśanaṃ vikalpasametyarthaḥ। yathā
kiñcidakriyaṃ yathā ātmā। tatra pūrvo vikalpa eva samīcīṃnaḥ ayaṃ tu vikalpaḥ na samīcīnaḥ ityatra niyāmakaṃ kimapi nāsti। tathā ca yaduttaraṃ tat vikalpasamā। pakṣatulyatākathanam sādhyasamā। sādhyaśabdo atra pakṣavācī। yathā tatraiva
tathā loṣṭaḥ' ityapyāyātam। tathā ca yadyātmani kriyāvattvaṃ sādhyate ātmeti na vācyam। aloṣṭasadṛśa ātmā, nātmasadṛśo niyāmakābhāvāt iti। dṛṣṭāntasya pakṣatulyatākathanamiti। sādhyate asminniti vyutpattyā
sādhyaśabdaḥ pakṣavācī। dṛṣṭāntaḥ pakṣatulya ityāpādanaṃ sādhyasamā। śiṣṭaṃ spaṣṭam।"hetvādyavayavasāmarthyayogī dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tra dṛṣṭānte prasajataḥ sādhyasamaḥ। yadi yathā loṣṭaḥ tathā ātmā, prāptastarhi yathā ātmā tathā loṣṭa iti। sādhyaścāyamātmā
kriyāvāniti kāmaṃ loṣṭo api sādhyaḥ। atha naivam, na tarhi yathā loṣṭaḥ tathā ātmā"iti bhāṣyam। pratyavasthānam prāptisamā। prāptiśca sādhyahetvoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam। yathā tatraiva kriyāhetuguṇavattvenaiva kimiti
ubhayoraviśeṣāt iti। prāptyā pratyavasthānamiti। sādhyena saha ekādhikaraṇavṛttitvaṃ sādhyasyāpyastītyaṅgīkaraṇīyam। tathā ca sādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ puraskṛtya sādhyenaiva hetuḥ sādhyatām। evaṃ ca ātmā kriyāvān
prāptisametyarthaḥ। ubhayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāviśeṣādityarthaḥ। pratyavasthānam aprāptisamā। yathā tatraiva pūrvoktadoṣādaprāptasya sarvaṃ sādhayet iti। ayameva hetuḥ sādhyābhāvaṃ kimiti na
sādhayet। sādhyameva tu sādhayedityatra vinigamakābhāvāt iti। aprāptyā pratyavasthānamiti। aprāptiḥ sādhyahetvoḥ asāmānādhikaraṇyam। atraivaṃ vikalpaḥ kartavyaḥ। ātmā kriyāvān sādhyata iti pratyavasthānāt prāptisamā। dvitīye
na sādhayet। tathā ca sarvaḥ sarvaṃ sādhayet। tathā heturyathā aprāptisametyarthaḥ। sādhanaparamparāpraśnaḥ prasaṅgasamā। yathā kriyāvattve kriyāhetuguṇavattvaṃ sādhanam। tatra kiṃ sādhanam? na hi sādhanaṃ vinā
kasyacit siddhirasti। evaṃ tatrāpi kiṃ sādhanamityādi। lakṣayati - sādhanaparamparāpraśna iti। sādhanaparamparā viṣayakaḥ praśnaḥ prasaṅgasamā।"sādhanasyāpi sādhanaṃ vaktavyamiti prasaṅgena pratyavasthānaṃ prasaṅgasamaḥ"iti bhāṣyam। śiṣṭaṃ
spaṣṭam। sādhyābhāvasādhanam pratidṛṣṭāntasamā। yathā atatraiva loṣṭadṛṣṭāntena kiṃ na syāt। loṣṭadṛṣṭāntena kriyāvattvaṃ ākāśadṛṣṭāntena niyāmakābhāvāt' iti।
pratidṛṣṭāntasamāmāha - dṛṣṭāntāntareṇeti। ātmā kriyāvān dūṣaṇodbhāvanaṃ pratidṛṣṭāntasamā।"kriyāvān ātmā kriyāhetuguṇayuktaṃ ākāśaṃ niṣkriyaṃ dṛṣṭathmati। kaḥ punarākāśasyaṃ kriyāhetuguṇaḥ, vāyunā saṃyogaḥ"iti bhāṣyam।
pratyavasthānam anutpattisamā। yathā aghaṭo na nityaḥ janyaikātvāt' ekatvotpatteḥ pūrvaṃ tadabhāvāt nityatvam। nityaścet tarhi anutpanna eveti। anutpattyā pratyavasthānamiti। janyaṃ ca tat ekatvaṃ ca
janyaikatvam, tasmāt। tathā ca anityatvaṃ bādhitāmiti bhāvaḥ।"tathā ca sādhanāṅgapakṣahetudṛṣṭāntānāṃ utpatteḥ prāk hetvabhāva ityanutpattyā pratyavasthānaṃ anutpattisamaḥ। viśvanārthaḥ।
pradarśyaṃ saṃśayodbhāvanaṃ saṃśayasamā। yathā aśabdo anityaḥ sādharmyaṃ astīti ubhayasādharmyadarśanāt saṃśayaḥ syāt। ekapariśeṣe niyāmakābhāvāt' iti। sādhāraṇadharmaṃ pradarśyeti।"nityānityasādharmyāditi
saṃśayakāraṇopalakṣaṇam। tena samānadharmadarśanādi viśvanāthaḥ। sādhyaviparītasādhakahetvantarodbhāvanam prakaraṇasamā। satpratipakṣodāharaṇameva atrodāharaṇaṃ bodhyam।
vādyaktahetoriti। śabdaḥ anityaḥ kṛtakatvāt ghaṭavat iti vādinā pratyavasthānaṃ prakaraṇasametyarthaḥ। hetutvāsambhavena ahetutvakathanam ahetusamā। yathā tadānityatvarūpasādhyasya tadānīmabhāvāt kasya sādhakam। atha
sādhyamanityatvam। yadi ca ubhayaṃ ekakālavṛtti tadā kiṃ kasya sādhanaṃ kiṃ kasya sādhyam। vinigamakābhāvāditi। hetusameti pāṭhe tu kālatraye api hetutvasya asambhavakathanaṃ hetusametyarthaḥ। lakṣayati - kālatraye apīti। kālatraye api hetutvāsambhavakathanapūrvakaṃ
ahetutvakathanam ahetusamā। kasya sādhakamiti। anityatvasya kāryatvaṃ na sādhakamityarthaḥ। pūrvakālāvacchedena iti bhāvaḥ। kasya sādhyamanityatvamiti। anityatvaṃ kāryatvasya sādhyaṃ
na bhavatītyarthaḥ। kālatrayaśabdena kāryakālatatpūrvakālatatpaścātkālāḥ vivakṣitāḥ।"heturahetunā na viśiṣṭayate। ahetunā sādharmyāt pratyavasthānam ahetusamaḥ"iti bhāṣyam। arthāpattipuraskāreṇa sādhyābhāvodbhāvanam arthāpattisamā।
niyāmakābhāvāt"iti। lakṣayati - arthāpattipuraskāreṇeti। śabdaḥ anityaḥ kṛtakatvāt iti arthādāpadyate nityasādharmyāt nitya iti। asti ca nityena ākāśena arthāpattisametyarthaḥ।"arthāpattyā pratipakṣaṃ sādhayataḥ
arthāpattisamaḥ। yadi prāyatnānantarīyakatvāt anityasādharmyāt anityaḥ śabda iti, tadā arthādāpadyate nityasādharmyāt nitya iti। asti tvasya nityena sādharmyaṃ asparśatvam"iti bhāṣyam। ekatarāvadhāraṇa iti। anityasādharmyādanityatvamevetyavadhāraṇa
ityarthaḥ। sarvāviśeṣaprasaṅgodbhāvanam aviśeṣasamā। yathā tatraiva prameyatvādirūpeṇa tatsādharmyeṇa sarvasyaivānityatvaṃ syāt। iti।
lakṣayati - sarvāviśeṣaprasaṅgodbhāvanamiti। śabdo anityaḥ sarveṃṣāmaviśeṣaprasaṅgaḥ। sattvaprameyatvādirūpasya ekasya dharmasya sarveṣu sattvāt। tathā ca sanmātravṛttidharmeṇāviśeṣāpādanamaviśeṣasamā। tathā ca sarveṣāmabhede
pakṣādivibhāgo na syāt। sarveṣāmekajātīyatve avāntarajātyucchedaḥ, sarveṣāmanityatve jātyādivilaya iti viśvanāthaḥ nirūpayati। sādhanopapattikathanam upapattisamā। yathā ayadi anityatvasādhanaṃ kiñcidupapadyata iti nityatvaṃ kiṃ na syāt' iti।
lakṣayati - ubhayapakṣasādharmyeṇeti। dvayorapi pakṣayoḥ sādhanamupapadyata iti kathanam upapattisamā। śabdasya anityatvapakṣe yathā sādhane upapattisameti yāvat। upalabdhisamā। yathā śabdo anityaḥ prayatnānuvidhāyitvāt ghaṭavat
prayatnānuvidhāyitvaṃ śabde asti iti। sodāharaṇaṃ lakṣayati - vādyakteti। vādinā nirdiṣṭasya kāraṇasyābhāve api sādhyopalambhāt pratyavasthānam upalabdhisamaḥ। tathā ucyate, na tatsambhavati, dhūmaṃ vinā ālokādito api vahnisiddheḥ।
tathā ca na tasya sādhakatvamiti pratikūlatarkaḥ iti viśvanāthaḥ। anupalabdhisamā। yathā - ajalādeḥ vidyamānasyāpi āvaraṇavaśāt śabdādyāvaraṇamapyupalabhyeteti। atrottaram-yadi bhavadbhiḥ āvaraṇasiddhiḥ' iti।
lakṣayati - vādineti। naiyāyikaistāvat śabdānityatvaṃ evaṃ sādhyate nopalabhyate। na hi ghaṭādyāvaraṇakuḍyādivat śabdasyāvaraṇamasti, tadanupalabdheriti। tatraivaṃ jātivādī sidhyet। tathā ca anupalabdhipramāṇakaḥ āvaraṇābhāvo na syāt api tu
āvaraṇopapattireva syāditi śabdanityatve noktaṃ bādhakaṃ yuktamiti। viśvanāthaḥ। nityatvānityatvavikalpāt dharmiṇo nityatvasādhanam nityasamā। yathā aśabdasya yat anityatvaṃ bhavadbhiḥ ucyate tat nityaṃ anityaṃ vā।
tathātvamāgatam। atha anityaṃ tadā śabde kadācit nityatvam' iti। - dharmasyeti। śabdasyāpi tathātvamāgatamiti। śabdasyāpi nityatvaṃ prasaktamityarthaḥ। dharmiṇaṃ vinā dharmasya sthityabhāvena dharmasyānityatvasya
nityatve sadātanatve dharmī śabdo api nityaḥ syāditi bhāvaḥ। śabde syādityāpādanaṃ nityasamā iti viśvanārthaḥ। anityasamā। yathā ayadi anityena ghaṭane sādṛśyāt śabdaḥ anityaḥ sarvasyānityatvaprasaṅgaḥ' iti।
lakṣayati - anityadṛṣṭānteti। anityena ghaṭena sādharmyāt anityatvamaniṣṭaṃ sampadyate। so ayaṃ anityatvena pratyavasthānāt anityasama iti bhāṣyam। vyāptimapuraskṛtya anityasamā। sādhyapadādaviśeṣasamāto vyavacchedaḥ tatra sarvāviśeṣa
evāpadyate na tu sarvasya sādhyavattvam iti viśvanārthaḥ। anyakoryeṇāpi sambhavābhidhānaṃ kāryaṃsamā। yathā tatraiva prayatnānuvidhāyitvadarśanāt। tathā ca tasya iti। kvacit kāraṇasameti pāṭhaḥ। tasyāpi akāraṇasya
samatvābhidhānam' iti rītyā ukta evārthe paryavasānamavaseyam। atra te anusandheyāḥ। - vādyuktahetoriti। yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ prayatnānuvidhāyitvāt āvarakanivṛttau ceti। tatra svarūpotpattyabhiprāyeṇa vādinokte
na svarūpotpattāviti śabdasyānityatvaṃ na sidhyatīti। evaṃrītyā pratyavasthānaṃ kāryasametyarthaḥ। pulliṅgatayā prayujyate। tatra jāterviśeṣyatvavivakṣāyāṃ samaśabdasya strīliṅgatvam। nyāyasūtrakārastu-'sādharmyavaidharmyasamau'
ityādirūpeṇa pulliṅgatayaiva nirdiśati। tasyāyaṃ bhāvaḥ - vādyaktasya iti tadanurodhena samaśabdasya pulliṅgeteti। taduktaṃ ityuktarūpajātiviśeṣābhiprāya ityāhuḥ"iti। nyāyabhāṣyakārādayo apīti pratiṣedhaśabdasya sūtre pulliṅganirvāhaṃ manyante। viśvanāthanyāyapañcānanastu
asādharmyasamādayo jātivikalpāḥ। vividhaḥ kalpaḥ vikalpaḥ prabhedaḥ' nirvahati। evaṃ vādinā sādhane kriyāmāṇe tatra prativādinā udbhāvyamānaḥ asaduttaraviśeṣaḥ jātiḥ। tasya jātiśabdavācyatā jāyamānatvanibandhanā। tathā ca"sādharmyavaidharmyābhyām
pratyavasthānam jātiḥ"iti। kathāyāṃ pravṛttayoḥ uttamūruvīrarāghavācāryasvāminaḥ nirūpayanti। te eva svāminaḥ sāmyaṃ ca samaśabdena lakṣyate। sūtre samaśabdaḥ pratiṣedharūpahetuviśeṣaṇībhūtaḥ hetugataṃ sāmyaṃ darśayati। athāpi
vaktṛgatasāmyamapi vivakṣitam। tadāha vārtikakāraḥ -"samīkaraṇārthaṃ prayogasamaḥ। sādharmyameva samaṃ tasya prayogasya sa sādharmyasamaḥ"iti। atra samīkaraṇārthamityanena vastutaḥ sāmyābhāve api samīkaraṇoddheśo jñāpyate। na hi saddhetorasaddhetunā nirākaraṇaṃ sāmyāpādanaṃ vā bhavati। kena kasya samīkaraṇamiti cet
- vādinā prativādinaḥ samīkaraṇam। tathā ca prativādinā ityuktaṃ bhavati। deśikacaraṇāstu nyāyapariśuddhau jātiprayogaḥ kriyata ityuktaṃ bhavati। deśikacaraṇāstu nyāyapariśuddhau tadeva sāmyaṃ samaśabdena pratipādyata iti nirvahanti।
sthūladṛṣṭyā pratīyate। tataḥ nāmabhedamātramiti śaṅkā avatarati। tatrāpi sūṣmadṛṣṭyā vicāryaṃmāṇe lakṣaṇeṣu bhado avagantuṃśakyate। tadetanmanasi nidhāyāha - atra granthagauravabhayāt sūkṣmaprakārāḥ na darśitāḥ iti। kiṃ ca āsāṃ saviśeṣametadakhilaṃ pravyaktamuktaṃ rahaḥ"।।
pratipāditam। tatra prativādinā yat asaduttaramucyate tadeva lakṣyam। tasya sādharmyaṃsamādiṣu yatrānatarbhāvaḥ tallakṣaṇameva lakṣaṇam। utthitirnāma janma। sthiteḥ padaṃ sthitipadaṃ jātyuttarasthiteḥ āśrayaḥ। sthitipadatvena vivakṣitaḥ। īdṛśajātiprayogasya mūlaṃ
sādharmyādyākārakadarśanam। phalaṃ tu vādinaḥ svoktahetau prativādinā duṣṭatvabhramotpādanam। śātanaṃ vādinā prativādyuktasyāsaduttarasya jātirūpasya nirākaraṇam। sūtrakārastu jātyuttarasya nirākaraṇaprakāraṃ pratijāti viśadaṃ pratipāditavān। saptāṅgakatvaṃ
tu nyāyapariśiṣṭe tatra tatra sūcitameva। sarvamidaṃ vistarabhayāt atropekṣitamiti bhāvaḥ। apajayahetuḥ nigrahasthānam। lakṣayati - vādina iti। idaṃ ca yadyapi chalādāvapyasti
tathāpyarthāntarādirūpanigrahasthānamadhye antarbhāvāt adoṣaḥ। hetvābhāsavat। apasiddhāntaḥ, hetvābhāsāśca nigrahasthānāni। tasyāvāntarabhedān daśayati pratijñetyādinā। yatra
pratijñāhāniḥ। yathā aśabdo anityaḥ pratyakṣaguṇatvāt' ityatra anityatvapratijñāṃ jahāti। lakṣayati - yatra pratijñātārtheti। pratijñātasya sādhyasya yat viruddhaṃ tadaṅgīkāraḥ pratijñātasya sādhyasya tyāgo vā pratijñāhāniḥ। idaṃ
svadṛṣṭānte abhyanujānan pratijñāṃ jahātīti pratijñāhāniḥ"ityādi bhāṣyānusāri lakṣaṇam। viśvanāthastu -"svapakṣeparapakṣadharmābhyanujñā pratijñāhāniḥ। svayaṃ viśiṣyābhihitaparityāga iti phalitārthaḥ। seyaṃ pakṣahetudṛṣṭāntasādhyatadanyahānibhedāt pañcadhā bhāvati। yathā śabdaḥ iti। evaṃ tatraiva śabdo anityaḥ aindriyakatvāt ityukte
hetoranaikāntikatvamiti pratyukte astu kṛtakatvāditi heturiti। sādhanavikala iti pratyukte astu tarhi mahānasaviditi। evaṃ atraiva siddhasādhanena pratyukte astu tarhiṃ indhanavāniti। anyahānistu hetoriti"ityāha। tadanusāreṇa dinakaryām -
proktam। pratijñātārthakathanam pratijñāntaram। yathā kṣityādikaṃ guṇajanyam asaviṣayaka' iti guṇaviśeṣaṇadānam। lakṣayati - parokteti। guṇaviśeṣaṇadānamiti। saviṣayakaguṇajanyatvaṃ
sādhyam। adṛṣṭasya tu saviṣayakatvābhāvāt tajjanyatvamādāya na siddhasādhanamiti bhāvaḥ। apratijñātārthasyetyupalakṣaṇam। hetvatiriktārthaṃsyeti tattvam। tena udāharaṇāntaram, upanayāntaram, viśvanāthaḥ। hetvantaraṃ tu sūtrakāreṇa pṛthaṅnigrahasthānatvena
nirdiṣṭam। svoktasādhyaviruddhahetukathanam pratijñāvirodhaḥ। yathā - dravyaṃ guṇabhinnam rūpāditaḥ pṛthaktvena anupalabhyamānatvāt iti। lakṣayati - svoktasādhyeti। rūpāditaḥ pṛthaktvena anupalabhyamānatvaṃ hi
guṇābhinnatvavyāpyam, na guṇabhinnatvasādhakam। ato guṇabhinnatvābhāvavyāptasya hetoḥ kathanāt pratijñāvirodha ityarthaḥ। dūṣite tadapalāpaḥ pratijñāsannyāsaḥ। yathā aśabdo anityaḥ dūṣite svoktamapalapati akenocyate śabdo anityaḥ' iti।
lakṣayati svokter'the iti। pratijñāhānau pratijñātārthasya tyāgaḥ pratijñāsannyāse tu tasyāpalāpa iti bhedaḥ। viśeṣaṇāntaropādānam hetvantaram। yathā aśabdo anityaḥ sati' iti viśeṣaṇadānam।
- parokteti। paroktadūṣaṇoddidhīrṣayā hetvantaramityarthaḥ। jātimattve satīti viśeṣaṇe datte tu sāmānye jātimattvābhāvāt na vyabhicāraḥ। prakṛtānupayuktārthakathanam arthāntaram।
yathā-nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavattvāt iti hetuḥ। hetupadaṃ ca hinotestunipratyaye niṣpannam; padaṃ ca suptiṅantam ityādi। - prakṛtānupayukteti। prakṛtānākāṅkṣitārthābhidhānamityarthaḥ। avācakaśabdaprayogo nirarthakam। yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ
jabagaḍadaśatvāt ityādi। pariṣatprativādyabodhaprayojakapadaprayogaḥ avijñātārtham। tacca akliṣṭānvayaṃ aprasiddhārthakaṃ tvaritoccāritam' ityādirūpam। lakṣayati - pariṣaditi। vādināṃ trivāramuktamapiprativādinā
sadasyaiśca yanna budhyate tat avijñātārtham। janakavācakavākyaprayogo avijñātārtham। vācaketyanena nirarthakāpārthaṅkavyudāsaḥ' iti viśvanārthaḥ। tādṛśaṃ vākyaṃ abhūstanaṃ himabheṣajavat' ityādikam। bhūstanamityasya parvata ityarthaṃḥ।
himasya bheṣajam agniḥ tadvān iti himabheṣajavadityasthārthaḥ। aagnirhimasya bheṣajam' iti śruteḥ। parasparānanvitapadasamūhaḥ apārthakam। yathā-śabdatvaṃ ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ nityaṃ anityaṃ ca prameyatvāt ityādi।
paraspareti। abhimatavākyārthabodhānukūlākāṅkṣāśūnyapadasamūhaḥ apārthakamityarthaḥ। vyutkrameṇa kathanam aprāptakālam। yathā śabdatvāt śabdaḥ anityaḥ ityādi।
lakṣayati - avayavānāmiti।"pratijñādīnāṃ avayavānāṃ yathālakṣaṇaṃ arthavaśāt kramaḥ। tatrāvayavaviparyāsena vacanaṃ aprāptakālam"iti bhāṣyānusārīdaṃ lakṣaṇam। viśvanāthastu-avayavasya kathaikadeśasya viparyāsaḥ vaiparītyam। tathā ca
samayabandhaviṣayībhūtakathākramaviparītakrameṇābhidhānaṃ paryavasannam। pādaḥ। jayaparājayavyavasthā caturthaḥ pādaḥ। evaṃ pratijñāhetvādīnāṃ kramaḥ। tatra sabhākṣobhavyāmohādinā vyatyastābhidhānaṃ aprāptakālam' iti pratipādayati।
yatkiñcidavayavaśūnyāvayavābhidhānam nyūnam। adhikahetvādikathanam adhikam। yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabdatvāt śrāvaṇatvācca ityādi। kathitasya punaḥ kathanam punaruktam। yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ, śabdaḥ
anityaḥ ityādi। punaruktaṃ lakṣayati - anuvādaṃ vineti। niṣprayojanaṃ punarabhidhānaṃ punaruktam। anuvādastu vyakhyārūpaḥ saprayojanakaḥ। ato na tatrātivyāptiḥ। tathā ca
śabdapunaruktam। yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ anitya iti। abhidhānamarthapunaruktam। yathā śabdaḥ anityaḥ dhvanirnirodhadharmaka iti। trirabhihitasyāpi ananuvādaḥ ananubhāṣaṇam।
lakṣayati pariṣadeti। vādinā triruktasya pariṣadā vijñātārthasya ananubhāṣaṇam। ajñānasāṅkaryanirāsāya ajñānamanāviṣkurvateti ityācāryāḥ। na ca apratibhāsāṅkaryam, uttarapratipattāvapi sabhākṣobhādinā ananubhāṣaṇasambhavāditi viśvanāthaḥ।
buddhvāpi uttarasya asphūrtivaśāt tūṣṇīṃbhāvaḥ apratibhā। uttarārhamiti। na cātra ananubhāṣaṇasyāvaśyakatvāt tadeva dūṣaṇamastviti vācyam। paroktānanuvāde hi tat। apratibhāyāṃ tu paroktānuvāde api uttarāpratipattiriti viśeṣāt।
vikṣepaḥ। asambhavaditi। kālāntare kartuṃ śakyaṃ vastuta idānīṃ bhavitumanarhaṃ yat kāryaṃ tatra vyāsaṅgamudbhāvya kathāvicchedo vikṣepaḥ। tena vāstavaśirorogādinā pratibandhe vā na vikṣepaḥ। ayatra kartavyaṃ
paścāt kathayāmīti vikṣepo nāma nigrahasthānam' iti bhāṣyam। doṣamanuddhṛtya parapakṣe doṣābhidhānam matānujñā। - svapakṣa iti। svasiddhānte paroktaṃ doṣamaṅgīkṛtyānuddhṛtya ca parasiddhānte api samāno doṣa ityudbhāvanaṃ matānujñetyarthaḥ।
yathā-puruṣatvāccedahaṃ coraḥ tata eva bhavānapi cora ityādikam। paryanuyojyopekṣaṇam। paryanuyojyopekṣaṇaṃ lakṣayati - udbhāvanārheti। nigrahasthānaṃ prāpto asītyananuyogaḥ। etacca kasya parājaya
ityanuyuktayā pariṣadā vacanīyam। na khalu nigrahaṃ prāptaḥ svakaupīnaṃ vivṛṇuyāt' iti bhāṣyam। cet-satyam। madhyasthenaiva idamudbhāvyam, vāde ca svayamudbhāvane apyadoṣaḥ' iti viśvanāthaḥ।
grantheṣu vedāntadeśikakṛtanyāyapariśuddhau ca bahuvivecitamasti। tatsarvaṃ sāvadhānaṃ parāmṛśya kaścinmahānprabandhaḥ pṛthageva lekhanīyaḥ। prakaraṇagranthe etāvadeva paryāptamiti vistarabhayāduparamyate। nigrahasthānodbhāvanam niranuyojyānuyogaḥ।
tadviruddhasiddhāntamatamālambyottaradānam upasiddhāntaḥ। dravyādiṣu antarbhāvaḥ yathāyathaṃ bodhyaḥ। atiriktaḥ sūtrārthaḥ sugama ityabhiprāyeṇāha - śeṣamiti। pratijñāhānītyādinā। dinakarīgranthe pratijñāhānyādīnāṃ
tata evāvaseyaḥ। asaduttararūpajāteḥ guṇe antarbhāvaḥ। padārthāntaramiti cet - na। pratibandhakābhāvasya kāryamātre kāraṇatvena śakteranupayogāt। kāraṇatvasyaiva śaktipadārthatvāt।
pratibandhakatā vācyā। sā ca vahnau dāhānukūlaśaktisvīkāra eva nirvahati। pratibandhakatāyāḥ kāryāṃnukūlaśaktivighaṭakatvarūpatvāt। ityasaṅgatamiti prābhākaraḥ śaṅkate - nanviti। nanvevaṃ śaktisiddhāvapi tasyā atiriktatvāsiddhiriti cet - na। yato na
tāvaddravyātmikā śaktiḥ guṇādivṛttitvāt। vināśaśālitvāt। evaṃ cātiriktapadārthatvasiddhiriti। nanu kāraṇībhūtābhāvapratiyogitvam। tacca maṇyabhāvasya hetutvādeva dāhānutpattisambhavaḥ। itthaṃ cātiriktaśaktisvīkāro anucita iti
samādhatte - pratibandhakābhāvasyeti। nanu adāhotpāde vahniḥ śaktaḥ' - kāraṇatvasyeti। nanu maṇyādyabhāvasya hetutve maṇisamavadhānadaśāyāṃ satyapyuttejake dāho na syāt। manmate tu maṇyādyapasāraṇadaśāyāmiva aṅgīkāreṇa na doṣa iti cet - na।
uttejakābhāvaviśiṣṭamaṇyādyabhāvasya kāraṇatvāṅgīkāreṇa adoṣāt। na kalpanīyatayā gauravamiti vācyam। dāhānukūlaśakti prati anantaśaktitatprāgabhāvataddhvaṃsakalpane gauravāditi saṅkṣepaḥ। iti śaktiḥ padārthāntaram। ityāśaṅkitaṃ dīpikāyām। tatra
nanvanalaṃsayoge satyapīti। karatalasya analasaṃyoge satyapi maṇyādisattve karatalasya dāho na jāyate maṇyādyasattve dāho jāyate। maṇyādeḥ dāhapratibandhakatvaṃ vācyam। pratibandhakatvaṃ ca kāryānukūlaśaktivighaṭakatvam। tathā ca dāhānukūlā yā agniniṣṭhā
śaktiḥ sā maṇinā nāśyate। ataḥ śaktiviśiṣṭavahnereva dāhajanakatvāt dāhaḥ। itthaṃ ca kāryānukūlaśaktivighaṭakatvāt vinā nopapadyata padārthā ityuktiḥ saṅgacchata iti śaṅkiturbhāvaḥ। nanvevamiti।
saptapadārthātiriktatvaṃ kathamityarthaḥ। yato na tāvat dravyātmiketyādi। śaktiḥ dravyabhinnā guṇādivṛttitvāt guṇatvādivat। śaktirhi rūpādiguṇeṣu kriyādau cāsti। tadanukūlaśaktimattvāt śakteḥ kriyāvṛttitvācca। tathā ca
dravyamityarthaḥ। guṇādivṛttitvādevetyarthaḥ। śaktiḥ guṇakarmānyatarabhinnā guṇādivṛttitvāt guṇatvādivat। syādityālocya anyatarabhedasya sādhyatvamanusṛtam। yatra guṇabhedaḥ karmabhedaśca ubhayamasti tatraiva guṇakarmānyatarabhedaḥ saṃbhavatīti bhāvaḥ।
sāmānyādyanyatamarūpeti। śaktiḥ sāmānyādyanyatamabhinne utpattivināśaśālitvāt ghaṭādivat। utpattimattvamātrasya hetutvaṃ sāmānyādyanyatamabhedābhāvavati dhvaṃse utpattimattvasattvāt vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya vināśaśālitvāditi। dhvaṃsasya vināśābhāvāt na
vyabhicāraḥ। vināśāśālitvāmātroktau uktasādhyābhāvavati prāgabhāve vināśitvasattvāt vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya utpattiniveśaḥ। prāgabhāvasyānādeḥ utpattivirāhat na vyabhicāraḥ। tathā ca utpattivināśobhayavattvaṃ utpattiviśiṣṭavināśavattvaṃ vā hetuḥ।
sāmānyādītyatra ādiśabdena viśeṣasamavāyābhāsava gṛhyata। pariśeṣānumānena śakteratiriktapadārthatvaṃ sidhyatīti bhāvaḥ। iti dīpikāgranthaḥ śakteḥ padārthatvakhaṇḍanāya pravṛttaḥ। kāryamātre pratibandhakābhāvasya kāraṇatvamastu nāma। tāvatā śakteḥ padārthatvaṃ
tātparyamāha-pratibandhakatvaṃ neti। pratibandhakatvaṃ cetyarthaḥ। maṇyabhāvasya hetutvādeveti। evakāreṇa kāryānukūlaśaktivighaṭakatvavyavacchedaḥ। tathā ca maṇeḥ tatpratiyogitvāt pratibandhakatvamupapadyate। tathā ca
anyathānupapattirūpārthāpattipramāṇasyābhāvāt na śaktisiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। tadabhāvarūpakāraṇāntarābhāvādeveti। maṇyabhāvarūpaṃ yat kāraṇāntaraṃ tadabhāvādevetyarthaḥ। atra antaraśabdaprayogāt dāhaṃ prati vahniḥ maṇyabhāvaviśiṣṭavahniḥ kāraṇam। vahniviśiṣṭamaṇyabhāvaḥ kāraṇaṃ vā
sūcitam। kāraṇatārūpatve apīti। nanu kāraṇatvaṃ kathaṃ nātiriktaṃ iti cet - atrāhuḥ। kāraṇatvamiti āgnitvā udijātau vā abhāva vā kāraṇatvasyāntarbhāva iti। spaṣṭamidaṃ kusumāñjalādau।
maṇyādyabhāvasya hetutva iti। candrakāntamaṇiḥ dāhapratibandhakaḥ tadabhāvaḥ dāhahetuḥ। yatra vahnau candrakāntamaṇisaṃyogakāle jāyate। tatra candrakāntamaṇyabhāvarūpasya kāraṇasyābhāvāt tava mate kathaṃ dāhaḥ? mama mate tu maṇyabhāvaḥ na dāhakāraṇam। api tu
śaktiviśiṣṭavahnireva kāraṇam। candrakāntamaṇinā aṅgīkaraṇīyeti śaṅkiturbhāvaḥ। atra uttejakaśabdena pratibandhakasattve api kāryotpattiprayojakaḥ sūryakāntamaṇyādirucyate। bhavati।
uttejakābhāvaviśiṣṭeti। yatra maṇiḥ uttejakaṃ ca vartate tatra dāhotpattirūpapadyata iti śakteranupayoga iti bhāvaḥ। ananugatatvāditi। gauravamiti। anekeṣāṃ uttejakābhāvānāṃ kāraṇatāvacchedakakukṣau praveśāditi bhāvaḥ।
dāhānukūlaśaktiṃ pratīti। maṇisattve uttejakābhāvaviśiṣṭamaṇyabhāvaḥ śaktiṃ prati kāraṇamiti vācyam। tatprāgabhāvataddhvaṃsādīnāṃ ca kalpaneneti bhāvaḥ। nanu taduttejakābhāvaviśiṣṭamaṇisattvāt dāhānutpādaprasaṅgaḥ। kiṃ ca
dāhotpattiprasaṅgaśca ityata āhasaṅkṣepa iti। pūrvoktadoṣau vāraṇīyau iti bhāvaḥ। sahajaśaktirniṃrākṛtā। kāṃsyādau śuddhidarśanāt ādheyaśaktiḥ aṅgīkāryā iti cet - na।
śuddhipadārthatvāt। śaktimatkāṃsyādereva tadarhatvāt। aspṛśyasparśeṃ sati śakternāśāt bhasmasaṃyoge tu punaḥ śakterutpādāt tadarhatā। evaṃ ca kāṃsyādau ādheyaśaktiḥ svīkāryā। na ca kāṃsyādau bhojanādikaṃ prati
iti vācyam। prakṛte ca aspṛśyasparśasya asaṃspṛśyasaṃyogarūpatayā nanu bhasmādineti। prathamenādipadena amlādeḥ dvitīyena ca tāmrādeḥ parigrahaḥ। kḷptadhvaṃsaviśeṣeṇaiva kāṃsyādeḥ śuddhatvopapattau bhasmādisaṃyogeti। yatra kāṃsyādau bhasmādisaṃyogadhvaṃsānantaraṃ
śuddhyāpattiḥ ataḥ sahitāntaṃ dhvaṃsaviśeṣaṇam। sāhityaṃ cātra ityataḥ yāvaditi। tathā ca tatra yāvatāṃ aspṛśyasparśābhāvānāṃ niravacchinnaviśeṣaṇatāsambandhena asattvāt noktadoṣa iti bhāvaḥ। kālīnāntamabhāvaviśeṣaṇam। tathā ca tava
iti bhāvaḥ। bhasmādinā' ityādinā dīpikāyām। sahajaśaktiḥ ādheyaśaktiśceti śaktidvayasya mīmāṃsakairaṅgīkārāt। prathamenādipadenāmlāderiti। kāṃsyaṃ tāmramāmlena śudhyati।
bhūmiḥ nārī tu rajasā tathā।।' vacanamatrānusaṃhitam। dīpikāyām bhasmādisaṃyogeti। bhasmādisaṃyogadhvaṃsa eva kāṃsyādeḥ śuddhirityarthaḥ। yatra kāṃsyādau bhasmādisaṃyoganāśānantaraṃ punaraspṛśyavasatusparśaḥ। tatkāle
śuddhipadārthatve tadānīmapi śuddhatvāpattiḥ। tadvāraṇāya bhasmādisaṃyogadhvaṃse viśeṣaṇam। aspṛśyasparśakāle aspṛśyasparśapatiyogikābhāvaviśiṣṭatvaṃ nāstīti na doṣaḥ। sāhityaṃ ca atra svarūpasaṃbandhaghaṭitasāmānādhikaraṇyarūpam। ataḥ
na bhavati। kāṃsyādau yatkiñcidaspṛśyavastusparśakāle api pūrvatanabhasmādisaṃyogadhvaṃso astīti śuddhatvāpattiḥ। ataḥ yāvattvaniveśaḥ। tadānīṃ yāvadabhāvāntargatasya yādṛśāspṛśyavastusparśo asti tadabhāvasya asattvāt na doṣaḥ। na
niveśyatāmiti vācyam। vijātīyeṣvanekeṣu sāmānyadharmasyātrāsambhavāt। saṃyogasyāvyāpyavṛttitayā niravacchinnadaiśikaviśeṣaṇatāsambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśyam। yatra bhasmādisaṃyogasamānakālīnatvaviśeṣaṇam।
vidyamāna iti tadarthaḥ। evaṃ ca tatra vidyamānasya aspṛśyasparśābhāvasya vidyamānatvaṃ nāstīti na doṣaḥ। evaṃ ca bhasmādisaṃyogadhvaṃsa śuddhiriti phalitam। tadāha - yatra kāṃsyādāvityādinā। saṃbandhaviśeṣaniyantritamiti।
niravacchinnadaiśikāviśeṣaṇa tāsambandhaghaṭitamityarthaḥ। padārthāntaram, yatheṣṭaviniyogayogyatvasya svatvarūpatvāt। tadavacchedakaṃ ca pratigrahādilabdhatvameveti। mataṃ nirasyati - svatvamapīti। apinā anuktasamuccānayakena
pratiyogitvādiparigrahaḥ। nanu tarhi svatvaṃ kiṃsvarūpam ityata āha - yatheṣṭeti। tadavacchedakaṃ ceti। tādṛśayogyatvaprayojakamityarthaḥ। bahutaramūhanīyam। iti। tatpadārthantaramiti। svatvaṃ na dravyātmakam
guṇādivṛttitvāt। ata eva na guṇakarmānyatarātmakam। na ca sāmānyādirūpam, nityatvaprasaṅgāt। mama svatvaṃ utpannam, tava iṣṭāpatteḥ kartumaśakyatvāt। nāpyabhāvātmakam, bhāvatvena pratīyamānatvāt। ataḥ kḷptapadārthānantarbhūtatvāt svatvaṃ
padārthāntaramiti pūrvapakṣaḥ। yatheṣṭaviniyogayogyatāniyāmakaṃ pratigrahādinā labdhatvameva svatvam। tacca saṃyogādirūpam, nātiriktapadārtha iti siddhāntaḥ। prayatnajanakacikīrṣājanakajñānaviṣayo vidhiḥ। tatpratipādakaḥ
liṅādirvā। kṛtyasādhye pravṛttyadarśanāt-kṛtisādhye pravṛttidarśanāt kṛtisādhyatājñānaṃ pravartakam। na ca viṣabhakṣaṇādau nityanaimittikasthale pravartakatvāt। na cānanugamaḥ, svaviśeṣaṇavattāpratisandhānajanyatvasyānugatatvāditi guravaḥ। tanna -
kṛtisādhyeṣṭasādhanatājñānasyaiva cikīrṣādvārā prayatnajanakatvāt। na pratyavāyaparihārasya pāpakṣayasya ca phalatvakalpanāt। tasmāt kṛtisādhyeṣṭasādhanatvameva liṅādyarthaḥ। pratijānīte atheti। svaparamatasādhāraṇaṃ vidhitvaṃ tāvat nirvakti
- prayatneti। prayatnajanikā yā cikīrṣā tajjanakaṃ yajjñānaṃ tadviṣaya ityarthaḥ। gurumate kṛtisādhyatājñānasya, svamate kṛtisādhyatvaviśiṣṭesādhanatve ca lakṣaṇasaṅgatiḥ। abhidhāyakasya vidhimatābhiproyaṇāha - tatpratīti।
tādṛśajñānaviṣayakāryatvādipratipādakaliṅādirityarthaḥ। liṅādirityādinā loṭtavyādisaṅgrahaḥ। gurumatamāśaṅkate kṛtyasādhya iti। kṛtyasādhyatvenāvagata ityarthaḥ। cikīrṣādvārā pravṛttijanakamityarthaḥ। na ca
kṛtyasādhyatvajñānābhāvatvena tattve gauravāt। pratibandhakatvakalpanena mahāgauravācca iti dik। pravṛttyāpattiḥ। kṛtisādhyatājñānasya tatrāpi sattvādityāśaṅkāṃ nirācaṣṭe na cetyādinā। iṣṭasādhanatāliṅgaketi। aayam
madiṣṭasādhanatvāt' ityānumāniketyarthaḥ। pravartakatvādityanenānvayaḥ। jyotiṣṭomayāgādāvityarthaḥ। vihitakāletyādi। snānādau pravartakatvādityarthaḥ। aaham
vihitakālaśucijīvitvādijñānajanyatvamavaseyam। ananugama iti। pravṛttisāmānyaprayojakasya ekasyābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ। svaviśeṣaṇavattevyādi। svaṃ pravartamānapuruṣaḥ, tasya viśeṣaṇaṃ
tatsambandhasya pratisandhānaṃ jñānaṃ tajjanyatvasyetyarthaḥ। kāraṇatāvacchedakalāghavenetyarthaḥ। tanmate kāraṇatāvacchedakasya janyatvādighaṭitatvāt gauravamiti bhāvaḥ। kṛtisādhyeṣṭasādhanateti। tatra
balabadaniṣṭānanubandhitvamapyantarbhāvanīyam। tena na kṛtisādhyatvena pravṛttyāpattiḥ। viśiṣṭajñānatvāvacchinnasya kāraṇatvakathanaṃ tu prācāṃ matena। navyamate kṛtisādhyatvādijñānānāṃ pṛthageva daṇḍacakrādinyāyenana kāraṇatvāt। pravṛttītyarthaḥ।
pratyavāyeti। pratyavāyasya parihāraḥ prāgabhāvaḥ, tasya duḥkhajanakābhāvatayā tannāśasyaiva iṣṭatvena phalatvamiti bhāvaḥ। na ca sandhyāvandanaprayojyatvasya tatra sattvena phalatvākṣaterityavadheyam। parihartumiti। na ca vidhyanirūpaṇena kathaṃ mūlasya nyūnatā, saptānāṃ
pratijñāyāḥ nirūḍhatvāditi vācyam। sarvaprameyasaṃgrāhake atra nyūnataivetyāśayāt। prayatnajaniketyādi। pravṛttirūpaprayatnaṃ prati aidaṃ kuryām' ityākārikā cikīrṣā kāraṇam। cikīrṣāṃ prati kāraṇam। naiyāyikamate aidaṃ matkṛtisādhyatve sati
vidhilakṣaṇasya tayoḥ samanvaya ityarthaḥ। matābhiprāyeṇetyarthaḥ। tathā ca vātsyāyanabhāṣyam "yadvākyaṃ vidhāyakaṃ codakaṃ sa vidhiḥ" [nyāṇsū-] iti"yadvākyaṃ vidhāyakaṃ deśakaṃ sa vidhiḥ"iti tatra vārtikam। vākāro anāsthāyāmiti। ityavagamāt iti bhāvaḥ। ananu kṛtyasādhye pravṛttyadarśanāt'
iti dīpikoktamayuktam। kṛtyasādhye api kṛtisādhyatābhrameṇa pravṛttidarśanādityata āha kṛtyasādhyatvenāvagata ityartha iti। na pravṛttiḥ ataḥ nāsaṅgatiriti bhāvaḥ। nanu pravṛttiṃ prati cikīrṣāyā āha cikīrṣādvārā pravṛttijanakamityartha iti। na ca
kṛtyasādhyatveti। kṛtyasādhyatvajñānakāle pravṛttivāraṇāya hi kṛtisādhyatājñānasya pravṛttihetutvamuktam। pravṛttiṃ prati pravṛttivariyituṃ śakyate। na ca lāghavānavakāśa iti vācyam। gauravamiti śaṅkiturāśayāt। samādhatte
kṛtyasādhyatājñānābhāvatveneti। kṛtisādhyatājñānatvāpekṣayā kṛtyasādhyatājñānābhāvatvasya kāraṇatāvacchedakasya gurutvādityarthaḥ। kṛtisādhyatvābhāveti। pravṛttiṃ prati kṛtisādhyatvābhāvajñānasya teṣāṃ api kāraṇatvaṃ vaktavyamiti mahāgauravam। tadapekṣayā
kṛtisādhyatājñānasyaikasya kāraṇatve lāghavamiti bhāvaḥ। iṣṭasādhanatāliṅgaketyādi। kāmyakarmasu pravṛttiṃ prati kṛtisādhyatvajñānaṃ hetuḥ। aidava jyotiṣṭomādirūpaṃ kāmyakarma yannaivaṃ tannaivaṃ yathā caityavandanam' ityanumānaṃ draṣṭavyam।
kṛtisādhyatājñānaṃ kāraṇam। vihitakāle śucitve sati jīvitvaṃ sandhyāvandanādinityakarmasu nimittam। snānādirūpanaimittikakarmasu aśucittve sati jīvitvaṃ nimittam। tathā ca tatra aaham yo naivaṃ sa naivaṃ yathā nāstikaḥ ityanumānaṃ pravartate। na ca
kāraṇatāvacchedakadharmasyābhāvāditi vācyam। sadbhāvāt। svaṃ pravartamānaḥ puruṣaḥ tasya viśeṣaṇaṃ tadvṛttidharmaḥ svaviśeṣaṇavattājñānajanyatvasyānugatakāraṇatāvacchedakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। matkṛtisādhya ityādi। ayam kāmyaḥ jyotiṣṭomādiḥ। atra hetau
vṛṣṭyādau madiṣṭasādhanatvarūpahetusattvāt vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya satyantam। vṛṣṭyādeḥ matkṛtiṃ vināpi sattvāt matkṛtiṃ vinā asattvaṃ nāstīti na vyabhicāraḥ। anupapadyamānatve sati ityasya asattve satītyarthaḥ। matkṛtiṃ vinetyatra matpadānupādāne madiṣṭasādhane
anupapadyamānatve sati madiṣṭasādhanatvarūpahetusattvāt vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya tatra matpadam। parakṛtapākasya matkṛtiṃ vināpi parakīyakṛtyā upapadyamānatayā satyantābhāvāt na vyabhicāraḥ। matkṛtiṃ vinā asattvarūpahetusattvāt vyabhicāraḥ। tadvāraṇāya
iṣṭasādhanatvāditi viśeṣyam। madīyaśrame macchatroriṣṭasādhanatvāt vyabhicāratādavasthyam। tadvāraṇāya madiṣṭasādhanatvāditi। madīyaśramasya macchatrviṣṭasādhanatve api madiṣṭasādhanatvaṃ nāstīti na vyabhicāraḥ।
svecchādhīnatvaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ deyam। anyathā nāntarīyakaśrame api uktahetujñānajanyakṛtisādhyatājñānasattvena taduddeśena pravṛttyāpatteḥ। svapadaṃ yatra pravartate tatparam। nāntarīyakaśrame tu na tadviṣayakecchādhīnakṛtisādhyatājñānamiti na tatra pravṛttyāpattiḥ। evaṃ ca
deyam। anyathā anyecchādhīnamatkṛtisādhye madiṣṭasādhane nāntarīyakajalasaṃyogādau vyabhicārāpatteḥ। na caivaṃ sati iti vācyam। asya hetvantaratvāt na doṣa iti vadanti। vihitakālaśucijīvitvajñānādhīnasyeti। vihitakālikaṃ
yat śucitvaviśiṣṭajīvitvaṃ tadviṣayakajñānajanyasyetyarthaḥ। āśaucam। tasya kṛtisādhyatājñānasya। pravṛttisāmānyaprayojakasyeti। pravṛttitvāvacchinnakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatāvacchedakasyetyarthaḥ।
kāraṇatāvacchedakalāghavenetyartha iti। laghutvenetyarthaḥ। laghutvamevopapādayati tanmata iti। gurumata ityarthaḥ। janyatvādighaṭitatvādityatra ādipadena kāryatājñānatvaṃ parāmṛśyate। tathā hi svaviśeṣaṇavattājñānajanyatvamātraṃ na
tajjanyatvena pravṛttiṃ prati kāraṇatvāpatteḥ। api tu svaviśeṣaṇavattājñānajanyakṛtisādhyatājñānatvenaiva kāraṇatvaṃ vācyam। gauravamiti bhāvaḥ। balavadaniṣṭeti। tathā ca
pravṛttihetuḥ। madhuviṣasampṛktānnabhojane tu tatkāle bhāvaḥ। balavadaniṣṭānanubandhitvaṃ nāma iṣṭotpattināntarīyakaduḥkhādhikaduḥkhājanakatvam। balavaddveṣaviṣayaduḥkhājanakatvaṃ vā। nanu
prācīnamatānusāreṇa tathoktamityāha - viśiṣṭajñānatvāvacchinnsyeti। navyamata iti। pūrvoktāsvārasyāt na viśiṣṭajñānatvāvacchinnasya kāraṇatvam। kintu balavadaniṣṭānanubandhitvajñānatvāvacchinnasya pṛthageva kāraṇatvam। yathā daṇḍacakrādīnāṃ ghaṭaṃ prati
daṇḍaviśiṣṭacakratvādinā tadvaditi bhāvaḥ।niṣphale pravṛttyabhāvāt bhāvaḥ। nivṛttyātmakaprayatnavyāvartanāyoktam pravṛttītyartha iti। na bhāvaḥ। duḥkhajanakābhāvatayeti। duḥkhajanakapratiyogikābhāvatayetyarthaḥ। pratyavāyasya duḥkhajanakatayā
tadabhāvasya duḥkhajanakābhāvatvam। svarūpasambandharūpasyeti। siddhasya saṃrakṣaṇarūpo yaḥ tatkāraṇatvamatra vivakṣitam। ataḥ iti bhāvaḥ। kāryaṃ pratīyate। yāgasya āśutaravināśinaḥ
kāryaṃmapūrvameva liṅādyarthaḥ। kṛteḥ saviṣayatvāt viṣayākāṅkṣāyāṃ yāgo viṣayatvenānveti। akasya niyojyaparatayānveti। kāryabāddhā niyojyaḥ। tena vākyārthaḥ sampadyate। vaidikaliṅtvāt ayāvajjīvamagnihotraṃ
vācyam kalpyate। kriyākāryeṃ lakṣaṇā iti cet - na। tannirvāhārtham avāntaravyāpāratayā apūrvakalpanāt। kīrtanādinā nāśaśruteḥ na yāgadhvaṃso vyāpāraḥ।
śaktiriti gurumataṃ āśaṅkate - nanviti। icchāviśeṣarūpasya yāgasyeti। āśutaravināśinaḥ - tṛtīyakṣaṇavṛttidhvaṃsapratiyoginaḥ। sthāyi - phalaparyantasthāyi। anvayaprakāraṃ darśayati - kāryaṃ kṛtisādhyamiti। yāge kṛtisādhyatvaṃ sākṣāt। apūrvaṃ tu
yāgadvāreti bodhyam। idam matkṛtisādhyamiti jñānavānityarthaḥ। vidhyarthamukhyaviśeṣyakaṃ śābdabodhaṃ darśayati - teneti। svargakāmasya liṅarthe kārye tadekadeśe ca yāgasya anvayenetyarthaḥ। nyāyamate tu tatra
svargakāmaḥ' iti vākyārthabodhaḥ। nanu apūrvasya samānaviṣayakatvena hetuhetumadbhāvaḥ। evaṃ ca kāryatvāvacchinne yatra kutracit śaktigrahaḥ। yogyatābalācca aparvūrūpakāryasya śābdabodhe bhānaṃ, na hi yāgaviṣayakamanyatkāryaṃ sambhavatīti। nanu nitye
phalābhāvāt kathaṃ tatra apūrvabodhakatā ityata āha - yāvajjīvamiti। apūrvameveti। paṇḍāpūrvamityarthaḥ। laukikasthale apūrvabhānāsambhavādāha - ārogyeti। dhātvarthaniṣṭhakāryatva ityarthaḥ। laukikālaukikasādhāraṇyena
yāgasyeti। ayogyatvāt yāgasya svargasādhanatvena bhānaṃ na sambhavatītyuktadoṣaṃ nirācṣṭe - ayogyeti। ayogyatāsaṃśayasattve api tasyāvighaṭakatvāt śābdabodho bhavatyeveti bhāvaḥ। ityāha - tannirvāhārthamiti। nanu yāgadhvaṃsasyaiva vyāpāratvamastu
kimapūrvakalpanenetyata āha-kīrtanādineti। ādinā "karmanāśājalasparśātkaratoyāvilaṅghanāt। dharmaḥ kṣarati kīrtanāt।।" ityatroktakarmanāśājalasparśādiparigrahaḥ। dhvaṃsasya
vyāpāratve svargadhārāpattirityapi dūṣaṇāntaraṃ vibhāvanīyam। karmanāśā, karatoyā, gaṇḍakī iti nadīviśeṣāḥ। pratīyata iti। apūrvaṃ kāryatvena pratīyata ityarthaḥ। liṅo hi kāryatvāvacchinne śaktiḥ। prakāśikāyām ayogyatvāditi।
svargasādhanatvānvayayogyatāvirahādityarthaḥ। bauddherevāṅgīkārādāha-tṛtīyakṣaṇeti। māsādiparyantasthāyitvasyānupayogādāha - phalaparyantasthāyīti। svargotpattiparyantaṃ vartamānamityarthaḥ। vidhyarthamukhyaviśeṣyakamiti।
liṅarthakāryamukhyaviśeṣyakamityarthaḥ। liṅaḥ kṛtisādhyamityarthaḥ। kṛtau svargakāmasya samavetātvasambandhenānvayaḥ, viṣayatāsambandhena yāgasyānvayaḥ। tathā ca svargakāmasamavetā ityāśayaḥ। svargaṅkāmasya kārye anvaya ityuktāvapi
prāptāprāptavivekena kṛtāvanvaya eva vivakṣitaḥ। kāryaikadeśe kṛtāvityarthaḥ। tanmate liṅtvena abhidhīyate। ākhyātatvena rūpeṇa kṛtirabhidhīyate kṛtisādhyatvādīnāṃ trayāṇāṃ dhātvarthe yoge āśrayatāsambandhenānvayaḥ।
yāgasyānukūlatāsambandhena ākhyātārthakṛtāvanvayaḥ। kṛterāśrayatāsambandhena prathamāntārthe svargakāme anvayaḥ। tathā ca svargakāma iti bodhaḥ। na tu samānaviṣayakatveneti। taddharmāvacchinnatadviṣayakopasthiteśca hetuteti netyarthaḥ। yatra
kutraciditi। yāgādikriyāyāmityarthaḥ। yogyatābalāditi। svargasādhanatvānvayayogyatābalādityarthaḥ। niṣphalamapūrvaṃ paṇḍāpūrvamityucyate। prayojanatvaṃ prābhākarerucyate। kriyārūpasya kāryasya dhātunaiva
iti। kāryaśaktasya liṅaḥ tatra kāryatve lakṣaṇetyatheḥ। lakṣaṇetyarthaḥ' iti nṛsiṃhaśāstriṇaḥ prāhuḥ। vākyādiṣṭasādhanatvenetyādi। ajyotiṣṭomeva svargakāmo yajeta' śābdabodhaḥ ādau jāyate। tadanantaraṃ dvikṣaṇāvasthāyino yāgasya
liṅarthatvaṃ na sambhavatīti tātparyam। karmanāśā, karatoyā, gaṇḍakī, iti nadīviśeṣāṇāṃ saṃjñāḥ। yatnārthakatvam। pacati pākaṃ karotīti vivaraṇadarśanāt, kiṃ prayatnārthakatvaniścayāt। ratho gacchatītyādau anukūlavyāpāre
lakṣaṇā। adevadattaḥ pacita', adevadattena pacyate taṇḍulaḥ' ityādau kartṛkarmaṇoḥ nākhyātārthatvam। kintu tadgataikatvādīnāmeva। tayorākṣepādeva lābhaḥ। lokavyutpattīti।
lokavyavahāretyarthaḥ। sa ca yo yatra pravartate sa kṛtisādhyatveneṣṭasādhanatvena ca tajjñānavānityevaṃrūpaḥ। kecittu yadicchayā yatra pravṛttiḥ tattatsādhanamiti lokavyavahāra ityāhuḥ। niyamabalāditi tadarthaḥ। sarvatreti śeṣa iti vyācakhyuḥ।
ākhyātatveneti। tacca saṅketasambandhenākhyātapadavattvaṃ tiptvādikameva śaktatāvacchedakamiti tu navyāḥ। yatnārthakatvam - kṛtitvāvacchinnavācakatvam। kṛtitvāvacchinne nānyatheti bhāvaḥ। nanu ratho gacchati ityādau ākhyātasya
vaktavyetyata āha - ratho gacchatītyādāviti। vyāpāre gamanasyānvayalābhāya। navyāḥ punaḥ gacchatītyatra ākhyātasya jānātītyādāviva āśrayatve nirūḍhalakṣaṇā। na cāśrayatāsambandhenaiva nirarthakamiti। nāmārthayoriva
tathānvayāsambhavāt। stokaṃ pacatītyādau stokādeḥ dhātvarthe poke anvayāt abhedātirikteti dhyeyam। vaiyākaraṇamataṃ nirācaṣṭe - devadatta iti। nākhyātārthatvamiti। ākhyātasya kartrādau śaktisvīkāre anantakṛtyādeḥ śakyatāvacchedakatvamaṅgīkartavyam।
