lāghavamiti bhāvaḥ। tadgataikatvādīnāmeveti। ākhyātārthatvamiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ। ādinā kṛtyādiparigrahaḥ। nanu tarhi kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kathaṃ lābha ityata āha - tayoriti। paramatena। svamate tu prathamantapadenaiva tallābhāt। adevadattaḥ taṇḍulaṃ pacati'
ityanvayabodhaḥ। adevadattena pacyate taṇḍula' ityatra tu adevadattasamavetakṛtijanyapākakarmībhūtastaṇḍulaḥ' iti śābdabodhaḥ। ca dvitīyā syāt। tatra kartṛkarmaṇoḥ ākhyātenānabhidhānāditi vācyam। anabhihite kartṛtve tṛtīyāyāḥ tādṛśe ca karmatve
dvitīyāyā vidhānenādoṣāditi dhyeyam। yo yatreti। yaḥ kṛtisādhyatkmiṣṭasādhanatvaṃ cāvagamyata ityarthaḥ। vyavahāraparatayā navyānāṃ matamāha - navyāḥ panuriti। tacca saṅketasaṃbandheneti।
saṅketo asti sa tibādiḥ saṅketasaṃbandhena ākhyātapadavān। tibādiniṣṭham। tat śaktatāvacchedakamityarthaḥ। yathā tibādiṣu aṣṭādaśasu ākhyātapadasya kṛtiśaktatāvacchedakamityāhuḥ। tanmatamāha - tiptvādikameveti। atra
śaktatākalpanāyāḥ ucitatvam"iti vyutpattivādagrantho anusandheyaḥ। sūcanāya kṛtitvāvacchinnavācakatvaṃ ityuktam। dīpikāyāṃ pacati pākaṃ karotīti। tatsamānārthakapadāntareṇa tadarthakathanaṃ vivaraṇam। apacati' iti vivaraṇīyapade pac ti iti bhāgadvayamasti। apākaṃ
vivaraṇam, akaroti' ityanena ati' ityākhyātasya vivaraṇam। yatnaḥ kṛdhātorarthaḥ। tathā ca karotinā vivaraṇāt ākhyātasya yatnārthakatvam। evaṃ akiṃ karoti' iti praśnasya pacati ityuttaraṃ dīyate। tatra praśnavākye kiṃ śabdasya jijñāsāviṣayadharmāvacchinnor'thaḥ।
dvitīyāyāḥ viṣayatvamarthaḥ। tatrādheyatāsambandhena kiṃpadārthasyānvayaḥ। viṣayatvasya nirūpakatāsambandhena kṛtāvanvayaḥ। tathā ca jāyate। apacati' iti vākyena pākaniṣṭhaviṣayatānirūpakakṛtiriti bodho bhavati। tathā ca jijñāsitadharmāvacchinnaviṣayakakṛtivācakasya
bhavitumarhatīti ākhyātasya yatnavācakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। prakāśikāyām jijñāsitasambandhabodhakamiti। jijñāsāviṣayadharmāvacchinnapratiyogikaviṣayatvarūpasambandhabodhakam ityarthaḥ। pākasambandhabodhakatva iti। pākaviṣayakatvabodhakatva ityarthaḥ।
tannivartakatvamiti। jijñāsānivartakatvamityarthaḥ। kṛtibodhakatvāsambhavāditi। acetane rathe yatnarūpakṛterbādhitatvāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu ratho gacchatītyādau ākhyātasyānukūlavyāpāre lakṣaṇetyuktirna yuktā। anukūlatvasya
tathaiva tātparyamityāha - vyāpāre anukūlatvotkīrtanamiti। navyāḥ punariti। dīghitikārādayaḥ ityarthaḥ। maṇikṛnmatamāśaṅkate - na cāśrayatāsambandhenaiveti। anyathā acaitraḥ pacyate' pāke anvayāpattariti bhāvaḥ।
vaiyākaraṇamatamiti। arthaḥ tatrābhedena taṇḍulasyānvayaḥ। karmaṇaḥ svaniṃṣṭhakarmatānirūpakatvasambandhena dhātvarthe pāke anvayaḥ। apacati' ityatra tipaḥ kartā arthaḥ। tatra devadattasyābhedenānvayaḥ। kartuḥ
dhātvarthapāke svaniṣṭhakartṛtānirūpakatvasambandhenānvayaḥ। tathā ca dhātvarthamukhyaviśeṣyako bodhaḥ। devadattena pacyate taṇḍulaḥ ityatra tṛtīyāyāḥ kartā arthaḥ। tatra devadattasya abhedenānvayaḥ, kartuśca pāke anvayaḥ। ākhyātasya karma arthaḥ tatra taṇḍulasyābhedena karmaṇaśca
dhātvarthe anvayaḥ। devadattābhinnakartṛkaḥ taṇḍulābhinnakarmakaḥ pāka iti śābdabodhaḥ। devadattaḥ taṇḍulaṃ pacati ityatra dvitīyāyāḥ karmatvamarthaḥ। tatrādheyatāsambandhena taṇḍulasyānvayaḥ। karmatvasya nirūpakatāsambandhena
dhātvarthe pāke anvayaḥ। ākhyātasya kṛtirarthaḥ। tatrānukūlatāsambandhena dhātvarthapākasyānvayaḥ। kṛterāśrayatāsambandhena devadatte anvaya iti prathamāntārthamukhyaviśeṣyako bodhaḥ। devadattena pacyate taṇḍula ityatra tṛtīyāyāḥ kṛtirarthaḥ। tatra devadattasya samavāyenānvayaḥ।
kṛterjanyatāsambandhena dhātvarthapāke anvayaḥ। ākhyātasya karmatvamarthaḥ। tatra nirūpitatvasambandhena pākasyānvayaḥ। karmatvasyāśrayatāsambandhena bodhaḥ। arthaḥ। odanapadottaradvitīyāyāḥ akhaṇḍopādhirūpaṃ karmatvamarthaḥ।
tatrādheyatāsambandhena taṇḍulasyānvayaḥ। karmatvasya svanirūpakadhātvarthapākānukūlatvasambandhena ākhyātārthakṛtāvanvayaḥ। devadattasyāpi tatraivānvayaḥ। dhātvarthapākasya kṛtāvanvayaḥ। svaniṣṭhakaraṇatānirūpakaudanoddeśyakatvasambandhena
pākasya kṛtāvanvaya iti paryavasyati। tathā ca devadattasamavetā taṇḍulakarmakapākānukūlā pākakaraṇikā kṛtiriti bodhaḥ। aiteṣāṃ mate ākhyātarthakṛtiḥ śābdabodhe mukhyaviśeṣyatayā bhāsate। pākasya kṛtau karaṇatvaṃ ca kṛtiṃ prati uddeśyabhūtaudanakaraṇatvāt। yatra tu
karmatāsambanadhena kṛtāvanvayaḥ। devadattasamavetā pākakarmikā kṛtiriti bodhaḥ। caitreṇa odanaḥ pacyate ityatrāpi tṛtīyāyāḥ kartṛtvamarthaḥ। tasya svanirūpakapākānukūlatvasambandhena ākhyātārthakṛtāvanvayaḥ। dhātvarthasya pākasya
svakaraṇakaudanoddeśyakatvasambandhena kṛtāvanvayaḥ। ākhyātasya tatra karmatvaṃ bhāvanā cārthaḥ। karmatve odanasyānvayaḥ। karmatvasya svanirūpakapākānukūlatvasambandhena bhāvanāyāmanvayaḥ। tathā ca pākakaraṇakaudanoddeśyikā bhāvenati śābdabodha iti।
pūrveṇānvaya iti। tathā ca ca kartṛkarmagatā ekatvādisaṅkhyā kṛtiḥ kālaśca ākhyātārthaḥ। kartṛkarmagatasaṅkhyāyāmanabhihitāyāmityarthaḥ। atha vā kartṛtve karmatve cānabhihite ityarthaḥ। nātaḥ devadattaḥ pacati ityatra
taṇḍulapadottaraṃ dvitīyāyā vā apattiḥ। agre ca spaṣṭamidam। kṛtyādiparigraha iti। paramateneti। mīmāṃsakamatenetyarthaḥ। akartā cākṣepalabhyaḥ' iti nyāyaprakāśādau nirūpitatvāt।
dhātoreva prakarṣe śaktiḥ। upasargāṇāṃ dyotakatvameva, na tatra śaktiḥ। vācakatvamataṃ nirasyati prajayatītyādāviti। nanu dhātunaiva - upasargāṇāmiti। dyotakatvam - tātparyagrāhakatvam। tena aitaranipātānām
vācakatvam' iti sūcitam। tathā hi-ekakārasya bahutaramūhanīyam। tātparyamiti graho bhavati। ataḥ dhātorarthaviśeṣe tātparyagrahajanakatvamupasargāṇāmiti bhāvaḥ।
upasargātiriktanipātānāmityarthaḥ। ityādikaṃ bahutaramūhanīyamiti। anīlam sarojaṃ bhavatyeva' ityādau evakārasya atyantāyogavyavacchedor'tha ityūhanīyamityarthaḥ। atyantāyogavyavacchedaśceti। viśeṣyasaṅgataivakārasya
anyayogavyavacchedor'thaḥ। yathā pārtha eva dhanurdhara ityādau pārthānyasmin dhanurdhaṃratvayogo vyavacchidyate। tatra anyaḥ, yogaḥ, abhāvaśceti trayaḥ evakārasya pṛthak śakyāḥ। anyaśabdārthaḥ bhedavān। bhede pārthasya pratiyogitāsambandhenānvayaḥ। sambandharūpe yoge
prakṛte tādātmyātmake pratiyogitvena dhunardhaṃrasyānvayaḥ। yogasyābhāve pratiyogitvenānvayaḥ। abhāvasya svarūpasambandhena anyasminnanvayaḥ। evaṃ dhanurdharasya abhedasambandhena pārthe anvayaḥ। tathā ca pārthaḥ dhanurdharābhinnaśceti śābdabodho jāyate। pārthasya
viśeṣyatayā anyaviśeṣaṇatayā ca dvirbhānam। evaṃ dhunardharasya evakārārthayogaviśeṣaṇatayā pārthaviśeṣaṇatayā ca dvirbhānam। viśeṣaṇasaṅgataivakārasya ayogavyavacchedor'thaḥ। yathā aśaṅkhaḥ pāṇḍara eva' ityādau śaṅkhe pāṇḍarāyogo vyavacchidyate।
tatraivakārasya yogābhāve abhāve ca śaktiḥ। sambandhātmake yoge pāṇḍarasya pratiyogitayā anvayaḥ। yogābhāvasya pratiyogitayā abhāve anvayaḥ। abhāvasya svarūpasaṃbandhena śaṅkhe anvayaḥ। tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ pāṇḍarayogābhāvābhāvavān iti śābdabodhaḥ।
atyantāyogavyavacchedor'thaḥ। yathā anīlaṃ sarojaṃ bhavatyeva' nīlabhavanātyantāyogo vyavacchidyate। atyantatvaṃ abhāvaśca tatra evakārārthaḥ। atyantatvaṃ ca vyāpakatvam। tacca bhedapratiyogitānavacchedakatvam। bhede
sarojasyādheyatāsambandhenānvayaḥ। bhedapratiyogitānavacchedakatvasya abhāve anvayaḥ। abhāvasya svarūpasambandhena ayoge anvayaḥ। evaṃ nīlakartṛkabhavanasya nīlatvātmakasya ayogaikadeśe yoge pratiyogitvenānvayaḥ। tathā ca
nīlatvapratiyogikasambandhābhāvaḥ iti śābdabodhaḥ। ayoge sarojatvavyāpakatvavyavacchedabodho varṇita iti। adhikam jayarāmanyāyapañcānanakṛtapadārthamālāyāṃ ca draṣṭavyam। paramaprayojanaṃ mokṣaḥ। tathā hi aātmā vāre draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavyo
satyapyasambhāvanānivṛtteḥ yuktyanusandhānarūpamananasādhyatvāt। mananopayogipadārthanirūpaṇadvārā śāstrasyāpi mokṣopayogitvam। caramaduḥkhadhvaṃsalakṣaṇamokṣo jāyate। jñānameva mokṣasādhanam। mithyājñānanivṛtterjñānamātrasādhyatvāt। atamevaṃ
sādhanāntaraniṣedhācca। padārthajñānasyeti। padārthatattvajñānasyetyarthaḥ। anyeṣāmavāntaraprayojanānāmapi sadbhāvādāha - parameti। ātmadarśanamiṣṭasādhanamiti yāvat। ātmadarśanopāyaṃ darśayati
śrotavya ityādinā। ārtha-krameṇa śābdakramaḥ tyakto bhavati, aagnihotraṃ juhoti' ayāvagūṃ pacati' ityādivat। asambhāvanānivṛtteriti। aprāmāṇyajñānanivṛtterityarthaḥ। yuktyanusandhāneti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ yuktibhiranucintanaṃ mananam। tacca
ātmana itarabhinnatvenānumānam। tacca bhedapratiyogītarajñānasādhyam। tadarthaṃ sakalapadārthanirūpaṇamiti। mokṣopayogitvaṃ viśadayati tadanantaramiti। mananānantaramityarthaḥ।
sakalakāmanāviṣayeti। apunarbhavarūpatvāt sarveṣāmapīṣṭaḥ yo mokṣaḥ tatprayojanakatvamityarthaṃḥ। yadapekṣayā anyat prayojanaṃ na bhavati tat paramaprayojanam। yadapekṣayā anyat prayojanaṃ bhavati tat avāntaraprayojanam। prayojanāntarāsādhanatve sati prayojanatvaṃ
paramaprayojanatvam। prayojanāntarasādhanatve sati prayojanatvaṃ avāntaraprayojanatvam। nanu"ātmā vā are śravaṇāderdarśanasādhanatvamityāśaṅkyāha - ārthakrameṇeti। prayojanavaśena yaḥ kramaḥ saḥ ārthakramaḥ। yathā agnihotrayavāgūpākayoḥ।
pūrvamanuṣṭhīyate। padārthabodhakavākyānāṃ yaḥ kramaḥ saḥ pāṭhakramaḥ। tena ca padārthānāṃ kamaḥ āśrīyate। aprāmāṇyajñānanivṛtteriti। aprāmāṇyajñānasya nivṛttiḥ mananena bhavati। mananaṃ cānu mityātmakam। vyatirekyanumānaprayogo draṣṭavyaḥ।
bhedapratiyogītarajñānasādhyamiti। yakajñānajanyamanumityātmakaṃ mananamityarthaḥ। ātmetara padārthaviṣayakajñānotpādanārthamityarthaḥ। pratyāhṛtya-nigṛhya, viṣayasaṃyuktāni yathā na bhaveyustathā kṛtvetyarthaḥ। manaḥpratyāhṛtya -
manaḥ indriyasaṃyuktaṃ yathā na syāt tathā kṛtvā। sākṣātkartavye ātmani manasaḥ praṇidhānaṃ sthāpanaṃ yogaḥ। viśeṣadarśanenaiveti। darśanenaivetyarthaḥ। tathā prakṛte apīti। ātmagatasya nivartate ityarthaḥ।
। । kāṇādanyāyamatayorbālavyutpattisiddhaye। racitastarkasaṅgrahaḥ।। ।। iti
tarkasaṃgrahaḥ samāptaḥ।। । । mokṣasādhanatvasmaraṇāt jñānakarmaṇoḥ samuccaya iti cet - na। duritakṣayam।
vimalīkurvannabhyāsena ca pācayet।। kvacijjñānāt kaivalyaṃ labhate naraḥ"।। sākṣāt। tasmāt padārthatattvajñānasya mokṣaḥ paramaprayojanamiti sarvaṃ ramaṇīyam।
। । naraḥ' ityādineti। ādinā akṣīyante cāsya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe tathā' ityādismṛteśca saṃgrahaḥ। atrāyaṃ kramaḥ duritakṣayarūpātmaśuddhirbhavati। tato viṣayeṣu vairāgyam। tataḥ
śravaṇādau pravṛttiḥ। tataḥ śravaṇādikrameṇa tattvajñānotpattau pūrvoktamithyājñānanāśādikrameṇa mokṣaniṣpattiḥ। adhikam tarkakarkaśavicāracāturīdhurīṇairiti। candracūḍāya maṅgalam।।
। । śrīyante ceti। puṇyapāparūpāṇi karmāṇi naśyantītyarthaḥ। bhasmīkarotītyarthaḥ।
ātmasākṣātkāre satītyādi।"duḥkhajanyapravṛttidoṣaḥ nyāyasūtramatrābhisaṃhitam। prathamataḥ avicchinnatailadhārāvat ātmā dehādibhinnatvena sākṣātkriyate। ayaṃ sākṣātkāra eva tattvajñānamityucyate। anena tattvajñānena dehādau ātmābhedabhramarūpaṃ
mithyājñānaṃ nivartate। tādṛśadoṣāṇāmanutpattau rāgadveṣamoharūpā doṣāḥ notpadyanate। tādṛśadoṣāṇāmanutpattau vihitaniṣiddhakarmasu pravṛttiḥ na bhavati। pravṛttyabhāvācca puṇyapāparūpau dharmāndharmau notpadyete। dharmādharmayoranutpattau ca śarīraprāṇasaṃyogarūpaṃ janma
na bhavati। vināśe ca caramaduḥkhasya dhvaṃsarūpo mokṣo bhavati iti bhāvaḥ। tameva viditveti। taṃ atikrāmati। ātmatattvajñānavāneva saṃsāranāśavān bhavatītyarthaḥ।
vi। sādhanāntaraniṣedhāditi। ātmatattvajñānādanyasya sādhanasya niṣedhādityarthaṃḥ। mokṣāprāpteḥ tattvajñānaṃ bhagavatprīṇanayāgādirūpaṃ karma cobhayaṃ sādhanamityarthaḥ। samuccaya
iti। jñānakarmasamudāyaḥ mokṣasādhanam। parasparasahakāreṇa jñānakarmaṇorūbhayoḥ mokṣasādhanatvaṃ na jñānamātrasyetyarthaṃḥ। jñānaṃ ca vimalīkurvanniti। dehendriyādivilakṣaṇātmajñānaṃ mananenāprāmāṇyajñānānāskanditaṃ kurvannityarthaḥ।
phalonmukhaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ। prakāśikāyāṃ tarkakarkaśeti। tarkamūlakaḥ tatra vā dhuriṇaiḥ samarthairityarthaḥ। vimarśaḥ tatra yā cāturī cāturthaṃ tayā tatra vā dhuviṇaiḥ samarthairityarthaḥ। candracūḍāya maṅgalamiti । maṅgalamiti samarpaṇākriyāviśeṣaṇam। maṅgalaṃ yathā syāt tathā
candracūḍāya samārpayadityarthaḥ। yathā īśvarārpaṇabuddhyā kriyamāṇaṃ bhāvaḥ।। vyākhyeyaṃ samapūryata।। vyākhyaiṣā janayenna vā।
prītiṃ parāmāvakṣyati dhruvam।। । । ।। śrīgurucaraṇāravindābhyāṃ namaḥ।।
।। prakāśikāvyākhyā prasāraṇā।। nidhāyetyādiślokasyāyaṃ vākyārthaḥ। tathā hi - hṛdi ityatra saptamyāḥ nirūpitatvamarthaḥ। tasya ca
vṛttitvaprakārakāhāryajñānarūpanipūrvakadhādhātvarthaghaṭakavṛttitve anvayaḥ। viśeṣyatvaṃ viśeṣyitvaṃ vār'thaḥ। prakṛtyarthasya viśeṣyatve ādheyatayā viśeṣyitve vā nirūpitatvasambandhenānvayaḥ। lyapaḥ dhvaṃsor'thaḥ। tatra prakṛtyarthasya pratiyogitayānvayaḥ। dhvaṃsasya ca
kriyata ityatra kṛdhātvarthakṛtāvanvayaḥ। [] guruvandanamityatra bodhānukūlatādṛśacetanakartṛko vyāpāro vandanam। viśeṣyatānirūpitor'thaḥ। tasya cābhedasambandhena prakāratāyāmanvayaḥ। prakṛtyarthasyādheyatayā viśeṣyatve anvayaḥ।
dvitīyārthaḥ। atrāpi lyapaḥ pūrvavadevārthaḥ। [] bālānāmityatra ṣaṣṭhyāḥ bodhānvayi samavetatvam arthaḥ। tatra nirūpitatvasambandhena prakṛtyarthasyānvayaḥ। [] sukhabodhāyetyatra sukhaṃ yathā syāttathā bodhaḥ। sukhaścāsau bodhaśceti samānādhikaraṇasamāsaḥ। arthapradarśanamātraparam। anyathā tṛtīyāsamāsānupapatteḥ। sukhaśabdaśca
abhārāpagame sukhī saṃvṛtto aham' itivat duḥkhābhāve upacaryate। sa ceha dharmiparaḥ। bodhāyetyatra aedhānāhartuṃ vrajati' ityarthe sūtreṇa prāptā caturthī utpattyanukūlavyāpāraviṣayakecchāṃ bodhayati। kṛtāvanvayaḥ। utpattau ca bodhānvayaḥ। ākhyātasyādheyatayā
vidheyatvaṃ cārthaḥ। viśiṣṭabodhaḥ spaṣaṭaḥ dīpikāyām [] viśveśvaramiti। - vidheyakavartamānakālīnakṛtimānahaṃ iti bodhaḥ। svapratiyogisamānakartṛkatvasvādhikaraṇakālavṛttitvobhayasambandhena। śivamityādi। pūrvārdhasya
bodhaḥ। [] yadvandanenetyādyuttarārthasya mando apīti bodhaḥ। apiśabdārthaḥ caikakṣaṇāvacchedena ekādhikaraṇāvṛttitvaṃ sādṛśyānvayi। upadeśaścājñātajñāpanaṃe viṣayatāviśiṣṭaśabdarūpam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ
snirūpakajñānajanakatvasvasāmānādhikaraṇyobhayasambandhena। svaprākkālāvacchinnajñānaviṣayatvābhāvasambandhena। aasyārthasyopadeśa' ityādau ṣaṣṭhyartha ādheyatvam। tasya copadadeśapadārthaghaṭakaviṣayatāyāmanvaya iti bodhyam।
dīpikāyām [] cikīrṣitasyetyādi। kṛñdhātoḥ kṛtirarthaḥ sanaḥ icchā। kṛtiniṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpitaviṣayatāsambandhāvacchinnaprakāratāśrayor'thaḥ। kṛteḥ viśeṣyatāsambandhenecchāyāmanvayaḥ। tasyāśca nirūpitatvasambandhena prakāratāyāmanvayaḥ। sā ca icchā
agranthaviṣayakakṛtirbhavatu' ityākārikā। [] nirvighnaparisamāptyarthamityatra nirvighnaṃ yathā yathā samāptiriti vigrahaḥ। [] nirvighnaparisamāptaya ityatra tu pūrvavadutpādakavyāpārecchaiva caturthyarthaḥ। vyāpāraśca pratibhādirūpaḥ। samāptiśca caramavarṇaghvaṃsaḥ tadanvitaṣaṣṭyarthaḥ
granthasyetyatra sambandhaḥ svaghaṭakacaramavarṇapratiyogitvarūpaḥ। etattattvamasmadviracitasamāpti [vicāre] draṣṭavyam। śikṣayitumityarthaḥ। atumarthācca bhāvavacanāt' iti sutraṇa caturthī। apaktuṃ vrajati' ityarthe apākāya vrajati' ityādivat। tatrecchaiva
caturthyarthaḥ। tasyāśca nibandhapadārthajñānajanakaśabdarūpabindhane anvayaḥ। aśiṣyā apyevaṃ kuryuḥ' ityākārakānugraharūpecchaiva śikṣāpadārthaḥ। tatra śiṣyāṇāṃ viśeṣyatāsambandhenānvayaḥ। aavaśyakartavyatvaprakārakajñānaṃ śikṣā'
iti tu asmaddinakaraṭiṣpaṇyāmativistareṇa nirastam। ktapratyayasya viśeṣyatānirūpitaviṣayatāsambandhāvacchinnaprakāratāśrayor'thaḥ। dhātvarthaḥ ādyakṛtiḥ। kṛtāvadyatvaṃ ca dhvaṃsaviśiṣṭānyatvaparyavasitam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ svottaratvasvapratiyogikṛtiviśiṣṭatvobhayasambandhena।
svasāmānādhikaraṇyasvaviṣayagranthaviṣayakatvobhayasambandhena। atra bhrāntapuruṣīyajalatāḍanādyācaraṇavat' ityanumānaṃ nirastam। tattuccham। bhrāntapuruṣīyānuṣṭhānaviṣayatayā bādhāpatteḥ। kṛtiviśiṣṭatvābhāveti। kṛtiviśiṣṭatvaṃ ca viṣayatāsambandhena।
paryavasānena tadapekṣayā asmaduktasyaiva yuktatvāt। yadapi amaṅgalādyācaraṇaṃ pāpajanakam' ityunamānam tadapi heyam। pāpotpattikalpane pramāṇābhāvāt। yadyapi pratijñāyāṃ na śiṣyāvadhānaphalakatvāt na doṣaḥ। ata eva aśiṣyāvadhānāya
saṅgacchate। avadhānaṃ ca manaso vikṣeparāhityaṃ vijātīyamanoyoga iti yāvat। caturthyarthaḥ utpattyanukūlavyāpārecchā। sa ca iti śiṣyān prati guroḥ śabdaprayogaḥ। [] svagranthasya itaragranthanetyādi।
svagranthaviśeṣyaketaragranthajanyaprayojanajanakatvābhāvaprakārakajñānajanakaśabdānukalūkṛtimānityanvayabodhaḥ। dīpikāyām [] maṅgalasya samāptisādhanatvaṃ nāstīti। maṅgalaṃ samāptisādhanatvābhāvavadityarthaḥ। tādṛśasādhanatvābhāvo maṅgalavṛttiriti vā।
[] anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ vyabhicārāditi। svāvacchinnetyādi। svapadena yaddharmāvacchinnasattve api kāryaṃ na jāyate tadgrāhyam। tacca kapālākāśasaṃyogasyānvayavyabhicāritvaṃ na nirvahati।
atastudapādānam। kāryatāvacchedakanirūpitatādṛśāvacchedakasambandhāvacchedakatvābhimatadharmavattvam। vyatirekavyabhicāraśca kāraṇābhāve api kāryotpattirūpaḥ। kāryatāvacchedakāvacchinnādhikaraṇaviśiṣṭakāraṇatāvacchedakavattvam।
yāvadavacchinnādhikaraṇakūṭavattvasambandhāvacchinnādheyatvobhāyasambandhena। pratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena svaviśiṣṭatvaparyavasitam। svaviśiṣṭakaraṇatāvacchedakadharmāvacchinnanirūpitādhikaraṇatātvasambandhena। svāvacchinnavyāpyatāvacchedakatvasambandhāvacchinnatvasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena।
pratiyogitāvacchedakatā cādheyatāsambandhena। tādṛśādheyatāśūnyakāraṇatāvacchedakadharmavattvam anvayasahacāraḥ। vyatirekasahacāraḥ। kāraṇatāgrahahetuḥ। vyatirekavyabhicāragrastarāsabhādivāraṇāya
vyatirekasahacāragrahaḥ tathā। yabhicāra grahau ca krameṇa sahacāragrahapratibandhakau। na vyabhicāra ityanenānvaya iti। ato na vyabhicāra ityuttaravākyenānvaya ityarthaḥ। vighnānyūnasaṃkhyākatvasya
balavattarasyeti। vaniṣṭhābhāvīyetyādi। prathamasvapadaṃ kāryatāvacchedakāvacchinnādhikaraṇaparam। dvitīyasvapadaṃ kāraṇatāvacchedakaparam। evamuparitanasvapadāni
kāraṇatāvacchedakadharmaparāṇi। vyabhicāragrahauceti। anvayavyabhicāragrahaḥ vyatirekasahacāragrahapratibandhaka ityarthaḥ। vighnadhvaṃsadvāreti।
svajanyavighnadhvaṃsasambandhenetyarthaḥ। ata eva samāptirbhavati। balavattaratvaṃ ca vaijātyaviśeṣaḥ। [] āhuḥ ityasvarassūcitaḥ। tadbījantu ityādipadānāmāvṛttānāmarthadvayabodhakatvānupapattireva। nanu
maṅgalakartavyatābodhakaśrutyanumāpakatvaṃ labhyate। śrutibodhitāpravṛttapravṛttiviṣayatvalakṣaṇakartavyatārahitabhojanasādhāraṇatvāt। asnātvā bhuñjīta' ityādiḥ tatkartavyatābodhiketi vācyam। tasyāḥ bhojane snānottarakālīnatāmātravidhānaparatvāt। bhojanasya
rāgaprāptatayā tadvidhiparatvāsambhavāt। aaprāpte hi śāstramathavat' iti। kartavayatve kṛtividheyatve। kiṃ śabdaḥ kṣepe। tathā ca maṅgalakartavyatāpramitikaraṇaṃ na kimapītyarthaḥ। śiṣṭācārasyoktayuktyā śrutyanumāpakatvāsambhavāt iti bhāvaḥ।
tadapahāsyam। viṣayatātmakagauṇakarmārthakasya tavyādipratyayasya viṣayatāprayojakadharmavadarthakatāyāṃ pramāṇābhāvāt। anyathā boddhavyaśabdādāvapi tathā prasaṅgāt। ata eva [] maṅgalasya śrutibodhitakartavyatākatvaṃ vyavasthāpayituṃ śaṅkata ityavataraṇikādānamapi saṅgacchate।
vyavasthāpanam। tumunaḥ icchaivārthaḥ। tasya śaṅkāyāmanvayaḥ। svaviṣayetyādi। śaṅgāviṣayakecchā tadviṣayatvaṃ ca śaṅkāyām। maṅgalasya
kuryāmiti pūrvapakṣecchā jāyata iti bhāvaḥ। [] śiṣṭetyādi। hetusādhyādipradarśanapūrvakamanumānasvarūpaṃ vivṛṇoti - [] tathāhītyalaukikāvigītaśiṣṭācāraviṣayatvāditi। atrālaukikatvasamānādhikaraṇāvigītatvasamānādhikaraṇaśiṣṭācāraviṣayatvādityāśayaḥ।
pūrvapadārthatāvacchedakasamānādhikaraṇottarapadārthatāvacchedakabodhakatvavyutpatteḥ। bodhitaṃ na saṃghaṭate। amaṅgalaṃ śrutibodhitakartavyatākam' ityanumitividheyatvasya śrutibodhitakartavyatākatva eva sattvāt। śruteśca adavacchedakakoṭipraviṣṭatvāt। vidheyakoṭipraviṣṭatve api
vidheyatvaṃ na svīkartuṃ śakyam। tathā sati vahnitvamanumitamiti [] atrāyamāśaya ityādinā। anumiteḥ pūrvamasiddhatvāditi। anumitiprākkālīnajñānaviṣayatānavacchedakatvādityarthaḥ। tena parāmarśaviṣayatve api mahānasīyavahnyādeḥ na vidheyatānupapattiḥ। atra
sādhyasambandhasiddhimātreṇaiva sambhavati। parvato vahnimānityādau parvatīyavahnyādivadityavadheyam। tādṛśaśrutyatiriktasya maṅgalakartavyatāyāṃ pramāṇatvaṃ vyavacchidyate। tacca na yujyate। amaṅgalaṃ kartavyaṃ samāptiphalakatvāt'
ityanumānasya tatra pramāṇatvaṃ sambhavatītyata āha - [] evakāro apyarthaka iti। tadbījantu vyāpakatāghaṭakatvasāmānādhikaraṇyaghaṭakatvayorasambhavaḥ। yathāśrutadīpikāvākyārthāsvārasyaṃ ceti। vidhimantarā rāgādīti। atra cāntarāśabdasyābhāvor'thaṃḥ। tasya sāmānādhikaraṇyasambandhena rāge
anvayaḥ। atra ca vidheḥ svabodhitakartavyatākatvasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvasambandhenānvayaḥ। sāmānādhikaraṇyaghaṭakadvitīyavṛttirviṃṣayatayā। tadavacchedaketi।
vidheyatāvacchedaketyarthaḥ। prayojyatvamarthaḥ। ktapratyayārthaḥ vidheyaḥ। tathā ca phalitam। yadyapi maṅgale rutibodhatakartavyatākatvasandehena tātparyam। ata eva
rātriśrāddhādivāraṇāyāvigītatvaviśeṣaṇamapi saphalam। anyathā tatra tadvaiyarthyāt। avigītatvaṃ dharmaśāstrādyadhīnanivṛttiviṣayabhinnatvam। ādipadena niṣphalatvapramāsaṅgrahaḥ। tena anu kuryāt niṣphalam' ityādeḥ anuvādarūpatve vyutkramakṛtadarśādau na vyabhicāraḥ।
etatsarvamabhipretyāgre [] saṅkṣepa ityuktam। [] vedoktatvajñāneneti। śiṣṭatvamityarthaḥ। vedāvihitahiṃsādikarmāṇi vedoktatvabhrameṇa yaḥ karoti tadvāraṇāya vedoktatvajñānaṃ pramārūpamiti bhāvaḥ। [] ahiṃsādikartarīti। trāhiṃsāśabdena hiṃsāvirodhivyāpāro
vivakṣitaḥ। dīpikāyām [] niṣiddhatvāditi। idaṃ cāpātataḥ। na kuryādityāderanuvādarūpatāyāḥ prāgevoktatvāt। [] tarkapadasyetyādiṣaṣṭhyāḥ viśeṣyatvamarthaḥ। tasya bhrame anvayaḥ। bhramamityatra nivṛttyanvayi pratiyogitvaṃ dvitīyārthaḥ। nirvacane anvayaḥ। dīpikāyām saṅkṣepeṇeti। svalpatvenetyarthaḥ।
vaiśiṣṭye tṛtīyā, tacca kathanānvitam। atrāhiṃsāśabdeneti। ahiṃsākartarītyanupapannaṃ syāt। hiṃsāvirodhivyāpāro ahiṃsetyarthaḥ। naño atra virodhyarthakatvaṃ
atadanyatadviruddhatadabhāveṣu nañ' iti śāstrakṛdvacanam। [] padasambandhitvāṃśasyeti। na ca viṣayatve abhidhārūpitatvasya vyarthatvāt kiṃ tadabhidhāneneti vācyam। viṣayatāyāmabhidhānirūpitatvasya niveśenādoṣāt।
vṛttyaniyāmakatayā hetutāvacchedakasambandhatvaṃ savivādamityabhiprāyaḥ। vācyam। abhidhāviṣayatvasya nirūpitatvasambandhenābhidhāviśiṣṭatvena lakṣaṇatvādityāśayāditi। dīpikāyām [] padārthān vibhajate iti। vipūrvakabhajadhātoḥ
svasamabhivyāhṛtadvitīyāntapadopasthāpyatāvacchedakavyāpyadharmaprakārakajñānajanakaśabdor'thaḥ। dvitīyāntapadaupasthāpyatāvacchedakatvamupalakṣaṇam। evamuttaratrāpi bodhyam। nanu pṛthivyādipadārthānāmanantatvāt kathaṃ padārthānāṃ [] dravyatvādirūpā iti। nanvatropādhiṣu
kiṃ nāma saptatvam? na tāvat saṅkhyārūpaṃ sambhavati uktayukteḥ। saṅkhyārūpatvāyogāt। na ca bhramamādāya tadapapattiriti vācyam। saptavyavahārānupapattiprasaṅgāt। tathāpi ekamātravṛttidharma ekatvam। abhidhānirūpiteti।
abhidhayā anirūpitaṃ viṣayatvaṃ yasyetyarthaḥ। abhidhīyaviṣayatvasyeti। abhidhayā nirūpitaṃ yat viṣayatvaṃ tasyetyarthaḥ। kiñcidviśiṣṭānyatvam।
bhedavadanyatvaṃ vā। tathā cāyamanugamaḥ pitaguṇaniṣṭhaviśeṣyatvādyanyatamavaddharmaviśiṣṭatvaṃ saptatvam। viśiṣṭatvaṃ vācyam। evaṃ ca tatrāpi bhedeṣu saptatvasyoktarityā apekṣābuddhiviśeṣasyaiva vaktavyatayā anavasthāprasaṅgāditi cet - na।
sattvopagamāt na samūhālambanajñānamādāyātiprasaṅgaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyasambandheneti। [] evamagrimagranthasyāpīti। navaiva dravyāṇītyādiretyarthaḥ। dīpikāyām
adhikasaṃkhyāvyavacchedārthakatvāditi। atrādhikasaṃkhyāśabdaḥ aṣṭamapadārthaparaḥ। vyavacchedo nāma niṣedhasiddhiḥ। tathā ca atrīn aṣṭamapadārthaniṣedhasiddhiriti bhāvaḥ। prakṛtasaptatvaviśiṣṭasaṃkhyā adhikasakhyāpadārthaḥ। [] nanvatiriktaḥ padārtha iti। yadyapi
padārthavibhājakadharmaḥ atirikto vā na vetyarthaḥ। svāśrayavṛttitveti। tadvṛttitvaṃ aṣṭatvasaṃkhyāyām। dravyatvādyabhāvatvāntānyatamādhikaraṇavṛttitvam। tathā ca
dharmiprasiddhyā koṭiprasiddhyā ca vikalpasiddhiḥ। durghaṭatvāt। vikalpe anyatarakoṭerabādhitatvaniyamāt tādṛśakūṭādhikaraṇatvasya cāprasiddhatvāt kūṭatvasya durvacatvācca। na। bhedānāmekaviśiṣṭāparatvena niveśe aprasiddhiprasaṅgena
tāvadviviṣayakadhīviṣayatvasya pratyekameva bhedeṣu sattvāt। [] iti vyavacchedārthakatvāditi। ityākārakaniścayaphalakatvādityarthaḥ। na ca tādṛśaniścaya eva māstu iti śaṅkanīyam। ṣoḍaśapadārthānāṃ kḷptapadārthāntarbhāvasādhane tādṛśavyāptiniścayasyāvaśyāpekṣitatvāt। [] saṃgrahe dravyaguṇetyādi। atra ca dravyādyanyatamatvasambandhena aekatra
vyutpattivaicitryāt। apadārthatvaṃ dravyādisaptānyatamatvavyāpyam' iti bodhastu auttarakāliko mānasa eva। prapañcitaṃ cedadasmābhiranyatra। dīpikāyām [] dravyādisaptānyatamatvaṃ nāmetyādi। atrāyamāśayaḥ
eva dravyādyanyatamatvaṃ, evaṃ vaiparītyamapyevamūhyam। anyathā durvacatayā tādṛśābhāvasyāpi aprasiddhyāpatteḥ। yadyapi saptatvasya tadviṣayakadhīviśeṣaviṣayatvarūpatvaṃ suvacam। tathāpi viṣayatvasya pratyekaṃ vartate। asmatpakṣe tu tādṛśabhedaṃ prati
sudhībhiḥ vibhāvanīyam। [] vastutastvityādi। idamatra nirvahatīti lakṣaṇāśrayaṇamayuktam। kiñcillakṣaṇā hi śakyasambandharūpā tādṛśānyatamavati lakṣaṇā na śakyate। tathā śaktyaprasiddhiḥ upapādanāyaiva।
[] dravyamiti jātyekavacanamiti। nanvatra kiṃ nāma jātigatamekatvam? na tāvat guṇaḥ। tatra tadanaṅgīkārāt। iti cet, ucyate-ekamātravṛttidharmāvacchinne ekavacanasya śaktiḥ। prakṛtyarthe anvayaḥ। avacchedakatvaṃ ca
avacchedakatā cāśrayatāsambandhena। jātyekatvaparavākyasthale prakṛtyarthe anvayaḥ। sā ca svāśrayāśrayatvasambandhena। ekatvamanyatrāpi bodhyam। svāśrayatveti। svaṃ
paśumadbhedaḥ tatpratiyogitāvacchedakatvaṃ ca paśau। svakaraṇaketyatra svaśabdaḥ prakṛtyarthapaśuparaḥ। svāśrayāśrayatvetyādi। prathavasvaśabdaḥ ekatvaparaḥ। dvitīyasvaśabdaḥ tṛtīyasvaśabdaśca prakṛtyarthadravyaparaḥ।
bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā tatkatvamityarthaḥ। svaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvamiti yāvat। [] mīmāṃsakamatamityādi। dūṣaṇaṃ anupapannatvaprakārakajñānānukūlayuktikathanam। tumuna icchaivārthaḥ,
tasyāḥ upanyāse ūrvavadevānvayaḥ। [] atiriktatvaṃ vyasthāpayitum ityatrāpi uktarītireva। nirākaraṇaṃ tu abhāvaprakārakajñānānukūlaśabdaḥ। [] antarbhāvamityatra dvitīyāyāḥ pratiyogitvamarthaḥ। tasya nirākaraṇaikadeśe abhāve anvayaḥ।
viṣayasādhakatvaṃ dyotyate। ataḥ tasyā bhramatve na viṣayasādhakatvamiti śaṅkānirāsāyābādhitetyuktam। atra ca dravyasādhakahetudvayakathanaṃ yūnādhikadṛṣṭāntamabhisandhāya। [] kālikādisambandheneti। atrādipadena viṣayatāsambandhasya parigrahaḥ। na tu daiśikaviśeṣaṇatāyāḥ, tathā sati mūrteṣu
sādhyasattvena vyabhicārānavakāśāt। [] atiprasaktatve apīti। janyaguṇadāvityādiḥ। dravyatve siddhe satīti। atra dravyatva iti saptamyāḥ anumitirūpasiddhirarthaḥ। tasyā uttarakālīnatvasambandhena nirākaraṇe anvayaḥ। dīpikāyām [] tamaso
nākāśādipañcake antarbhāva iti। tamovṛttirityanvayabodhaḥ। [] vāyāvanantarbhūtatvasādhakahetvantarasattvāt। na hi sparśābhāvāderapi ākāśādyanantarbhūntatvasādhakatvaṃ sambhavati, yabhicārāt।
navīnamatamanusṛtya prakāśikāyām [] vastutastviti। iti। ityarthaḥ। nyūnādhikadṛṣṭāntamabhisamndhāyeti। tamaso
tātpayam। vyabhicārāditi। tamaḥ ākāśādyanantarbhūtaṃ sparśābhāvāditi hi prayoktavyam। tatra ca sādhyābhāvavati ākāśādau sparśābhāvasattvāt vyabhicāra ityarthaḥ।
[] viṣamavyāptamiti। viṣamavyāptatvaṃ ca sādhyāvyāpakatve sati sādhyavyāpyatvam। samavyāptatvaṃ ca sādhyavyāpakatve sati sādhyavyāpyatvam। nanu sārvakālikagamanaṃ labhyate।
vāyvanantarbhūntatvasādhane vyabhicāra ityata āha [] sadāgatiḥ vijātīyakriyeti। evaṃ ca vaijātyaviśeṣasya janyavāyukriyāyāmapi sattvāt na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। kḷptadravyeṣvanantarbhāvādityartha iti। idamatra pariśeṣānumānaṃ yathā ghaṭa iti।
sādhyakoṭau dravyatvaniveśaḥ। guṇādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya hetukoṭau dravyatvaniveśaḥ। guṇādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya hetukoṭau dravyatvaniveśaḥ। guṇādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya hetukoṭau dravyatvaniveśaḥ। pṛthivyādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya
pṛthivyādīti। pṛthivyādyanantarbhūntatvaviśiṣṭadravyatvaṃ heturiti। vyatirekavyāpterdurgrahatvāditi। dīpikāyām [] prauḍhetyādi। prauḍhatvamutkṛṣṭatvaṃ mahattvāśrayatvam, tejaḥ paramāṇuvāraṇāya mahatvaniveśaḥ।
tejastruṭivāraṇayotkṛṣṭatvaniveśaḥ। prakāśakatvaṃ codbhūtānabhibhūtarūpavattvam। cakṣurādivāraṇāyodbhūteti। suvarṇādivāraṇāyānabhibhūteti। ghaṭādivāraṇāya tejaḥ- padam। tadabhāveneti।
sadāgatimattvabhāvene tyarthaḥ। mahāprabhāvatvāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāva eva tamaḥ। digityuktam। prakāśikāyām [] ālokāsahakṛteti।
ālokājanyacākṣuṣanirūpitalaukikaviṣayatvāditi paryavasitārthaḥ। tenānyatra cakṣuṣaḥ ālokarūpasahakārikāraṇaviśiṣṭatve api na kṣatiḥ। kālavidhayā ālokasya kāraṇatvāt asiddhiriti cet - na। kālatvāvacchinnālokaniṣṭhajanakatākatvābhāvasya niveśāt।
spārśanamādāya ghaṭādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya cākṣuṣeti। viṣayatāyāṃ ghaṭādīnāmityādinā। aghaṭe tama' ityākārakapratyakṣe alaukikyā jñānapratyāsattyā ghaṭādīnāṃ viṣayatve api na tatra vyabhicāra ityarthaḥ। pustakepu atamovān ghaṭaḥ' iti pāṭho anupapannaḥ।"asmāyāmedhāsrajoviniḥ"
rūpaniṣpatteḥ। matupguṇayorasambhavāt। upanītaṃ viśeṣaṇatayaiveti bhānāsaṃbhavenālaukikaviṣayatāmādāya ghaṭādau vyabhicārāsambhavācca। vidāṅkurvantu vidvāṃsaḥ। [] vyāpyadharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvam। idaṃ ca
pakṣadṛṣṭāntayorabhedaśaṅkānirāsāya। ayamatra bhāvaḥ - gauravamanantāvayavakalpanayāpi। tattamaścākṣuṣasyākasmikatvavāraṇāya asādhāraṇakāraṇāntarakalpanasyāvaśyakatayā gauravamiti। [] prāgabhāvādītyādipadenadhvaṃsaparigrahaḥ। [] āvaśyaketi। idaṃ ca tamobhāva eva tejaḥ kiṃ na syāditi vinigamanāvirahaśaṅkānirāsāya। anyathā auṣṇaṃ tejaḥ' iti
uṣṇasparśapratītyanupapattiprasaṅgāt। dīpikāyām [] dravyatvajātimattvamiti। atra jātipadaṃ samavāyena dravyatvasya lakṣaṇatvalābhāya। na tu tadapi lakṣaṇaghaṭakaṃ, tathā sati vyāpyatānavacchedakatvena vyāpyatvāsiddhyāpātāt। prakāśikāyām
[] saṃyogajanakatāvacchedakatayeti। atredamanumānamabhimatam - daṇḍādiniṣṭhaghaṭādikāraṇatāvaditi। asiṃdhyato dharmasya jātitve parāmarśāt dravyatvajātyavacchinnatvasiddhiḥ। kiñcijjātyavacchinnatvasya pratibandhakābhāvaniṣṭhakāraṇatāyāṃ vyabhicāraḥ syāditi tadupekṣitam।
arthāntaramiti vācyam। tatsamaniyatadharmasyaiva tadavacchedakatvāt tadādāyānumānaparyavasānāsambhavāt। asattādikaṃ yadi sattādijātyavacchinnatvānumityasambhavāt। evamuttaratrāpi bodhyam। samavāyena saṃyogāpattivāraṇāya bodhyam।
[] lakṣaṇalakṣyatāvacchedakayorabheda iti। ityākārakasiddhisattvāt anumityanupapattiḥ। asamānākārakaniścayasyāpi pratibandhakatvāt। siṣādhayiṣānudhāvane ca prayāsagauravamityabhiprāyaḥ।
dravyam' ityākārakaprācīnamatopanayasya bādhakābhāvāt। śābdabuddhiṃ pratyeva taddharmabhedasya kāraṇatvasya vaktavyatvāt। anyathā adravyaṃ jātimat' ityādiprayogānupapatteḥ। yatkiñcillakṣyāvṛttitvamityartha iti।
niṣkarṣaḥ। anyathā yathāśrute asambhavāpatteḥ। asambhavino vāraṇāya dvitīyadalam, lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। kālikasambandhena tatsambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ।
sattvāt taddoṣatādavasthyamiti vācyam। lakṣaṇatāvacchedakadharmaḥ tasya vivakṣitatvāt। yadyapi tādṛśapratiyogitāvacchedakatāparyāptyadhikaraṇatvavivakṣayā na doṣaḥ। [] alakṣye lakṣaṇasyeti। iśeṣaṇatāviśeṣeṇa
lakṣyatāvacchedakāvacchinnapratiyogitākabhedavannirūpitalakṣaṇatāghaṭakasambandhāvacchinnādheyatvamityarthaḥ। ghaṭādau ghaṭādibhedāsattvāt gandhādaiṃ nātivyāptiḥ। na vā kālikena jalādau gandhasattvamādāya। viśeṣaṇatāviśeṣeṇetyasya bhedavatve anvayaḥ।
pṛthivyādibhedasya kālikasaṃbandhena sattvāt taddoṣatādavasthyam। labhyate। tacca na yujyate - ativyāptadharme atiprasaṅgāt ityataḥ prakāśikāyāṃ mātrapadaṃ kṛtsnārthakatayā vyācaṣṭe [] mātrapadamiti। [] sambandhaviśeṣetyādi। lakṣaṇatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnodheyatāpratiyogitākasvarūpamevātrasaṃbandhaviśeṣaḥ।
paryavasitam। tena dvitvādyavacchinnādheyatāpratiyogitākasvarūpasya guṇādivṛttitvaṃ prati vyadhikaraṇatvāt। atra ca mātrapadasya labhyate। tathā satyativyāptadharme atiprasaṅgāt vivakṣitumaśakyaṃ cetyālocya etat [] lakṣyavṛttitvasāmānyābhāvasphorakamiti।
lakṣaṇatāvacchedakadharmavattvamasambhavaḥ। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatvaṃ dvitvādyavacchinnapratiyogitayā asambhavāpatteḥ। etena viśeṣarūpeṇa saṃsargatvānabhyupagame api na kṣatiḥ। lakṣyatāvacchedakādiprakāreṇaivādhikaraṇapraveśaḥ। tena sambandhāntareṇa
lakṣyatāvacchedakādyadhikaraṇamādāya na doṣaḥ। [] ekaśaphavattvamitīti। yadyapi śate saḍkhyārūpam। api tu svāśrayapādavṛttitvasvabhinnatvobhayasambandhena śaphaviśiṣṭānyatvarūpaṃ pāribhāṣikaṃ jñeyam। ativyāptiśarīre
lakṣyavṛttitvaniveśanamanāvaśyakamityabhiprāyeṇa [] duṣṭasaṅkarepīti, nyāyāditi। duṣṭasvarūpaikye api bhāvaḥ। prācīnagrantheṣu digiti dṛśyate। tatra cāyaṃ bhāvaḥ - tatroktanyāyāvakāśaḥ। ekatrāsambhavina evānyatra vyavahāre
bādhakābhāvāt tatroktanyāyāvakāśa iti। labhyate। avyāptyādipratyekadoṣagrastadharmeṃ'pi ityartha iti। yāvat pratyekādhikaraṇasyaiva kūṭādhikaraṇatvāt na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। [] avyāptyādītyādipadenāsambhavaparigrahaḥ।
[] anyādṛśamiti। tathā ca asādhāraṇapadaṃ vakṣyamāṇārthe pāribhāṣikamiti। sādhāraṇaṃ na bhavatītyasādhāraṇaṃ iti vyutpattyā prakāśikāvataraṇikātātparyam। aavyāptyasambhavagrastayorvāraṇāya pāṭhaḥ prāmādikaḥ।
tatrāvyāptyaprasakteḥ। [] avyāptasyeti prācīnakośeṣu pāṭho dṛśyate। samavāyena lakṣaṇamityādāvasambhavini gaganadāvativyāptiḥ। tatpāṭhasādhutvāsambhavāt। yadi ca tatpāṭhasādhutve apyāgrahaḥ, tadā
niveśena tadupapādanīyam। [] tatpadasya sārthakyamāha - [] dharmapadamiti। [] lakṣaṇatāghaṭakasambandheneti। lakṣyatāvacchedakasambandhena vivakṣaṇīyamityarthaḥ। [] vyāpakatvādityādinā vyāpyatvaparigrahaḥ। asādhāraṇatvamiti niṣkarṣaḥ। vaiśiṣyaṃ ca
vacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvobhayasambandhena। avacchadekatvamiti। prathamasambandhaghaṭakamavacchedakatvamityarthaḥ। tathā ca lakṣyatāvacchedake tatpratiyogitāvacchedakatvaṃ sāsnāditve। evaṃ svaṃ gotvaṃ
lakṣaṇatāvacchedake sāsnāditve draṣṭavyam। evaṃ ca lakṣaṇatāvacchedakaparamiti vivekaḥ। svāvacchinnādhikaraṇavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhena। lakṣaṇatāghaṭakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। jalādau kālikādinā
gandhādisattvāt vyāpyatāyāṃ tanniveśaḥ। anyacca svayamūhyam। [] asādhāraṇatvasya vighaṭakā iti। atra vipūrvaghaṭadhātoḥ abhāvor'thaḥ। tathā ca ityarthaḥ। tādṛśābhāvaścātivyāpteiśeṣyābhāvaprayuktaḥ। avyāptyasambhavinośca viśeṣaṇābhāvaprayukta ityabhipretyāha - [] ativyāptāviti। pakṣatāvacchedakasāmānādhikaraṇyamātreṇa
hetvabhāvavattvaṃ bhāgāsiddhiḥ। tadavacchedena tadabhāvavattvaṃ svarūpāsiddhiriti vivekaḥ। atra ca bhāgāsiddheḥ avacchedakāvacchedena pakṣadharmatājñānaṃ prati virodhitayā hetvābhāsatvamiti dhyeyam। [] vyāvṛttireveti। ayamāśayaḥ -
avyāvṛttirvyavahāro vā lakṣaṇasya prayojanam' iti। vyāvṛttiḥ itarabhedaḥ। vyavahāraḥ jñānajanakaśabdaḥ। prayojanaṃ jñāpyam। tathā ca vyāvartakatvam itarabhedānumāpakatvam। vyāvahārikatvaṃ vyavahārānumāpakatvam। prakṛte ca vyāvṛttireva lakṣaṇajñāpyā
ityekaṃ matam। vyāvṛttivyavahārobhayaṃ jñāpyamityaparaṃ matam। ativyāptiriti। vyāvartakasyetyatra vyāpyatvarūpaviśiṣṭeti। vyāpyatvarūpaṃ yat viśiṣṭaṃ tadabhāvasaṃpādakāḥ।
viśeṣyābhāveti। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpyatvarūpaṃ yadviśeṣyaṃ tadabhāvaprayukta ityarthaḥ। viśeṣaṇābhāveti। lakṣyatāvacchedakavyāpakatvarūpaṃ yadviśeṣaṇaṃ tadabhāvaprayukta ityarthaḥ।
vyāṅpūrvakavṛtudhātoritarabhedor'thaḥ। akapratyayasyānumitijanaka ityabhiprāyeṇāha [] itarabhedānumitijanakasyetyartha iti। anumitijanakatvaṃ liṅgaparāmarśasyaiva, na tu parāmṛśyamānaliṅgasya। tathā ca gandhādervyāvartaṅkatvānupapattiḥ। na
iti vācyam। evamapi abhidheyatvādāvativyāptikathanāsaṅgateśca। tasyāpyuktarītyā lakṣyatvāt। na ca tādṛśajanakatāvacchedakaviṣayatāśrayatvaṃ taditi vācyam। evamapi itarabhedavyāptidhaṭakābhāvādāvativyāpteḥ
vyāvartakatāpatteśca। tathā ca dharmatvameva lakṣaṇalakṣaṇamityāśaṅkāyāṃ niṣkarṣārthamāha [] itarabhedavidheyetyādi। pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviśeṣyatānirūpitaviṣayatetyarthaḥ। tadasat। samānākārakajñāneṣu viṣayatābhedābhāvena udāsīnāṃśe
samūhālaṃbanamādāyāsambhavasya durvāratvāt। pakṣatāvacchedakāvacnnitvaniveśaḥ। kiñcidavacchinnatvaniveśe api madupekṣitam। vastutastu mukhyaviśeṣyatānirūpitatvameva prakāratāyāṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā bhāvasyādheyatvaṃ lakṣaṇamityādau
yādheyatve atiprasaṅgāt। atra vyāvartakatāprasaṅgaḥ। ata itarabhedavidheyakatvasya tatra niveśaḥ। itarabhedatvāvacchinnavidheyatākatvaṃ vivakṣaṇīyam। aghaṭaḥ niveśyam। atyathā
marśīyajanakatāmādāyāvyāptigrastadharme atiprasaṅgāt। niveśyā। anthā pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchedena tatsāmānādhikaraṇyamātreṇa taddoṣatādavasthyam। athaivamapi pṛthivītarabhedādāvativyāptirduvāraiva। na ca
iti vācyam। evamapi tathātvāt। tādṛśānumityanupadhāyakajñānavṛttitvasya niveśāsaṃbhavāt। vivakṣitatvāt। tādṛśajanyatāviśiṣṭaviṣayatvamiti niṣkarṣaḥ।
svanirūpitajanakatāvacchedakatvasvāśrayānumityupadhāyakāprāmāṇyajñānānāskanditajñānīyatvobhayasambandhena। bhramaviśiṣṭānyatvam। panthāḥ। [] eveneti। nanu
pṛṣṭhatāḍanena daṇḍabhaṅganyāyāt; ata āha [] uktalakṣaṇeti [] abhidheyatvādibhinnatvaṃ ceti। idamatra tadbhinnatvaniveśanaṃ prakṣālanādinyāyenāyuktam। sattvāt ativyāptiḥ - iti tanna। ghaṭādilakṣaṇe jñānavadanyatvādāveva lakṣaṇagamanāt। ato
vivakṣitatvāditi। [] na tāvatsāmānyato bhedānumāpakatvamiti। sāmānyato bhedatvena। tasilo avacchinnatvamarthaḥ। tasya ca bhedānumāpakatvaghaṭakabhedavidheyatāyāmanvayaḥ। [] yatkiñcidubhayatvāvacchinnapratiyogitāketi। aghaṭaḥ vyāvartakatvasya sūpapādatvāt iti bhāvaḥ। yadyapi aghaṭo bhedavān
vyāvṛttisādhāraṇyārthamapi tathoktiḥ। anyathā siddhasādhanāpatteḥ iti dhyeyam। vyatirekidharmāṇāṃ yakiñcibdyavartakatayeti। gauḥ tadupapādanasambhavāditi bhāvaḥ। [] nāpi
viśiṣyetyādi। itarabhedatvāvacchinnavidheyatākānumitijanakatāvacchedakaniruktaviṣayatāśrayatvamityarthaḥ। dharmintāvacchedaketyādinyāyena na doṣaḥ। [] gotvādisamanaiyatyasya tatrāsattvāditi। padārthatvasamaniyatatvasya lakṣyāprasiddhyā alakṣaṇatvena
tatra tatsattvasyākiñcitkaratvāt iti bhāvaḥ। iti। svāvacchinnetarabhedānumāpakatvasambandhena gotve sādhya ityarthaḥ। tenāgre abhidheyatvādau vyabhicārakathanaṃ saṃgacchate। anyathā durvacatvāt। asmatpakṣe tu padārthatvaṃ prati uktasambandhasya
vyadhikaraṇatayā sādhyābhāvasya prasiddhatvena vyabhicāraḥ suvaca eva। [] abhidheyatvādibhinnatvaṃ ceti। cakāro vākārārthaḥ। anyathā taddharmāvacchinnetarabhedabhinnatvasya niveśenaiva tatsamuccāyakatvāsambhavādasaṅgateḥ। atra sāmānyavyāptisthale
prakṛte anumitisambhavaḥ ityabhipretyāha - [] adhikavicāra iti। [] tena rūpeṇa vyavahartavyajñānaṃ vineti। itarabhedādiprakāreṇa pakṣaviṣayakaparāmarśaṃ vinetyarthaḥ। tadrūpāvacchinneti।
lakṣyatāvacchedakapṛthivītvādyavacchinanapratipādaketyarthaḥ। vyavahārāsambhavāt - vyavahārānumānāsambhavāt। tathā ca taddharmāṃvacchinnavyāvahārikatvam। tacca aghaṭaḥ pṛthivīti vyavahartavyaḥ, akṣatamiti bhāvaḥ। etena dīpikāyāṃ lakṣaṇaprayojanatve lakṣaṇajñāpyatve
vyavahārasādhanatvāt vyavahārānumāpakatvādityartho bodhyaḥ। sambhavati। yadvā pratiyogivyadhikaraṇalakṣyaniṣṭhābhāvapratiyogitvasyaiva nāvyāptirityāśayena śaṅkate prakāśikāyām [] nanvityādi। guṇāśrayatvalakṣaṇamiti। guṇātmakalakṣaṇamityarthaḥ। āśrayatvakathanaṃ lakṣaṇatāghaṭakasambandhapradarśanāya। etena -
avyāpyavṛttittvāt। guṇapratiyogikatvopalakṣitasamavāyena guṇavattvasya samavāyaikyapakṣe guṇādāvativyāptiḥ। dūṣaṇamanavakāśam। sattāviśeṣaṇatvabhramavāraṇāya [] jātiviśeṣaṇamiti। atra ca guṇasamānādhikaraṇatvaṃ guṇasamavāyivṛtterguṇatvasya vyudāsaḥ। atha aekaṃ rūpaṃ
pṛthagvyavahāraprasaṅgaḥ। svāvadhikapṛthaktvasāmānādhikaraṇyasya svasminnapyabādhāt iti cet - na। sāmānādhikaraṇyasya svasmin svāvadhikapṛthaktvasambandhatvānupagamāt। kalpanākalpanayośca phalānurodhitvāt। vastutastu arūpaṃ rasāt pṛthak' ityādau
bhānābhyupagamāt na doṣa iti। [] kālikādītyādipadena samavāyasvarūpobhayaghaṭitasāmānādhikaraṇyaparigrahaḥ। [] hetudharmitāvacchedakaketi। hetvavacchinnaviśeṣyatāketyarthaḥ।
asamānākārakasiddheścāvirodhitvāditi bhāvaḥ। ayamatrāśayaḥ - vyatirekavyāpteranumānāṅgatvena na kāpyanupapattiḥ। lakṣaṇaprayojanasiddhirnirābādhaiveti। upādhisaṅkarasyādoṣatvādityata āha - [] jātitvenābhimateti।
jātitvenāpāditetyarthaḥ। tathā ca tulyayuktyā doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। jñānajanakasvalpaśabdarūpasaṅgrahābhedabodho varṇanīyaḥ। prathamatrikasya madhye athaśabdaḥ। vyakterityādiślokoktajātibādhakatvaṃ ca
jātijātimattvānyataraprakārakajñānapratibandhakajñānaviṣayatvam। bhedavadanyatvaṃ vā। tajjñānasya tadvadanyatvajñānavidhayā uktobhayasambandhena prameyaviśiṣṭatvādirūpānekasamavetatvaghaṭitajātitvajñānapratibandhakatvam। svasamavetatveti।
nīlaghaṭarūpaprameyaviśiṣṭe ghaṭatvaṃ tadbhinnatvamākāśatve। evaṃ svaṃ tadanyatvamākāśe iti bodhyam। jātiviśiṣṭatvaparyavasitam। tacca jātitvābhāvavyāpyamiti virodhitvam। tasya ca
siddham। jātiviśiṣṭatvam। tadapi ca jātitvābhāvavyāpyameva। tasya tathātvaṃ ca dharmaśāstrasiddham। viruddhajātīnāṃ parasparaṃ vyāpyajātyā saṃbandhatrayaniveśaḥ।
ttajjātijñānakāraṇatānantyarūpāniṣṭaprasañjanarūpeha vivakṣitā। jātirjātimatītyākārakajñānavirodhitvam। svatovyāvṛttatvarūpalakṣaṇasvarūpasya hāniḥ। svatovyāvṛttatvaṃ ca jātimattve anupapattiḥ। sajātīyānāṃ padārthānāṃ parasparaṃ bhedaḥ
ityāpattiviṣayatayā viśeṣasya jātimattve bādhakatvam। aayaṃ niyamena jātipuraskāreṇaiva vyāvartakatāyā vyabhicārāpatteḥ। asamavetatvam। tacca bahuvrīhibalāt samavetatvasāmānyābhāvaparyavasitam। tajjñānasya
nityānekasamavetarūpajātimattājñānavirodhitvam। etatsarvamabhipretyaiva [] saṅkṣepa ityuktam। dīpikāyām [] laghutvasya gurutvābhāvarūpatvāditi। na ca gurutvasya laghutvābhāvarūpatvamādāya vinigamanāviraha iti। svatantrecchasyeti nyāyenādoṣāt iti bhāvaḥ।
[] asamavāyīti। na cātra saṃyogabhinnatve sati asamavāyikāraṇamāstāmiti vācyam। ādyapatanāsamavāyikāraṇādau ativyāptivāraṇāya saṃyogāṃśasyāpi sārthakyāt। [] sattāyāḥ dravyatvāpekṣayetyādi।
apekṣāśabdasya pratiyogitānirūpakatvamarthaḥ। tṛtīyāyāśca vaiśiṣṭyam। adhikadeśavṛttitvaṃ ca svapratiyogyadhikaraṇavṛttitvasvādhikaraṇavṛttitvobhayasambandhenābhāvaviśiṣṭatvam। tṛtīyāntārthadravyatvaniṣṭhapratiyogitānirūpitatvaviśiṣṭatvānvayaḥ।
adhikadeśavṛttitvenetyatra tṛtīyāyā abhedor'thaḥ। paratvamiti vākyārthaḥ। [] dravyatvādīnāṃ sattāto aparatvamiti। vāśrayādhikaraṇavṛttyabhāvapratiyogitvarūpam। saṅkhyātvavyāpyadharmāvacchinnaprakāratākatādṛśaniścayaviśeṣyatvābhāvavattvam।
svāśrayeti। svaṃ dravyatve iti dravyatvasya sattāto aparatvamiti bhāvaḥ। viveka iti। tathā ca sāmānyaṃ trividham kevalaparam, kevalāparam, parāparam ceti।
lābhāt tadakathanamiti bhāvaḥ। nanu sattāyāḥ kevalaparatvakathanamanupapannam। premayatvādijātisattvāt sattāyāḥ iti। saṅkhyārūpam, samavāyāvṛttitvāt avyāvartakatvāt ca। evakāraśca
īdṛśapāribhāṣikatve tātparyagrahaḥ। yadvā ekatvamubhayāvṛttidharmaḥ। rkiñcidviśiṣṭānyatvam। evakārasya cādheyatāśrayabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvam abhāvaśca khaṇḍaśor'thaḥ। samavāyasya nirūpitatvasambandhenānvayaḥ।
nābhāve anvayaḥ। tādṛśābhāvasyacaikapadārthe anvayaḥ। tathā ca samavāyaḥ iti bodhaḥ iti abhiprāyeṇāvatārayati - dīpikāyām [] samavāyasya bhedo nāstītyāheti। atra ca bhedaḥ ādheyatāśrayabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakadharmaḥ। samavāyasyetyatra ṣaṣṭyā
nirūpitatvamarthaḥ। tasya ca bhedapadārthaghaṭakādheyatāyāmanvayaḥ। asadhātvarthādheyatāyāmapi vyutpattivaicitryādanvayaḥ। bhede anvayaḥ। tathā ca samavāyanirūpitādheyatvābhāvavāniti bodhaḥ।
taparāparatvāditi। rītyā parāparatvamiti bhāvaḥ। vyutpannatayā samavāyadvitvapakṣe apyuktavākyārthasaṅgatiḥ। yadvā bhedaḥ anyonyābhāvaḥ।
ekamātravṛttidharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākatvamarthaḥ। samavāyasyeti samavāyavṛttitvasyāsadhātvarthādheyatāyāmanvayaḥ। tathā ca samavāyaniṣṭhā samavāyanirūpitavṛttitvavāniti। itiśabdasya ityākārakamarthaḥ। tasya cābhedasambandhena
jñānotpattiprayojakaśabdarūpabrūñarthaikadeśe jñāne anvayaḥ। tasya cākhyātārthakṛtāvanvayaḥ। anukūlatāsambandhena tādṛśajñānaṃ ca prakṛte mānasarūpaṃ bodhyam। tena prakṛte tasya śabdarūpatvāsaṃbhave api na kṣatiḥ।
prakāśikāyām [] rūpasamavāyeti। ayamatrāśayaḥ-tatsambandhena tatprakārakabhramatvaṃ ca tatsambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākatadabhāvavadviśeṣyakatvāvacchinnatatsambandhāvacchinnaprakārakatvam। tacca avāyuḥ samavāyena rūpavān' iti jñāne akṣatameva। tena tatpratiyogikatvāvacchinnanirūpakatākatatsambandhānuyogitāśrayaviśeṣyatākatvaghaṭitam।
iti na tādṛśajñānasya pramātvaprasaṅgaḥ। evaṃ rūpavattāprasaṅgaḥ ityabhipretya [] digityuktam। dīpikāyām [] uddeśakramānusārādityādi। pañcamyāḥ prayojyatvamarthaḥ। jñānoddeśaprayojyaśabdānukūlakṛtimāniti bodhaḥ।
prakāśikāyām [] prāthamye - prathamavaktavyatve। [] lakṣaṇīyavastuparamiti। prakṛtalakṣaṇāśrayayāvadvastuparimityarthaḥ। prakṛtalakṣaṇāśrayaghaṭādipratipādake atiprasaṅgatādavasthyam। tathā ca deyamiti bhāvaḥ। [] mātrapadamitīti। atra kecit
lakṣyatāvacchedaketarāprakārakatvaṃ mātrapadalabhyam। lakṣaṇavākyasya taditaralakṣaṇapratipādakatvānna tatrātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ- ityāhuḥ। tattuccham। mātrapadasya tallabhyatvāt। lakṣyatāvacchedaketarasaṃbandhavyavacchedabodhakatāyāṃ
vyutpattivirodhasya spaṣṭatvāt। padārthadvayasaṃsargabodhasyaiva lakṣyatāvacchedaketarāprakārakaśābdabodhāprasiddheśca। evaṃ ca uddeśalakṣaṇam। ato na pṛthivyādibhāge ativyāptiḥ। tādṛśasamudāyatvaniṣṭhanyūnavṛttitānirūpakatvena viśeṣaṇīyam। tena
na lakṣaṇādivākye ativyāptiḥ। tādṛśasamudāyatvaṃ ca vyāptisambandhena uddeśapadapravṛttinimittam। tenāśrayatayā tasyaikadeśasādhāraṇatve api na kṣatiḥ। samudāyatvasya vyāsajyavṛttitvena niveśaḥ। ataḥ dhīviśeṣaviṣayatvarūpasya tasyānanugame api na kṣatiḥ। yadi ca
tādṛśavarṇatvavyāpakadharmavattvamevoddeśalakṣaṇaṃ vaktavyam। svīkārānnātiprasaṅgāvakāśaḥ। yadyapi paryāyapadāntarādhīnaśābdabodhe prayojanāyojyaśabdānukūlakṛtimāniti bodhaḥ। prakāśikāyām [] prāthamye - prathamavaktavyatve। [] lakṣaṇīyavasatuparamiti। prakṛtalakṣaṇāśrayayāvadvastuparimityarthaḥ। tena na ghaṭādipade
prakṛtalakṣaṇāśrayaghaṭādipratipādake atiprasaṅgatādavasthyam। tathā ca deyamiti bhāvaḥ। [] mātrapadamitīti। atra kecit lakṣyatāvacchedaketarāprakārakatvaṃ mātrapadalabhyam। lakṣaṇavākyasya
taditaralakṣaṇapratipādakatvānna tatrātivyāptiriti bhāvaḥ- ityāhuḥ। tattuccham। mātrapadasya lakṣaṇāpratipādakatvasyaiva tallabhyatvāt। vyutpattivirodhasya spaṣṭatvāt। padārthadvayasaṃsargabodhasyaiva
lakṣyatāvacchedaketarāprakārakaśābbodhāprasiddheśca। evaṃ ca uddeśalakṣaṇam। ato na pṛthivyādibhāge ativyāpti। tādṛśasamudāyatvaṃ ca tādṛśasamudāyatvaniṣṭhanyūnavṛttitānirūpakatvena viśeṣaṇīyam। tena na lakṣaṇādivākye ativyāptiḥ। tādṛśasamudāyatvaṃ ca
vyāptisambandhena uddeśapadapravṛttinimittam। tenāśrayatayā tasyaikadeśasādhāraṇatve api na kṣatiḥ। samudāyatvasya vyāsajyavṛttitvena niveśaḥ। ataḥ dhīviśeṣaviṣayatvarūpasya tasyānugame api na kṣatiḥ। yadi ca viṣayatvamavyāsajyavṛttīti nāyaṃ
tādṛśavarṇatvavyāpakadharmavattvamevoddeśalakṣaṇaṃ vaktamavyam। svīkārānnatiprasaṅgāvakāśaḥ। yadyapi janyatāyāmasaṃbhavaḥ। tathāpi ato na doṣaḥ।
eva pṛthivyuddeśalakṣaṇamitirītyā tattaduddeśalakṣaṇaṃ bodhyam। na ca kiñcittvaniveśādananugama iti vācyam। tādṛśajanakatānirūpitādhikaraṇatāviśiṣṭadharmavattvasya vivakṣitatvāt। svādhikaraṇatāsvaviśiṣṭaviśiṣṭaviṣayatāśrayavarṇantvasambandhena।
svanirūpakajanakatāvacchedakatvasvāśrayajñānīyatvobhayasambandhena। tādṛśadharmaviśiṣṭānyatvam। adhikaraṇatāvaiśiṣṭyaghaṭakatayā paryavasitaḥ। ata eva apṛthivī gandhavatī' iti vākye nātiprasaṅga iti madekapariśīlitaḥ panthāḥ।
tādṛśāvayavasamevatādyakṛtimattvaṃ labhyate। āṅpūrvakasya rabhateḥ ādyakṛtibodhakatvāt। ktapratyayasya vidheyatvamarthaḥ। taccāsaṅgatam। kṛteḥ ātmamātradharmatvādityata āha [] ārabdhe janya u iti। [] parasparavirodhenetīti। virodhaḥ pratībandhakatvam, tatra svanirūpakavṛttitvasvāśrayavṛttitvobhayasambandhena। [] surabhigandhaṃ prati asurabhigandhasyetyādi। atra samavāyena
nobhayagandhotpattiriti bhāvaḥ। pratibandhakatāvacchedakasaṃbandhagauravādanādeyam। [] svāśrayasamavetatvasaṃbandhenetyādiriti। tṛtīyārthaḥ। tacca pratītisaṃbhavenetyatra pratītāvanveti। tṛtīyāyāḥ prayojyatvamarthaḥ।
tasya samavāyena gandhapratītau bhramadoṣavidhayā prayojakatvaṃ bodhyam। dīpikāyām [] citragandhānaṅgīkārāditi। tathā ca citragandhasyāsattvādavyāptirastyeveti bhāvaḥ। nyāyeneti। atrāyamāśayaḥ surabhyasurabhigandhavatparamāṇubhyāṃ
dvyaṇukamārabdham। tatastryaṇukādikrameṇa mahāvayaviparyantamutpannam। tatra ghaṭe gandhāsaṃbhavāt paramāṇugandhasya cāpratyakṣatvāt। vastutastu paramāṇugandhaviṣayakālaukikapratyakṣaṃ saṃbhavatyeva। yadi cāyaṃ
iti। [] gandhasamānādhikareṇeti। atrāpi pūrvavadevārtho bodhyaḥ। anyathā pūrvarītyā doṣāt। dravyabhinnabhinnatvam, tathā ca kathamasaṃbhavavāraṇamityata āha - [] dravyatvanyūnavṛttītyarthakamiti। dravyatvābhāvavadavṛttitvameva sattāvāraṇāya kuto na niveśyata ityata āha - [] teneti। [] dravyatvavyudāsa iti। dravyatvasya
svābhāvavadavṛtti'pi svasamānādhikaraṇābhāvapratiyogitvavirahāt। kālikasaṃbandhena tādṛśadharmavattvamādāyātivyāptivāraṇāya [] jātīti। nityatvamātramatra vivakṣitam। anekasamavetatvasya prakṛte avyāvartakatvāt। pṛthivījalānyataratvasya samavāyasaṃbandhaghaṭitasāmānādhikaraṇyavirahāt। kālikasaṃbandhena
tādṛśadharmavattvasya vivakṣaṇīyatayā uktānyataratvamādāya doṣāprasakteśca। nityatvaviraheṇaiva vāraṇaṃ bodhyam। [] svāśrayasaṃyuktatvasaṃbandhenetyādiriti। atrāpi pūrvavadevārtho varṇanīyaḥ। [] anugatarūpeṇa - svaniṣṭhādheyatāvacchedakātiriktatvenetyarthaḥ।
bhūtalādau ghaṭādisaṃyogini ativyāpteḥ। evaṃ samavāyādīnāṃ tādṛśarūpeṇa saṃbandhatvamapyaprāmāṇikam। bodhyamiti। pṛthivyāḥ samavāyena gandho lakṣaṇaṃ, samavāyena kapālasya ghaṭo lakṣaṇamiti bhāvaḥ।
dvividhā nityā anityā ceti। dve vidhe yasyāḥ sā dvividhā, vidhā uddeśyatāvacchedakapṛthivītvādisākṣādvyāpyadharma iti yāvat। dvitvasaṃkhyāśrayavibhājakadharmavati prakṛte vidhāpadasya nirūḍhalakṣaṇā। dvipadaṃ tātparyagrāhakam। nityānityayoḥ
nityānityānyataratvasaṃbandhenānvayaḥ pṛthivyām। sarvatra vibhāgavākyasthale tathā vyutpatteḥ svīkārāt। iti śabdaḥ hetugarbhaviśeṣaṇadyotakaḥ। tathā ca yataḥ tathā tataḥ pṛthivī dvitvāśrayatādṛśadharmavatīti bodhaḥ। ata eva nityānityapadayoḥ
strīliṅgatvamupapannam, tayoḥ pṛthivīpadasamānādhikaraṇatvāt। yattu-nityānityapade nityatvānityatvapare। tayorabhedasaṃbandhena vibhājakadharme anvaya - iti, tattuccham। ubhayābhedasya vibhājakadharme asaṃbhavāt।
mānābhāvāt। yādṛśārthasya lakṣaṇayā yatkiñcitpadārthabodhaḥ nityatvamanityatvamiti prayogāpatteḥ। pratibandhakatvādikalpane mahāgauravāpatteḥ। paramāṇurdviṃvidhaḥ-nityo anityaśca। dravyaṃ dvividham-pṛthivī jalaṃ
ceti prayogāpattiriti cet-na। dvividhetyādibahuvrīhau nirūḍhalakṣaṇā। viśeṣitatvaṃ ca svavyāpakapṛthivītvādisākṣādvyāpyavyāpyatvāśrayatvasvāśrayatvobhayasambandhenetyadoṣaḥ। cetyādiprayogaḥ। yadyapi nityatvānityatvayorjalādisādhāraṇatayā na
tayostathātvamakṣatam। sākṣātpadaṃ ca apṛthivī trividhā nityānityapaṭaśceti' ityādi prayogavāraṇāya। aāpo dvividhāḥ- nityānityāśceti' ityādāvapyuktaiva rītiḥ। nopādeyam।
iti prayogānavakāśaḥ। evaṃ ca bahuvrīhau tādṛśadvitvaviśiṣṭāśrayadharmavati nirūḍhalakṣaṇā। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ vasetyādibhedavattvatādātmyobhayasambandhena। svāśrayādhikaraṇakālavṛttitvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena।
pṛthivīsāmānyavibhāgo vā kāryapṛthivīvibhāgo vā। nādyaḥ, nityapṛthivyāḥ śarīrādāvantarbhāvāsambhavāt। nāpi rdvintīyaḥ, punaśśabdasvārasyavirodhāt। tena hi yaddharmāvacchinnasya prāgvibhāgaḥ prakāśikāyām [] atreti। tathā ca apunastrividhā' ityādau
pṛthivīsāmānyasyaiva vibhāgaḥ। aviṣayo mṛtpāṣāṇādiḥ- ityatra ādipadena paramāṇuparigrahasambhavāt। taijasaparamāṇusaṅgrahāditi bhāvaḥ। atra punaśśabdāsvārasyamavasarabījam। idamatra bodhyam - atra apunaḥ
śarīrāderekatra dvayamiti rītyā bhedapadārthe anyonyābhāve anvayaḥ। pañcamyāḥ prayojyatvamarthaḥ। śarīrādiviśeṣitabhedavṛttitritvaviśiṣṭavibhājakadharmavatīti bodhaḥ। bhedasya prayojakatvaṃ ca svajñānādhīnāpekṣābadhidvārā। uktarītyā
anyatrāpi bodhaḥ ūhyaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca pūrvavaditi। svasetyādibhedavāveti। svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvani ṣṭhavacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvetyarthaḥ। [] viṣayo mṛtpāṣāṇādiriti।
mṛtpāṣāṇādiniṣṭhāditānirūpakaḥ pārthivaviṣaya iti bodhaḥ। uddeśyatāvacchedakaniṣṭhatannirūpitādheyatāviśiṣṭatvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ svāśrayadharmatāviśiṣṭataddharmavattvasambandhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svavyāpyadharmāvacchinnabodhakapadapūrvapadapratipādyatāvacchedakatvasvavyāpyatvobhayasambandhena।
svaviṣayakajñānaviṣayasamudāyaghaṭakatvaṃ āditvam। svaṃ pārthivādiviṣayaḥ। tathā ca vyācakruḥ। atastantusamadāyatvasya dhīviśeṣaviṣayatvarūpatayā viśiṣya tattatpadārthajñāne samudāyatvasyaiva durnirūpatvāt।
tattatpadāsarvajñajīve asambhavāt। sambandhakoṭau prāmāṇyam। vyāpyatvaṃ cātra tatsāmānādhikaraṇyam, na tu tadabhāvavadavṛttitvam। tena aprameyaḥ pṛthivyādiḥ' ityādivākyasya na prāmāṇyānupapattiḥ।
prāmāṇyam। sāmānādhikaraṇyaniveśācca mṛtpāṣāṇādiriti vākyasya na prāmāṇyam ityalamativistareṇa। dravyasamānādhikaraṇabhinnatvamantyāvayavitvamiha vivakṣitam। śarīratvajātireva kuto lakṣaṇatayā noktā। evamindriyasyāpi
indriyatvajātimattvam। na ca śarīṃratvāderjātitvemānābhāvaḥ। adavācyatāpakṣakānumānasyaiva tathātvāt ata āha - śarīratvamiti। padavācyatāpakṣakānumānasyeti। śarīrapadavācyatā kiñciddharmāvacchinnā padavācyatātvāt ghaṭapadavācyatāvat ityanumānasyetyarthaḥ।
saṃyogasyodbhūtatvarūpajātyanākrāntatvāt। ataḥ tatpadaṃ [] udtatvaṃ na jātiriti। [] śuklanvādinā sāṅkaryāditi। saṅkara eva sāṅkaryam। cāturvarṇyāditvāt svārthe ṣyañ। tena pṛthivītvādinā saṅkarāditi pūrvagranthenāvirodhaḥ। [] kāraṇatvānupapatteriti।
tattududbhūtānyatamatvena cākṣuṣaṃ prati ekahetutvaṃ suvacam। vinigamanāviraha iti tu nāśaṅkanīyam। udbhūtatvasya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāve vinigamanāvirahasya tulyatvāt। vinigamanāviraheṇa mahāgauravaprasaṅgācceti। sāmānyaguṇabhinnetyarthaḥ। tena
dravyatvādikamādāyāsambhavavāraṇāya guṇapadamiti dhyeyam। rūpābhāveti। udbhūtarūpābhāvetyarthaḥ। tena nābhāvasya yogyatānupapattiḥ। [] sannikarṣaghaṭakatayeti। ayamatra bhāvaḥ- kālacakṣussaṃyoge akṣatameva। anyathā
rūpābhāvapratyakṣānupapatteriti। [] manaḥ padamiti। kāle sukhaṃ nāstīti hetutvaṃsvīkārāt। tathā ca tattadbhedakūṭaniveśagauravabhayena sarvamatasādhāraṇyāyoktaviśeṣaṇaṃ niveśitamiti bhāvaḥ। [] prayojanakathanaparatayeti। etena ghrāṇendriye anumānapramāṇamapi
sūcitam। tathā hi gandhasākṣātkāraḥ manobhinnendriyakaraṇakaḥ mānasānyapratyakṣasāmānyasākṣātkāratvāt। ghaṭādicākṣuṣajñānasāmānyaṃ mānasānyeti। [] evamuttaratra jñeyamiti। iti sūcanāya। śītasparśavatyaḥ āpaḥ ityādisaṅgrahavākye api
evameva bodhyam। na tu tadapi lakṣaṇapraviṣṭam। varṇayati। pradarśayati adbhiḥ indhanamityādinā। tathā ca indhanaśabdaḥ bhāve
lyuḍanta iti bhāvaḥ-ityāhuḥ। [] suvarṇasyetyādi। bodhaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaprayojyecchāviṣayatvasvaviṣayasamānakartṛkatvobhayasambandhena। [] sūvarṇaṃ pārthivamiti dīpikāvākyam sarvaṃ vākyamasati bādhake
viśeṣyanighnatvābhāvāccetyarthaḥ। vyāpāraviṣayaketyādi। vyāpāraḥ svamatasthāpanarūpaḥ। svaprayojyeti। svaṃ vyāpāraviṣayakecchā tatprayojyā। icchā pūrvapakṣaṃ tādṛśakṛtau।
suvarṇaviśeṣyaketyādi। prathamaviśiṣṭāntasya śaṅkānivṛttyanukūlavyāpāre dvitīyaviśiṣṭāntasya kṛtau cānbayaḥ। prathamavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svaprayojyatvasvasāmānādhikaraṇyobhayasaṃbandhena। svaprayojyecchāviṣayatvasvaviṣayasamānakartṛkatvobhayasaṃbandhena।
[] pārthivatvasādhakamityādinā। tena niravakāśā। suvarṇaṃ pārthivamevetyeva pratijñārthasya vācyatayā tatra caivakāreṇa taijasatvābhāvalābhāt। [] etena taijasatvābhāvasādhakahetukathanena। ayaṃ
prati kāraṇatāntaraṃ kalpanīyam। tasya pārthivatve tu na pṛthivītvasādhakapramāṇatayā sambhavatīti। [] suvarṇasya pītimagurutvāśrayata ityādi। bodhaḥ। [] asati pratibandhaka ityādi।
pratibandhakātyantābhāvaviśiṣṭātyantānalasaṃyogaviśiṣṭadravatvādityarthaḥ। agnisaṃyuktaghaṭe vyabhicāravāraṇāya dravatvaniveśanam। vaiśiṣṭyadvayaṃ ekakṣaṇāvacchinnaikādhikaraṇavṛttitvarūpam। [] atyantānalasaṃyogī pītimāśraya ityādi। atra cātyantānalasaṃyogīti
tadupādānam। jalamadhyasthaghṛte sāmānādhikaraṇyena vācyatvena ghaṭadāvaṃśato bādhavāraṇāya pītimāśrayatvamupāttam। pakṣatāvacchedakatvasvīkārāt na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। hetuḥ।
sādhyam। na ca dṛṣṭāntapakṣasādhāraṇasvatvānanugamāt pakṣe bodho dṛṣṭānte sādhyavaikalyaṃ vā। evaṃ dravadravyāntaretyatra vācyam। tṛtīyasaṃbandhaniveśaḥ। sidhyati dravye vyabhicārāvāraṇāya
hetukoṭau gurutvaniveśaḥ। rītyāanavasthā syāditi gurutvopādānam [] jalādikamādāyeti। atra ādānaṃ grahaṇam। tacca prakṛte viṣayatārūpam। lyapaḥ samānakartṛkatvamātramarthaḥ viṣayatārūpaparyavasānaśabdārthānvitam। samānakartṛkatvaṃ ceha
tannirūpakanirūpitatvam। jalādikamityatra dvitīyāyāḥ ādheyatvamarthaḥ। tannirūpakanirūpitānumānaviṣayatvarūpārthāntaradharmikasaṃbhavitvaprakārakajñānānukūlavyāpārakartetivākyārthaḥ। svasaṃyuktatvetyādi। svaṃ dravadravyaṃ jalaṃ tatsaṃyuktatvaṃ dhṛte, svaṃ jalaṃ jalamadhyasthadhṛte samanvayaḥ। pakṣe tu svaṃ suvaṇagatatejobhāgaḥ
iti samanvayaḥ। dīpikāyāñ [] sparśānumeyo vāyuriti। atra ca sparśapadaṃ sparśatvaparam। vāyurityasaṃgatamityapāstam। yadvā tādātmyasaṃbandhena sparśasyaiva hetutvaṃ vivakṣitamiti nāsaṃgatiḥ। anumānaprakāraśca
pārthivādisparśavat' u iti [] vāyauvātīti। atra ca vāyau iti saptamyāḥ gaganamarthaḥ। tasya ca samānakālīnatvasambandhena upalambhe anvayaḥ। yadyapi guṇatvādrūpavaditi hetudṛṣṭāntayorabhidhānaṃ guṇatvahetukānumānāntaramapyuktamiti dhyeyam।
manassamavetaḥ syāt tarhi laukikapratyakṣaviṣayo na syāt। bhāvaḥ। [] udbhūtasparśavadityādi। atra ca ghrāṇendriye vyabhicāravāraṇāya prathamamudbhūteti। udbhūtatvasyābhāvakūṭātmakasya
dravyatve api sattvāt taddoṣa ityataḥ sparśapadam। vāyau tadvāraṇāya pārthivatvaniveśaḥ। vāyāvapyanudbhūtarūpasattvāt dravyatvasattvācca udbhūtarūpaniveśaḥ। atra copalabhyamānasparśāśrayasya pṛthivītvādikaṃ prasaktaṃ na tu pṛthivyādestadāśrayatvam।
ato aprasaktapratiṣedhaparihārāya yojanamāha- [] asyetyādi। dīpikāyāñ [] na vibhucatuṣṭayamiti। tadanyatamaṃ netyarthaḥ। anyathā siddhasādhanaprasaṃgāt, ekatrobhayādibhedasattvāditi dhyeyam। navīnāstu vāyoḥ pratyakṣatāṃ varṇayanti। tanmatamākṣeptumanuvadati [] nanu vāyuḥ pratyakṣa
ityādinā। nanu pratyakṣatvaṃ pratyakṣaviṣayatvaṃ, tathā ca vāyorapi iti। yadyapyalaukikatādṛśapratyakṣaviṣayatvamapi vāyorastīti sādhyatve tātparyānna doṣaḥ। anirūpitāntaṃ ca mānasaviṣayatāmādāyārthāntaravāraṇāya। ata eva
sādhyavyāpakatābhaṅgasya nāvakāśaḥ। tvagindriye vyabhicāratādavasthyam। sparśapadaṃ tu laukikaviṣayatāśrayadravyatvādikamādāya। ākāśe vyabhicāravyudāsāya। sparśasya samavāyena hetutvasūcanāya
āśrayatvakathanam। dīpikāyām [] udbhūtarūpasyeti। atrodbhūtapadaṃ prācīnaikadeśibhiḥ sādhanāvyāpakatvopapattyartham। prakāśikāyāñ [] sādhyavyabhicāronnayanasambhavāditi। yadyapi śuddhasādhyavyabhicāro api, vyāptigrahavirahāt। tathāpi
paścādanumātuṃ śakyamiti bhāvaḥ। atha vā pakṣadharmavati sādhanāvyāpakatvena śuddhasādhyavyabhicāra evānumātuṃ śakyaḥ। sādhanāśrayapakṣadharmavanniṣṭhātyantābhāvapratiyogitvam। evaṃ sādhyāśrayapakṣadharmavanniṣṭhābhāvāpratiyogitvamiti। evamupādhyantare api
draṣṭavyam। udbhūtarūpaṃ vā upādhiḥ। tasya rūpādāvapi sattvena sādhyavyāpakatvāt pakṣabhūtavāyāvasattvena sādhanāvyāpakatvācca। upadarśitadharmaviśeṣasya upādhitvasūcanāyaiva pakṣadharmāvacchinnasādhyavyāpakatvakīrtanam।
veti madekapariśīlitaḥ panthāḥ। viśeṣyavyabhicārasiddhiḥ iti vadanti। yato viśiṣṭavyabhicāraḥ viśiṣṭābhāvadvṛttitvameva। na tu viśeṣaṇavyabhicārāsahitaviśeṣyavyabhicāraḥ। prattakṣasparśavattvādau
tadasaṃbhavāt। udbhūtarūpaśūnyatveti। rūpādiguṇe dravyatvābhāvaprayuktobhayābhāvasya asya bahirindriyajanyapratyakṣaviṣayatvarūpasādhyavyāpakatvam। samavāyasaṃbandhetyādi।
svābhāvīyetyasya svābhāvanirūpitetyarthaḥ। dravyaniṣṭhādhikaraṇatāyāmanvayaḥ। rūpādiniṣṭhādhikaraṇatāyāṃ sādhyavyāpakatvamiti bhāvaḥ। ghaṭādiniṣṭhādhikaraṇatāyāṃ dravyaniṣṭhatvasadbhāve api udbhūtarūpābhāvanirūpitatvaṃ nāsti। ataḥ
tatsaṃbandhena udbhūtarūpaṃ ghaṭādāvastīti sādhyavyāpakatā bodhyaḥ। śuddhasādhyavyabhicāronnāyakatvānirvāha eveti। dīpikāyāñ [] prāṇasya kutrāntarbhāva ityādi। tathā ca daśamadravyatvaṃ prāṇasya, vāyāvantarbhāve api kāryavānucāturvidhyaṃ vā prasajyeteti bhāvaḥ।
vāyvantarbhāvācca na daśamadravyatvamityāśaya iti bhāvaśca।"sa saṃgrahavākye upādhibhedādityatra pañcamyāḥ prayojyatvamarthaḥ। tasya alabhata' ityatra dhātvarthasambandhe anvayaḥ। sa ceha vācyatvarūpaḥ। eko apītyatra ekatvaṃ prāṇatvanyūnavṛttidharmaśūnyatvam। apiratra
virodhārthakaḥ। virodhaśca samabhivyāhṛtapadārthantāvacchedakaikatvādhikaraṇanirūpitopādhibhedānavacchi nnavṛttikatvābhāvaḥ। tasya ca sambandhe anvayaḥ। tathā ca sa iti bodhaḥ।
virodhārthakatāmāhuḥ। dharmiṇi ekatvāvirodhalābhena pṛthakkathanavaiyarthyāt। asmanmate tu tatsārthakyāt। ke te upādhaya ityāśaṅkāyāmupādhiśabdārthamāha dīpikāyām [] sthāneti। tatra pramāṇamāha prakāśikāyām
[] hṛdi prāṇa ityādi iti। dīpikāyām [] cikīrṣāvaśāditi। yadyapīśvarecchā nityaiva। tathāpyetatkāle tatkāla eva tatra kriyātpattiḥ nānyadeti niyama upapadyate। evaṃ saṃjihīrṣāvaśādityatrāpi bodhyam। cākṣuṣadravyatvādityatra cākṣuṣaṃ
cābhipretyārthamāha- [] cākṣuṣatve satītyādi। idaṃ ca janyadravyatvasya sādhyatābhiprāyeṇa। bodhyaḥ। etatsaṃgrāhakamevādipadamiti dhyeyam। [] kāryatve anavasthāprasaṅgāditi। dhīnamerusarṣapagataparimāṇatāratamyānupapattirūpāniṣṭaprasajjanād ityarthaḥ। uktatarkabalāt nityāvayavasamaveta ityanumitirutpadyata iti bhāvaḥ।
[] prakāśikāyāṃ saṃkṣepa iti। yatsūkṣmamupalabhyate। paramāṇuḥprakīrtitaḥ।।' smṛtiprāmāṇyabalāt dvyaṇukaparamāṇvoḥ svīkāra āvaśyaka iti।
digiti। atrāyamāśayaḥ sarvaśabdasya mahāpralasya ca lakṣaṇam। vyāpakatvaṃ ca svaniṣṭhadhvaṃsapratiyogitāsaṃbandhena। svananiṣṭhatvaṃ ca kālikasaṃbandhena। etena kāryāṇāṃ bhāvakāryāṇāṃ cānantānāṃ
parijñānāsambhavāt etallakṣaṇakathanamasaṃgatamityapāstamiti। [] dyotanāyeti। tathā ca śabdaguṇakamiti yasminniti bahuvrīṃhiriti bhāvaḥ। nanu taccaikamiti saṃgrahavākye karmadhārayoparītyādinyāyamiti। karmadhārayopari vidyamānaḥ
bhāvārthakapratyayaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyabodhaka iti nyāyamityarthaḥ। vyavahartavyabhedasyaiva niyāmakatvāt। tathā ca aghaṭākāśavyavahāraḥ prāṇāpānādivyavahārabhedānupapatteḥ। evaṃ ca darśitānumāne prāṇāpānādivyavahāramādāya vyabhicāraḥ। tathā ca prakṛte
na tasyākāśabhedasādhakatvam' iti samādhānamabhisandhāyāha- [] ghaṭākāśo maṭhākāśa ityādīti। [] anekatve - ākāśatvanyūnavṛttidharmavattve। [] pramāṇam - pramā, tasya viśeṣyatāsambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvadityarthaḥ। tathā ca iti vyatirekyanumānamākāśasya ekatve pramāṇamupadarśitam। ākāśatvanyūnavṛttidharmaśūnyatvādevetyarthaḥ।
ekatvam। atrāyamanugamaḥ-bhedaviśiṣṭākāśatvakatvaṃ tat। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasvāśrayatvobhayasambandhena। avacchedakatā svavyāpyadharmaviśiṣṭatvasambandhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaviruddhadharmaviśiṣṭatvasambandhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svasetyādibhedavattvasambandhena - ityāhuḥ। vibhājakadharmadvayaśūnyatvaṃ taditi। padārthavibhājakadravyatva - dravyavibhājakākāśatvayoḥ sattvenāsambhavāpatteḥ। dhyeyam। ākāśakāladigātmanāṃ sādhāraṇaṃ vibhutvaṃ na jātiḥ।
ananyathāsiddhaliṅgānupalambhenānumānāsambhavāt। śabdasya vaiparītyasyāpi suvacatvāt। na ca vibhupadavācyatāvacchedakatayā vibhutvajātisiddhiriti vācyam। ulyayuktyā bhūtatvasyāpi jātitvāsiddheḥ।
paramamahatparimāṇavattvaṃ vibhutvamiti। avaibhavāt ityabhiprāyeṇa prakārāntareṇa vibhutvaṃ nirvakti- [] sarvamūrteti। atra ca paṭādisaṃyuktaghaṭādivāraṇāya sarvapadam। kriyāviraheṇa parasparasaṃyogābhāvāt asaṃbhavanirāsāya mūrtapadam। saṃyogavadarthakam। ata evoktadoṣavāraṇāya mūrtapadaṃ
nityamūrtaparamiti pralapitamanādeyam। dravyapadavaiyarthyāpātācca। vā nopādeyameva tat। tāvatpratiyogikaikasaṃyogāprasiddhyā asambhavaḥ। tāvatāṃ tadghaṭitasamudāyavattvasya ākāśādāvabhāvāt sa eva doṣaḥ। yattu -
doṣaḥ। na ca mūrtatvajātipakṣe tulyayuktyeti। bhūtapadavācyatāvacchedakatayetyarthaḥ। svasāmānādhikaraṇyasvābhāvasāmānādhikaraṇyasvasamānādhikaraṇātyantābhāvapratiyogitvaitattritayasaṃbandhenetyarthaḥ।
vācyam। dravyapadasya saṃyogavadarthakatāyāḥ prāgevāveditatayā sutarāmadoṣācceti। apekṣābuddhiviśeṣaviṣayatvarūpasya vibhupadavattvarūpalakṣyatāvacchedakavatyanyasmin tasyāsattvāt avyāpteḥ। tattatsamudāyacatuṣṭayavattvasya lakṣaṇatve asaṃbhavāpatteḥ। tasya
kutrāpyasattvāt। tāvadanyatamavattvasya tathātve tādṛśānyatamatvasya vyāsajyavṛttidharmāvacchinnānuyogitākābhāvānupagame asambhavāpatteḥ। ghaṭādāvativyāpteḥ kathamidaṃ saṃgacchate। gaganādisaṃyuktatvaṃ nāstīti labhyate। evaṃ ca svāsaṃyuktamūrtadravyakaṃ
phalitam। atra gaganādyasaṃyuktamūrtāprasiddhyā svapadena gaganādyupādānāsambhavāt gaganādau lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। gaganāderapi svāsaṃyuktaguṇāditvādasambhavavāraṇāya mūrteti। mūrtatvajātipakṣe saṃyogyarthakaṃ dravyapadam। tādṛśaghaṭādeśca gaganādyasaṃyuktatve api
saṃyogitvavirahānnāsambhavaḥ। na caivaṃ mūrtapadavaiyarthyam, guṇāderatathātvāditi vācyam। tathāpi gaganādeḥ tasyāvaśyakatvāditi - tadapyasat। duṣkaratvāt। svāsaṃyuktamūrtasaṃyuktakatvatādātmyobhayasambandhena
dravyatvaniveśena tadvāraṇe api utpannavinaṣṭapṛthivyādāvativyāpteḥ। viśeṣaṇāntaraniveśasya rakṣālanāddhinyāyenāyuktatvācca। svaniṣṭhasaṃyuktatvasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākātyantābhāvavivakṣaṇānnotpannavinaṣṭapṛthivyādāvativyāptiḥ। sarvamūrtadravyasaṃyogitvamityanena vivakṣitam। tādṛśadharmavattā ca
svarūpasamavāyānyatarasambandhena। nātaḥ kālātmādāvavyāptirityapi parāstam। udakṣaratāyā durvāratvāt। vibhupadārthadvaividhyaprasaṅgācca। sarvamūrtetyādermūrtadravyatvavyāpakatvamarthaḥ। sarvaśabdasya
samabhivyāhṛtapadārthatāvacchedakavyāpakatvārthakatvāt। vyāpakatā ca svānuyogikasaṃyogapratiyogitvasaṃbandhena। etallābhāyaiva saṃyogītyuktam। yadyapi svānuyogikasaṃyogapratiyogitvasambandhena tadiha vivakṣitam। atyantābhāvapratiyogitāvacchedakasyāpi
prakṣālanāddhinyāyeti। aprakṣālanāddhi paṅkasya dūrādasparśanaṃ varam' iti nyāyenetyarthaḥ। madekapariśīlitaḥ panthāḥ। paricchannatvaṃ nāpakarṣarūpam, yenoktadoṣaḥ syāt। api
tvākāśādyanyatamāsamavetatvam। mūrtatvaghaṭitatvenānyonyāśrayaprasaṅgāt। ato na paramāṇuṣu avayāptiriti manasi nidhāyāha prakāśikāyām [] vastutastviti। [] anāgatādītyādinā vartamānaparigrahaḥ।
[] ghaṭakatayeti। atītādivyavahāraṃ prati abhedastṛtīyārthahetutvānvitaḥ। vastutastu atītatvaṃ śabdaprayogādhikaraṇakālavattvam। bhaviṣyatvaṃ ca śabdaprayogādhikaraṇakālavattvam। vartamānatvaṃ ca ādheyatāsambandhena
vartata iti śabdaprayogādhikaraṇakālavattvam। evaṃ ca vyavahāre tadavacchedakaviṣayatāvattvarūpaṃ vyavahārahetutvaṃ kālasyākṣatameva। ghaṭakatayetyasyāpi tādṛśaviṣayatāśrayatayetyarthaḥ। tādṛśakṣaṇaviśiṣṭatvaparyavasitaṃ nirvācyamiti dhyeyam।
atītatvādiprakārakajñānasyeti। ghaṭaḥ vartamānakālavṛttidhvaṃsapratiyogo ityākārakajñānasyetyarthaḥ। tādṛśavyavahārajanakatāvacchedaketyasya antimaprakāratāyāmanvayaḥ। tadāśrayatayetyarthaḥ।
grāhyā, ato nātiprasaṅga iti। tatrātītādivyavahārānupapatteriti bhāvaḥ। [] digiti। yadyapi svīkartavyamiti noktarītyā atiriktakālasiddhiḥ। tathāpi
sarvādhāratvasya kriyādāvativyāptibhramaṃ nirākāroti [] atretyādinā। pratīcyādītyādinā udīcīdakṣiṇayoḥ parigrahaḥ। [] samavāyena jñānavadityartha iti। anyathā kālikādinā jñānavati kālādāvativyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। ayā īśvarasya jñānasvarūpatvabodhanāditi bhāvaḥ। a vijñānam' iti śrutau vijñānapadasya arśa ādyajanyatvaṃ
vā nandyāditvāt kartarilyupratyayāntatvaṃ vābhipreyatyāha - [] vijñānavadarthakateti। nanvīśvare sukhābhāvāt kathamuktaśruteḥ prāmāṇyamityāśaṅkyāha - [] atreti। [] sukhī saṃvṛtto ahamitivaditi। tādṛśavākyasthasukhaśabda ivetyarthaḥ। atra-uktaśrutau, ānandaḥ- ānandaśabdaḥ duḥkhābhāve upacaryata iti।
saptamyā ādheyatvamarthaḥ। nirūpakatvamāśyātārthaḥ। phalitam। teyati। anityaṃ vijñānamānandaṃ brahma' iti śrutyetyarthaḥ।
mukhyārthaparatvaṃ varṇayatāṃ navīnānāṃ matamāha [] navīnāstviti। nanvīśvare janyamukhābhāvāt kathamānandaśabdasya mukhyārthakatvamata āha [] nityasukhamiti। darśitaśrutibalādityādiḥ। [] vijātīyeti। anyathā parātmanaḥ pareṇa manasā pratyakṣāpatteriti bhāvaḥ।
gaganādivat'ityanumānadvayaṃ vivakṣitam। tena na cārvākamate pakṣāprasiddhiḥ। avacchedakāvacchedena sādhyasiddheruddeśyatvāt nāṃśatassiddhasādhanam। [] nāpyanumānam liṅgābhāvādityatrāpi vastutvādityanumānamavaseyamiti।
[] digiti। ayamatra bhāvaḥ - yadyapi kāryatvāvacchinnaṃ prati kṛtitvena kāraṇatvamapyāvaśyakam। evaṃ tādṛśānvayavyatirekāviśeṣāt। evaṃ ca akāryaṃ kṛtijanyaṃ [] aparokṣajñānāderityādipadena cikirṣāparigrahaḥ। [] cikirṣādikamityādipadena kṛtiparigrahaḥ। nanu ayaḥ sarvajñaḥ
[] sarvaviditīti। vastutastu sarvavidityasya sarvaṃ vidantīti vyutpattyā sarvavyāpta ityarthaḥ। vida lābha iti dhātoḥ kvipi tādṛśār thasambhavāditi dhyeyam। nanu [] jīvasya lakṣaṇamāha - jīva itīti dīpikāyām [] jīvastu pratiśarīraṃ bhinna iti saṃgrahavākyāvataraṇamayuktam।
svarūpaparatvamabhisandhāya vyācaṣṭe - [] svarūpamāhesyartha iti। [] mūle prati śarīraṃ bhinna iti। atra ca khaṇḍaśor'thaḥ। anyathā sāmānyato vyāpakatvasya vyāpyaviśeṣāghaṭitasya durvacatvena dvitīyārthatānupapatteriti dhyeyam।
labhyate। jīvātmanyekatvopagame api īdṛśārthanirvāhāt ātmabhedasya śarīratvavyāpakatvākṣateḥ। vivakṣitam। api [tu] svasamānādhikaraṇabhogāvacchedakatvasvapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasaṃbandhena svaviśiṣṭayogajadharmādyajanyaśarīrāvacchinnabhogavattvasaṃbandhena। śarīre
[tva] svasamānakālīnatvobhayasaṃbandhena। ato noktadoṣaḥ। etadevābhipretyāha - [] samānākāliketyādi। kiṃ tarhi jīvalakṣaṇamityāśaṅkāyāmāha - dīpikāyām [] sukhādikaṃ jīvalakṣaṇamiti। atra sukhopādānaṃ prācīnamatamanusṛtya। anyathā navīnamate uktarītyā
īśvare ativyāpteḥ। ādinā duḥkhadveṣayoḥ parigrahaḥ। prakāśikāyām [] anyathā-śarīrātiriktasyātmatve। siddhānte manuṣyādiśabdasya manuṣyo ahamityādipratītyupapattirityabhisandhāyoktam [] abhimāna iti। [] yanmadhyamaparimāṇamityādi। parimāṇe
madhyamatvaṃ ca paramāṇutvaparamahattvabhinnatvam। tathā cātmanastathātve saṅkocavikāsaśālitvāpattyā anityatvaprasaṅga iti bhāvaḥ। [] digiti। ayamatra bhāvaḥ- yadi ca dṛṣṭānurodhenaiva kalpanasya sarvasammatatvāt।
ekagrahavartidīpaprasaraṇasya grahāntare adṛṣṭeḥ। evaṃ vyāpitvapratipādakāgamo api tatra pramāṇamiti। dīpikāyām [] sparśarahitatve satīti। vāyāvativyāptibhiyā rūpādirahitatvopekṣaṇam। saṅgrahe [] pratyātmaniyatatvāditi।
viśiṣṭārthaḥ। tallābhaḥ kathamiti cet ittham - pratipadasamabhivyāhṛtamātmapadaṃ prātisvikarūpeṇa tattadātmavyaktiparam। tadanyasamavetajñānājanakatvam। tathā ca svajanyajñānāśrayayatkiñcidātmabhinnasamevatajñānājanakatvādityarthaḥ।
ekaikasya manasa iti śeṣaḥ। jñānajñāpyatvaṃ pañcamyarthaḥ anantatve anvetīti - tattuccham। ātmaśabdasyātmatvajātiviśiṣṭaśaktitayā tattadvyaktitvāvacchinnaparatve tasya lakṣaṇāprasaṅgāt। ātmanāmanantatvena viśiṣṭa durjñeyatvācca।
vasetyādibhedavattvarūpavyāpakatāsaṃbandhena anvayaḥ। svādhikaraṇatā tādātmyasaṃbandhena। svasetyādibhedavattveti। svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvani ṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavatvasaṃbandhenatyarthaḥ।
ubhayasaṃbandhena। evaṃ cātmapadasya mukhyārthaparatāpi sutarāṃ saṅgacchate। ata eva saṅgrahaṭippaṇyāmuktamarthāntaramapi dūrato apāstam। nanu lāghavāt sarveṣāmapyātmanāṃ ekameva mana āstāmityatrāha - [] sarvātmanāmityādi। nanu manaso aṇutva eva
uktadoṣaḥ syāt। na hi vayaṃ tasyāṇutvaṃ svīkurmahe। api tu vibhutvameva। tathā ca sarvātmanāṃ manasa ekatve api sarvendriyairekadā tadanupapattirityabhiprāyeṇa śaṅkate - dīpikāyām [] nanu mana ityādinā। [] sparśarahitatve satītyādi।
pṛthivyādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya satyantam। guṇādau vyabhicāranirāsāya viśeṣyam। atra ca manaso aṇutve ānantyaṃ kalpanīyam। vibhutve tu na tatheti lāghavamiti tarkasattvāt bhāvaḥ। samavāyena
[] vibhudvayeti। [] kriyādītyādinā saṃyogaparigrahaḥ। dīpikāyām [] tadā suṣuptiriti। idamatra bodhyam - tu tādṛśadeśānuyogikamanaḥpratiyogikasaṃyogaḥ। tathā sati acaitraḥ svapiti', amaitraḥ suṣuptaḥ' ityādivākyānāmaprāmāṇyāpātāt। tatra
tādṛśasaṃyogavirahāt। kartṛpratyayasya cāśrayatvabodhakatvāt। ata nidrānāḍyavacchinnātmamanoyorūpe' iti ca। jīvanayoniyatnasyākhyātārthatāprasakterevābhāvācca। yadyapi noktāpattiḥ। yadyapyākhyātāderāśrayatvādyarthakatāyā apyanyatra kḷptatvāt
tattātparyeṇa manaḥ svapiti ityādiprayogāpattiḥ durvāraiva। tathāpi sarvānumatam। tatra svapidhātusamabhivyāhṛtapratyayasyānuyogitva evānāditātparyaṃ kalpyate। anyathā tatsaṃsargasyāpi śābdabodhaviṣayatvakalpanāpattyā gauravāt। na
caivaṃ caitro na svapitītyādau nañarthābhāvānvayānupapattiḥ। vṛttyaniyāmakatvenābhāvapratiyogitānavacchedakatvāditi vācyam। vṛttyaniyāmakasyāpyabhāvapratiyogitāvacchedakatāghaṭakasambandhatvopagamenādoṣāt। kalpane gauravamiti vācyam।
atiriktakalpanāvirahāt। na caivamapi vācyam। bhavanmate api prāguktagauravasattvena sāmyāt। na ca prakāratvamāvaśyakamiti vācyam। tādṛśayuktīnāṃ vistareṇānyatrāsmābhirnirastatvāt। svapitītyetāvanmātrasya
bodhakatvopapattaye ākhyātāderanuyogitārthakatāyā āvaśyakatvāt। saṃsargatayā bhāne na ko api dāṣaḥ। tathāpi bodho bhāvatviti na tatrāsmākamāgrahaḥ। jānātītyādāvapyevameva bodhyam। evaṃ bhavanmate purītat
svapitītyādiprayogasya prāmāṇyaṃ durvāram। asmanmate tu neti madekapariśīlitaḥ panthāḥ। saṅgrahaḥ। atra ca ghaṭādyupalabdhisādhanībhūtacakṣurādinirāsāya sukhādīti। ātmanyativyāptivāraṇāya viśeṣyam। yadi ca
anyathā kālavidhayā tajjanake cakṣurādāvativyāpteḥ। tathā ca tadāpyāha - prakāśikāyām ātmamanoyogāditi। ādipadena sukhādiparigrahaḥ। tathā ca sukhādimānasatvāvacchinnaṃ prati manasaḥ bhāvaḥ। [] aṇutvasiddhiriti। idamatra
tarkasahakṛtamiti। saṃgrahavākyam। atra ca cakṣurmātragrāhya ityanane cakṣurviśiṣṭadharmāśrayagrāhya iti bodhaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvacakṣuṣṭvaniṣṭhādheyatvobhayasambandhena।
adhikam anyatra prapañcitaṃ asmābhiḥ। prakāśikāyām [] na rūpe sambhavatīti। rūpasyātmamanogrāhyatvāditi bhāvaḥ। [] tathāpi tvagindriyeti। yadyapi tvarūpacakṣuritarāgrāhyatvavivakṣaṇe na doṣaḥ। tathāpi tvagādeḥ viśeṣaṇīyatayā ca gauravamityālocya tatparityāgaḥ। [] tvagagrāhyatvetyādi। tvācanirūpitalaukikaviṣayatāśūnyatvaṃ
cākṣuṣanirūpitalaukikaviṣayatāvatvaṃ ca jātiviśeṣaṇamatra vaktavyam। kālavidhayā rūpacākṣuṣajñānajanakatve api na kṣatiḥ। evaṃ gurutvādeḥ cākṣuṣe upanayamaryādayā bhāne api nātivyāptiḥ। atra rasādivāraṇāya cākṣuṣeti। prabhādivāraṇāya guṇavibhājaketi। guṇatvavyāpyetyarthaḥ।
evetyādi। tathā ca darśitātivyāptivāraṇā jātighaṭitapariṣkārasyāvaśyakatayā tvagagrāhyatvādeḥ। bhāvaḥ। dīpikāyām [] avyāpyavṛttinīlādīti। atrāvyāptivṛttitvaviśeṣaṇaṃ
vivakṣitam। tacca vapratiyogitvasvādhikaraṇanirūpitakiñciddeśāvacchinnādheyatvobhayasaṃbandhenābhāvaviśiṣṭatvam। nanu [] rūpasya vyāpyavṛttitvaniyamāditi dīpikoktirasaṅgatā। kālikāvyāpyavṛttitvasyāvaśyakatvādityata āha - prakāśikāyām [] vyāpyavṛttitveti। daiśikavyāpyavṛttitvetyartha
iti। daiśikavyāpyavṛttitvaṃ ca pūrvoktobhayasambandhanābhāvaviśiṣṭānyatvam। svapratiyogitvetyādi। svaṃ kapisaṃyogābhāvaḥ tatpratiyogitvaṃ tannirūpitāgradeśāvacchinnavṛttitvaṃ kapisaṃyoge astīti samanvayaḥ।
tarhyavyāpyavṛttiḥ syāditi tarkasahakṛtaṃ pramāṇaṃ vācyam। tatra rūpasya vyāpyavṛttitvaniyame vipratipannaṃ prati dūṣaṇāntaramāha - [] idamupalakṣaṇamityādinā। evaṃ ca pramāṇamiti bhāvaḥ। prāgabhāvādītyādinā dhvaṃsaparigrahaḥ। nanu nopeyate। parasparavirodhena vyāpyavṛttinīlādisamudāyo api na
dīpikāyām। sāmānādhikaraṇyena tatra rūpasattvādāha - prakāśikāyām [] samavāyenetyādiriti। amavetatvīyasambandhasya svarūpasya kāraṇatāvacchedakatvākalpanayā lāghavamabhisandhāyāha - [] svāśrayasamavetatvasambandhena rūpamiti। jñānagatapratyakṣatvajātau pratyakṣaviṣayatveti। nanu
kāraṇatvamucitamityato dūṣaṇāntaramāha - [] citrāvayavāvayavaketyādinā। dīpikāyām [] tasmāt paṭasyetyādi। ayamatra bhāvaḥ ayaṃ paṭaḥ atra ceti। nīlīdisamudāyasya citrarūpatvābhāva ityarthaḥ। yadvā rūpasya vyāpyavṛttitva ityarthaḥ। athavā citrarūpasyātiriktatva ityarthaḥ।
sāmānādhikaraṇyasaṃbandheneti। svādhikaraṇavṛttitvasaṃbandhenetyarthaḥ। saṃbandhena paṭasya tanturūpavattvam। samavetatvīyeti। kāraṇatāvacchedakasaṃbandhatvaṃ vaktavyam। svāśrayasamavetatvasaṃbandhena
lāghavamiti। kāraṇatāvacchedakadharmalāghavamapyatra bodhyam। atiriktatvasiddheḥ citrarūpamiti vyavahriyata iti। citrarasāsiddhau hetumāha - [] dravyalaukiketyādi। tathā cāyaṃ prameyatvādityanumānamanukūlatarkavirahādaprayojakamiti bhāvaḥ। atra
citrarasāṅgīkāra āvaśyaka iti tvanāśaṅkanīyam। tatrāvayavarasasyaiva āmānādhikaraṇyena bhānābhyupagamāt। yatra ca utpannaṃ tatra rasapratītirnopeyata eva। dharmiṇaḥ rāsanapratyakṣe upanayamaryādayaiva bhānābhyupagamāt। paramāṇurasasyāpi
viśeṣyavidhayālaukikapratyakṣāsambhavāt। upanītaṃ viśeṣaṇatayaiveti naiyāyikasiddhāntāditi। vastutastu tasasya vyāpyavṛttitvaniyame pramārūpāyā nānupapattiḥ। sarvamidamabhisandhāyoktam [] saṅkṣepa iti। paramāṇurase avyāptiḥ। rasanagrāhyajātimattvavivakṣāyāmapi
rasanetyādi। uṇatvanyūnavṛttitvaṃ vivakṣitam। ityādilakṣaṇe asambhavaḥ। sparśasyatvagitarātmādigrāhyatvāt। evaṃ paramāṇusparśe avyāptiḥ। tvagragrāhyatvāt ityata āha - [] cakṣuragrāhyetyādi। sāmānādhikaraṇyeneti। svāśrayasamavetatvasaṃbandhenetyarthaḥ।
vivakṣitamiti। guṇatvanyūnavṛttitvaṃ ca guṇatvasamānādhikaraṇatve sati guṇatvasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvam। tacca cākṣuṣanirūpitalaukikaviṣayatāśūnyatvam। tvagindriyagrāhyatvaṃ ca tvācanirūpitalaukikaviṣayatāvattvam।
vāyutvajātimādāya vāyāvativyāptivāraṇāya upāttam। [] parāvṛttyādītyādinā rūpāntaraparigrahaḥ। yojanāmāha [] ghaṭe āmanikṣipte satīti। tathā ca ghaṭapadottarasaptamyā āmasaṃyogor'thaḥ। tasya
cottarakālīnatvasaṃbandhena śyāmaghaṭanāśe anvaya iti bhāvaḥ। paramāṇuniṣṭharūpotpattyuttarakālīnatvaṃ labhyate। taccayuktam - svīkārāt ato yojanayā anvayamāha [] śyāmaghaṭanāśa ityādi। jāti iti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca nāśapadottarasaptamyāḥ utpattirarthaḥ।
tasyāścottarakālīnatvasambandhena rūpāntarotpattāvanvaya iti bhāvaḥ। [] svatantreṣviti। viśakaliteṣvityarthaḥ। ārambhakasaṃyogarahiteṣviti yāvat। pūrvavinaṣṭāvayavivyatiriktāvayavītyarthaḥ। [] ata
eveti। avayavinyapi paramāṇuvat pākāṅgīkārādevetyarthaḥ। nanu pratyabhijñāsājātyamavalambate। nirvāpitāropitadīpe seyaṃ dīpajvāleti pratyabhijñāvat na tvekasyā eva vyakteḥ kāladvayasambandham। ato na virodha ityato dūṣaṇāntaramāha - [] anantāvayavītyādi। nāśādītyādinā
prāgabhāvaparigrahaḥ। [] vāraṇasambhavāditi। vaijātyasyāvayavarūpājanyāvayavirūpavyāvṛttatvāditi bhāvaḥ। pūrvavaddoṣa iti।
gurutvasyopanayamaryādayā bhāne api nāsambhavaḥ ativyāptirvetyarthaḥ। [] yathāyogyamiti। tathā ca rūpādicatuṣṭayapadaṃ tādṛśacatuṣṭayānyatamaparamiti bhāvaḥ। matabhedanobhayagranthasaṅgatiriti tasya jātirūpatvamevetyāha - [] udbhūtatvaṃ jātirityādinā। guṇaghaṭitetyarthaḥ।
[] na doṣaḥ - na pūrvotataragranthavirodha ityarthaḥ। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - dravyagatasāṃkaryasyaiva jātibādhakatvokteḥ। jātitvābhāvavyāpyatāyā upagamena jātibādhakatvaṃ svīkriyate। na tu guṇādisādhāraṇasvādhikaraṇaghaṭitajātisāṅkaryasyeti।
cātathābhūtasya na jātibādhakatvamiti dhyeyam। prakṛtagranthamupapādayatāṃ matamāha - kecittviti। āhurityanenāsvarasaḥ sūcitaḥ। tadbījantūdbhūtatvasya pratyakṣaprayojakamitidīpikāgranthāsaṅgatiriti।
[] bhāvapradhāna iti। bhāvaḥ pradhānaṃ bodhayatīti bhāvaḥ। kāryatvāvacchinnakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatvena। nanu ekavyaktyupādāne aparavyaktyasaṃgrahaḥ। svātyantābhāvasamānādhikaraṇaṃ
niṣkṛṣṭārthamāha [] svapratiyogitvetyādi। yadyapi tādātmyādirūpādhikapadārthaniveśāt gauravamiti tadupekṣitam। samavāyādinā ghaṭatvādessattvāt tatrātivyāptiḥ। na ca tatsambandhenādheyatvasya vivakṣayā na doṣa iti vācyam।
yattvatattvānanugamena lakṣaṇasya tattadvyaktiviśramāpātāt। tat, vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svapratiyogitvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svapratiyogitāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvasvādhikaraṇanirūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena। saṃyogādisambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākaghaṭatvādyabhāvasyāvyāpyavṛttitāprasaṅgāt।
tatsattvāt। svābhāvādhikaraṇavṛttitvaniveśāt nāyaṃ doṣaḥ iti vācyam। yattvatattvānanugamasya durvāratvāt। svāśrayāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasaṃbandhena। ādheyatāyāṃ
svanirūpakābhāvādhikaraṇanirūpitatvasvāśrayāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svanirūpitapratiyogitātvasambandhāvacchinnā। ato na ko api doṣaḥ। yadvā pratiyogitāviśiṣṭatvaṃ tat, vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
vācyam। dravyānyatvaviśiṣṭasattābhāvādāvativyāpteḥ। ghaṭādau tatsattvāt। na cābhāvatvaviśiṣṭatvaṃ adhikaraṇatāviśiṣṭatvaṃ vā tat। prathame vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svanirūpitapratiyogitvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasambandhena। svāvacchinnādhikaraṇanirūpitatvasvanirūpitapratiyogitāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvobhayasambandhena। dvitīye adhikaraṇatā svanirūpitapratiyogitātvasambandhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svanirūpakābhāvatvāvacchinnādhikaraṇanirūpitatvasvāśrayāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvobhayasambandhena। ato na doṣaḥ। atra dravyānyatvaviśiṣṭasattābhāvo nāstītyapratyayāt guṇādau tādṛśasattābhāvābhāvatvena vṛttyanupagamāditi vācyam। tasya sarvatrābhinnatayā taddoṣatādavasthyāt।
adhikaraṇatāviśiṣṭatvamavyāpyavṛttitvam। adhikaraṇatā ca svaviśiṣṭapratiyogitātvasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca kiñciddharmāvacchinnaprakāratānirūpitasaṃsargatvobhayasambandhena। abhāve svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayatvavasetyādibhedavattvobhayasambandhena।
svādhikaraṇatā ca svāvacchedakatāsambandhena। svasetyādibhedavattveti। svādhikaraṇavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvetyarthaḥ। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā ca ādheyatāsambandhena।
svāśrayāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvaviśiṣṭādhikaraṇanirūpitatvībhayasambandhena। adhikaraṇe svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svasetyādibhedavattvasambandhena। svādhikaraṇatvaṃ ca svanirūpakaviṣayatāvacchedakatāsambandhena।
svarūpasambandhāvacchinnādheyatāvacchedakatāsambandhena। yadyapi svaviśiṣṭādhikaraṇatāvannirūpitatvaṃ niveśyam। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāvacchinnapratiyogitākabhedanirūpitatvasvasetyādibhedavattvobhayasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā svaviśiṣṭāvacchedakatāsambandhena।
svāśrayanirūpitasvarūpasambandhāvacchinnādheyatvanirūpitatvasvanirūpakaviṣayatāvacchedakatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvobhayasambandhena। ratiyogitāviśiṣṭatvamavyāpyavṛttitvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭādheyatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvasvāvacchedakadharmāvacchinnatvasvanirūpakābhāvādhikaraṇanirūpitatvatritayasambandhena।
ena viśiṣṭasattvasya nāvyāpyavṛttitvamiti dhyeyam। pratiyogitāviśiṣṭatvamityādi। pratiyogitā kapisaṃyoganiṣṭhā pratiyogitāśrayatvāt। evaṃ kapisaṃyogasyāvyāpyavṛttitvam।
