viśiṣṭasattvasyeti। viśiṣṭasattāniṣṭhāyāḥ [] kecidityasvarasassūcitaḥ। tadbījantu janyamātrasya kālatvapakṣe janyarūpādāvativyāptiriti। atra cāvacchinnāntena janyatāviśeṣaṇena ghaṭitamekaṃ lakṣaṇam।
lakṣaṇam iti vivekaḥ। anyathā ekatra lakṣaṇe ubhayaniveśane prayojanābhāvāt। tattaddhvaṃsavyaktitvāvacchinnaṃ prati tādātmyena tattatpratiyogivyakteḥ kāraṇatayaiva saṃyogā - [dya] tivyāptivāraṇāditi bodhyam। darśitārthatātparyagrāhakatvopagamena pariharati - [] etattātparyeti।
labhyate। taccāsambhavi, paratvādeḥ [] dīpikāyāṃ paravyavahāretyādi। asamavāyikāraṇatvamātrasya gurutvalakṣaṇatve tantudvayasaṃyogādāvativyāptiḥ। patanakāraṇatvasya sphuṭaivetyālocyādyapadasya kṛtyamāha - [] dvitīyādīti।
kathaṃ tadvāraṇasambhava ityata ādyatvamanyādṛśaṃ nirvakti - [] prakāśikāyām ādyatvamiheti। svasamānādhikaraṇetyādi। athātra svapadamanuyogiparam vā pratiyogiparam vā। nādyaḥ, ādyapatanavyaktīnāmānantyāt। tenaikopādāne itarāsaṅgrahāt। tāvadanyatamattvaṃ tu asarvajñadurjñeyam। anyatamattvaghaṭakabhedānāṃ mitho
viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāve vinigamanāvirahaśca। nāpyuttaraḥ, tādṛśayatkiñcidekapatanavyaktibhedasya dvitīyādipatanasādhāraṇatvāt। tāvadanyatamatvāvacchinnabhedavattvasya vā prāguktadoṣadūṣitatvāt। sthūlānugamaḥ।
sūkṣmānugamaḥ। ratiyogini svatvādare tu patanaviśiṣṭānyatvamiti sthūlānugamaḥ। prathamapatane sattvāt tasya ādyatvopapattiḥ। svasamānādhikaraṇetyādi। prathamasvaśabdaḥ ādyapatanaparaḥ। dvitīyasvaśabdaḥ
ādyapatanavadbhedaparaḥ। ādyapatanasamānādhikaraṇaṃ yat dvitīyapatanaṃ tadāśrayatvaṃ tatpratiyogitāvacchedakatvaṃ cādyapatane astīti samanvayaḥ। pratiyoginītyādi। prathamapatane astīti samanvayo bodhyaḥ।
svasamānakālikatvetyādi। dhvaṃsapadena prathamapatanadhvaṃso grāhyaḥ। vācyaḥ। tathāhi - prathamasvapadaṃ prathamapatanadhvaṃsaparam। tādṛśadhvaṃsasamānakālikatvaṃ dvitīyapatane asita। dvitīyasvapadaṃ dvitīyapatanaparam। dvitīyapatanaṃ hi
svasamānādhikaraṇapatanapratiyogikatvasambandhāvacchinnā bhavati। tathā ca tadanyatvamādyapatane iti bodhyam। dhvaṃsaviśiṣṭānyatvamiti sūkṣmānugamaḥ। tādṛśādheyatvasthāne doṣaḥ। yadyapi vṛkṣāt saudhe patitasya phalādeḥ
saudhātpatanadaśāyāṃ tatra niruktamādyatvamasambhavi। tathāpi tatra parantu saudhāvadhikapataneṣu prāthamikapatanasyādyatvaṃ sambhavati। tacca vācyam। evaṃ ca vṛkṣāvadhikapatanasya avadhiviśeṣaghaṭitameva caramatvaṃ nirvācyam।
sambhavasthalābhiproyaṇetyavadheyam। dīpikāyām [] guṇapadamiti। na caivamadṛṣṭavāraṇāya vyarthamiti vācyam। asamavāyikāraṇabhūtacūrṇādivāraṇāya tadāvaśyakatvāt। prakāśikāyām [] piṇḍībhāvassaṃyogaviśeṣa iti। dhāraṇakarṣaṇādiyogya
ityarthaḥ। śabdamātre ākāśasya samavāyikāraṇatāyāḥ spaṣṭatvādāha - [] ādye asamavāyikāraṇamityādi। sarvavyavahārahetutvaṃ buddhilakṣaṇaṃ phalitam। śukādyuccaritavyavahārahetutvasya buddhāvabhāvāt।
vyavahāropadhāyakatvābhāvāt tatrāvyāptiḥ। sarvavyavahārahetutvamityata āha - [] jñānatvamātraṃ lakṣaṇamiti। svapratiyogīti। atra svapadaṃ prathamapatanadhvaṃsaparam। tatpratiyogi prathamapatanam,
tatsamānādhikaraṇatvaṃ dvitīyapatane। idaṃ ceti। [] saṃskārasya trividhatvāditi। tathā ca iha bhāvaḥ। [] bhāvanākhya itīti। tathā ca bhāvanāyāḥ smṛtihetutvāt nāyaṃ doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। [] saṃskārajanyatvasya sattveneti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - jñānapratyāsatteḥ
icchādyanuvyavasāyena ghaṭādibhānānupapatteḥ। evaṃ ca saṃskārasyāpi nānumityādāvativyāptiṃriti bhāvaḥ। [] tathāpi cakṣurādīti। na idānīṃ spṛśāmi' imi mānasapratyabhijñāyāmativyāptiḥ। tanniveśe tvasambhavaḥ। jñānasāmānye manasaḥ karaṇatvāt। evaṃ cakṣurādeḥ
kālādividhayā smṛtihetutvādasambhavaśceti vācyam। pratyakṣatvāvacchinnapratiyogitākabhedasya vā niveśyatvāt। udakṣaratāpattiriti। jñānatvaniveśenāpīcchādivāraṇasambhavādāha - smṛtīti। [] etatphalamanubhavatvaniveśaprayojanam। [] yatretīt i। atra ca aghaṭapaṭobhayaṃ ghaṭa' ityādijñānānāmapi
āṃśikapramātvasyeṣṭatvāt na tatrātivyāptiśaṅketi bhāvaḥ। ghaṭa'ityādijñānasyālakṣyatve api tatra nātiprasaṅgaḥ। tādṛśādhikaraṇatādinyūnavṛttitvāt। na ca nirdharmitāvacchedakakapramāyāmavyāptirita vācyam।
tādṛśādhikaraṇatādyata vacchedakadharmānavacchinnaviśeṣyatāniveśāt। na nirdharmitāvacchedakakabhrame ativyāptiriti vācyam। tādṛśabhramasyāprāmāṇikatvāt - ityāhuḥ। durvāratvāt।
nātiprasaṅgaḥ। nāpi nirdharmitāvacchedakapramāyāmavyāptiḥ। yattu - - tattuccham। aetadghaṭatadghaṭobhayaṃ ghaṭa' iti pramāyāmavyāpteriti vadanti। uktāvyāpterevāvaraṇāt। mānābhāvāt tadanyūnānatiprasaktasyaiva tadavacchedakatvopagamāt।
mahāgauravaprasaṅgāt। anitiriktavṛttitvarūpatadavacchedakatvaniveśe ityādi pramāyāmavyāpteḥ। [] nanu tadvatītyasyetyādi। nañarthānvayānupapatteḥ viśeṣyatārthakatvāsambhavādāha- [] saptamyartho viśeṣyitvamiti। yadvā bhūtalaṃ vahnimāt, parvato
svīkārya ityekaṃ matam। tannirūpitaviṣayitārūpayoḥ viśeṣyitvaprakāritvayoravacchedyāvacchedakabhāvastathetyaparaṃ matam। tatra dvitīyamatamanusṛtyāha - viśeṣyitvamiti। atra ca viśeṣyatāyāḥ pramātvam। viśeṣyitāyāstadarthatve tu
prakāritāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyitāvadanubhavatvaṃ tat। prathame vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca vāvacchedakasaṃbandhena svāśrayavanniṣṭhatvasvanirūpitatvobhayasambandhena। svāvacchinnatvasvanirūpitaprakāratāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyatānirūpitatvobhayasambandhena। svāvacchedakasambandhenasvāśrayavanniṣṭhatvasambandheneti। [] tadvatīsyasya tatsaṃbandhinītyartha iti। prathame
prakāratāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyatānirūpakānubhavatvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca vanirūpitatvasvaviśiṣṭapratiyogitānirūpitānuyogitāśrayaniṣṭhatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svāvacchedaketyādi। rajate idaṃ rajatamiti jñāne samanvayaḥ kriyate। svaṃ
tādṛśaviśeṣyatānirūpakānubhavatvaṃ idaṃ rajatamiti jñāne astīti। idaṃ rajatamiti pramāyāmastīti samanvayaḥ। svanirūpitatvetyādi। svaṃ rajatatvaniṣṭhaprakāratā tannirūpitatvaṃ rajataniṣṭhaviśeṣyatāyām। evaṃ svaṃ prakāratā tadviśiṣṭā
rajatasyānuyogitvāt tadāśrayarajataniṣṭhatvaṃ viśeṣyatāyām। svāśrayaḥ rajatatvaṃ tanniṣṭhatvaṃ pratiyogitāyām। evaṃ svaṃ prakāratā saṃbandhena pratiyogitāvati samavāyatve tadvadbhedāsaṃbhavāt। api svavadbhinnatvarūpaṃ svasetyādibhedavattvaṃ ca pratiyogitāyāmasti।
tathā yoktobhayasaṃbandhena prakāratāviśiṣṭā pratiyogitā bhavatīti। evamuttaratrāpi ūhanīyam। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayaniṣṭhatvasvasetyādibhedavattvobhayasambandhena। svādhikaraṇatvaṃ ca svāvacchedakatāvacchedakatāsambandhena।
bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatāsvanirūpakatvīyavilakṣaṇāvacchedakatāsambandhena। bhrame nātivyāptiḥ। na vā aguṇādyanyatvaviśiṣṭasattāvān guṇa' saṃsargatāpakṣe ativyāptiḥ। yadyapi saṃyogasamavāyādīnāṃ svarūpataḥ svāvacchedakasaṃbandhanirūpitatvameva pratiyogitāyāṃ niveśyam।
nātiprasaṅgaḥ। yadi tādṛśobhayasambandhāvacchinnaprakāratāmādāya durvāretyucyate। tadā svāśrayaniṣṭhatvasvasetyādibhedavattvobhayasambandhena। svādhikaraṇatā svāvacchedakasaṃsargatāsambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā
svanirūpakatāsambandhena। svāvacchedakaparyāptāvacchedakatāvatvaṃ niveśyam। tacca svasetyādibhedavattvaparyavasitam। svādhikaraṇāvacchedakatā ca caivamanavacchinnaghaṭatvādiprakāratākapramāyāmavyāptiriti vācyam।
svavaiśiṣṭyaniveśanādoṣāt। anavacchinnaprakāratāṃ pratyuktasaṃbandhasya vyadhikaraṇatvāt। tathā ca viśiṣṭasattāvā niti bhrame nātiprasaṅgaḥ। svāśrayaniṣṭhatvasvāvacchedakasambandhanirūpitatvasvaniṣṭhabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvatritayasaṃbandhena। avacchedakatvaṃ svaviśiṣṭadharmāvacchinnatvasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ
cāvacchedakatāsambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena। svānavacchedakadharmānavacchinnatvaṃ tu na śakyaniveśam। svāvacchedakāprasiddhyā prāguktapramāyāmavyāpteḥ। pratiyogitāyāṃ tādṛśadharmāvacchinnatvasattvane taddoṣānirāsāditi।
tanna। aviśiṣṭasattāvān guṇa' ityādibhrame ativyāpteḥ। guṇādinirūpitādheyatāvacchedakatvānapāyāt। ādheyatādiviśeṣaṇasyaiva ādheyatādyavacchedakatvāt। ata eva
anavacchinnasamavāyasya ca svīkṛtaṃ gadādhareṇa siddhāntalakṣaṇe। anyathā tadupapādanasyāsaṅgatatvāpātāt। darśitadoṣānavakāśāt। anyathā uktarītyā avyavasthāpattyā siddhāntalakṣaṇavirodhāpatteriti dhyeyam।
[] pramāṇāntaratāpatteriti। pratyakṣādicatuṣṭayātiriktapramāṇatāpatterityarthaḥ। sattvāditi bhāvaḥ। [] saṅgrahe tadabhāvavatītyādi। atra ca
prakāritāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyitāvattvaviśeṣitaṃ vānubhavatvaṃ bhramatvam। vaviśiṣṭaikamātravṛttidharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvavanniṣṭhatvasvan irūpitatvobhayasambandhena। vaviśiṣṭaikamātravṛttidharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvavanniṣṭhatvasvan irūpitatvobhayasambandhena। svāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvasvāśrayaniṃṣṭhatvobhayasambandhena। dvitīye
vaiśiṣṭyaṃ coktarītyā vayamūhyam। atra saṃsargamadhye svāśraye nāvyāpyavṛttiprakārakapramāyāmatiprasaṅgaḥ। vastutastu doṣa iti sāram। svābhāvasya svāvacchedakatayā bhrame bhānavirahādāha - dīpikāyām [] saṃyogābhāveti। nanu
[] atredamavadheyamityādi। idamatra cintanīyam - lakṣaṇabhedavarṇanamayuktatamam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca vanirūtipatvasvaviśiṣṭādhikaraṇaniṣṭhatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaviśiṣṭābhāvavattāsambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca abhāve
svāśrayānadhikaraṇavṛttitvasvaviśiṣṭapratiyogitākatvobhayasambandhena। svāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnatvasvāśrayaniṣṭhatvobhayasambandhena। svaviśiṣṭeti। svaviśiṣṭetyasya ekamātravṛttidharmāvacchinnapratiyogitāyāmanvayaḥ।
viśeṣyatāyāmiti rītyā samanvayaḥ kāryaḥ। svayamūhyamiti। prakāritāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyitāvadanubhavatvaṃ bhramatvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāvacchinnasvanirūpitaprakāratāviśiṣṭaviśeṣyatānirūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena।
svaviśiṣṭaikamātravṛttidharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvavanniṣṭhatvasvani rūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvasvāśrayaniṣṭhatvobhayasambandhenetyūhyamityarthaḥ। svanirūpitatvetyādi। atrānugabhe svaśabdāḥ sarve api prakāratāparāḥ। samanvayaḥ pūrvavadūhyaḥ।
praveśena mahāgauravaprasaṅgāt। na ca [] yadavacchedena ityādi dīpikāvākyasvarasyānurodhera tathāvarṇanamiti vācyam। kapisaṃyogītyādipramāyāmativyāpteḥ। avyāpyavṛttiprakārasthalīyabhramalakṣaṇasya durvāratvāt।
viṣayabādhaviraheṇeṣṭāpatterayogāt। tasmāt uktadīpikāvākyaṃ bhramatvena lakṣyatāpradarśanaparam। evaṃ ca dīpikāyām [] vivakṣitatvādityasya lakṣyatvenetyādiḥ। [] viśeṣyitveti। atra yadyapi viśeṣyatāprakāratayoḥ tathāpi śiṣyadhīvaiśadyāya prakārāntaramapyuktamiti dhyeyam। dīpikāyām [] prasaṅgāditi। atra pañcamyartho jñānajanyajijñāsādhīnatvaṃ
vibhāgānvitam। kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ ityākāṅkṣāyāmāha - prakāśikāyām [] smṛtasyopekṣānarhatvamityādi। smṛtasya dveṣyajñānaviṣayatāvirodhirūpam। tacca prakṛte pramitikaraṇatvam। prakṛte asambhavenāsaṅgateḥ। vastutastu
nirūpyaniṣṭhaupodghātādivyātiriktaḥ sambandhaḥ prasaṅgasaṅgatiḥ। prakṛte ca caturvidhatvena pramitisādṛśyameva pramāṇasya tādṛśamiti। svabhinnatvasvaviśiṣṭaśabdaviśiṣṭatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca । svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svāvacchinnakarmakanirūpaṇottaratvasvabhinnadharmāvacchinnaviśeṣyakalakṣaṇādiprakārakajñānajanakatvobhayasaṃbandhenaḥ। śabdavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca ādheyatvasvaprayojakecchāviśiṣṭatvobhayasambandhena। icchāvaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca ādheyatvasvajanakajñānaprakāratvobhayasambandhena। svaniṣṭhaprakāratānirūpitavyāpyatvaprakāratānirūpitadharmaprakāratān irūpitaprakāratvaprakāratānirūpitanirūpakatvaprakāratānirūpitajñānatvāvacchinnaviśeṣyatākatvasaṃbandhena।
saṅgatipadārthaḥ। tatra pratyakṣatvaniṣṭhādheyatāsambandhena pratyakṣasya prathamadharme anvayaḥ। dharmatvonānvayitāvacchedakadharmaviśeṣabodhakatvaṃ saṅgatipadasya vyutpattisiddham। dvitīyadharmānvayabodhakatvamapi tathā।
dharmaviśiṣṭatvameva saṅgatiḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaviśiṣṭādhikaraṇatāviśiṣṭatvasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svabhinnadharmāvacchinnapratiyogitākabhedanirūpitatvasvaviśiṣṭaśabdavi śiṣṭabobhayasambandhena। śabde svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca prāgvat। śabdavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
ādheyatvasvaprayojakecchāviśiṣṭatvobhayasambandhena। ādheyatā svanirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakadharmāvacchinnaviśeṣyakalakṣaṇādi prakārakajñānajanakatvasambandhena। svanirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvopalakṣitadharmavyāpyadharmaprakārajñānatvāvacchinnaviśeṣyatākatvasambandhāvacchinnādheyatvaprayojakasamaraṇaviśiṣṭatvobhayasambandhena। svaprayojakasaṃbandhaniṣṭhatvasvanirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakadharmaprakārakatvasambandhāvacchinnādheyatvobhayasambandhena।
adhikaraṇatāvaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayāśrayatvasambandhena। atra ca svīkāryā। [] adṛṣṭāderityādinā īśvaraparigrahaḥ। [] anubhavatvavyāpyeti। yadyapi jñānasāmānyahetubhūtasyātmadāderavāraṇāt tadupekṣā। idaṃ bhramajanakadoṣe ativyāptivāraṇāya। nanu
niruktapramāṇalakṣaṇasya cakṣussaṃyogādāvativyāptiḥ। na ca dravyatvaniveśāt na doṣa iti vācyam। tathā sati vyāptijñānādeḥ satītyapīti। vyāpāravattvaṃ ca svajanakatvasvajanyajanakatvobhayasaṃbandhena kiñcidviśiṣṭatvam।
vyāpāratvaṃ ca tajjanyatve sati tajjanyajanakatvam। satyantam। phalavāraṇāya viśeṣyam। svajanyatvasvajanyajanakatvobhayasambandhena prameyaviśiṣṭatvamanugatārthaḥ। tadā janyatāviśiṣṭatvaṃ tadvācyam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svāśrayatvasvanirūpakajanyajanakatvobhayasambandhena। atha vā svāśrayajanakatvasvanirūpakajanyatvobhayasambandhena। janyatāviśiṣṭatvamityanugamo bodhyaḥ। phalajanakatāprayojakajanakatānirūpakatvaṃ vyāpāratvam। tena
kulālaputrādeḥ kulālādivyāpāratāprasaṅgasya nāvakāśaḥ। yadvā tajjanyajanakatvaṃ tādṛśajanakatāvacchedakasambandhatvarūpamiha bodhyam। nanvevaṃ sati śrotrendriyasya pramāṇatānupapattiḥ। tatra samavāyasyaiva [] śrotreti। nanu kāraṇatvaṃ phalāvyavahitapūrvavṛttitvam। tacca
kāraṇatāvacchedakasambandhena vācyam। anyathā yāgādeḥ svargādikāraṇatvānupapatteḥ। tathoktau tu svajanyāpūrvasambandhena yāgādestathātvāt nānupapattiḥ। evaṃ ca vyāpārasambandhāvacchinnakāraṇatvameva karaṇatvam। vyāpāravattve satīti
tatrānatiprasaṅgāt। tathā ca śabdavṛttilaukikaviṣayatāsambandhena sambhavatītyata āha [] śabdo veti। tathā ca svavṛttiśabdatādātmyasambandhena śrotrasya kāraṇatvaṃ sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। [] vadantīti। navīnamatamāha [] yadvilambāditi।
kāryotpattyabhāvaviśiṣṭatvaparyavasitam asādhāraṇatvamiti niṣkarṣaḥ। tena na svatvānanugamaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaprayojakībhūtābhāvapratiyogitvasvādhikaraṇakṣaṇavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatāvasetyādyavacchedakatvasambandhena।
svādhikaraṇatā svetaraprakṛtakāryakāraṇādhikaraṇatvasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā ādheyatvasambandhena। yastu svasetyādyavacchedakatvasambandheneti। svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhenetyarthaḥ।
svādhikaraṇetyatra ca svaśabdaḥ kāryotpatyabhāvaparaḥ। svasetyādītyatra svaśabdaḥ daṇḍādikāraṇaparaḥ। svetaretyatrasvaśabdaḥ daṇḍādikāraṇaparaḥ। tadviśiṣṭatvaṃ daṇḍe iti tasyāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvam। svaṃ daṇḍe। evaṃ svaṃ ghaṭotpattyabhāvaḥ tadadhikaraṇakṣaṇe vartate yaḥ bhedaḥ
daṇḍavadbhedaḥ tatpratiyogitāvacchedakatvaṃ ca daṇḍe। grāhyaḥ। tādṛśakṣaṇo na bhavati। ataḥ daṇḍavadbhedaḥ tādṛśakṣaṇavṛttiḥ। ghaṭotpattyabhāvaviśiṣṭatvāt daṇḍasva ghaṭāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvanirvāhaḥ।
vasetyādibhedattvasaṃbandhena। svādhikaraṇatvādikaṃ prāgvaditi rītyā anugamaḥ। sa tu tādātmyādiniveśena gauravadūṣitatvādanādaraṇīyaḥ। svabhinnatvaniveśanenāpi svavāraṇasambhavaḥ। evaṃ saṃyogādinā kapālādīnāṃ ghaṭādhikaraṇatvādyanupapattiḥ। evaṃ kāryādhikaraṇe
kāraṇābhāvasambhavāt sa eva doṣaḥ। evaṃ sarveṣāmeva dvitvādyavacchinnābhāvapratiyogitvādasambhavaḥ। ato niṣkarṣamāha [] kāryatāvacchedakasaṃbandhenetyādi। atra prākkāraṇatāghaṭakatvenābhimatasambandhāvacchinneti pūraṇīyam। tena na
sambandhāntarāvacchinnakāraṇābhāvamādāya doṣa iti dhyeyam। tṛtīyāntayatpadaṃ kāraṇatāvacchedakatvābhimatatantutvādyavacchinnaparam। ṣaṣṭhyantayatpadaṃ anyathāsiddhatvābhimatatantutvādiparam। svasetyādibhedavattvasaṃbandheneti।
svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyotākabhedavattvasambandhenetyarthaḥ। - [] yena tantunetyādi। atra ca sahaśabdaḥ sāhityam। taccaikakriyānvayaḥ। kriyā ca dhātuta eva labhyata ityanvaya eva sahaśabdārthaḥ। aananyalabhyaśabdārthaḥ' iti nyāyāt। sa cātra
prakāratānirūpakatvarūpaḥ। yeneti tṛtīyāyāḥ prakāratānvitamādheyatvamarthaḥ। viśeṣaṇasaṅgataivakāramahimnā avapūrvakagamidhātvarthajñāne tādṛśaprakāratānirūpakatvānvayaḥ। ṣaṣṭhyantārthayaddharmāvacchinnaviśeṣyakatvasya jñāne anvayaḥ। prakāratvaṃ ca
prathamāntapadārthānvayi। tathā coktasaṃbandhena bodhaḥ। evaṃ ca phalitam। dharmaviśiṣṭadharmavattvam vaiśiṣṭyaṃ cādheyatāsaṃbandhena। sā ca
svasetyādibhedavattvasambandhena। svādhikaraṇatā svāvacchinnaviśeśyakaprakṛtakāryaniyatapūrvavṛttitvaprakārakajñānatvasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacdedakatā svāvacchinnaprakāratānirūpakatvasambandhena। sāmānyapadārthavyāpakatvaniveśanam। viṣayatāmātraniveśe daṇḍādeḥ
svenānyathāsiddhiprasaṅgaḥ iti prakāratāniveśanam। paṭaṃ prati tanturūpasya rūpatvena na kāraṇatvaṃ vyabhicārādeva। ataḥ tadānīṃ sūcanāyānatiprasaktetyuktam। [] tantuviṣayakameveti।
tantvitarāsamavetatve sati nikhilatantusamavetatvarūpatvāditi bhāvaḥ। [] saṅkṣepa iti। yadyapi tantunā bodhyā। ata eva yatpadasya yaddharmāvacchinnaparatayā vyākhyānādeva tantutvena tantoranyathāsiddhivāraṇasambhavaḥ। tantuḥ
paṭaniyatapūrvavṛttiriti jñāne tantutvasya svarūpata eva bhānāt। evaṃ ca śūnyāntaviśeṣaṇaṃ vyarthathmati śaṅkā nirastā। tadāśrayavṛttirūpatvāvacchinnasyānyathāsiddhivāraṇāya tatsārthakyāt। svetaragatānvayavyatirekānadhīnānvayavyatirekavattvam। anvayaśca
prakṛtakāryasattāprayojakasattāvattvam। vyatirekaśca prakṛtakāryavirahaprayojakavirahanirūpakatvam। atra ca ādṛśasattāviśiṣṭatve sati tādṛśavyatirekaviśiṣṭatvamityanugamaḥ। svāśrayatvasvavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasaṃbandhena।
avacchedakatvaṃ svabhinnagatānvayādhīnatvasambandhena। dvitīye vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svāśrayatvasvavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā svabhinnagatavyatirekādhīnatvasambandhena। atra ca satyantaṃ vā viśeṣyadalaṃ vā ekaikamevopādeyam। ubhayaniveśe
tādṛśaviśiṣṭābhāva eva svatantrānvayavyatirekaśūnyatvam। tādṛśasattetyādi। prakṛtakāryavyatirekaprayojakavyatirekaviśiṣṭatvamityarthaḥ। prakṛtakārya paṭaḥ tatsattāprayojakasattāśrayatvaṃ tantoḥ। evaṃ
tantumadbhedaḥ tatpratiyogitāvacchedakatvaṃ tantau। evaṃ tantvabhāvaḥ tatpratiyogitvarūpaṃ tadāśrayatvaṃ tantau। evaṃ draṣṭavyaḥ। bhedaviśiṣṭatvamityanugamaḥ। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svāvacchinnabhedavattāsambandheneti। tattu dhyeyam। yadavacchinnamiti lakṣaṇaṃ sampadyate। tatra cāvacchedakakoṭipraviṣṭasyāvacchedakatvānādare daṇḍatvādāvavyāpteḥ।
sahaśabdopādāne cāsmaduktārthaparyavasānena doṣavirahāditi। ata suvaceti dhyeyamiti bhāvaḥ। tantutvasya tadvyaktitvena kāraṇatve api prathamānyathāsiddhimupapādayatāṃ matamāha - [] itarānvayeti। kiñcidviśiṣṭatvamanyathāsiddhatvamiti tu niṣkarṣaḥ।
[] dīpikāyām anyaṃ pratītyādi। anyaṃ prati prakṛtakāryetarakāryaṃ prati। apūrvavṛttitve' ityatra saptamyāḥ ayasya ca bhāvena'ityuktanyāyena jñānamarthaḥ। tasya ca janyatāsambandhenāvagame anvayaḥ। tathā ca
dvitīyānyathāsiddhasya lakṣaṇamiti phalitam। tatra ca kāraṇatājñānaṃ lakṣaṇagamanamityāśayenāha prakāśikāyām [] tathā ceti। anekadravyasamavetatveti। aṇubhinnadravyatvetyarthaḥ। [] tadupasthiteḥ prāgabhāvopasthiteḥ। svāśrayānvayetyādi। sarvatra svaśabdaḥ tanvādibhedaparaḥ।
yatsamavetamityādi। kāryamityatra yadityādiḥ kāryaṃ yatsamavetaṃ yadanuyogikasamavāyavat utpadyata ityarthaḥ। dhātvartha ādyakṣaṇāvacchinnādheyatvam। ākhyātārtha āśrayatvam। bhāsate। sadantaviśeṣaṇatāvacchedakasyoddeśyatāvacchedakatvaniyamāt।
uddeśyatāvacchedakavidheyayoravacchedyāvacchedakabhāvabhānavyutpatteḥ। tatha prati tatsamavāyikāraṇamiti vākyārthaḥ। atra ca yattatpadayoḥ yattaddharmāvacchinnaparatāmabhisandhāyāha - prakāśikāyām [] yaddharmāvacchinnamityādinā। evaṃ ca samavāyikāraṇasya lakṣaṇaṃ phalitam। tatra ca ghaṭādipratyakṣe
samavāyasambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśanam। na doṣaḥ। asamavāyikāraṇe ativyāpitavāraṇāya kāraṇatāyāṃ tādātmyasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। saṃgrahe [] kāryeṇa kāraṇena vā sahetyādi। atra ca kāryeṇa sahaikasminnarthe
samevataṃ sat yatkāraṇaṃ tadekaṃ asamavāyikāraṇam। kāraṇena vākyabhedena yojanā। vākāraśca etaddyotaka eva। sahaśabdārthaḥ samavetapadārthatāvacchedakasamavetatve anvitam। kāryeṇetyatra tṛtīyāyāḥ adhikaraṇatānvayinirūpitatvamarthaḥ। ekapadamatra
yatkiñcitparam। arthapadottarasaptamyāḥ nirūpitatvamarthaḥ। tathā ca kāraṇamiti eko vākyārthaḥ। evaṃ kāraṇenetyādivākye api bodhyam। vastutaḥ saṃgrahe [] kāryeṇa sahetyādi। atra sahaśabdārthaṃḥ sāhityam। taccaikakriyānvayitvarūpam। prakṛte
samavetatvanirūpakatvaparyavasitam। kāryeṇetyatra tṛtīyārtha ādheyatvam, ekaśabdo adhikaraṇaparaḥ। artha ityatra samavetatvānvayinirūpitatvamarthaḥ। tathā ca iti phalitam। kāraṇenetyādāvapi evameva bodhyamiti tu sāram।
kāraṇenetyatra kasya kāraṇamityākāṅkṣāyāṃ āha - prakāśikāyām [] svakāryeti। svakāryasya samavāyikāraṇenetyarthaḥ। atra ca asamavāyikāraṇasāmānyasya lakṣaṇam। kāraṇatāyāṃ dvitīyāsamavāyikāraṇasya ca tadeva lakṣaṇaṃ bodhyam। samavāyasambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। dvitīyāsamavāyikāraṇe
samavāyasambandhāvacchinnatvaniveśaḥ। prathamāsamavāyikāraṇe svāśrayasamavetatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvaniveśeḥ। atra niveśanīyamityavadheyam। tṛrītantusaṃyogāderapi tattadasamavāyikāraṇalakṣaṇa iti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ
viśeṣaṇalakṣaṇe api tadbhinnatvaṃ niveśanīyamiti tu na samyak। turītantusaṃyoge apyakṣatatvāt। yadyapyevamapi tantvākāśasaṃyogādau viśiṣṭalakṣaṇasya ativyāptiḥ। tadbhinnatvasyāpi niveśe iti।
saṅgrahe [] tadubhayabhinnamityādi। nimittakāraṇalakṣaṇe tadubhayapadaṃ samavāyyasamavāyikāraṇadvayaparamityāha - dīpikāyām [] samavāyītyādi। atra ca tatkāryaviśiṣṭaṃ tatkāryaṃ prati nimittakāraṇamiti lakṣaṇaṃ vācyam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svanirūpitasamavāyikāraṇatvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasvanirūpitāsamavāyikāraṇatvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasvanirūpitakāraṇatvatri tayasambandhena।
yadyapi dhvaṃsādau pratiyogyādeḥ nimittakāraṇatvahāniḥ। ābhāvakārye tatkāryavaiśiṣṭyaṃ niveśyamiti na doṣaḥ। dhvasādikaṃ tādṛśasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākatadabhāvasaulabhyāt। ata eva sāmānyatassamavāyyādibhinnatvāsambhavanibandhanā na kṣatiriti।
[] turīyaviṣayatānirūpakatvasyeti। anyathā saviṣayakatvābhāvena jñānatvameva nirvikalpakasya bhajyeta। jñānatvasya bhāvaḥ। [] viśeṣyādividhayetyādi। idaṃ ca viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasambandhānavagāhīti yathāśrute asambhavaḥ। nirvikalpake
tadbhānasyāpyavarjanīyatvāt। paraṃ tu ghaṭaghaṭatvasamavāyeṣu tatra turīyaviṣayatāmātramityāśayena pūritam। ādipadena prakārasaṃbandhayoḥ parigrahaḥ। viśeṣyatvādinetyarthaḥ। viśeṣyādyanavagāhītyatra dhātvartho avagāhanam, tṛtīyārtho abhedaḥ viṣayatānvayi nirūpakasya nañarthabhede anvayaḥ। tathā
ca viśeṣyatvādyabhinnaviśeṣyādiniṣṭhaviṣayatānirūpakabhinnatvalābhaḥ। tatra viśeṣyatādinirūpakābhinnamātraṃ lakṣaṇamityabhiprāyeṇāha - [] tathā ceti। [] jñānatvaghaṭitamiti। ghaṭādiṣvativyāptivāraṇāya idamuktam। [] viśeṣyaviśeṣaṇasambandhānavagāhītyatra dīpikāvākye na dvandvaḥ। vyācakṣāṇānāṃ matamāha - [] kecittviti।
viṣayatāśrayetyarthaḥ। tajjñānīyaviṣayatāśrayavaiśiṣṭyapratiyogitvaṃ tajjñāne prakāratvamityarthaṃḥ। nanu ghaṭabhūtalasaṃyogā iti jñāne ghaṭasya prakāratāpattiḥ। ata āha - [] saṃsargāvacchinneti। nanu pūrvoktayuktyā nirvikalpake api saṃsargabhānasyāvaśyakatvāt asambhava ityata āha [] saṃsargateti। lāghavādityasya
saṃsargāvacchinnaviṣayatāśanyatvarūpalakṣaṇāpekṣayetyādiḥ। tathā ca saṃsargānavagāhitvaṃ saṃsarganiṣṭhaviṣayatvānirūpakatvam। saṃsarganirūpitāvacchinnatvavadviṣayatāśūnyatvam। tatra ca saṃsargāvacchinnetyādilakṣaṇāpekṣayā gauravam।
bhāvaḥ। anyathā uktarītyā nirvikalpake ativyāpteriti bhāvaḥ। ayamatra bhāvaḥ - dīpikāvākyāsvārasyam। asmanmate tu lakṣaṇatrayalābhārthatayā na taduktivaiphalyamiti। ananu viśiṣṭabuddhirviśeṣaṇajñānajanyā
pratītyādi। atra [yadi] viśiṣṭabuddhitvaṃ na syāditi tarko abhimata ityāśayenāha - [] bhāva iti। dīpikāyāñ [] anavasthāprasaṅgāditi। jñānamanumitau bhāsate। athavā viśeṣaṇaniṣṭhāyāṃ iti bhāvaḥ। idaṃ ca svasmin
yadviśeṣaṇaṃ tadviṣayakadhījanyatvarūpasādhyaviśeṣalābhāyābhihitam। tadanyaviśeṣaṇajñānajanyatvasiddhimādāyārthāntaratāpatteriti bhāvaḥ। saṅgrahe [] indriyārthasannikarṣajanyamityādi। idaṃ ca janyapratyakṣasyaiva lakṣyatvābhiprāyeṇa। teneśvarapratyakṣasya nityatvāt
tatrāvyāptiśaṅkānirāsaḥ। anyathā tatsaṅgraho bodhyaḥ। atra yadyapi ātmamanaḥsaṃyogasya jñānasāmānyahetutvāt anumityādāvativyāptiḥ। manasa janyatāyāmanubhavatvavyāpyadharmāvacchinnatvaniveśāt na doṣaḥ।
yathāśrute jñānapadametattātparyagrāhakam। niruktobhayābhāvaniveśane tvākāśādivāraṇāya jñānapadam। jñānatvaṃ lakṣaṇam। anumityādīnāṃ vyāptyādijñānakaraṇakatvāt na tatrātivyāptiḥ।
īśvarapratyakṣasyājanyatvāt। janyapratyakṣe tu indriyasyaiva karaṇatvācca lakṣaṇasamanvayaḥ। nirvikalpakasya savikalpakāraṇatvāt karaṇatvaṃ niveśitamityāhuḥ। dīpikāyām [] dravyapratyakṣa ityādi। atra ca
cakṣussaṃyogasya kāraṇatvaṃ vācyam। tatra rūpādau vyabhicārāvāraṇāya kāryadiśi dravyavṛttitvaniveśanam। vyabhicāravāraṇāya laukikatvapraveśaḥ। evaṃ daṇḍādyaṃśe tadbodhyam। evaṃ davyasamavetavṛttilaukikaviṣayatāsaṃbandhena
cākṣuṣaṃ prati svarūpasaṃbandhena cakṣussaṃyuktasamavāyasya kāraṇatvam। atra vyabhicāranirāsāya kāryadiśi vṛttyantam। yadyapi tadavasthodoṣaḥ। tathāpi dravyānyatvasya samavetaviśeṣaṇatvābhyupagamāt na doṣaḥ। vṛttyantaṃ ca
rūpatvādijātipratyakṣe vyabhicāravāraṇāya bodhyam। tadvāraṇāya viṣayatāyāṃ laukikatvaniveśaḥ। evaṃ nīlādyaṃśe tathā। evaṃ dravyasamavetasamavetavṛttilaukikaviṣayatāsaṃbandhena cākṣuṣaṃ prati cakṣussaṃyuktasamavetasamavāyasya kāraṇatvam।
vyabhicāravāraṇāyātra laukikatvaniveśaḥ। svatantratryaṇukapakṣe tryaṇukatadrūpādau vyabhicāravāraṇāya vṛttyantam। matāntare api tādṛśaviṣayatāyā ākasmikatāvāraṇāya tanniveśyameva। vṛttyantam। śabdatvasāmānyapratyāsattijanye atītādiśabdaviṣayake
laukikatvaniveśanam। śabdasamavetavṛttilaukikaviṣayatāsaṃbandhena śrāvaṇaṃ prati śrotrasamavetasamavāyasya kāraṇatvam। śabde vyabhicāravāraṇāya vṛttitvaviśeṣaṇam। vyabhicāravāraṇāya laukikatvaniveśaḥ। evamanyatrāpi bodhyam।
kathaṃ sannikarṣaṃṣāḍvidhyam। yadi ca tāsāṃ viśeṣaṇatātvenānugamaḥ tarhi saṃyuktasamavāyādīnāṃ samavāyatvenānugamaḥ। kiṃ na syādityāśaṃṅkāṃ nirākaroti [] atredamavadheyamityādinā। [] viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvasannikarṣeti।
viśeṣyatvaviśeṣaṇatvānyatarasannikarṣetyarthaḥ। [] ghaṭopalabdhidaśāyāmityādi। ghaṭavattāniścayadaśāyāmāpattiḥ। na ca ghaṭābhāvarūpaviṣayavirahādeva na ghaṭavati deśe ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣaprasaṃgaḥ। ghaṭāsattve kathaṃ ghaṭavattāniścayasaṃbhava iti vācyam। ghaṭaśūnyadeśe api
ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣāpattisambhavāt। ghaṭādimati deśe api dharmyantaraghaṭitasannikarṣabalena ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣāpattisaṃbhavācceti। [] pramāṇāntaratvamityādi। yadyapyanyat pramāṇaṃ pramāṇāntaramiti tattusahakāritayopagatāyā anupalabdheḥ naiyāyikairapyupagatam।
ko api doṣaḥ। abhāvapramiteḥ pratyakṣarūpāyā eva naiyāyikairupagamāt। ata evāgre vijātīyapramitikaraṇatvakalpanamityuktam। nanu [] tarkasyetyādinā। [] viparyaye - āpādakābhāvavyāpyābhāve। pratiyogitvaṃ koṭyanvitaṃ saptamyarthaḥ। tatkoṭiparyavasāyitvaṃ - tasya tarkasya
koṭiḥ āpādyarūpā tadviṣayakatvamityarthaḥ। [] sattvasya - sattvaprasakteḥ virodhinī yā upalabdhiriti। svarūpataḥ। tathā ca taddhatubhūtāpādyavyatirekaniścayapratibandhakatvam। pratibandhakatvaṃ vivakṣaṇīyam। anyathā
āhāryapratiyogyupalambhadaśāyāmabhāvagrahānāpatteriti vadanti [] virodhitvaviśeṣaṇamiti। nanvandhakāre niṣkṛṣṭārthamāha - [] pratiyogisattetyādinā। pratiyogisattvaviṣayakāpattijanyāpattiviṣayetyarthaḥ। atrāyamāśayaḥ - sarvatrābhāvapratyakṣasthale'yadyatra iti। [] pratiyogisattāpādanetyādinā
pratiyoginiṣṭhavyāpyatānirūpitavyāpakatvaṃ vivakṣaṇīyam। adhikaṃ muktābalīprakāśādau draṣṭavyamiti। keṣāñcinmatamāha- [] kecittviti। ata eva upalambhābhāve tādṛśaprayojyatvaviśeṣaṇadānādeva। [] āhurityasvarasasūcanam।
tadbījantu pratiyogisattve tarkitatvaviśeṣaṇavaiyarthyam। pūrvamate tarkitapadasyopayogaḥ। etanmate tu kvāpyupayogaḥ। evamadhikaraṇabhedenābhāvabhedavirahāt andhakāre ghaṭābhāvapratyakṣāpattyavāraṇaṃ ceti। nyūnatāparihārāyāha - [] atredamiti। [] tatra-darśitatrividhapratyāsattimadhye। nanu
kathametādṛśārthalābha ityatrāha - [] sāmānyamityādi। dhūmatvādisāmānyetyarthaḥ। jātītyarthaḥ। viṣayo veti। nanu pratyāsatitopagamenetyata āha - [] atīteti। nanu vinaiva sannikarṣamindriyeṇa tatpratyakṣaṃ kuto na syādityatrāha - [] indriyāṇāmiti। asannikṛṣṭānāmityasya pratyakṣetyasya ca
tadarthetyādiḥ। upayujyata ityanuṣajyate। [] saurabheṇeti। tadindriyagrahaṇayogyapadārthasyaiva yogyeti। muktāvalīprakāśoktaṃ kāraṇatāvacchedakasambandhādikamabhisandhāyāha - saṅkṣepa iti।
। । [] pratyakṣopajīvakatvasaṅgatyeti। pratyakṣasya saṅgatyetyarthaḥ। nirūpaṇānvayi jñānajanyajijñāsāprayojyatvaṃ tṛtīyārthaḥ। jñāne ca viṣayitayā prakṛtyarthānvayaḥ। saṅgatipradarśanaṃ
syāditi tannirāsāya। pūrvottaragranthayoḥ ekavākyatāpratipattirapi saṅgatipradarśanaprayojanamityapi draṣṭavyam। tādṛśapratipattiśca ityādyanyatra vistaraḥ। [] lakṣayatīti dīpikāvākyāt lakṣaṇaprakārakajñānajanakaśabdānukūlakṛtimānityartho labhyate। tatra
syāditi nirūpayatītyuktam। nirūpaṇaṃ ca lakṣaṇasvarūpaprāmāṇyādyanyatamaprakārakajñānānukūlaśabdaḥ ato na nyūnatā। evamagre api draṣṭavyam। saṅgrahe [] anumitikaraṇamanumānamiti। itivadatra na nirākāṅkṣatā। anumitikaraṇatvaṃ
cānumitiniṣṭhānubhavatvavyāpyadharmāvacchinnkāryatānirūpitakāraṇatāśrayatvam। kathamuktavākyasya prāmāṇyamityata āha - anumānapadasyeti। tathā bhāvaḥ। pūrvadalakṣaṇāvirahapakṣa iti। pūrvapadalakṣaṇāpaśe tu
anumānapadasyānumitikaraṇārthakatve api na nirākāṅkṣateti bhāvaḥ। ativyāptiḥ। nanu parāmarśajanyaṃ jñānamityanumiterlakṣaṇaṃ sambhavatīti taduktisāphalyāmiti vācyam। vyabhicāraśaṅkāyā durvāratvāt। ataḥ saṅgrahe
anumitilakṣaṇakathanamucitamityabhiprāyeṇa bhāvamāha - [] tathā ceti। virītajñānamātropalakṣaṇaparamityabhiprāyeṇāha - [] viparītajñānottarapratyakṣaṃ pratīti। miśrādīnāmiti śeṣaḥ। etena prātyakṣikaniścaye nātivyāptiriti sūcitam। nanu [] sthāṇupuruṣasaṃśayānantaramiti dīpikāvākyamasaṅgatam।
sthāṇupuruṣakoṭikatvāyogāt ityata āha - [] idamiti। [] āhuḥ ityasvarasasūcanam। tadbījantu pratyakṣajananādityuttaragranthavirodhaḥ। sthāṇureveti pratyakṣajananāditi vaktavyatvāt। ataḥ tādṛśagranthaparyālocanayā kintu eka eva saṃśaya iti।
teneti। ātmādeḥ bhāvaḥ। iti। nanu puruṣa iti pratyakṣajananāditi vaktavyam kimevakāropādānenetyāśaṅyāha - [] puruṣa evetīti। nanu
idamupalakṣaṇamiti। [] idaṃ bādhakayuktipradarśanam। [] upalakṣaṇam bādhakayuktyantarasyāpi sūcakam। nanu viśiṣṭaparāmarśatvāvacchinnatvameva kuto na niveśitam। kāraṇatvopagamāt। evaṃ viśeṣapadarśanasya
syāt। saṃśayottarapratyakṣe tivyāpteranavakāśādintyata āha - [] eteneti। janakatāyāṃ pakṣatāsahakṛtaparāmarśajanyatvasyaiva vivakṣaṇenetyarthaḥ। [] viśeṣaṇatāvacchedakaprakārakanirṇayavidhayetyanena tādṛśaviśiṣṭaparāmarśatvāvacchinnajanakatākatvamastīti sūcitam। saṅkṣepa iti। atrāyamāśayaḥ pakṣatāsahakṛtasyaiva parāmarśasya
tadartho vaktavyaḥ। evaṃ pakṣatāpratyakṣe ativyāptivāraṇāya parāmarśajanyatvopādānam। parāmarśajanyatveti। parāmarśaniṣṭhajanakatānirūpitajanyatvetyarthaḥ।
viśakalitajñāneti। jñānadvayasādhāraṇyānurodhenetyarthaḥ। jñānaviśiṣṭajñānatveneti। karādiviśeṣyakapuruṣatvavyāpyatvaprakārakajñānaviśiṣṭakaradiṃprakārakedantvāvacchinnaviśeṣyakajñānatvenetyarthaḥ।
ativyāpteranavakāśāditi। virahāditi bhāvaḥ। doṣaḥ। pakṣatāpratyakṣatvaparāmarśapratyakṣatvoḥ avacchedakayoḥ bhedādityādikaṃ anumitigranthādau vistareṇoktaṃ draṣṭavyamiti।
śakyamityabhiprāyeṇa śaṅkate - [] yadyapīti। ghanagarjanena sambhavatīti nātṛ tadvivakṣaṇaṃ śakyamityabhiprāyeṇa samādhatte - [] tathāpīti। [] sādhyānumitīcchāyā iti। atra itīcchādaśāyāmanumityāpattiḥ। anumityasāniveśe api ghaṭānumitiḥ bhūyāt itīcchāyā vāraṇāsambhavaḥ।
bhūyāditīcchāvāraṇaṃ na sambhavati। haṭasādhyobhayasamūhālambanānumiterviṣayatvasambhavāt। ataḥ bodhyaḥ। abhāvapratiyogitāyāṃ ca tādṛśecchātvāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśyam, tena tādṛśecchāghaṭobhayābhāvādikamādāya a doṣaḥ।
tādṛśecchātvāvacchinnatvaṃ ca tādṛśecchātvaparyāptāvacchedakatākatvam। tacca ādaśecchātvetaradharmānavacchinnatvaparyavasitam। tena caitrasya na doṣa iti। yat pakṣatāpratyakṣatvaṃ tadavacchinnatvābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ।
ghaṭasādhyeti। aghaṭavahnyubhayānumitirbhūyāt' iti icchā atra vivakṣitā। na doṣa iti। siddhisiṣādhayiṣobhayasattvakāle na pakṣatānupapattirityarthaḥ।
tādṛśecchātvetyādi। tathā ca ghaṭavahnyubhayānumitirbhūyāditīcchāyāḥ tādṛśābhāvasya na uttejakābhāvarūpatetyāśaya। nānumityanupapattiḥ। evamagre api pratiyogitāyāṃ viśiṣṭasiddhitvetaradharmāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśyam। tena
yatkiñcidātmavṛttitvaviśiṣṭatādṛśasiddhyabhāvasya ca vyudāsaḥ। anyathā siṣādhayiṣāṃ vinā siddhisattve anumityāpatteḥ। yadyapi siṣādhayiṣāvirahasyaivāsaṃgrahaḥ। tathāpi vivakṣaṇīyam। evaṃ
niveśyamiti। evamanyatrāpi bodhyam। [] samavāyenābhāva iti। sattvāt anumityanupapattiḥ ataḥ samavāyenetyuktam। avacchinnapratiyogitākatvamabhāvānvayi tṛtīyārthaḥ। nanu siddhisiṣādhayiṣayoḥ sattve anumittyanupapattitādavasthyam।
siṣādhayiṣāyāḥ samavāyenātmanyeva sattvāt ityata āha - [] svarūpetyādi। tathā ca siṣādhayiṣāvirahavaiśiṣṭyaṃ siddhau na svarūpasambandhena, yenoktadoṣaḥ syāt। api tu tathā ca noktadoṣa iti bhāvaḥ। [] tadviśiṣṭāyāssaddheriti bhramo nirastaḥ। tathā sati siddhisiṣādhayiṣayoḥ
tādṛśaprakārakatveti। siṣādhayiṣāvirahapadena vivakṣita iti bhāvaḥ। sattve anumityanupapattitādavasthyāt। siddhyabhāvarūpaviśeṣyavirahāditi dhyeyam। [] siddhessamavāyenābhāva ityartha iti।
viśiṣṭasiddhidaśāyāmanumitivāraṇāya samavāyenetyuktam। atra sattvādanumityanupapattiḥ, ataḥ tanniveśaḥ। anavacchinnasvarūpasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvaṃ tadarthaḥ। tena ghaṭādyavacchedena siṣādhayiṣāvirahasya siṣādhayiṣāvatyapyātmani sattve api na kṣatiḥ।
vaktavyam। anyathā siddhisattve ghaṭādyavacchedena tadabhāvasattvāt viśiṣṭasiddhidaśāyāmanumityāpatteḥ। [] sādhyasiddhiḥ pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭa ityādi। pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviśeṣyatānirūpitasādhyatāvacchedakadharmasaṃbandhāvacchinnaprakāratāśālisaṃśayānyajñānamityarthaṃḥ।
pakṣatāvacchedakāderniveśanam। vahnimānityādyanumitivirodhitāvāraṇāyeti bodhyam। parvato saṃśayānyatvaniveśanam। tacca na sāmānyataḥ saṃśayabhinnatvama, tathā svapratiyogamattveti। svaṃ siṣādhayiṣāvirahaḥ tatpratiyogi
siṣādhayiṣā tadvattvamātmanaḥ। sa eva doṣa iti। siddhisiṣādhayiṣayoḥ sattve api anumityanupapattirityarthaḥ। sādhyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvāprakārakatvam।
vahnyabhāvavānityādigrahasyāpratibandhakatvaprasaṅgaḥ। tathāpi tādṛśābhāvatvāvacchinnaprakāratātannirūpakatvābhāvavivakṣaṇāt na doṣaḥ। svarūpasambandhāvacchinnatvaṃ niveśanīyam। anyathā parvataḥ vahnyabhāvavāṃścetyādiniścayasyāpi virodhitāpattiḥ।
niveśyaḥ। anyathā parvato vahnimān vahnimadanyo veti saṃśayasya virodhitāpattirityalamadhikena। sambhavati। tadeva ca na ghaṭate। yogyavibhuviśeṣaguṇānāṃ siddhiścetyādinā। [] ataḥ samūhālambanaparyantānudhāvanāt।
parāmarśeti। anyathā yatra prathamaṃ parāmarśaḥ tataḥ siddhiḥ, tataḥ siṣādhayiṣā, tataḥ anumitiḥ na jāyata eva। parāmarśasya pūrvaṃ naṣṭatvāt ato nātra prayojanaṃ sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ। tathā ca sattve vyabhicāra iti bhāvaḥ।
[] saptamītatpuruṣāṅgīkāra iti। nanvatra vyāptiviśiṣṭasya pakṣadharmateti ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣaḥ kuto nāśritaḥ, sa eva cāśrayaṇīyaḥ। durvañcatvena saptamyanupapatteriti cet - na। sādhuriti sūcanāyaiva iha saptamīsamāsādaraḥ। tatra pramāṇaṃ
coktasūtre cakāropādānameva। anyathā tadvaiyarthyāpatteriti। spaṣṭaṃ cedam vyutpattivāde saptamyarthavicāre। nanu parāmarśatvāpattyā tato anumityāpattiḥ ato niṣkarṣamāha - [] vyāptyavacchinnetyādinā। atra ca vyabhicāristhale vyāptighaṭakatāvatpadārthānāṃ niveśanīyā। tathā ca
hetuprakāratānirūpitavyāpakatvaprakāratānirūpitasādhyaprakāratānirūpi tasāmānādhikaraṇyaprakāratānirūpitetyarthaḥ। niveśyā। vahnivyāpyadhūvān hradaḥ, parvato ghaṭavāniti viśeṣyatāprakāratayornirūpyanirūpakabhāvaniveśaḥ। vahnivyāpyadhūvat pakṣatāvacchedakaniveśaḥ। parvato vahnivyāpyadhūmavān na veti
saṃśayādanumitivāraṇāya niścaya ityuktam। niścayatvaṃ ca na sāmānyataḥ saṃśayabhinnatvamāṃśikasaṃśayasyājanakatvāpatteḥ। kiṃ tu dhyeyam। ityabhiprāyeṇāha dīpikāyām [] yatretyādi। [] abhinayaḥ abhilāpakaśabdakathanam। [] sāhacaryaniyama iti
saṃgrahavākye sahacarata iti sahacarau tayorbhāvaḥ sāhacaryam। sāmānādhikaraṇyamityarthaḥ। tasya niyamaḥ prācīnamate sādhyābhāvavadavṛttitvādivaiśiṣṭyam। nīvīnamate eva pratyayārthaḥ svāditi gauravaṃ niyamasya viśeṣyatve durvāram।
noktarītyā gauravāvakāśa iti manasi nidhāya [] niyatasāmānādhikaraṇyamityuktam। [] sādhyābhāvavadavṛtti tvādirūpamiti। ādinā sādhyavadanyāvṛttitvaparigrahaḥ। sādhyābhāvavadavṛttitvādirūpaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ ghaṭakamiti yāvat। tādṛśaṃ yatreti vyutpattyā sādhyābhāvavadavṛttitvādighaṭitamityarthaḥ। atra vahnimān
gaganādityādiviruddhavāraṇāya iśeṣyam। dravyaṃ sattvāt ityādivyabhicārivāraṇāya iśeṣaṇam। vahne'rityādāvapi prayojanaṃ bodhyam। kecittu - sāhacaryaniyama [] niyatasāmānādhikaraṇyamiti - iti vyācakruḥ। tadasat

viśeṣaṇamiti। niyamarūpaṃ viśeṣaṇamityarthaḥ। śabdārthakathanamiti tattvam। tathā ca niyatasāmānādhikaraṇśarīre bhāvaḥ। tathātve doṣamāha []
idaṃ vācyamityādinā। atra ca [] sādhyābhāvāpratisaddheriti। [] pratiyogitānavacchedakasādhyatāvacchedakāvicchannetyartha iti। ativyāptivāraṇāya viśiṣya sādhyatāvacchedakapraveśaḥ। yadyapi tviti nyāyādakṣatam। tathāpi tādṛśapratiyogitānavacchedaketyādinā
na doṣaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ svasetyādibhedavattvasaṃbandhena। svādhikaraṇatā avacchedakatāsaṃbandhena। tathā ca mahānasīyatvādau tādṛśaviṣayatāvacchedakatāvirahāt lakṣaṇasaṅgatiḥ। viṣayatāyāṃ sādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviṣayatā tadvattvamityarthaḥ। svapadena
hetusamānādhikaraṇaḥ ghaṭādyabhāvo grāhyaḥ। svasetyādibhedavattvaṃ nāma svādhikaraṇavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvam। vahnitvāvacchinnaviṣayateti samanvayo bodhyaḥ। avacchedakatvaṃ tannirūpakatvarūpamiti na kṣatiriti। na
taddoṣatādavasthyamiti vācyam। taditarasambandhānavacchinnatvaparyavasitasya vivakṣitatvāt। [] hetutāvacchedakāvacchinnaparamiti। rakṛtahetutāvacchedakatāvyāpakatāvacchedakatākanirūpakatākaparami tyarthaḥ। tādṛśanirūpakatākatvamadhikaraṇatānvayi। tena viśiṣṭasattāhetuke
parāstā। niveśyam। yatra tatra pūrvoktarītyā vilakṣaṇāvacchedakatākatvamiti na kiñcidavahīnam। tātparyamiti dhyeyam।
guṇakarmānyatvaviśiṣṭetyarthaḥ। nanu viśiṣṭaśuddhayorbhendāt kathaṃ hetvadhikaraṇatva guṇāderityata āha - [] viśiṣṭasyeti। dravyatvābhāvasya hetvadhikaraṇaguṇādiniṣṭhatve apīti yojanā। guṇādītyādinā karmādisaṅgrahaḥ।
ādheyatā vivakṣitā। tathā ca prakṛtahetutāvacchedakatāvyāpikā yā vivakṣitam। tena dravyaṃ viśiṣṭasattvāt ityatra hetutāvacchedakatā guṇakarmānyatvaviśiṣṭasattāvān' iti pratītivirahāt। api tu guṇakarmānyatvaviśiṣṭasattāvat' iti pratīteḥ। ataḥ
nāvyāptiriti bhāvaḥ। svarūpasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhādheyatānirūpakādhikaraṇanirūpitasamavāyasaṃbandhāvacchinnavṛttitvam। tadavacchinnanirūpitādhikaraṇatāvattvena guṇāderatathātvāditi bhāvaḥ। saṃyogādyavacchinnavahnyādyabhāvasattvāt apyavyāptisambhavaḥ। tathāpi
prakārāntareṇa phalamāha - [] nāvyāptiriti। ātmabhinnaṃ hetvadhikaraṇatāviraheṇa lakṣaṇasamanvayasambhavāt nāsambhavo darśitaḥ। saṃyogasāmānyābhāvasya vṛkṣe savivādatvādāha [] kapīti। [] pratiyogivaiyadhikaraṇyasyeti। yadyapi sāmānyataḥ pratiyoginiveśe tādṛśaviśeṣaṇākrāntābhāvāprasiddhiḥ।
vyāpterasarvajñadurjñeyatāpattiḥ। tathāpi niveśyamiti na doṣaḥ। atra ca svapratiyogyadhikaraṇāvṛttitvasya vyabhicāriṇyatiprasaṅgaḥ। adhikaraṇabhedenābhāvabhedaviraheṇa sādhyābhāvasya vyāpakatāghaṭakatvāsambhavāt।
[] adhikamiti। ghaṭādyabhāvaḥ। evaṃ prayitogitā saṃyoganiṣṭhā, tannirūpakaḥ saṃyogābhāvaḥ tadanyaḥ ghaṭādyabhāva iti samanvayo draṣṭavyaḥ। saṅgrahe [] svayamevetyādi। asya vākyasya

nyāyabahirbhūntavākyavārakatvena sārthakyamāha - [] vākyapadasyeti। nigamanaghaṭake sādhyavānayamiti bhāge atiprasaṅga vyudāsāyāvayavatvasya praveśaḥ। [] agre api - hetvādilakṣaṇe api। dīpikāyām [] pañcamyantamityādi। pañcamī antaḥ yasmin iti vyutpattyā pañcamīviśiṣṭatvaparyavasitam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ vaghaṭitatvasvaniṣṭhabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasambandhena।
avacchedakatā vaghaṭakapadapūrvatvasambandhena। tanniveśaphalasya tasmāt liṅgapratipādakatvaniveśaphalamāha - prakāśikāyām [] ayaṃ na daṇḍādityādinā। [] daṇḍasaṃyogājanyetyādi। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayorupādānam। tadantatvaparyantaniveśasya nigamanavāraṇameva phalam। parvato
vahnimānityādipratijñāyāḥ pañcamyantatvavirahāt tadupekṣaṇam। ayaṃ daṇḍādityādeḥ sampradāyavirodhāt na daṇḍādityuktam। puṃstvādirūpaliṅga paratāyāḥ liṅgapade bhramavāraṇāyāha - [] hetviti। yadyapi daṇḍasaṃyogājanyadravyatvāta vivakṣaṇāt na doṣaḥ।
yatpadaṃ tatpūrvatvābhāvavatī yā pañcamī tadghaṭitatvaṃ samudāye। pañcamīparam। pañcamyantasamudāyaparam। daṇḍādityākārakasyaiva nigamanasya vācyatvena tatrātiprasaṅgaḥ।
na। liṅge vyāptyaṃśasyādhikasya bhānāditi। upanayādāvapi vyāptipratipādakatvasattvāt āha - [] prakṛtahetumatītyādi। vādivākye svārasikalakṣaṇāyā evātiprasañjakatvādāha - [] nirūḍheti। anāditātparyaviṣayībhūtārthaniṣṭhetyarthaḥ। sambhavati
sārthakatve nairarthakyamanyāyyamiti āśayavānāha - [] athaveti। nanūdāharaṇāt vyāptibodhābhāve tasya vyāptiparatvaṃ na nirvahatītyata āha - [] tathāceti। tathā vyāptipratipādaketyanena vivakṣitaṃ upapādanīyamiti bhāvaḥ। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - ayaṃ na daṇḍāt syāt। evaṃ nirdhūmo
dhūmavānityādyanvayyudāharaṇasya yattadarthāvivakṣāyāmanupapattiriti। dīpikoktopanayalakṣaṇasya nigamane ativyāptimāśaṅkyāha - [] pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭaviśeṣyaketi। nirūpyanirūpakabhāvaniveśāt na doṣa iti bhāvaḥ। [] prayujyata itiśeṣapūraṇeneti। idaṃ ca pakṣadharmatājñānāya - kriyāpadasāpekṣatvāduktam। pakṣadharmatājñānamartho yasmāditi
vyutpattisvīkāre tu śeṣapūraṇasya nāvaśyakatā। vacanamityadhyāhāreṇa napuṃsakatvamiti dhyeyam। [] nigamanalakṣaṇe hetossādhyamiti pañcamīsamāsaḥ। pañcamīti yogavibhāgenopapādanīyaḥ। yadvā hetoḥ sādhyamiti ṣaṣṭhī śaiṣikī
jñānajñāpyatvaṃ bodhayati। idānīṃ asup sape'ti samāso bodhya hetujñāneti। [] sādhyavadviṣayaketi। tādṛśasādhyaprakārakapakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviśeṣyatāketyarthaḥ। nanu dīpikāyām [] abādhitatvādikamiti।
ādipadenāsatpratipakṣitatvaparigrahaḥ। abādhitatvādikam - abādhitatvādipratipattiḥ। tena yathāśrute viṣayasya janyatvaghaṭitaprayojanatvāsambhavādasaṅgatiriti nirastam। uttarakālamityatyantasaṃyoge dvitīyā। tena
jāyata iti labhyate। uktarītyā tatpratipatteḥ śābdatvāsambhavādāhaprakāśikāyām [] mānaso draṣṭavnaya iti। kḷptasyeti। etena niyatapūrvavṛttitvamubhayasammatamiti sūcitam। dīpikāyām
[] kimarthamaṅgīkartavya iti। taddhetoreveti nyāyāditi bhāvaḥ। [] atra tvadabhimatetyādi। etena mīmāṃsakasyāpi jñānadvaye pūrvavṛttitvaṃ kalpanīyamiti sūcitam। [] śābdetīti। tadbodhakapadamantareṇa tadbhānāsambhavāditi
bhāvaḥ। etena pratyakṣasthale sannikarṣavaśāt kasyacit sūcitam। dīpikāyām [] parāmarśasyāvaśyakatayeti। viśiṣṭaparāmarśasyānumitipūrvamupeyatayetyarthaḥ। nanaṃ kvacit viśiṣṭaparāmarśakalpanayetyata āha [] lāghaveneti। kasya
lāghavamityāśaṅgāyāmāha prakāśikāyām [] kalpanālāghavenetyartha iti। [] jñānadvaye-vyāptijñānatvapakṣadharmatājñānatvāvacchinnadvaye। [] viśiṣṭaparāmarśe-vyāptiviśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhiparāmarśatvāvacchinne। pūrvoktadharmāvacchinnadvaye tatkalpanasya gurutvāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu nopeyate। api tu vyāptigrahaviśiṣṭapakṣadharmatājñānatvena tathātvamupeyate। evaṃ
durapahnavam। vinigamanāvirahastulya eva। viśiṣṭaparāmarśāvyavahitottaratvaṃ niveśyaiva parihartavyaḥ। anyathā vyabhicāraprasaṅgāt ityatrāha [] vastutastviti। [] avadheyamiti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ -
dvidhā jñānatvasya ca praveśaḥ āvaśyakaḥ। asmanmate tu na tathā। evaṃ vinigamanāvirahāt kāraṇatādvayaṃ tanmate vaktavyam। asmanmate tu kāraṇatādvayāvakāśaḥ। evaṃ viśiṣṭavaiśiṣṭyāvagāhitvāyogāditi lāghavamiti। [] vinigamanāviraheṇeti। liṅgaviśeṣitaparāmarśatvenaiva
kāraṇatvaṃ vaktavyamityatra niyāmakābhāvenetyarthaḥ। uddeśyatāsaṃbandhena dhūmādihetoḥ kāraṇatvaṃ durghaṭamityāśayenāha - [] tatrāpyanumiteriti। hetusādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyarūpānvayasahacāraparaḥ। grahagrāhyatvaṃ tṛtīyārthaḥ। ata eva kevalavyatirekinirāsaḥ। vyatirekeṇetyatrāpi
vyatireko vyatirekasahacāraḥ। sādhyābhāvahetvabhāvayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyarūpaḥ। tṛtīyārthaḥ pūrvavat prakāśikāyām anvayasahacāretyādi। kevalavyatirekivāraṇāya satyantam। kevalānvayivyudāsāya viśeṣyam। anvayavyāptimattvamātraniveśe
ityādivyatirekivāraṇāsambhavaḥ। uktapariṣkāre iti na doṣaḥ। viśeṣyadale tu viśiṣṭayaiva vyāptirupādeyā। na tu tādṛśagrahagrāhyatvenāpīti bodhyam। saṃgrahe [] vahnau sādhya iti। vahniniṣṭhasādhyatānirūpakaṃ dhūmavattvamityarthaḥ। dṛṣṭāntavākye mahānasādipadaṃ saptamyantam।
yatretyanurodhāt। kevalānvayitvameva hetorlakṣaṇam kuto noktamityata āha - [] kevalānvayisādhyaketi। ghaṭo abhidheyaḥ pṛthivītvāt ityādihetorityarthaḥ। [] tadeva kevalānvayitvameva। nanu
gaganābhāvavān meyatvāt ityādāvavyāptiḥ। sādhyasya gaganādyātmakābhāvapratiyogitvāt। evaṃ saṃyogābhāvavān saṃyogādyātmakābhāvapratiyogitvādityatrāha - [] niravacchinneti। sapatamīnirdeśyaṃ yat vilakṣaṇamavacchedyatvaṃ tadrahitetyarthaḥ। tenādheyatāyāḥ kiñciddharmāvacchedyatvaniyame api na
kṣatiḥ। tathā ca gaganādeḥ vṛttimattvābhāvāt saṃyogādiniṣṭhavṛtteḥ niravacchinnatvavirahācca noktadoṣadvayāvakāśa daiti bhāvaḥ। kecittu - svavirodhivṛttimadatyanatābhāvāpratiyogitvaṃ kevalānvayitvam। tāvadanyatamatvaṃ ca durgraham। pratiyogyupādāne
vṛttimadatyantābhāvaviśiṣṭānyatvaṃ tat। aiśiṣṭyaṃ svapratiyogitvasvaniṣṭhabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhāyasambandhena। avacchedakatā svādhikaraṇavṛttitvasaṃbandhāvacchinnā। ato na doṣa ityāhuḥ। taccintyam
vṛttimattvaviśeṣaṇaniveśavaiyarthyāpatteḥ। saṃyogābhāvasya kevalānvayitābhaṅgāpatteḥ। saṃyogādirūpābhāvasya tathātvāt। vṛttāvapi niravacchinnatvaniveśane ca prakṣālanāddhinyāyāpatteḥ।
anvayavyāptiśūnyatve sati vyatirekavyāptimattvamartho labhyate। atra viśeṣyamiti bodhyam। tacca na ghaṭate niściteti। atrāpyanvayavyatirekivyabhicāriṇoḥ vāraṇāya viśeṣaṇaviśeṣye।
vyatirekavyāptimattvamevālam na lakṣaṇāsaṅgatiriti। tadatiriktadṛṣṭāntadaurlabhyenānvayavyāptiniścayāsambhavāditi bhāvaḥ। vikalpāsaṅgaterāha - [] pṛthivītaratvāvacchinneti। nanu ādye [] yatretyādinā dīpikoktaṃ dūṣaṇamasaṅgatam।
atyantābhāvaḥ ghaṭābhāvaḥ tadviśiṣṭaḥ ghaṭaḥ tadanyatvaṃ abhidheyatvādeḥ। ghaṭasyeti। anvayasahacāreti। iṣṭāpattiḥ kuto na saṃbhavatītyāśṅkya bhāvamāha - [] tathāceti। [] prasiddhānumānam vahnyādisādhyakadhūmādihetukānumānam।
gandhavatvādityādikamapi। [] sapakṣeti। sapakṣatvamatra sādhyaprakārakaniścayaviśeṣyatvam na tu sādhyavattvamātram asambhavāt। eva syāt na tu saddheturiti bhāvaḥ। nanu viśeṣyajñānavirahe api
ityākārakāt parāmarśāt sambhave bādhakābhāva ityata āha - [] aprasiddheti [] abhiprāyeṇeti। tathā cāprasiddhasādhyake api bhāvaḥ। evena sādhyaviśeṣyakānumitivyavacchedaḥ। [] jalādīnāmityādi। trayodaśānyonyābhāvā iti karmadhāraya etanmata iti dhyeyam। kecittu mate tu jalāditrayodaśeti punarbahuvrīhiḥ। anyathā caturdaśātmakasamudāyālābhāt।
trayodaśānyonyābhāva iti ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ। [] trayodaśatvāvacchinneti dīpikāvākye trayodaśatvaṃ samudāyatvaviśeṣa iti sūcitam। avacchinnatvaṃ vaiśiṣṭyaṃ bhedagatam। trayodaśetyādivākye kathaṃ tallābha ityata āha - [] jalādītyādiriti। tathā ca śeṣapūraṇena tādṛśārbhalābha iti
bhāvaḥ। matāntarasādhāraṇyena vyatirekavyāpteranumityaṅgatvasthāpanānupapattiśca। evaṃ iti vyākhyānakleśaḥ। svāyatte śabdaprayoge īdṛśavakrābhidhānasya prāthamyamātraparatve asvārasyam ceti। dīpikāyām [] ekādhikaraṇavṛttitvābhāvāditi। ekādhikaraṇavṛttitayā
anumiteḥ prāṅniścatatvābhāvādityarthaḥ। sādhyābhāveti। api tu jalādibhedakūṭamiti। etena dīpikāvākyasthaṃ melanamityantaṃ vyākhyātam। yadyapi kūṭatvasyaikaviśiṣṭāparatvarūpatve
vāyvādibhedaviśiṣṭatejobhedasya sādhyatvasvīkārāt na doṣaḥ। vyāsajyavṛttitvābhyupagamena pravṛttaḥ। anyathā punaruktarītireveti dhyeyam। [] anumityaṅgatvam anumitiprayojakatvam। [] agre api - jalāditrayodaśatvāvacchinnabhedātmakasādhyasyetyatrāpi।
asmaduktarītyā yathāśrutārthasyaiva upapatteḥ। jalādīti śeṣapūraṇasyāyuktatvamityasvarasaḥ āhurityanena sūcitaḥ। virodhaḥ। evamanyatrāpi bodhyam। tādṛśavyāpakatā ca svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitvīyādheyatāsambandhāvacchinnāvacchedakatāsambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvamiti।
pakṣalakṣaṇamiti labhyate। tacca hrado vahnimānityādau viśeṣyatāsambandheneti। [] sapakṣalakṣaṇādikamityādi। viśeṣyatāsaṃbandhena sādhyaprakārakaniścayavattvaṃ sapakṣalakṣaṇam। ādipadagrāhyaṃ vipakṣalakṣaṇamapi tena saṃbandhena sādhyābhāvaprakārakaniścayavattvam। anyathā hradādau
bhrāntapuruṣīyopanyāsānupapatteḥ। dīpikāyām [] niścitatveneti। itaravilakṣaṇatvenetyādi। dīpikāyāñ [] uktetyādi। yadyapi tādṛśasiddhyabhāvaḥ ghaṭādāvapyastīti parvato vahnimānityādau tatrātiprasaṅgaḥ। tathā ca pakṣapadapravṛttinimittatopeyata iti na doṣaḥ। ādṛśasya iha parvatatvādeḥ ghaṭādāvabhāvāditi bodhyam।
nirūpye'tyantopādānasya prayojanamāha - [] asaddhetunirūpaṇa iti। kṛta iti śeṣaḥ। tathā ca kṛtiḥ sapatamyarthaḥ। tasyā uttarakālīnatvasambandhena smaraṇe anvayaḥ। [] prasaṅgasaṅgatyeti। asaddhetutvādirūpayeti śeṣaḥ। []
taditi। hetuvadābhāsanta itīti। idaṃ cārthapradarśanaparam, na tu vigrahapradarśanaparam। vigrahastu hetava ivābhāsā iti vaktavyam। tādātmyena saddhetuprakārakabhramaviśeṣyatetyarthaḥ। bhramahetudoṣaśca
pañcamyantapadapratipādyatvarūpaḥ। dīnapikāyām [] saddhentu nirūpyetyādi tadanukūlavartamānakālīnakṛtimānityakhaṇḍabodhaḥ। atrāsaddhetumityasya dehalīdīpanyāyenobhayatrānvayaḥ। prathamavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svapratiyogisamānakartṛkatvasvāśrayakālavṛttitvobhayasambandhena।
svaprayojyecchāviṣayatvasvaviṣayasamānakartṛkatvobhayasambandhena। saddhetumityatra satpadasyārthamāha - prakāśikāyām [] vyāptyādiviśiṣṭeti। ādinā pakṣadharmatāparigrahaḥ। tādṛśasyeti। - doṣalakṣaṇa ityādi।
prāptyarthakadhātorjñānārthakatvāditi bhāvaḥ। [] atrānumitipadamityādi। ayamāśayaḥ-anumitipadaṃ na tu parāmarśasyānumitikaraṇatvenātra praveśaḥ। yadyapi parvato tadviṣaye ativyāptiḥ। bādhādyasaṅgrahabhiyā tādṛśānyataratvavyāpakapratibadhyatāniveśāsambhavāt। tathāpi
na doṣaḥ। ata evānumitikaraṇatvena parāmarśaniveśopekṣā। bhramabhinnetyarthaḥ iti। bhamatvaṃ ca saṃsargaviśiṣṭānyaprakāratānirūpakatvam। tena parvato nirvahniriti jñānasya kiñcidaṃśe pramātve api na kṣatiḥ।
[] yadrūpāvacchinnaviṣayaketi। ityādyekadeśajñānamādāyāsambhavassyāditi tadupekṣā। kastarhi niṣkṛṣṭahetvābhāsalakṣaṇaṃ pradarśayati - [] evaṃ ceti। grāhyaḥ, tadavacchinnatvaṃ rajatatvaniṣṭhaprakāratāyāmasti। evaṃ svaṃ samavāyaḥ
rajatatvaniṣṭhaprakaratāyāmasti। eṃva svaṃ samavāyaḥ tatpratiyogi rajatatvaṃ tanniṣṭhatvaṃ ca prakāratāyāmasti। ataḥ uktatritayasaṃbandhena rajatatvaniṣṭhaprakāratā tannirūpakatvaṃ bhrama iti। pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭarūpasattvaṃ hetvābhāsatvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca
svaviśiṣṭapratibadhyatānirūpitapratibandhakatāviśiṣṭatvasambandhena। tvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasvāvacchinnaviśeṣyatānirūpitasādhyavyāpyahetuprakāratāśāliparāmarśavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākaprat iyogitākabhedavattvobhayasambandhena। pratibandhakatāvaiśiṣṭyaṃ ādheyatāsambandhena। sā ca vasetyādibhedavattvasaṃbandhena। svādhikaraṇatā
svāvacchinnaviṣayakānāhāryāprāmāṇyajñānānāskanditaniścayatvasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā svarūpasambandhena। tenātrāyaṃ doṣa ityādau na vākyabhedaḥ। atrāyaṃ pratibadhyapratibandhakabhāvaniṣkarṣaḥ। tacchālyanāhāryatvādiviśiṣṭajñānatvena virodhitvam। atra jātimān
anavacchinnatvaniveśanam। evaṃ pratibadhyadiśi kālikatvādinā saṃyogatvāvacchinnasarṃsatāpraveśa iti dhyeyam। jñānaviśeṣaniveśe prayojanamāha - [] taneti। [] aprāmāṇyajñānaviśiṣṭasyeti। viṣayatvasāmānādhikaraṇyobhayasambandhenetyādiḥ।
pakṣatāvacchedakam। doṣatāvacchedakarūpaparaḥ। miśravyākhyāmupanyasyati - [] paretvityādinā। tathā ca na duṣṭanirūpaṇapratijñāvirodha iti bhāvaḥ। [] idam -
anumitipratibandhakayathārthajñānaviṣayatvam। evena doṣavyavacchedaḥ। nanu parvato bādhabhramamādāyātiprasaṅgaḥ। tasyāpyanumitipratibandhakatayā hetau tatprakārakagrahasya yathārthatvasambhavādityata āha - [] parantviti। nanu jñāyamānavyabhicārādipratibandhakatāmatāśrayaṇe lakṣaṇavākyārthānupapattirityata āha - [] tadarthastviti।
anumitītyādilakṣaṇavākyārthastvityarthaḥ। svaviṣayaketyarthaḥ jñānaviśeṣaṇam। lakṣye lakṣaṇaṃ grāhayati - [] dhūmavānityādinā। [] ukteti। ekajñānaviṣayaprakṛtahetutāvacchedakadharmavattvarūpetyarthaḥ। evamagre api [] darśitetyasya।
dhūmābhāvavadvṛttitvaviśiṣṭavahnyādirūpavyabhicāretyarthaḥ। dhūmādityādāvativyāptiḥ। hrado dhūmavānityādyanumitipratibandhako sattvāt ityāśaṅkāṃ nirārakaroti [] prakṛteti। prakṛtapakṣakaprakṛtasādhyakaprakṛtahetuketyarthaḥ। nātivyāptirityanena sambandhaḥ। [] yathārthapadānupādāna ityādi। yadyapyanupadameva parvato
nātiprasaṅgaprasaktirityuktatvāt। kathametatprayojanakathanasaṅgatiḥ। rāsabhādāvatiprasaṅga ityāśayāt na doṣaḥ। na caivaṃ saddhetāvityuktirayukteti vācyam। iha saddhetupadasya prakṛtahetubhinnaparatvāt। tathā ca saddhetāvapi pakṛtahetubhinne api
rāsabhādāviti śeṣaḥ। apinā prakṛtahetusaṃgrahaḥ। dṛṣṭāntatayā bhramapramāsādhāraṇyenaiva jñānasya lakṣaṇe niveśāditi bhāvaḥ। yathārthapadetyarthaḥ। atrāyamasvarasaḥ sphuṭatayā labhyate। uktarītyā tasya duṣṭalakṣaṇatve tu doṣalakṣaṇaṃ naiva labhyata iti śiṣyadhīvaiśadyāsiddhiḥ। yadyapyanumitipratibandhaketyanena
pratibandhakayathārthajñānetyādyukterasvārasyamiti। saṅgrahe [] sādhyābhāvavadvṛttiriti। atra kecit - vahnimān dhūmādityādau ativyāptiḥ। sādhyābhāvavatī yā dhūmādhikaraṇatā tannirūpitādheyatvasya dhūmādau sattvāt। na ca
iti vācyam। evamapi dhūmādhikaraṇatā parvatānyā dhūmādhikaraṇatātvādityādau ativyāpteḥ। tatra sādhyābhāvavān dhūmādhikaraṇatātve sattvāt। na ca sādhyābhāvavannirūpitatve sati vivakṣaṇāt a doṣa iti vācyam। evamapi dhūmādhikaraṇatā
tyatrātivyāpteḥ। na doṣa iti। sādhyabhāvavatparvatanirūpitatvābhāvādauditi bhāvaḥ। ityatrātivyāpteriti। tatra hi sādhyābhāvavān parvataḥ
ityativyāpterityarthaḥ। sādhyābhāvavadviśiṣṭādheyatvaṃ vivakṣitam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svanirūpitatvasvaniṣṭhādhikaraṇatānirūpitatvobhayasambandhena। ato na doṣa iti vācyam। evamapi prameyatvādhikaraṇatā
prameyatvādhikaraṇatātvāt ityatrātivyāpteḥ। sādhyābhāvavatī yā prameyatvādhikaraṇatātvaniṣṭhādhikaraṇatānirūpitādheyatāyāṃ sattvāt। vācyam। ādheyatāyā adhikaraṇanirūpakatvābhāvenoktadoṣānavakāśāditi vācyam। evamapi
ādheyatvādhikaraṇatātvādityatrātivyāpteḥ। sattvāt। na doṣa iti vācyam। tathā sati sādhyābhāvavadavṛttitvarūpavyāpteḥ kevalānvayigranthavirodhāpatteḥ। tatra tādṛśavyāpterabhedasyoktatvāt।
svanirūpakatvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhapratiyogitākātyantābhāvasvani rūpitatvobhayasambandhena। sādhyābhāvavadviśiṣṭādheyatvaṃ vivakṣitamiti na doṣaḥ। ādheyatāyā adhikaraṇanirūpakatāvirahāt iti vācyam। uktapariṣkārāsambhavāt।
niveśyamiti na doṣaḥ। sarvasaṃmatatvāt iti vācyam। tathāsati dhūmavān vahneritpayādāvasambhavāpatteḥ। nirūpakatayā ayogolakādimato aprasiddheriti vadanti।
sādhyābhāvavadviśiṣṭādheyatvaṃ vivakṣitam। vailakṣaṇyaṃ cākhaṇḍopādhiḥ। na ca tatra mānābhāva iti vācyam। kāryatāyāḥ saptamyarthatāyā apyāvaśyakatvāt। vailakṣaṇyasya cākhaṇḍopādhirūpādanyasya nirvaktumaśakyatvāt iti bodhyay।
ityāhuḥ। taccintyam - parvatānyā prameyādhikaraṇatātvādityādāvavyāpteḥ। prameyatvena prakṛtahetorapi tādṛśādhikaraṇatānirūpakatvāt iti। prakāśikāyām [] sādhyatāvacchedakadharmasaṃbandhāvacchinneti।
sādhyatāvacchedakadharmasambandhaparyāptāvacchedakatāketyarthaḥ। tena vyāvṛttiḥ। tādṛśāvacchedakatākatvaṃ ca tādṛśadharmetaradharmānavacchinnatve sati sādṛśasambandhetarasambandhānavacchinnatvam। ativyāptivāraṇāya। [] sādhyābhāvavattāyām
sādhyābhāvaniṣṭhādheyatāyām। nanu kapisaṃyogī etatvādityādau ativyāptiḥ। śuddhaviśeṣaṇatāyāstādṛśatvādityata āha - kapīti। tādṛśasambandhaḥ। yadi ca
taddoṣatādavasthyamityucyate। tadā pratibandhakaḥ taddharmaparyāptādheyatāvacchedakatāniveśāt na doṣaḥ। na vācyam। tādṛśaniścayasāmānyaṃ pratibandhakamityarthavivakṣaṇāt। tathā ca jñānatvavṛttidharmaparyāptāvacchedakatākatvaṃ niveśyam। vṛttiśca
svasetyādi bhedavattvasaṃbandhena। svādhikaraṇatā svaparyāptāvacchedakatākasaṃsargatākasādhyābhāvaprakāratānirūpitaviśeṣyatāvacchedakatānirūpakaniścayatvasaṃbandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatāsvāśrayaviśiṣṭatvasaṃbandhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ tādātmyasvaviśiṣṭapratibadhyatānirūpitapratibandhakatvobhayasambandhena।
svaviśeṣyatāvacchedakadharmāvacchinnaviśeṣyatānirūpitasādhyatāvacchedakadharmasambandhāvacchinnaprakāratāśālyanāhāryajñānavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasaṃbandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasaṃbandhena। nāto vyabhicārasya viśiṣṭaikārtharūpatābhaṅga iti। [] sapakṣavṛttitveti। nanu sapakṣatvaṃ yadi sādhyavattvamātraṃ tadā asambhavaḥ। śabdatvādāvanityatvādisāmānādhikaraṇyasattvādityata āha -
[] sapakṣapadamiti। nanu śabdādāvanityatvādisādhane tasyāsādhāraṇahetvābhāsatetyāśaṅkyāha - [] śabda ityādi। [] sampradāyavidaḥ prāñcaḥ। navīnamatasya nirduṣṭatvāt prāhurityuktam। [] anvayavyatirekadṛṣṭāntarahito anupasaṃhārī iti [] anvayavyatireketi। yatkiñciddharmiṇi sādhyaniścayasya
daladvayopādānam। virodhāsādhāraṇyayorabhedaprasaṅgaḥ ityata āha - [] sādhyābhāveti। sākṣāt - parāmarśamadvārīkṛtya। tadabhāvavyāpyavattājñānavidhayeti yāvat। sādhye anvayaḥ। pakṣa ityadhyāhāryam। prācīnamate
vidyata ityasya jñāyata ityarthaḥ karmākhyātāśrayaṇāt। navyamate tu kartrākhyātāśrayaṇena vartata ityarthaḥ। sādhakam - vyāpyatayā gṛhyamāṇamityarthaḥ। navīnamate tu vyāpyamityartha yatsambandhītyādi। [] navīnāḥ punariti। sādhyābhāvavyāpyahetvantaravatpakṣaḥ
satpratipakṣaḥ। vyāptiścānvayato vyatirekataśca bodhyā। tadgrahaśca tadabhāvavyāpyavattāgrahavidhayānumitivirodhīti bhāvaḥ। [] pakṣe pakṣatāvacchedakaviraha iti। tajjñānasya pakṣatāvacchedakaviśiṣṭapakṣagrahavirodhitvam। [] pakṣe hetvabhāva iti। tadgrahasya ca
pakṣadharmatāvagāhiparāmarśavirodhitvaṃ bodhyam। nanu upadheyasaṅkare apīti nyāyāt। ataḥ sopādhiko vyāpyatvāsiddha ityasaṅgatamiti hetvābhāsapañcatvavyāghātāpattirityata āha - [] upādheriti। nanu tayorvyāpyatvāsiddhāvantarbhāvāt na tadvirodha ityāha - [] atredamavadheyamityādinā।
saṃgrahe [] sādhyavyāpakatve satītyādi। atra ca vahnimāndhūmādityādau dravyatvāderghaṭādeśca vāraṇāya daladvayopādānam। nanu dvitvādyavacchinnābhāvapratiyogitvāt। kiṃ tu sādhyavanniṣṭhābhāvapratiyogitānavacchedakadharmavattvam। tathā ca
sādhyavyāpakatvāt upādhitāpattirityata āha - prakāśikāyām [] sādhyavyāpakatvetyādi। sādhyatāvacchedakasaṃbandhena ya pādhitāghaṭakadharmaḥ tadvattvamityarthaḥ। ayamatrānugamaḥ bhedaviśiṣṭopādhitāvacchedakadharmavattvaṃ upādhilakṣaṇam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ svāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭopādhitāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnasādhanavanniṣṭhābhāvīyapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasambandhena।
svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svapratiyogitāvacchedakatāsambandhena। avacchedakatā iti। upādhitāvacchedakasambandhapraveśaphalamāha teneti। upādhitāghaṭakasambandhaviśiṣṭopādhitāghaṭakadharmavattvaṃ lakṣaṇam। vadanti। vastutastu avacchedakatāviśiṣṭadharmavattvam tat। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ
svāśrayatvasvaviśiṣṭāvacchedakatvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvobhayasaṃbandhena। iti। upādhitāvacchedakadharma ityarthaḥ। upādhitāghaṭakasaṃbandhetyatrāpi upādhitāvacchedakasaṃbandhetyarthaḥ। svāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvasvaviśiṣṭapratiyogitānirūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena।
svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svanirūpakapratiyogitāviśiṣṭatvasaṃbandhena। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ sādhanatāvacchedakāvacchinnavannirūpitādheyatāvacchedakasambandhāvacchinnasādhyatāvacchedakāvacchinnavannirūpitādheyatāvadabhāvīyatvobhayasaṃbandhena। ato na sambandhāntarāṇyādāya dūṣaṇāvakāśa iti। vāyuḥ pratyakṣa ityādau udbhūtarūpādeḥ guṇādisādhāraṇaśuddhasādhyavyāpakatvābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ। [] yaddharmaviśiṣṭasādhyetyādi।
pakṣadharmādiviśiṣṭopādhitāvacchedakadharmavattvamiti niṣkarṣaḥ। svāvacchinnasādhyanirūpitatatsambandhāvacchinnavyāpakatāvacchedakatvasvāvacchinnasādhananirūpitatatsambandhāvacchinnāvyāpakatāvacchedakatvobhayasaṃbandhena। adhikaraṇatāviśiṣṭarūpavatvaṃ vivakṣitam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ sambandhena।
svāśrayāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvasvanirūpakapakṣadharmādiviśiṣṭasādhyavanniṣṭhātyantābhāvīyatvobhayasaṃbandhena। adhikaraṇatā ca svāvacchinnasādhanavanniṣṭhābhāvīyatvasambandhāvacchinnā। tenātrāyamupādhirityatra na vākyabhedaḥ। vastutastu adhikaraṇatāviśiṣṭadharmavattvamupādhilakṣaṇam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ
svanirūpakabhedapratiyogitākādhikaraṇatānirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvasvaviśiṣṭapratiyogitānirūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svaviśiṣṭasādhyavannirūpitādheyatāvadabhāvīyatvasvanirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakādhikaraṇatāśrayasambandhāvacchinnatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svāśrayasaṃmbandhāvacchinnatvasaṃbandhena। dvitīye vaiśiṣṭyaṃ svanirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakādhikaraṇatānirūpakabhedapratiyogi tāvacchedakasaṃbandhāvacchinnatvasvaviśiṣṭapratiyogitānirūpitatvobhayasaṃbandhena।
svanirūpakabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakādhikaraṇatāśrayasambandhāvacchinnatvasvaviśiṣṭasādhanavannirūpitādheyatāvadabhāvīyatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svāśrayasambandhāvacchinnatvasambandhena। atra sādhyavattvaṃ saṃbandhāntareṇa sādhyādhikaraṇamādāya na doṣaḥ। na vā viśiṣṭasattāvān jāterityādau dravyatvāderūpādhitānupapattiḥ। evaṃ
sādhanatāvacchedakāvacchinnavattvam। tena sādhanādhikaraṇamādāya na doṣaḥ। na vā dravyaṃ viśiṣṭasattvādityādau guṇāderupādhitāpattiḥ evaṃ vyāvṛttyantaramavaseyam। parvatīyadhūmādherityarthaḥ। []
pakṣadharmatākathanam। tena bāhyapratyakṣaviṣayatvasya sādhyatāyāṃ dravyatvamātrameva pakṣadharma iti sūcitam। [] anityatvavyāpakamiti। dīpikāvākye anityatvapadasya janyatvavināśitvasādhāraṇatvāt prakṛtānuguṇyārthamāha [] vināśitveti। anyathā tādṛśasādhyavyāpakatvopādanaparatvaṃ tādṛśagranthasya na saṃbhavatīti bhāvaḥ।
ityadhyāhāryam। tathā yaddhetusaṃbandhi yat sādhyaṃ tadabhāva ityarthaḥ। sambandhaśca hetusādhyabhāvalakṣaṇaḥ। atra bādhādiniścayānāṃ kutra kena rūpeṇa pratibandhakatvamityāśaṅkāyāmāha - dīpikāyām bādhasyetyādinā।
doṣaviśeṣe api prayogādāha prakāśikāyām [] bādhasya sādhyābhāvavattāniścayasyeti। dīpikāyām [] satpratipakṣasya virodhijñānajanakasāmagrītveneti। satpratipakṣasya satpratipakṣajñānasya। virodhijñānajanakasāmagrītvena tadabhāvavattājñānajanakasāmagrītvena। tadabhāvavyāpyavattājñānatvenaiva pratibandhakatvamucitam, lāghavāt।
virodhitvamāvaśyakam। etena virodhijñānajanakatvena virodhitvamityapi pratyuktamiti prāhuḥ। tanmataṃ darśaṃyati prakāśikāyām [] vastutastviti। nanu dīpikāyām tasyāvyabhicārābhāvarūpatvāsambhavāt ityata āha- [] bhāvapradhānanirdeśatayeti। [] evamagre apīti। viruddhasyetyādāvityarthaḥ। vastutastu
iti dhyeyam। nanu sādhyābhāvavadvṛttitvajñānasya hetudharmikasya ityanubhavasiddham, tacca nopapadyate। sādhyābhāvavadvṛttitvajñānasya ityāśaṅkyāha - [] hetāviti। hetusamānādhikaraṇetyādivyāptītyarthaḥ। [] maṇimantrādinyāyeneti।
tādṛśavyāptigrahāvirodhitve api na taddaśāyāṃ tadāpattiriti bhāvaḥ। [] viśiṣṭavyāptyabhāvatayetyādi। athātra dhūmavān vahnerityādau tadabhāvasya sutarāmaprasiddhyā kathamābhāsatā। na ca - eva hetuniṣṭhaḥ vyāpyatvāsiddhiriti na doṣaḥ।
vācyam। tathā sati prāguktavyabhicārādīnāmābhāsatānupapateraśakyaparihāratvāditi। maivam। yataḥ svasetyādyavacchedakatvasambandhena।
vyabhicāraḥ। vyāpyatvāsiddhiḥ। uktagranthasyāpyatraiva tātparyam। ato na dhūmavān vahnerityādau uktarītyā tadaprasiddhiriti madekapariśīlitaḥ panthā। vivakṣita iti nāprasiddhiriti vadanti। tattuccham dhūmavān
tadvirodhitayā hetvābhāsatāyā durvañcatvāt। darśitajñāne tulyavittivedyatānyāyena niyamatastadbhāne mānābhāvāt। pratyakṣarūpe hetvābhāsatāyā ayuktatvāt। tādṛśaparāmarśasya tādṛśobhayābhāvagrahapratibadhyatvāyogāt। tādṛśaparāmarśe
viparītaniścayapratibadhyatvāsaṃbhavācca। dhūmatvatvādyanavacchinnavidheyatāvacchedakatākānumityanupapattiprasaṅgāt। iti tadapi na sat। kāraṇatāvacchedakagarbhe vyāpyatvāsiddheḥ। [] viśiṣṭavyāptyabhāvatayeti dīpikāvākyena
hetuniṣṭhābhāvasyaiva doṣatāpratīteḥ tāvatāpi tadanupapādanācca। mahāgauravācca iti sarvamanavadyam। dīpikāyām [] vyāptisaṃśayādhāyakatveneti। ādhāyakatvaṃ prayojakatvam। nanu prakāśikāyām [] hetāvasādhāraṇyādīti। ādinā
anupasaṃhāritvasaṃgrahaḥ। navīnamataṃ tu prāgevoktamiti bhāvaḥ। [] vyāptijñānapratibandhakaḥ vyāptijñānavirodhidhīviṣayaḥ। paramukhanirīkṣakasyetyatra pratibandha ityādiḥ। atrāyamāśayaḥ
tadanutpādaprayojakatvam। vyabhicāritāsambandhena upādhiviśiṣṭahetāvatiprasaṅgāt। evaṃ ca nātivyāptiriti। bhāvaḥ। [] āśrayāsiddhāvantarbhavatīti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ -
āśrayasya pakṣatāviśiṣṭasyāsiddhiḥ ceneti vigrahaḥ। tathā ca pakṣatāvacchedakāvacchinnasya tadānīmasiddheḥ। sādhyavatpakṣasya tatrāntarbhāva ucita iti bhāvaḥ। siddhasādhanasyāśrayāsiddhyantarbhāvaprayojakaṃ pakṣatāvighaṭakatvamupapādayati [] prakāśe tanamata iti।
prācīnamata ityarthaḥ। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ pakṣatāvighaṭakatvaṃ āśrayāsiddhitvam। vighaṭakatvaṃ ca virodhigrahaviṣayatvam। pakṣatā ca prācīnamate। tathā ca pakṣaniṣṭhapakṣatāvacchedakavirahasnya sādhyavatpakṣasya ca niścayadaśāyāmuktapakṣatāyā asambhavāt। ubhayorapi
vibhāgavyāghātaśaṅketi bhāvaḥ। siddheḥ pūrvaṃ parato vā yatra siṣādhayiṣā tatra siṣādhayiṣāvirahakālāvacchedena siddheḥ। śaṅkānirāsāyoktañ [] kevalamiti। anena siddheḥ siṣādhayiṣāsāhityābhāvavyavacchedaḥ। tathā ca siddheḥ pūrvaṃ parataśca
ityarthaḥ।। ।। iti prasaraṇākhyāyāṃ dīpikāprakāśavyākhyāyāmanumānaparicchedaḥ।। । ।
prayojyatvamarthaḥ। tasya śrudhātvarthaśābdabodhe anvayaḥ। iti śabdasya śabdānvayītyākārakatvamarthaḥ। yattu itiśabdaḥ tādṛśānupūrvyavacchinnavākyaparaḥ, śrudhātoḥ śrāvaṇapratyakṣamarthaḥ। tatra anyāyyatvāt। prakāśe [] avasarasaṅgatyeti।
pratibandhakībhūtaśiṣyajijñāsānivṛtyuttarakālīnāvaśyavaktavyatvamavasaraḥ। tṛtīyārthādikaṃ sarvamapi pūrvavat। padapadārthasambandhaviṣayakajñānatvaṃ lakṣaṇamuktam - tanna yujyate। tādṛśānumityādāvativyāpteḥ। atastādṛśasaṅgrahavākyaṃ
- [] upamitisvarūpamiti। kiṃ tarhi tasyā lakṣaṇamityākāṅkṣāyām lakṣaṇaṃ tviti। gamyetyantam upamititvasya jātirūpatāyāṃ pramāṇasūcanāya। [] etena smaranniti vartamānanirdeśena। [] āhuriti। atra ca saṃgrahakārasya upamitiḥ phalamiti matapradarśanam। tathāsati śabdaprayogasya
tādṛśagranthavyākhyānānaucityamarucibījam। gosadṛśo gavayapadavācya iti svarūpātideśetyādiḥ। [] udbodhakāntareti। sādṛśyaviśiṣṭapiṇḍadarśanātiriktādṛṣṭādirūpodbodhaketyarthaḥ। [] sādṛśya darśanānantaramityādi। atropamiteḥayaṃ
upamitirupagantavyetyabhiprāyeṇoktam [] gavayatvādirūpalaghudharmet i। tādṛśadharmāvacchinnaviśeṣyatāketyarthaḥ। [] idam-sādṛśyadarśanasya upamitihetutāpradarśanaṃ, upalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyamāṇārthasūcakam। [] sādṛśyādītyādinā vaidharmyasaṃgrahaḥ। ।। iti prasaraṇākhyāyāṃ dīpikāprakāśikāvyākhyāyāṃ upamānaparicchedaḥ।।

bodhakatvāsambhavaḥ। evamaṣṭakāpadasthāne api paryāyapadāntaraprakṣepo bodhya iti bhāvaḥ। idaṃ cārthaviśeṣabodhāpatteriti pāṭhamabhisandhāya। arthaviśeṣabodhānāpatteriti pāṭhe tu tannaiyatyānupapatterityarthaḥ।
[] anumānānusaraṇamiti। bodhyaḥ। prathamavakturapi sāmānyarūpeṇa jñātatvāt urktaṃ viśiṣyeti। prathameti kriyāviśeṣaṇam। prāthamyaṃ ca vacane
dhvaṃsaviśiṣṭānyatva paryavasitam। veśiṣṭyaṃ svasamānākālīnatvasvapratiyogivacanapratipādyārthapratipādakatvobhayasambandhena।। dīpikāprasaraṇākhyāyāṃ prakāśavyākhyāyāṃ śabdaparicchedaḥ।। । ।
[] pramāṇaprasaṅgāditi। ramāṇanirūpitasvajanyavṛttiniṣṭhatvātmakaprasaṅgasaṅgaterityarthaḥ। annirūpitasmṛtaniṣṭhopekṣāviṣayatāvirodhirūpātmakasaṅgaterityarthaḥ। tacca rūpaṃ prakṛte paratogrāhyatvam। smṛtiśca
vajanyavṛttiniṣṭhatvasambandhena jāyate। atha vā pramāṇaṃ pramā, annirūpitasvavṛttiniṣṭhatvātmakaprasaṅgasaṅgaterityarthaḥ। jñānajanyajijñāsādhīnatvaṃ pañcamyarthaḥ। tathā ca granthābhinnaśabdānukūlavartamānakālīnakṛtimāniti bodhaḥ।
svatogrāhyamityatra [] jñānagrāhaketi। [] parata ityatra paraśabdaḥ anumānādipara ityāśayenāha - [] anumānādīti। ādinā āptoktaśabdaparigrahaḥ। pramāṇanirūpitetyādi। pramāṇanirūpitetyasya saṃgatāvanvayaḥ। svaṃ
tathā ca yannirūpaṇānantaraṃ yannirūpyate tayoreva saṃgatirūpaḥ saṃbandhaḥ। pramāṇanirūpitā saṃgatiḥ paratogrāhyatve vaktavyā। sā ca svajanyavṛttiniṣṭhatvātmakaprasaṅgarūpeti bhāvaḥ। tannirūpitetyādi।
upekṣaviṣayatāvirodhirūpaṃ paratogrāhyatvaṃ tadātmikā saṃgatiḥ। svajanyetyādi। svaṃ pramāṇam, tajjanyā pramā tadvṛtti pramātvaṃ tanniṣṭhatvaṃ paratogrāhyatve। tannirūpitetyādi।
tannirūpitā pramānirūpitā, saṃgatirityanvayaḥ। svaṃ pramātadvṛtti pramātvaṃ tanniṣṭhatvaṃ paratogrāhyatve। svaśabda iti। svaśabdo atra svīyavācī san jñānagrāhakasāmagrīpara iti bhāvaḥ।

bodhaviśeṣaṇam। pravartaka iti śeṣaḥ। [] evaṃ ca - uktarītyā vicārapravṛttau ca। [] vicāropayogitvamiti। vipratipatterityādiḥ। atra jñānaprāmāṇyamiti pakṣanirdeśaḥ। ghaṭakatvaṃ saptamyarthaḥ jñānapadānvitam। [] tādṛśeti। aprāmāṇyāgrāhakajñānagrāhakayāvatsāmagrījanyetyarthaḥ। [] atrauktamatatraye। ghaṭakatvaṃ saptamyarthaḥ gurumatānvayi। [] taditi। []
evaṃ ca uktarītyā vyavasthāpane ca। nanu āha [] viśiṣṭeti। tadrūpetyādiḥ। yāvaditi sāmagrīviśeṣaṇam। ata evāgre jñānagrāhakayāvadityuktam। pramitikaraṇatvarūpaprāmāṇyasya paraiḥ
svatogrāhyatvānupagamena tatra vicārāsambhavādāha [] vastutastviti। pramitikaraṇatvavyāvṛttiḥ na sambhavati। parāmarśādeḥ tadasat। jñānasyaiva prāmāṇyamityavadhāraṇavivakṣā pramitikaraṇatvasyendiyasādhāraṇasya vyāvṛttisambhavāt। sarvaṃ
vākyamiti nyāyena śabdenaiva tādṛśārthalābhāt। nanu viśiṣṭa āha - [] taddharmeti। yāvatpadasya samabhivyāhṛtapadārthatāvacchedakavyāpakatvaparatvāditi bhāvaḥ। [] phalataḥ tātparyataḥ। [] sāmānyarūpeṇa।
taddharmaprakārakatvarūpajñānaviśeṣaṇāviśeṣitena jñānatveneti yāvat। jñānānvayini vaiśiṣṭye tasil। anyathā ghaṭatvādighaṭitaprāmāṇyasya ghaṭatvādiprakārakajñānagrāhakagrāhyatvābhāvena vidhau bādhāpatteḥ। idaṃ dīpikāvākyamasaṅgatam ata āha - [] vyavasāyaniṣṭhetyādiḥ।
iti strīliṅganirdeśa eva kārya ityata āha - [] sāmānya iti। tathā ca liṅgaviśeṣāvivakṣāyāṃ napuṃsakasyaiva nirdeṣṭavyatayā noktadoṣa iti bhāvaḥ। tasyāprāmāṇyamiti ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣabhramavāraṇāya [] saptamīti। [] yādṛśaprāmāṇyami tyādi। atrāyaṃ niṣkarṣaḥ taddharmaghaṭitaprāmāṇyaṃ kiñcidviśiṣṭamiti। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ
tādātmyasvavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasambandhena। vasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatāsambandhena। svaviśiṣṭataddharmaprakārakajñānagrāhakasāmagrījanyatānatvasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena।
taddharmaghaṭitaprāmāṇyaparaḥ। svaviśiṣṭetyasya jñānagrāhakasāmagryāmanvayaḥ। taddharmaghaṭitaprāmāṇyamiti phalitam। etatsamanvayaprakāraḥ itthamsvaṃ ghaṭatvavati ghaṭatvaprakārakatvarūpaṃ pramātvaṃ tadāśrayaḥ। niṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavatī bhavati।
tatreti saṃbandhadvayopapattiriti। paścāttaneṣvanugameṣvapyevamūhyam। savāśrayaniṣṭhaviśeṣyatānirūpitāprāmāṇyaniṣṭhaprakāratāśālijñānajanakatvasaṃbandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā svanirūpitaviṣayitāsambandhena। yadvā viṣayitāviśiṣṭatvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ
svanirūpakatvasvavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasambandhena। svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatāsambandhena। svādhikaraṇatā svāśrayaviśeṣyaketyādi prāgvat। atra ca sāmagryāṃ yāvattvapakṣe kiñcidviśiṣṭatvaṃ sthūlānugamaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ
tādātmyasvaviśiṣṭajñānaviṣayatvobhayasambandhena। svavaiśiṣṭyaṃ svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasambandhāvacchinnasvani ṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena। svaviśiṣṭajñānagrāhakatāvacchedakavyāsajyavṛttitvasambandhena। svāśrayaviśeṣyakāprāmāṇyaprakārakajñānajanakatāvacchedakatvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasaṃbandhena।
bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā svotpādakatāvacchedakatāsambandhena। svatastvaśarīre tattanniveśadaurghaṭye api na kṣatiḥ। evaṃ ca gurvāndimate niruktakiñcidviśiṣṭatvaṃ na susādhamiti। śaṅkate [] nanviti। aprasiddhimupapādayati [] na hīti। [] ekam - ekajātīyam। [] na janyata ityanvayaḥ। atra ca
noktāprasiddhiriti। śaṅkate [] na ceti। prayojanakathanamanucitamityāśaṅkāṃ parijihīrṣurāha - [] yāvattvetyādi। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ agrāhakāntasya nirvahati। prāmāṇyagrāhakasāmagīmādāya prāmāṇye svatastvasya sūpapādatvāt। tatra tadviśeṣaṇasattve tu aprāmāṇyagrāhakasāmagryā api

vyāpakatvaṃ vivakṣitamiti nāsaṅgatiḥ। [] svata eva gṛhyata iti। eve'tyarthaḥ। tathā cāyaṃ kriyāsaṅgata evakāraḥ nīlaṃ sarojaṃ bhavatyevetivat। ato na virodha iti tasya apyarthakatākathanamanupapannamiti। idamatra bodhyam - sāmagryāṃ
yāvattvapraveśe jñānaviśiṣṭatvaṃ sūkṣmānugamaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ viṣayatvasvavṛttibhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvobhayasambandhena। avacchedakatā svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatāsambandhena। svādhikaraṇatvādikaṃ pūrvavat। [] viśiṣya -
tattatkāraṇakūṭatvena। tādrūpyeṇetyatra jñāne yāvattvapraveśe bhedaviśiṣṭatvamiti sūkṣmānugamaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ svapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasvāśrayatvobhayasambandhena। avacchedakatvaṃ svasamānādhikaraṇabhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatvasambandhāvacchinnam।
svādhikaraṇatā svaviśiṣṭajñānagrāhakasāmagrījanyagrahatvasayambandhena। svāśrayaviśeṣyakāprāmāṇyaprakārakajñānajanakatvasambandhāvacchinnasvaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena। bhedapratiyogitāvacchedakatā svanirūpitaviṣayitāsambandhena। [] saṅkṣepa ityanena prāmāṇyavādagādādharyāmuktaṃ sarvamabhisaṃhitam।
tadvadviśeṣyakatvāvacchinnatatprakārakatvaṃ hi tatpramātvam। tatkathaṃ purovartinītyādidīpikāvākyasaṅgatirityata āha - [] purovartinīti। nanu purovartini viśiṣṭaprāmāṇyabhānasiddhiranuvyavasāyādāvityata āha - [] naiyāyikā apīti। nanu viśiṣṭabuddhau viśeṣaṇajñānasya āha - [] anupasthitayorapīti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ -
phalānurodhena prakṛte na tādṛśakāraṇatvakalpanamiti। tannirasanaprakāro bodhya iti। na ca tathāsati ghaṭaṃ jānāmītayādau karmatārūpatvāditi, tatra dvitīyānupapattiriti vācyam। grāmādau tadupagamāt। ghaṭaṃ jānātītyādiṣu tadanabhyupagamāt
viṣayatālakṣaṇagauṇakarmatāyā eva tatra svīkaraṇāt। anyathā iṣṭatvādirūpapadārthāntarakalpanāpātāt iti। [] saṅkṣepa iti। ayaṃ bhāvaḥ - taccāprāmāṇyaprakāratānirūpitaviśeṣyatvasāmānādhikaraṇyobhayasambandhāvacchinnajñānatvāvacchinnapratiyogitākābhāvaḥ।
evaṃ bhramatvajñānābhāvapramātvagrahābhāvāvapi niveśyau। kalpanīyam। adhikaṃ prāmāṇyavādādau draṣṭavyamiti। [] prāmāṇyavyavasthāpakahetoḥ saphalapravṛttijanakatvarūpetyādiḥ। siddhasādhanamāśaṅkya evakārapūraṇena vyācaṣṭe - [] prāmāṇyasyānumānādita eveti। [] etena - anuvyavasāyādau prāmāṇyabhānāsambhavasthāpanena। []
vyabhicāra iti। utpattidharmikaparatastvaprakārakajñānānukūlaśabdaḥ tatkartetyanvayabodhaḥ। [] mātreti। mātrapadamatrakārtsnyaparam। [] vyudāsa iti jñānatvādīnāmatathātvāditi bhāvaḥ। nanu pramāniṣṭhakāryatvātiriktadharmāvacchinnakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatvam।
evaṃ ca kālādivāraṇe api ātmādivāraṇamaśakyamata āha - [] pramātvādhiketyādi। pramātvaviśiṣṭakāryatānirūpitakāraṇatvamiti niṣkarṣaḥ। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ vādhikaraṇavṛttitvasvaviśiṣṭadharmāvacchinnatvobhayasaṃbandhena। svādhikaraṇetyādi।
pramāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvamityarthaḥ। svaṃ pramātvaṃ tadadhikaraṇaṃ pramā pramātvaviśiṣṭā kāryatā bhavatīti samanvayo jñeyaḥ। svaniṣṭhāvacchedakatākapratiyogitākabhedavattvasambandhena। avacchedakatā svādhikaraṇavṛttitvasvābhāvādhikaraṇavṛttitvobhayasambandhena।
kāryatāyāṃ pramāniṣṭhaniveśaphalamāha - [] bhrameti। [] ityādāvityādinā vaṃśoragabhramādisaṅgrahaḥ। [] pittādītyādinā maṇḍūkavasañjanādigrahaṇam। [] visaṃvādoti। tadabhāvavati tatprakāraketyarthaḥ। etena dharmiṇo aprasiddhyā niṣodho anupapanna iti śaṅkā nirastā।

prakāratāviśiṣṭetyādi। parvato vahnimān na veti saṃśaye vahniḥ tadabhāvaśca prakāraḥ। vahnitadabhāvayorvirodhaḥ saṃsargatayā bhāsate। sthitiḥ। etāṃ manasikṛtya anugamasya samanvayo jñeyaḥ। tathā hi - svaṃ tannirūpakatvaṃ ca parvato vahnimānna veti saṃśaye astīti। atra
iti siddhantādityapi dhyeyam। anyat pūrvavaditi। tathā ca prakāratāviśiṣṭajñānatvaṃ saṃśayatvam। vaiśiṣṭyaṃ ca svaviśiṣṭaprakāratānirūpakatvobhayasaṃbandheneti bhāvaḥ।
saṃśayatvam। dvitīye vaiśiṣṭyaṃ vanirūpitaviśeṣyatāvacchedakāvacchinnaviśeṣyatānirūpitatvasvāvacchedakāvacchinnaviṣayatānirūpitavirodhaviṣayatānirūpitatvasvānavacchedakāvacchinnatvatritayasambandhena। ato na doṣa iti। [] tantrāntare - advaitaśāstre। [] tatprakārakatvetyādi ityādināṃ tadabhāvavanniṣṭhaviśeṣyatāniyapitatanniṣṭhaprakāratākatvaparigrahaḥ। ayamāśayaḥ yadyapi idaṃ rajatam bhūtalaṃ
saṃśayānyatvaniveśāt na doṣaḥ। tadaṃśe saṃśayatvaṃ caikasmin dharmiṇi tattadabhāvobhayaprakāratakatvamiti। puruṣatvaniścayo jāyatāmitīcchāyā vācyatvāt। anyathā bādhakālīlanecchājanyajñānatvalakṣaṇasyāhāryatvasya tatrāsambhavāt।
